Samarāiccakahā

by Haribhaddō

paṇamaha vijiasudujaya-nijiasuramaṇua-visamasarapasaraṁ

tihuaṇamaṅgalanilayaṁ vasahagaïgayaṁ jiṇaṁ usahaṁ

paramasirivaddhamāṇaṁ paṇa?māṇaṁ visuddhavaranāṇaṁ

gayajō jōīsa sayaṁbhuvaṁ vaddhamāṇaṁ ca

sēsē ciya bāvīsē jāi-jarā-maraṇabandhaṇavimukkē

tēlōkamatthayatthē titthayarē bhāvaō namaha

uvaṇēu maṅgalaṁ vō jiṇāṇa muhalālijālasaṁvaliā

titthapavattaṇasamaē tiavimukkā kusumavuṭṭhī

dēu suhaṁ vō sura-siddha-maṇuavandrēhi sāyaraṁ namiā

titthayaravayaṇapaṅkayaviṇiggayā maṇaharā vāṇī

alaṁ pavittharēṇa. suṇaha sōavvāī, pasaṁsaha pasaṁsaṇijjāiṁ, pariharaha parihariavvāiṁ, āyaraha āyariavvāiṁ. tattha—

sōavvāiṁ narā-’mara-sivasuhajaṇayāi atthasārāī

savvannubhāsiāī bhuṣaṇammi païṭṭhiajasāī

tāī ciya vibuhāṇaṁ pasaṁsaṇijāī taha ya jāiṁ ca

tēhiṁ ciya bhaṇiāī sammatta-nāṇa-caraṇāī

parihariavvāī tahā kugaīvāsassa hēubhūāī

micchattamāiāī lōgaviruddhāī ya tahēva

āyariabvāiṁ aṇissiēṇa sammatta-nāṇa-caraṇāī

dōgaccaviuḍaṇāī cintāmaṇirayaṇabhūāī

ettha puṇa ahigārō tā sōavvēhi patthuapabandhē

sabannubhāsiāī sōabbāī ti bhaṇiyamiṇaṁ

vocchaṁ tappaḍibuddhaṁ bhaviyajaṇāṇandayāriṇiṁ paramaṁ

saṁkhēraō mahatthaṁ cariahaṁ taṁ nisāmēha

tattha ya tivihaṁ kahāvatthu ti puvyāyariyapavāō. taṁ jahā-dina, divyamāṇusaṁ, māṇusaṁ ca. tattha divyaṁ nāma jattha kēvala mēva dēvacariaṁ vaṇijjāi. divyamāṇusaṁ puṇa jattha doṇhaṁ pi divyamāṇusāṇaṁ. māṇusaṁ tu jattha kēvalaṁ māṇusacariyaṁ ti. ettha sāmanaō cattāri kahāō havanti. taṁ jahā-atthakahā, kāmakahā, dhammakahā, saṁkiṇṇakahā ya. tattha atthakahā nāma, jā atthō vāyaṇapaḍibaddhā, asi-masi-kasi-vāṇijja-sippasaṁgayā, vicittadhāuvāyāipamuhamahōbāyasaṁpaüttā, sāma-bhēya-uvappayāṇa-daṇḍāipa yatthaviraïā sā atthakaha tti bhaṇṇaï. jā uṇa kāmōvāyāṇavisayā, vitta-vapu-yaya-kalā-dakṣiṇṇaparigayā, aṇurāyapulaïapaḍi vattijōasārā, duībāvāra-ramiyabhāvāṇuvattaṇāipayatthasaṁgayā sā kāmakaha tti bhaṇṇaï. jā uṇa dhammōvāyāṇagōyarā, khamā-madava-’jjava mutti-tava-saṁjama-sacca-sōyā-’’kiṁcana-baṁbhacērapahāṇā, aṇuvyaya-disi-dēsā-’ṇatthadaṇḍaviraī-sāmāiya-pōsahōvavāsō-vabhōga paribhōgā-’tihisaṁvibhāgakaliyā, aṇukampā-’kāmanijjarāipayatthasaṁpaüttā sā dhammakaha tti. jā uṇa tivaggōvāyāṇasaṁbaddhā, kavva kahā-ganthatthavittharaviraïyā,lōiya-vēyasamayapasiddhā,uyāharaṇa-hēu-kāraṇōvavēyā sā saṁkiṇṇakaha tti vucaï. ēyāṇaṁ ca kahāṇaṁ tivihā sōyārō havanti. taṁ jahā-ahamā, majjhimā, uttama tti. tattha jē kōha-māṇa-māyā-lōha-samācchāiyamaī, paralōyadaṁsaṇaparaṁmuhā, iha lōgaparamatthadaṁsiṇō, niraṇukampā jīvēsu, tē tahāvihā tāmasā ahamapurisā duggaïgamaṇakandujjayāē, sugaïpaḍivakkhabhūyāē, paramatthaō aṇatthabahulāē atthakahāē aṇusajjanti. jē uṇa sadāivisayavisamōhiyamaṇā,bhāvariu-indiyāṇukūlabattiṇō, abhāviyaparamatthamaggā, imaṁ sundaraṁ, imaṁ sundarayaraṁ ti sundarāsundarēsu aviṇicchiyamaī, tē rāyasā majjhimapurisā buhajaṇōvahasaṇijjāē, viḍambaṇamettapaḍi baddhāē, iha parabhavē ya dukkhasaṁvaḍḍiyāē kāmakahāē aṇusajjanti. jē uṇa maṇagaṁ sundarayarā, sāvekkhā ubhayalōēsu, kusalā vavahārana yamaēṇaṁ, paramatthaō sāravinnāṇarahiyā, khuddabhōēmu abahumāṇiṇō, aviyaṇhā udārabhōgāṇaṁ, tē kiṁci sattiyā majjhimapurisā cēva āsayavisēsaō sugaï-duggaïvattiṇīē, jīva-lōgasabhāvavinbhamāē, sayalarasanīsandasaṁgayāē, vivihabhāvapasūinibandhaṇāē saṁkiṇṇa kahāē aṇusajjanti. jē uṇa jāi-jarā-maraṇajaṇiyavēraggā, jammantarammi vi kusalabhāviyamaī, niviṇṇā kāmabhōgāṇa, mukkapāyā pāvalē vēṇa, vināyaparamapayasarūvā, āsanā siddhisaṁpattīē, tē sattiyā uttimapurisā sagga-nivvāṇasamāruhaṇavattiṇīē, buhajaṇapasaṁ. saṇijjāē, sayalakahāsundarāē, mahāpurisasēviyāē dhammakahāē cēva aṇusajjanti.

tō ahaṁ piiyāṇi divya-māṇusakatthugayaṁ dhammakaha cēva kittaïssāmi. bhaṇiyaṁ ca akayaparōvayāraniraēhiṁ, uvaladdhaparamapaya maggēhiṁ, samatiṇa-maṇi-mutta-leṭṭha-kaścaṇēhiṁ sāsayasivasokkhabaddharāēhiṁ dhammasatthayārēhiṁ.

dhammēṇa kulapasūī dhammēṇa ya divvarūpasaṁpattī

dhammēṇa dhaṇasamiddhī dhammēṇa suvitthaḍā kittī

dhammō maṅgalamaülaṁ ōsahamaülaṁ ca sambadukkhāṇaṁ

dhammō balamavi viulaṁ dhammō tāṇaṁ ca saraṇaṁ ca

kiṁ jaṁpiēṇa bahuṇā? jaṁ jaṁ dīsaï samatyajiyalōē

indiya-maṇābhirāmaṁ taṁ taṁ dhammaphalaṁ savvaṁ

bhīmammi maraṇa kālē mottūṇaṁ dukkhasaṁviḍhattaṁ pi

atthaṁ dēhaṁ sayaṇaṁ dhammō cciya hōi susahāō

pāvēi ya suralōyaṁ tattō vi sumāṇusattaṇaṁ dhammō

tattō dukkhavimokkhaṁ sāsayasokkhaṁ lahuṁ mokkhaṁ

taṁ kuṇaï jāṇamāṇō, jāṇaï ya suṇēi jō u majjhatthō

kusalō ya dhammiyāō kahāu savvannubhaṇiyāō

tā paḍhamaṁ dhammaguṇaṁ paḍucca cariya ahaṁ pavakkhāmi

ārāhagē-yarāṇaṁ guṇadōsavibhāvaṇaṁ paramaṁ

navapuvvabhavanibaddhaṁ saṁvēgakaraṁ ca bhavvasattāṇaṁ

cariyaṁ samarāiccassa ’ntirannō muṇaha vocchaṁ

etthaṁ bahuyā u bhavā doṇha vi uvaōgiṇō na tē savvē

navasu paropparajōgō jattō saṁkhā imā bhaṇiyā

jaha tēṇēva bhagavayā girisēṇuvasaggasahaṇapajjantē

saṁjāyakēvalēṇaṁ sirlḍa vēlaṁdhara murassa

muṇicandassa ya rannō dēvīṇa ya nammayāpahāṇāṇaṁ

saṁkhēvēṇa phuḍatyaṁ ahamavi taṁ saṁpavakkhāmi

bhaṇiyaṁ ca puvvāyariēhiṁ—

"guṇasēṇa-aggisammā sīhā-’’ṇandā ya taha piyā-uttā

sihi-jāliṇi māra-muyā dhaṇa-dhagasirimō ya paha-bhajjā

jaya-vijayā ya sahōyara dharaṇō lacchī ya taha paī-bhajjā

sēṇa-visēṇā pittiya-uttā jammammi sattamaē

guṇacanda-vāṇamaṁtara samarāicca girisēgapāṇō u

ekkassa taō mokkhō bīyassa agantasaṁsārō

nagarāi-khiīpaïṣṭuṁ jayaüra-kōsaṁbi-musammanayaraṁ ca

kāyandī māyandī campā ojhā ya ujjēṇī

guṇasēgassukkhāō sōhamma-saṇaṁkumāra-bambhēsu

mukkā-’’ṇayā-’’raṇēsuṁ gēvejjā-’ṇuttarēsuṁ ca

iyarassa u uvavāō vijjukumārēsu hōi nāyabyō

sēsō aṇantarō uṇa rayaṇāīsuṁ ahakkamasō

sāgaramēgaṁ pañca ya nava-paṇṇarasēva taha ya aṭṭhārā

vīsaṁ tīsaṁ tettīsamēva paḍhamasta dēvēsu

dēvēsu saṅkapaliyaṁ sāgaratiya satta dasa ya sattarasa

bābīsaṁ tettīsaṁ bīyassa ṭhiī u naraēsu"

ēvamēyāō cariyasaṁgahaṇigāhāō. saṁpayaṁ ēyāsiṁ cēva gurūvaēsāṇusārēṇaṁ vittharēṇaṁ bhāvatthō kahijjaï atthi ihēba jambuddīvē dīvē, avaravidēhē vāsē, uttuṁgadhavalapāgāramaṇḍiyaṁ, naliṇivaṇasaṁchanaparihāsaṇāhaṁ, muvibhattatiya caükka-caccaraṁ bhavaṇēhiṁ jiyasurindabhavaṇasōhaṁ khiipaïṭṭhiyaṁ nāma nayaraṁ.

jattha vilayāu kamalāī kōilaṁ kuvalayāī kalahaṁsē

bayaṇēhi jaṁpiēṇa ya nayaṇēhi gaīhi ya jiṇanti

jattha ya narāṇa vasaṇaṁ vijjāsu, jasammi nimmalē lōhō

pāvēsu sayā bhīrutaṇaṁ, ca dhammammi dhaṇabuddhī

tatya ya rāyā saṁpuṇṇamaṇḍalō mayakalaṅkaparihīṇō

jaṇamaṇanayaṇāṇandō nāmēṇaṁ puṇṇacandō ti

antēurappahāṇā dēvī nāmēṇa kumuiṇī tassa

saï vaḍḍiyavisayasuhā iṭṭā ya raï va mayaṇassa

tāṇa ya suō kumārō guṇasēṇō nīma guṇagaṇāiṇṇō

bālattaṇaō vaṁtarasurō nya kēlippiō, ṇavaraṁ-

tammi ya nayarē atīva sayalajaṇabahumaō, dhammasatyasaṁghāyapāḍhaō, lōgavavahāra-nīikusalō, appārambha-pariggahō, jannadattō nāma purōhiō tti. tassa ya sōmadēvāgabbhasaṁbhūō, mahallatikōṇuttimaṅgō, āpiṅgalabaṭṭalōyaṇō, ṭhāṇamettōvalakkhiyaciviḍanāsō, bilamettakaṇṇasannō, vijiyadantacchayamahalladasaṇō, baṁkasudīharasirōharō visamaparihassabāhujuyalō, aïmaḍahavacchatthalō, kavisamala mbōyarō, ēkapāsunnayamaharūlaviyaḍakaḍiyaḍō, visamapaïṭṭhiūrujuyalō, parithūlakaḍhiṇahassajaṅghō, visamavitthiṇṇacalaṇō, huyavahasihā jālapiṅgakēsō, aggisammō nāma puttō tti. taṁ ca kōuhallēṇa kumāraguṇasēṇō pahayapaḍapaḍaha-muiṅga-vaṁsa-kaṁsā-layappahāṇēṇa mahayā tūrēṇa nayarajaṇamajhē sahatthatālaṁ hasantō nacāvēi, rāsahammi ārōviyaṁ, pahabahuḍimbhavindaparivāriyaṁ, chittaramayadhariyapoṇḍarīyaṁ, maṇa haruttālavajantaḍiṇḍima, ārōviyamahārāyasaī, bahusō rāyamaggē suturiyaturiya hiṇḍāvēi. ēvaṁ ca païdiṇaṁ kayantēṇēva tēṇa kayatthi jjantassa tassa veggabhāvaṇā jāyā. cintiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa.

bahujaṇadhikārahayā uvasaṇijjā ya sabalōyassa

puci akayasupuṇṇā sahanti paraparibhavaṁ purisā

jaï tā na kaō dhammō sappurisanisēviō ahannēṇaṁ

jammantarammi dhaṇiyaṁ suhāvahō mūḍhahiyaēṇaṁ

ihi pi phalavivāgaṁ uggaṁ dachuṭṇamakaya puṇṇāṇaṁ

paralōyabandhubhūyaṁ karēmi muṇisē viyaṁ dhammaṁ

jammantarē vi jēṇaṁ pāvēmi na ērisaṁ mahābhīmaṁ

sayalajaṇōhasaṇijja biḍambaṇaṁ dujaṇajaṇāō

ēvaṁ ca cintiya pavanavēraggamaggō niggaō nayarāō. pattō ya māsamettēṇa kālēṇa tabbisamasandhisaṁṭhiyaṁ, baüla-campagā 'sōga-punnāga-nāgāulaṁ, pasantamaya-mayāhivapamuhaviruddhasāvayagaṇaṁ, surahihavigandhagambhiṇudāmadhūmapaḍalaṁ, vimalasalilagiriṇaīpa sāhiyaviyaḍa pērantaṁ, tāvasajaṇajaṇiyahiyayapariōsaṁ supariōsaṁ nāma tavōvaṇaṁ ti.

saṁpāviūṇa ya taō dīhaddhāṇaparikhēiyasarīrō

vīsamiūṇa muhuttaṁ tavōvaṇaṁ aha pavihō sō

diṭṭhō ya tēṇa vakkala-viyaḍajaḍā-’jiṇa-tiṇḍadhārī ya

bhūirayakayatipuṇḍō āsannakamaṇḍalū sōmō

bhisiyāē suhanisaṇṇō kayalīharayantarammi jhāṇagaō

parivattentō dāhiṇakarēṇa ruddakkhamālaṁ ti

mantakkharajavaṇēṇa ya īsi viyalantakaṇṭhaüṭṭaüḍō

nāsāē nimiyadiṭṭhī viṇiyāriyasēsavāvārō

ayasimayajōgapaṭṭayapamāṇasaṁgayakayāsaṇavisēsō. tāvasakulappahāṇō ajjavakōḍiṇṇanāmō tti. picchiūṇa ya harisavasullasiyarōmaścaṇaṁ, dharaṇinimiyajāṇukarayalēṇaṁ, uttimaṅgēṇaṁ puṇō puṇō pahayakhiitalēṇaṁ ahō! dhannō, ahō! dhannō tti bhaṇamāṇēṇaṁ paṇamiō tēṇaṁ. tēṇa vi ya taṁ tahā pecchiūṇa atihibahumāṇakaraṇalālasēṇa jāṇajōgaṁ pamottūṇaṁ sāgaya vayaṇapurassaraṁ ahō! āsaṇaṁ āsaṇaṁ ti bhaṇamāṇēṇaṁ bahumaniō. taō uḍayaṅgaṇanisēvitāvasakumārōvaṇīē isiṇā ya uvavisasu ettha tti bhaṇiō saviṇayaṁ ubaviṭṭhō viṭṭharē tti. pucchiō ya isiṇā — kuō bhavaṁ āgaō? ti. taō tēṇa savittharō nivēiō sē attaṇō vuttantō. bhaṇiō ya isiṇā-vaccha! puvakayakammapariṇaïvasēṇaṁ ēvaṁ parikilēsabhāiṇō jīvā havanti. tā narindāva māṇapīḍiyāṇaṁ, dāriddadukkhaparibhūyāṇaṁ, dōhagga-kalaṅkamiyāṇaṁ, iṭhṭhajaṇaviōgadahaṇatattāṇa ya ēyaṁ paraṁ iha-paralōyamuhāvahaṁ parama nivvuiṭāṇaṁ ti. ettha—

pecchanti na saṅgakayaṁ dukkhaṁ avamāṇaṇaṁ ca lōgāō

doggaïpaḍaṇaṁ ca tahā vaṇavāsī savvahā dhannā

ēvamaṇusāsiēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ aggisammēṇaṁ-bhagavaṁ! ēvamēyaṁ, na saṁdēhō tti. tō jaï bhayavaō mamōvari aṇukampā, uciō vā ahaṁ ēyassa vayavisēsassa, tā karēha mē ēyavayappayāṇēṇāṇuggahaṁ ti. isiṇā bhaṇiya-vaccha! vēraggamaggāṇugaō tumaṁ ti karēmi aṇuggahaṁ, kō annō ēyassa uciō tti. taō aïkantēsu kaïvayadiṇēsu saṁsiūṇa ya savittharaṁ niyayamāyāra,pasatthē tihi-karaṇa-muhutta-jōga laggē dinā sē tāvasadikkhā. mahāparibhavajaṇiyavēraggāisayabhāviēṇa yāṇēṇa tammi cēva dikkhādivasē sayalatāvasalōyapariyariyagu rusamakkhaṁ kayā mahāpaïnnā. jahā-jāvajjīvaṁ maē māsāō māsāō cēva bhottavvaṁ, pāraṇagadivasē ya paḍhamapaviṭṭhēṇaṁ paḍhamagēhāō cēva lābhē vā alābhē vā niyaniyadhvaṁ, na gēhantaramabhigantavvaṁ ti. ēvaṁ ca kayapaïnassa tassa, jahākayaṁ païnnamaṇupālintassa aïkkantā bahavē puvvalakkhā. tavōvaṇāsannavasantaüranivāsiṇō ya lōyassa guṇarāiṇō jāō taṁ paï aīva bhattibahumāṇō. ahō! ayaṁ mahāta vassī ihalōyanippivāsō, sarīrē vi daḍhamappaḍibaddhō, ēyassa saphalaṁ jīviyaṁ ti. bhaṇiyaṁ ca—

jaṇapakkhavāyabahumāṇiṇā vi jattō guṇēsu kāyayō

āvajanti guṇā khalu abuhaṁ pi jaṇaṁ amacchariyaṁ

iō ya puṇṇacandō rāyā kumāraguṇasēṇaṁ kayadārapariggahaṁ rajjē abhisiściūṇa saha kumuiṇīē dēvīē tabōvaṇavāsī jāō. sō ya kumāraguṇasēṇō aṇēyasāmantapaṇivaïyacalaṇajuyalō, nijjiyaniyamaṇḍalāhiyāṇēgamaṇḍalō, dasadisi visadr̥nimmalavissuyajasō, dhamma-ttha-kāmalakkhaṇativaggasaṁpāyaṇaraō mahārāyā saṁvuttō ti. annayā ya kālakamēṇēva jahāsuhaṁ sayalajaṇasalāhaṇijjaṁ saha vasaṁta sēṇāē mahādēvīē rajjasokkhaṁ aṇuhavantō āgaō vasantaüraṁ, paviṭṭhō ya mahāmaṅgalokkhārēṇaṁ, pūjiō ya paürēhiṁ, gaō samaṁ tēhi pāusalīlāvalambisōhiyaṁ vimāṇacchandayaṁ nāma pāsāyaṁ. jattha mēhaduddiṇacchāyāṇuyāriṇīō bahalakālāgarudhūmasaṁtaīō, sōyāma ṇīō viva vihāyanti rayaṇāvalīō, jaladhārāō viva dīsaṁti muttāvalīō, balāyāpanniyāō viva vihāyanti camarapantiyāō, indāuhacchāyāvahāriṇīō palambiyāō paṭṭasuyamālāō, gandhōyagāva sēyasurabhigandhā bhūmibhāgā, ruṇṭantamahuyarakulāulāvaïṇṇā pupphōvayārā. kiṁ bahuṇā jaṁpiēṇaṁ?

purisāṇa mōhaniddāmuttāṇa vi simiṇaya pitra kahēi

pubdhi kayāṇa viyaḍaṁ phalaṁ ca jō bhāgadhēyāṇaṁ

tattha ya jahāṇurūvaṁ paüra jaṇaṁ sammāṇēūṇa visajjiēmu tēsu, vivihaṇāḍaya-cchanda-naṭṭiyāiṇā maṇaharēṇa viṇōēṇa vigami ūṇa taṁ ahōratta,biiyadivasammi ya saṁpāiyasayalagōsakincō uciyavēlāē cēva niggaō vāhiyāli. parivāhiyā ya tēṇaṁ bahavē valhīya -turukka-vajarāiyā āsā. tajjaṇiyakhēyāvaṇanimittaṁ ca uvaviṭṭhō vāhiyālōtaḍaniviṭṭhē sahassambavaṇujāṇē. etthantarammi gahiya nāraṅgakaṭṭhiṇayā āgayā duvē tāvasakumārayā. diṭṭō ya ṇēhi rāyā, abhinandiō ya sasamayapasiddhāē āsīsāē. abbhuṭṭhāṇāsaṇapa yāṇāiṇā uvayārēṇa bahumanniyā ya rāiṇā. bhaṇiyaṁ ca ṇēhi-mahārāya! mugihīyanāmadhēēṇa amhē kulabaïṇā bhavaō caürāsamagurussa, sukayadhammādhammavavatthassa sarīrapaüttipariyāṇaṇanimitta pēsiyā. ēvaṁ sōūṇa saṁpayaṁ tuma pamāṇaṁ ti. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ — kahiṁ sō bhayavaṁ kulavaha tti. tēhiṁ bhaṇiyaṁ — iō nāidūrē supariōsanāmē tabōvaṇē tti. taō ya sō rāyā bhatti-kōugēhiṁ gaō taṁ tavōvaṇaṁ ti. diṭṭhā ya tēṇaṁ tattha bahavē tāvasā kulavaī ya. taō saṁjāyasaṁvēgēṇaṁ jahārihamabhivandiyā. uvaviṭṭhō kulavaïsamīvē, ṭhiō ya tēṇa saha dhammakahāvābārēṇa kaṁci kālaṁ. taō bhaṇiō ya ṇēṇa saviṇayaṁ paṇamiūṇa bhayavaṁ kulavaī. jahā karēhi mē pasāyaṁ sayalaparivārapariṁgaō mama gēhē āhāragahaṇēṇaṁ. kulavaïṇā bhaṇiyaṁ — vaccha! ēvaṁ. kiṁ tu ēgō aggisammō nāma mahātāvasō, sō ya na païdiyaha bhunaï, māsāō māsāō, tattha vi ya pāraṇagadivasē paḍhamapaviṭṭhō paḍhamagēhāō cēva lābhē vā alābhē vā niyattaï, na gēhantaramuvagacchaï. tātaṁ mahātavassi mottūṇa paḍivanā tē patthaṇā. rāiṇā bhaṇiya-bhagavaṁ! aṇugihīō mhi. aha kahiṁ puṇa sō mahātāvasō? pecchāmi ṇaṁ tāva, karēmi tassa darisaṇēṇa appāṇaṁ vigayapāvaṁ. kulabaïṇā bhaṇiyaṁ — vaccha! ēyāē sahayāravīhiyāē hēhā jhāṇavaragaō ciṭṭhaï. taō sō rāyā sasaṁbhantō gaō sahayāravīhiyaṁ. diṭṭhō ya tēṇa paümāsaṇōvaviṭhṭhō, thiradhariyanayaṇajuyalō, pasantavicittacittavāvārō, kiṁpi tahāvihaṁ jhāṇaṁ jhāyantō aggisammatāvasō tti. taō rāiṇā harisavasapaïyadr̥ntapulaēṇa paṇa miō. tēṇa vi ya āsīsāē sabahu māṇamēvāhiṇandiō, sāgayaṁ tē bhaṇiūṇa ubabisāhi tti saṁlattō. uvavisi ūga suhāsaṇatthēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ rāiṇā-bhayavaṁ! ki tē imassa mahādukkarassa tavacaraṇavasāyassa kāraṇaṁ? aggisammatāvasēṇa bhaṇiya-bhō mahāsatta! dāriddadukkhaṁ, paraparihayō, virūvayā, tahā mahārāyaputtō ya guṇasēṇō nāma kallāṇamittō tti. taō saṁgāyaniyanāmāsaṁkēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ rāiṇā-bhayavaṁ! ciṭṭhaü tāva dāridadukkhāiyaṁ vavasāyakāraṇaṁ, aha kahaṁ puṇa mahārāyaputtō guṇasēṇō nāma kallāṇamittō ti. aggisammatāvasēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — mahāsatta! ēvaṁ kallāṇa mittō. suṇa—

jē honti uttamanarā dhamma sayamēva tē parajanti

majjhimapayaī saṁcōiyā u na kayāi vi jahannā

cōēi ya jō dhammē jīvaṁ vivihēṇa kēṇaï naēṇa

saṁsāracārayagaya sō naṇu kallāṇamittō ti

taō rāiṇā kumāravuttantaṁ sumariūṇa bhaṇiyaṁ lajjāvaṇayavaya ṇēṇa-bhayavaṁ! kahaṁ puṇa tumaṁ tēṇa tēlōkabandhubhūē dhammē cōiō? aggisammatāvasēṇa bhaṇiya-bhō mahāsatta! nānāvihāō, cōyaṇāō, tā kahaṁci nimittamettēṇaṁ cēva cōiō mhi. taō rāiṇā cintiyaṁ. ahō! sē mahāṇubhāvayā, paribhavō vi yāṇēṇōvayāracōyaṇa tti gahiō. paraparivāyaṁ ca pariharantō suddhasahāvattaṇō na taṁ pi mannēi! ahō! dāruṇaṁ akajjaṁ maē pāvasammēṇāśuciṭṭhiyaṁ. tā kahēmi sē akajjāyaraṇa kalaṅgadūliyaṁ apāṇaṁ. ēvaṁ cintiūṇa jaṁpiyamaṇēṇa-bhayavaṁ! ahaṁ sō mahāpātra kammayārī tuha hiyayasaṁtāvayārī aguṇa sēṇō tti. aggisammatāvasēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — bhō mahārāya! sāgayaṁ tē. kaha tuma aguṇasēgō? jēṇa taē para paṇḍajīviyamettavihavō ahaṁ īisiṁ tabavibhūī pāviśrī tti. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ — ahō! mahāṇubhāvayā. kiṁ vā tavassijaṇō piyaṁ vajjiya annaṁ bhaṇiuṁ jāṇaï? nē ya miyaṅkabimbāō aṅgārakhuṭṭīō paḍanti. tā alaṁ ēiṇā. bhaya! kayā tē pāraṇagaṁ bhavissaï? aggisammēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — mahārāya! paścahi diṇēhiṁ. rāiṇā bhaṇiya-bhayavaṁ! jaï nāīva uvarōdō, tā kāyayō mama gēhē pāraṇaēṇaṁ pasāō. vināō ya maē kulavaïṇō sayāsāō tujjha païnnāvisēsō, aō aṇā gayaṁ patthēmi tti. aggisammēṇa bhaṇiya-mahārāya! āgacchaü tāva sō diyahō, kō jāṇaï antarē kiṁpi bhavissaï. avi ya—

payaṁ karēmi ēhi ēyaṁ kāūṇa puṇa imaṁ kallaṁ

kāhimi kō ṇu mannaï, suviṇayatullammi jiyalōē?

annaṁ ca mahārāya!

dhī jiyalōyasahāyō jahiyaṁ nēhāṇurāyakaliyā vi

jē pubaṇhē diṭṭhā, tē avaraṇhē na dīsanti

tā mahārāya! āgacchaü tāva sō diyahō tti. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ — bhayavaṁ! vigghaṁ mottūṇa saṁgacchaha. aggisammatāvasēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ jaï ēvaṁ tē nibbandhō, tā ēvaṁ paḍivannā tē patthaṇā. taō rāyā paṇamiūṇa harisavasapulaïyaṅgō kaṁci vēlaṁ gamēūṇa paviṭṭhō nayaraṁ. kayā kulavaïṇō saparivārassa bhattivibhavāṇurūvā pūyā. aïkantēsu ya pañcasu diṇēsu pāraṇagadivasē paḍhamaṁ cēva paviṭṭhō aggisammatāvasō pāraṇa ganimittaṁ rāyagēhaṁ ti. tammi ya diyahē kahaṁci rāiṇō guṇasēṇassa atīva sīmavēyaṇā samuppannā. taō āulīhūyaṁ savvaṁ cēva rāyaülaṁ, paviṭṭhā ya tattha vējasatthavisārayā vejjā, uggāhenti nāṇāvihāō cigicchāsaṁhiyāō, pōsijanti bahuvihāī ōsahāī, dijjanti sirakhēyāvahāriṇō vicittarayaṇalēvā. kiṁkāyanyamūḍhā uvahasiyasukkavihassaïbuddhivihavā vi mantiṇō. patthuyaṁ purōhiēhiṁ mantagambhi ṇāhuippayāṇasāraṁ santikammaṁ. tahā milāṇasurahimalladāmasōhaṁ, suvaṇṇagaddēviyaliyaṅgarāyaṁ, bāhajaladhōyakavōlapattalēhaṁ, karayalapaṇāmi yapavvāyavayaṇapaṅkayaṁ, ubviggamantēuraṁ. tahā virattakanduyakīlaṁ, paricattacittayammavāvāraṁ, virayagīyanaccaṇārambhaṁ, avahatthiyabhūsaṇakalāvaṁ, dummaṇavimaṇaṁ kannayantēuraṁ. vettajaṭṭhinimiyavicchāyamuhasōhā ya paḍihārā, rannō vēyaṇāisayasūyagō dummaṇā maḍa hakañcuiyā, parica taniyayavāvārā vicittā sūyagārappamuddā niōgakāriṇō tti. taō sō aggisammatāvasō ēvaṁvihē rāyakulē kaṁci vēlaṁ gamēūṇa vaya ṇamettēṇāvi kēṇa vi akayapaḍivattī niggaō rāyagēhāō tti. niggantūṇa gaō tavōvaṇaṁ, diṭṭhō ya tāvasē hiṁ, bhaṇiō ya tēhi-bhayavaṁ! akayapāraṇagō viva parimilāṇadēhō lakkhijasi, tā kiṁ na kayaṁ pāraṇayaṁ? na paviṭhṭhō iyāṇi tattha rannō guṇasēṇassa gēhaṁ? ti. aggisammatāvasēṇa bhaṇiya-paviṭṭhō ahaṁ narindagēhaṁ, kiṁtu sō nūrṇa apaḍusarīrō rāyā, jaō ubiggapariyaṇaṁ savvaṁ cēva taṁ maē gēhama balōiyaṁ, tō ahaṁ taṁ tahāvihaṁ daṭṭhumasahaṁtō lahuṁ cēva niggaō tti. tābasēhi bhaṇiyaṁ — kō saṁdēhō, daḍhamapaḍusarīrō rāyā, annahā kaha tārisīē tavassijaṇabhattīē bhayavaō pāraṇagaṁ muṇēūṇa sayaṁ cēva dattāvahāṇō na hōi? annaṁ ca-aīva bhagavaō uvari bhattibahumāṇō tassa naravaïssa, jēṇa kulavaïsamakkhaṁ bahuyaṁ sambhūyaguṇakittaṇaṁ tēṇa kayaṁ āsi. aggisammatāvasēṇa bhaṇiya-āroggaṁ sē havaü guruya ṇapūyagassa, kiṁ mama āhārēṇaṁ ti. paḍiyannō māsōvavāsavayaṁ. iō ya rāiṇā guṇasēṇēṇaṁ uvasantasīsavēyaṇēṇaṁ pucchiō pariyagō. ajja tassa mahātavassissa pāraṇagadiyahō, tō sō āgaō, pūiō vā kēṇaï na vatti? tēhiṁ saṁlattaṁ-mahārāya! āgaō āsi, kiṁtu tuha sīsavēyaṇājaṇiahiyajasaṁtāvaparicattaniyayakajjabāvārē pariyaṇē na kēṇaï saṁpūiō pucchiō vā. amuṇiyavuttantō ya vicittaṁ tē pariyaṇamavalōijaṇa kaṁci kālaṁ gamēūṇa ubdhiggō viya niggaō rāyagēhāō tti. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ — ahō! mē ahannayā, cukkō vi mahālābhassa, saṁpattō ya tavassinaṇadēhapīḍākaraṇēṇa mahantaṁ aṇatthaṁ ti. ēvaṁ vilaviūṇaṁ viiyadiyahē pahāyasamara cēva gaō tabō vaṇaṁ. diṭṭhā ya tēṇa kulavaïppamuhā bahavē tāvasā, lajā-viṇōṇayaüttimaṅgēṇa paṇamiyā ya ṇēṇaṁ vihiṇā. ahiṇandiō ya āsī sāē kulavaïppamuhēhiṁ savvatāvasē hiṁ. ubavisasu mahārāya! sāgayaṁ tē bhaṇiō ya kulavaïṇā. taō rāyā avaṇayaüttimaṅgō, savisēsa lajjāmantharō, vimukkadīhanīsāsaṁ uvaviṭhṭhō kulavaïssa puraō. taṁ ca tahā vicittaṁ rāyāṇaṁ daṭṭaṇaṁ bhaṇiyamaṇēṇaṁ-vaccha! uciggō viya lakkhīyasi, tā kahēhi mē uvvēyakāraṇa, jaï akahaṇīyaṁ na hōi. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ — atthi bhagavaō vi nāma akahaṇīyaṁ. annaṁ ca-akahaṇī yavatthuvisaübigagassa na juttaṁ tavōvaṇāgamaṇaṁ. kulabaïṇā bhaṇiyaṁ — sāhu vaccha! sāhu, uciō tē vivēgō, tā kiṁ-uvvē. yakāraṇaṁ ti? rāiṇā bhaṇiya-bhagavaō āṇa tti kariya kahīyaï; annahā kahaṁ īisaṁ nisaṁsacariyaṁ kahiuṁ pāriyaï? kulavaïṇā bhaṇiyaṁ vaccha! savvassa jaṇaṇībhūō khu hōi tavassijaṇō. taō kā taṁ paï lajja tti. tā kahēu bhavaṁ, jēṇa muṇiyavuttantō bhaviya kēṇaï uvāēṇa'vaṇēmi taṁ uvvēyaṁ ti. rāiṇā bhaṇiya-bhaya! jaï ēvaṁ, tā suṇasu. ēsa aggisammatāvasō paḍhamaṁ cēva mama mandapu. ṇṇassa, asamikkhiyakāriṇō, asarisajaṇasarisāyaraṇanirayassa saṁbandhiṇā nivvēēṇa tāvasō saṁvuttō. ēyassa pavannuttamavayassa vi taṁ maē asarisajaṇāyaraṇaṁ na paricattaṁ ti daḍhaviggō mhi. kulabaïṇā bhaṇiyaṁ — vaccha! jaï pavaṁ, tā alaṁ saṁtappiēṇaṁ, kiṁ kāraṇaṁ. jaï tuha saṁbandhiṇā kāraṇēṇa tāvasō saṁvuttō, tā tuma cēva imassa dhammapavattagō kallāṇamittō tiḥ kimubbiggō si? na yāvi ēhi tuha paralōyabhīruṇō, ahigayadhammasatthassa kiṁpi asajaṇāyaraṇaṁ saṁbhāvēmi. kiṁ vā sē kayamiyāṇi nivēēhi mē. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ -bhayavaṁ! iyāṇiṁ tāva ēyaṁ uvaṇimantiūṇa māsapāraṇayapaviṭṭhassa sīsavēyaṇābhibhūēṇa pamāyaō aṇiuttapariyaṇēṇaṁ āhārantarāyakaraṇēṇaṁ kayaṁ sē dhammantarāyaṁ ti. kulavaïṇā bhaṇiyaṁ — vaccha! jaṁ kiṁci ēyaṁ, na tuma ettha avarajjhasi. na tibbavēyaṇābhibhūyā purisā kajja makajaṁ vā viyāṇanti. na ya tassa āhārantarāyakaraṇēṇaṁ dhammantarāyaṁ havaï, avi ya tavasaṁpayā. tā alamuvvēgēṇaṁ ti. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ bhayavaṁ! jāva tēṇa mahāṇubhāvē mama gēhē āhāragahaṇaṁ na kayaṁ, tāva kahamumvēvō avēi? kulabaïṇā bhaṇiyaṁ — vaccha! iyāṇiṁ sē avi gghēṇa jaṁ pāraṇagaṁ bhavissaï, tahiṁ tē gēhē āhāragahaṇaṁ karissaï tti. taō kulavaīṇā sadāviō aggisammatāvasō. sabahumāṇaṁ hatthē gihiūṇa bhaṇiō ya ṇēṇa — vaccha! jaṁ tumaṁ akayapāraṇagō niggaō narindagēhāō, ēēṇaṁ daḍhaṁ saṁtappaï rāyā. kallaṁ ca ēyassa aīva sīsavēyaṇā āsi, aō vēyaṇāparavvasēṇa na tuma paḍiyaghiō tti na ēsa avarajjhaï. bhaṇiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa jāva mama gēhē aggisammatāvasēṇa āhāragahaṇaṁ na kayaṁ, na tāva mē uvvēvō avēi aō iṇḍiṁ saṁpattapāraṇagakālēṇa bhavayā avigghēṇa mama vayaṇāō narindabahumāṇaō ya ēyassa gēhē pāraṇagaṁ kariyavvaṁ ti. aggisammatāvasēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — bhaya! jaṁ tubbhē āṇavēha. akāraṇē saṁtappaï rāyā, jō na kiṁci mē paralōyaviruddhamaṇuciṭṭhiyamaṇēṇaṁ! taō rāyā ahō! sē mahāṇubhāvaya ti kaliūṇa paṇamiūṇa tavassijaṇaṁ ca kaṁci vēlaṁ pajjuvāsiya paviṭṭhō nayaraṁ.

puṇō ya kālakamēṇa rāiṇō visayamuhamaṇuhavantassa, aggisammassa ya dukaraṁ tavacaraṇavihiṁ karentassa samaïkkantō māsō tti. etthantarammi ya saṁpattē pāraṇagadivasē nivēiyaṁ sē ranō vikkhēvāgaēhi niyayapurisēhiṁ. jahā-mahārāya! aïvisamaparaka magavviyaṁ, visamadōṇīmuhappaviṭṭhaṁ, akayaparirakkhaṇōvāyaṁ appamattēṇa māṇahaṅganaravaḍaṇā, iharahā visayaviṇāsamavalōiūṇa, vīracariya mavalambiya, vīsatthasuttēsu narindapāikkasu, jāē aṭṭarattasamaē, atthamiē rayaṇivahūpiyayamē tēlokkamaṅgalapaīvē miyakē saya labalasahiēṇamavakkhandaṁ dāūṇa aïpamattaṁ tē viṇijjiya sennaṁ. saṁpaï dēvō pamaraṇaṁ ti. taō rāiṇā ēyaṁ sudūsahaṁ vayaṇamāyaṇṇi ūṇa kōvāṇalajaliyarattalōyaṇēṇaṁ, visamaphuriyāharēṇa, nidayakarābhihayadharaṇivaṭṭhēṇaṁ amarisabasaparikkhalantavayaṇēṇaṁ samāṇattō pari yaṇō. jahā-dēha turiyaṁ payāṇayapaḍahaṁ, sajjēha dujjayaṁ karibalaṁ, pallāṇēha dappudhuraṁ āsasāhaṇaṁ, saṁjattēha dhaya-māloksōhiyaṁ sanda ganivahaṁ, payaṭṭāvēha nāṇāpaharaṇasāliṇaṁ pāika sēn ti. tō naravaïsamāēsāṇantaramēvāyaṇṇiya payāṇayapaḍahasaī, karivaravirāyantamēha jālaṁ, ūsiyadhaya-camara-chattasaṁghāyabalāyapariyayaṁ, nisiyakaravāla-kontasōyāmaṇisaṇāha, saṅkha-kāhalātūranigghōsagajiyaravapūriya disaṁ, ayāladudiṇaṁ piva samantaō viyambhiyaṁ narindasāhaṇaṁ ti. etthantarammi ya rahabarārūḍhē narindaguṇasēṇē, ṭhāviē puraō salila puṇṇē kaṇayakalasē, pahaē jayasirisamupphālaē maṅgalatūrē, paḍhantēsu, vivihamaṅgalāī bendivandrēsu, aggisammatāvasō pāraṇaganimittaṁ paviṭṭhō narindagēhaṁ ti. taō tammi mahājaṇasamudaē āulīhūē narindaniggamaṇanimittaṁ pahāṇapariyaṇē na kēṇaï samuvalakkhiō ti. taō kaṁci vēlaṁ gamēūṇa dariyakari-turayasaṁghāyacamaḍhaṇabhīō niggaō naravaïgēhāō. etthantarammi ya gahiyasaṅkucchāēhi, muṇiyajō isasatthaparamatthēhi bhaṇiyaṁ jōisiēhi-dēva! pasatthaṁ muhuttaṁ, niggacchasu tti. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ — aja tassa aggisammatāvasassa pāraṇaga divasō, paḍivannaṁ ca tēṇa kulavaïvayaṇāō mama gēhē āhāragahaṇaṁ kāyavvaṁ ti. tā āgacchaü tāva sō mahāṇubhāvō. taō taṁ kayabhōyaṇavihāṇaṁ paṇamiūṇa gamissāmō. tō āsannavattiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ kulaputtaēṇa-dēva! sō khu mahāṇubhāvō saṁparya cēva pavisiūṇa dariyakari-turayasaṁghāyacamaḍhaṇabhīō niggaō rāyagēhāō. ajja vi ya na nayarāō niggacchaï ti takkēmi. taō ēyamāyaṇṇiūṇa sasaṁbhantō rāyā payaṭṭō tassa maïggē, diṭṭō ya gēṇa nayarāō niggacchantō aggisammatāvasō. taō ōyariūṇa rahabarāō, bhattinibbharaṁ nivaḍiūṇa calaṇēsu vinnattō sabahumāṇaṁ. bhayavaṁ! karēha pasāyaṁ, viṇiyattamu tti. ahamabhippēē vi gamaṇē tuha cēvāgamagamaṇuṣālentō ettiyaṁ vēlaṁ ṭhiō mhi, jāva tumaṁ pavisiūṇa mama gēhaṁ alakkhiō cēva mē pahāṇapariyaṇēṇa niggaō si, tā niyattamu tti. aggisammatāvasēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — mahārāya! viiyavuttantō cēva mē tumaṁ païnnāvisēsassa; tā alaṁ tē imiṇā vava sāraṇaṁ. sañcapaïnnā khu tavassigō habanti, nibisēsā ya lābhālābhēsu. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ — bhayava! lajiō mhi imiṇā pamāyacari ēṇaṁ, tuha tibbatavajaṇiyasarī rapīḍāō vi mē ahiyā saśērapīḍā, daḍhaṁ dahaï maṁ saṁtāvāṇalō, paṇastaï viya mē hiyayaṁ, akkhippaï ya mē vāṇī, mahāpāvakammakāriṇaṁ ca mannēmi appāṇaṁ; tā sayaladuhiyasattabandhubhūbhō, akāraṇavacchalō bhayavaṁ tumaṁ cēva mē imassa dukkhassa ubasamōvāyaṁ cintēhi. aggisammatāva sēṇa cintiyaṁ. ahō! sē mahārāyassa mahāṇubhāvayā. akayapāraṇagēṇa maē ettiyaṁ khijjaï tti. ahō! sē guruyaṇasustūsāṇurāō. tā na jāva maē ēyassa gēhē pāraṇayaṁ kayaṁ, na tāva ēsa satthō hōi ti cinti ūṇa bhaṇiyaṁ ca tēṇa-mahārāya! animittaṁ tē dukkhaṁ. tahāvi ēyassa imō ubasamōvāō. avigvēṇa saṁpattē pāraṇagadivasē puṇō vi cēva gēhē āhāragahaṇaṁ ka rassāmi tti paḍivannaṁ maē, tā mā saṁtappasu ti. taō dharaṇinihiyajāṇu-karayalēṇaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ rāiṇā bhayavaṁ! suṭhṭha muṇiō imassa dukkhassa uvasamōvāō. ahavā vimalanāṇanayaṇō cēva tavassijaṇō hōi, kiṁ vā na yāṇaï ti? tā aṇugihīō mhi. sarisaṁ imaṁ tuha akāraṇava layāē. tā gaccha tuma tavōvaṇaṁ. ahaṁ puṇa na sakkuṇōmi pañcaggapamāyakalaṅkadūsiō bhagavantaṁ kulabaïmaklōiḍaṁ ti. ēvaṁ bhaṇiya paṇa miūṇa ya aggisammatāvasaṁ niyattō rāyā. na maē iyāṇiṁ gantavvaṁ ti kaliūṇa visajjiō ya tēṇaṁ māṇabhaṅgassa upari vikkhēvō. aggisammō viya gantūṇa tavōvaṇaṁ,nivēiūṇa kulavaṇō jahāvittaṁ vuttataṁ, vaccha! sāhu kayaṁ ti ahiṇandiō ya kulabaïṇā pavannō vayavi sēsaṁ ti. aṇudiyahaṁ ca pavaḍḍamāṇasaṁvēgēṇa rāiṇā sēvijjantassa tassa samaïcchiō māsō, pattō ya ranō maṇōrahasaēhiṁ pāraṇayadiyahō. tammi ya pāraṇayadiyahē rāiṇō guṇasēṇassa dēvī vasanta sēṇā dārayaṁ pasūya tti. nivēiyaṁ ca rāiṇō harisavasēṇa paphullavayaṇapaṅkayāē saparitōsaṁ paḍihārīē-mahārāya! dēvī vasantasēṇā tumhāṇaṁ an dayanimittaṁ payāṇaṁ bhāgadhēēhiṁ muhaṁsuhēṇaṁ dāraya pasya tti. taō rāiṇā puttanammabhudayasaṁjāyarōmaścaṇaṁ dāūṇa paḍiḍārīē kaḍaya-kē ūra-kaṇṇālaṅkārā iyaṁ aṅgābharaṇaṁ, dinā samāṇattī. vasuṁdharē! samāisamu ṇaṁ mama vayaṇāō jahāsannihiyē paḍihārē. jahā-mōyāvēha kālaghaṇṭāpaōēṇa mama rajjē sabyabandhaṇāṇi, davāvēha ghōsaṇāpubdhayaṁ aṇavekkhiyāṇurūva mahādāṇaṁ, visajjāvēha jiyasattuppamuhāṇaṁ naravaīṇaṁ mama puttajamma paütti, nivēēha dēvīputtajammabhudayaṁ paürāṇaṁ, kārāvēha ayālacchaṇabhūyaṁ nayaramahasavaṁ ti. samāiṭṭā ya tīē jahāiṭṭa paḍihārā. aṇuciṭṭhiyaṁ ca rāyasāsaṇaṁ paḍihārēhiṁ. avi ya—

kārāviyaṁ ca tēhiṁ tūraravuppuṇṇa isadisābhōyaṁ

unnāmiēkakarayalanacantavilāsiṇisamūha

antēuriyāhīranta puṇṇavattuttarīyarapottaṁ

savisēsapasāhiyasamilantarāmāyaṇāiṇṇaṁ

piṭṭhāgayamuhipahārabhīrurāmāvimukkasikkāraṁ

mayabasavilāsiṇījaṇanacāvijjantakacuiyaṁ

sucantakarapphāliyatālāyaramurayamahuranigdhōsaṁ

dāṇaparituṭṭhabahubandivandraügghuṭṭajayasaī

naccantamaḍahavāmaṇa cēḍīhāsijjamāṇanaranāhaṁ

baddhāvāṇayanivahaṁ baddhāvaṇayaṁ maṇabhirāmaṁ

pabattō ya vasantaürē nayarē mahāmahūsavō. ēvaṁvihē ya dēvīputtajammabhudayāṇandiē mahāpamattē saha rāiṇā rāyapariyaṇē aggisa mmatāvasō pāraṇaganimittaṁ rāyaülaṁ pavisiūṇa vayaṇamettēṇāvi kēṇaï akayapaḍivattī asuhakammōdaēṇaṁ aṭṭajjhāṇadūsiyamaṇō lahuṁ cēva niggaō. cintiyaṁ ca ṇēṇaṁ-ahō! sē rāiṇō ābālabhāvaō cēva asarisō mamōvari vērāṇubandhō tti. pecchaha sē aïṇigūḍhāyā ramācariyaṁ, jēṇa taṁ tahā mama samakkhaṁ maṇāṇukūlaṁ jaṁpiya karaṇēṇa vivarīyamāyaraï ti cintayantō sō niggaō nayarāō. etthantara mmi ya annāṇadōsēṇaṁ abhāviyaparamatthamaggattaṇa ya gahiō kasāēhiṁ, avagayā sē paralōyavāsaṇā, paṇaṭṭhā dhammasaddhā, samāgayā sayaladukkhataruvīyabhūyā amettī, jāyā ya dēhapīḍākarī atīva bubhukkhā. ākarisiō bubhukkhāē. taō—

paḍhamaparīsahavaïēṇa tēṇa annāṇakōhavasaraṇaṁ

ghōraṁ niyāṇamēyaṁ paḍivannaṁ mūḍhahiyaēṇaṁ

jaï hojja imassa phalaṁ maē suciṇṇassa vayavisēsassa

tā ēyarasa vahāē païjammaṁ hōja mē jammō

na kuṇaï paṇaīṇa piyaṁ jō purisō vippiyaṁ ca sattūṇaṁ

kiṁ tassa jaṇaṇijovvaṇaviuḍaṇamettēṇa jammēṇaṁ?

sattū ya ēsa rāyā mama sisubhāvāu cēva pāvō tti

avarāhamantarēṇa vi, karēmi tō vippiyamimassa

iya kāūṇa niyāṇaṁ appaḍikantēṇa tassa ṭhāṇassa

aha bhāviyaṁ subahusō kōhāṇalajaliyacittēṇa

etthantarammi pattō ēsō tavōvaṇaṁ. aṇēyaviyappaṇiyakucintāsaṁdhukkiyapavaḍḍamāṇakōhāṇalō ya kulavaī sēsatāvasē ya parihariūṇa alakkhiō cēva gaō sahayāravīhiyaṁ, uvaviṭhṭhō ya vimalasilāviṇimmiē cāurantapīḍhē tti. aṇusayava sēṇa puṇō vi cintiumā raddhō. ahō! sē rāiṇō mamōvari paḍiṇīyabhāvō. kahaṁ savvatāvasamajjhē ahaṁ sē ōhasaṇijjō tti? jēṇa mē païnāvisēsaṁ nāūṇa niyaḍibahulō tahā tahōvaṇimantiya asaṁpāḍaṇēṇa pāraṇayassa kila maṁ khalīkarēi ti. taṁ mūḍhō khu sō rāyā ki mē ēyāvatthagayassa khalīkarīyaï. tahā aṇāhāṇaṁ, dubbalāṇaṁ, paraparihayāṇaṁ ca sattāṇaṁ kayantē ṇēva viṇivāiyāṇaṁ jā khaliyāraṇā, na sā māṇiṇō māṇa māpūrēi ti, visēsaō samasattu-mittāṇaṁ paralōyavāvāranirayāṇaṁ tēvassīṇaṁ ti. ahavā aparicattāhāramettasaṅgassa mē ēdahamettā kaya tyaṇa tti. tā alaṁ mē jāva jīvaṁ cēva parihavānimittēṇaṁ āhārēṇaṁ ti gahiyaṁ jāvajjīviyaṁ mahōvavāsavayaṁ. etthantarammi ya paricattaniya yavādārō asuhajjhāṇadūsiyamaṇō, tavaparikkhīṇadēhō, diṭṭhō tattha tābasēhi. bhaṇiyaṁ ca tēhiṁ-bhayavaṁ! aïparikkhīṇadēhō, asaṁpāviya kusumavilēvaṇokkhārō lakkhijasi, tā ki iyāṇi pi tē na saṁjāyaṁ pāraṇayaṁ ti? aggisammatāvasēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — na saṁjāyaṁ ti. tāvasēhiṁ bhaṇiyaṁ — kahaṁ na saṁjāya? kiṁ na paviṭhṭhō tassa rāiṇō guṇasēṇassa gēhaṁ? aggisammatāvasēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — paviṭṭhō. tāvasēhi bhaṇiyaṁ — tā kahaṁ tē na saṁjāyaṁ ti? tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — bālabhāvāō cēva mē sō rāyā aṇavaraddhavēriō khaliyāriō ahaṁ tēṇa pubbiṁ. maē puṇa na jāṇiō, avagaō sē iyāṇi vērāṇuvandhō. viṇīō diva lakkhi jjaï, jāva micchāviṇīyassa na sē vērāṇubandhō avēi jēṇōvahāsabuddhīē mēṁ uvaṇimantiūṇaṁ aṇajjavilasiēṇaṁ cēva tēhiṁ tēhiṁ māyāpayārēhiṁ cēva kila mēṁ parihavaï tti. ajaṁ ca tēṇa viyāṇi ūṇa mama pāraṇagadivasaṁ sahasā cēva kārāviōpamōō. tō ahaṁ pavisiūṇaṁ rāyagēhaṁ abahumāṇiō cēva muṇiyanarindaparivārābhippāō lahuṁ cēva niggaotti. taō tāvasēhiṁ bhaṇiyaṁ — bhayava! na ēvaṁ tavassijaṇavacchalē narindaguṇasēṇē saṁbhāviyaï, ahavā vicittasandhiṇō hi purisā havanti, kiṁ vā na saṁbhāviyaï? natthi avisaō kasāyāṇaṁti bhaṇiūṇa nivēiyaṁ tēhiṁ accumbiggēhiṁ kulavaïṇō. jahā-bhayavaṁ! na tassa aggisammatāvasassa imiṇā vuttantēṇa saṁpayaṁ pi pāraṇayaṁ saṁvuttaṁ ti. taō sasaṁbhantō turiyamāgaō aggisammasamīvaṁ kulabaī. saṁpūiō ya tēṇa aggisammēṇa jahāṇurūvēṇāvayārēṇaṁ. tō tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — baccha! kahamiyāṇi pi tē na saṁjāyaṁ pāraṇayaṁ ti? ahō! sē asarisasamāyaraṇaṁ rāiṇō guṇasēṇassa. aggisammatāvasēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — bhayavaṁ! pamāiṇō cēva rāyāṇō havanti, kō vā tassa dōsō? mama cēvāparicattāhāramettasaṅgassa ēsa dōsō, jēṇa tassa vi gēhaṁ pavisāmi tti. paricattō ya maē saṁpayaṁ jāvajīvāē cēva sayala parihavavīyabhūō ēdahamettō vi saṅgō. aō vinavēmi bhayavantaṁ ēyammi atthē; nāhamanahā āṇavēyayō tti. kulavaïṇā bhaṇiyaṁ vaccha! jaï paricattō āhārō, gaō iyāṇi kālō āṇāē. saccapaïnnā khu tavassiṇō havanti. kiṁ tu tumaē narindassa uvari kōvō na kāyayō. jaō —

"savvaṁ puvvakayāṇaṁ kammāṇaṁ pāvara phalavivāgaṁ

avarāhēsu guṇēsu ya nimittamittaṁ parō hōi

ēvamaṇusāsiūṇaṁ paḍiyāragē tāvasē nirūviya gaō kulabaī. iō ya rāiṇā guṇasēṇēṇaṁ tahā ayālacchaṇasokkhamaṇuhavantē pariyaṇē aïkkantāē pāraṇagavēlāē sumariyaṁ, jahā pāraṇayadivasō khu ajja tassa mahātavassirasa. ahō! mē ahamnayā, na saṁpanna cēva mahātavassissa pāraṇayaṁ ti tabakēmi. pucchiō ya ṇēṇa jahāsannihiō pariyaṇō. kiṁ sō mahāṇubhāvō tāvasō ajja ihā gaō na va tti? taō tēṇa niuṇaṁ gavēsiūṇaṁ nivēiyaṁ-dēva! āgaō āsi, kiṁ tu dēvīputtajammabhuyayāhiṇandiē aïpamattē pariyaṇē na kēṇaï uvacariō tti taō lahuṁ cēva niggaō. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ — ahō! mē pāvapariṇaī. tassa mahātavassissa dhammantarā yakaraṇēṇaṁ dēvīputtajammabhuyayaṁ pi āvayaṁ cēva samatthēmi. sabahā na mandapuṇṇāṇaṁ gēhēsu vasuhārā paḍanti. na ya pamāyadōsasiō ahaṁ udantanimittaṁ pi sē pārēmi muhamavalōiṅa. tā gaccha, bhō sōmadēvapurōhiya! mamāvināyapariyaṇabhāvō cēva gavēsiūṇa tassa mahātava ssissa vuttantaṁ kiṁ tēṇa vavasiyaṁ? ti lahuṁ nivēēhi āsaṅkaï viya mē hiyayaṁ. ēvaṁ ca samāṇattō sōmadēvapurōhiō gaō tavōvaṇaṁ. diṭṭhō tēṇa bahutavassijaṇaparivāriō, giriṇaītaḍāsannaniviṭṭhamaṇḍavagaō,dī harakusaraïyasattharōvaviṭṭhō, amarisarasāḍhattarāyakahāvāvaḍō aggisammatāvasō tti. paṇamiō viṇaōṇayaüttimaṅgēṇaṁ sōmadēvēṇaṁ. tēṇaṁ ciya āsīsāpuvvayaṁ sāgaya ti bhaṇiūṇa uvavisasu tti āiṭṭhō. uvaviṭhṭhō sōmadēvapurōhiō. bhaṇiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa-bhayaba! aïparikkhīṇadēhō lavikhajjasi, tā kimayaṁ ti? aggisamma tāvasēṇa bhaṇiya-nirīhāṇaṁ, annaō samāsāiyavittīṇaṁ aṅgaṁ cēva kisaṁ tavassīṇaṁ ti. sōmadēvēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — ēvaṁ ēya, nirīhā cēva tava ssiṇō havanti; kiṁtu dhaṇa-dhana-hiraṇṇa-suvaṇṇa-maṇi-mottiya-ppavāla-duppaya-caüppaēmu, na uṇa dhamma-kāōvayāragē āhāramettē vi. na ya īisā ettha lōyā, jē tumaē vi sarisāṇaṁ muttimaggapavanāṇaṁ, avisēsasattu-mittāṇaṁ, samataṇa-maṇi-mutta-kaścaṇāṇaṁ, saṁsārajalahipōyāṇaṁ āhāramettaṁ pi na denti tti. aggisammatāvasēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — saccamēyaṁ, na ēyārisā ettha lōyā mottūṇa narindaguṇa sēṇaṁ ti. sōmadēvēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — bhayavaṁ! kiṁ kayaṁ narindaguṇasēṇēṇa? dhammaparō khu sō rāyā suṇīyaï tti. aggisammatāvasēṇa bha ṇiyaṁ-kō annō dhammaparō, jō viṇijjiyaniyamaṇḍalō vi tavassijaṇaṁ pasajjhaṁ vāvāēi ti. sōmadēvēṇa cintiya-parikuviō khu ēsō tāvasō. jahā ya dīharakusaraïyasattharōvaviṭṭhō lakkhijjaï, tahā narindanivvēēṇaṁ cēvāṇēṇa paḍivannamaṇasaṇaṁ bhavē. pucchijjantō ya ēsō asōyavvaṁ sāmiparivāyaṁ geṇhaï. tā annaō cēva uvalahiya vuttantaṁ sāmiṇō nivēēmi tti. paṇamiūṇa taṁ niggaō sōmadēvō. pucchiō ya ṇēṇaṁ kusakusumavāvaḍaggahatthō, abhisēyakāmō, girinaī samōyarantō tāvasō. bhayavaṁ! kiṁ paḍivannaṁ aggisammatāvasēṇa? tēṇa vi ya bāhajalabhariyamantharanayaṇēṇaṁ savittharamāikkhiyaṁ tayaṇuṭāṇaṁ. gaō sōmadēvō, nivēiyaṁ ca ṇēṇaṁ jahōvaladdhaṁ rāiṇō. taō rāyā ahiyayarajāyanivvēō, cintābhāranissahaṁ aṅgaṁ dharamāṇō, sayalantēura-pahāṇapariyaṇaparivāriō pāikō cēva aggisammapa cāyaṇanimittaṁ payaṭṭō tabōvaṇaṁ. saṁpattō rāyahaṁsō vva kalahaṁsiyaparivāriō tabōvaṇāsannaṁ vitthiṣṇaṁ girinaïpuliṇaṁ etthantarammi ya muṇiyanarindāgamaṇēṇaṁ, paphullavayaṇapaṅkaēṇaṁ rāiṇō āgamaṇamaggisammatāvasassa nivēiyaṁ muṇikumāraēṇaṁ. taō aggisammatāvasēṇa kō hajalaṇapajjaliyasarīrēṇaṁ sadāviō kulabaī, lajiūṇa jahōciyamukkhāraṁ niṭṭhuraṁ bhaṇiō-bhō! bhō! na pārēmi ē yassa akāraṇavēriṇō narindāhamassa muhamavalōiṅa, tājaṁ kiṁci bhaṇiya bāhiraō caïva visajjēhi ethaṁ. kulayaïṇā cintiyaṁ-avahariō khu ēsō kasāēhiṁ. taō juttaṁ cēva tāva pañcaggakasāyadr̥siyacittassa narindadaṁsaṇaṁ parihariuṁ ti gaō narā. hēyasammuhaṁ thēvaṁ bhūmi kulabaī. diṭṭhō ya ṇēṇa parimilāṇadēhō saparivārō rāyā. paṇamiō ya saviṇayaṁ saparivārēṇaṁ rāiṇā. ahiṇandiō ya āsīsāē kulabaïṇā, bhaṇiō ya ṇēṇa-mahārāya! ēhiḥ ēyāē cammagavī hiyāē upavisamha. rāiṇā-bhaṇiya — ja bhayavaṁ āṇavēi. gayā campagavīhiyaṁ. upaviṭṭhō vimalasilāniviṭṭhē kusāsaṇē kulabaī, purāō ya sē dharaṇīē caïva saparivārō rāmā. tō kulabaïṇā bhaṇiya-mahārāya! kīsa iyāṇiṁ sakalattaparivārēṇaṁ aṇuciyaṁ ēihamētaṁ bhūmiṁ caraṇāgamaṇamaṇuciṭṭhiyaṁ? rāimā bhaṇiyaṁ — bhayavaṁ! aṇuciyakāriṇō cēva amhē, ahavā maējārisāṇaṁ purisāhamāṇaṁ imaṁ cēvōciyaṁ, jaṁ mahātabassijaṇassa pamāyaō vāvāyaṇēṇa dhammantarāyakaraṇaṁ ti. tā kiṁ ēiṇā aṇivvaḍiyahiyayasabbhāvēṇa niyaḍīmantiēṇa? bhayavaṁ! kahiṁ puṇa sō mahāṇubhāvō aggisammatāvasō? paṇamāmi taṁ, sōhēmi tassa dasaṇēṇa pāvakammakāriṇaṁ appāṇaṁ ti. kulabaïṇā bhaṇiyaṁ — mahārāya! mā ēdahamettaṁ saṁtappasu tti. ṇa ēēṇa tuha nivvēēṇamaṇasaṇaṁ kayaṁ tiḥ kiṁ tu kappō cēvāyaṁ tavassijaṇamsa, jaṁ carimakālammi aṇasaṇavihiṇā dēhaparicayaṇaṁ ti. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ — yavaṁ! kiṁbahuṇā mantiēṇa? pecchāmi tāva taṁ mahāṇubhāvaṁ. kulabaïṇā bhaṇiyaṁ — mahārāya! alamiyāṇiṁ tāva tassa dēsaṇēṇaṁ. jhāṇavāvaḍō khu sō, tā kiṁ sē ahippēyakajantarāēṇaṁ? gaccha tumaṁ nayariṁ, puṇō kahiṁci pekkhējasu tti. tō jaṁ bhayavaṁ āṇavēi, puṇō āgacchissāmi tti bhaṇiūṇa añcanta dummaṇō uḍiō rāyā, paṇamiūṇa kulapaī payaṭṭō nayariṁ. taō ekkēṇaṁ sāṇukōsēṇaṁ ca bāṭatāvasakumārēṇaṁ aṇu gacchiūṇa thēvabhūmibhāyaṁ nivēiō sē aggisammābhippābhō tti. taō rāiṇā cintiyaṁ-kimiha puṇāgamaṇēṇaṁ? jaï paraṁ kulabaī ā yāsē pāḍijjaï. tā na juttaṁ mamēhaṁ nayarē vi ciṭṭiuṁ, mā sē mahāṇubhāvassa tassa asōyacaṁ pi anaraṁ muṇissaṁ ti ēvaṁ cintayantō pattō vasantaüraṁ. pucchiyā ṇēṇaṁ saṁbacchariyā kayā amhāṇa khiipaïṭṭhiyagamaṇadiyahō parisujjhaï tti? tēhiṁ ca niccaṁ takammavāvaḍatta ṇēṇōvaladdha sōhaṇadiṇēhi vinattaṁ-’mahārāya kallaṁ cēva parisujjhaïti. taō rāiṇā samāṇattō pariyaṇō payaṭṭaha lahuṁ kallaṁ ti. taō biiyadiyahē mahayā caḍayarēṇa niggaō rāyā. aṇavarayapayāṇaēhiṁ ca pattōmāsamettēṇa kālēṇa khiipaïdriyaṁ. tī ūsiyavicittakēuni vaha, vivihakayāsōī, sōhiyasapupphōvayārarāyamaggaṁ, dhavaliyayāsāyamālōvasōhiyaṁ, mahāvibhūīē pariṭhṭhō nayaraṁ, tattha vi ya tōraṇani mmiyavandaṇamālaṁ, savisēsasaṁpāiyamahōvayāraṁ sabaobhaī nāma pāsāyaṁ. tatya ya tammi cēva diya hē āgō māsakappavihārēṇa ahā. saṁjamaṁ viharantō sīsagaṇasaṁparivuḍō, saṁpuṇṇaduvālasaṅgī, ōhi-maṇanāṇāisayajuttō, savvaṅgasundarāhirāmō, pahamajōvaṇasirīsamaddhā siyasarīrō, maṇḍaṇamiva vasumaīē, āṇandō vya sathalajaṇalōyaṇāṇaṁ, pañcāēsō vva dhammanirayāṇaṁ, nilaovya paramadhannayāē, ṭhāṇamiva ādēyabhāvassa, kulaharaṁ piva khantīē, āgarō iva guṇarayaṇāṇaṁ, vivāgasavvassamiva kusalakammassa, mahāmahantanivavaṁsasaṁbhūō vijaya sēṇō nāma āyariō tti. sō ya asōyadatta sē dvipaḍibaddhē, jiṇāyayaṇamaṇḍiē aṇunaviya oggahaṁ ṭhiō asōyavaṇujjāṇē. jattha nīibaliyā viva naravaī dullaha vivarā sahabārā, parakalattadaṁsagabhīyā viva sappurisā ahōmuhaṭṭhiyā vāvītaḍapāyavā, viṇivaḍiyasappu risacintāō viva aḍālaviḍālāō aïnuttayalayāō darida-kāmihiyayāī piva samantaō āulāī layāharāī, visayapasattā viva pāsaṇḍiṇō na sōhanti limbapāyavā, navavaragā, viva kumumbhara tanivasaṇā virāyanti rattāsōyā, kiṁ bahuṇā? jattha maṇōrahā viva jīvalōyassa bahuvuttantā unnāśapāyayā. tahā himagirisiharāī pitra uttuṅgadhavalāī jiṇāyayaṇāī. tattha ya bahuphāsuē bhūmibhāē ahāsaṁjamaṁ sō bhayavaṁ caraṇakaraṇaniraō parivasaī. iō ya rāiṇā guṇasēṇēṇaṁ asthāiyāgaēṇaṁ pucchiyaṁ. kēṇa bhē ajja iha accheśyabhūyaṁ kiṁci vatthu diḍhē ti? tō uvaladdhavi jayasēṇāyariēṇa paṇamiūṇa rāyāṇaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ kallāṇaēṇaṁ-mahārāya! diḍaṁ maē accheśyaṁ. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ — kahē hi, kiṁ tayaṁ ti? kallāṇaēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — iha asōgadattaseṭṭipaḍibaddhē apōyavaṇujjāṇē sayaladahavvadaṁsaṇamahūsavō,lāyaṇṇajoṇhāpavāhapamhaliyacaüdisābhōō sayalakalāsaṁgaō viya mayalanchaṇō, paḍhamajovvaṇatthō vi viyārarahiō, viṇijjiyakusumabāṇō vi tavasiriniraō, paricattasavva saṅgō vi sayalajaṇokkhārī, muttimantō viva bhayavaṁ dhammō, diṭṭhō maē gandhārajaṇavayāhivassa samarasēṇassa nattuō, lacchisēṇassa puttō paḍivanasamaṇaliṅgō vijayasēṇō nāma āyariō ti. taō rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ — ahō! tuma kayapuṇṇō, pāviyaṁ taē phalaṁ lōyaṇāṇaṁ. ahaṁ piṇaṁ bhayavantaṁ mottūṇamantarāyaṁ suē vandissāmi tti. aïkkantāē rayaṇīē kayasayalagōsakiccō rāyā gaō tamujāṇaṁ. diṭṭhō ya ṇēṇa aṇēyasamaṇapariyariō, saṁpuṇṇasārayasasi vva tārayaṇaparivuḍō vijayasēṇāyariō. taō harisubbhinnapulaēṇa, āṇandabāhajala bhariyalōyaṇēṇaṁ, dharaṇinihittajāṇukarayalēṇaṁ saviṇayaṁ paṇamiō aṇēṇa. dinnō ya sē guruṇā vi sārīramāṇasāṇēgadukkhaviuḍaṇō,sāsa yasivasokkhataruvīyabhūō dhammalābhō tti. taō aṭṭhārasasīlaṅgasahassabhāravahē, siddhivahanimbharāṇurāyasamāgamacintādubbalē sēsasāhu ṇō vandiūṇa uvaviṭhṭhō gurusamīvē. vimhiō ya tassa rūpa-cariēhiṁ. bhaṇiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa bhayavaṁ! kiṁ tē sayalasaṁpuṇṇamaṇōrahassāvi īisa nivvēyakāraṇaṁ? jēṇa iō tō sasambhamanivaḍantanarindamaülimaṇippabhāvisaravicchuriyapāyavīḍhaṁ rāyalacchi ujjhiya imaṁ īisaṁ ihalōyanippivāsaṁ vayavisēsaṁ paḍivannō si tti. vijayasēṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — mahārāya! saṁsārammi vi nivvēyakāraṇaṁ pucchasi? naṇu sulahamettha nivvēyakāraṇaṁ. suṇa—

nāraya-tiriya-narā-’marabhavēsu hiṇḍantayāṇa jīvāṇaṁ

jamma-jarā-maraṇabhaē mottūṇa kimatthi kiṁci muhaṁ?

kiṁ atthi nāragō vā tiriō maṇuō surō va saṁsārē

sō kōi jassa jammaṇa-maraṇāī na honti pāvāī?

tēhi gahiyāṇa ya kahaṁ hōi raī hariṇataṇayāṇaṁ va

kūḍayapaḍiyāṇa daḍhaṁ vāhēhi viluppamāṇāṇaṁ

savvēsiṁ sattāṇaṁ khaṇiya pi hu dukkhamettapaḍiyāraṁ

jā na karēi naṇu suhaṁ lacchī kō tīē paḍibandhō?

kēṇa mamethuppattī kahiṁ iō taha puṇō vi gantavvaṁ

jō ettiya pi cintēi ettha sō kō na niviṇṇō?

annaṁ ca-ettha mahārāya! mahāsamuhamajjhagayaṁ rayaṇamiva cintāmaṇisaṁnibhaṁ dullabhaṁ māṇusattaṇaṁ, tahā kharapavaṇacāliyakusaggajala binducañcalaṁ jīviyaṁ, kuviyabhuyaṅgabhīsaṇaphaṇājālasannihā ya kāmabhōgā, sarayajalahara-kāmiṇīkaḍakkha-gayakaṇṇa-vijjucañcalā ya riddhī, akayamuhatava-caraṇāṇaṁ ca dāruṇō tiriyanāraēmu vivāgō tti. avi ya—

bhaya-rōga-sōga-piyavippaōgabahudukkhajalaṇapajjaliē

naḍapecchaṇayasamāṇē saṁsārē kō dhiī kuṇaï?

saï sāsayammi ṭhāṇē tassōvāē ya paramamuṇimaṇiē

ēgantasāhagē supurisāṇa jattō tahiṁ juttō

ēvaṁ ca, mahārāya! saṁsārō cēva mē nivvēyakāraṇaṁ. tahavi puṇa nimittamettamēyaṁ saṁjāyaṁ ti. muṇa-atthi ihēva vijaē gandhārō nāma jaṇavaō, tattha gandhārapuraṁ nāma nayaraṁ. tannivāsī ahaṁ tatthēva ciṭṭhāmi. mittō ya mē bīyahiyayabhūō sōmavasupurōhiyaputtō vihāvasū nāma. sō ya kahaṁci āyaṅkapīḍiyadēhō viṇijjiyasurāsurēṇa maccuṇā mama samakkhamēva pañcattamuvaṇīō. tō ahaṁ taviō yāṇalajaliyamāṇasō ciṭṭhāmiḥ jāva āgayā ahāsaṁjamavihārēṇaṁ viharamāṇā vāsāvāsanimittaṁ cattāri sāhuṇō, ṭhiyā ya nayarāō nāidūrē mahāmahantāē giriguhāē. siṭṭā ya mē aïpiya tti kariya niyayapurisēhiṁ. gō ahaṁ sigdhamēva tē vandiuṁ. dihā ya tattha bhayavantō sajjhāyavāvaḍā, vandiyā pahaṭṭavayaṇapaṅkaēṇa, ahiṇandiō bhayavantēhiṁ dhammalāhēṇa. pucchiyā maē ahāvihāraṁ. aṇusāsiō bhayavantēhiṁ. taō tē mahāmuṇī kaṁci vēlaṁ pajjuvāsiya paviṭṭhō nayaraṁ. tē ya bhayavantō savvakālamēva vāsāvāsē māsōvavāsēṇaṁ jayanti tti uvaladdhaṁ maē sammattaṁ. pavaḍamāṇasaṅkassa ya païdiṇaṁ sēvamāṇassa mē aïkantā cattāri māsā. carimarayaṇīē jāyā mahaṁ cintā. kallaṁ khu tē mahātavassī gacchissanti. tō ahaṁ addhajāmāvasēsāē rayaṇīē niggaō bhayavantadaṁsaṇanimittaṁ nayarāō. gaō ya thē bhūmibhāgaḥ jāva payaliyā vasumaī, gajjiya gandhāragiriṇā, pavāiō surahimāruō, ujjōviyaṁ nahaṅgaṇaṁ, vitthariō jayajayārayō. taō ahaṁ abbhahiyajāyaha risō turiya turiya patthiō jāva pecchāmi gandhāragiriguhāsamī vē, avahariyaṁ taṇāiya, samīkayaṁ dharaṇivaḍhaṁ pavuṭṭhuṁ gandhōdayaṁ, uvaïṇṇā pupphōvayārā, nivaḍiyā dēvasaṁghāyā, thuṇanti bhayavantē sāhuṇō. ahō! bhē muladdhaṁ māṇusattaṇaṁ, khaviyā rāgādaō, parājiyaṁ kamma sennaṁ, tiṇṇō bhavasamuddō, pāviyā sāsayasivasuhasiddhi ti. tō maē cintiyaṁ-āvinbhūyaṁ nr̥ṇamēēsiṁ kēvalaṁ mukkā jāijarāmaraṇadukkhavāsassa. etthantarammi dihā maē kēvalapahāvaō cciya rayaṇamayasīhāsaṇōvaviṭhṭhā, viṇiyaṭṭabhavapavaścā, pasa ntacittavāvārā, kēvalasirīsamaddhāsiyasarīrā, muttimantā viva guṇagaṇā bhayavantō sāhuṇō tiṁ. taō maē cintiyaṁ-na ettha saṁdēhō, saṁpuṇṇamēva ēēsiṁ kēvalanāṇaṁ ti. taō āṇandabāhajalabhariyalōyaṇēṇaṁ, rōmañcapulaïyaḍrēṇaṁ, vimhayavasupphullalōyaṇēṇaṁ, dharaṇinimiya jāṇukarayalēṇaṁ, tahāviha, añcantasōhaṇaṁ, aṇācikkhaṇīya avasthantaramaṇuhavantē bandiyā maē, vandiūṇa ya uvaviṭhṭhō tēsiṁ puraō. patthuyā kēvaliṇā kahā. payattā pucchiu hiyaïcchiyaṁ dēva-naragaṇā. taō maē cintiyaṁ-kiṁ puṇō ahamē ē bhayavantē pucchāmi? jāva āvaḍiō hiyayasallabhūō cittammi mē vihāvam. taō maē cintiyaṁ-’aha kahiṁ puṇa mē mittō vihāvara uppanō hōu' ēya pucchāmi tti cintiūṇa pucchiō maē bhagavaṁ kēvalī. bhayavaṁ! atthi iō kōi kālō pañcattamuvagayassa mē mittassa. tā kahiṁ sō uvavannō? kiṁ vā saṁpayamavatthantaramaṇuhavaï? kiṁ vā mama muṇiyaparamatthamaggassa vi taviōyāṇalajaṇiyasaṁtāvō cittammi nōvasamaṁ jāi tti? kēvaliṇā bhaṇiyaṁ — suṇa, atyi ihēva gandhārapurē nayarē ūsaïnnō nāma batthasōhagō. tassa mahupiṅgā nāma gēhasuṇiyā. tīsē gabhammi muṇaō ubavannō tti. sō ya aïkaḍhiṇarajjusaṁdāmiō, bubhukkhāparimilāṇadēhō, sōhaṇigakuṇḍaniyaḍavattī, rāsaha khurappahārabhīō ihēva saṁpayaṁ dāruṇamavatyantaramaṇuhavaï. jammantarammi ya pukvaraddhabharahakusumapura nivāsiṇō tē kusumasārasaniyassa seṭṭhi puttassa sirikantābhihāṇā accantavallahā pattī āsi tti. tayabhāsaō ya tē taviōyāṇalajaṇiyasaṁtāvō cittammi ṇoksamaṁ jāi. taō maē ēyaṁ sōuṇaṁ saṁjāyanivvēēṇaṁ tannēhamōhiyamaṇēṇa ya tassa paḍimokkhaṇanimittaṁ pēsiyā ūsadinnavatthasōhagagihaṁ niyayapurisā, bhaṇiyā ya taṁ lahuṁ mōyāviya, viiṇṇapāṇa-bhōyaṇaṁ gihiya ihēvāgacchaha tti. taō gayā tē purisā, sigdhaṁ ca saṁpāḍiyaṁ majjha sāsaṇaṁ imēhiṁ, āgayā ya taṁ geṇhium̐. diṭṭhō ya sō maē pisuyāsayagahiyataṇuruhō, kīḍāniyarasaṁpāiyakhayatiō, aïkhīṇasarīrō, sasantacalirajīhākarālō, dhavalavihāvijjamāṇadasaṇāvalī, mandamandaṁ parisakamāṇō nāidūraō cēva suṇaō tti. jāō ya mē taṁ tahāvihaṁ dahaṇa mahantō saṁvēgō. cintiyaṁ ca maē-ahō! dāruṇō saṁsāravāsō. ēvaṁvihāvasāṇaḥṇi ettha jīvāṇaṁ pemmavilasiyāī.

etthantarammi ya pattā mama samīvaṁ saha tēṇa tē purisā. nivēiō ṇēhi dēva! ēsa sō suṇaō ti. taō sō maṁ daṭṭaṇa payalaṁtadī halaṅlō, bāhajalabhariyalōyaṇō, uggīvamavayāliyāṇaṇō kiṁpi tahāvihaṁ aṇācivakhaṇīya avasyantaraṁ pāviūṇamārasiumāḍhattō. taō maē pucchiō kēvalī. bhayavaṁ! kimēyaṁ ti? tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — durantapuvyabbhāsaō paṇaō tti. maē bhaṇiyaṁ — bhaya! kimēsa maṁ paccahiyāṇaï? bhayavayā bhaṇiyaṁ — na visēsaō, kiṁtu sāmanaō ti. īisō cēva ēsa saṁsārasahāvō tti, jammaṇantarabhavabhatthā bhāvaṇā aṇābhōgaō vi kaṁci kālaṁ aṇuvattaï tti. taō maē bhaṇiya-bhayavaṁ aha kassa kammassa ēsa vivāgō? bhayavayā bhaṇiyaṁ jāimayamāṇajaṇiyassa. maē bhaṇiyaṁ — bhayavaṁ! kōvi yāṇēṇa māṇō kō ti? bhayakkhā bhaṇiyaṁ - suṇa, etya cēvāṇantarajammē pavattē mayaṇamahūsavē, niggayāsu vicittavēsāsu, nayaracaccarīsu, taruṇajaṇavandraparigaēṇa bahujaṇapasaṁsaṇijja vasantakīlamaṇuhavantē ṇa diṭṭhā samā sannacāriṇī vatthasōhagacacaritti. daṭṭhūṇa ya annāṇadōsēṇaṁ jāi-kulāigabiēṇaṁ kahaṁ nīyacacarī amhāṇa caccarīē samāsanaṁ pari bayaï ti kayatthiyā vatthasōhagā. pahāṇō tti kariya dahayaraṁ kayatthiūṇa saṁjamiyasavvagattō nēyāviō cārayaṁ usadinō. ettha ntarammi garuyamāṇapariṇāmavaliṇā baddhaṁ parabhavāuyaṁ. nivattē ya mayaṇamahūsavē nagaralōēṇa mōyāviō usadinnō. ēsō ya takkamma pariṇāmavasō mariūṇa ettha upavanō tti. taō maē cintiyaṁ-ahō! appamuhaṁ niyāṇaṁ bahudukkhaphalaṁ, dhiratthu saṁsāravāsassa. tā pucchāmi bhayavantaṁ kiṁ pajjavasāṇamēyaṁ niyāṇaṁ? kiṁ vā ēsa bhaviō, abhaviō vā? siddhigāmī asiddhigāmī saṁpattavīō vā na va? tti cintiūṇa pucchiyaṁ maē. taō bhayavayā bhaṇiya-suṇa, jaṁpajjavasāṇamēyaṁ niyāṇaṁ iō suṇayabhavāō ēsa ahāuyaṁ pāliūṇa uvvaṭṭō samāṇō imassa cēva usadinnassa gēhapasyāē ghōḍapaḍigābhihāṇāē rāsahīē ganmammi rāsahattāē uvavajihi tti. tō ya niggaō samāṇō usadinnassa amaṇōramō, kilēsasaṁpāviyasarīravittī, garuyabhāruvvahaṇaparikkhēiyasarīrō, jīviyasamayaṁ ciṭṭhiūṇa maō samāṇō usadinasaṁgayassa cēva māidinnasanniyassa caṇḍālassa aṇahigābhihāṇāē bhāriyāē kucchisi napuṁsagattāē uvavanjihi ti. tō ya nikkhantō samāṇō kurūpadōhaggakalaṅkadūsiō, aparinnāyavisayasaṅgō, kaṁci kālaṁ napuṁsagattāē jīviūṇa sīhaviṇivāiyasarīrō dēhaṁ pamottūṇa tīsē cēva caṇḍālamahiliyāē kuñchisi isthigattāē ubavajihi tti. taō viṇiggayamettō cēva paḍhamabālabhāvavattī bhuyaṅgaḍakō mariūṇa ūsadinnassa cēva gabhadāsīē dattiyābhihāṇāē kucchisi napuṁsagattāē uvavajihi tti. taō viṇiggō samā ṇō jaccandhamaḍahakhujjō sabalōyaparibhūō kaṁci kālaṁ napuṁsagattaṁ parivāliūṇa payatta nayaraḍāhē kisāṇuṇā chārīkayasarīrō paścatta muvagacchiūṇa tīsē cēva gambhadāsīē kucchisi itthiyattāē upavajihi tti. samuppannō ya pīḍhasappī bhavissaï ti. taō etthēva nayarē rāyamaggēṇa gacchantō viyariēṇa mattahatthiṇā vāvāiyō samāṇō imassa cēva ūsadinnassa kālajaṇiyābhihāṇāē bhāri yāē kucchisi itthigattāē uvavajihi tti. jāyā samāṇī kamēṇa saṁpattajovvaṇā. dinā ya ūsadinnēṇa ūsarakkhiyābhihāṇassa añcantadāridābhibhūyassa. itthiyā kayapāṇiggahaṇā āvanasattā hōūṇa pasūisamaē cēva mahāvēdaṇāhibhūyā kālaṁ kāūṇa sajaṇaṇīē cēva puttattāē uvavajihi tti. samuppanō ya sō bālabhāvē cēva gandhāranimnagātīrammi khellamāṇō ūsadinasattuṇā cilāyanāmēṇa riuputtō tti gihiūṇa sirōharānibaddhagaruyasilāyalō dahammi parikkhippihii. ēyapajjavasāṇamēyaṁ niyāṇaṁ. bhaviō ya ēō siddhigāmī ya, kēvalamasaṁpattabīō tti. taō maē bhaṇiya-bhaya. kahiṁ puṇō sō jalamaraṇāṇantaraṁ upavajihii ti? kayā vā bīyasaṁpattī muttisaṁpattī ya bhavissaï? bhagakkhā bhamiyaṁ-muṇa, jalamaraṇāṇantaraṁ vāṇamantarēsu uavajihi tti. taō tammi cēva jammē āṇandatitthayarasamīvē sāsayasuhakappapāyavēkavīyaṁ sammattaṁ pāvihii. taō caügaïsamāvannō saṁkhejjēsu samaïthiēma bhavagga haṇēsu, ihēva gandhārajaṇavaē pāviūṇa naravaïttaṇaṁ, amaratēyavijāharasamaṇagaṇisamīvē paranjiūṇa payajja, saṁpattakēvalō muttiṁ pāvi ssaï tti. taō mamēyaṁ sōūṇa jāō saṁvēō, niyattā bhavacāragāō maī. taō aṇunadiya jaṇaṇi-jaṇaē, kāūṇa jahōciyaṁ karaṇijja, nikkhantō mugahīyanāmadhēyassa bhagavaō indadattagaṇaharassa samīthē. tā ēyaṁ mē nivvēyakāraṇaṁ ti. guṇasēṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ bhayavaṁ! kayatthō si, sōhaṇaṁ nivvēyakāraṇaṁ. jaṁ puṇa imaṁ bhaṇiyamāsi. jahā—

saï sāsayammi ṭhāṇē tassōvāē ya paramamuṇimaṇiē

ēgantasāhaē supurisāṇa jattō tarhi juttō tti

aha kiṁ puṇa taṁ sāsayaṁ ṭhāṇaṁ, kō vā tassa sāhaō uvāō ti?. vijayasēṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — mahārāya? sāsayaṁ ṭhāṇaṁ nāma, jattha pāṇiṇō aṭṭhavihakammamalakalaṅkavippamukkā, jamma-jarā-maraṇa-rōya-sōyāiuvaddavarahiyā, niruvamanāṇadaṁsaṇasuhabhāiṇō, aṇaṁtaṁ āyā midīhamaddhaṁ kālaṁ ciṭṭhanti. taṁ puṇa sayalāisayarayaṇāyarēhi, tēlōkabandhavēhi, surāsurapūirahiṁ, savvannūhi bhaṇiyaṁ. imassa cēva cōdasa :rajjūsiyassa khettalōgassa cūḍāmaṇibhūyaṁ paramapayaṁ ṭhāṇaṁ ti. sāhaō uṇa uvāō imassa sammatta-nāṇa-caraṇalakkhaṇō paḍivāiō tti. ēsō ya gihidhammasāhudhammēhiṁ vavatthiō. tattha gihidhammō duvālasavihō. taṁ jahā-paśca aṇuvvayāī, tiṇṇi guṇavvayāī, cattāri sikkhāvayāī ti. sāhudhammō uṇa dasavihō. taṁ jahā—

ēyamsa uṇa duvihassa vi dhammassa mūlavatthu sammattaṁ. taṁ puṇō aṇāikammasaṁtāṇaveḍhiyassa jentuṇō dullaha havaï ti. taṁ ca kammaṁ aṭṭahā, taṁ jahā-nāṇāvaraṇijja, darisaṇāvaraṇijja, vēyaṇijjaṁ, mōhaṇijjaṁ, āuyaṁ, nāma, gōtaṁ, antarāyaṁ ca. ēyassa uṇa nimittaṁ-micchattaṁ, annāṇaṁ, aviraī, pamāō, kasāyā, jōgā yatti. ēgapariṇāmasaṁciyassa ēyassa duvihā ṭhiī samakkhāyā. taṁ jahā-ukkōsiyā ya jahaniyā ya. tattha ṇaṁ jā sā ukkōsiyā, sā tivyāsuhapariṇāmamaṇiyāṇaṁ nāṇāvaraṇa-darisaṇāvaraṇa-vēyaṇīya antarāyāṇaṁ tīsaṁ sāgarōvamakōḍākōḍīō, mōhaṇijjassa ya sattariṁ, nāma-gōyāṇaṁ vīsaṁ, tettīsaṁ ca sāgarōvamāī āuyassa tti. jahannā uṇa tahāvihapariṇāmasaṁciyassa vēyaṇīyassa bārasa muhuttā, nāma-gōyāṇaṁ aṭṭha, sēsāṇaṁ bhinnamuhuttaṁ ti. ēvaṁṭhiyassa ya imassa kammassa ahāpavattakaraṇēṇa jayā ghasaṇadhōlaṇāē kahavi ēga sāgarōvamakōḍākōḍiṁ mottūṇa sēsāō khaviyāō havanti, tīsē vi ya ṇaṁ thēvamettē khaviē, tayā ghaṇarāyadōsapariṇāmalakkhaṇō, nāṇāvaraṇa-darisaṇāvaraṇa-’ntarāyapaḍivānasahāyabhāvō, mōhaṇīya kammanivvattiō, accantadumbhēō kammagaṇṭhī havaï. bhaṇiyaṁ ca—

“gaṇṭhi tti sudubbhēō kakkhaḍaghaṇarūḍhagūḍhagaṇṭhi ca

jīvassa kammajaṇiō ghaṇarāgadōsapariṇāmō”

taṁ ca pattē samāṇē atthi ēgē jīvē, jē taṁ bhindaï, atthi ēgē jīvē jē nō bhindaï. tattha ṇaṁ jē sē bhindaï sē apuvakaraṇēṇaṁ bhindaï. taō tammi bhinnē samāṇē aṇiyaṭṭīkaraṇēṇaṁ kammavaṇassa, dāvāṇalēgadēsaṁ, sivasuhapāyavassa niruvahayavīya, saṁsāracāra yassa mōyāvaṇasamatthaṁ, cintāmaṇirayaṇassa ya lahuyabhāvajaṇayaṁ, aṇāimmi saṁsārasāyarē apattapuvvaṁ, pasatthasammattamōhaṇīyakammāṇu vēyagōvasamakkhayasamutthaṁ, pasama-saṁvēya-nivvēyā-’ṇukampāiliṅga, suhāyapariṇāmarūvaṁ sammattaṁ pāuṇaï, tallāhasamakālaṁ ca duvē nāṇāṇi, taṁ nahā-maïnāṇaṁ ca suyanāṇaṁ ca. taō tammi pattē samāṇē sē jīvē bahuyakammamalamukkē, āsannaniyasarūvabhāvē, pasannē, saṁviggē, nidhiṇṇē, aṇukampāparē, jiṇavayaṁpa āvi havaī. bhaṇiyaṁ ca—

"sammattaṁ uvasamamāiēhi lakkhijjaē uvāēhiṁ

āyapariṇāmarūvaṁ bajhēhi pasatthajōgēhi

ettha ya pariṇāmō khalu jīvassa muhō u hōi vinnēō

kiṁ malakalaṅkamukkaṁ kaṇayaṁ bhuvi sāmalaṁ hōi?

payaīi ya kammāṇaṁ viyāgiṅa vā vivāgamamuhaṁti

avaraddha vi ṇa kuppaï uvasamaō savvakālaṁpi

nara-vibuhēsarasokkhaṁ dukkhaṁ ciya bhāvaō u mannantō

saṁvēgaō na mokkhaṁ mottūṇaṁ kiṁci patthēi"

nāraya-tiriya-narā-’marabhavēmu nivvēyaō vasaï dukkhaṁ

akayaparalōyamaggō mamattavisavēgarahiō vi

daṇaṁ pāṇinivahaṁ bhīmē bhavasāgarammi dukkhattaṁ

avisēsaō'ṇukampaṁ duhā vi sāmatthaō kuṇaï

mannaï tamēva saccaṁ nīsaṅgha jaṁ jiṇēhi pannattaṁ

suhapariṇāmō savvaṁ kaṅkāivisottiyārahiō

ēvaṁvihapariṇāmō sammadiṭṭhī jiṇēhi pannattō

ēsō ya bhavasamudaṁ lāi thēvēṇa kālēṇaṁ

taō ya tīsē vi ya ṇaṁ ṭhiīē paliōvamapuhuttamettē khīṇē paramatthaō suhayarapariṇāmagabbhaṁ dēsaviraī paḍivajjaï. taṁ jahā-thūla gapāṇāivāyaviramaṇaṁ vā, thūlagamusāvāyaviramaṇaṁ kā, thūlayādattādāṇaviramaṇaṁ vā, paradāragamaṇaviramaṇaṁ vā, sadārasaṁtōsaṁ vā, aparimi yapariggahaviramaṇaṁ vā. sē ya ēvaṁ dēsaviraïpariṇāmajuttē, paḍivannāṇubbaē, bhāvaō aparivaḍiyapariṇāmē nō khalu samāyaraï imē aïyārē. taṁ jahā-bandhaṁ vā, vahaṁ vā, chavicchēyaṁ vā, aïbhārārōvaṇaṁ vā, bhattapāṇavocchēyaṁ vā tahā sahasabhakkhāṇaṁ vā, rahassabbhakkhāṇaṁ vā, sadāramantabhēyaṁ vā, mōsōvaēsaṁ vā, kūḍalēhakaraṇaṁ vā tahā tēṇāhaḍaṁ vā, takarapaōgaṁ vā, viruddharajjāikamaṁ vā, kūḍatula-kūḍamāṇē vā, tappaḍirūvagavavahāraṁ vā; tahā ittariyapariggahiyāgamaṇaṁ vā, apariggahiyāgamaṇaṁ vā, aṇaṅgakīḍaṁ vā, paravivāhakaraṇaṁ vā, kāmabhōga tivyāhilāsaṁ vā; tahā khettavatthupamāṇāikkama vā, hiraṇṇa-suvaṇṇapamāṇāikkama vā, dhaṇē-dhanapamāṇāikkama vā, dupaya-caüppaya pamāṇāikkama vā, kuviyapamāṇāikkama vā; tahā annē ya ēvaṁjāiē saṁsārasāgarahiṇḍaṇanimittabhūē suhapariṇāmabhāvō cēva nō āyaraï tti. tahā imē ēyārūvē uttaraguṇē ya paḍibrajaï. taṁ jahā-udisiguṇavvayaṁ vā, ahōdisiguṇavayaṁ vā, tiriyadisiguṇavvayaṁ vā; tahā bhōgōvabhōgaparimāṇalakkhaṇaguṇavvayaṁ vā, uvabhōga-paribhōgahēu-kharakammāiparivajaṇaṁ vā; tahā avajjhāṇāyariya-pamāyāyariya-hiṁsa payāṇa-pāvakammōvaēsalakkhaṇāṇatthadaṇḍavirahaguṇavvayaṁ vā,tahā sāvajjajōgaparivajaṇa-niravajjajōgapaḍisēvaṇālakkhaṇasāmāiyasikkhā vayaṁ vā, tahā disivayagahiyassa disāparimāṇassa païdiṇapamāṇakaraṇadēsāvagāsiyasikkhāvayaṁ vā, tahā āhāra-sarīrasakāra-bambhacēra avvāvāralakkhaṇapōsahasikkhāvayaṁ vā, tahā nāyāgayāṇaṁ, kappaṇijjāṇaṁ, anna-pāṇāīṇaṁ davvāṇaṁ dēsakāla-saddhā-sakārakamajuyaṁ parāē bhattīē āyāṇuggahaṭāē saṁjayāṇaṁ dāṇaṁ ti, iilakkhaṇātihisaṁvibhāgasikkhākkhaṁ vā. sē ya ēvaṁ kusalapariṇāmajuttē paḍivanaguṇavvaya sikkhāvaē bhāvaō aparivaḍiyapariṇāmē nō khalu samāyaraï imē aïyārē. taṁ jahā-uḍadisipamāṇāikkama vā, ahōdisipamāṇāikamaṁ vā, tiriyadisipamāṇāikkama vā, khettabuddhiṁ vā, saïantaraddhaṁ vā, tahā sacittāhāraṁ vā, sacittapaḍibaddhāhāraṁ vā, appaüliōsahibha kkhaṇaṁ vā, duppaüliōsahibhakkhaṇaṁ vā, tucchōsahimakkhaṇaṁ vā; tahā iṅgālakammaṁ vā, vaṇakammaṁ vā, sōgaḍikammaṁ vā, bhāḍiyakammaṁ vā, phōḍiyakammaṁ vā, dantavāṇijja vā, lakkhavāṇijjavā, kēsavāṇijja vā, rasavāṇijjaṁ vā, visavāṇijja vā, jantapīlaṇakammaṁ vā, nilla. chaṇakammaṁ vā, davaggidāvaṇayaṁ vā, asaïpōsaṇaṁ vā, sara-daha-talāyasōsaṇayaṁ vā, tahā kandappaṁ vā kukkuiyaṁ vā, mōhariyaṁ vā, saṁjuttā higaraṇaṁ vā, uvabhōgaparibhōgāirēga vā, tahā maṇaduppaṇihāṇaṁ vā, vayaduppaṇihāṇaṁ vā, kāyaduppaṇihāṇaṁ vā, sāmāiyassa saïakaraṇaṁ vā, sāmāiyassa aṇavaṭṭhiyassa karaṇaṁ vā; tahā āṇavaṇapaōgaṁ vā, pēsavaṇapōgaṁ vā, sadāṇuvāittaṁ vā, rūvāṇuvāittaṁ vā, bahiyāpoggalapa kkhēvaṇaṁ vā; tahā appaḍilēhiyaduppaḍilēhiyasejjāsaṁthāradurūhaṇaṁ vā, appamajjiyaduppamajjiyasē jjāsaṁthāradurūhagaṁ vā, appaḍilēhiya duppaḍilēhiyaüccāra-pāsavaṇavigiśvaṇayaṁ vā, appamajjiya-duppamajjiyaüccāra-pāsavaṇavigiścaṇayaṁ vā, pōsahōvavāsassa samma aṇa ṇupālaṇayaṁ vā, tahā sacittanikkhivaṇayaṁ vā, sacittapihaṇayaṁ vā, kālāikkama paravavaēsaṁ vā, annē ya ēvaṁjāiē guṇavvayasikkhāvayāiyārē nāyaraï. taō ṇaṁ sē ēmēyāṇurūvēṇaṁ kappēṇaṁ vihariūṇa tīsē kammaḍhiīē pariṇāmavisēsēṇaṁ tammi vā jammē, aṇēgēsu vā jammēsu saṁkhejjēsu sāgarōvamēsu khaviēmu sabaviraïlakkhaṇaṁ khamā-maddava-ujjava-muttī-tava-saṁjama-sacca sōyā-’’kiścaṇa-bambhacērarūvaṁ jaïdhamma pāuṇaï. taō ēvaṁ cēva uvasamaseḍhī, ēvaṁ cēva kharagaseḍhē tti. bhaṇiyaṁ ca—

sammattammi u laddhē paliyapuhuttēṇa sāvaō hōjā

caraṇōvasamakhayāṇaṁ sāgarasaṁkhantarā honti

ēvaṁ appaḍivaḍiē sammattē dēva-maṇuyajammēsu

annayaraseḍhivajja ēgabhavēṇaṁ ca savvāī

tō khavagaseḍhiparisamattīē sāsayaṁ aṇantaṁ, kēvalabaranāṇadasaṇaṁ pāuṇaï. taō kamēṇaṁ khaviyasēsabhavāvaggāhikammasē, savva kammavippamukkē pāuṇaï sāsayaṁ ṭhāṇaṁ ti. etthantarammi ya guruvayaṇāyaṇṇaṇajaṇiyasuhapariṇāmāṇaladaḍḍabahukammendhaṇēṇaṁ, bhāvaō pavanasammattā-ṇuvyaya-guṇavvaya-sikkhāvayaguṇahāṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ guṇasēṇēṇaṁ-bhayavaṁ! dhannō'haṁ. jēṇa maē pāvamalapakkhālaṇaṁ, rāgāi visaghāyaṇaṁ, pasamāiguṇakāraṇaṁ, bhavacārayanissāraṇaṁ muyaṁ tē vayaṇaṁ ti. tā āisaha saṁpayaṁ, jaṁ maē kāyadhvaṁ ti. ahavā āiṣṭuṁ cēva bhayavayā. tā dēhi mē tāva gihidhammasārabhūē aṇuvdhayāiē guṇaṭṭhāṇē. guruṇā bhaṇiyaṁ — kiccamēyaṁ taējārisāṇaṁ bhavvasattāṇaṁ ti vihipuvvayaṁ dinnāṇi sē aṇuvvayāṇi, aṇusāsiō ya bahuvihaṁ. taō vandiūṇa paramabhattīē saparivāraṁ guruṁ paviṭṭhō nayaraṁ. kayabhō. yaṇokkhārō ya pariṇayappāē diyahē puṇō vi niggaō tti. bandiyā ya ṇēṇa dēvaguravō. kālōiyamaṇusāsiō ya gurugā. taō ya kaṁci vēlaṁ pajjuvāsiūṇa vihiṇā puṇō nayaraṁ paviṭṭhō tti. ēvaṁ ubhayakālaṁ gurudaṁsaṇa-tavvayaṇasuṇaṇasokkhamaṇuhavantassa aīō māsō, pariṇō sē dhammō. kappasamattīē ya gaō annatya bhayavaṁ vijayasēṇāyariō ti. tō akvantēsu kaïvayadiṇēsu rāiṇō guṇasēṇassa pāsāyatalasaṁṭhiyassa kahavi sōūṇa hāhāravasadagambhiṇa maraṇanaravaïṇō viva payāṇaḍhakaṁ, saṁsārarakkhasassa viva aṭṭahāsaṁ, jīvalōyassa viva pamāyacariyaṁ mayagaḍiṇḍimasaī, pecchiūṇa taṁ kayantabasavattiṇaṁ, caüpurisadharayakārya, kandantabandhujaṇaparivāriyaṁ sarva, paramasaṁ vēgabhāviyamaïssa, indayālasarisajīvalōyamavagacchiūṇa dhammajjhāṇajalapakkhāliyapāvalēvassa samuppannā cintā-amhē vi ēvaṁ cēva maraṇadhammāgō tti. ahō! ṇu khalu ēvaṁ virasāvasāṇē jīvalōē tē dhannā, jē tēlōkabandhubhūē, acintacintāmaṇisannihē, paramarisi savvannudēsiē dhammē kayāṇurāyā agāravāsāṇō aṇagāriśra pavvayanti. taō ya pāṇavaha-musāvāya-adattādāṇa-mēhuṇa-pariggaha virayā, vāyālīsēsaṇādōsaparisuddhapiṇḍaggahiṇō, saṁjōyaṇāipañcadōsarahiyamiyakālabhōiṇō, pañcasamiyā, tiguttā, niraïyāravayapa- ||padamō bhavō ripālaṇatyamēva iriyāsamiyāipaṇavīsabhāvaṇōvavēyā, aṇasaṇa-mūgōyariyāi-pāyacchitta-viṇayāisabāhiranbhintaratavōguṇappahāṇā, māsāiyāṇēgapaḍimādhāriṇō, vicittadavvābhiggaharayā, aṇhāṇa-lōya-laddhāvaladdhaviniṇō, nippaḍikammasarīrā, samataṇa-maṇi-leṭchu kaścaṇā, kiṁ vahuṇā, aṭṭhāra pasī laṅgasahassadhāriṇō, uvamāīyavibuhajaṇapasaṁsiyapasamasuhasamēyā, aṇēgagāmā-’’yara-nagara-paṭṭaṇa maḍamba-dōṇamuha-saṁnivēsasayasaṁkulaṁ vihariūṇa mēiṇi, micchattapakamaggapaḍibaddhē ya saddhammakahaṇadivāyarōdaēṇaṁ vōhiūṇa bhavvakamalā. yarē, mahātabañcaraṇaparikammiyasarīrā jigōvaïṭṭhēṇa maggēṇa kālamāsē kālaṁ kāūṇa pāōvagamaṇēṇa dēhaṁ paricayanti. taō ahaṁ pi iyāṇi igrēṇa cēva vihiṇā dēhaṁ paricaïsaṁ ti. pattō ya maē bhavasayasahassadullahō, sayalalōyālōyadivāyarō, sāsayasuhappayāṇēkakappapāyayō sayalatēlōkaniruvamacintāmaṇī, viyaḍasaṁsārajalahipōyabhūō, dhammasārahī, bhayavaṁ vijayasēṇāyariō ti. aō pavajāmō dhīrapu. risasēviyaṁ kammavaṇadāvāṇalaṁ ēyassa samīvē mahāpavaja ti. cintiūṇa sadāviyā ṇēṇa subuddhipamuhā mantiṇō. kahiō ya tēsiṁ niyayāhippāō. taō tappasaṅgaō cēvōvaladdhajiṇavayaṇasārēhiṁ bhaṇiyaṁ ca tēhi-ahō! mahāpurisasahāvāṇurūvaṁ dēvēṇa mantiyaṁ. khara pavaṇacāliyanaliṇajalamajjhagayacandabimbacaścalammi jīvalōē kiñca mēṁ bhaviyāṇaṁ ahāmuhaṁ, mā karēha paḍibandhaṁ ti. annaṁ ca-dēva! kō nāma kassaï muhittaṇaṁ pavajiūṇaṁ taṁ palittajālāvalīparigayāō gēhāō nisarantaṁ vārēi? palittaṁ ca savvadukkhajalaṇēṇa saṁsāra gēhaṁ ti. tā bahumayaṁ nāma amhāṇamēyaṁ dēvassa vavasiyaṁ. asamatthā ya amhē buddhivihavēṇa bhavaō maraṇaṁ nivārēuṁ ti. taō rāiṇā ēyamāyaṇṇiuṇa ēvamēyaṁ ti, kō tumbhē mottūṇa mama annō hiō ahiṇandiuṇa sabahumāṇaṁ pahaṭṭhamuhakamalēṇaṁ davāviyaṁ āghōsaṇā puvvayaṁ mahādānaṁ, kārāviyā bhattivihavāṇurūvā jiṇāyayaṇāīsu aṭṭāhiyā mahimā, sammāṇiō ya paṇaïvaggō, bahumāṇiyā paürajaṇavayā, dinnaṁ candasēṇābhihāṇassa jeṭṭaputtassa rajja, paḍivanā bhāvaō pancajjā. suē ya iō gamissāmi, jattha bhayavaṁ vijayasēṇāyariō ti cintiūṇa ṭhiō vivittadēsammi sancarāiyaṁ paḍimaṁ. iō ya sō aggisammatāvasō apaḍikvantō cēva tanniyāṇāō kālaṁ kāūṇa vijjukumārēsu divaḍapaliōvamaṭṭiī dēvō jāō tti. dinō ya tēṇa uvaōgō kiṁ maē huyaṁ vā, jalu vā, dāṇaṁ vā dinnaṁ, jēṇa maē ēsā divyā dēvaḍī patta tti. ābhōiō ya ṇēṇa puvajammavuttantō, kuvibhō ya uvari guṇasēṇassa. vihaṅgēṇāhōiūṇa āgō tasta samīvaṁ. diṭṭhō ya ṇēṇa paḍimaṁ ṭhiō guṇasēṇō. taō ya—

paḍima ṭhiyassa tēṇaṁ viubbiyā kōhamūḍhahiyaēṇa

nirayāṇalajaliyasihā (nihā) aïghōrā paṁsuvuṭṭhi tti

tīē ya ḍajjhamāṇō aṇāulaṁ garuyasattasaṁpannō

cintēi bhāviyamaṇō dhammammi jiṇappaṇīyammi

sārīra-māṇasēhiṁ dukkhēhi abhidyammi saṁsārē

sulahamiṇaṁ jaṁ dukkha dulahā saddhammapaḍivattaü

dhannō'haṁ jēṇa maē aṇōrapārammi bhavasamuddammi

bhavasayasahassadulahaṁ laddhaṁ saddhammarayaṇamiṇaṁ

ēyassa pabhāvēṇa pālijjantassa saï payattēṇaṁ

jammantarammi jīvā pāvanti na dukkhadōgaccaṁ

tā ēsō ciya saphalō majjhamaṇāyaraṇadōsaparihīṇō

saddhammalābhagaruō jammō gāimmi saṁsārē

vilihaï ya majjha hiyayammi jō kaō tassa aggisammassa

paribhavakōvuppāō taki akajja kayaṁ pacchā

eṇhi puṇa paḍivannō mēti samvēsu cēva jīvēsu

jiṇavayaṇāō ahayaṁ visēsaō aggisammammi

iya sō muhapariṇāmō tēṇaṁ viṇivāiō u pāvēṇaṁ

mariūṇaṁ uvavannō dēvō sōhammakappammi

aha sāgarōvamāū jāō candāṇaṇē vimāṇammi

dēvāṇuppattivihiṁ samāsaō etya bucchāmi

ōhēṇaṁ ciya jaha tē havanti jaṁ ca ’ccharādaō tēsiṁ

nibattantiyarē jaha paramaṁ dēvassa karaṇijjaṁ

jaha mēhā-’saṇi-tiyasindacāva-vijjūṇa saṁbhavō hōi

gayaṇammi khaṇēṇa tahā dēvāṇa vi hōi uppattī

sō puṇa mottūṇa imaṁ dēhaṁ vimalammi dēvasayaṇijjē

nivvattēi sarīraṁ divyaṁ antōmuhuttēṇaṁ

tammi samayammi tattha ya gāyanti maṇōharāi gēyāī

kusumapayaraṁ muyanti ya saṁbhamarayaṁ tiyasavilayāō

naccanti divvavinbhamasaṁpāiyatiyasakōuhallāō

vajantavivihamaṇaharatisarīvīṇāsaṇāhāō

dēvā ya harisiyamaṇā karenti ukisīhanāyaṁ ca

muṇiūṇa tassa jammaṁ sudullahaṁ sayala(vaṇammi

iyarō vi ya kāmaguṇē sadda-phāsa-rasa-rūpa-gandhē ya

divvē samaṇuhavantō hiṭṭhō uṭṭhēi sayarāhaṁ

surayaṇanayaṇāṇandō divvaṁ dēvaṁsuyaṁ ahikhivantō

bhāsuravarabondidharō saṁppuṇṇō sārayasasivva

tiyasavilayāu tattha ya tēhi ya laḍahāu mahuravayaṇēhiṁ

jaya jaya jaya tti nandā! thuṇanti hiṭāu ēēhiṁ

tiyasā vi paramahilā gaṇḍayalāvaḍiyakuṇḍalujjōyā

suratarukusumāharaṇā namanti jayasadahalabōlaṁ

aha taṁ divbapariyaṇaṁ daṭṭaṇaṁ lōyaṇēṇa saṁbhantō

dinnaṁ huyaṁ va kiṁ mē imaṁ phalaṁ jassa divvaṁ ti

kāūṇa ya uvaōgaṁ divvēṇaṁ ōhiṇā visuddhaṇaṁ

muṇiūṇa sucariyaṁ tō karēi aha dēvakaraṇijja

sāsayajiṇapaḍimāṇaṁ pūrya pūyāruhō mahārammaṁ

potthayarayaṇaṁ ca tahā vāēi muhuttamettaṁ tu

aha tiyasamundarīō nijiyamuhayandacandrabimbāō

pīṇughnayasupasāhiyavarathaṇaharabandhuraṅgīō

tivalītaraṅgabhaṅguramajjhavirāyantahārarammāō

muhalarasaṇāhiṇandiyavitthiṇṇaniyambabimbāō

tattatavaṇijjasannihamaṇaharathōrōrujuyalakaliyāō

nahayandasamujōṣiyakummunnayacalaṇasōhāō

gāḍhapariōsapasariyavilāsasiṅgārabhāvarammāō

pecchaï samūsiyāō vammahasarasalliyamaṇāō

kiṁkaragaṇē ya dhaṇiyaṁ aṇuratē divvavihavasaṁpannē

tiyasabhavaṇāi pecchaha sāmiya! iya jaṁpirē laḍahē

tiyasavilayāhi samayaṁ jayasahapaṇāmiyappabhāvāhiṁ

mōhaṇaviyakkhaṇāhiṁ pecchaï tō tiyasabhavaṇāī

vitthiṇṇamaragayasilāsaṁcayasaṁjaṇiyaviyaḍapīḍhāī

maṇirayaṇakhaïyamaṇaharaphalihamaṇibhittijuttāī

vēruliyakhambhaviraïyavicittavarasālibhajjiyasayāī

taha divyakhaggacāmarapajjuttakuḍantarālāī

varavivihadēvacchandayaviraïyapallaṅkasayasanāhāī

parilambiyapaṭṭhuṁsuyamuttāvalijaṇiyasōhāī

tiyasatarukusumamaṇḍiyakuṭṭimasakantabhamaravandrāī

dhūvaghaḍiyāulāī parilambiyarayaṇadāmāī

aha tēsu tiyasamundarinivahēṇa samaṁ purā mukayapuṇṇō

ciṭṭhaï parituṭṭhumaṇō bhuñjantō divvavarabhōē

bhuñjisē sō vi divvē bhōē candāṇaṇē vimāṇammi

surasundarīhiṁ saddhiṁ jahicchiē sāgaramaṇaṇaṁ

guṇasēṇa-aggisammā jaṁ bhaṇiyamihāsi taṁ gayamiyāṇi

sīhā-ṇandā ya tahā jaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ taṁ nisāmēha

atthi ihēva jambuddīvē dīvē aravidēhē khettē aparimiyaguṇanihāṇaṁ tiyasapuravarāṇugāri ujāṇārāmabhūsiyaṁ samatthamēiṇitilaya bhūyaṁ jayaüraṁ nāma nayaraṁ ti. jattha surūvō ujjalanēvatthō kalāviyavakhaṇō lajjāluō mahilāyaṇō, natya ya paradāraparibhōyammi kilīvō, paracchiddāvalōyaṇammi andhō, parāvavāyabhāsaṇammi mūō, paradavvāvaharaṇammi saṁkuciyahatthō, parōvayārakaraṇēkatallicchō purisava ggō. tattha yaṁ nisiyanikkaḍiyāsiniddaliyadariyariuhatthimasthaücchaliyabahalaruhirārattamuttāhalakusumapayaracciyasamarabhūbhibhāō rāyā nāmēṇa purisadattō tti. dēvī ya sē sayalantēurappahāṇā sirikantā nāma. sō imāē saha nirupamē bhōē bhugjim. iō ya sō candāṇa ṇavimāṇāhibaī dēvō ahāuyaṁ pāliūṇa taō cuō sirikantāē gambhē ucavannī tti. divō ya ṇāē suviṇayammi tīē cēva rayaṇīē nikhamasihisihājālasarisakēsarasaḍābhārabhāsurō vimalaphaliha-maṇisilā-nihasa-haṁsa-hāradhavalō āpiṅgalavaṭṭasupasanta lōyaṇō miyaṅkalēhāsarisaniggayadāḍhō pihulamaṇaharavacchatthalō aïtaṇuyamajhabhāō suvaṭṭiyakaṭṭhiṇakaḍiyaḍō āvaliyadīhalaphūlō supaïṭṭhiōrusaṁṭhāṇō ki bahuṇā, sabbasundarāhirāmō sīhakisōragō vayaṇēṇamuyaraṁ pavisamāṇō tti. pāsiūṇa ya taṁ suhaviuddhāra jahāvihiṇā siṭṭhō daïyassa. tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — aṇēyasāmantapaṇivaïyacalaṇajuyalō mahārāyasahassa nivāsaṭṭhāṇaṁ puttō tē bhavissaï. tō sā taṁ paḍisuṇēūṇa jahāsuhaṁ ciṭṭhaï. pattē ya uciyakālē mahāpurisagambhāṇubhāvēṇa jāō sē dōhalō. jahā-dēmi sabasattāṇama bhayadāṇaṁ, dīṇāṇāhakivaṇāṇaṁ ca issariyasaṁpayaṁ, jaïjaṇāṇaṁ ca uvaṭṭhambhadāṇaṁ sabbāyayaṇāṇaṁ ca karēmi pūyaṁ ti. nivēiō ya imō tīē bhattārassa. amahiyajāyaharisēṇaṁ saṁpāḍiō ya tēṇaṁ. tassa saṁpāyaṇēṇa jāō mahāpamōō jaṇavayāṇaṁ. avi ya —

savva cciya dhannāṇaṁ hōi avatthā parokkhārāē

bālasasissa va udaō jaṇassa bhuvaṇaṁ payāsēi

tō jahāsa hēṇa dhammanirayāē parokkhārasaṁpāyaṇēṇaṁ suladdhajammāē aïkantā nava māsā addhahamarāindiyā. tō pasatthē tihi karaṇa-muhutta-jōē sukumālapāṇi-pāyaṁ sayalajaṇamaṇōrahēhiṁ dēvī sirikantā dārayaṁ pasaya tti. nivēiō ranō suhakariyābhihāṇāē dāsiyāē puttajammō. parituṭṭhō rāyā, dinnaṁ ca tīē pāriōsiyaṁ. kārāviyaṁ ca bandhaṇamōyaṇāiyaṁ karaṇijja, pavattō ya nayarē mahāṇandō, sōhāviyā nayarimaggā, pasamāviō rayō kuṅkumajalēṇaṁ, vippaïṇṇāī ruṇṭantamahuyarasaṇāhāī vicittakusumāī, kayāō haṭṭabhavaṇasōhāō, pahabhavaṇēsu samāhayāī maṅgalatūrāī saharisaṁ ca nacciyaṁ rāyajaṇanāgarēhi ti. amhē, tā alaṁkarāvīyaü āsaṇapariggahēṇaṁ imaṁ paēsaṁ ēsō, kīraü sē sajjaṇajaṇāṇa sambandhapāyavavīyabhūyaṁ sāgayaṁ, dijjaü sē sahatthēṇa kālōciyaṁ vasantakusumābharaṇasaṇāhaṁ tambōla ti. kusumāvalīē bhaṇiya-halā! na sakkuṇōmi aïsajjhasēṇa imaṁ ēyassa kāuṁ; tā tumaṁ cēva ettha kālōciyaṁ karēhi tti. etthantarammi ya pattō tamuddēsaṁ kumārō. taō sajjiūṇāsaṇaṁ bhaṇiō piyaṁkarīē — sāgathaṁ raïvirahiyassa kusumacāvassa, iha uvavisa u mahāṇubhāvō. taō sō sapariōsaṁ īsi vihasiūṇa āsi ya ahaṁ ettiyaṁ kālaṁ raïdi rahiō, na uṇa saṁparya ti bhaṇiūṇamuvaviṭhṭhō. uvaṇīyaṁ ca piyaṁkariyāē māhavī kusumamālāsaṇāhaṁ kaladhōyamayataliyāē tambōlaṁ, gahiyaṁ ca tēṇa. etthantarammi ya āgaō kusumāvalījaṇaṇīē āhavaṇanimittaṁ pēsiō saṁbharāyaṇō nāma kannantēuramahalalagō. diṭṭhā ya tēṇa sāṇurāyaṁ apecchantamaddhacchipecchiēhiṁ kumāramavalōentī kusumāvalī. cintiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa. samāgaō mayaṇō raīē, jaï vihī aṇuvattissaï. taō pañcāsanamāgantūṇa kumāramahiṇandiya bhaṇiyaṁ saṁbharāyaṇēṇaṁ. vacchē! kusumāvali! dēvī muttāvalī āṇavēi aïciraṁ kīliyaṁ, mā sarīrakhēdō tē bhavissaï, tā lahuṁ āgantavva ti. taō sā jaṁ ammā āṇavēi tti bhaṇiūṇa sasaṁbhamaṁ kumāramavalōentī niggayā ujjāṇāō, pattā ya kumāraṁ cēva cintayantī niyayagēhaṁ. taō dēviṁ paṇamiūṇamārūḍhā dantavalahiyaṁ. taō kumāraṁ cēva aṇusarantī vimukkadīhanīsāsā samuvaviṭhṭhā pallaṅkasayaṇijjē; visajjiō ya tīē saṁmāṇiuṁ sahīsatthō. aha sēviuṁ payattā sejja aṇavarayamukkanīsāsā. mayaṇasarasalliyamaṇā niyakajjaniyattavāvārā.

nālihaï cittayammaṁ na ya ’ṅgarāyaṁ karēi karaṇijja

nāhilasaï āhāraṁ ahiṇandaï nēya niyabhavaṇaṁ

cirapariciyaṁ pi pāḍhēi nēya muya-sāriyāṇa saṁghāyaṁ

kīlāvēi maṇaharē caḍulē na ya bhavaṇakalahaṁsē

viharaï na hammiyatalē majjaï na ya gēhadīhiyāē u

sārēi nēya vīṇaṁ pattacchejja pi na karēi

na ya kanduēṇa kīlaï bahu mannaï nēya bhūsaṇakalāvaṁ

hariṇi ba jūhabhaṭṭhā aṇusaramāṇī tayaṁ cēva

khaṇaruddhanayaṇapasarā avasā khaṇadhariyadīhanīsāsā

khaṇaruddhadēhaceṭṭā khaṇapiravāya (milāṇa) muhakamalā

etthantarammi tīsē dhāvīē niyasuyā samāṇattā

nāmēṇa mayaṇalēhā bīyaṁ hiyayaṁ va jā tīē

jahā-kīlāsundarujāṇagamaṇakīlāē daḍhaṁ parissantā kusumāvalī, lahuṁ ca tīē aja visajjiyāō sahīō, tā gihiūṇa pavi ralajalasittaṁ tāliyaṣṭaṁ bandhēūṇa kaïvayakappūravīḍagāṇi ubasappāhi ēyaṁ ti. samāēsāṇantaraṁ ca saṁpāiyajaṇaṇivayaṇā rasantamaṇinē urā pattā kusumāvalīsamīvaṁ saharisā mayaṇalēhā. diṭṭhā ya tīē varasayaṇīyamajhagayā gurucintābharanīsahaṁ aṅgaṁ vahantī kusumāvali tti. taō aṇālavaṇamuṇiyasunnabhāvāē vinattā mayaṇalē hāē. sāmiṇi! kimēvamubbiggā viya lakkhīyasi, kinna saṁpannā tē gurudē vayāṇaṁ pūyā? kinna sammāṇiyāō sahīō? kina kayā atthijaṇapaḍivattī? kina gahiō kalākalāvō? kina parituṭṭō tē guruyaṇō? kinna viṇīō tē parivārō? kināṇurattō sahīsatthō? kina saṁjāyaï tē samīhiyaṁ ti? āṇavēu sāmiṇī, jaï aka haṇīyaṁ na hōi. taō kusumāvalīē sasaṁbhama sahatthēga alaē saṁjamē ūga bhaṇiyaṁ. atthi piyasahīē vi nāma ahaṇīya. tā muṇa kusumāvacayaparissamēṇa mē jarakalā viya saṁvuttā, tajaṇiō ya paripīḍēi maṁ pariyāvāṇalō, tannimittā ya viyambhaï aṅgēsu araī, na uṇa kiṁci annaṁ ujvēyakāraṇaṁ lakkhēmi tti. mayaṇalēhāē bhaṇiyaṁ — jaï ēvaṁ, tā geṇha kappūravīḍagāṇi, parivīēmi tē kīlākhē yanīsahaṁ aṅgaṁ. kusumāvalīē bhaṇiya-kiṁ mē ēyāvatyaṁ gayāē kappūravīḍaēhiṁ, alaṁ ca parivīiēṇa. ēhi gacchāmō bālaka.yalīharayaṁ. tattha sajjīkarēhi mē atthuraṇaṁ, jēṇa tahiṁ gayāē avēi ēsō pariyāvāṇalō tti. taō mayaṇalēhāē bhaṇiyaṁ. jaṁ sāmiṇī āṇavēi. gayāō ya sabhavaṇujjāṇatilayabhūyaṁ bālakayalīharayaṁ. sajjīkayaṁ ca sē mayaṇalēhāē sundaramatthuraṇaṁ. nivannā ya tattha kusumāvalī. samappiyāṇi sē kappūravīḍayāṇi. vīsambhakatālāvaṇiyapariōsaṁ ca tāliyaṇṭēṇa vīiumāraddhā mayaṇalēhā. kusumāvalī puṇa aya ṇḍadinnasannahuṁkārā nihuyamukkanīsāsa taṁ cēva hiyayasallabhūyaṁ puṇō puṇō aṇusarantī ciṭṭaï. taō mayaṇalēhāē cintiyaṁ-kiṁ puṇa imīē imassa annahāviyārabhāvassa kāraṇaṁ ti. pucchiyā ya tīē. sāmiṇi! pattē imammi taruṇajaṇāvinbhamullōlasāgarē vasantasamaē ki tumaē ajja kīlāsundaraṁ gacchantīē gayāē vā tattha acchariyaṁ diṭṭhaṁ ti. taō mayaṇāvatthāsahāvaō cēva vāmattaṇēṇaṁ mayaṇassa aṇa bhippēyaṁ pi bhaṇiyaṁ kusumāvalīē-sahi! diṭṭhō maē kīlāsundarujjāṇammi raïvirahiō viva kusumāuhō, rōhiṇī viōiō viva mayalanchaṇō, paricattamaïrō viva kāmapālō, sacīviuttō viva purandarō, taviyatavaṇijasarisavaṇṇō nahamaūhamañjariyacalaṇagulivi bhāō, sūnigūḍhasirāsaṁdhāṇō aṇubaddhapiṇḍiyābhāō, maṇaharamaūrajaṅghō, antōnigūḍhajāṇusaṁdhāṇō, mayaravayaṇāgārajāṇumatthaō, aïsu ndarasusaṁgayōrujuyalō, viulakaḍiyaḍābhōō maṇaharataṇumajjhabhāō, pīṇavisthiṇṇavacchatthalō, unnayasiharaṁparivaṭṭhulabāhujuyalō, aṇu vvaṇakopparavibhāō, pīṇapakōhadēsō, ājāṇulambiyapasatthalēhātribhūsiyakarayalō, āyambanaliṇakararuhō, susamāuttāharapuḍō, sama musaṁgayadhavaladasaṇō, ārattatibhāgadīhavisālalōyaṇō, uttuṅganāsiyāvaṁsō, viulaniḍālabaṭṭō, susamāuttakaṇṇapāsō, kasiṇasusiṇi ddhakuḍilakuntalabhārō, candaṇakayaṅgarāō, vimaladugullaniyaṁsaṇō, mahallamunāhalamāvihūsiyasirōharō, vimalacūḍārayaṇapasāhiyaütti maṅgō, kiṁ bahuṇā jōpaēṇa-rūvaṁ piva rūvassa, lāvaṇṇaṁ piva lāvaṇṇassa, sundaraṁ piva sundērassa, jōvaṇaṁ piva jovvaṇassa, maṇōrahō viya maṇōrahāṇaṁ mahārāyassa puttō sīhakumārō ti. taō muṇiyaannahāviyārabhāvanibandhaṇāē cintiyaṁ mayaṇalēhāē. ṭhāṇē khu sāmiṇīēvīō bhayō aṇurāō. ahavā na kamalāyaraṁ vajjiya lacchī annattha ahiramaha. tassa vi ya bhagavaō aṇaṅgassa viya raī na ēyaṁ vajjiya annā uciya tti. cintiūṇa jaṁpiyamimīē. sāmiṇi! sundarō khu sō kumārō niyaguṇēhiṁ. jahā uṇa ajja subuddhī maē dēvīpēsaṇagayāē rāiṇā saha mantayantō suō, jaï taṁ tahā bhavissaï, tō raïsaṇāhō viya pañcavāṇō sayalamundarō bhavissaï tti. kusumāvalīē bhaṇiyaṁ 'kiṁ suō? ti. tīē bhaṇiyaṁ — ēvaṁ suō. ajjasubuddhiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ — dēva! mahārāyapurisadattassa sīhakumārassa kaē kusumāvaliṁ maggamāṇassa garuō aṇuvandhō. dadaṁ ca tēṇa ettha vuttantē ahaṁ bhaṇiō mhi tahā tumaē kāyavvaṁ, jahā ēsā kusumāvalī sarisaguṇēṇaṁ kumārasīhēṇaṁ saṁjujaï tti. annaṁ ca, dēva! na taṁ vajjiya kusumāvalīē annō uciō tti. etthantarammi lajjā-harisanibbharāē kiṁpi abhaṇaṇīyaṁ avatthantaraṁ pāviūṇa aliyakōvakalaṅkasaṁpāyaṇēṇa candasarisavayaṇāē bhaṇiyaṁ kusumāvalīē. halā! asaṁbaddhapalāviṇi! kimēyamēvaṁ palavasi? mayaṇalēhāē bhaṇiyaṁ — sāmiṇi! kiṁ vā ettha asaṁbaddhaṁ ti. kiṁ aṇuciyā māṇasasaranivāsiṇō rāyahaṁsī varahaṁsassa. taō dēvēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — bhō subuddhi! pahavaï mahārāō mama pāṇāṇaṁ pi. taō subuddhiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ — dēva! juttamēyaṁ ti. ēvaṁ ca jāva vīsatthamantiēṇaṁ ciṭṭhanti, tāva āgayā ujjāṇavālī pallaviyā nāma cēḍī. vinattā ya tīē kusumāvalī. sāmiṇi! dēvī āṇavēi. gaccha tumaṁ dantavalahiyaṁ, jaō āṇattaṁ dēvēṇa ajja savisēsasōhāsaṁpāyaṇābhirāmaṁ sajjēyadhvaṁ bhavaṇujjāṇaṁ, etya kila mahārāyaputtēṇa sīhakumārēṇa āgantavvaṁ ti. taō ēyamāyaṇṇiya jaṁ dēvī āṇavēi tti saharisaṁ gayā dantavalahiyaṁ. iō ya sajjiyaṁ bhavaṇujāṇaṁ. tō ya sāyaraṁ uvaṇimantiūṇa kusumāvalīdaṁsasuyayāē abhippēyāgamaṇō cēva āṇīō sīhakumārō. kaō sē bhōyaṇasaṁpāyaṇāiō uvayārō. pacchā paviṭhṭhō bhavaṇujāṇaṁ. diṭṭhō ya tēṇa gihasāriyārāvamuhalō dakkhālayāmaṇḍavō navavarō viva ārattapallavanivasaṇōvasōhiō asōyanivahō, caḍulakalahaṁsacāliyakaïmalō ya bhavaṇadīhiyānaliṇivaṇasaṇḍō, maïhuyaraparahuyārāvamuhalō ya sahayāranikurambō, kusumamahupāṇamuiyabhamirabhamarālipariyariō ya māhavīlayāmaṇḍavō, nāgavallīnivahasamāliṅgiō ya pūga phalīpayarō suyandhaparimalāvāsiyadisāmaṇḍalō ya kuṅkumagocchaniyarō, mahuramāruyandōlirō ya lōyaṇasuhaō kayalīharaō tti. ṭhiō ya māhavīlayāmaṇḍavammi.

etthantaraṁmi ya mayaṇalēhāē bhaṇiyā kusumāvalī. sāmiṇi! mahāṇubhāvāṇaṁ suyaṇabhāvāō puccaniyattiō cēva sambandhō hōi. sō cēva uciyasaṁbhāsaṇa-phulla-tambōlappayāṇāiṇā payāsijjaï tti. tā pēsēhi sē sarīrapaüttipucchaṇāpubvayaṁ ēyabhima kālē asaṁbhāva ṇijabhāvaṁ sahatyārōviyapiyagumañjarīkaṇṇāvayaṁsa kōmalanāgavallīdalasaṇāhaṁ ca tambōlaṁ ahiṇavuppannāṇi ya kakōlayaphalāī niya kalākōsallapisuṇagaṁ ca kiṁci tahāruvaṁ acchērayabhūyaṁ ti. taō kusumāvalīē bhaṇiyaṁ — jaṁ piyasahi! tē paḍihāyaï, taṁ sayaṁ cēva aṇuciṭṭhaü piyasahī. tō mayaṇalēhāē vaṇiyāsamuggaya cittavaṭṭiyaṁ ca uvaṇēūṇa bhaṇiyā kusumāvalī. sāmiṇi! cittāṇurāī khu sō jaṇō; tā ālihaü ettha sāmiṇō samāṇavarahaṁsayaviuttaṁ tadasaṇūsuyaṁ ca rāyahaṁsiyaṁ ti. taō muṇiyamayaṇalēhābhippāyāē īsi vihasiūṇa ālihiyā tīē jahōvaïṭṭhā rāyahaṁsiyā. mayaṇalēhāē vi ya avatthāsyagaṁ sē lihiyaṁ imaṁ uvari duvaīkhaṇḍaṁ. jahā—

ahiṇavanēhanimbharukkaṇṭhiyanirupacchāyavayaṇiyā

sarasamuṇālavalayaṁgāsammi vi saï mandāhilāsiyā

dāhiṇapavaṇavihuyakamalāyaraē vi adinadiṭṭhiyā

piyasaṁgamakaē na uttammaï kaha vararāyahaṁsiyā

taō ghettūṇa ēvaṁ cittavaṭṭiyaṁ pudhavaṇiyaṁ ca pāhuḍaṁ gayā māhavīlayāmaṇḍavaṁ mayaṇalēhā. kusumāvalīpiyasahi ti pariyaṇāō muṇiūṇa sāyaramabhiṇandiyā kumārēṇaṁ. taō sasaṁbhamaṁ tassa calaṇajuyalaṁ paṇamiūṇa bhaṇiyaṁ mayaṇalēhāē-mahārāyaputta! cittāṇurāī tuma ti taō cittāṇurāiṇīē ahaṁ taha paüttinimittaṁ pēsiyā rāyadhūyāē kusumāvalī ē, tahā sahatyārōviyāṇurāēṇa ya ēsā ahiṇa vuppannā piyaṅgamañjarī niyanāgāllīsamuppannadalamahagyaṁ ca tambōlaṁ ahiṇavuppannāṇi ya kakōlayaphalāī ēyāī ca kila iṣṭavisiṭāṇaṁ dijanti, tā tumaṁ cēva joggō tti kaliūṇa pēsiyāiṁ sāmiṇīē, ēsā vi cittagayā rāyahaṁsiyā pāvaü tē daṁsaṇasuhelli ti, bhaṇi umuraṇīyāiṁ ca ta ē. taō kumārēṇa saharisaya giṇhiūṇa kayā kaṇṇē piyaṅgumañjarī āvīlaṁ mottūṇa, samāṇiyaṁ ca tambōlaṁ, abbha hiyajāmaharisēṇa palōiyā rāyahaṁsiyā, vāiyaṁ ca sē apratyāsyagaṁ uvari lihiyaṁ duvaīkhaṇḍaṁ. taō tambōlasamāṇaṇapajāulavēyaṇayāē mayaṇaviyāraō ya parikhalantavisayamahurakkharaṁ maṇiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa-ahō! sē cittakōsallaṁ. aha kiṁ puṇa daṁsaṇāō cēva muṇijjamāṇā vi avasthā imēṇa puṇaruttōvannāsamettēṇa duvaīkhaṇḍēṇa sūiyā. mayaṇalēhāē bhaṇiyaṁ — mahārāyaütta! na ēsā sāmiṇīē sūiyā, kiṁtu ēyamālihiyaṁ pecchi ūga maē kayaṁ imaṁ dubaīkhaṇḍaṁti. kumārēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — -jujjaï paḍhamalihiyaṁ daṭṭhūṇa sahiyāṇaṁ atyāṇuvāyakaraṇaṁ ti. maggiyā ṇēṇa pattachē jakattarī. kappiō ya nāgavallīdalē rāyahaṁsiyāvatthāṇurūvō vararāyahaṁsaō, phuḍakkharā ya ēsā hiya yasaṁvāyaṇanimittaṁ gaha tti jahā—

mariūṇa na saṁpattī piyāē kaliūṇa ēsa varahaṁsō

dhārēi kaha vi pāṇē aṇukūlanimittanōēṇa

taō niyasirōharāō ōsāriūṇa dinnā imīē tisamuhasārabhūyā pāriōsiyaṁ muttāvalī, samappiyaṁ ca nāgavallīdalaṁ. īsi vihasiūṇa bhaṇiyā ya ēsā, vattavvā tumaē kusumāvalī. jahā-atthi amhāṇaṁ dadaṁ cittāṇurāō, muṇiyaṁ tumaē ima, vinnāyaṁ ca amhēhi pi tē cittakōsallaṁ; tā puṇō ēvaṁ cēva cittāṇurāiṇō jaṇassa niyacittakōsallāisaraṇaṁ āṇandaṁ karijjāsi tti. taō ja mahārāyaüttō āṇavēī tti bhaṇiūṇa paṇāmapubvayaṁ niggayā mayaṇalēhā, pattā ya kusumāvalīsamīvaṁ. āikkhiō tīē jahāvattō vuttantō, samappiyaṁ nāgavallīdalaṁ, diṭṭhō ya kusumāvalīē varahaṁsaō, bāiyā ya gāhā, parituhā hiyaēṇaṁ.

ēvaṁ ca païdiṇaṁ mayaṇasaragōyarāvaḍiya naṇamaṇāṇandayārēhi vijāharī-cakavāya-mahuyarapamuhacittapāyaṣēpaṇēhiṁ pavaḍḍamāṇāṇurā yāṇaṁ jāva vōlenti thēvadiyahā, tāva rāiṇō purisadattassa patthaṇāmahagya dinnā lacchikantanaravaïṇā kumārasī hassa kusumāvali tti. nivēiyaṁ ca ēvaṁ piyaṁkariyāē kusumāvalīē. jahā—

dinnā sīhakumārassa suyaṇu siṭṭhē ya vahalapulayāē

aṅgēsu pariōsō mayaṇō bva viyambhiō tissā

etthantaraṁmi ya athinivahasamīhiyabhahiyadinnadaviṇajāyaṁ vajantamaṅgalatūravāpūriyadisāmaṇḍalaṁ nacantavēsavilayāyaṇuppaṁkabaddha sōha sayalajaṇamaṇāṇandayārayaṁ dōhiṁ ca narindēhiṁ kayaṁ vaddhāvaṇayaṁ ti.

kāūṇa ya tēhi taō vārijamuhō gaṇāviō diyahō

ghōsāviyaṁ puṇō vi ya jahicchiyādāṇamaccatthaṁ

pattami ya taṁmi diṇē tattō kusumāvalī pasatthaṁmi

bandhujubaīhi sahiyā pamakkhaṇakaē muhurtami

āsandiyāē maṇaharadhavaladugullotyayāē rammāē

ṭhaviyā puvābhimuhō ragāvalicaüurantaṁmi

maṇipaṭṭayammi nimiyā calaṇā saṁkantarāyasōhillē

tapphaṁsamuhāsāyaṇarasapallaviē vva vimalammi

vaïcchīuttēṇa ya nahamaūhapaḍibannasalilasaṅkēṇa

pakkhāliumaṇavajjaṁ nimmaviyaṁ tīē nahayammaṁ

rattaṁmuyaparihāṇā ahiyaṁ viyasantavayaṇasayavattā

āsannaravisamāgamapuvadisivahu va ārattā

dubbaṅkura-dahi-akkhayabāvaḍahatyāhiṁ rattavasaṇāhiṁ

jubaīhi avivāhi vihiṇā ya pamakkhiyā tāhi

puppha-phalōdayabhariēhi kaṇayakalasēhi pahāviyā navaraṁ

ūmiṇiyā supasatthaṁ savvaṅgaṁ puṇṇavattēṇaṁ

dinnā ya akkhayā sē gurūhi pariōsabahalapulaēhiṁ

sabyōsahigandhaḍḍē dhaṇakēsē uttimaṅgammi

tattō vi ya sasivayaṇā navara pasāhijiuṁ samāḍhattā

jāvayarasēṇa paḍhamaṁ maṇaharacalaṇā kayā tīsē

niyakantisacchahēṇa ya kuṅkamarāēṇa jaḍiyāō sē

pīṇē thaṇa kalasajuē abhilihiyā pattalēhāō

kālēyamīsacandaṇarasēṇa nimmajjiyaṁ ca muhakamalaṁ

daïō va sāṇurāō kaō ya sē samayaṇō aharō

navasarayakālaviyasiyakuvalayadalakantirāyasōhillaṁ

kayamujalaṁ pi kajjalayaraściyaṁ lōyaṇāṇa juyaṁ

mahumāsalacchiyā iva ummillā sē muhāmma varatilaō

uvariraïyālayāvalialiulabalaēhi pariyariō

aha kalasahāyaḍriyasabhavaṇavāvirayarāyahaṁsāī

calaṇēsu piṇāī maṇaharamaṇinē urāī sē

nahasasimaūhasaṁvaliyarayaṇasaṁjaṇiyaviuṇasa hāhi

paḍibannāō maṇiviḍhiyāhi taha aṅgulīō tti

baddhaṁ ca daïyahiyayaṁ va tīē viyaḍē niyambavimbammi

suraū savavaratūraṁ nimmalamaṇimēhalādāmaṁ

bāhulayāmlēsuṁ raïyāō jaṇamaṇēkaṇāō u

bāhusariyāu tīsē mayaraddhayavāgurāō vva

baddhō ya thaṇaharōvari maṇaharavarapaümarāyadalaghaḍi ō

pabarō pabaṁgabandhō niyambasaṁsattō taha ya

muttāhārō thaṇabaddhasaṁgasaṁjāyakāmarāō ba

kaṇṭhamavalambiūṇaṁ nīvi sē phusiumāḍhattō

kaṇṭhammi vimalamaṇaharamottiyadusurullayaṁ piṇaddhaṁ sē

kuṅkumakayarāēmu ya savaṇēsuṁ rayaṇacakkalayāō

ujjōiyaṁ ca dhaṇiyaṁ tissā vayaṇaṁ miyaṅkalēhāē

dhavalakuḍilāē pavaraṁ pōsalacchīē va suhāē

ghaṇakasiṇakuḍilamaṇaharasirōruhugdhāyakaliyasōhillē

vimalaṁ cūḍārayaṇaṁ nimiyaṁ sē uttimaṅgammi

paḍhamaṁ dīsihii imā mottūṇa mamaṁ ti rayaṇachāyāē

paḍivanamaccharāē ba otyayaṁ tīē savvaṅgaṁ
