ēvaṁ ca jāva kusumāvalī pasāhijaï, tāva pasāhaṇaniuṇavāravilayāhiṁ pasāhiyammi sīhakumārē nivēiyaṁ rāiṇō purisadattassa gahi yasaṁkucchāēhiṁ muṇiya jōisasatthasārēhiṁ jōisiēhiṁ āsanaṁ pasatyaṁ hatthaggahaṇamuhurta ti. taō ya sīhakumārō naravaïsamāṇattapari yaṇapavattiō vajantamaṅgalatūravādūriyasayaladisāmaṇḍalō pavaṇapaṇacantadhayabaḍugghāyasundarahavarārūḍharāyalīyapariyariō maṇaharanahō kkhārakusalāvarōhasundarīvendrēṇa'ñcantaruddharāyamaggō dhavalapasāhiyakarivarārūḍhō miyaṅkasēṇāmarasēgakumārapariyariō mahusarayasaṁgaō vva kusumāuhō sāhilāsamavalōijamāṇō pāsāyamālātalagayāhiṁ purasundarīhiṁ pattō salīla vivāhamaṇḍavaṁ ti. dhariō ya tassa dārē visēsujalanēvacchēṇaṁ gahiyagyasakārēṇaṁ ammayājaṇēṇaṁ maggiyō āyārimayaṁ ti. tō harisavasupphullalōyaṇō jāiyambhahiyaṁ dāūṇa ōiṇṇō karivarāō. bhaggā ya sē rayaṇakañcīsaṇāhēṇaṁ sōpaṇṇamusalēṇaṁ bhiuḍi tti. taō maṇḍavatalammi jaṇanivahaṁ niru mbhiya nīō samāgamamundarīhiṁ varō.

ciṭṭhaï ya jattha siyavara dugullapacchāiyāṇaṇā bahuyā. sarayambhacandamaṇḍalasaṁchāiyakōmuinisi vva. kārāviō salīla avirubbhantāi kōuyāī ca. tā jāiō muhacchaviphēḍāvaṇiyaṁ ca sahiyāhi.

taō īsi vihasiūṇa mamaṁ cēva ēvaṁ sakaja ti bhaṇiya dinamāyārimayaṁ. phēḍiyā muhacchavī. divā ya tēṇa asōyapalla vakayāvayaṁsā īsiviyasantavayaṇakamalā sajjhasaharisanibbharā maṇōharassavi maṇahāriṇaṁ kiṁpi tahāvihaṁ divvaṁ vilāsavinbhamamaṇuha vanti kusumāvali ti.

pāṇiggahaṇaṁ ca taō pāraddhaṁ gīyamaṅgalugghāyaṁ

bandhavahiyayāṇandaṁ annonnabaddharāyāṇaṁ

hatthā paḍhamaṁ ciya kālavittharaṁ visahiuṁ acāentā

tīē varassa ya ghaḍiyā nimmalanahayandakiraṇēhi

vettaṇa tēṇa paḍhamaṁ maüē hiyayammi sāṇurāyammi

gahiyā taō karammi ya paviyambhiyasēyasalilammiḥ

ghettaṇa ya tēṇa karē maṇaharakacchantarāu āṇīyā

paparamahacāurantaṁ tiyasavahū suravimāṇaṁ va

kaṇayama ujjalavarapaümarāyapajjattadaṇḍiyāraïyaṁ

raïyadugullaviyāṇayaparilambiyamōtiōūlaṁ

ōūlalaggamaragayamaūhahariyāyamāṇasiyacamaraṁ

siyacamaradaṇḍacāmīyarappahāpiñjarahāyaṁ

adāyagayavirāyantarammavarapakkhasundarīvayaṇaṁ

varapakkhasundarīkkhaṇajaṇiyabahupakkhapariōsaṁ

pariōsapayaḍarōmañcabandisaṁghāyakaliya pērantaṁ

pērantavirahayāmalavicittamaṇitārayānivaha

tārayanivahapasāhiyatōraṇamuhanimiyasuddhasasilēhaṁ

sasilēhāvijjōiyavittharasiyamaṇḍavanahaṁ tu

avalaggō ya saharisaṁ maṇibhūsaṇakiraṇabhāsurasarīrō

udayagiri piva sō cāurantayaṁ diyasanāhō bva

kusumāvalīē rāyantavimalasiyavaradugullavasaṇāē

paviyasiyavayaṇakamalāē divasalacchīē va samēō

vahuyāē tattha dhūmēṇa varamuhaṁ pecchasu tti va bhaṇantā

bāhatthēvā ōṇayamuhīē pārasu sē paḍiyā

etthantarammi ya pāraddhō jaṇāṇamuvayārō. dijanti mahamahentagandhāiṁ vilēvaṇāī, ruṇṭantamahuyarasaṇāhāī kusumadāmāī aïsura higandhagandhiṇō paḍavāsā, kappūravīḍayapahāṇāī tambōlāiṁ, dugulla-dēvaṅgapaṭṭa-cīṇa-ddhacīṇāī pavaravatthāī, kēūra-hāra-kuṇḍala tuḍiyappamuhā āharaṇavisēsā, turaka-balhīya-kambōya-vajarāiāsakaliyāī ghōḍayavandrāī, bhada-mandavaṁsappamuhā ya gayavisēsā.

etthantarammi jalaṇē ghaya-mahu-lāyāhi aha huṇijantē

pāraddhaṁ ca bahu-varaṁ bhamiuṁ tō maṇḍalāiṁ tu

paḍhamammi vahūpiuṇā dinnaṁ hiṭṭhēṇa maṇḍalavarammi

bhārāṇa sayasahassaṁ aghaḍiyarūvaṁ suvaṇṇassa

bīyammi hāra-kuṇḍala-kaḍisuttayatuḍiyasāramāharaṇaṁ

taïyammi thāla-kacōlamāiyaṁ ruppabhaṇḍaṁ tu

dinnaṁ ca caütthammi vahūē pariōsapayaḍa pulaēṇaṁ

piuṇā muṭhṭha mahagdhaṁ cēlaṁ nāṇāpayāraṁ ti

purisadattēṇa vi ya ranā savihavāṇurūvō accantapasāyamahagghō kō jaṇāṇamuvayārō, dinnaṁ ca vimalamaṇi-rayaṇa-mutsāhala saṇāhaṁ vahuyāē aṇagdhēyamāharaṇaṁ.

ēvaṁ vittē vivāhamahūsavē kālakamēṇa pavaḍḍamāṇāṇurāyaṁ sayalajaṇasalāhaṇijjaṁ visayasuhamaṇuhavantāṇaṁ aïkantā aṇēgē varisalakkhā. annayā ya āsaparivāhaṇanimittaṁ gaēṇa kumārasīhēṇa diṭṭhō nāgadēvujāṇē bahuphāmuē paēsē aṇēyasamaṇaparivāriō khamā-madana-java mutti-tava-saṁjama-sacca-sōyā-kiñcaṇa-bambhacēraguṇanihī paḍhamajōvaṇatyō rūvāiguṇajuttō saṁpuṇṇa duvālasaṅgī sasissāṇaṁ suttassa atthaṁ kahēmāṇō dhammaghōsō nāma āyariō tti. tō taṁ daṭṭhūṇa taṁ paï aīva bahumāṇō jāō. cintiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa. dhannō khu ēsō, jō saṁsāravirattabhāvō sayalasaṅgacāī paramaparōvayāraniraō ēvaṁ vaṭṭaï tti. tā gantūṇa ēyassa samīvaṁ pucchāmi ēyaṁ-kiṁ puṇa imassa maṇō. havalaliyasamayavattiṇō nivvēyakāraṇaṁ jahaṭṭhiyaṁ ca dukkhasaṁkulaṁ ca saṁsāraṁ ti. taō dūrāō cēva ōyariūṇa jaccavollāhakisōrāō gō tassa samīvaṁ. paṇamiō ya dhammaghōsō. ahiṇandiō ya bhagavayā dhammalāhēṇa. taō vandiūṇa sēsasāhuṇō bhattini bharamuva viṭṭhō sahāyasundarē guruṇō pāyamūlē. nivvaḍiyasaṁvēgasāraṁ pucchiō ya ṇēṇa bhayavaṁ dhammaghōsō. bhaya! kiṁ tē sayalaguṇasaṁpayākula harassa vi īisō nivvēō, jēṇa imaṁ ayālē cēva samaṇattaṇaṁ paḍivanōsi? tō bhayavayā bhaṇiyaṁ — bhō mahāsāvaya! natthi idāṇimagālō sāmaṇṇassa. kiṁ na pahavaï ayālē nijiyasurāsurō sayalamaṇōrahasēlavajjāsaṇī piyajaṇaviōēkaparamahēū vibuhajaṇasaṁvēgavaḍaṇō maccu tti. annaṁ ca-mahāsāvaya! sōhaṇabhāvāō caramakālē vi jaï sēvijjaï dhammō, sō ciya paḍhamaṁ kimajuttō? rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ — bhayavaṁ! nō ajuttō, kiṁ tu nānimittō nivvēō tti nivvēyakāraṇaṁ pucchāmi. bhayavayā bhaṇiyaṁ — saṁsārō cēva nivvēyakāraṇaṁ, tahavi puṇō visē saō ōhināṇiniyacariyakahaṇaṁ ti. rāiṇā bhaṇiya-bhayavaṁ! kērisaṁ ōhināṇinīyacariyakahaṇaṁ ti? bhayavayā bhaṇiyaṁ. suṇa atthi ihēva vijaē rāyaüraṁ nāma nayaraṁ. tanivāsī ahaṁ bhavasarūvō cēva tavirattamaṇō ciṭṭhāmi jāva, āgaō aṇayasamaṇa sāmī thēvadiyahuppannōhināṇōvaladdhapuṇṇapāvō amaraguttō nāma āyariō tti! jāō ya lōē lōyavāō ahō ayaṁ mahātavassī khīṇāsabadārō samuppannaōhināṇanayaṇō jahaṭṭhiyadhammadēsaṇāladdhisaṁpannō tti. tō tanayarasāmī arimaraṇō nāma rāyā, annō ya nayarajaṇavaō niggaō tassa dēsaṇa ḍiyāē, saṁpattō sē pāyamūlaṁ. vandiō bhayavaṁ naravaïṇā nayara jaṇavaēṇa ya. ahiṇandiō ya dhammalāhēṇa bhayavayā naravaī nayarajagavaō ya. uvaviṭṭhō ya guruvayaṇabahumāṇamahāyō ahāphāsuē dharaṇibaḍhē rāyā nayarajaṇavaō ya. pucchiō ya bhayavaṁ ahāvihāraṁ rāiṇā. aṇusāsiō ya tēṇaṁ. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ — bhaya! saṁpannaṁ tē bhūyabharissavattamāṇasthagāhagaṁ ōhi. nāṇaṁ. tā karēhi mē anuggahaṁ. āikkha niyayacariyaṁ, kayā kahaṁ vā bhayavayā saṁpattaṁ sāsayasivasōvapāyavēkabīyaṁ sammattaṁ, dēsavi raī vā, iha annabhavēmu vā sāmaṇṇaṁ tti. bhayacyā bhaṇiyaṁ. suṇa atthi ihēva vijaē campāvāsaṁ nāma nayaraṁ. tatthāīyasamayammi sudhaṇū nāma gāhāvaī hotyā, tassa dhariṇī dhaṇasirī nāma, tāṇa ya sōmābhihāṇā ahaṁ suyā āsi. saṁpattanovyaṇā ya dinā tannayaranivāsiṇō nandasatthavāhaputtassa ruddadēvassa. kaō ya ṇēṇa vivāhō. jahāṇurūvaṁ visayamuhamaṇuhavāmō tti. jāva tattha ahāva.ppavihārēṇa viharamāṇā vivihatavakhaviya dēhā muyarayaṇapasāhiyā rūvi vva sāsa ṇadēvayā samāgayā bālacandā nāma gaṇiṇi tti. diṭṭhā ya sā maē sasurakulāō māikulamahigacchantīē vihāraniggamapaēsē. taṁ ca mē da?ṇa samuppannō pamōō, viyasiyaṁ lōyaṇēhiṁ, paṇaṭṭhuṁ pāvēṇaṁ, usasiyamaṅgēhi, viyambhiyaṁ dhammacittēṇaṁ. taō maē nāidūraō cēva viṇa yaraïyakarayalañjalīē sabahumāṇamabhivandiyā bhayavaī. tīē vi ya dinō sayalamuhasassa bīyabhūō dhammalābhō tti. jāyāō ya mē taṁ paï aīva bhattipīīō. pucchiō ya maē bhayaīē paḍissaō, sāhiō sāhuṇīhi. taō aha jahōciēṇa vihiṇā pajjuvāsiuṁ pavattā. sāhiō mē bhayavaīē kammavaṇadāvāṇalō dukkhasēlavajjāsaṇī sivasuhaphalakappapāyavō vīyarāgadēsiō dhammō. taō kamma kkhaōvasabhāvaō pattaṁ sammattaṁ, bhāviō jiṇadēsiō dhammō, virattaṁ ca mē bhavacārayāō cittaṁ. tamō ya sō ruddadēvō kammadōsēṇa paōsaṁ kāumāraddhō. bhaṇiyaṁ ca tēṇa. paricaya ēyaṁ visayasuhavigyakāriṇaṁ dhammaṁ. taō maē bhaṇiyaṁ. alaṁ visayasuhēhiṁ. aïcaścalā jīvalōyaṭṭhiī, dāruṇō ya vivāō visayapamāyassa. tēṇa bhaṇiya-viyāriyā tuma, mā diṭṭha paricaïya adiḍhē raī karēhi. maē bhaṇiyaṁ kimettha di8 nāma? pasugaṇasāhāraṇā imē visayā, pañcakkhōvalabbhamāṇasuhaphalō ya kahaṁ adiṭṭhō dhammō tti? taō sō ēvamahila ppamāṇō ahiyayaraṁ paōsamāvannō. pariccattō ya tēṇa maē saha saṁbhōgō. variyā ya nāgadēvābhihāṇassa satthavāhassa dhr̥yā nāgasiri nāma kannagā, na saṁpāiyā tāyava humāṇēṇaṁ nāgadēvasatyavāhēṇa. ruddadēvēṇa cintiyaṁ. na ēyāē jīvamāṇīē ahaṁ dāriyaṁ lahāmi, tā vāvāēmi ēyaṁ. taō māyācariēṇaṁ kahiṁci ghaḍagayamāsīvisaṁ kāūṇa saṁṭhaviō ēgadēsē ghaḍaō. aïkantē paōsasamaē saṁpattē ya kāmiṇijaṇasamāgamakālē bhaṇiyā haṁ tēṇa. uvaṇēhi mē imāō navaghaḍāō kumumamālaṁ ti. taō ahaṁ tassa māyācariyamaṇavabujjhamāṇā gayā ghaḍasamaüvaṁ. avaṇīyaṁ tassa duvāraḍekkaṇaṁ dharaṇimāuliṅgaṁ. taō hatthaṁ chōṇa gahiō bhuyaṅgō. ḍakkā ahaṁ tēṇa. taō taṁ sasaṁbhamaṁ ujjhiūṇa sajjhasabhayavēviraṅgī samallīṇā tassa samīyaṁ. ḍakā bhuyaṅgamēṇaṁ ti siha ruddadēvassa. niyaḍīpahāṇō ya āulīhaō rudadēvō. pāraddhō tēṇa niratyaō cēva kōlāhalō. etthantarammi ya sīiyaṁ mē aṅgēhi, viyaliyaṁ sandhīhiṁ, uvyattiyaṁ pirva hiyaēṇaṁ, bhamiyaṁ piva pāsāyantarēṇa, parivattiyaṁ piva puhavīē, avasā ahaṁ nivaḍiyā dharaṇivaḍhē. aō paramaṇācikkhaṇīyamavatthantaraṁ pāviūṇa pubbasammattāṇubhāvaō caïūṇa dēhaṁ sōhammē kappē līlāvayaṁsaē varavimāṇē paliōvamahiī dēvattāē uvavaśnō mhi. tattha ya pavaraccharā parigaō divvē bhōē uvabhuñjāmi jāva, ruddadēyō vi taṁ nāgadattasatyavāhadhūyaṁ pariṇīya tīē saddhiṁ jahāṇurūvē bhōē uvabhuciūṇa kāla. māsē kālaṁ kāūṇa rayaṇappabhāē puḍhavīē khaṭṭakkhaḍābhihāṇē naraē paliōvamāū cēva nāragō uvavannō tti. taō ahaṁ ahāuyaṁ aṇupāli ūṇa cuō samāṇō ihēva vijaē suṁsumārē raṇṇē suṁsumāragirimmi hatthittāē upavanō, saṁpattō ya kalabhagāvatthaṁ. etthantarammi ya iyarō vi narayāō uvvahiūṇa tammi cēva girivarē sugapakkhittāē ubavannō tti. aïkantō ya sisubhāvaṁ, diṭṭhōya ahaṁ tēṇa tammi cēva girivarē sahāvaramaṇīēsu nalavaṇēsu karēṇusaṁghāyaparigaō salīlaṁ paribhamantō tti. taō maṁ dardūṇa punvabhavabbhāsāō ukkaḍakammōdayāō ya samuppannō mamōpari vērapariṇāmō. cintiyaṁ ca tēṇaṁ-kahaṁ puṇa ēsa kuñjarō imāō bhōgasuhāō vaściyacō tti. uvāē gavēsiumā raddhō. annayā līlāraī nāma vijāharō, sō miyaṅkasēṇassa bijjāharassa bhaïṇiṁ candalēhābhihāṇiṁ avahariūṇa tabbhaēṇēvāgaō tamuddēsaṁ. bhaṇiō ya tēṇa sō sugō-ahaṁ etya girinigubjē ciṭṭhāmi āgamissaï ya ettha ēgō vijjāharō, tō na tumaē tassa ahaṁ sāhiyanvō gaō ya sō mamaṁ sāhiyabbō, taō tē kiṁci paḍirūvamukkhāraṁ karissāmi, ēvaṁ kaē muṭhṭha mē uvakayaṁ ti jaṁpiūṇamōiṇṇō viyaḍataḍā bhōgasaṁṭhiya giriniguja. iyarō vi tammi cēvuddēsē nāraṅgapāyavasāhāgaē nīḍē ciṭṭhaï, jāva āgantūṇa gaō miyaṅkasēṇō. etthantarammi ya karēṇupariṁgaō ahaṁ āgaō tamuddēsaṁ. taō maṁ daṇaṁ cintiyaṁ sugēṇa-atthi iyāṇi avasarō mē samīhiyassa. taō niyaḍibahulēṇa sajāyāē sahābhimantiūṇa mama savaṇagōyarē bhaṇiyaṁ — sundari! suyaṁ maē bhayavaō siṭṭhamaharisissa samīvē, jahā ihaṁ suṁsumārapancaē savvakāmiyaṁ nāma paḍaṇamatthi; jō jaṁ abhilasiū paḍaï, sō takkhaṇēṇa cēva taṁ pāvaï tti. tō maē pucchiyaṁ-bhaya! kahiṁ puṇa tamuddēsa? tēṇa sāhiyaṁ-jahā imassa sālataruvarassa vāmapāsēṇaṁ ti. tā alaṁ imiṇā tiriyabhāvēṇa, ēhi, vijāharapaṇihāṇaṁ kāūṇaṁ tahiṁ nivaḍāmō. paḍissuyaṁ ca mē imaṁ jāyāē. gayāiṁ tamuddēsaṁ, kō paṇihī, niyaḍiyāī girinigulē, sāhiyaṁ līlāraïṇō. samuppaïō ya saha candalēhāē gayaṇayalamalaṁkarentō līlāī. diṭṭhō ya amhēhi. satruppannā mē cintā-ahō sabyakāmiyapaḍaṇāṇubhāvō, jamēyaṁ mugamihuṇayaṁ kayavijjāharapaṇihāṇamiha nivaḍiūṇa takkhaṇā cēva vijjāharamihuṇayaṁ jāyaṁ. tā alaṁ amhāṇa pi imiṇā tiriyabhāvēṇa. taō dēvapaṇihiṁ kāūṇa nivaḍāmō ettha amhē vitti. ēvaṁ ca saṁpahāriūga paṇihiṁ kāūṇa niyaḍiyā tattha amhē. etthantarammi ya uppaïyaṁ suyamihuṇayaṁ, na lakkhiyamamhē hiṁ. taō saṁcuṇiyaṅgōvaṅgō ahaṁ kilē samaṇuhaviūṇa aāmanijjarāē kamma khaviūṇa uvavannō kusumasēharābhihāṇē vaṁtarabhommanayarē dēsūṇapaliōvamāū catarō tti. tattha ya udārē bhōē bhuñjāmi jāva, iyarō vi suyattāē mari ūṇa rayaṇappabhāē cēva puḍhavīē lōhiyāmuhābhihāṇē naraē samuppannō dēsūṇapaliōcamaṭṭiī nāragō ti. taō ahaṁ ahāuyamaṇupā liūṇa cuō samāṇō ettha cēva vidēhē annammi vijaē cakavālaürē nayarē appaḍihayacakarasa satyavāhassa sumaṅgalāē bhāriyāē kucchisi puttattāē uvavanō tti. jāō ya uciyasamaēṇa, païṭāviyaṁ ca mē nāmaṁ cakkadēvō, pattō ya bālabhāvaṁ. etthantarammi ya sō suyanāragō naragāō ubaṭṭiūṇa tattha cēva nayarē sōmasammassa nivapurōhiyassa nandivaddhaṇābhihāṇāē bhāriyāē kucchisi puttattāē uvavannō tti, jāō ya kālakkamēṇaṁ, païṭāviyaṁ ca sē nāmaṁ jannadēvō, pattō ya kumārabhāva. etthantarammi ya jāyā mama tēṇa saha pīī sabbhāvaō, tassa uṇa kaïyavēṇaṁ. taō pubbabhavabhatthakammadōsēṇaṁ ujjuyassa vi aṇujjuō mama saṁpayāmaccharī vaścaṇāchalēṇa chidāī gavēsiumāraddhō. alahamāṇēṇa ya paricintiyamaṇēṇa-na ēsō ēvaṁ chaliuṁ pāriyaï, tā etya uvāō. candaṇasatthavāhagēhaṁ musiūṇa ēyassa gēhē ritthaṁ muyāmi, pacchā ya kēṇaï uvāēṇaṁ nivēiūṇa rāiṇō saṁpayāō bhaṁsaïssaṁ ti. aṇuciṭṭhiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa jahāci ntiyaṁ. uvaṇēūṇa ya mē gēhē ritthaṁ bhaṇiyamaṇēṇa-vayaṁsa! ēyaṁ payattēṇa saṁgōvāvēsu tti. maē vi ya akālāṇavaṇajāyasaṅkaga aṇi cchamāṇēṇāvi ēyassa dakkhiṇṇabahulayāē saṁgōviyaṁ ti. pabattō ya nayarē jaṇarayō, jahā muṭṭhuṁ candaṇasatyavāhagēhaṁ ti. taō āsa ḍiyaṁ mē hiyaēṇaṁ-nr̥ṇamēyaṁ ēvaṁ bhavissaï tti. gaō jannadēvasamīvaṁ, pucchiō ya sō maē-kahamēyaṁ vavatyiyaṁ ti. tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — mā annahā samatthēhi. tāya bhaēṇa maē ēyaṁ bhavaō samappiyaṁ, na puṇa annaha tti. taō avagayā mē saṅkā. patthantarammi ya jāṇāviyaṁ canda. ṇasatyavāhēṇa rāiṇō, jahā dēva! gēhaṁ mē muṭṭhuṁ ti. kimavahariya ti pucchiyaṁ rāigā. nivēiyaṁ candaṇēṇaṁ, lihāviyaṁ ca rāiṇā, bhaṇiyaṁ caṇēṇa-arē! āghōsēha ḍiṇḍi mēṇaṁ, jahā-muṭṭhuṁ candaṇasatthavāhagēhaṁ, abahariyamēyaṁ ristha nāyaṁ. tā jassa gēhē kēṇaï vavahārajōēṇa taṁ ritthaṁ ritthadēsō vā samāgaō, sō nivēēu rāiṇō caṇḍasāsaṇasma. aṇivēiōvalambhē ya rāyā sabadhaṇāva hārēṇa sarīradaṇḍēṇa ya nō kha missaï tti. taō payaṭṭamāghōsaṇaṁ. aïkkantē ya taïmmi gaēsu pañcasu diṇēsu jāṇāviyaṁ jannadēvēṇa rāiṇō. jahā-dēva! na juttaṁ cēva mittadōsapayāsaṇaṁ, kiṁ tu paralōyaïhalōyaviruddha sēviṇā ahiyāyaraṇēṇa attaṇō vi ya amittēṇa alaṁ mē mittēṇaṁ. na uvekkhi yavvaṁ jāṇantēṇaṁ rāyajaṇāhiyaṁ. aō īisa pi dēvassa nivēīyaï. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ — bhaṇāu ajō. jannadēvēṇa bhaṇiya-dēva! suṇa. suyaṁ maē cakadēvāsannapariyaṇāō, jahā imaṁ candaṇasatyavāhagēhaṁ cakkadēvēṇa muṭṭhuṁ, saṁgōviyaṁ ritthaṁ niyayagēhē. ēvaṁ sōūṇa dēvō pamāṇaṁ ti. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ — aja! asaṁbhāvaṇijamēyaṁ, kulappasuō kkhu sō, tā kahaṁ imaṁ añcantaviruddhaṁ karissaï. jannadēvēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — dēva! natthi annāṇalobhavasagāṇamasaṁbhāvaṇijja. kō ya dōsō kulassa, kiṁ na habanti surabhikusumēsu kimiō. tā nirū vāvēhi tāva kēṇaï payārēṇa tassa gēhaṁ ti. tō jutta mēya ti cintiūṇa samāṇattaṁ caṇḍasāsaṇēṇa karaṇaṁ. bhaṇiyā ya kāraṇiyā nayaramahantagēhiṁ saha vettūṇa candaṇasatthavāha bhaṇḍāriyaṁ palōēha cakadēvassa gēhē taṁ paṇa8 ritthaṁ ti. taō kimēiṇā asaṁbhāvaṇijjēṇaṁ, ahavā āēsagāriṇō amhē tti mantiūṇa, mēlaviya nayaramahantagē ghettūṇa candaṇasatyavāhabhaṇḍāri jāmamettē vāsarē samāgayā mē gēhaṁ pahāṇanayarajaṇāhiṭṭhiyā kāraṇiya tti. pucchiō ya tēhiṁ aī-satyavāhaputta! na tē kiṁci kēṇaï ēvaṁjāiyaṁ ritthaṁ saṁvavahāravaḍiyāē uvaṇīyaṁ ti. tō maē asaṁjāyasaṅkēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — nahi nahi tti. tēhiṁ bhaṇiyaṁ — na tara kuppiyavvaṁ rāyasāsaṇamiṇaṁ, jaṁ tē gēhamava lōiyavvaṁ ti. maē bhaṇiyaṁ — na etya avasarō kōbassa, payāparirakkhaṇanimittaṁ samārambhō dēvassa. taō paviṭṭhā mē gēhaṁ saha nayaravuḍḍēhi rāyapurisā. avalōiyaṁ ca tēhiṁ nāgāpayāraṁ daviṇajāyaṁ, diṭṭhaṁ ca payattahāviyaṁ candananāmaṅkiyaṁ hiraṇṇavāsaṇaṁ, nīṇiyaṁ bāhi, daṁsiyaṁ candaṇabhaṇḍāriyassa. abalōiūṇa sadukkhamiva bhaṇiyaṁ ca tēga-aṇuharaï tāva ēyaṁ, na uṇa nissaṁsayaṁ viyāṇāmi tti. kāraṇiēhi bhaṇiya-vāēhi tāva avahariyanivēyaṇāpattagaṁ, kiṁ tatya imaṁ īisaṁ abhilihiyaṁ na pa ti. vāiyaṁ pattagaṁ, diṭṭhamabhilihiyaṁ sajjhasī bhūyā nāyarakāraṇiyā. bhaṇiyaṁ ca tēhi — satthavāhaputta! kuō tuha imaṁ. tō maē vi cintiyaṁ — kaha sambhāvaṭhāviyaṁ mittanāsaṁ payā sēmi. mā nāma tēṇāvi karhi ci ēsō ēvaṁ cēva samāsāiō bhavē. tā kahaṁ niyapāṇabahumāṇāō mittapāṇē paricayāmi tti cintiūṇa bhaṇiyaṁ maē— niyagaṁ cēva ēyaṁ ti. tēhi bhaṇiyaṁ — kahaṁ candaṇanāmaṅkiyaṁ? maē bhaṇiyaṁ — na yāṇāmō, kahiṁci vāsaṇaparāvattō bhavi ssaï. tēhiṁ bhaṇiya-kisaṁkhiyaṁ kiṁ vā hiraṇṇajāyametthaṁ ti? maē bhaṇiyaṁ — na muṭhṭha mumarāmi, sēī cēva jōēha. kāraṇiēhi bhaṇiyaṁ — vāēha pattagaṁ, kiṁdaviṇajuttaṁ kiṁsaṁkhiyaṁ vā taṁ candaṇasatyavāhavāsaṇaṁ ti. vāiyaṁ pattagaṁ jāva dīṇāradaviṇajuttaṁ dasasahassasaṁkhiyaṁ ca. taō chōḍāviyamaṇēhiṁ miliō pattagatthō. vimhiyā nāgarakāraṇiyā. paricintiyaṁ ca tēhiṁ. kahaṁ appaḍihayacakkasatthavāhaputē maē taṁ cēvāṇucintiūṇa taṁ cēva sihaṁ ti. tēhiṁ ciya dhiratthu dēvassa tti bhaṇiūṇa mantiyaṁ. anaṁpi tē na kiṁci parasantiya gēhē ciṭṭhaï? maē bhaṇiya-na kiṁci. taō tēhiṁ pattagaṁ vāiūṇa savisēsamavalōiyaṁ mē gēhaṁ, diṭṭhaṁ ca jahāvāiyaṁ niravasēsa mēva ritthaṁ etthantarammi ya kuviyā mamōvari ārakkhigā. nīō tēhiṁ naravaïsamīvaṁ. sāhiō buttantō caṇḍasāsaṇassa. bhaṇiō mhi rāiṇā. satyavāhaputta! vināubhayalōyamaggō tuma, tā na tui ēyamērisamasāhucariyamasaṁbhāvaṇijja saṁbhāvēmi tti. tā kahēhi tātra, paramatyō tti? taō maē taṁ cēva cintiūṇa bāhajalabhariyalōyaṇēṇaṁ na kiṁpijī pēyaṁ naravaïpuraō tti. taō rāiṇā samuppannāsaṁ kēṇāvi tāyabahumāṇō asarisaṁ vayaṇamabhāsiūṇa kayatthaṇaṁ cākāūṇa nidhisaō samāṇattō mhi, nīgiōya rāyapurisēhiṁ nayarāō, mukkō ya nayaradēvayāvaṇasamīvē. paḍiniyattā rāyapurisā. samuppanā ya mē cintā-kimēdahamettaparibhavabhāyaṇēṇaṁ aja vi jīviēṇaṁ. tā ēyamni nayaradēvayāvaṇasamāsannē naggōhapāyavē ukkalambēmi appāṇaṁ ti. cintiūṇa payaṭṭō nagōhasamīyaṁ. etthantarammi ya kahiṁci ābhōiūṇa imaṁ vaïyaramōhiṇā samuppannā mamōvari nayaradēvayāē aṇukampā. āvēsiūṇa rāyajaṇaṇi sāhiyaṁ jahaṭṭhiyamēva ēvaṁ tīē rāiyō. bhaṇiō ya rāyaḥ-imāē maïlaṇāē amugammi nayara jāṇāsannē naggōhapāyavē umbandhaṇēṇa attāṇayaṁ paricaïuṁ vavasiō cakka dēvō. tā lahuṁ nivārēhi, taṁ sammāṇiūṇa ya pavēsēhi nayaraṁ ti. taō kōhanēhāulayāē saṁkiṇaṁ rasamaṇuhavantō rāyā arē geṇhaha durāyāraṁ jannadēvaṁ ti āisiūṇa pahāṇavārūyārūḍhō samaṁ ahāsannihiyapariyaṇēṇaṁ turiyaturiyaṁ nigaō nayarāō, pattō ya nayarujāṇaṁ. diṭṭhō ya ahaṁ rāiṇā naggōhapāyavasāhāgaō uttarīyanibaddhapāsammi ḍhōiyāē sirōharāē attāṇayaṁ pavāhiukāmō tti. taō sō dūraō cēva saṁbhamāisayaniyaḍiyasāraṁ bhō cakkadēva! mā sāhasaṁ mā sāhasaṁ ti bhaṇamāṇō sigṣayaratajjiyāē vārūyāē samallīṇō pāyavasa mīvaṁ. sayamēva avaṇīō pāsaō, geṇhiūṇa ya karammi ṭhāviō ahaṁ tēṇa vārūyāpaṭṭiyāē. bhaṇiō ya sabahumāṇaṁ-bhō satthavāhaputta! juttaṁ nāma bhavaō maē vi pucchi yassa sambhāvāsāhaṇaṁ?. taō maē cintiyaṁ-hanta kimēyaṁ ti, payāsiyaṁ bhavissaï kēṇaï mittagujjhaṁ.

etthantarammi ya bhaṇiyaṁ rāiṇā-bhō sasthavāhaputta! sāhiō mama ēsa vaïyarō ambaṁ pavisiūṇa bhayavaīē nayaradēvayāē, jahā nidōsō tumaṁ, dōsayārī ya ettha durāyārō jannadēvō. tā khamiyatvaṁ tumaē, jamaē amuṇiyaparamatyēṇaṁ kayatthiōsi tti. taō maē hanta saṁpattō vasaṇaṁ jannadēvō tti cintiūṇa bhaṇiō rāyā-dēva! rāyadhammō'yaṁ, payāparirakkhaṇasamujjayassa natthi dōsō dēvassa. jannadēvamūlamuddhiṁ pi gavēsēu dēvō, na tammi mahāṇubhāvē aṇāyaraṇaṁ saṁbhāvīyaï. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ — gaviṭṭhā mūlasuddhī, sāhiyaṁ bhayavaīē— savvamiṇaṁ tēṇa pāvēṇa vavasiyaṁ ti. sāhiya dēvayākahiyaṁ rāiṇā. ṭhiyaṁ ca mē cittē tuha dōsapayāsaṇēṇaṁ ti bhaṇiūṇa sāhiō jannadēvakahiyavuttantō. tō maē cintiyaṁ — hanta kimēyaṁ asaṁbhāvaṇija. etthantarammi ya āṇi yō rāyapurisē hi bandhē ūṇa jannadēvō, nivēiō rāigō. bhaṇiyaṁ ca tēṇa-arē ēyassa jibbhaṁ chindiūṇa uppāḍēha lōyaṇāī. visaṇṇō jannadēvō. taō maē calaṇēsu nivaḍiūṇa vinnattō rāyā-dēva! mama ēsa avarāhō khamīyaü, muccaü jannadēvō. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ — satyavāhaputta! na juttamēyaṁ, durāyārō khu ēsō, tā anaṁ vinnavēhi tti. maē bhaṇiyaṁ — dēva! alamannēṇaṁ ti, jaï mamōvari bahumāṇō dēvassa, tā imaṁ cēva saṁpāḍēu dēvō. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ — alavaṇīyavayaṇō tuma ti, tuma cēva jāṇāsi! tō maē dēvapasāō tti bhaṇiūṇa nivaḍiō(a) calaṇēsu mōyāviō jamnadēvō, pēsiō ya ahaṁ rāiṇā niyayabhavaṇaṁ taō sammāṇiūṇa mahayā vibhūīē gaō sabhavaṇaṁ ti. jāō ya lōyavāō, ahō! jannadēvassa jahannattaṁ. samuppannō ya mē nivvēō. peccha, īisō pariṇāmō tti. ahō! asārayā saṁsārassa, vicittayā kamma pariṇaīē, dullakkhāṇi pāṇicittāṇi. tā na yāṇāmō kimettha juttaṁ ti.

etthantarammi ya samāgaō tattha mugihiyanāmō aggibhūī nāma gaṇaharō. ṭhiō ya nayarujjāṇē. diṭṭhō maē bāhiriyāgaēṇaṁ. jāō ya mē taṁ paï bahumāṇō, paṇamiō ya sō maē, dhammalābhiyō ya tēṇaṁ ubaviṭṭhō tassa pāyamūlē. pucchiō bhayavaṁ savvadukkha viuḍaṇasamatthaṁ dhammaṁ. sāhiō bhagavayā khamāigō sāhudhammō. taṁ ca suṇamāṇassa samuppannā dēsaviraïpariṇaī pavaṭṭamāṇasaṁvēgassa jāō bhavavirāgō. cintiyaṁ ca maē-alaṁ saṁsārapavaḍaṇāmettaphalēṇaṁ imiṇā parikilēsēṇaṁ, pavajjāmō pavvajja ti etthantarammi ya galiō kammasaṁghāō, payaliyā bandhapaṭṭiī, vihāviyaṁ attapiriēṇaṁ, samuppannā sabaviraïpariṇaï ti. kahāva sāṇē ya vinnattō maē bhayavaṁ gurū. aṇuggihīō ahaṁ bhayavayā, virattaṁ ca mē cittaṁ bhavapaścāō, tā āisaü bhayavaṁ kiṁ maē kāyavvaṁ ti.

taō tēṇa suya(yā)sayanāṇiṇāmama bhāvaṁ viyāgiūṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — jujjaï bhavaō mahāpurisasēviyaṁ samagattaṇaṁ kāuṁti. taōmaē tassa samī vammi cēva pavanaṁ samaṇattaṇaṁ, parivāliyaṁ ca vihiṇā. tō ahāuyaṁ pāliūṇa kālamāsē kālaṁ kiccā dēhaṁ caïūṇa navasāgarōvamāū vēmāṇiyattāē uvavannō mhi bambhalōē, iyarō vi ya jannadēvō tisāgarōvamaṭṭhiī sakarappabhāē nāragō ti. taō ahamahāuyaṁ pāliūṇa dēvalōgāō cuō samāṇō ihēva vidēhē gandhilāvaī vijaē rayaṇapurē nayarē rayaṇasāgarasta satthavāhassa sirimaīē bhāriyāē kucchisi puttattāē upavanō ti. iyarō vi ya taō naragāō uccaṣṭiūṇa āhēḍagamuṇaō bhakkhi mariūṇa tisāgarōvamāū tatthēva uvavajiūṇa tō ya ucaṭṭō nāṇātiriēmu āhiṇḍiūṇa tatthēva rayaṇapurē tāyagharadāsīē nammayābhihāṇāē suyattāē uvavannōti. uciyasamayammi jāyā ya amhē, pattā ya bālabhāvaṁ. païṭāviyāī nāmāī, majjhaṁ candasārō, iyarassa aṇāhagō tti. pattā ya jovvaṇaṁ. kō maē dāra saṁgahō. ēvaṁ ca visayāsattā ciṭṭhāmō. puvvabhakabhāsaō ya na imassa mamōvari vaścaṇāpariṇāmō avēi. annayā ya āgaōtattha māsa kappavihārī bhayavaṁ vijayavaddhaṇāyariō. pavanō ya maē imassa pāyamūlē sāvagadhammō. annayā ya taṁ puraṁ dīhadaṇḍajattāgaē naravaïmmi, gāmantaragaēsu amhēsu vijhakēunāmēṇa savarasēṇāvaïṇā hayavihayaṁ kāūṇa avaṇīō kōi lōō. suyaṁ ca amhē hiṁ. samāgayā taṁ puraṁ. diṭṭhaṁ ca masāṇāgāramaṇugarintaṁ, gavēsāviyaṁ māṇusaṁ jāva sabamēva dharaï, navaraṁ candakantā mē bhāriyā avahaḍa tti. taō samuppannā araī, jāyā ya cintā-hā! kahaṁ sā tavassiṇō mamādiviōgā pāṇē dhārissaï ti. etthantarammi ya bhaṇiō dēvasammābhihā ṇēṇaṁ vuḍḍamāhaṇēṇaṁ-satthavāhaputta! mā saṁtappa. puṇō vi ēyammi cē disaē siritthalābhihāṇāō sanivēsāō ēvaṁ cēva savarēhi avaṇīō jaṇō āsi. sō niravasēsō akhaṇḍiyacarittasabassō mahayā daviṇajāēṇa mukkō tti. taō ahaṁ ēyamāyaṇṇiūṇa aïkantēsu kaïvayadiṇēsu sabhūmimuvagaēsu sabarēsu aṇahagaduiō ghētūṇa savvasāraṁ daviṇajāyaṁ susaṇiddhasaṁbhiyaṁ ca pāhēyaṁ payaṭṭō candakantāvimokkhaṇanimittaṁ ti.

iyō ya tīē mama viōgavihurāē cārittakhaṇḍaṇāsaṅkiṇīē ya karhici suṇgagāmāsannakūvayaḍāvāsiyāē sabaravāhiṇīē nisācara masamayammi, pavattē ya payāṇagakōlāhalē pērantarakkhaṇāvāvaḍēsu savarasaṁghāēsu jīviyaniravekkhāē tammi cēva jiṇṇakūvammi pavāhiō appā. paḍiyā ya jalamajjhē, na mayā ya jalappabhāvēgaṁ. tō taggaya cēva paḍikūvagamahiṭṭhiūṇa ciṭṭhiumāraddhā. kicchapāṇā ya jīviyasēsēṇaṁ cēva jāva pāṇē dhārēi, tāva pattā amhē tamuddēsaṁ. aṇahagassa vi ya punvabhavanimittaō tayatyasaṁdarisaṇaō ya samuppannō mamōvari vañcaṇāpariṇāmō. cintiyaṁ ca ṇēṇaṁ— kahamēsō vaściyanyō tti. taō sō aṇēyaviyappasamāuliyahiyō ahaṁ ca muddhasa hāvō tti ēvaṁ vaccāmō. pāhē yadaviṇajāyāṇi ya pattēyaṁ hatthagōyarāṇi havanti. annayā ya mama hatthē pāhēyaṁ tassa daviṇajāyaṁ ti. ēvamaṇugacchamāṇā pattā tamuddēsaṁ, jattha sā candakantā ciṭṭhaï. diṭṭhō ya sō kūvō. etthantarammi ya atyamiō sahassarassī, luliyā sajhā. taō cintiyamaṇahagēṇaṁ-hatthagayaṁ mē daviṇajāyaṁ, vijaṇaṁ ca kantāraṁ, samāsanō ya pāyālagambhīrō kūvō, pavattō ya avarāha vivarasamacchāyagō andhayārō. tā ēyammi ēyaṁ pakkhiviūṇa niyattāmō imassa thāṇassa tti cintiūṇa bhaṇiyaṁ ca tēṇa-satyavāhaputta! dhaṇiyaṁ pivāsābhibhūō mhi. tā nihālē hi ēyaṁ jiṇṇakūvaṁ kimettha udagaṁ atthi, natyi tti? taō maē gahiyapāhēyapoṭṭalēṇaṁ cēva nihāliō kūvī. etthantarammi ya suvisatthahiyayassa lōyassa viya maccū āgaō mama samīyamaṇahagō. sahasā pakkhittō tammi ahamaṇahagēṇa, paḍiō ya udagamajjhē. niyattō ya sō taō vibhāgāō. ahamavi ya sasaṁbhantō laggō paḍikūvagēkadēsē. parāmuṭṭhā ya bhayavihalaṅghalā candakantā thīsahāvaō bhayakāyarā. bhaṇiyaṁ ca tīē namō arihaṁtāṇaṁ ti. taō maē pañcabhinnāō sadō. ūsasiyaṁ mē hiyaēṇaṁ. bhaṇiyā ya sā abhayamabhayaṁ jiṇasāsaṇarayāṇaṁ ti. tīē vi ya pañcabhinnāō mē sahō. rōviuṁ payattā, samāsāsiyā sā maē, pucchiyā ya vuttantaṁ. sāhiō ya tīē, maē vi ya niyagō tti. bhaṇiyaṁ ca tīē-hā! duṭṭhu kayaṁ aṇahagēṇa. mara bhaṇiyaṁ sundari! na du? kayaṁ, paramośyārī khu sō mahāṇubhāvō, jaṁ tumaṁ saṁjōiya tti. appanihāṇa ya aïkannā rayaṇī, uggaō aṁsumālī.

taō maē dinnaṁ candakantāē pāhēyaṁ. bhaṇiyaṁ ca tīē— kahamahaṁ tumaē agahiyammi geṇhāmi tti. taō maē nēhakāyaraṁ sē hiyayaṁ kaliūṇamakālē cēva gahiyaṁ pāhēyaṁ, bhuttaṁ ca amhēhiṁ. taō cintiyaṁ maē-kēṇa puṇa uvāēṇa amhē imāō bhavasamudāō viva kūva sasaṁbhrāntō lagnō pratikūpakaïkadēśē. parāmr̥ṣṭā ca bhayavihvalāṅgī candrakāntā, strīsvabhāvatō bhayakātarā. maṇiāṁ ca tayā namō'rhadbhya gāō u tarissāmō tti. ēvaṁ ca cintayantāṇaṁ kaïvayadiṇēsu khīṇaṁ pāhēyaṁ, paṇaṭā jīviyāsā. jāyā ya mē cintā-kahaṁ pāviūṇa jiṇamayaṁ akāūṇa paca jamakayatthō marissāmi tti. etthantarammi phuriyaṁ sē vāmalōyaṇēṇaṁ, mamāvi dāhiṇēṇaṁ. jaṁpiyaṁ ca tīē ajjaputta! vāmaṁ mē lōyaṇaṁ phuriya'ti. taō sāhiō sē maē hiyayasaṁkappō iyaracakkhuphuraṇaṁ ca. samāsāsiyā ya ēsā. sundari! imēhiṁ nimittavisē sēhiṁ avassa amhāṇaṁ na cirakālāṇusārī ēsa kilēsō, tā na tumaē saṁtappiyavvaṁ ti. paḍissuyamimīē. ēvaṁ ca jāva ahōrattaṁ nivasāmō, tāva samāgaō sabararāyahāṇīō rayaṇapuranivāsiṇō nandivaddhaṇābhihāṇassa satyavāhassa santiō rayaṇapura gāmī cēva satthō tti. uyaganimittaṁ ca samāgayā purisā gahiūṇa lambaṇā. divāī amhē imēhiṁ. nivēiyaṁ satyavāhassa. kayama ciyāpaōēṇaṁ samuttārāviyāī tēṇaṁ,pañcabhinnāyāṇi ya. pucchiyāī vuttanta, sāhiō vittharēṇaṁ,vimhiō ēsō,taō patthiyāī rayaṇaüraṁ jāva aïkkantēsu pañcasu payāṇa ēmu parivahantē satthē rāyapattaṇīō nāidūradēsabhāē diṭṭhō kaṅkālamettasēsō yāmapāsāvaḍiyadaviṇajāō kēsariṇā dīhanidāvasamuvaṇīō aṇaḍagō tti. daviṇōbalambhēṇa pañcabhinnāō amhē hiṁ. taō taṁ tahāviha vivāgaṁ pecchiūṇa samuppanō mē vivēgō, khōvasamamuvagayaṁ cārittamōhaṇīyaṁ. saṁjāō sayalajīvalōyadullahō caraṇapariṇāmō. taō ahaṁ tahāvihapa baḍamāṇapariṇāmō cēva āgō sanayaraṁ. pavanō ya jahāvihīē vijayabaddhaṇāyariyasamīvē pavvajja. ahāuyamaṇuvāliūṇa vihiṇā ya mottūṇa dēī, ukvannō sōlasasāgarōvamāū vēmāṇiyattāē mahāsukkakappammi, iarō vi ya aṇahagō sīhavāvāiyasarīrō satta sāgarōvamahiī vālugappahāē nāragō tti. taō ahamahāuyaṁ pāliūṇa dēvalōgāō cuō samāṇō ihēba jambuddīvē dīvē bhārahē vāsē rahavīraürē nayarē nandivaddhagasta gāhāvaïssa surasundarīē bhāriyāē kucchisi puttattāē uvavannō mhi. iyarō vi taō naragāō uvvaṭṭiūṇa vijhagiripacaē agasattaśavāyaṇaparō sīhattāē uvavannō. taō sīhattāē uvavajiūṇa puṇō vimariūṇa sattasāgarōvamāū tatthēva uvavanjiya tō ya ucaṭṭō nāṇātiriēmu āhiṇḍiya tasyēva nayarē saümasatyavāhassa nandimaīē bhāriyāē puttattāē upacannō ti. uciyasamayammi jāyā amhē, pacā bālabhāvaṁ. païṭāviyāī nāmāī-majjhaṁ aṇaṅgadēvō, iyarassa dhagadēvō tti. ābālabhāvō jāyā piī mama sambhāvaō, iyaraspta kaïyavēṇaṁ. kumārabhāvammi ya pattō maē dēvasēgagurusamī vē sāṇṇubhāsi ō dhammō. pattā ya jōvaṇaṁ. santē viya puvvapurisajjiē daviṇajāē abhimāṇaō kimaṇēṇa punyapurisajjiēṇaṁ ti dayasaṁgaha nimittaṁ gayā rayaṇadīvaṁ. nihattāī rayaṇāī, kayā saṁjuttī, payaṭṭā niyadēsamāgantuṁ. etthantarammi ya puyakayakammadō sēṇa cintiyaṁ dhaṇadēvēṇa-kahaṁ puṇō vaściyavvō ēsa agaṅgadēvō. viyapiyā ya tēṇaṁ aṇēgē micchāviyappā. ṭhāviō siddhantō. abābāiō ēsa na tīraē vaściu ti, tā yāvārami ēyaṁ. paricintiō ubāō bhōyaṇē sē visaṁ dēmi tti. annayā ya satthimaīsannivē samaṇupattāṇaṁ bhothaṇanimittaṁ gaō dhaṇadēvō iṭṭamaggaṁ. kārāviyaṁ ca tēṇa bhōyaṇaṁ, phakkhittaṁ ca ēgammi laḍḍugē visa. cintiyaṁ ca tēṇaṁ — ēyaṁ sē dāhāmi ti. āgacchantassa aṇēgaviyappāvahariyacittassa saṁjāō vivajī. bhōyaṇavēlāē gahiō tēṇa visalaḍḍugō, dinō mamaṁ ca iyarō tti. pabhuttā anhē jāva thēvavēlāē cēva thāriō dhaṇadēvō. taō kimēyaṁ ti āulīhūō ahaṁbīō bhavō jāva kiṁkāyabvamūḍhō thēvakālaṁ ciṭṭhāmi, tāpa acnuggayāē visassa vicittayāē kammapariṇāmassa ubaraō dhaṇadēvō. jāyā mē cintā hā kēṇa uṇa ēvaṁ vavasiyaṁ ti. taō amuṇayavr̥ttantō mahāsōyābhibhūyamāṇasō āgaō sanayaraṁ. miṭṭhō vuttantō tassa māṇusāṇaṁ. viiṇṇaṁ ca tēsiṁ amahiyayaraṁ rayaṇajāyaṁ. sēsarayaṇa nāyaṁ pi ya jahāṇurūvaṁ kusalapakkhē nijiūga tannivvaēṇa cēṣa tayappabhiimannā yavisayasaṅgō pavannō dēvasēṇāyariyasamīvē pacanaṁ ni. parivāliūṇa ahāuyaṁ vihiṇā ya mōnūṇa dēhaṁ pāṇayammi kappē upabannō ēga ṇavīsasāgarōvamāū dēvō tti, iyarō vi visamaraṇāṇantaraṁ paṅkappabhāē puḍhabīē navasāmavamāū nāragō ti. ta' ahamahāuyaṁ aṇuvā liūṇa cuō samāṇō ihēba jambuddīvē dīvē ēravaē khētē hathiṇāurē nayarē harinandissa gāhāvaïssa lacchimaīē bhāriyāē kucchisi puttattāē uvavannō. iyarō di tō naragāō uccaṭṭiya uragattaṇaṁ pāviūṇamaṇēgasattavāvāyaṇaparō dāvāṇaladaḍadēhō mariūṇa tīē cēya paṅkappabhāē puḍhavīē kiṁcūṇadasasāgarōramāū nāragō hōūṇa taō ubaṭṭō, tiriēmu āhiṇḍiya tammi cēva hathigāurē indanāmassa buḍḍaseṭṭhissa nandimaīē bhāriyāē kucchisi putta tāē ucavannō tti. uciyasamayammi jāyā amhē. païṭāviyāī nāmāī-majjhaṁ dhīradēvō, iyarassa dōṇagō tti. pattā ya kumārabhāvaṁ, samappiyā ya lē hāyariyassa. jāyā ya amhāgaṁ puavaṇiyā cēva piī. taō gahiyakalā. kalāvēṇaṁ maē paḍivannō māṇabhaṅgagurusamī vē jiṇadēsiō dhammō, mamokkhāravaścaṇakusalēṇa davvaō dōṇaēṇāvi. taō ya mē dhammā ṇurāēṇa tappabhiī taṁ paï samupamā thirayarā piī. samappiyaṁ sē pabhūyaṁ daviṇajāyaṁ. bhaṇiō ya ēsō— vakaharaha aṇindiēṇa maggēṇa ! taō sō vavahariumāraddhō. vidvattaṁ ca tēga pabhūyaṁ daviṇajāya. etthantarammi puvakayakammavāsaṇādōsēga jāō sē mamōpari ahiṁgō vañcagāpariṇāmō. cintiyaṁ ca tēṇaṁ-ajjiyaṁ pabhūyaṁ daviṇajāya, bhāgiō ya vīradēvō ēyasta, tā kēga uga uvāēṇa vañciyakō lakṣmīmatyā bhāryāyāḥ kukṣaü putrāyōpapannaḥ. iārō'pi tatō narakāduvr̥ttya uragatvaṁ prāpyānēkasattvavvāpādanaparō dāvānaladagdhadēhō mr̥tvā ēsō, na ya muṇaï jahaṭṭiyaṁ ṇē kōi vavahāraṁ. tā kiṁ abalambāmi? ahavā ēyammi paripanthagē na mē aliyavayaṇaṁ nivvahaï. tā vāvāēmi ēyaṁ. taō jamahaṁ :maṇissāmi, taṁ cēva agghissaï tti saṁpahāriūṇa pāraddhō tēṇa samuvayārō. kārāviō mahantō pāsāō, ukaribhūmibhāē ya tassa aṇiyamiyakhīlajālō ṇijjūhagō. cintiyaṁ ca tēṇaṁ. vīradēvaṁ pāsāyapavēsanimittaṁ nimantiūṇa daṁsēmi sē nijjūhagaṁ. taō sō rammadaṁsaṇīyayāē nijjūhagassa sahasā ārōhaïssaï. tō ya tanivaḍaṇēṇa nivaḍiō samāṇō na bhavissaï tti. ēvaṁ ca kaē samāṇē lōyavāō vi parihariō hōi. saṁpāiyaṁ tēṇa jahāsamīhiya. bhututtarakālaṁmi ya ārūḍhā duvē vi amhē saparivārā pāsāyaṁ. etthantaraṁmi ya paṇaṭṭhā sē maī. mama dēsaṇanimittaṁ kēvalō cēvārūḍhō nijjūhagaṁ. jāva ya nārōhāmi ahayaṁ, tāva nivaḍiō. hāhāravaṁ karēmāṇō samōḍaṇṇō ahayaṁ jāva dihrō pañcattamuvagaō dōṇagō tti. samuppannō mē nivvēō. cintiyaṁ maē. dhiratyu jīvalōyassa, ēvamavasāṇaṁ saṁsāraceṭṭiyaṁ. tō ahaṁ tassa mayakiccaṁ kāūṇa tannivēēṇa cēva paḍivannō māṇabhaṅgagurusamīvē samaṇaliṅgaṁ. parivāliūṇa ahāuyaṁ uvavannō hechimōvarimagēvejjaē kiṁcūṇapaṇuvīsasāgarōvamāū dēvō; iyarō vi dōṇī tahāviharudda jjhāṇōvagaō dhūmappabhāē puḍhavīē duvālasasāgarōvamāū nāragō tti. tō ahaṁ surāuyamaṇubhujiūṇa cuō samāṇō ihēba jambuddīvē dīvē ettha cēva vijaē campāvāsē nayarē māṇibhaddassa seṭṭhissa dhāriṇīē bhāriyāē kucchisi puttattāē uvavannō, jāō ya uciyasama ēṇaṁ. païṭāviyaṁ mē nāmaṁ puṇṇabhadō tti. paḍhamaṁ ca kila maē ghōsamuccārayantēṇa amara tti saṁlattaṁ. aō duiyaṁ pi mē nāma amaraguttō tti. sākkhagihuppattīē ya ā bālabhāvāō vēva papannō maē jiṇadēsiō dhammō. etthantaraṁmi ya iyarō vi taō naragāō ughaṭṭi ūṇa sayaṁbhūramaṇē samuddē mahāmacchō bhaviya añcantapāvadiṭṭhī maō samāṇō tīē cēva dhūmappabhāē duvālasasāgarōvamāū cēva nāragō hōūṇa ucaṭṭō samāṇō nāṇātiriēsu āhiṇḍiya taṁmi cēva nayarē nandāvattassa seṭṭhissa sirinandāē bhāriyāē kucchisi dhūyattāē uvavannō jāyā ya uciyasamaēṇaṁ. païṭāviyaṁ ca sē nāma nandayanti tti. pattā ya jōvaṇaṁ, viigṇā ya majjhaṁ. nibattiyaṁ pāṇiggahaṇaṁ. samu ppannō ya mē taṁ paï siṇēhō, tīē vi ya tahēba. ēvaṁ ca visayasuhamaṇuhavantāṇaṁ gaō kōi kālō. puvyakayakammadōsēṇa ya sē mamōvari vaścaṇāpariṇāmō nāvēi, jēṇa samappiyasabagharasārā vi māyāē vavaharaï. sāhiyaṁ ca mē pariyaṇēṇaṁ, na uga pattiyāmi tti. annayā ya sāhiyaṁ mē tīē. jahā paṇaṭṭhaṁ savvasāraṁ kuṇḍalajuyalaṁ. taṁ puṇa sayaṁ cēva avahariūṇa samāulībhūyā. bhagiyā ya taō maē. sundari, thēvamēyaṁ ti, kimēhahamettēṇaṁ saṁrambhēṇa. annaṁ tē kuṇḍala juyalaṁ kārāvēmi. kārāviyaṁ kuṇḍalajuyalaṁ. aïkantēsu kaïvayadi ṇēsu abbhaṅgagavēlāē samappiyaṁ sē nāmaṅkiyamuddārayaṇaṁ, saṁgōviyaṁ ca tīē niyayābharaṇakaraṇḍaē. vattē ya ṇhāṇabhōyaṇasamaē kāūṇama garāyaṁ parigeṇhiūṇa tambōlaṁ asaṁjāyāsaṁkēṇa cēva taō karaṇḍa gāō saī cēva gahiyaṁ maē muddārayaṇaṁ. diṭṭhaṁ ca puvvanaṭṭhaṁ savvasāraṁ kuṇḍa lajuyalaṁ. jāyā ya mē cintā kimayaṁ puṇō laddhaṁ ti. etthantaraṁmi sasajjhasā viya āgayā nandayantī. diṭṭhaṁ ca tīē majjha hatthaṁmi muddārayaṇaṁ. viliyā sā. lakkhiō sē bhāvō. taō ahaṁ sigdhamēva niggaō gēhāō. cintiyaṁ ca tīē-dilu imēṇa kuṇḍalajuyalaṁ tā kimettha kāyavvaṁ. jāyaṁ mē lahuttaṁ, paṇaṭṭhō ēsō vi. tā jāva sayaṇavaggē vi mē lāghavaṁ na uppajjaï, tāva vāvāēmi ēyaṁ ti. ēsō ya ettha uvāō, sajjaghāyaṇaṁ sē kammaṇajōgaṁ paüñjāmi. kō tīē kēvalāē cēva aṇēyamaraṇāvahadavvasaṁjōēṇaṁ jōgō. saṁṭhavantī ya tamē gadēsē ḍakā bhuyaṅgamēṇaṁ. sāhiyaṁ ca mē purōhiēṇaṁ rudadēvēṇaṁ. gō ahaṁ sasambhantō gihaṁ. diṭṭhā ya kasiṇamaṇḍalavisavāviyasarīrā jīviyametta mēsā nandayantī. taṁ ca tahāvihaṁ daṭṭaṇa samuppannā mē cintā. dhiratthu māindajālasarisassa jīvalōyassa. bāhajala bhariyalōyaṇēṇaṁ ca sagaggayakkharaṁ bhaṇiyā maē. sundari, kiṁ tē bāhaï? jāva na jaṁpaï tti. taō visaṇṇō ahaṁ, paṇaṭṭhā jīvi yāsā. tahāvi gāruḍiyā ettha pabhāṇaṁ, acintā mantasatti tti sadāviyā gāruḍiyā. diṭṭhā ya tēhiṁ. visaṇṇā ya tē. bhaṇiō ya ṇēhiṁ. satthavāhaputta, kāladaṭṭhā khu ēsā na gōyarā mantastra. tā na kuppiyavvaṁ tumaē tti bhagiūga niggayā gāruḍiyā. tō akkandaṇavilavaṇavāvaḍassa mē pariyaṇassa vimukkā jīviēṇaṁ, kayaṁ sē uddhadēhiyaṁ. tō ahaṁ tannivvēēṇaṁ cēva pavaḍḍamāṇasaṁvēgō dhiratthu jīvalōyassa ti paricintiūṇa ya asārayaṁ caïūṇa kilēsāyāsakāriṇaṁ saṅgaṁ pavanō pavvajja ti. sā uṇa tavassiṇī tahā mariūṇa samuppannā tamappahābhihāṇāē narayapuḍhavīē. āuṁca sē igavīsaṁ sāgarāī. ēyaṁ mē cariyaṁ ti ēyaṁ ca sōūṇa saṁjāō rāyanāyarāṇaṁ nivēō. pucchiyaṁ ca rāiṇā. bhayavaṁ, kō uṇa tīē avaō ya pariṇāmō bhavissaï? bhayavayā bhaṇiyaṁ. tīsē aṇantasaṁsārāvasāṇē muttī, mama uṇa ihēba jammē tti.

taō ahamēyamāyaṇṇiūṇa tassa cēva bhayavaō samīvē aṇēyanāyarajaṇaparigaō pavanō pavvajja

ēyaṁ mē visēsakāraṇaṁ ti

sīhakumārēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — sōhaṇaṁ tē nivvēyakāraṇaṁ. aha kaïgaïsamāvannarūbō uṇa ēsa saṁsārō, kiṁvisiṭṭāṇi vā iha sārīramāṇasā ṇi suhadukkhāṇi aṇuhavanti pāṇiṇō, kō vā estha saṁsāracāragavimōyaṇasamatthō bhayava! dhammōti? dhammaghōsēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — vaccha! suṇa, jaṁ taē pucchiyaṁ—

ettha tāva caügaïsamāvannarūvō saṁsārō. gaīō puṇa imāō. taṁ jahā-narayagaī, tiriyagaī, maṇuyagaī, dēvagaī. muhadukkha cintāē puṇa, kuō saṁsārasamāvannāṇaṁ jāijarāmaraṇapīḍiyāṇaṁ rāgāidōsagahiyāṇaṁ visayavisāvahiyacēyaṇāṇaṁ ca sattāṇaṁ suhaṁ ti? na kiṁci suhaṁ, bahuṁ ca dukkhaṁ. ettha mē suṇa nāyaṁ—

jaha nāma kōi purisō dhaṇiyaṁ dālidukkhasaṁtattō

mottaṇa niyaṁ dēsaṁ paradēsaṁ gantumāraddhō

lajhēūṇa ya ’dēsaṁ gāmāgaranayarapaṭṭaṇasaṇāhaṁ

thēvēdiya hēhi navaraṁ kahaṁci panthāu pabbhaṭṭhō

pattō ya sāla-sarala-tamāla-tālāli-baüla-tilaya-nicula-akolla-kalamba-vajula-palāsa-sallaī-tiṇisa-nimba-kuḍaya naggōha-khaïra-sajja-’jjuṇa-mba-jambuyaniyaraguvilaṁ dariyamayaṇāhakharanaharasiharāvāyadaliyamattamāyaṅgakumbhatthalagaliyabahalaruhirāratta muttāhalakusumapayaraciyavisthiṇṇabhūmibhāgaṁ vaṇakōla-saraha-vasaha-pasaya-vagdha-taraccha-’cchabhalla-jambuya-gaya-gavaya-sīha-gaṇḍayāi ruṭṭhaduṭṭhasāvayabhīsaṇaṁ dariyavaṇamahisajūhasamālōḍiyāsēsapallalajalucchalantuttasthanalayaramukkanāyabahiriyadisaṁ mahāḍaviṁ. tīē ya taṇhā chuhābhibhūpaṇa dariyavaṇaduṭṭhasāvayaravāyaṇṇaṇuttatthalōyaṇēṇaṁ dīhapahaparissamuppannasēyajaladhōyagattēṇaṁ mūhadisācakaṁ visamapahakhalantapayasaṁ cāraṁ paribhamantēṇa tēṇa diṭṭhō ya palayaghaṇavandrasannihō nidraviyāṇēyapahiya jaṇabaḍiucchāhō gaddavbhagajjiyaravāvūriyaviyaḍaraṇṇudēsō maggaō turiyaturiyaṁ dhāvamāṇō uddhīkaüddaṇḍasuṇḍō vaṇahatthi tti. taha ya nisiyakaravālavāvaḍaggahatthā vigarālavayaṇakāyā bhīmaṭṭa hāsasaṁjuttā asiyavasaṇā puraō mahādudarakkhasi tti. taō ya tē daṭṭaṇa maccubhayavēviraṅgō avalōiyasayaladisāmaṇḍalō puvadisāē udayagirisiharasannihaṁ niruddhasiddhagandhavvamihuṇagaïyaṇapayāramaggaṁ mahantaṁ naggōhapāyavaṁ avalōiūga paricintiuṁ payattō. kahaṁ?

jaï nāma kahavi ēyaṁ raviturayakhuramachinnaghaṇapattaṁ

naggōhamāruhējā chuṭṭēja tō gaïndarasa

iya cintiūṇa bhīō kusasūī bhinnapāyatalamaggō

vēgēṇa dhāviūṇaṁ viyaḍaṁ vaḍapāyavaṁ pattō

taṁ pecchiuṁ visaṇṇō naggōhaṁ gayaṇagōyarāṇaṁ pi

dullaṅghaṇijjamuttuṅgakhandhamāruhiumasamatthō

tāva vaṇaduṭṭhahatthi mantharagaṇḍālijālapāmukkaṁ

huliyaṁ samalliyantaṁ daṭṭhuṁ baḍapāyavudēsaṁ

abbhahiyabhayapavēvirasavvaṅgō vuṇṇavayaṇataralacchaṁ

ettō iō niyantō pecchaï kūrva taṇochannaṁ

aha maraṇabhīruēṇaṁ naggōhāsannajiṇṇakūvammi

appā nirāvalamba mukkō khaṇajīvalōhēṇa

uttuṅgabhittijāō sarathambhō tambhi tattha ya bilaggō

paḍaṇābhighāyakuviē pecchaï ya bhuyaṅgamē bhīmē

caüsu vi taḍīsu dariē visalavasaṁvaliyanayaṇasihi jālē

unbhaḍaphaḍākarālē pavelliraṅgē ḍēsiukāmē

phukārapavaṇapisuṇiyamavayacchiyavayaṇamagaramahō ya

diggayakarōrukāyaṁ kasiṇaṁ rattacchibībhacchaṁ

jāvēsō sarathambhō tāva mahaṁ jīviyaṁ ti cintantō

avayacchaï uddhamuddō pecchaï ya sutikkhadāḍhillē

dhavalakasiṇē ya turiyaṁ duvē tahiṁ mūsaē mahākāē

niccaṁ vāvaḍavayaṇē chindantē tassa mūlāī

tāva vaṇavāraṇēṇa ya vijjhāiṁ naraṁ apāvamāṇēṇaṁ

kuviēṇa viiṇṇāī dhaṇiyaṁ naggōharukkhammi

saṁcāliyammi tammi ya avaḍōpari viyaḍasāhasaṁbhūyaṁ

khuḍiūṇa tammi paḍiyaṁ mahujālaṁ jiṇṇakūvammi

tō kuviyadudrumahuyariniyaraḍasijjantasavvagattassa

sīsammi nivaḍiyā kaha vi navaraṁ jōēṇa mahubindū

ōyaliūṇa ya vayaṇaṁ kahavi paviṭṭhā u uttimaṅgāō

khaṇamāsāiumicchaï puṇō vi annē nivaḍamāṇē

agaṇēumayagarōragakarimsayavilayamahuyaribhayāī

mahubindurasāsāyaṇagēhibasā harisiō jāō

bhaviyajaṇamōhaviuḍaṇapañcalamaccatyamiyamudāharaṇaṁ

parigappiyamēyassa ya upasaṁhāraṁ nisāmēha

jō purisō sō jīvō caügaïbhamaṇaṁ ca raṇṇapariyaḍaṇaṁ

vaṇavāraṇō ya maccū nisāyariṁ jāṇa taha ya jaraṁ

vaḍarukkhō uṇa mokkhō maraṇagaïndabhayavajiō navaraṁ

āruhiuṁ visayāuranarēhi na ya sakaṇijjō ti

maṇuyattaṁ puṇa kūbō bhuyaṅgamā taha ya honti u kasāyā

khaïō jēhiṁ maṇussō kajākajāhaṁ na muṇēi

jō vi ya puṇa sarathambhō sō jīyaṁ jēṇa jīvaï jīvō

taṁ kiṇhadhavalapakkhā khaṇanti dahamundurasamāṇā

jāō ya mahuyarīō ḍasanti taṁ tē u vāhiṇō vivihā

abhibhūō jēhi narō khaṇaṁ pi sokkhaṁ na pāvēi

ghōrō ya ayagarō jō sō naraō visayamōhiyamaṇō tti

paḍiō u jammi jīvō dukkhasahassāī pāvēi

mahubindusamē bhōē tucchē pariṇāmadāruṇē dhaṇiyaṁ

iya vasaṇasaṁkaḍagaō vibuhō kaha mahaï bhottuṁ jē?

'tō bhē bhaṇāmi sāvaya! visayasuhaṁ dāruṇaṁ muṇēūṇa

cavalataḍivilasiyaṁ piva maṇuyattaṁ bhaṅguraṁ taha ya

suyaṇasamāgamasōvakhaṁ cavalaṁ jovvaṇaṁ pi ya asāraṁ

sokkhanihāṇammi syā dhammammi maī daḍhaṁ kuṇam

sīhakumārēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — bhaya! kērisō dhammō tti? bhagavayā bhaṇiyaṁ — suṇa, khamāigō. bhaṇiyaṁ ca khantī ya manajjavamottī tavasaṁjamē ya boddhavvē. saccaṁ sōya ākiṁcaṇaṁ ca bammaṁ ca jaïdhammō. tattha khantī nāma sammannāṇapudhagaṁ vatthusahāvālōyaṇēṇa kōhassa aṇudayō, udayapattassa vā viphalīkaraṇaṁ. ēvaṁ madavayā vi māṇassa aśudaō, udayapattaspa vā viphalīkaraṇaṁ. ēvamajjavayā vi māyāē aṇudayō, udayapattāē vā viphalīkaraṇaṁ. ēvaṁ muttī vi lōhassa aṇudayō, udayapattassa vā viphalīkaraṇaṁ ti. tayō puṇa duvihō-bāhirō abbhintarō ya. bāhiraō aṇasaṇāigō. bhaṇiyaṁ ca—

aṇasaṇamr̥ṇōyariyā vittīsaṁkhēvaō rasaccāō

kāyakilēsō saṁlīṇayā ya bajjhō tabō hōi

abbhintaraō puṇa pāyacchittāiō. taṁ jahā—

pāyacchitaṁ viṇaō vēyāvaccaṁ tahēva sajjhāō

jhāṇaṁ ussaggō vi ya anbhintaraō tavō hōi

saṁjamō ya sattarasavihō. bhaṇiyaṁ ca—

paścāsavavēramaṇaṁ paścindiyaniggahō kasāyajaō

daṇḍattigaviraī saṁjamō u iya sattarasabhēō

saccaṁ puṇa nikhajabhāsaṇaṁ. sōyaṁ ca saṁjamaṁ paï niruvalēvayā. ākiṁcaṇaṁ ca dhammōvagaraṇāirēgēṇamapariggahayā. bambhaṁ ca aṭṭhā rasavihā'bambhavajaṇaṁ ti. ēsō ēvaṁbhūō jaïdhammō ti.

ēyaṁ ca sōūṇa āvibbhūyasammattapariṇāmēṇa bhāvaō pavannasāvayadhammēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ sīhakumārēṇaṁ-bhagavaṁ! sōhaṇō jaïdhammō. ēyaṁ kāumasamatthēṇa tāva kiṁ kāyav ti? dhammaghōsēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — sāvayattaṇaṁ. kērisaṁ tayaṁ ti? kahiyaṁ sammattamāiyaṁ. pavannō davvaō vi. taō appāṇaṁ kayakiccaṁ mannamāṇō kaṁci vēlaṁ pajjuvāsiūṇa dhammaghōsaṁ bandiūṇa ya saviṇayaṁ paviṭṭhō nayaraṁ. sāhiō tēṇa vuttantō kusumāvalīē. pavannā ya ēsā vikahaṁci kammakkhaōvasamaō sāvayadhammaṁ. aṇudiyahaṁ ca dhammaghōsagurupajjuvāsaṇaparāṇaṁ aïkkantō māsō. bhāviyāṇi jiṇadhammē. annayā ya purisadattōrāyā amiyatēyagurusamīvē sōūṇa dhamma ahisiściūṇa rajjē sīha kumāra saṁjāyasaṁvēgō saha mahādēvīē sirikantāē parannō muttimaggaṁ. sīhakumārō vi dhammādhammavavatthaparipālaṇaraō sayalajaṇamaṇāṇa ndayārī aṇurattasāmantamaṇḍalō dīṇāṇāhakiviṇajaṇośyārasaṁpāyaṇaraī jahōiyaguṇajuttō rāyarisī samuvajāō tti. ēvaṁ ca añcantā ṇurattaṁ ca piyapaṇaïṇi piva mēiṇi muṁjantassa aïkantō kōi kālō. etthantarammi sō aggisammatāvasadēvō taō vijjukumārakāyāō caviūṇaṁ saṁsāramāhiṇḍiya aṇantarabhavē ya kiṁpi bālatavavihāṇaṁ kāūṇa mottūṇa taṁ dēhaṁ puncakammavāsaṇāvivāgadōsēṇa samuppanō kusu māvalīē kucchisi. diṭṭhō tīē sumiṇaō. jahā-paviṭhṭhō mē uyaraṁ bhuyaṅgamō, tēṇaṁ ca niggacchiūṇa ḍakkō rāyā nivaḍiō siṅghā saṇāō. taṁ ca daṭṭaṇa sasajjhasā viya viuddhā kumumāvalī. amaṅgalaṁ ti kaliūṇa na sāhiō tīē daïyassa. pavaḍamāṇagabbhā ya taddōsaō cēva na bahu mannaē naravaī. rāyā ya ahiyaṁ siṇēhaparavasō. bhaṇiyā ya pariyaṇēṇaṁ sāmiṇi! na juttamēyaṁ ti. tīē bhaṇiyaṁ — kim ahaṁ karēmi? sāhiyaṁ pariyaṇēṇaṁ — jahā dēvaṁ na bahu mannasi tti. tīē bhaṇiyaṁ — nūrṇa ēsa gambhadōsō bhavissaï. annahā kahamahaṁ ajjaüttaṁ na bahu mannēmi. annayā samuppannō sē dōhalō, jahā-imassa cēva rāiṇō antāṇi khāija tti. cintiyaṁ ca tīē pāvayārī mē ēsa gambhō, tā alaṁ imiṇā. itthīsahāvaō ya bhattāranēhaō ya samuppannō sē vavasāō, jahā pāḍēmi ēyaṁ ti. tō ālōciūṇa pahāṇapariyaṇaṁ kajjagaruyayāē ya aṇunnāyā tēṇa gamaparisāḍaṇaṁ kāumāraddhā. na ya sō nikāiyakammadōsēṇa paḍaï tti.

taō sā aṇēgōsahapāṇēṇaṁ ḍōhalayāsaṁpattīē ya paridubalā jāyā. pucchiyā ya rāiṇā-sundari! ki tē na saṁpajjaï, kēṇa vā tē khaṇḍiyā āṇā, kiṁ vā maē paḍikūlamāsēviyaṁ, jē nivvē ēṇa tuma appōyagā viva kumuiṇī ēvaṁ jhijasi tti? taō paḍihiyayaladdha nēhaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ kusumāvalīē-ajjaütta! īdisō mē nivēō, jēṇa cintēmi attāṇayaṁ vāvāēmi tti. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ — sundari! kiṁni mittotti? kusumāvalīē bhaṇiyaṁ — ajjaütta! bhāgadhēyāṇi mē pucchasu tti bhagiūṇa bāhajalabhariyalōyaṇā sagaggayā saṁvuttā. taō rāiṇā mahantō sē nivēō, tā alaṁ tāva imiṇā kahāē cēva, ahaṁ ēyaṁ akkhivāmi ti cintiūṇa akkhitā kahā, kaō annō pasaṅgō. puṇō ya sē samāhūō mayaṇalēhāpamuḍō pariyaṇō, sabahumāṇaṁ ca bhaṇi bhō rāiṇā. kiṁ juttaṁ tumhāṇaṁ suṇiyanibandhaṇāṇaṁ pi ēvaṁ kasiṇapakkhacandalēhaṁ va parikhijamāṇiṁ dēviṁ uvekkhiuṁ ti. na ya asajjhavatthuvisaō ēsa nivvēō, aō jīvalōvasārabhūyā mē dēvī. kiṁ ca taṁ vatthu, jaṁ mē pāṇēsu dharantēsu cēva dēvīē na saṁpajjaï tti. mayaṇalēhāē bhaṇiyaṁ — mahārāya! ēvamēya; navaramitthīya ṇasulahō avivēgō cēva kēvalaṁ ettha avarajjhaï. tā suṇaü mahārāō. mahārāya! ēyamiyāṇi pi kahiuṁ pārīyaï, tahā vi na annō uvāō tti kāūṇa kahīyaï. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ — aṇurūvamēyaṁ saṁbhamassa; jaṁ uvāyasajhaṁ taṁ sayamēva kīraha, iyaraṁ nivēiyaï tti, tā kahēu bhōī, kō ettha paramatthō tti? taō mayaṇalēhāē sasajjhasāē viya ācikkhiō gambhasaṁbhavāō dōhalayadōsēṇa gabbha sāḍaṇāvasāṇō vavahārō ti. rāiṇā cintiyaṁ-ahō! sē dēvīē mamōvari asāhāraṇī nēhō, jēṇāvaccajammaṁ pi na bahu mannaï tti. asaṁpāyaṇēṇaṁ ca dōhalayassa mā gambhavivattī sē bhavissaï tti uvāyaṁ cintēmi. visajjiō ya tēṇa jamahaṁ kālōciyaṁ bhaṇissāmi, taṁ tahā kāyavvaṁ ti bhaṇiūṇa dēvīpariyaṇō. sadāviō maïsāgarō nāma mahāmantī. siṭṭhō imassa ēsa vuttantō. cintiyaṁ ca tēṇaṁ, juttaṁ dēvīē vavasiya. ahavā mā sē imiṇā uvāēṇa tīsē vi dēhapīḍā bhavissaï. tā ēsa tāva ettha uvāō-bubhukkhiyassa rāiṇō kā rimā antā poṭṭavāhiṁ dāūṇa nettapaṭṭāiṇā susiliṭṭhā ya kariya pecchamāṇīē cēva dēvīē kaḍḍiūṇa dijanti. pacchā ya pamyāē cēva gabbhamantarēṇa cintissāmō ti cintiūṇa nivēiō naravaïssa niyayāhippāō. bahu maniō rāiṇā. bhaṇiyā ya maïsāyarēṇa dēvī-sāmiṇi! tahā kaḍḍēmi dēvassa antē, jahā aïsō na vivajaï ti. gambhasahāvarattaṇēṇa paḍisuyaṁ tīē. kaō sō uvāō, saṁpannō dōhalō. pacchā visāyamuragayāē darisiō sē rāyā. taō samāsatthā ēsā. bhaṇiyā ya mantiṇā-sāmiṇi! paḍhamapasyāē na tāva dēvassa nivēyaṇīō gabbhajammō, avi ya mamaṁ ti; pacchā jahōciyaṁ karissāmi tti. paḍisuyaṁ tīē. annayā uciyasamaē pariṇayappāē diyahē pasūyā dēvī. sadāviō tīē maïsāyarō. bhaṇiyā ya tēṇa-sāmiṇi! akusalō viya dēvassa ēsa gambhō lakkhī yaï. tā alaṁ imiṇā, annattha saṁvaḍaü, maō dēvassa nivēiyaï tti. tīē bhaṇiya-juttamēyaṁ ti. mamaṁ ciya hiyaēṇa mantiyaṁ amaccēṇaṁ ti. taō pēyaṭṭāviō māhavīyābhihāṇāē dāsacēḍīē dāraō. gayā thēvaṁ bhūmibhāgaṁ. etthantarammi diṭṭhā rāiṇā, pucchiyā ya ki m ēyaṁ ti? taō sasajjhasāē vēvamāṇīē bhaṇiyaṁ māhaviyāē dēva! na kiṁci tti. etthantarammi ruiyaṁ bālēṇa. taō dārayaṁ dadrūṇa kuviēṇēva bhaṇiyaṁ rāiṇā-ā pāvē! kimēyaṁ vavasiyaṁ ti? taō thīsahāvakāyarayāē sāhiō sayalavuttantō māhaviyāē. taō rāiṇā gahiō dāraō. cintiyaṁ ca ṇēṇaṁ, na ēsa ēyāṇa hatthē puṇō bhavissaï tti. samappiō annadhāvīṇaṁ sāviyāō ya tāō. jaï kahavi dārayassa pamāō bhavissaï, tā viṇaṭṭhā mama hatthāō tubbhē. nibbhacchiyā dēvī maïsāyarō ya kārāviyaṁ ca dēvīmanti cittāṇurōhiṇā īsi pacchannabhūyaṁ tahāvihaṁ vaddhāvaṇayaṁ. ēvaṁ ca aïkkantō kōi kālō. païṭāviyaṁ nāma dārayassa āṇandō tti. vaḍhiō ēsō, gāhiō kalākalāvaṁ. puvvakammadōsēṇa naravaī paï visamacittō. dinnaṁ sē juvarajaṁ.

anayā pacantavāsī āḍaviō dummaī nāma sāmantarāyā duggabhūmibalagaviō vitthakō sī harāyassa. nivēiyaṁ rāiṇō. visa jiō tēṇa tassuvari vikkhēvō. sabhūmibalaguṇēṇaṁ ca sō parājiō tēṇa. nivēiē ya kuviō rāyā, payaṭṭō sayamēva amarisēṇaṁ. gaō payāṇayatiyaṁ. etthantarammi sindhunaīpuliṇē parivahantē payāṇaē karivarōvariṭṭiēṇaṁ jalāō nāidūrammi ahō kaṭṭhaṁ ti jaṁpiraṁ dilu maṇuyavandraṁ. gaō taṁ cēva bhūmibhāgaṁ rāyā jāva diṭṭhō tēṇa mahākāō aïkasiṇadēhacchavī viṇintanayaṇavisajālābhāsurō gahiyarasanta maṇḍukkagāsō bhayāṇayaviyariyāṇaṇaduppechō duyayarapavelliraṅgō mahayā kurarēṇa gasijjamāṇō juṇṇabhuyaṅgamō, kurarō vi diggayakarōrukāraṇa rattacchabībhaccha ēṇaṁ ayagarēṇa. jahā jahā ya ayagarō kuraraṁ gasaï, tahā tahā sō vi juṇṇabhuyaṅgamaṁ, juṇṇabhuyaṅgamō vi ya rasantamaṇḍukkayaṁ ti. taṁ cēva ēvaṁ vihaṁ jīvalōyasahāvavinbhamaṁ mūḍhahiyayāṇandakārayaṁ sappurisanivvēyahēuṁ vaïyaramavalōiūṇa visaṇṇō rāyā. cintiyaṁ ca ṇēṇaṁ, hanta! ēvaṁ vavatthiē kō uṇa iha uvāō? gasiyappāō kurarō ayagarēṇē, kurarēṇa vi bhuyaṅgamō, bhuyaṅgamēṇa maṇḍukkō tti kaṇṭhagaya pāṇā vi ētē na annonnaṁ viramanti, avi ya ahiyayaraṁ pavattanti, na ya annayaraviṇāsaṇāē mōyāviyā ēē saṁpayaṁ jīvanti. tā kiṁ imiṇā apaḍiyāragōyarēṇa vatthuṇā pulōipaṇaṁ. tajjāviō mattavāraṇō, gaō āvāsaṇiyābhūmi, ārāsiō saha kaḍaēṇaṁ, kayaṁ uciyakaraṇijjaṁ. tō addhakhīṇāē jāmiṇīē suttaviuddhō rāyā. ayagarāivaïyaraṁ sariūṇa cintiuṁ payattō. kahaṁ āvāyamettamahurā vivāgavirasā visōramā visayā. abuhajaṇāṇa bahumayā vibuha jaṇavivajjiyā pāvā.

ēyāṇamēsa lōō karaṇa mōnaṇa sāsayaṁ dhammaṁ

sēvēi jīviyatthī visaṁ va pāvaṁ suhābhiraō

dukkhaṁ pāvassa phalaṁ nāsaō pāvassa dukkhiō niccaṁ

muhiō vi kuṇaü dhammaṁ dhammassa phalaṁ viyāṇantō

maṇḍukkō iva lōō tucchō iyarēṇa pannaēṇaṁ va

ettha gasijaï sō vi hu kurarasamāṇēṇa annēṇa

sō vi hu na ettha sabasō jamhā ayagarakayantavasagō ti

ēvaṁvihē vi lōē visayapasaṅgō mahāmōhō

tā alaṁ yē aṇēyadukkhataruvīyabhūēṇa ahōpurisigāvikārapāraṇaṁ rajjēṇaṁ ti. rajjaṁ hi nāma pāyālaṁ piva duppūraṁ, jiṇṇabhavaṇaṁ piva sulahavivaraṁ, khalasaṁgayaṁ pica virasāvasāṇaṁ, vēsitthiyāhiyayaṁ piva atthavallahaṁ, vammīyaṁ pitra bahumuyaṅga, jīvalōyaṁ piva a ṇiṭṭhiyakajja, sappakaraṇḍayaṁ piva jattaparivālaṇijja aṇabhinnaṁ visambhasuhāṇaṁ, vēsājōvaṇaṁ piva bahujaṇābhilasaṇīyaṁ, akāraṇaṁ ca suddhaparalōyamaggassa tti. tā ēvaṁ pariccaïya payajāmō dhīrapurisasēviyaṁ ubhayalōyasuhāvahaṁ samaṇattaṇaṁ ti. aha kahaṁ puṇa patthuya vavisaē lāghavaṁ na bharissaï? ahavā thēvamēyaṁ ēgajammapaḍibaddhaṁ ti. ēvaṁ cintayantassa aïkkantā rayaṇī, kayaṁ gōsakiccaṁ, païṭṭhaṁ mantimaṇḍalaṁ.

etthantarammi nivēiyaṁ sē vijayavaïnāmāē paḍihārīē-mahārāya! ēsō khu dummaī dēvaṁ sayamēva patthiyaṁ viyāṇiya caṇḍaṁ ca dēvasāsaṇamakgacchiya sirōharāvaddhaparasū dēvasāsaṇāikkamaṇajāyapacchāyāvō kaïvayapurisaparivāriō ihēvāgaō dēvadaṁsaṇasuhābhilāsī paḍihārabhūmīē ciṭṭhaï. ēyaṁ sōūṇa dēvō pamāṇaṁ ti. taō pulōiō rāiṇā maïsāyarō. bhaṇiyaṁ ca tēṇa ījiyāgārakusalēṇa-pavisaü, kō etya dōsō? saraṇāgayavacchalā cēva rāiṇō havanti. taō rāiṇā aṇunāō paviṭṭhō dummaī dēva ēsā sirōharā ēsō ya kuhāḍō tti bhaṇiūṇa paḍiō calaṇēsu. taō abhayaṁ dāūṇa bahu māṇiō rāiṇā, kaō sē ahiyayarasakārō. niyattiūṇa ya rāyā gaō jayaüraṁ. nivēiō rāiṇā niyayābhippāō mantimaṇḍalassa. tēṇa vi ya kiccam ēvēyam iha vaṁsasaṁbhavāṇaṁ rāyāṇaṁ sēsayāṇaṁ pi, kiṁ puṇa tumhāṇaṁ jiṇavayaṇa bhāviyamaīṇaṁ ti, ubhayalōyasāhāraṇaṁ ca saphalaṁ jīviyaṁ dēvassa, vaṇadavasanihā ya kāmabhōgā indhaṇāō cēva jala nti kiṁpāgaphalasamāṇā ya vivāgē, ayaṇḍamaṇōrahabhaṅgakārī ya pahavaï viṇijjiyamurāsurō maccu tti kaliūṇa bahu maniō. tō sadāviyā saṁvacchariyā, bhaṇiyā ya tēṇa-nirūvēha āṇandakumārassa rajjābhisēyadivasaṁ. tēhiṁ bhaṇiyaṁ — jaṁ dēvō āṇavēi. nirūviūṇa sāhiō ṇēhiṁ pañcamō divasō. taō uvaṇīyāī ahisēyamaṅgalāī. taṁ jahā-macchajuyalaṁ puṇṇa kalasō dhavala kusumāī mahāpaümā siddha tyayā puḍhavipiṇḍō vasahō mahantayaṁ dahiyapuṇṇaṁ ca bhaṇḍayaṁ mahārayaṇāī gōrōyaṇā sīhacammaṁ dhavalāyavattaṁ bhadāsaṇaṁ cāmarāō duruyā acchasurā mahādhaō gayamaō dhannāī dugullāṇi annāṇi ya ēvamāiyāī pasatthadavvāī ti. etthantarammi paricintiyaṁ rāiṇā-kāūṇa māṇandakumārassa rajāhisēyaṁ taō gamislāmi dhammaghōsagurusamī ti. ēvaṁ ca cintayantō ahisēyadiṇaṁ paḍicchamāṇō ciṭṭhaï. iō ya puvyakayakammadōsaō amuṇiyanarindāhippāō ghaḍiō dummaïṇā saha āṇandakumārō. mantiyaṁ ca tēhiṁ kahaṁci vaścaṇā paōēṇa vāvāēmō mahārāyaṁ ti. suō ahisē yavuttantō. micchāhinivēsēṇa sacittaduṭṭayāē ya viparīō pariṇaō āṇandassa. cintiyaṁ ca tēṇaṁ-nūṇamahamaṇēga imiṇā vayaē sēṇa māriuṁ vavasiō. tā kahamahamēvaṁ chalijjāmi. ahavā saccaē vi ēyammi vuttantē alaṁ mē rajjēṇa, jaṁ mē ēēṇa dinnaṁ saṁpajjaï. taṁ puṇa salāhaṇijja, jamēyaṁ vāvāiūṇa balā gheppaï ti. etthantarammi sadāviō rāiṇā āṇandō. jāva necchaï āgantuṁ, tō paḍihāraduiō gaō kumārabhavaṇaṁ rāyā. tēṇa vi ya na iō sundaratarō patthāvō ti kaliūṇa puvāṇusayadōsēṇa sahasā haṇa haṇa tti bhaṇiūga ukkhāyāsiṇā akayaparirakkhaṇōvāō muvisatthacittō paḍihāraṁ vāvāiūṇa gāḍhappa hārīkaōrāyā. etthantarammi samuṭṭhāiō kalayalō, saṁjāō nayarasēnasaṁkhōhō, pariveḍhiō samantaō rāyasāhaṇēṇa āṇandō, pāraddhō saṁgāmō. taō rāiṇā niyasarīradōhasavahēṇa sāviyaṁ sennaṁ. bhaṇiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa. kiṁ bhē iyāṇi jujjhiēṇaṁ? ahaṁ tāva vāvāiō cetra davvō, mā ēyaṁ pi vāvāēha, tā karēha rāyābhisēyaṁ ēyassa, ēsa bhē rāya tti. etthantarammi samāṇanō dummaī bandhēhi ṇa nibiḍa bandhēhi. taō jaṁ kumārō āṇavēi tti bhaṇiūṇa āsannībhūō ya sē dummaī. pāḍiyā kulaputtayā, nibhacchiō nāyarajaṇō. taō bandhāviūṇa pañcaïyapurisēhiṁ sukayaparirakkhaṇōvāō kō rāyā. ahiṭṭhiyaṁ rajja,ṭhāviyāō vavatthāō, vasīkayaṁ sāmantamaṇḍalaṁ.

taō aṇusayavasēṇa nēyāviō nayaracārayaṁ naravaī. taṁ ca añcantanimmahamāṇapurīsakalamalagandhaṁ phuḍiyabhittipamuttasirīsivaṁ bhiṇi bhiṇāyamāṇamasayamakkhiyājālaṁ darivivaramuhaviṇiggayamūsaükkaraṁ uparivilambamāṇōrayanimmōyaṁ lūyātantuviraïyaviyāṇayaṁ, vāsaharaṁ piva dussamāē, līlābhūmi piva adhammassa sahōyaraṁ pitra sīmantayamsa, saṁhā viya sambadukkhasamudayāṇaṁ, kulaharaṁ pira savvajāyaṇāṇaṁ, vi ssāsabhūmi piva maccuṇō, siddhikhettaṁ piba kayantassa tti. taō mahācārayaṁ nīō dēvō tti sōūṇa sahasā vimukkakandabhēravaṁ aṇavarayanivaḍamāṇēhi mahallamuttāhalasarisēhiṁ aphajalabāhabinduhiṁ saṁpāiyahārasōhaṁ dēvasōēṇaṁ cēva parimilāṇadēhaṁ nirujjhamāṇaṁ pi niuttapurisēhiṁ maṅgalamaṇivalayajhaṇajhaṇāravuddāmaṁ sabhūyāhiṁ balāō pelliūṇa tē urapoṭṭakuṭṭaṇujjayaṁ taō ya aṇuiyadharaṇiparisakkaṇēṇaṁ sāsasamājariyāṇaṇaṁ paricattakuḍilabhāvattaṇēṇa vi ya adaṁsaṇīyā dēvāvastha tisūyagēhiṁ piva lambālaēhiṁ niruddhanayaṇapasaraṁ cārayamēva pattaṁ kusumāvalīpamuhamantēuraṁ ti. diṭṭhō ya tēṇa kālalōhamayaniyalasamāūriō narabaī. taō asōyapallavāgārēhiṁ hatthēhiṁ aṇuci yāsēvaṇabahulō saṁsārō tti daṁsayantaṁ piva hāralayāvahaṇajaṇiyakhēyaṁ pitra vacchatthalaṁ tāḍayantaṁ ahiyayaramakkandiuṁ pabattaṁ ti. taō rāiṇā ārakkhigēhiṁ ca kahakahavi nivāriyaṁ. bhaṇiyaṁ ca rāiṇā-kimaṇēṇāyāsamettaphalēṇa ahammāṇubandhiṇā ya sōēṇaṁ. aïbahuvi cittarūvō khu ēsa saṁsārō, khēlaṇayabhūyā imassa savvē sarīriṇō, dunnivārō ya pasarō puvakayakammassa, jalaharantaraviṇiggayasōyāma ṇīvalayacañcalā lacchī, suviṇayasamō saṁgamō. ēvamavasāṇāṇi etya rāgavilasiyāṇi. tā kimēiṇā avivēyajaṇāṇusarisēṇa pala viēṇa? pattamēva tubbhēhi jīvalōyasārabhūyaṁ jiṇavayaṇaṁ. tā taṁ cēva aṇuciḍhēha. na taṁ mottūṇa annō dukkhakkhaōvāō tti. taō tamēyamāyaṇṇiya ēvamēvēyaṁ na annaha ti kaliūṇa ya aṇujāṇāviūṇa naravaī jīviyaniravekkhayāē balā cēvāṇandassa gandhavvadattāē vijjāharasamaṇiyāē sayāsē pavanna pacanaṁ ti.

iō ya païdiṇaṁ kayatthaṇāē vi kōhavasabhagacchamāṇēṇa ēdahamettaṁ mē jīviyaṁ kālōiyaṁ saṁpayamaṇasaṇaṁ ti paḍivanna rāiṇā. āra kkhigēhiṁ nivēiyaṁ āṇandassa, kuviō ēsō, pēsiō tēṇa dēvasammō nāma niyamahallaō gaccha bhuñjāvēhi tti. vattavvō ya ēsō abhu ñjamāṇaṁ niyamā vāvāēmi tti. gaō dēvasammō, diṭṭhō tēṇa rāyā, bhaṇiō ya-dēva! devvavasayāṇaṁ pāṇiṇaṁ visamā kajagaï tti. ēsō ya dēvō nāma aṇārāhaṇīō viṇaēṇa, aguṇagāhī guṇīṇaṁ, akālannū samīhiyassa, kēvalamaṇatyō jaṇāṇaṁ, mattahatthi vva sacchandayārī, gaṅgāpavāhō va ujjukuḍilō mahāhavō vva nivāyadakkhō, visagaṇṭhi va nāṇukūlō rasāṇaṁ, paḍikūlō ya samīhiyāṇaṁ aṇukūlō asamī hiyassa. tā jaï vi ēsa ēvaṁbhūō tahāvi purisēṇa khaṇamavi na purisayārō mottavvō tti. jēṇa mahārāya! pucōvajjiyāṇaṁ kammāṇaṁ cēva ēvaṁ nāmaṁ devyō, taṁ ca purisayārajēyamēva vaṭṭaï ti. tā āvalambēu dēvō purisayāraṁ, karēu āhāragahaṇaṁ. jīvamāṇō hi purisō laḍiūṇāvayaṁ avassaṁ dēva! saṁpayaṁ pāvēitti. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ — bhō dēvasamma. na mukō maē cēva ahākālāṇurūvō purisayārō. paḍivanā ya bhāvaō pavvajjā. aō na saṁpayābhilāsaparaṁ mē cittaṁ. uciyakālaṁ ca nāūṇa paḍivanna aṇasaṇaṁ. aō na āhāra gahaṇaṁ karēmi tti. tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — akīramāṇammi āharagahaṇē suō tē kuppissaï. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ — akāraṇō sē kōvō, saccapaïnnā khu tavassiṇō havanti. tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — dēva! viiyavuttantō cēva tuma kumāracariyassa; tā mā tē pamāyaṁ karissaï. etthantarammi cirāyaï dēvasammotti saṁjāyāmarisavēgō ghettūṇa khaggaṁ āgaō āṇandō. bhaṇiyaṁ ca tēṇa-jaï na āhāragahaṇaṁ karēsi, tā imiṇā kayantajīhāṇugāriṇā karavālēṇa sīsaṁ tē chindāmi. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ—

jāṇantō maraṇantaṁ dēhāvāsaṁ asāsayamasāraṁ

kō udhiēja nara vara! maraṇassa avassa mantavvē

gambhapabhiimāvīī salilacchēē saraṁ va sūsantaṁ

aṇusamayaṁ maramāṇaṁ jiyaï tti jaṇō kahaṁ bhaṇaï 1

saṁpatthiyāṇa paralōgamēgasatthēṇa satthiyāṇaṁ va

jaï tattha kōi puraō vacaï bhayakāraṇaṁ kimiha 1

jīyamaṇiñcamavassaṁ maraṇaṁ ti maṇammi nicchayaṁ jassa

sūṇāyārapasussava kā āsā jīviē tassa?

haṁdi! jarādhaṇuhatthō vāhisayaviiṇṇasāyagō ēi

māṇusamayajūhavahaṁ vihāṇavāhō karēmāṇō

na gaṇēi pañcavāyaṁ na ya paḍiyāraṁ cirāṇuvati vā

sacchandasuhaṁ viharaï hari va maccū mayakulēsu

ēka cciya niviṇṇā puṇō puṇō jāiuṁ ca mariuṁ ca

jē bhavamaccubbiggā bhamarōgaharaṁ aṇu varanti

jaramaraṇarōgasamaṇaṁ jiṇavayaṇarasāyaṇaṁ amayasāraṁ

pāuṁ pariṇāmamuhaṁ nāhaṁ maraṇassa bīhēmi

jhōsiyapāvamalāṇaṁ parisāḍiyabaṁbhalōhaniyalāṇaṁ

kiṁ kuṇaï kālamaraṇaṁ kayapaḍiyāraṁ maṇussāṇaṁ

ajjiyatabodhaṇāṇaṁ kalēvaraharē vi nippivāsāṇaṁ

saṁlihiyasarīrāṇaṁ maraṇaṁ pi varaṁ suvihiyāṇaṁ

mugahiyatavapatthayaṇā nivisiūṇa niyamēṇa appāṇaṁ

maraṇaṁ magganti maṇōrahē hi dhīrā dhiisahāyā

jassa mayassēgayarō saggō mokkhō va hōi niyamēṇa

maraṇaṁ pi tassa naravara! ūsavabhūyaṁ maṇūsassa

aṇavarayarōgabhāsuravasaṇavisāṇugayadīhadāḍhassa

kattha gaō vā muccaï kayanta kaṇhāhipōyassa

na vi juddhaṁ na palāyaṁ kayantahathimmi agghaï bhayaṁ vā

na ya sē dīsaï hatthō geṇhaï ya dadaṁ amokkhō ya

jaha vā luṇāi sāsāi kāsaō pariṇayāi kālēṇa

iya bhūyāī kayantō luṇāi jāyāiṁ jāyāī

jaï tāva maccupāsā sacchandamuhaṁ surēsa viyaranti

añcantamaṇōyārō jattha jarārōgavāhīṇaṁ

kiṁ puṇa vāhijarārōgasōganiccuduyammi māṇussē

maccussa sō pamāō jaṁ jiyaï narō nimēsaṁ pi.

tā mā adhīrajaṇa sēviyassa ayasasta dēhi u(a)vayāsaṁ

na hu maccudāḍhalīḍhaṁ indō vi pahū niyattēuṁ.

iya mayamāraṇamettēṇa vaccha! mā niyakulaṁ kalaṅkēhi

geṇhāmi kahaṁ cattaṁ hanta! savāyāē āhāraṁ?

sōūṇa iyaṁ vayaṇaṁ kōvāṇalajaliyarattanayaṇēṇa

japaï ajjāvi kaha pahaō sīsammi khaggēṇaṁ

paricintiyaṁ ca tēṇaṁ namō jiṇāṇaṁ ti muṇiyatattēṇaṁ

punyakayakammadōsō ēsō tti visuddhabhāvēṇaṁ

savvō puvakayāṇaṁ kambhāṇaṁ pāvaē phalavivāṇa

avarāhēsu guṇēsu ya nimittamettaṁ parō hōi

ēvaṁ ca cintayantō puṇō vi hantūṇa pāvakammēṇaṁ

viṇivāiō mahappā akalusacittō sakalusēṇaṁ

mariūṇa ya uvavannō saṇaṁkumārammi mukharō juimaṁ

aha pañcasāgarāū līlārāmē vimāṇammi

iyarō vi ya kāūṇaṁ rajjaṁ mariūga rayaṇapuḍhavīē

uvavannō nēraïō ukkōsāū mahāghōrō

vakkhāyaṁ jaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ sīhā-padā ya taha piyāputtā

sihi-jāliṇimāisuā ettō ēvaṁ pavakkhāmi

atthi ihēva jambuddīvē, avaravidēhē khettē aparimiyajaṇanivāsa, aṇaṇuhūyavāhivēyaṇaṁ, adiṭṭhaparacakkavinbhama, sundarapuranāyagabhūyaṁ kōsaṁbanāma nayaraṁ. jattha sarala sahāvō, thirasiṇēhāṇubandhō, aṇaṅgarāyahāṇī, dhammaphalakappō itthiyājaṇō. jattha piyaṁvaō, sañcavayaṇō, paḍhamābhibhāsī, dhammaniraō ya maṇussabaggō. tattha ya aṇēyasamarasaṁghaṭṭaviṇijjiyadariyanarindāvaṇayapalhatthaviyaḍamaüḍakōḍirayaṇappa hārajiyacaraṇajuyalō rāyā nāmēṇa ajiyasēgō tti. tassa ya sayalarajacintaō, attāṇanivisēsō indasammō nāma māhaṇasacivō. muhaṁkarā sē bhāriyā. iō ya sō āṇandanāraō sāgarōvamantammi naraē khaviūṇa, annē vi kiṁcūṇē cattāri sāgarōvamē saṁsārē samāhiṇḍiya indasammassa māhaṇassa muhaṁ karāē bhāriyāē kucchisi itthiyattāē upavanō ti. jāyā uciyasamaēṇaṁ. kayaṁ sē nāma jāliṇi ti kahāṇayavisē sēṇa. pattā jovvaṇaṁ. dinnā tassa cēva rāiṇō buddhisāgarābhihāṇasacivaputtassa bambhadattassa. kayaṁ pāṇiggahaṇaṁ. bhuñjamāṇāṇa bhōē gaō kōi kālō.

iō ya sō sīhadēvō taō dēvalōgāō caviūṇa acintamāhappayāē kammassa, tīsē cēva jāliṇīē kucchisi puttattāē uvavannō tti. diṭṭhō ya tīē tīē cēva rayaṇīē sumiṇaō-jahā kira suvaṇṇamayapuṇṇakalasō mē uyaraṁ paviṭṭhō, sō ya asaṁjāyapariōsāē viṇiggaō samāṇō kahakaha vibhaggō tti. taṁ ca daṭhūṇa sasajjhasā vi ya viuddhā ēsā. jāō sē saṁkiṇṇō muharasō. na sāhiō ya tīē sumiṇō daïyassa. taō sē vaḍiuṁ payattō gabbhō. jāyā sē dēhamaṇapīḍā. cintiyaṁ ca tīē— vāvāēmitāva ēyaṁ pāva gabhaṁ ti. paüttāī gabbhasāḍaṇāī. kammavivāmaō na vivannō gambhō. muṇiō ya vuttantō bambhadattēṇa. niuttō tēṇa pariyaṇō pasūisamaē, jahā gambhavivattī na havaï tahā tubbhēhiṁ jaïyavvaṁ avi ya bhaṭṭiṇīpariōsanimittaṁ kaïṁci cittaṁ sē vañciūṇa mama nivē iyavvō ti. taō jāō sē dōhalaō-karēmi savvasattāṇamāṇandaṁ, saṁpāḍēmi dēvayāyayaṇāṇaṁ mahāpūyāō, pūēmi bhayavantē dhammaniraē mahātabassī, muṇimō kiṁci paralōyamaggaṁ ti. saṁpāḍiō sē bhattārēṇa ḍōhalō. gambhapabhāvēṇa jāyā maṇōramā lōyassa. pattō ya sūisamaō. pasūyā ēsā. cintiyaṁ ca tīē-kahaṁ puṇa ēsa eddahamettapariyaṇasamakkhaṁ vāvāiyavvō tti? etthantarammi muṇiyataya bhippāyāē bambhadattavayaṇaṁ sariūṇa bhaṇiya bandhujīvābhihāṇāē bālasahīē. bhaṭṭiṇi! pāvō khu ēsa gabbhō. tā alamimiṇā kilēsā— yāsakāraēṇa, varaṁ viiściō ēsō tti. taō kasāyaparavasāē vāvāyaṇammi sahiyaṇalajjāluyāē bhaṇiyaṁ jāliṇīē tumbhē jāṇaha tti. tamō avaṇīō dāraō, nivēiō bambhadattassa. kayaṁ sē tēṇa sayalaṁ sutthaṁ. nīṇiō lōgavāō vāvana gabbhā bhaṭṭiṇi tti. ēvaṁ ca aïkkantō kōi kālō. païṭāviyaṁ nāma bālayassa sihi ti. vaḍiō kalākalāvēṇa dēhōvaca paṇa ya. saṁpāiyaṁ sē niravasēsaṁ kālōciyaṁ bambhadattēṇaṁ. gahiyō pacchā udaraputtō tti. vināō ya vuttantō imiṇā sumiṇaya dasaṇa-gabbhasāḍaṇāiō ya jaṇaṇīē. vēraggiō ēsō.

etthantarammi muṇiyavuttantā puttassa kasāiyā sē jaṇaṇī. cintiyaṁ ca tēṇa-kiha?

ēvaṁvihā kasāyā pāvā bhavaviḍavimūlajalaoghā

mokkhatthamujjaēhiṁ vajjēyayā payattēṇa

ettō kammavivuḍḍī, taō bhavō, tattha dukkhasaṁghāō

tattō ubviyamāṇō payahēja taē mahāpāvē

bhaṇiyaṁ ca—

kalusaphalēṇa na jujjaï kiṁ cittaṁ tatya jaṁ vigayarāgō

santē vi jō kasāē nigiṇhaï sō vi tattullō

takasāōdaēṇaṁ ca sā kuviyā bambhadattassa. paricattaṁ ca sayalakaraṇijja. bhaṇiō bambhadattō. ēyaṁ vā piyaṁ karēhi, mamaṁ vatti, ēyammi aparicattē nāhaṁ pāṇasāhāraṇaṁ udayaṁ pi geṇhāmi tti. nisāmiō ēsa vuttantō sihikumārēṇa. accubiggō niggaō gēhāō. cintiyaṁ ca tēṇa-peccha mē pāvapariṇaī, jēṇa jaṇaṇī vi ēvaṁ vaï ti. ēyavaïyarēṇaṁ ca tāō vi mē duhiō. tā na juttaṁ mē iha acchiuṁ. ēvaṁ cintiūṇamaṇāpucchiūṇa tāyaṁ niggaō nayarāō.

gaō asōgavaṇujjāṇaṁ. diṭṭhō ya tattha asōyapāyavatalaṁgō, sasissaparivāriō, ēgavihasaṁjamaraō, dōasajjhāṇavirahiō, tidaṇḍarahiō, caükasāyamahaṇō paścindiyaniggahaparō, chajjīvanikāyavacchalō, sattabhayavippamukkō, aṭṭhamayaṭṭhāṇarahiō, navabambhacē bhaṇitaṁ ca—

raguttō dasavihadhammamuṭṭhiyamaṇō, ekkārasaṁganāṇī, bārasatavacaraṇakammaniraō ya vijayasiṁhō nāmāyariō tti. tō taṁ daṭṭaṇa samu pannā tassa pītī. cintiyaṁ ca tēṇa-dhannō khu ēsō, jō aṇavadviyasiṇēhavibhamē saṁsārē, ēvaṁ dhammē niraō ti. tā pucchāmi tāva ēyaṁ, kiṁ puṇa ēyassa nivvēyakāraṇaṁ, jēṇa ēsō ēvaṁ dhammē niraō tti. gaō tassa samīvaṁ. saviṇayaṁ paṇamiō bhayavaṁ. kō guruṇā vi dhammalāhō. ubaviṭṭhō tassa pāyamūlē. pucchiō ya bhayavaṁ-kiṁ tē nivvēyakāraṇaṁ? jēṇaṁ ēvaṁ pi sabaṅgasundarāhirāmō, sundarāhirāmayāō cēva pisuṇiyaniyavibhavavitthārō, vibhavavityārā saṁghiyasayaṇabaggō, sayaṇavagganiravekkhamimaṁ īisaṁ nissaṅgayaṁ pavannō si. guruṇā bhaṇiyaṁ — suṇa, kimiha aḍhimaṁsaruhirasaṁgaē sarīrē vi sundarataṁ? kō vā āyāsamētaphalē vihavavitthārē paḍi bandhō, kō vā mumiṇayasamāgamacañcalē sayaṇē tti. avi ya—

sayaṇassa vi majhagaō rōgābhihaō kilissaï ihēgō

sayaṇō vi ya sē rōgaṁ na ’viriścaī nē ya nāsēi

majjhammi bandhavāṇaṁ ēkō maraï kaluṇaṁ ruyantāṇaṁ

na ya ṇaṁ dhārēi taō bandhujaṇō nēva dārāī

ekkō karēi kammaṁ phalamavi tassekkaō samaṇuhōi

ekkō jāyaï maraha ya paralōyaṁ ekkaō jāi

pattēyaṁ pattēyaṁ niyagaṁ kammaphalamaṇuhavantāṇaṁ

kō kassa jaē sayaṇō kō kassa va hōi anajaṇō?

mariūṇa vēriō vi hu jāyaï jaïṇagō, muō vi hum̐ rivū tti

tā agavaṭṭhiyabhāvē sayaṇē saṅgō ti mōhaphalaṁ

annaṁ ca. suṇa, amhāṇamēva jaṁ vattaṁ—

atthi ihēva vijaē laïcchinilayaṁ nāma nayaraṁ. tattha sāgaradattō nāma satyavāhō, sirimaī sē bhāriyā, tāṇaṁ ahaṁ suō tti. kumārabhāvē vaṭṭamāṇō gaō tannayarāsannamēva lacchipavayaṁ. diṭṭhō ya tattha ēgammi vibhāgē siṇiddhapattasaṁcaō, dharāpaviṭhṭhadīhapāyagō, nāliēripāyavō tti. taṁ ca daṇi samuppannaṁ mē kōuyaṁ. cintiyaṁ ca maē-ahō! acchariyaṁ. eddahamettassavi pāyavassa ēdaha mettāō vibhāgāō ōyariūṇa pāyaō dharaṇiṁ paviṭṭhō tti. tā nūṇametya kāraṇēma hōyavvaṁ.

etthantarammi ya ayaṇḍammi cēva saṁjāō mē pamōō, viyambhiō surahimāruō, vimukō sahajō vi vērāṇubandhō pasugaṇēhi, bhuvaṇasirīē viya samaddhāsiō lacchipavvaō, sabbōuyakusumēhi vi puphiyāī kāṇaṇujjāṇāī, pamuiyā vihaṁgasaṁghāyā, maṇaharuttālaramma ca guñjiyaṁ chappayāvalīhiṁ, visuddhapayāsamatāvaṁ ca tamuddēsamujjōiuṁ payattōravī. tō maē cintiyaṁ aha puṇa kiṁ imaṁ bhuvaṇacchērayaṁ ti. etthantarammi taruṇaravimaṇḍalanihaṁ, suvisuddhajaccakavaṇaṁ, aṇēyarayaṇamaṇḍiyaṁ, jayajayaravābūriyanahaṅgaṇaṁ, gijjantatiyasamaṅgalaṁ, nivaḍantakusumavuddhi, aṇēyatiyasapariyariyaṁ, vijiyasaṁsāracakapisuṇaya, avara disāō samōvayanta bhayavaō ajiyadēvatitthayarassa didaṁ maē dhammacakkaṁ ti. tayaṇantaraṁ ca mahagdhaguṇarayaṇabhūsiyā siyambaradhāriṇō aṇēgē sāhayō, taō suradhariyakundadhavalāyabattō dunduhiniṇāyabahiriyanahaṅgaṇō, virāyantadivyabhāmaṇḍalō, suravaïsamukhittacārucāmarō, surāsuramaṇuyavandrasaṁthuō, kālāyarupavaratu rukkadhūvamahamahentagandhō, gandhavaṭṭibhūō añcantasōmō kañcaṇamayadivdhakamalāvalīē parisakkamāṇō bhayavaṁ, tilōyanāhō, nitthiṇṇa bhavasamuddō ajiyadēvatitthayarō tti. taṁ ca da ṭhūṇa samuppaṇṇō mē pamōō, paṇaṭṭhuṁ micchattatimirēṇaṁ, viyambhiyaṁ dhammavavasāraṇaṁ. cintiyaṁ ca maē-dhannō ahaṁ, jēṇa maē tilōyacintāmaṇī bhayavaṁ uvaladdhō tti.

etthantarammi ya kaya tiyasēhiṁ bhayavaō maṇikaṇayakalahōyamayanimmiyapāyāratiyaṁ suvihattadivyatōraṇaṁ, rayaṇamayavicittaka visīsaya, ūsiyamahākē univahaṁ, guñjantamahuyarāmōyasōhiyaṁ, ūsiyasiyāyavattamaṇaharaṁ, vēruliyadivasīhāsaṇaṁ, mahallasīhadhayacakama ṇḍiyaṁ samōsaraṇaṁ ti. paviṭṭhō bhayavaṁ. patthuyā dhammakahā. kahiō bhagavayā asāsaō jīvalōgō. agaō amhāṇaṁ. taō taṁ puvvakōuyaṁ samaṇussarantēṇa pucchiō bhayavaṁ maē tilōyanāhō. bhaya! kiṁ puṇa tassa nāliēripāyavassa pāyaō ōiṇṇō, kiṁ atthi tattha daviṇajāyaṁ kiṁ vā nahi (nihī), kiṁparimāṇaṁ vā, kēṇa vā taṁ ṭhaviyaṁ, kīisō vā tassa vivāgō tti? bhagavayā bhaṇiyaṁ — muṇa, lōhadōsēṇa pāyō ōiṇṇō. atthi tattha daviṇanāyaṁ. taṁ ca dīṇārasattalakhaparimāṇaṁ. tumaē tēṇaṁ ca nāliēri jīvēṇa ṭhāviyaṁ. dhammasāhaō ya vivāgō ēyassa. maē bhaṇiyaṁ — bhayavaṁ! kahaṁ puṇa maē imiṇā ya ṭhaviyaṁ, kahaṁ ca mama īdisō vivāgō imassa vi īdisō tti. bhagavayā bhaṇiyaṁ—suṇa,

atthi ihēba vijaē amaraüraṁ nāma nayaraṁ. tattha amaradēvō nāma gāhāvaī hotyā. sundarī sē bhāriyā. tāṇaṁ ca tubbhē duvē vi upparopparajāyagā guṇacandabālacandābhihāṇā ya puttaya tti. saṁpattajovvaṇā ya mahantaṁ cēlāibhaṇḍaṁ ghettūṇa vāṇijjavaḍiyāē āgayā imaṁ dēsaṁ. viṇiōiyaṁ bhaṇḍaṁ, samāsāiō iṭṭhalāhō. etthantarammi vijayavammanaravaïṇā āḍhattō lacchinilayasāmī sūratēō nāma naravaī. sō ya nayarē gajhaṁ chōga gahiyasāranayaralōō ārūḍhō imaṁ pavvayaṁ. tumbhē vi tēṇēva naravaïṇā saha ghettūṇa daviṇajāyaṁ para balabhaēṇa ārūḍhā lacchipavvayaṁ. ṭhiyā ya ēyammi paēsē nihāṇīkayamālōciūṇa imaṁ daviṇajāyaṁ. aïkantō kōi kālō. taō lōhadōsēṇa bhāgiō tti kariya visapōgakaraṇēṇaṁ vāvāviō tumaṁ guṇacandēṇa. suddhasahāvattaṇēṇaṁ ca uvavannō vaṁtarasurēsu. guṇacandō vi ya aparibhujiūṇa taṁ davvaṁ ettha cēva pacaē mahābhuyaṅgaḍakō mariūṇa uppanō rayaṇappahāē narayapuḍhavīē nāraō. tō tuma dekhaṇa paliōvamamahāuyaṁ pāliūṇa taō cuō etthēva vijaē ṭēkaṇāurē nayarē hariṇandissa satyavāhassa vamumaīē bhāriyāē kucchisi putta tāē upavanō si. jāō kālakkamēṇaṁ. païṭāviyaṁ ca tē nāmaṁ dēvadattō tti. pattō kumārabhāvaṁ. etthantarammi taō vi guṇacandō naragāō udhvaṭṭiūṇa lōhadōsēṇametthēva lacchipavvaē ēyassa cēva nihāṇassa paccāsannapaēsē uppannō bhuyaṅgamō ti. pariggahiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa taṁ davvaṁ. etthantarammi lacchinivāsiṇīdēvayāmahammi samāgaō tumaṁ lacchipavvayaṁ. kayā dēvayāē pūyā. dinnaṁ dīṇāṇāhāṇa davi ṇajāyaṁ. saṁpāiō bhōyaṇōvayārō. taō tumaṁ puvyabhavasiṇē hēṇaṁ rammayāē pavvayassa paribhamantō āgaō imaṁ uddēsaṁ. diṭṭhō bhuyaṅgamēṇaṁ. taō lōhadōsēṇa ēsa ēyaṁ daviṇajāyaṁ geṇhissaï tti ḍakō caraṇadēsammi. accuggayāē visassa takkhaṇā cēva nivaḍiō dharaṇivaḍhē. pāsavattiṇā ya tē pariyaṇēṇa vāvāviō bhuyaṅgamō. uppannō etthēva patraē sīhattāē ti. tuma pi mariūṇa etthēva vijaē kayaṅgalāē nayarīē sivadēvassa kulaüttayassa jasōharāē bhāriyāē kucchisi puttattāē uvavannō si. jāō kālakkamēṇa. païṭāviyaṁ ca tē nāma indadēvō tti. pattō jovvaṇaṁ. iō ya tēṇa sīhajīvēṇa punvabhavanbhatthabhāvaṇāō ōhasannāē pariggahiyaṁ taṁ davvaṁ. ēvaṁ ca gaō kōi kālō. annayā ya vīradēvanakhaṇā niyasāmiēṇa pēsiō tuma lacchinilayasāmiṇō māṇahaṅgassa samīvaṁ. āgacchamāṇō ya kaïvaya. purisaparivāriō kālakkamēṇa pattō imaṁ uddēsaṁ. upaviṭṭhō nīvapāyavassa heḍhē. etthantarammi giriguhāmuhagaēṇaṁ diṭṭhō si sīhēṇaṁ. taō lōhasannāvivajjāsiyacittaṇaṁ vāvāviō si imiṇā, imō vi ya tumaē ti. uvavannā ya tubbhē etthēva vijayammi siritthalagē paṭṭaṇē jakhadāsasanniyassa caṇḍālasta māijakkhāē bhāriyāē jamalabhāugattāē tti. jāyā kālakkamēṇaṁ. païṭāviyāī nāmāī tujjhaṁ kālasēṇō, iyarasma caṇḍa sēṇō tti. pattā ya jōjaṇaṁ. annayā āhēḍayanimittaṁ gayā lacchipavvayaṁ, vāvāiō kōlō. sō ya ēyammi vēva nihāṇakapaēsē visasiō. pajāliō jalaṇō. jalaṇapakaṁ taṁ khāiuṁ payattā. etthantarammi kaṭṭārayaṁ nisāṇiūṇa kahaṁci aṇa tthadaṇḍaō cēva dharaṇiṁ khaṇamāṇēṇa ukladō nihāṇayakalasassa ēgadēsō caṇḍasēṇēṇaṁ. pavattō gōviuṁ, lakkhiō ya tumaē. taō dabalōhēṇaṁ vīsatthō tumaṁ vāghāiō tēṇa. unabannō vālayappahāē naragapuḍhavīē pañcasāgarōvamāū nāragō. imō vi tahabalobhēṇa taṁ caïva dēsaṁ amuścamāṇō aïkantēsu kaïvayavarisēsu anuciūṇa taṁ davvaṁ annavēriyacaṇḍālaviṇivāiō samāgō uppanō tamābhihāṇāē naraya puḍhavīē aṭārasasāgarotramāū nāragō tti. taō tuma paḍi puṇṇē ahāuē naragāō ubaṭṭhiūṇa etthē. vijaē sirimaīē sannivēsammi sālibhahassa gāhāvaïssa nandiṇīra bhāriyāē kucchisi puttattāē uvavannō tti. jāō ya kālakamēṇa. païṭāviyaṁ tē nāma bālasundarō tti. pattō jōvaṇaṁ. etthantaramma sīladēvāṇagārasamīvē pattō taē apattapubbō jiṇavarapaṇīō dhammō. paripāliyaṁ sāvayattaṇaṁ. kaō ya jahāvihiṁ dēhaccāō. upavannō lantayābhihāṇē dēvalōē kiṁcūga tērasasāgarōvamāū vēmāṇiō tti. tattha paribhunniūṇa divyabhōē ahāuyaparikkhaēṇa cuō samāṇō etthēva vijaē hathigāurē nayarē muhatthissa nagarasēhissa kantimaīē bhāriyāē kucchisi puttattāē uvavannō si, iyarō vitaō naragāō uvvaṭṭiūṇa tatthēva nayarē tujjha cēva piuṇō sōmilābhihāṇāē gharadāsīē kuñchisi puttattāē tti. jāyā kālakamēṇa. païṭāviyāī nāmāī-tujjha samudadattō, iyarassa maṅgalagō tti. pattā ya tumbhē ahākamēṇēva kumārabhāvaṁ.

etthantarammi pavannō taē aṇaṅgadēvagaṇisamīvē jiṇadēsiō dhammō. kayā dēsaviraī. pariṇīyā ya lacchinilayaśasiṇō sāvayassa acalasatthavāhassa dhūyā jiṇamaī. annayā ya maṅgaladuiō jiṇamaīnimittamēva payaṭṭō lacchinilayaṁ. āgaō ya kaïvayapayāṇagēhiṁ. pattō tamuddēsaṁ, jattha nihāṇaṁ ti. taō bahulapattalayāē paēsassa vīsa miyō muhattayaṁ. diṭṭhō ya taē pāmāḍajjhāḍayassa imammi paēsē viṇiggaō pāyō. bhaṇiyaṁ kōugēṇa-bhō maṅgalaga! ettha parasē kēṇaï daviṇajāēṇa hōyatvaṁ. tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — nihālēmō ti. taē bhaṇiyaṁ — alaṁ imiṇā. kōugamettamēva mē kahaṇanimittaṁ, na uṇa daïviṇalōhō. tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — ahiyayaraṁ mē kōuyaṁ tā nihālēmō, kō estha paramatthō tti? tō aṇabhippēyaṁ pi bhavaō payaṭṭō taṁ tahāvihēṇa tikkhasārakaṭṭēṇa khaṇium̐ ti. diṭṭō ya tēṇa thēvabhūmibhāē kalasakaṇṭhaō. taō puvakayakammalōhadōsēṇa cintiyaṁ maṅgalagēṇa. ahō! mahatthō ēsa nihī. jaï kahaṁci bhaṭṭidārayaṁ vaściu gi hiuṁ pāviyaï ti. etthantarammi diṭṭhō tumaē vi kalasa kaṇṭhagō. bhaṇiō ya ēsō-bhada maṅgalaga! alaṁ imiṇā; ēhi, nayaraṁ gacchāmō tti. taō pūriūṇa tamuddēsaṁ hiṭṭhō viya payaṭṭō maṅgalagō. bhaṇiō ya tumaē-bhadda! na taē kassaï puraō ēsa vaïyarō ahigaraṇa hēubhūō jaṁpiyavvotti. tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — bhaṭṭidāraya! na jaṁpāmō. cintiyaṁ ṇēṇa-maē vi viṇā ēsa ēyaṁ geṇhissaïtti. aō sē ēsa payāsō. tā kahaṁ ahaṁ imiṇā vaścijjāmi. tā jāva cēva na geṇhaï ēsa ēyaṁ, tāva cēva ahaṁ kēṇaï uvāēṇa vāvāissaṁ ti. etthantarammi pattā nayaraṁ. ārāmasamīvaṭṭhiēṇaṁ bhaṇiō tumaē maṅgalagō. bhada maṅgalaga! gaccha, sasurakulapaütti mē kuō vi uvalahiya saṁvāēhi, jēṇa pavisāmō nayaraṁ ti. payaṭṭō maṅgalagō. cintiyaṁ ca ṇēṇaṁ-paviṭṭhō khu ēsō lahuṁ cēva ēyaṁ geṇhissaï. tā tahāṇuciṭṭhāmi, jahā na ēsa etya pavisaï. gacchantō ya mē suhavāvāyaṇijō bhavissaï. tā ēyaṁ sē nivēēmi. jahā, itthisahāvaō kulaviruddhamācari ūṇa pavisiyā tē ghariṇī. aō añcantamubbiggaṁ tē sasurakulaṁ. suyaṁ ca amhāṇamāgamaṇamēēhiṁ, aō ahiyayaraṁ lajjiyāṇi. tā na juttametya pavisiuṁ ti saṁpahāriya taō nayaraṁ pavisiūṇa kayakālakkhēvō māyācariēṇa vivaṇṇamuhacchāō āgō tē samīvaṁ. nivēiyaṁ jahā cintiyaṁ. taō visaṇṇō tumaṁ. cintiyaṁ ca tumaē-dhiratthu isthibhāvassa, jamēvaṁvihā vi sāvayakuluppannā vi suvinā yajiṇavayaṇasārā vi ubhayalōyaviruddhamāyaraï. ahavā natthi dukaraṁ mōhabhāvassa. tā alaṁ mē iyāṇi pi gihavāsēṇa. pavajjāmō tittha yarabhāsiyaṁ sāhudhammaṁ. ēvamavasāṇō khu ēsa siṇēhabandhō. tā alaṁ mē sagihagamaṇēṇaṁ pi. iō cēva gacchāmi, jattha bhagavaṁ aṇa ṅgadēvō. ēsō vi maṅgalagō iō cēva vaccaü gharaṁ, krimimiṇā kilisiēṇaṁ ti saṁpahāriūṇa bhaṇiō jahācintiyamēva maṅgalagō. cintiyaṁ ca ṇēṇaṁ-ahō!! ēsa māyācariēṇaṁ maṁ vaściūṁ ujaō. tā kahamahamimiṇā vañcijāmi tti. tā bhaṇāmi tāva ēyaṁ. jāva tuma na cintiyadēsaṁ pattō si, tāva kahamahaṁ bhavantaṁ pariccayāmi. ēvaṁ kaïvayadiṇāṇi imiṇā saha gacchiūṇa vāvāissaṁ imaṁ ti. cintiūṇa bhaṇiō tumaṁ imiṇā. paḍibhaṇiyaṁ ca tumaē. bhada maṅgalaga! jaï tē nibbandhō, tā ēvaṁ havaü ti. taō pucchissāmō kaṁci sāhuṁ, kahiṁ bhayavaṁ aṇaṅgadēvō tti? mantiūṇa patthiyā tumbhē paḍipahēṇa. aïkantā kaïvi vāsarā. annayā aïvisamaraṇṇama jjhattinahayalasarantaramabhigaē diṇayaramma mahāsāhasa ti kaliūṇa accantakhuddahiyaēṇaṁ lōhadōsaō tahā vi aṇiyattamāṇēṇaṁ suvī satthahiyō cēva pahaō tuma piḍidēsammi churigāē maṅgalagēṇaṁ ti. etthantarammi adāṇapaḍivannō aṇēyasamaṇapariyariō tatthēva parasē sahasā samāgaō agaṅgadēvō. diṭṭhō tuma aggagāmiēhiṁ sāhūhiṁ. etthantarammi sajjhasēṇa churiyamavahāya naṭṭhō maṅgalagō. cintiyaṁ ca tubhaē-hā! kimēyaṁ ti. kiṁ takarā samāgayā bhavē. jōviyaṁ piṭṭhaō, jāka diṭṭhō sasaṁbhamāulaṁ pāyamāṇō maṅgalagō cintiyaṁ ca tumaē-na ettha annē cōrā dīsanti, palāyaī ya ēsō. tā kimēyaṁ ti? etthantaramni diṭṭhā sōṇiyāṇurañjiyā churiyā. gahiyā ya sā taē paccabhinnāyā ya taō saṁjāō tē viyapō. kimēyaṁ maṅgalagēṇa vasiyaṁ bhavē? ahavā na ēyassa kiṁpi ēvaṁ vavasāyakāraṇaṁ uspekkhāmi. tā sadēmi tāva ēvaṁ ti. ēsēva mē ettha paramatthaṁ sāhissaï. sadiō maṅgalagō, jāva ahiṁyayaraṁ palāiumāraddhō tō avagaō tē viyappō. hanta! ēēṇa cēva kvasiya ti. tā kiṁ puṇa sē imassa vavasāyasta kāraṇaṁ. āmōiō nihāṇayavr̥ttantō. cintiyaṁ ca tumaē-natthi akaraṇijja nāma lōhavasagāṇaṁ ti. aō cēva nimittaō jiṇamaīvuttantī vi imiṇā vigappiō bhavē. annahā kahaṁ tārisī mahākūlapasūyā suvināyajiṇāyaṇasārā ya tārisaṁ ubhayalōgaviruddhaṁ karissaï. etthantarammi pattā tē sāhakō tamuddēsaṁ. paccabhinnāō ya tēhiṁ. vandiyā ya tumaē. dhammalāhiō sāhūhiṁ. pucchiō ya tēhiṁ. sāvaya! kipēyaṁ ti? sāhiō tumaē tēsiṁ jahāvattō vuttantō. samāsāsiō sāhūhiṁ. etthantarammi diṭṭhō aṇaṅgadēvēṇaṁ. vandiō sō taē. abhiṇandiō tuma imiṇā dhammalāhēṇa. pucchiō paüttiṁ. sāhiyā tumaē. samāsāsiō guruṇā. niyattō tumaṁ samaṁ sāhugacchēṇa. pattō thāṇēsaraṁ nāma sannivēsaṁ. ṭhiō tattha gurū māsakappaṁ. paüṇō tē pahārō. uvaladdhā jahaṭṭhiyā jiṇamaīpaüttī. cintiyaṁ ca tumaē-ahō! maṅgalassa vañcaṇāpagārō, ahō! vicittayā mōhassa, ahō! aṇuvāēyayā saṁsārassa. tā jaï vi akhaṇḍiyasīlā jiṇamaī, tahāvi alaṁ gihāsamēṇa. saṁpāḍēmi ubhayalōgasuhāvahaṁ samīhiyaṁ. suvināyajiṇavayaṇasārā ya sā tullacittā ya mē pāēṇa. tā sōūṇa imaṁ vaïyaraṁ sā vi ya pavvaïssaï tti. ēvaṁ ca kaē sā vi hu tavassiṇī imāō dukkhabahulāō bhavasamuddāō samuttāriyā havaï. alaṁ ca apavvaïyassa tīē daṁsaṇēṇaṁ. bahuvigdhā caraṇapaḍipattī, suhāvahā ya ēsā cēva tti cintiūṇa pavvaïō aṇaṅgadēvagurusamīvē. aïkkantō kōi kālō. suō ēsa vaïyarō kuōvi jiṇamaīē. saṁviggā ēsā. cintiyaṁ ca tīē. sōhaṇamaṇuciṭṭhiyaṁ ajjaü tēṇa. kilēsāyāsabahulō ēsa saṁsārō, viōgāvasāṇō ya saṁgamō, dāruṇō ya vivāgō visayaparibhōgassa, dullahaṁ ca maṇuyabhāvaṁmi jiṇamayaṁ, ubhayalōyasuhāvahaṁ ca ēvaṁ cēva tti. taō sā ēvaṁ vicintiūṇa aṇunaviya jaṇaṇijaṇaē aṇunāyā tēhiṁ āgayā taṁ annēsamāṇī, jattha tumaṁ. diṭṭhō ya aṇāē. pecchiūṇa nivvuipurapaṭṭiyaṁ tumaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ ca aṇāē. ajjaütta, sōhaṇamaṇuciṭṭhiyaṁ tumaē. chinnā mōhavallī. avalambiyaṁ sappurisacariyaṁ. samuttāriyā ahaṁ appā ya imāō bhavasamuddāō tti. ahiṇandiūṇa pavanā pavvajja aṇaṅgadēvagurusamīvē. aïkkantō kōi kālō. niraïyāraṁ sāmaṇṇamaṇuvāliūṇa tumaṁ kālakkamēṇa maō samāṇō uvavannō paṇuvīsasā garōvamāū gēvejjagasurō tti. iyarō vi maṅgalagō tamatthaṁ pariggahiya mahāsilāsaṁcaocchāiyaṁ ca kāūṇa tammamattēṇa tatthēva dēsē kuṇi māhārēṇa kilēsasaṁpāiyavittī ahāuyaṁ pāliūṇa maō samāṇō uvavanō tamābhihāṇāē narayapuḍhavīē bāvīsasāgarōvamāū nāragō tti. tō ya mahayā parikilēsēṇa tamahāuyaṁ pāliūṇa uvyaṭṭō samāṇō etthēva vijaē rahabaddhaṇaē gāmē velliyagassa caṇḍālassa gēhē chēlagattāē uvavannō tti. pattō ya jōvaṇaṁ. annayā ya bahuchēlagamajjhagaō tō rahavaddhaṇāō jayatthalē nijamāṇō pattō imaṁ nihāṇa guddēsaṁ. samuppannaṁ ca sē tamuddēsamavalōiūṇa puvvabhavabbhāsaō jāissaraṇaṁ. taō lōhadōsēṇa viyaṭṭō velliyagassa necchaï taō uddēsāō annatthamabhigantuṁ, cōijjantō vi puṇō puṇō niyattaï tti. kōhābhibhūēṇaṁ vāvāiō velliyagēṇa. uppannō tatthēva nihā ṇaguhēsē mūsaō. pariggahiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa ōhasannāē taṁ davvaṁ. aṇuvāliyaṁ kaṁci kālaṁ. annayā sōmacaṇḍō nāma jyāriō kahaci parimbhamantō āgō tamuddēsaṁ. uvaviṭhṭhō sālapāyavasamīvē. taō annāṇalōhadōsēṇa tassa puraō sāmarisamiva paribhamiumāḍhattō. vāvāiō ya tēṇaṁ. samuppannō ya tassēva paṇaṭṭhasavaṇanāsigāē duggiligābhihāṇāē bhāriyāē kucchisi puttattāē tti. jāō kāla lakamēṇaṁ. païṭāviyaṁ ca sē nāma ruddacaṇḍō ti. pattō aṇēganaṇasaṁtāvagārayaṁ visapāyavō na jovvaṇaṁ. asamañjasaṁ ca vavahariumā rakhō. annayā gahiō khattamuhē. uvaṇīō rāiṇō samarabhāsurassa. samāṇattō vajjhō. bhinnō sūliyāē ārakkhiyanarēhiṁ. maō ya samāṇō samuppannō sakkarābhihāṇāē nāyapuḍhavīē kiṁcūṇatisāgarōvamāū nāragotti. tō ahāuyamaṇuvāliūṇa uvvaṭṭō samāṇō samuppannō etthēva vijaē etthēva lacchinilaē asōgadattassa sēhissa suhaṅkarāē bhāriyāē kucchisi itthigattāē tti. jāyā uci yasamaēṇaṁ. païṭāviyaṁ ca sē nāma siriyādēvi tti. pattā jovvaṇaṁ. dinnā sāgaradattasatthavāhaputtassa samuddadattassa. vattō vivāhō bhuñjanti bhōē tti. etthantaraṁmi tumaṁ gēvēja gēhitō caviūṇa imāē cēva kucchisi samuppannō puttattāē tti. jāō kālakkamēṇa. païṭṭā viyaṁ ca sē nāma sāgaradattō tti. pattō jovvaṇaṁ. paḍibuddhō ya dēvasammāyariyasamīvē. pariṇīyā īsarakkhandasāvagassa dhūyā nandiṇi tti. bhōgasuhamaṇuhavantāṇaṁ kālakamēṇaṁ jāō tē puttō. annayā ya puttajammabhudayanimittēṇaṁ cēva saparivārō āgaō ujjāṇigāē imaṁ cēva nihāṇaguhēsaṁ. diṭṭhō ya tumaē puttajjhayanivēsaṇanimittaṁ khaḍḍē khaṇamāṇēṇaṁ nihāṇagakalasakaṇṭhēgadēsō tti. taō tamannattha nivēsiūṇa taṁ ca paēsaṁ puṇaravi tahēva kariūṇa bhuttuttarakālē paviṭṭhō nayaraṁ. cintiyaṁ tumaē. kimetya juttaṁ ti ambaṁ tāva pucchāmi. sāhiō imīē ēsa vaïarō. pucchiyā ēsā kim ettha juttaṁ ti. tīē bhaṇiyaṁ. mama tāva taṁ paēsaṁ daṁsēhi, taō jaṁ juttaṁ, taṁ bhaṇissāmi tti. dāviō sē paēsō. annāgalōhadōsēṇa cintiyaṁ ca tīē. vāyāēmi ēyaṁ taō ēgāiṇī geṇhissāmi. ēya cintiuṇa bhaṇiō tumaṁ. puttaya, pabhūyanēyaṁ davvaṁ. ēyaṁmi gheppamāṇē kayāi narabaī avagacchē. taō ya sō sēsadavāvahāraṁ pi mā karissaï tā alaṁ tāva ēiṇā, avasarēṇa geṇhissāmō tti. taē bhaṇiyaṁ. amba, jaṁ tumaṁ āṇavēsi. paviṭṭhāī nayaraṁ. aïkantā kaïvi diyadā tujhaṁ suhēṇaṁ, imīē puṇaṁ puyabhavanmatyalōhadōsēṇa tuha maraṇacintōvāyapajjāulāē dukkhēṇaṁ ti. paricintiō uvāō dēmi sē pōsahōvavāsapāraṇayabhōyaṇē visaṁ ti. taō upāsalahusarīrō visappaōēṇa lahuṁ cetra na bhavissaï tti cintiūṇa paüttaṁ visaṁ. laddhō tumaṁ tēṇaṁ. etthantaraṁmi diṭṭhō nandiṇīē. kaō aṇāē kōlāhalō. taō ahiyayaraṁ tē kūjiuṁ payattā jaṇaṇī. saṁmiliō lōyanivahō. taō ēkēṇa siddhaputtēṇa visāvahāramantasāmatthaō sāhammiō tti kaliūṇa jīvāviō. samuppannā ya tē cintā. ēvamaṇēgōvadayabhāyagaṁ maṇuyāga jīvitaṁ. tā alaṁ gihavāsēṇaṁ. mā pugō vi mē pamattassa ēvamēva pāṇāvagamō bhavissaï. aō pavajjāmi pavaja ti cintiūṇa jahōciēṇa vihiṇā pavannō dēvasammagurusamīvē pavvaja ti. parivāliūṇa niraïyāraṁ kāūṇa ya kālamāsē kālaṁ unabannō tīsasāgarōvamāū gēvējagasurō ti. ēsā ca tē jaṇaṇī tahavvalobhēṇa tattha cēva sahatyasippa nimmiyaṁ mahāpeḍhē kāūga putta yahayariṇāmamaṇiyanarayāuyā abhuñjiūṇa taṁ davvaṁ mayā samāṇī dhūmappabhāē narayapuḍhavīē uvavannā pannarasasāgarokmaḍhiī nāragō tti. taō ubaṭṭā samāṇī nāṇātiriēmu āhiṇḍiya pubbabhavabhatyobhadōsaō ettha nāliēri pāyavattāē upabanna tti. tuma pi ya taō sāgaradatta seṭṭhigēhē sirimaīē kucchisi puttattāē uvavannō si. doṇhaṁ pi tumhāṇaṁ saṁpayaṁ imā avatthā. ēsa ettha baïyarō ti.

tō mamēyaṁ sōūṇa samuppannō saṁvēgō, virattō bhavacāragāō magō. aṇunnaviō bhayavantasannihāṇē tahavvavaïyaraṁ naravaī. aṇunnāō ya tēṇa tō taṁ gēhāviya sayaladuhi yasattāṇaṁ dāūṇa pabannā maē vijayadhammagagaharassa samīvē pabyajja tti.

sihikumārēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — bhayavaṁ! ēvamēyaṁ, īisō cetra ēsa saṁsārō. dhannō tumaṁ, jō ēvamabhipayaïō tti. aha kaïvihī puṇa dāṇāibhēyaṁ paḍucca paṇīō bhayavayā dhammō. bhayavayā bhaṇiyaṁ — suṇa

dhammō caüvvihō dāṇa-sīla-tava-vivihabhāvaṇāmaïō

sāvaya! jiṇēhi bhaṇiō tiyasinda narindanamiēhiṁ

dāṇaṁ ca hōi tivihaṁ nāṇā'bhaya-dhammuvaggahakaraṁ ca

jaṁ tattha nāṇadāṇaṁ tamahaṁ vocchaṁ samāsēṇaṁ

dinnēṇa jēṇa jīvō vinnāyā hōi bandha-mokkhāṇaṁ

taṁ hōi nāṇadāṇaṁ sivasuhasaṁpattibīyaṁ tu

dinnēṇa tēṇa jīvō puṇṇaṁ pāvaṁ ca bahuvihamasēsaṁ

sammaṁ viyāṇamāṇō kuṇaï pavittiṁ nivittiṁ ca

puṇṇammi pabattantō pāvaï ya lahuṁ narāmarasuhāī

nārayatiriyaduhāṇa ya muccaï pāvāu suṇiyattō

tiriyāṇa va maṇuyāṇa va amuramurāṇaṁ ca hōi jaṁ mukkhaṁ

taṁ savvapayattēṇaṁ pāvaï nāṇappayāṇēṇaṁ

pāvēi ya muvisālaṁ mokkhasuhaṁ muhaparaṁparēṇēva

tassēva pahāvēṇaṁ sundara! vimalassa nāṇassa

ēvaṁ ihalōyammi vi paralōyammi ya suhāi nāṇēṇaṁ

pāvēi jēṇa jīvō tamhā taṁ dāṇapavaraṁ tu

ihalōyapāralōiyamuhāī savvāī tēṇa dinnāī
