jīvāṇa phuḍaṁ savvannubhāsiyaṁ dēi jō nāṇaṁ

gayarāgadōsamōhō samvannū hōi nāṇadāṇēṇaṁ

maṇuyāmuramuramahiō kamēṇa siddhiṁ ca pāvēi

ēyaṁ khu nāṇadāṇaṁ sundara! saṁkhēvaō samakkhāyaṁ

dentassa gāhagassa ya hiyamēgantēṇa vinnēyaṁ

puḍhavi-daga-agaṇi-māruya-vaṇassaīkāiyāṇa jīvāṇaṁ

bēindiya-tēindiya-caürō-pañcindiyāṇaṁ ca

jā ēyāṇamahiṁsā samma maṇa-vayaṇa-kāyajōēhiṁ

taṁ hōi abhayadāṇaṁ musāhujaṇasēviyaṁ paraṁ

icchanti savvajīvā ninbharaduhiyā vi jīviuṁ jamhā

tamhā taṁ cēva piyaṁ tēsiṁ kusalēṇa vinnēyaṁ

jamhā ya naravarindō maraṇammi uvaṭṭhiyammi rajja pi

dēi sajī viyahēuṁ tamhā taṁ cēva iṭṭayaraṁ

dāyavvaṁ ca maīmayā jaṁ iṭṭhu hōi gāhagāṇaṁ tu

taṁ dāṇaṁ paralōē muhamicchantēṇa suvisālaṁ

dīhāū u suruvō nīrōgō hōi abhayadāṇēṇaṁ

jammantarē vi jīvō sayalajaṇasalāhaṇijjō ya

ēyaṁ tu abhayadāṇaṁ tiyasindanarindanamiyacalaṇēhiṁ

sāvaya! jiṇēhi bhaṇiyaṁ dujjayakammadalaṇēhiṁ

dhammōvaggahadāṇaṁ bhaṇṇaï sayamēva dadhamaviruddhaṁ

navakōḍīparisuddhaṁ dijjaï jaṁ dhammiyajaṇassa

taṁ puṇa asaṇaṁ pāṇaṁ vatthaṁ pattaṁ ca bhēsayaṁ joggaṁ

dāyavvaṁ tu maïmayā tahēva sayaṇāsaṇaṁ pavaraṁ

dāyavvaṁ puṇa sajjhāyanāṇanirayassa nirubagārissa

jō saṁjamatavabhāraṁ vahaï sayā tēṇuvaggahiō

kammalahuyattaṇēṇa ya sō appāṇaṁ paraṁ ca tārēi

kammagurū atarantō sayaṁpi kaha tāraē annaṁ 1

dāyavvaṁ puṇa taṁ kāraṇēhi caühi parisuddhaṁ

jiṇabhaṇiēhiṁ dāyaga-gāhaga-tahakāla-bhāvēhiṁ

dāyagasuddhaṁ bhaṇṇaï jō dāyā dēi nāṇasaṁpannō

aṭṭhamayaṭṭhāṇarahiō saddhārōmaściyasarīrō

nāōvayaṁ davvaṁ phāsugamaviruddhagaṁ ca lōgammi

ihaparalōyāsaṁsa mottūṇaṁ nijjarahī u

sukkhētammi va bīyaṁ vikkhittaṁ tassa bahuphalaṁ hōi

taṁ dāṇaṁ maṇuyāmarasivasuhasaṁpattijaṇayaṁ tu

jō puṇa saddhārahiō dāṇaṁ dēi jasakittirēsammi

ahimāṇēṇa va ēsō dēha ahaṁ kiṁ na dēmi tti

taṁ saddhājalarahiyaṁ vīyaṁ va na hōi bahuphalaṁ tassa

dāṇaṁ bahuṁ pi pavaraṁ siyacittassa mōhēṇa

kāūṇa ya pāṇivaha jō dāṇaṁ dēi dhammasaddhāē

dahiūma candaṇaṁ sō karēi aṅgāravāṇijja

karmalaghutvēna ca sa ātmānaṁ paraṁ ca tārayati

karmagururataran svayamapi kathaṁ tārayēdanyam?

mūḍhō lōyaviruddha dhammaviruddhaṁ ca dēi jō dāṇaṁ

sō appāṇaṁ taha gāhagaṁ ca pāḍēi saṁsārē

jāṇaha gāhagasuddhaṁ pañcamahavvayadharō u jō niyamā

gurususvasāniraō jōgammi samāhiyappā ya

taha khanti-madava-ujjavajuttō dhaṇiyaṁ ca vigayalōhō u

maṇa-vayaṇa-kāyaguttō paścindiyaniggahaparō ya

sajjhāyajhāṇaniraō suddhappā suddhasāhucariō ya

iha paralōē ya tahā savvattha dadaṁ apaḍibaddhō

mēru vva jō na tīraï uksaggasamīraṇēhi cālēuṁ

ēyārisammi dāṇaṁ gāhagasuddhaṁ tu vinnēyaṁ

sīlanvayarahiyāṇaṁ dijaï jaṁ puṇa dhaṇaṁ kupattāṇaṁ

taṁ khalu dhōvaï vatthaṁ ruhirakayaṁ sōṇiēṇēva

dinnaṁ suhaṁ pi dāṇaṁ hōi kupattammi asuhaphalamēva

sappassa jaha va dinnaṁ khīraṁ pi visattaṇamuvēi

tucchaṁ pi supattammi u dāṇaṁ niyamēṇa suhaphalaṁ hōi

jaha gāvīē viiṇṇaṁ taṇaṁ pi khīrattaṇamuvēi

hōi suhāsuhaphalayaṁ pattavisēsēṇa dāṇamēgaṁ pi

gāvī-bhuyaṅgapīyaṁ jaha udagaṁ hōi khīra-visaṁ

bhaṇṇaï ya kālasuddhaṁ dāṇaṁ kālōvavannayaṁ jaṁ tu

dijjaï tavassidēhōvayārakālammi suvisuddhaṁ

kālammi kīramāṇaṁ kisikammaṁ bahu phalaṁ jahā hōi

iya kālammi vi dinnaṁ dāṇaṁ pi hu bahuphalaṁ ṇēyaṁ

hōi ayālammi jahā avayāraparaṁ païṇṇaya bīyaṁ

dentassa gāhagassa ya ēvaṁ dāṇaṁ pi vinnēyaṁ

jāṇaha ya bhāvasuddhaṁ saddhā-saṁvēgapayaḍapulaō ya

kayakiccaṁ mannentō appāṇaṁ dēi jō dāṇaṁ

navakōḍīparisuddhaṁ dasadōsavivajjiyaṁ ca dēyaṁ pi

ēyaṁ pi bhāvasuddhaṁ pannattaṁ vīyarāgēhi

aṭṭaksaṭṭōvagaō avi suddhaṁ dēi kalasiyamaṇō u

sanidāṇaṁ ca na ēyaṁ bhāvavisuddhaṁ havaï dāṇaṁ

mokkhatthaṁ jaṁ dāṇaṁ taṁ paī ēsō vihī muṇēyavvō

aṇugampādāṇaṁ puṇa jiṇēhi na kahiṁci paḍisiddhaṁ

ēsō u dāṇamaïō dhammō saṁkhēvaō samakkhāō

ettō ya sīlamaïyaṁ tu bhaṇṇamāṇaṁ nisāmēha

jāṇaha ya sīlamaïyaṁ pāṇavahā-’liya-adinnadāṇāṇaṁ

mēhuṇa-pariggahāṇa ya viraī jā savvahā sammaṁ

taha kōha-māṇa-māyā-lōhassa ya niggahō daḍhaṁ jō u

khantīya maddava-ujjava-saṁtōsavicittasatthēhi

khaṇalavapaḍibujjhaṇayā saddhā-saṁvēgaphāsaṇā taha ya

cittēṇa nirīhēṇaṁ mettī vi ya sabyajīvēsu

ēyaṁ ca sēviūṇaṁ dhammaṁ jiṇadēsiyaṁ susīlamayaṁ

mugaī pāvanti narā ṭhaenti saï duggaïduvāraṁ

ēsō u sīlamaïō bhaṇiō dhammō jiṇēhi savvēhiṁ

sāvaya! paramagurūhiṁ dujayajiyarāgadōsēhiṁ

bhaṇṇaï tavōmaïō sa bāhira-’bbhantarassa ya tavassa

jamaṇuṭāṇaṁ kīraï asēsakammakkhayanimittaṁ

aṇasaṇamūṇōyariyā vittīsaṁkhēvaṇaṁ rasacāō

kāyakilēsō saṁlīṇayā ya bajjhō tavō hōi

pāyacchittaṁ viṇaō vēyāvaccaṁ tahēva sajjhāō

jhāṇaṁ ussaggō vi ya abhintaraō tavō hōi

ēvaṁ cariūṇaṁ tavaṁ jīvā iha-pāralōiyasuhāī

pāventi visālāī karenti dukkhakkhayaṁ taha ya

ēsō u tavōmaïō dhammō saṁkhēvaō samakkhāō

nisuṇaha ettō sundara! dhamma puṇa bhāvaṇāmaïyaṁ

samma sammaīsaṇa-nāṇa-carittāṇa bhāvaṇā jāō

vēraggabhāvaṇā vi ya paramā titthayaramattī ya

saṁsārajugucchaṇayā kāmavirāgō susāhu-jiṇasēvā

titthayarabhāsiyassa ya dhammassa pabhāvaṇā taha ya

mokkhasuhammi ya rāō aṇāyayaṇavajjaṇā ya supasatthā

saï appaṇō ya nindā garahā ya kahicikhaliyassa

ēsō jiṇēhi bhaṇiō aṇantanāṇīhi bhāvaṇāmaïō

dhammō u bhīmabhavavaṇasujaliyadāvāṇalabhūō

ēyaṁ caünvihaṁ phāsiūṇa dhammaṁ jiṇēhi pannattaṁ

sundara! aṇantajīvā pattā mokkhaṁ sadāsokkhaṁ

ō ēyamāyaṇṇiūṇa āvibhūō sihikumārassa jiṇadhammabōhō. bhaṇiō ya ṇēṇa bhayavaṁ vijayasiṅghō-bhayavaṁ! ēvamēva, īdisō cēva ēsa dhammō, na ettha saṁdēhō tti. kiṁ tu dāṇamaïyaṁ mottūṇa na sēsabhēyā imassa samma aviyalā tīranti gihatyēṇa kāuṁ. tā ācikkha bhayavaṁ! kērisō puṇa imassa mahāpurisasēviyassa, sayaladukkhāṇalajalassa, siddhivahusaṁgamēkahēuṇō samaṇattaṇassa jōgō tti. bhagavayā bhaṇiyaṁ — suṇa, samaṇataṇārihō āriyadēsuppaśnō, visiṭṭhajāikulasamaniō, khīṇappāyakammamalō, taō cēva vimalabuddhī dullahaṁ māṇusattaṇaṁ, jammō maraṇanimittaṁ, calāō saṁpayāō, dukkhahēyavō visayā, saṁjōgē viōgō, aṇusamayamēva maraṇaṁ, dāruṇō vivāgō tti ahigayasaṁsārasarūvō,taō cēva tamvirattō, payaṇukasāō, thēvahāsō, akōugō, kayanna, viṇīō, puvvaṁ pi rāyā-’macca paürajaṇabahumaō, adōsagārī, kallāṇaṅgō, saddhāvantō, thirasaddhō samuvasaṁpannō ya. sihikumārēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — bhaya. sōhaṇō samaṇatta ṇārihō bhayavayā pavēiō. ahaṁ puṇa samuvasaṁpannō. tā ēvaṁ nivēiē bhayavaṁ pamāṇaṁ ti. taō paricintiyaṁ bhayavayā-jahā khu ēsō mahābhāgavantō suhumapasiṇēsu viyakkhaṇō, añcantapasantarūvō, aïṇiuṇabhaṇiikusalō vi ya lakkhijaï, tahā bhaviyaramaṇēṇaṁ mahā kulapamaēṇaṁ bhavavirattacittēṇa ya. tā imaṁ tāva ettha pattakālaṁ, jaṁ ēsō uvasaṁgahijjaï ti cintiūṇa bhaṇiyaṁ ca ṇēṇaṁ-mahāsāvaya! na sēsaguṇavippahūṇō ihaṁ uvasaṁpajjaï. juttaṁ ca payaïnigguṇē saṁsāravāsē jamiṇaṁ samaṇattaṇaṁ, kiṁ tu dukkaramidaṁ. ettha khalu savvakālamēva samasattumittabhāvēṇa pāṇāivāyaviraī, appamattayāē aṇaliyabhāsaṇaṁ, dantasōhaṇamettassa vi adinnassa bajjaṇā, maṇa-vayaṇa-kārahi abbambhacēranirōhō, vattha-pattō-vagaraṇēhiṁ pi nimmamattayā, caüvbiharāibhattaviraī, uggamu-ppāya-ṇēsaṇāvisuddhapiṇḍagahaṇaṁ, saṁjōṣaṇāi paścadōsarahiyamiyakālabhōyaṇaṁ, pañcasamiyattaṇaṁ, tiguttayā, iriyāsamiyāibhāvaṇāō, aṇasaṇa-pāyacchitta-viṇayāisabāhiranbhinta ratavōvihāṇaṁ, māsāiyā ya aṇēgāō paḍimāō vicittā ya davvādaō abhiggahā, aṇhāṇaṁ, bhūmisayaṇijja, kēsalobhō, nippaḍi kammassarīrayā, savvakālamēva gurūṇaṁ nidēsakaraṇaṁ, khuhā-pivāsāiparīsahāhiyāsaṇaṁ, divvāiuvasaggavijaō, laddhāvaladdhavittiyā kiṁ bahuṇā? accanta dubahamahāpurisavūhaaṭṭhārasasīlaṅgasahassabharavahaṇamavissāmaṁ ti. tā tariyavvō khalu ayaṁ bāhāhiṁ mahāsamuddō, bhakkhiyabbō nirāsāya (ē) ēva vālugākavalō, parisakkiyadhvaṁ nisiyakaravāladhārāē, pāyavvā muhuyahuyavahajālāvalī, bhariyavbō sahumapavaṇakotthalō, gantavvaṁ gaṅgāpavāhapaḍisīpaṇaṁ, tōliyanvō tulāē mandaragirī, jēyavvamēgāgiṇā cāuraṅgabalaṁ, vidhēyavvā vivarīyabhamantaddhacakōvarithiulliyā, gahiyanyā agahiyapuvvā tihuyaṇajayapaḍāgā. ēōvamaṁ dukkaraṁ samaṇattaṇaṁ ti. taō ēyamāyaṇṇiūṇa pahaṭṭavayaṇakamalēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ sihikumārēṇa-bhaya! ēvamēyaṁ, jahā tumbhē āṇavēha. kiṁ tu viiyasaṁsārasa rūvassa pāṇiṇō tandhiōgujayassa tasmucchēyakāraṇaṁ na kiṁci dukaraṁ ti. bhayavayā bhaṇiya-ēvamēyaṁ, kiṁ tu taṁ cēva saṁsārasarūvaṁ pañcakkhōvalabbhamāṇāsundaraṁ pi aṇēyabhavabhāvaṇāō mōhēi pāṇiṇaṁ, mūḍhō ya sō na cintēi taspta rūvaṁ, na gaṇēi āyaī, na mannaē uvaēsaṁ, nābhiṇandaï guruṁ, na pecchaï kulaṁ, na sēvaï dhammaṁ, na vīhēi ayasassa, na rakkhaï vayaṇijja. savvahā taṁ tamāyaraï, jēṇa jēṇa sō ihalōē paralōē ya kilēsabhāyaṇaṁ hōī. tā nihaṇiyabvō khalu ēsa mōhō tti. sihikumārēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — bhayavaṁ! tassa vi ya nihaṇaṇē ēsēva uvāō, na ya aṇāḍhattakajjō purisō phalaṁ sāhēi, āḍhattē ya saṁsaō, ahavā uvāyapabattō asaṁsayaṁ cēva sāhēi. uvāō ya ēsa, jaṁ bhayavaō samīvē samaṇattaṇapava jaṇaṁ. nittharanti khalu kāyarā vi pōyanijāmayaguṇēṇa mahaṇṇavaṁ. na ya appa puṇṇāṇaṁ kusalabuddhī havaï. na ya samuppannāē vi imīē ēvaṁvihasayalaguṇasaṁpaōvavēyagurulāhō. tā karēhi mē bhayavaṁ! aṇuggahaṁ ti. bhayavayā bhaṇiyaṁ — vaccha! kaō cēva tuha maē aṇuggahō. kiṁ tu ēsā samayaṭṭiī amhāṇaṁ, jē saṁsiūṇa thēvamāgāstha, sikkhā viūṇā''vasmayaṁ aïkantēṣu kaïbayadiṇēsu taō dikkhijjaï ti. sihikumārēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — bhayavaṁ! aṇugihīō mhi. annaṁ ca—

nikkhantēṇa vi maē samayahiī cēva pāliyabdhā. tā ēvaṁ havaü tti.

ēvaṁ ca jāva mantayantā ciṭṭhanti, tāva āgaō kahiṁci tappaüni sōūṇa aṇēyalōyaparigō karēṇuyārūḍhō imassa cēva jaṇaō bambhayattotti. paṇamiō tēṇa bhayavaṁ vijayasiṁhāyariō. ahiṇandiō bhayavayā dhammalāhēṇa. uvaviṭhṭhō gurupāyamūlē. paṇamiūṇa bhaṇiō sihikumārēṇa tāya! saṁpāēhi abhaggapaṇaïpatthaṇō mē ēgaṁ patthaṇaṁ ti. bambhayattēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — vaccha! bhaṇasu. tuhāyattamēva mē jīviyaṁ. sihikumārēṇa bhaṇiya-tāya! viiyavuttantō cēva turma saṁsārasahāvassa. dullahaṁ khalu māṇusattaṇaṁ, aṇicā piyajaṇasamāgamā, caścalāō riddhīō kumumasāraṁ jovvaṇaṁ, paralōyapañcatthiō aṇaṅgō, dāruṇō visayavivāgō, pahavaï sayā aṇivāriyapasarō maccū. tā karēhi mē pasāyaṁ. ēvamavasāṇē iha jīvalōē aṇunāō tumaē vīyarāyappaṇīyajaïdhammāsēvaṇēṇa karēmi saphalaṁ maṇuyattaṇaṁ. tō suyasiṇēhēṇa bāhajalabhariyalōyaṇēṇaṁ sagaggaya bhaṇiyaṁ bambhayattēṇa-putta! ayālō ēsa jaïdhammassa. sihikumārēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — tāya! maccuṇō viya natthi ayālō jaïdhammassa ti.

etthantarammi bambhayattaparicāragēṇa nāhiyavādiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ piṅgakēṇa-bhō kumāra! kēṇa tumaṁ vippayāriō? na khalu ettha pañcabhūyavaïrittō paralōgagāmī jīvō samatthīyaï. avi ya ēyāṇi cēva bhūyāṇi sahāvaō cēva ēyappagārapariṇāmapariṇayāṇi jīvō tti bhaṇṇanti. jayā ya ēyāṇi caïūṇa samudayaṁ paścattamuvagacchanti, tayā maō purisō ti ahihāṇaṁ pavattaē. na uṇa etya kōi dēhaṁ caïūṇa ghaḍaciḍaō viva parabhavaṁ gacchaī. tā mā tumaṁ asantē vi paralōgē micchāhiṇivēsabhāviyamaī sahāvasundaraṁ visayamuhaṁ paricayamu, daṁsēhi vā dēhavaïrittaṁ dēhiṇaṁ. aō jaṁ taē bhaṇiyaṁ — jahā dullahaṁ maṇuyattaṇaṁ, tamasaṁbaddhamēva. jaōna taṁ sukaya-dukkayāṇu bhāvēṇa labbhaï, avi ya bhūyapariṇaīō, aō kimiyamāulattaṇaṁ. tahā jaṁ ca bhaṇiyaṁ aṇiccā piyajaṇasamāgamā , ēyaṁ pi akāraṇaṁ. jaō na tē nikkhantāṇaṁ pi annahā honti. tahā jaṁ ca bhaṇiyaṁ cañcalāō riddhīō , ēyassa vi na nikkhamaṇamēva paḍivakkhō, avi ya uvāēṇa parirakkhaṇaṁ ti. tahā jaṁ ca bhaṇiyaṁ kusumasāraṁ jovvaṇaṁ , ettha viya rasāyaṇaṁ juttaṁ, na uṇa nikkhamaṇaṁ ti. tahā jaṁ ca bhaṇiyaṁ paralōyapaccatthiō aṇaṅgō tti, ēyaṁ pi na sōhaṇaṁ, jō paralōō cēva natthi, na ya kōi taō āgantūṇamappāṇayaṁ daṁsēi. ēvamavi ya parigappaṇē aïppasaṅgō tti. tahā jaṁ ca bhaṇiyaṁ dāruṇō visayavivāgō tti, ēyaṁ pi na juttisaṁgaya; jō āhārassa vi vivāgō dāruṇō cēva, ēvaṁ ca bhōyaṇamavi paricaïavvaṁ. na ya hariṇā vijanti tti jakā cēva na vuppanti. [jayahiī ya ēsa ti] na ya uvāyannuṇō purisassa dāruṇattaṁ pi saṁbhavaï. tahā jaṁ ca bhaṇiyaṁ pahavaï ya sayā aṇivāriyapasarō maccu tti, ēyaṁ pi bālavayaṇa yētaṁ; jēṇa nikkhantassa vi ēsa aṇivāriyappasarō cēva, tēṇa vi ya samaṇēṇa pajjantē mariyavvaṁ ti. na ya pajantē mariyavvaṁ ti masāṇē cēvāvatthāṇamukvanna. na ya santē vi paralōē dukkhasēvaṇāō muhaṁ, avi ya suhasēvaṇāō cēva. jaō jaṁ cēva abbhasijjaï, tassēva pagarisō lōē diṭṭhō, na uṇa vivajaō tti. tā virama ēyāō vavasāō ti. siddikumārēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — savvamiṇamasaṁgayaṁ muṇa. ahavā na juttaṁ bhayavaō samakkhaṁ mama jaṁpiuṁ. tā bhayavaṁ cēva ettha bhaṇissaï ti. taō bhayavayā bhaṇiyaṁ — bhō mahāmāhaṇa! suṇa. jaṁ taē bhaṇiya, jahā kēṇa tumaṁ payāriō ti, ēsa jammantarambhatthakusalabhāvaṇābhāviyamaī appāvaraṇasaṁjuō vīyarāgavayaṇā vibhūyakhaōvasamabhāvēṇa samuppannatattanāṇō jahaṭṭhiyaṁ bhavasahāyamavayujjhiūṇa tō virattō, na uṇa kēṇaï vippayāriō tti. tahā jaṁ ca bhaṇiyaṁ — na khalu ettha pañcabhūyavaïrittō paralōgagāmī jīvō samatthīyaï, avi ya ēyāṇi cēva bhūyāṇi. sahāvaō cēva ēyappagārapari ṇāmapariṇayāṇi jīvō tti bhaṇṇanti, ēyaṁ pi na juttisaṁgayaṁ. jaō savvahā acēyaṇāṇi bhūyāṇi. tā kahaṁ imāṇaṁ ēyappagārapari ṇāmapariṇayāṇa vi ēsā pañcakkhapamāṇāṇubhūyamāṇā gamaṇāiceṭṭhānibandhaṇā cēyaṇā jujjaï tti. na hi jaṁ jēsu pattēyaṁ na vijaē, taṁ tēsiṁ samudaē vi havaï, jahā vālugāthāṇaē tellaṁ. aha pattēyaṁ pi imāṇi cēyaṇāṇi tti, taō siddhamaṇēgavēyannasamudaō purisō, ēgindiyā ya jīvā, ghaḍādīṇaṁ ca cēyaṇataṇaṁ ti. na ya ghaḍādīṇaṁ cēyaṇa tti. aō atthi khalu paścabhūyavaïrittō cēyaṇāsvō para lōgagāmī jīvō tti. taō ya ja bhaṇiyaṁ — jayā ēyāṇi caïūṇa samudayaṁ pañcattamuvagacchanti, tayā maō purisō tti abhihāṇaṁ pavattaï , ēyaṁ pi vayaṇamettaṁ cēva. cēyannassa tadaïrēgabhāvavittīō. na yāṇubhūyamāṇasarūvā cēva cēyaṇā nisēhiuṁ pārīyaï. tahā jaṁ ca bhaṇiyaṁ — na uṇa ettha kōi dēhaṁ caïūṇa ghaḍaciḍaō viva parabhavaṁ gacchaï tti, ēyaṁ pi aō cēva paḍisiddhaṁ vēiyavvaṁ, cēyaṇassa acēyaṇabhēyāō ti. tahā jaṁ ca bhaṇiyaṁ — tā mā tuma asantē vi paralōē micchābhiṇivēsabhāviyamaī sahāvasundaraṁ visayasuhaṁ paricayasu, daṁsēhi vā mē dēhavaïrittaṁ dēhiṇa', ettha vi ya suṇa-cēyannabhēyasiddhīē kahaṁ natthi paralōgō? vijamāṇē ya tammi kaha ēyassa micchābhiṇivēsō? kahaṁ ca pamugaṇasāhāraṇā viḍambaṇāmettarūvā cintāyāsabahulā maṇanivvāṇavēriṇō avinnāyavī sambhasuhasarūvā sahāvasundarā visaya tti, kiṁ ca tēhiṁtō suhaṁ? jaṁ puṇa sō dēhabhinnō na dīsaï , ettha kāraṇaṁ suṇa-muhumō aṇindiō ya sō vattaē, aō na dīsaï tti. pecchanti puṇa savvann. bhaṇiyaṁ ca vīyarāgēhi—

aṇindiyaguṇaṁ jīvaṁ adissaṁ maṁsacakkhuṇō

siddhā passanti savvannū nāṇasiddhā ya sāhuṇō

ēvaṁ ca paryapirapi vijayasiṁhāyariē īsi vihasiūṇa bhaṇiya piṅgakēṇa-bhayavaṁ! savvamasaṁbaddhamēva bhaṇiyaṁ bhayavayā. kahaṁ? suṇa jaṁ tāva bhaṇiyaṁ — savvahā acēyaṇāṇi bhūyāgi, tā kahaṁ imāṇaṁ ēyappagārapariṇāmapariṇayāṇa vi ēsā paccakkhappamāṇāṇubhūyamāṇā gamaṇāiceṭṭānibandhaṇā cēyaṇā jujjaï tti na hi jaṁ jēsu pattēyaṁ na vijjaē taṁ tēsi samudaē vi havaï, jahā vālugāthāṇagē tellaṁ , ēyaṁ kahaṁ jujjaï tti? na hi kāraṇāṇurūvamēva kajja bhavaï. kiṇṇa hōi siṅgāō sarō? kiṁ vā adissaparamāṇunippannaṁ ghaḍāi dessaṁ ti? ēvaṁ cēyaṇā vi takajā ya bhavissaï, bhūyavilakkhaṇā ya tti kō virōhō? jaṁ ca bhaṇiyaṁ — aha pattēyaṁ pi imāṇi cēyaṇāṇi tti, taō siddhamaṇēyacēyannasamudaō purisō, ēgindiyā ya jīvā ghaḍādīṇaṁ ca cēyaṇa tti iccetramādi, taṁ pi na sōhaṇaṁ. tēsiṁ cēva tahāvihapariṇāmabhāvaō, tadabhāvaō cetra na ghaḍādīṇaṁ ca cēyaṇa tti.

bhayavayā bhaṇiyaṁ — suṇa, jaṁ bhaṇiya— kiṇṇa hōi siṅgāō sarō ti?, sō hōi, na uṇa kāraṇāṇaṇurūvō, iyarasaravilakṣaṇa masiṇa-ghaṇa-laṇhāitaddhammasaṁkamāō tti. aha manasē, na sō visēsō vahārijaï ti. atthi tāva sō iyarasarahēusiṅgāṇamabhēyappa saṁgaō, visēsāvahāraṇē ujjamō kāyanbō tti. na hi ayaṁ thāṇussa abarāhō, jamandhō na parassaï tti. jaṁ ca bhaṇiyaṁ — adessaparamāṇu nippannaṁ ghaḍāi dessa ti, ēyaṁ pi na juttikkhamaṁ. jaō na ēgantēṇa addēsā paramāṇavō, jōgidaṁsaṇāō kajadaṁsaṇāō ya. na ya ēvaṁ bhūyadhammasaṁkramō cēyaṇāē tti, ayaṁ pi aō cēṣa paḍisiddhaṁ cēiyavvaṁ, cēyaṇaspa acēyaṇabhēyāō tti. aha manasē, sattālakkhaṇa dhammasaṁkamāō na dōsō tti. ēyaṁ pi na sōhaṇaṁ ti. tassa sayalabhāvasāhāraṇattēṇamaṇiyāmagattāō ti. taō saṁgayaṁ cēva maē bhaṇiyaṁ ti. tahā jaṁ ca bhaṇiyaṁ — tahāvihapariṇāmābhāvāō cēva na ghaḍādīṇaṁ cēyaṇa tti. eltha natthi pamāṇa; bhūyasamudayavaïrittapariṇāmabbhu vagamē ya annābhihāṇō jīvanbhuvagamō ti.

taō saviliyaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ piṅgakēṇa-bhayavaṁ! jaï ēvaṁ aṇindiyaguṇō jīvō, tā sarīrāō vibhinnō. ēvaṁ ca hontagē mama piyāmahō mahupiṅgō nāma, sō aṇēyasattasaṁghāyaṇaraō āsi tti. tuha darisaṇēṇa niyamēṇa naraē samuppannō. mamōvari aïsiṇēha saṁgaō ya āsi, ihalōyākaraṇijanivāraṇasīlō ya. tā kahaṁ sō taōṁ narayāō āgacchiūṇa diṭṭhavivāgō vimaṁ na nivārēi. bhayavayā bhaṇiyaṁ — suṇa, jahā mahāvarāhayārī, tikkhanaravaïsamāēsagahiō, rōdēhiṁ cārayapurisēhiṁ lōhasaṅkalānibaddha dēhō, ghōrandhayāra cārayanivāsī, paratantaō suppiyaṁ pi sayaṇaṁ dalr̥ pi na lahaē, kimaṅga puṇāṇusāsiuṁ? ēvamēva tē nāragā pamāyāvarāhakāriṇō tivvayarakammapariṇāmagahiyā caṇḍēhiṁ nirayapālēhiṁ vajjasaṅkalānibaddhadēhā tibandhayāraduruttaranarayanivāsiṇō kammaparatantā kaha niksamiu lahanti, jēṇa dēvāṇuppiyaṁ aṇusāsenti. bhaṇiyaṁ ca—

nirayāuē ajhīṇē nikkhamiuṁ nō lahanti naragāō

kammēṇa pāvayārī nēraïyā tē nihannanti

piṅgakēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — bhayavaṁ! jaï ēvaṁ, tā mamaṁ cēva piyā sōmapiṅgō nāma, sō accantaparalōyabhīrū, pāṇavahāiviraō, akasā. yasīlō, aṇēgajāgayārī pacchā ya samaṇavayaṁ ghettaṇa kaści kālaṁ parivāliya maō. sō ya tuha daṁsaṇēṇa niyamēṇa dēvēsu upavanō. accantavallahō ya ahaṁ tassa āsi. dhammaṁ ca mē dēsiyavvaṁ ti bhaṇiyamāsī. tā kahaṁ sō aparatantō vi samāṇō ihāgacchiūṇa maṁ na paḍivōhēi. bhayavayā bhaṇiyaṁ — suṇa, jahā nāma kōi daridapurisō, hīṇanāikularuṣō kvasāyaṁ kāūṇa gahiyakalākalāvō dēsantaramuva gantūṇa tappasāyaō kahiṁci pattarajō, kayavivihasundarīpariggahō, mahānarindapūiō, saṁjāyāṇēgasundarāvaccō, mahāsokkhasāgarāva gāḍhō na sumaraē lajjāvaṇijjassa kukalatta-puttabhaṇḍagasta, ēvaṁ cēva tē dēvā maṇuyattaṇamasāraṁ mannamāṇā dhammavavasāyaṁ kāūṇa gaïhiyaparalō gakalākalāvā surālayaṁ pāviūga puvvasukayapasāyaō dēviḍḍi pāviūṇa tiyasamundarīpariyariyā, mahāṇēgadēvagaṇapūiyā, samuppannāṇēyara inibandhaṇā, accantaraïsāgarāvagāḍhā na sumaranti vimaṇuyabhāvassa, kimaṅga puṇa āgacchanti? tā kahaṁ samaṇusāsaïnti? bhaṇiyaṁ ca—

"saṁkantadivyapēmā visayapasattā'samattakattavvā

aṇahīṇamaṇuyakajjā narabhavamamuhaṁ na enti surā"

piṅgakēṇa bhaṇiya-bhayavaṁ! jaï ēēṇa hēuṇā nāgacchanti, dēhabhinnō ya jīvō, tā imaṁ iha nayaravattaṁ cetra sabalōyapaccakkhaṁ virujjhaï. bhayavayā bhaṇiyaṁ — kahēhi, kiṁ taṁ narakātaṁ ti? piṅgakēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — muṇa, ettha nayarē ēgēṇa takkarēṇa naravaïbhaṇḍāyāraṁ muhamāsī. sō ya kahaṁci niggacchamāṇō gahiō niuttapurisēhiṁ. geṇhiūṇa salottagō cēva uvaṇīō naravaïssa. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ vāvāēha ēyaṁ. taō sō vahaniuttēṇa lōhakumbhīē pakkhittō pavikhaviūṇa ya ṭhaïyā lōhakumbhī. sammaṁ ṭhaḍyāī tattasīsaēṇaṁ.

taō dinnā rakkhavālayā. tahiṁ ca sō ubagō pañcattaṁ. na diṭṭhō suhumō vi sē niggamaṇamaggō tti. aō avagacchāmō, na annō jīvō tti. bhagavayā bhaṇiyaṁ — bhadda! jaṁ kiṁci ēvaṁ ti. suṇa, ihēgammi nayarē ēgō saṅigō vināṇapagarisaṁ saṁpattō sīhadārē vi saṅkha dhamentō savvanayaranaṇassa kaṇṇē vi ya dhamēi. sō ya rāiṇā pucchiō-kiyarē dhamēsi?. tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — dēva! sīhadārammi. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ — kahaṁ mama ṭhaïyaduvārē vi vāsaharaē pavisaï tti? tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — natthi sē paḍighāō tti. taō rāiṇā asaddahantēṇa sō purisō sasaṅkhagō cēva uḍiyāē pakkhittō, vuttō ya vāējasi saṅkha. ṭhaïyā uḍḍiyā jaüsārīkayā ya. vāiō tēṇa saṅkō. viniggaō sē saddō, ubaladdhō rāiṇā nāyarēhiṁ. na ya tassa niggamaṇachiddamuvaladdhaṁ ti. ēvaṁ ihāvi bhavē, kō virōhō tti? piṅgakēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — bhaya! na ēvamēyaṁ ti. suṇa. ihēvēgō takarajuvāṇaō mittēṇa mēṁ kāladaṇḍavāmiēṇa mama vayaṇāō tulāē tōliūṇa galakaramōḍapaṇa vāvāiō. sō ya puṇō vi tōliō jāva jattiō sajīvō, tattiō ajīvō vi. aō avagacchāmō, na annō jīvō; annahā ūṇagarūvō hontō tti. bhagavayā bhagiya-mada! jaṁ kiṁci ēyaṁ. suṇa, ihē gēṇaṁ gōvālēṇa vāyabhariō batthi puḍagō tulāē tōlāviō, rikō puṇō vi tōlāviō, jāva jattiō bhariō, tattiō rikkō vi. aha ya annō taō vāō tti. aha mannasē, sō maṇāgaṁ uṇagō tti. ēvaṁ ca hontagē iyarammi vi samō pasaṅgō. piṅgakēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — bhaya! na ēvamēyaṁ ti. suṇa, ihēva nayarē mittēṇa mē kāladaṇḍavāsiēṇa mama vayaṇāō ēgassa takarassa sarīrayaṁ saṁvattuvvattaya karentēṇa vi maggiō jīvō, na ya diṭṭō. taō sē sarīraya khaṇḍakhaṇḍāī karentēṇa puṇō vi maggiō, na ya dihō tti. aō avagacchāmō — na annō jīvō. bhayavayā bhaṇiyaṁ — bhadda! jaṁ kiṁci ēyaṁ. suṇa, ihēgēṇa maṇussēṇa araṇiṁ saṁvattuvvattayaṁ karentēṇa vi maggiō aggī, na ya diṭṭhō. tō tēṇa araṇiṁ khaṇḍakhaṇḍāī karentēṇa puṇō vi mangiō, na ya diṭṭhō tti. tā kiṁ sō na tammi atthi tti? aha mannasē natthi tti, ēvaṁ taō aṇuppāyapasaṅgō.

ēvaṁ ca bhaṇiē uttarappayāṇābhāvēṇa viliyamiva piṅgakaṁ pecchiūṇa bhaṇiyaṁ bhayavayā-tā ēvaṁ rukkhasāhāpayalaṇanimittapavaṇō vva adissamāṇō vi cakkhuṇā sarīracēvānimittabhūō jīvō atthi tti saddhēyaṁ. aha mannasē, pavaṇō phāsindiēṇa gheppaï. hanta! jīvō vi cittacēyaṇāiṁdhammāṇuha vēṇa gheppaï ti. bhaṇiyaṁ ca —

cittaṁ cēyaṇa sannā vinnāṇaṁ dhāraṇā ya buddhī ya. īhā maī viyakā jīvassa u lakkhaṇā ēē.

tā atthi jīvō tti. ēvaṁ ca hontaē jaṁ tumaē bhaṇiyamāsi, jahā — dullahaṁ khalu ēyaṁ māṇusattarṇa ti, ēyamasaṁbaddhaṁ cēva jō na taṁ sukayadukkhāṇubhāvēṇa labhaï, avi ya bhūyapariṇaīō tti, aō kimiyamāulattaṇaṁ tti, ēyamajutta. na hi paralōgagāmuē jīvē vijamāṇē cēva ēvaṁ samatthadhammārambhasāhagaṁ māṇusattaṇaṁ bhūyapariṇaïmettalabhaṁ ti. tahā jaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ — aṇiccā piyajaṇasamāgama tti, ēyaṁ pi akāraṇaṁ, jō na tē nikkhantāṇaṁ pi annahā honti , ēvaṁ pi na sōhaṇaṁ; jō nikkhantāṇamiha muṇīṇaṁ piyā-piyaviyappō cēva natthi tti. tahā jaṁ ca bhaṇiyaṁ — cañcalāō riddhīō tti, ēyassa vi na nikkhamaṇaṁ caïva paḍivakkhō, avi ya uvāraṇa parirakkhaṇaṁ ti, ēyaṁ pi bālavayaṇasarisaṁ cēva. jaō na dhammamēva mottūṇaṁ annō parirakkhaṇōvāō, asārāō ya imāō davariddhīō aṇēyasattā vayāriṇīō ya. tahājaṁ ca bhaṇiyaṁ — kusumasāraṁ jovvaṇaṁ ti, ettha vi ya rasāyaṇaṁ juttaṁ, na puṇō nikkhamaṇaṁ ti, ēvaṁ pi na saṁgayaṁ. jaō na nikkhamaṇadhammasāhaṇarasāyaṇāō paramatthacintāē annaṁ rasāyaṇaṁ ti. tahā jaṁ ca bhaṇiyaṁ — paralōyapaccatthiō aṇaṅgō tti, ēyaṁ pi na sōhaṇaṁ; jō paralōō cēva natthi, na ya kōi tō āgantūṇamappāṇayaṁ daṁsēi, ēvamavi ya pariyappaṇē aïppasaṅgō tti, ēyaṁ pi hu asāraṁ. vicittakiriyāṇuhava-jāissaraṇōvalambhatakahiyapaccayā vijamāṇuppāyāisiddhō kahaṁ paralōō cēva natyi? appāṇayādasaṇē ya bhaṇiyaṁ kāraṇaṁ. taha jaṁ ca bhaṇiyaṁ — dāruṇō visayavivāgō ti, ēyaṁ pi na juttisaṁgaya; jaō āhārassa vivāgō dāruṇō cēva, ēvaṁ ca bhōyaṇamavi paricaïyavvaṁ na ya hariṇā vijanti tti javā cēva na vuppanti tti, na ya uvāyannuṇō purisassa dāru ṇattaṁ pi saṁbhavaï tti ēvaṁ pi aṇālōiyavayaṇaṁ. jaō savvaṁ cēva saṁsāriyaṁ vatthu vivāgadāruṇaṁ ti. taṁ ca kamēṇa vajijjaē, ahippēō ya pavvajāphalaṁ saṁsārakkhaō cēva tti. na ya bandhuparivajaṇēṇa visayaparibhōgō tīraï tti. aō cciya na tēsu dāruṇattaṁ pi saṁbhavaï tti. taha jaṁ ca bhaṇiyaṁ — pahavaï sayā aṇivāriyapasarō maccu tti, ēyaṁ pi bālavayaṇamettaṁ ti; jēṇa nikkhantassa vi ēsa anivāriyapasarō cēva; na ya pajantē mariyavvaṁ ti masāṇē cēvāvatthāṇamuvavannaṁ, na ya santē vi paralōē dukkhasēvaṇāō suhaṁ, avi ya suhasēvaṇāō cēva, jaō jaṁ cēva anbhasijjaï tassēva pagarisō lōra diṭṭhō na uṇa vivajjaē ti, tā virama ēyāō vavasāyāō tti, ēyaṁ pi muddhajaṇa mōhaṇaṁ. jō na nikkhamaṇasāhiyaphalassa ēsa anivāriyapasarōti. nikkhamaṇassa hi phalaṁ jamhā jammābhāvajaṁ nivāṇaṁ, nivvāṇa pattassa ya imassa jīvassa na jammō, na jarā, na vāhī, na maraṇaṁ, na iṭṭhaviōgō, na aṇisaṁpaōgō, na bubhukkhā, na pivāsā, na rāgō, na dōsō, na kōhō, na māṇō, na māyā, na lōhō, na bhayaṁ, na ya annō vi kōi uvaddayō tti, kiṁ tu samvannū savvadarisī niruvama suhasaṁpannō tilōyacūḍāmaṇībhūō mokkhapaē ciṭṭhaï. aō kahaṁ tattha maccuṇō pasarō? na ya apayaṭṭakajjārambhō purisō phalaṁ sāhēi. kahaṁ ca païsamayamēva maraṇābhibhūyāṇaṁ kāpurisāṇaṁ tassa paḍiyāramacintayantāṇaṁ avatthāṇaṁ pasaṁsijjaï? aō na ya pajjantēmariyavvaṁ ti masāṇē cēvāvatthāṇamuvavanna ti pahasaṇappāyaṁ. na ya sayalasaṅgacāīṇa vīyarāgavayaṇēṇa kammakkhaüjjayāṇaṁ pariṇayacarittabhāvaṇāṇaṁ samaṇāṇaṁ jaṁ muhaṁ, taṁ cakkavaṭṭiṇō vi na jujjaï tti. bhaṇiyaṁ ca bhayavayā-"iha khalu saṁsārē na savahā muhamatthi, aṇabhinnāyasuhasa rūvā ya ettha pāṇiṇō, kammasaṁjōē dukkhaṁ tannivittī muhaṁ, ājāī dukkhaṁ tannivittī suhaṁ, jarā dukkhaṁ tannivittī suha, icchā dukkhaṁ tannivittī muhaṁ, piyaṁ dukkhaṁ tannivittī muhaṁ, saṁkilē sē dukkhaṁ tannivittī suhaṁ, maraṇaṁ dukkhaṁ tannivittī suhaṁ, 3.ṇāikamma saṁjōgaō ṇaṁ imē pāṇiṇō aṇabhinnā ya suhasarūvassa tti bēmi. ēvaṁ ājāi-jarā-icchā-piya-saṁkilēsa-maraṇēsu vi vibhāsā. sē jahā nāma kēi purisā ājāirōgakhettuppannā ājāirōgagahiyā adidvārōgapurisāiyā āmaraṇaṁ tabbhāvā aṇabhinnā ārogga suhasarūvassa, ēvaṁ cēva samaṇāusō! aṇāiapajjavasāṇāvaṭṭakhettavāsī imē pāṇiṇō tti. jēṇa daṭṭhūṇa vi ya ṇaṁ jahā tē arōgi purisaṁ tēsu tēsu rōgipurisāṇukūlēsu samāyārēsu avaṭṭamāṇaṁ savvarōganigdhāyaṇi kiriyamaṇusāsayantaṁ atthēgē païussanti, atthēgē uvahasanti, atthēgē avahīranti, atthēgē suṇanti, atthēgē na pariṇāmenti, atthēgē pariṇāmenti, atthēgē nāṇuciṭṭhanti, atthēgē aṇuciṭṭhanti, atthēgē sajhaṁ virāhentiatthēgē kicchasajhaṁ virānti, atthēgē na virāhentiḥ avirāhaṇāē ya ṇaṁ atthi kēi saba dukkhavimokkhaṁ karenti, karettā tabbhāvaṁ viuṭṭanti, taō aïkkantatabhāvē khalu ayaṁ purisē'viyaha abhinnāyāroggasuhasarūvē bhavaï, samaṇapariṇāmagāmī vi aviyaṭṭamabhinnāyāroggasuhasakhyā bhavanti, ēvamēva samaṇāusō! āvaṭṭakhettavāsī imē pāṇiṇō daṭṭhūṇa vi ya ṇaṁ bhāvāroggapurisaṁ tēsu tēsu kammasaṁjōgāīdukkhagahiyapurisāṇukūlēsu samāyārēsu aṭṭamāṇaṁ tadukkhanigyāyaṇi kiriya maṇusāsayantaṁ atthēgē (jāva-) aviyaṭṭamabhinnāyāroggasuhasarūvā bhavanti, na puṇa annahati.

aō na dukkhasēvaṇaṁ sāhukiriyā, avi ya suhaṁ cēva. bhaṇiyaṁ ca—

tiṇasaṁthāranibannō bi muṇivarō bhaṭṭharāga-maya-mōhō

jaṁ pāvaï muttisuhaṁ kattō taṁ cakkavaṭṭī vi?

aō suhasēvaṇāō cēva suhapayarisō tti savvaṁ cēvōvavannaṁ ti. etthantarammi āgandavāhajalabhariyalōyaṇēṇaṁ niyaḍiyahiya yasabbhāvaṁ pavaṭṭamāṇasammattapariṇāmēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ bambhayattēṇa-bhayavaṁ! ēvamēyaṁ, na annaha tti. bhāviō tēṇa jiṇadēsiō dhammō, pavanna sammattaṁ, cintiyaṁ ca vigayasammōhaṁ — ahō! mē suyassa sōhaṇō vavasāō ti. piṅgakēṇa vi ya pavanamuhapariṇāmēṇaṁ cēva bhaṇiyaṁ — bhaya! ēvamēyaṁ ti. aha kahaṁ puṇa puṇṇa-pāvāṇaṁ visēsō lakkhijjaï? bhayavayā bhaṇiyaṁ — suṇa, paccakkhaṁ cēva—

avirayaḍajjhantāguruvisaṅkhalucchaliyadhūmapaïḍihatthē

ekkē vasanti bhavaṇē nivaddhamaṇinimmalullōē

annē vi raïyaphuphumaviṇintadhūmōlipūriucchalē

juṇṇanihēlaṇavivarantarālaparisaṁṭhiyabhuyaṅgē

ekkē dhaklaharōvari miyaṅkakaradanturē saha piyāhiṁ

līlāē gaminti nirsi pēsalarayacāḍuyammē hi

annē vi sisiramāruyasīyapavēvirasamuddhasiyadēhā

kahakaha vi piyārahiyā vārantā dantavīṇāō

ēgē kaścaṇapaḍibaddhathōramuttāhalubbhaḍāharaṇā

vilasanti bahalakuṅkumabhasaliyavacchatthalābhōyā

annē vi saī mahiyalanisīyaṇuppanna kiṇiyapōṁgillā

maliṇajarakappaḍocchaïyaviggahā kaha vi hiṇḍanti

ekkē pūrenti maṇōrahāi jaṁ maggirāṇa pagatīṇaṁ

annē puṇa paragharahiṇḍaṇēṇa kucchi pi na bharenti

iya puṇṇā-puṇṇaphalaṁ pañcakkhaṁ cēva dīsaī lōē

taha vi jaṇō rāgandhō dhammammi aṇāyaraṁ kuṇaï

ettō ya tabisēsō lakkhijaï āgamabalēṇa. annaṁ ca—

anyē'pi racitaphumphumāviniryadhūmāvalipūritotsaṅgē

jīrṇanilayanavivarāntarālaparisaṁsthitabhujaṅgē

pugaṇēṇa mahāsōvakhā cakkī dēvā ya siddhigāmī ya

pāvēṇa kumāṇusa-tiriya-nārayā honti jīvā u

piṅgakēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — bhayavaṁ! ēvamēyaṁ aha kiṁ puṇa puṇṇakāraṇaṁ, pāvakāraṇaṁ vā aṇuṭāṇaṁ ti? bhayavayā bhaṇiyaṁ — suṇa, puṇṇakāraṇaṁ tāva sayalapāṇivaha-musāvāyā-’dattādāṇa-mēhuṇa-pariggahāṇa viraī, nisibhattavajjaṇaṁ, rāgadōsādiniggahō ya. pāvakāraṇaṁ puṇa iṇa mēva vivarīyaṁ ti. taō ēyamāyaṇṇiūṇa pavannō sāvayadhamma samaṁ bambhadattēṇa piṅgakō. bhaṇiyaṁ ca bambhadattēṇa-bhaya! ēsa mē sihi kumārō suō hōivavasiō ya ēsō mahāpurisōciē aṇuṭāṇē. aṇumayaṁ ca mē saṁpaya mimaṁ ēyassa vavasiyaṁ, tā kiṁ ēyassa aṇu ṭṭhāṇassa uciō, aṇuciō tti vā? bhayavayā bhaṇiyaṁ — na rayaṇāyarappasūrya rayaṇaṁ paḍibandhassa aṇuciyaṁ. taō harisavasuppulaïyaṅgēṇa karēu ēsa imaṁ mama pi maṇōrahagōyaraṁ ti cintiūṇa bhaṇiyaṁ bambhayattēṇa-vaccha! aṇunnāō maē tumaṁ karēhi tavasaṁjamujjōyaṁ ti. taō saharisaṁ paṇamiūṇa bhaṇiyaṁ sihikumārēṇa-tāya! aṇuggihīō mhi. taō vandiūṇa guruṁ paviṭṭhā nayaraṁ. vambhayattēṇa vi ya davāviyamāghōsaṇāpubdhayaṁ mahādāṇaṁ, karāviyā jiṇāyayaṇāīsu aāhiyā mahimā. taō pasatthē tihi-karaṇa-muhutta-jōgē mahayā pamōēṇa, divāra vibhūīē, pariyariō rāyanāyaraēhi, divaṁ siriyamārūḍhō, vajantēhiṁ maṅgalatūrasaṁghāēhi, pasaṁsijjamāṇō vibuhalō ēṇaṁ, sadukkhamālōrajjamāṇō purasundarī hiṁ, dentō jahāsamīhiyaṁ atthijaṇāṇa dāṇaṁ niggaō nayarāō sihikumārō. gaō jattha bhayavaṁ vijayasiṅghāyariō tti. ōiṇmō sibiyāō. bandiō gurū. guruṇā vi kaē āvassaē taṁ vāmapāsē ṭhariūṇa vandiyā paramaguravō. taō vihivandaṇaṁ dāūṇa bhaṇiyaṁ mihikumārēga-icchākārēṇa pabyāvēha. taō guruṇā icchāmō tti bhaṇiūṇa namōkārapāḍhēṇa vihi puvvayaṁ appiyaṁ sē syaharaṇaṁ sāhuliṅgaṁ ti. bahumāṇaō gahiyaṁ sihikumārēṇaṁ. vandiūṇa guruṁ puṇō bhaṇiyamaṇēṇa-icchākārēṇa muṇḍāvēha. taō icchāmō tti bhaṇiūṇa namōkārapuvvayaṁ atuṭṭāō guruṇā gahiyāō tiṇi aṭṭhāō. taō vandiūṇa guruṁ, bhaṇiyaṁ sihikumārēṇa-icchākārēṇa sāmāiyaṁ mē ārōvēha. icchāmō tti bhaṇiṇa tadārotraṇanimittaṁ samaṁ sihi kumārēṇa kaō ṇēṇa kāussa ggō, cintiō thaō, pāriō namōkārēṇa. taō namōkārapuvyayaṁ tiṇṇi vārāō kaḍiyaṁ sāmāiyaṁ, mahāsaṁvēgasāraṁ aṇukaḍviyaṁ sihikumārēṇa. taō gahiyā guruṇā vāsā, dinnā paramagurupāēma, tahā sannihiyāṇaṁ sāhumādīṇa ya. etthantarammi vandiūṇa gurūṁ bhaṇiyaṁ sihikumārēṇa-saṁdisaha, kiṁ bhaṇāmi? guruṇā bhaṇiyaṁ — vandittu pavēēha. taō vandiūṇa jaṁpiyamaṇēṇa-tumbhēhiṁ mē sāmāi yamārōviyaṁ, icchāmi aṇusa (si) ḍiṁ ti. vāsappayāgapuvvayaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ guruṇā-nitthāragapāragō guruguṇēhiṁ vaḍḍhāhi. taō vandiūṇa bhaṇiyaṁ sihikumārēṇaṁ-tubbhaṁ pavēiyaṁ, saṁdisaha, sāhūṇaṁ pavēēmi. guruṇā bhaṇiyaṁ — pavēēha. taō vandiūṇa namōkārapāḍhēṇa kayaṁ payā hiṇamaṇēṇa. nitthāragapāragō guruguṇēhi baḍḍāhi tti bhaṇamāṇēhi dinnā gurumādīhiṁ vāsā. ṭhiō maṇāgamaggaō. ēvaṁ tiṇi vārē. taō paḍiō paramagurupāēma. āyariyassa ya nisaṇṇassa, kayaṁ niruddhaṁ, aṇusāsiō guruṇā. ēvaṁ pavanō imassa pāyamūlē visujjha māṇēṇaṁ pariṇāmēṇaṁ jiṇōvadiṭṭhēṇaṁ vihiṇā sayaladukkhaparamōsahi mahāpavvajja ti.

ahiṇandiō āṇandabāhanalabhariyalōyaṇēṇaṁ rāiṇā bambhayattēṇaṁ nayarajaṇavaēṇa ya. aō kaïvayadiyahē tatthā''siūṇa samattē māsakappē gaō bhagavayā saha khettantarammi. ēvaṁ ca niraïyāraṁ sāmaṇṇamaṇuvālentassa aïkantā aṇēgē varisalakkhā. iō ya samuppannō jāliṇīē aṇuyāvō. hā! duṭhṭha maē vavasiyaṁ, jēṇa ēsō avāvāviō cēva niggaō tti. tā pēsēmi sē pēsalavayaṇasāraṁ saṁdēsaya puvvayaṁ kiṁci uvāyaṇaṁ, jēṇa ēsō puṇō vi kahaṁci ihāgacchaï, tō vāvāissaṁ ti. aṇuciṭṭhiyaṁ ca tīē jahāsamīhiyaṁ. pēsiō bahuvihasaṁdēsagabbhiṇaṁ kambalarayaṇamādāya sōmadēvō. gaō ya sō dēsavikkhāyāyariyapaüttipucchaṇēṇaṁ tamālasagnivēsasaṁṭhiyassa sihi kumārassa (samīvaṁ). diṭṭhō ya tēṇa paccuccāraēṇa sāhūṇa suttatthamaṇu māsayantō sihikumārō. vandiō pahaḍhavayaṇapaṅkaēṇaṁ. dhammalāhiō kumārēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — amba! aṇāyārō khu ēsō samaṇāṇaṁ, jaṁ mottūṇa mahuyaravitti ēgapiṇḍabhōyaṇaṁ ti. jāliṇīē bhaṇiya-jāya! tuma jāṇasi tti. ēvaṁ ca sō païdiṇaṁ sē karēi dhammadēsaṇaṁ. cintēi ya jāliṇī ēyassa māraṇōvāē, na yāvaḍaï kōi muhumō uvāō tti. annayā āgayā caüddasī. ṭhiyā sāhuṇō ubavāsēṇaṁ bhikkhāṇahiṇḍaṇēṇaṁ. mugiyā ya tīē. taō cintiuṁ payattā. jaï kahaṁci kallaṁ na ēsa vāvāijjaï, taō gamissaï pakkhasandhīē. na ettha annō kōi uvāō; tā karēūṇa kaṁsāraṁ tālapuḍasaṁjuyaṁ cēgaṁ visamō. yagaṁ gōsē uvaṇēmi ēyāṇaṁ, nibandhaō ya bhujāvissāmi ētē. taō sahatthaparivēsaṇēṇaṁ tammōyagappayāṇēṇaṁ vāvāissaṁ ima ti. saṁpā iyaṁ jahāsamīhiyamimīē. gayā gōsē cēva bhōyaṇaṁ ghettūṇa tamujāṇaṁ jāliṇī. diṭṭhā sihikumāraṇa, bhaṇiyā ya tēṇaṁ-amba! kimē gāgiṇī kiṁpi aṇuciyaṁ ghettūṇa āgayā si?. jāliṇīē bhaṇiyaṁ — jāya! attaṇō cēva puṇṇāhilāsiṇī tumhāṇa bhōyaṇaṁ ti. sihi kumārēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — amba! ēsō vi khu aṇāyārō caïva samaṇāṇaṁ, jamāhākaḍaṁ āhaḍaṁ ca mujjaē tti. kahiō sē vihī. taō tīē bhaṇiyaṁ — jāya! na annahā mē hiyayanivuī hōi, aphalaṁ ca mannēmi asaṁpāiē imammi jāyassa āgamaṇaṁ. tā avassaṁ taē imaṁ kāyavaṁ ti bhaṇiūṇa nivaḍiyā calaṇēsu. tō ya ujjuyasahāvaō pecchaha, sē dhammasaḍḍhā jāyasiṇēhō ya, tā mā sē vipariṇāmō bhavissaï tti, tō gurulāghavamālōciūṇaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ sihikumārēṇa amba! jaṁ tuma bhaṇasi tti. kiṁ tu na tumaē puṇō vi sāhunimittamārambhō kāyayō. jāliṇīē bhaṇiyaṁ — jāya! ēvaṁ jaṁ tuma bhaṇasi tti. sihikumārēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — jaï ēvaṁ, tō dēhi ēyassa sāhuṇō bhōyaṇajāyaṁ, taō bhunissāmi tti. jāliṇīē bhaṇiyaṁ — jāya! daṁsiyaṁ cēva tumaē māivacchalattaṇaṁ, tā kiṁ imiṇā, mama hatthāō bhottavvaṁ ti. sihikumārēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — amba! ēvaṁ āgacchaü pāraṇagavēla tti. taō āgayā pāraṇagavēlā. kumāravayaṇabahumāṇaō uvaviṭṭhā sāhuṇō. dināṇi tīē jahōciēṇa vihiṇā bhāyaṇāī. pariviṭṭhō ya musaṁbhiō kāsārō. pabhuttā ya sāhuṇō. dinnō ya bhuttasēsakāsārasaṁgaō cēva kumārassa tālapuḍalaḍḍuō, bhuttō ya tēgaṁ. āyantā ya sāhuṇō. avaṇīyāī bhāyaṇāī. etthantarammi āḍhattō ghārijiu si hikumārō. cintiyaṁ tēṇa kimēyaṁ ti? palōiyā ya sāhuṇō, jāva satthā ciṭṭhanti. taō gr̥hiyamaṇēṇa. ēvaṁ ca jāva thēvā vēlā aïkamaï, tāva paṇaṭā sē vāyā. cintiyaṁ ca ṇēṇaṁ-nūṇaṁ na bhavimsāmi tti. nivaḍiō dharaṇivaḍhē. āulīhayā sāhavō, jāliṇī ya. cintiyaṁ ca tēhi-kimēyaṁ akajjaṁ jaṇaṇīē sē kvasiyaṁ bhavissaï?

ghārijantō ya tō visēṇa kāūṇamaṇasaṇaṁ vihiṇā

paricintiuṁ payattō hanta! apuvaṁ kimēyaṁ ti?

dhī saṁsārasahāvō ambā (mbaṁ) kila dhammacaraṇajōēṇa

saṁsārakilēsāō mōyavissāmi acirēṇa

jāva na saṁpanna miṇaṁ samīhiyaṁ avigalaṁ apuṣṇassa

taha pāḍiyā ya ēsā pamāyaō ayasapammi

saṅkissaï ya aṇajō lōō etyaṁ asaṅkaṇijjaṁ pi

ambāē pucavuttantabhāviō mōhadōsēṇa

dhī imiṇā jamṇaṁ ambāē saṁkilēsajaṇaēṇaṁ

ahavā ēvaṁviha ēva ēsa pāvō ti saṁsārō

bhaṇiyaṁ ca —

pāventi ayasapay kēvi hu akaē vi ettha dōsammi

parabhavaniyāṇaō cciya kēi na pāventi hu kaē vi

jaṁ cittā kammagaī tā ēyaṁ ciya imīē pacchittaṁ

pubbi duñciṇṇāṇaṁ phalamasuhaṁ cēva kammāṇaṁ

ahavā na sōyaṇijjā saṁpayamēsā vi jīvalōyammi

simuhaphalakappatarūṁ jiṇadhamma pāviyā jēṇa

tā sumarāmō paramaṁ paramapayasāhagaṁ jiṇakkhāyaṁ

aha pañca namōkāraṁ saṁpaï ki sēsacintāē

tō sō suhapariṇāmō paścanamōkārabhāvaṇājuttō

mariūṇaṁ uvayanō tiyasabarō bambhalōgammi

navasāgarōvamāū raïlacchisamāgamē vimāṇammi

sāmāṇiō mahappā bambhasurēsassa divvajuī

iyarī vi kālasēsaṁ gamiuṁ mariūṇa sakkarappahāē

uvavanā nēraïō tisāgarāū mahāghōrō

sihijāliṇimāisuyā jaṁ bhaṇiyamihāsi taṁ gayamiyāṇiṁ

vocchāmi samāsēṇaṁ dhaṇadhaṇasirimō ya païmajjā

atthi ihēva jambuddīvē dīvē bhārahē vāsē sōhammasuralōyapaḍicchandayabhūyaṁ niccussavāṇandapamuiyamahājaṇaṁ avirayapavattapeccha ṇayasōhiyaṁ surasariyāsalilaniddhōyapērantaṁ susammanaparaṁ nāma puravaraṁ tuliyasurasundarīyaṇalaḍa hattaṇarūbavēsavihavāhiṁ paüraṅgaṇāhiṁ kaliyaṁ mayaraddhayapaḍāyāhi.

mottūṇa savvamannaṁ paratthasaṁpāyaṇekkatallicchō

jattha purisāṇa vaggō vahaï jahatthaṁ niyaṁ nāma

tattha paḍivaksanaraṇāhadoghaṭṭhakēsarī sudhā nāma rāyā. tassa bahumaō savvanayarēka seṭṭhī dīṇāṇāhakiviṇajaṇavacchalō bandhavaku muyāyarasasī lahuiyavēsamaṇavihavō tivaggasaṁpāyaṇaraī vēsamaṇō nāma satyavāhō tti. tassa samāgakularūvavihavasīlō siridēvī nāma bhāriyā. tāṇaṁ ca paropparaṁ siṇēhasāraṁ visayasuhamaṇuhavantāṇa aïkkantō kōi kālō. annayāvañcacintā samuppajjaï. taō tannayarasannihiyassa dhaṇadēvābhihāṇajakkhassa mahāpūyaṁ kāūṇa kayaṁ uvāiyamaṇēhiṁ. bhayavaṁ, jaï nō tuha pabhāvaō suuppattī bhavissaï, tō bhagavaō savvanayarajaṇāhiṭṭhiyaṁ mahāmahaṁ karissāmō, suyassa ya bhayavaō cēva nāmaṁ ukkhivissāmō ti.

taō tāṇa majjhimē vayasi vaṭṭamāṇāṇaṁ sō bambhalōyakappavāsī dēvō ahāuyamaṇuvāliūṇa taō cuō siridēvīē gambhē uvavannō tti. diṭṭhō ya tīē sumiṇayaṁmi tīē cēva rayaṇīē pabhāyasamayaṁsi uttuṅgadhavalakāō añcantalīlagāmī aṇavarayapayaṭṭadāṇō gaṇḍaya lāvaḍiyachappayāvalī caüdasaṇa bhāsurō ārattatālū lulantalīlākarō kaṇayasaṅkalābaddhaghaṇṭājuyalō rattacamarabhūsiyāṇaṇō aṅkusocchaï yakumbhamāōṁ ghummantacārulōyaṇasirī savvaṅgasundarāhirāmō mattahatthī vayaṇēṇamuyaraṁ pavisamāṇō tti. pāsiūṇa ya muhavibuddhā ēsā. siṭṭhō ya tīē jaïhāvihiṁ daïyassa. harisavasubhinnapulaēṇaṁ bhaṇiyā ya tēṇaṁ. sundari! sayalasayaṇagaṇanāyagō tē puttō bhavissaï. taō sā ēvaṁ ti bhattāravayaṇamahiṇandiūṇa pahaṭṭamuhapaṅkayā jāyā. tō visēsaō tighaggasaṁpāyaṇarayāē saṁpūriyasayalamaṇōrahāē abhajjamāṇapasaraṁ puṇṇaphalamaṇuhavantīē pattō pasūisamaō. taō pasatthē tihikaraṇa hunajōē muhaṁsuhēṇa pasūyā ēsā. jāō sē dāraō. nivēiō pariōsayāriṇīē gēhadāsīē vēsamaṇassa. parituṭṭhō seṭṭhī. di tīē pāriōsiyaṁ. davāviyaṁ ca tēṇa mahā. dāṇaṁ, kārāviyaṁ vaddhāvaṇayaṁ. tō aïkkantē māsē mahāvibhūīē sayalanayarajaṇaparigaō dhētūṇa dārayaṁ gaō ghēṇadēvajakkhālayaṁ seṭṭhī. saṁpāiyā tassa mahimā, pāḍiō calaṇēsu dāraō. kayaṁ sē nāmaṁ dhaṇaṁ tti. taō kālakkamēṇa pattō kumārabhāvaṁ.

etthantarammi sō jāliṇījīvanāraō taō narayāō uvvaṭṭiūṇa puṇō saṁsāramāhiṇḍiya aṇantarabhavē tahā'kāmanijarāē mari ūṇa taṁmi cēva nayarē puṇṇabhahassa satthavāhassa gōmaīē bhāriyāē kucchisi dhūyattāē uvavannō. jāyā uciyasamaēṇaṁ. kayaṁ sē nāma dhaṇasiri tti. pattā jovvaṇaṁ. dihā ya tēṇaṁ aṭṭhamīcandamahūsavē mayaṇalīlāharujjāṇāō raharūdhāriṇī sahiyaṇasamēyā sabhavaṇamuva gacchantī dhaṇasiritti. taō punabhavanbhatthamettīguṇāō sāhilāsaṁ palōiyā dhaṇēṇaṁ. tīē vi ya tahanbhatyamaccharāō suiramavalō iodhaṇō ti. lakkhiō sē bhāvō pāsavattiṇā sōmadēvābhihāṇēṇaṁ purōhiyamuēṇaṁ. savaṇaparaṁparāē samāgaō sakṇagōyaraṁ ēsa vuttantō vēsamaṇassa. taō variyā tēṇaṁ dhaṇanimittaṁ dhaṇasirī. dinnā sabahumāṇaṁ puṇṇabhaddēṇa. muṇiō ēsa vuttantō paropparamimēhi. parituṭṭhō dhaṇō niyahiyaēṇaṁ, dūmiyā dhaṇasirī. kayāī vēsamaṇapuṇṇabhadēhi mahāvaddhāvaṇayāī. vattō mahāvibhūīē sayalanayaracchērayabhūō vivāhō.

taō aïkkantō kōi kālō. ghaḍiyā ēsā tassa cēva gharapamaēṇaṁ nandayābhihāṇēṇaṁ cēḍēṇaṁ. sō ya kila aggisammassa tāvasapariyāē vaṭṭamāṇassa ajjavakōḍiṇṇapariyāraō saṁgamaō nāma paramamittō āsi tti. taō tīē saddhiṁ visēsaō viḍabbaṇāpāyaṁ visayamuhamaṇuhavantassa aïkkantō kōī kālō dhaṇassa. pattō ya sē kālakkamēṇaṁ navajalabhariyasarōvaravirāyantakamalāyarō kama lāyarpasattaümmattamahuraguñjantabhamirabhamaraülō bhamaraülucchāhiyasurayakhinnasaharisakalālāvihaṁsaülamuhalō muhalagōyālajubaïpāraddha sarasagēyaravocchaïyacchettamaggō sarayasamaō tti. avi ya—

nibbharakusumabharōṇayarasāumuhalēhi asaṇabāṇēhiṁ

kāsakuḍaēhi ya daḍhaṁ jattha isanti bva raṇṇāī

iti api ca

nissēsaṁ lavaṇōyahisalilaṁ mottūṇa jattha sōhanti

dhavalā ghaṇā puṇō pīyasarasaduddhōyahijala vva

dīsanti jattha sattacchayāṇa mayavāraṇēhi bhaggāī

gandhāyaḍiyagaṇḍālijālarusiēhi va vaṇāī

cirasaṁciyaṁ ca viuṇaṁ mukō ghaṇabandhaṇassa va miyaṅkō

saraümmattō vva jahiṁ jaṇassa joṇhaṁ pavikkhiraï

ēvaṁ guṇāhirāmē sarayasamaē diṭṭhō dhaṇēṇa tannayaravatthavvaō cēva samiddhidattō nāma satyavāhaputtō tti. dēsantarāō bahuyaṁ daviṇa jāyaṁ viviūṇa mahākattigīē dīṇāṇāhāgamaṇivāriyaṁ mahādāṇaṁ dentō ti. taō taṁ daṭṭaṇa cintiyaṁ dhaṇēṇa. dhannō khu ēsō, jō ēvaṁ niyabhuyajjiēṇaṁ daviṇajāēṇaṁ parośyāraṁ karēi. jāō vimaṇō. bhaṇiō ya pāsaparivattiṇā nandaēṇaṁ. satthavāhaputta, kimu. biggō viya tumaṁ jāō tti. sāhiō ya tēṇaṁ niyayāhippāō. nandaēṇaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ — satyavāhaputta, thēvamiyaṁ; atthi bhavaō vi mahā puṇṇōjiyaṁ daviṇajāyaṁ. tā dēu imānō vi visēyayaraṁ bhavaṁ pi. dhaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — kimaṇēṇa punvapurisajjiēṇaṁ. bhaṇiyaṁ ca lōē salāhaṇijjō sō u narō dīṇapaṇaïvaggassa. jō dēi niyabhuyajjiyamapatthiō davvasaṁdhāya.

na ya mē kiṁci niyabhujiyaṁ atthi. tā vinavē hi tāyaṁ. karēmi ahaṁ puvvapurisasēviyaṁ vāṇijja, gacchāmi disāyattāē. kālōciyamakuvvamāṇō purisō jīviyaṁ vihalīkarēi. kālō ya mē tivaggasāhaṇamūlaṁ atthamuvajjiṅa. tā karēhi mē pasāyaṁ samīhiya saṁpāyaṇēṇaṁ ti. vinatō tēṇaṁ seṭṭhī. bhaṇiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa. nandaya, ēvaṁ bhaṇāhi mē jāyaṁ. jahā-vaccha, atthi cēva tuha sayalanayara sedvihitō vi abbhahiyaṁ tivaggasāhaṇamūlaṁ atthajāyaṁ. tā karēhi imiṇā cēva jahāsamīhiyaṁ ti. nandaēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — tāya, atthi ēyaṁ tahavi puṇa na ēyassa annahā dhiī havaï. seṭṭhiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ — jahā ēyassa dhiī havaï tahā karēu tti. nivēiyamiṇaṁ nandaēṇa dhaṇassa. parituṭṭhō khu ēsō. kayā saṁjattī. payaṭṭiyaṁ nāṇāpayāraṁ bhaṇḍajāyaṁ. kārāviyamāghōsaṇaṁ. jahā-dhaṇō satyavāhaputtō imāō nayarāō tāmalittiṁ gacchissaï. tā tēṇa samaṁ jō kōi tanayaragāmī, sō payaṭṭaü. jassa jaṁ na saṁpajjaï pāhēyamuvagaraṇaṁ vā, tassa taṁ ēsa saṁpāḍēi ti payaṭṭō jaṇō.

etthantaraṁmi cintiyaṁ dhaṇasirīē. sōhaṇaṁ mē bhavissaï ēyassa pavasaṇēṇaṁ. āyaṇiyaṁ ca pañcāsannē gamaṇadiyahē, jahā nandaō vi imiṇā saha gamissaï tti. taō māyāvattiē bhaṇiō satyavāhaputtō. ajjaütta, patthiō tumaṁ; maē uṇa kiṁ kāyavvaṁ ti. tēṇa bhaṇiya-sundari, gurūṇaṁ susmusā. tō niyaḍipahāṇī bāhajalabhariyalōyagāē sadukkhamiva bhaṇiyaṁ dhasirīē — ajjaütta, hiyayasannihiyā gurū. jaï puṇa tumaṁ mēṁ ujjhiūṇa gacchahisi tā sihaṁ tuha imaṁ, avassamahamappāṇayaṁ vāvāissaṁ ti avvattasaī rōviuṁ pavattā. etthantaraṁmi samāgayā dhaṇassa jaṇaṇī. abbhutthiyā tēṇa. niggayā ya dhaṇasirī. lakkhiō sē bhāvō imīē. aṇusāsiō ya tīē bahuvihaṁ suō. jahā-jāya, dīhāṇi khu dēsantarāṇi, sulahō viōgō, dullahō puṇō vi saṁgamō, kilēsāyā sapaüraṁ ca atyōvajaṇaṁ, avisāō ya mūlaṁ imassa | tō jaï vi tuma sayalaguṇasaṁjuō, tahā vi visēsaō khamāiguṇēsu jattō kāyavvō. aṇavarayaṁ ca mē paüttī dāyaba ti. dhaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — amba, jaṁ tumaṁ āṇavēsi. tō gayā sē jaṇaṇī. visa jāviyā ya tīē vaha ['pēīgharāō, aṇujāṇaha tumhē dhaṇēṇa saha dhaṇasiriṁ gacchamāṇi ti. gatā saharisaṁ. aṇuṇṇāyā tēhiṁ] payaṭṭō satthō, aṇavarayapayāṇaēhiṁ ca pattō dumāsamettēṇa kālēṇa tāmalittiṁ. diṭṭhō naravaī. bahumaniō tēṇaṁ. niōiyaṁ bhaṇḍaṁ. na samāsāiō jahicchiyalāhō. taō cintiyamaṇēṇaṁ. kahamahaṁ asaṁpāḍiyamaṇōrahō gēhaṁ gacchāmi? tā pañcāsamma ēva bhayavaṁ rayaṇā yarō, ēyamavagāhāmi tti. na ya saṁsayamaṇārūḍhō purisō ēgantāvāyabhīrū sayalayaṇāṇandayāriṇi saṁpayaṁ pāvēi. kiṁ vā tīē rahiyassa purisasaṁkhāmettaphalasāhaēṇaṁ jīviēṇaṁ. tā aṇuciṭṭhāmi samudataraṇaṁ. saṁpahāriūṇa nandaēṇa dhaṇasirīē ya saha ṭhāviō siddhantō.

etthantaraṁmi ya uvaṭṭiyāē majjaṇavēlāē duitthamettanaracīranivasaṇō uddāmanaharavilihiyaṅgō sēḍiyāghasaṇadhavalapāṇī tambōlarā yarajjiyāharō parimilāṇakusumamuṇḍamālī jūyayaravandrapelliō bhayakāyaraṁ maggō pōēmāṇō āgaō jūyayarō tti. bhaṇiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa-ajja, saraṇāgaō mhi, tā rakkhaü ajjō ēēsiṁ aṇajjajūyayarāṇaṁ. dhaṇēṇaṁ bhaṇiya-bhada, vīsatyō hōhi aha kiṁnimittaṁ puṇa ēē bhadaṁ ahihavanti. tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — bhadda, ajja, bhāgadhēyāṇi mē puccha, na sakkuṇōmi ācikkhiuṁ. tō dhaṇēṇa ahō sē bhāvagaruō ālāō ti cintiūṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — bhada,alaṁ visāēṇa; kassa vi samadasāvibhāō na hōi, tā kahēu bhaddō ettha kāraṇaṁ. taō pañcāgayasaṁvēgēṇa bāharuddhanayaṇēṇaṁ sagaggayakkharaṁ sāhiyaṁ tēṇaṁ. ajja, vāṇiyayakulaphaṁsaṇō ubhayalōyaviruddhasēvī vibuhajaṇanindiō visapāyavō vva avayāranimittaṁ cēva pāṇiṇaṁ samuppanō mhi kusumaüranivāsī mahēsaradattō nāma ahayaṁ ti. sapuṇṇajaṇavajiēṇaṁ sayala dōsanihāṇabhūēṇaṁ jūēṇaṁ īisaṁ avatthaṁ pattō miha. tō dhaṇēṇa cintiyaṁ-ahō sē vivēgō, ēyāvatthāgaya pi appāṇayaṁ jāṇaï akajjāyaraṇaṁ ca parivēēi, tā garuō khu kōi ēsō cintiūṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. bhada, tā kiṁ tē karīyaü? taō tēṇa aṇuciyavibbhama milāyantalōyaṇaṁ sussantavayaṇaṁ khalantakkharaṁ daraṁ jaṁpiuṁ na jaṁpiyaṁ cēva. tō dhaṇēṇa hāriyaṁ kiṁpi bhavissaï, taṁ na caēi patthi ti atthō'vagacchiūṇa bhaṇiō nandaō. bhadda nandaya, pucchāhi ēē bāhiṁ paribbhamantē jūyayarē, jahā bhadāṇa kimavaraddhamimiṇā bhaddēṇaṁ ti. niggaō nandaō. pucchiyā tēṇa jūyayarā. siḍhē cimēhi. ēsō khu vāyāmayaganthēṇaṁ sōlasa suvaṇṇē hāriūṇa ajja sahiēṇa niruddhō vi chidaṁ lahiūṇa chōhabāvaḍāṇa amhāṇa adāūṇa suvaṇṇayaṁ palāiūṇa iha paviṭṭhō tti. taō sāhiyamiṇaṁ nandaēṇa dhaṇassa. bhaṇiō ya tēṇa-dēhi ēyāṇa sōlasa suvaṇṇē. dinnā nandaēṇa. gayā jūyayarā. bhaṇiō ya sō dhaṇēṇa-bhadda, udvēhi, muśca visāyaṁ. kajapahāṇā khu purisā havanti, visāyabahulō ya ithiyānaṇō. tā majjēu bhō. taō viliō viya uḍiō mahēsaradattō, majiō saha dhaṇēṇaṁ. dinnaṁ sē khōmajuyalaṁ, parihiyaṁ ca tēṇaṁ. bhuttuttarakālammi ya bhaṇiō dhaṇēṇaṁ-bhadda, ēgajāiō sajjaṇabhāvaō ya sāhāraṇaṁ tē imaṁ daviṇajāyaṁ. tā iō kiṁpi gihiūṇa saṁyaṁ cēva niōyamaṇuciṭṭhaü bhahō. kiṁ imiṇā bhahassa vi aṇabhimaēṇaṁ vibuhajaṇanindiēṇaṁ ubhayalōyaaīvakucchiēṇaṁ ahamajaṇatudvijaṇaēṇa jūyayāraceṭṭhiēṇaṁ ti. mahēsaradattēṇa cintiyaṁ ahō mē ahamnayā, tāyaruddadēvakulasarisaṁ imassa ceṭṭhiyaṁ, mama uṇa imaṁ īisaṁ ti. avi ya—

na vi taha parōvayāraṁ akarentō lāghavaṁ narō lahaï

jaha kijjantuvayārō parēṇa karuṇāpavannēṇaṁ

tā kiṁ imiṇā, abalambēmi pōrisaṁ, karēmi saṁpayaṁ pi sakulasarisaṁ ti. cintiūṇa bhaṇiyaṁ mahēsaradattēṇaṁ-ajja, dhannō khu ahaṁ, jassa mē tumaē saha daṁsaṇaṁ samuppannaṁ. aō paricattaṁ cēva maē saṁpayaṁ bahujaṇāṇahimayaṁ ceṭṭhiyaṁ, paḍivannō ahaṁ purisaguṇēhiṁ, vimukkō alacchīē. tā kiṁ bahuṇā jaṁpiēṇaṁ. abassamahaṁ ajappabhāvēṇēva ajjassa uvaē saparissama saphalaṁ karēūṇa ajja pekkhāmi tti bhaṇiūṇa niggaō gēhāō nayarīō ya. tō ya kiṁ karēmi, kiṁ lōmi daviṇajāyanimittaṁ bhagavantaṁ jalanihiṁ. attharahiō khu purisō apurisō cēva. daridassa hi na vitthiraï jasō, na viyambhaē kittī, na sajjaṇēṇa saṁgamō na parōvayārasaṁpāyaṇaṁ ti. ahavā ayaṇḍamaṇōrahabhagurēsu vijiyasurāsurēsu ya saharasuddāmabhamirēsu kāladaṇḍēnu kimaṇēṇālōiēṇaṁ. dullahaṁ māṇusajammaṇaṁ, tā aṅgīkarōmi bhayavantaṁ ubhayalōyamuhāvahaṁ dhammaṁ. ēvaṁ ca kaē samāṇē imassa vi satthavāhaputtassa paramatthaō uvagayaṁ cēva havaī' tti cintiūṇa pavannō piuvayaṁsayassa jōgīsarābhihāṇassa kāvāliyassa samīvē pavvajjaṁ ti.

iō ya nivēiō niyayāhippāō dhaṇēṇaṁ nandayadhaṇasirīṇaṁ. bhaṇiō ya tēhiṁ-kē amhē bhavaō samīhiyantarāyakaraṇassa?. jaṁ vō rōyaï, tamēva aṇucidaü ajō tti. taō gahiyaṁ dhaṇēga paratīragāmiyaṁ bhaṇḍaṁ, gavēsāviyaṁ pavahaṇaṁ.

etthantaraṁmi bhaṇiō dhaṇasirīē nandaō. jahā-vāvāēmō ēyaṁ, gacchāmō annattha, kiṁṇē samudataraṇēṇaṁ. nandaēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ hā na juttamēyaṁ, sāmī khu ēsō sammāviō ya. tā na tumaē ēvaṁ suviṇē vi cintiyavvaṁ ti. taō cintiyaṁ dhaṇasirīē. na ēsa ēyaṁ vavasaï tā ahaṁ cēva kēṇaï uvāēṇa ēyaṁ karissāmi tti. kaō tīē nāgadattāparivvāiyāō nisāmiūṇa āyaṅkakāraō kālantaranivāī kammaṇajōgō ti.

etthantaraṁmi saṁjattiyaṁ parahaṇaṁ, nimiyaṁ garuyabhaṇḍaṁ. taō pasatthadiyahami nimgaō dhaṇō, gaō vēlāulaṁ. dinnaṁ dīṇāṇāhāṇa daviṇajāyaṁ. saṁpūiō jalanihī. agghiyaṁ jāṇavattaṁ. ārūḍhō khu ēsō saha pariyaṇēṇa. ukkhittā nagarā, āūriō sakunda dhavalō siyavaḍō.

tō laṅghiuṁ pavattaṁ kacchahakarimayaraniyaratimikaliyaṁ

saṅghaülāuladēsaṁ pāyālatalaṁ va gambhīraṁ

jalagayajalaharapaḍimāpaḍivāraṇadaṁsaṇēṇa añcatthaṁ

dappurdharakarimayarucchalantasaṁkhōhiyataraṅgaṁ

vēlāulalavalī haranisaṇṇagandhavvamihuṇaramaṇijja

hīrindanīlamaragayamaūhaparirañjiyajalōhaṁ

maṇyācaladarimandiranisaṇṇasiddhavahupulaïyasuvēlaṁ

kappūrasaṇḍamaṇḍiyamahindakaridaliyaviyaḍataḍaṁ

pavaṇadhuyajalalavāhayasaïsarasantatīratālavaṇaṁ

vidumalayāhirāmaṁ sindhuvaī pavaṇavēgēṇa

akayapaḍiyārō mahāvāhiṇā. jāyaṁ sē mahōyaraṁ, parimukkāō bhūyāō, ussūṇaṁ vayaṇaṁ, gaṇḍiyāō jaṅghāō, phuḍiyā karacaraṇā, na rōyaï sē bhōyaṇaṁ, bāhijjaï tisāē, na ciṭṭhaï pīyamudayamudaraṁmi. taō visaṇṇō dhaṇō. cintiyaṁ ca tēṇa. kimēvamayaṇḍē cēva pāvavilasiyaṁ. ahavā natthi ayālō pāvabilasiyassa. tā kiṁ karēmi. uttammaï mē pariyaṇō, visaṇṇā dhaṇasirī, pavāyavayaṇō ya nandaō. tō kiṁ imammi cēva rayaṇāyarē vāvāēmi appāṇayaṁ ti. ahavā na ēvamēēsi muhaṁ hōi, avi ya ahiyayaraṁ duhaṁ ti. na ya akayapaḍiyārassa imaṁ kāpurisaceṭṭhiyaṁ jujjaï. bhaṇiyaṁ ca ambāē avisāiṇā hōyavvaṁ ti. pacāsannaṁ ca jahāsamīhiyaṁ avarakūlaṁ. tā imaṁ tāva ettha pattakālaṁ, nandayaṁ cēva bhaṇḍasāmittaṇē niuñāmi. vicittāṇi khu vihiṇō vilasiyāṇi. kō jāṇaï, kiṁ bhavissaï tti? sō ya tāva tāyamukayaṁ mama ya bhāiṇēhaṁ bahu mannamāṇō ēyaṁ dhaṇasiri bandhavahatthagayaṁ karissaï tti. cintiūṇa bhaṇiō ya tēṇaṁ nandaō dhaṇasirī ya. vayaṁsa nandaya, kammapariṇaïvasēṇa ēsā mē avasthā, paccāsannaṁ ca jahicchiyaṁ avarakūlaṁ, aṇēgāvāyapīḍiyaṁ ca jīviyaṁ savvasattāṇaṁ cēva visēsaō vāhipīḍiyasarīrāṇaṁ amhārisāṇaṁ ti. ahiṭṭhēhi imaṁ ritthaṁ, tuma cēva etthaṁ nāyagō, samuttiṇṇassa ya mē bhayavantaṁ jalanihiṁ pacchannassēva jahōciyaṁ upakkama karējāsi. taō jaï mē rōgāvagamō bhavissaï, taō sundaraṁ cēva, annahā u tāyamukayaṁ bahumannamāṇēṇa mamaṁ ca bhāuyasiṇēhaṁ pāviyacā taē bandhavāṇaṁ ēsā bhattāravacchalā dhaṇasirī. sundari, taē vi ya imō mōnūṇa pāvaṁ ahaṁ viya daṭṭabyō, na khaṇḍiyadhvaṁ imassa vayaṇaṁ. etthantarammi sadukkhaṁ cēva parunō nandaō dhaṇasirī ya kaïyavēṇaṁ. dhaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ vayaṁsa nandaya, na ēsa kālō visāyassa; tā abalambēhi pōrusaṁ,ujjhēhi kāurisabahumayaṁ kilīvattaṇaṁ niyamēhi niyayahiyayaṁmi kālōciyaṁ kajja. sundari, tumaṁ pi paricaya itthīyaṇahiyayarāyahāṇisōyaṁ, visumarēhi cintāyāsakāriṇaṁ siṇēhaṁ, avalambēhi kajja. ettha khalu sō purisō itthiyā vā pasaṁsijjaï, jō kālann. kālannū ya santō ucchāhavantō avassamāvayaṁ lōi tti. taō paḍivannamaṇēhiṁ dhanasāsaṇaṁ. pattāṇi mahākaḍāhaṁ nāma dīvaṁ. gaō nandaō ghettūṇa pāhuḍaṁ naravaïmavalōiuṁ. bahumaniō rāiṇā. dinamāvāsatthāmaṁ. ōyāriyaṁ bhaṇḍaṁ. uvaṇīyā dhaṇassa vejjā. pāraddhō ukkamō. tajjōgadāṇaō na ya sē vāhī avēi. taō cintiyaṁ nandaēṇaṁ. na niyadē samapattassa imasta ēsa vāhī avēi ti, taō na juttamiha kālamakkhiviuṁ. taō niōiyaṁ bhaṇḍaṁ, gahiyaṁ ca paḍibhaṇḍaṁ, sajjiyaṁ jāṇavattaṁ. divō naravaī, saṁpūiō tēṇa. payaṭṭō niyadēsamāgantuṁ.

aïkkantēsu kaïvayapayāṇaēmu cintiyaṁ dhaṇasirīē. kahaṁ na vivannō ēsō. sadēsamuragayāē ya dullahō ēyassa vāvāyaṇōvāō, jīvamāṇō ya ēsō niccē mē hiyayasallabhūō tti. tā imaṁ ettha pattakālaṁ. ṭhāi cēva ēsō pādakkhālayaṁmi rayaṇīē, tō imami cēva jalayarasattamāsurē sāyarē pakkhivāmiti. pakkhittō ya ēsō cavalabhāvaō jāṇavattassa andhayārayāē rayaṇīē tahamaṭṭhō cēva nissaṁsayaṁ na bhavissaï. ēvaṁ ca kara samāṇē ēsō vi nandaō mē sāsaō bhavissaï ti cintiūṇa saṁpāiyaṁ dhaṇasirīē jahāsamīhiyaṁ. pakkhittō jāmāvasēsāēm̐ rayaṇīē pādakkhālayanimittamuḍiō pāyālagambhīrē samuddammi satyavāhaputtō. ṭhiyā kaṁci kālaṁ. kaō tīē hāhāravō. uḍiō nandaō. pucchiyā ēsā sāmiṇi! kim ēyaṁ kim ēyaṁ ti. taō sā attāṇamaṇutāḍayantī sadukkhamiva ahiyayaraṁ rōviuṁ pavattā. hā ajjaütta hā ajjaütta tti bhaṇantī nivaḍiyā dharaṇivaḍhē. taō nandaēṇa saṁjāyāsaṅkēṇa satyavāhaputtasejja nirūviya tamapekkhamāṇēṇa sagaggayakkharaṁ puṇō vivāhittā sāmiṇi, kim ēyaṁ kim ēyaṁ ti. dhaṇasirīē bhaṇiyaṁ — ēsō khu ajjaüttō āyamaṇanimittamuṭṭiō pamāyaō samuddē nivaḍiō tti. taō ēyamāyaṇṇiūṇa bāhajalabhariyalōyaṇō tannēhamōhiyamaī tammi cēva attāṇayaṁ pakkhiviumāḍhattō nandaō, dhariō pariyaṇē. taō añcantasōyāṇalajaliyamāṇasō na ettha uvāyantaraṁ kamaï ti visaṇṇō. dharāviō tēṇa bōhitthō. annēsiūṇa gōsē uccāiyā naṅgarā, payaṭṭō sadukkhaṁ ahippēyadēsābhimuhō. iō ya sō satyavāhaputtō paḍaṇasamaṇantaramēva samāsāiyapuvabhinnarōhitthaphalagō sattarattēga samuttariūṇa sāyaraṁ lavaṇajalāsēvaṇa vigayavāhī saṁpattō tīramāyaṁ. uttiṇṇō sāyarāō puṇō jāyamiva attāṇayaṁ mannamāṇō uvaviṭhṭhō timirapāyavasamīvē. cintiyaṁ ca tēṇaṁ ahō māyābahulayā itthiyāvaggassa,ahō nisaṁsayā dhaṇasirīē, ahō asarisō mamōvari vērāṇubandhō, ahō lahuiyaṁ ubhayakulamimīē. tā kiṁ puṇa sē imassa vavasāyassa kāraṇaṁ? ahavā avivēyavahulē isthiyāyaṇē kō kāraṇaṁ pucchaï ti? itthiyā hi nāma nivāsō dōsāṇaṁ, nimittaṁ sāhasāṇaṁ, uppattī kavaḍāṇaṁ, khettaṁ musāvāyassa, duvāraṁ asēyamagāssa, āyayaṇamāvayāṇaṁ, sōvāṇaṁ narayāṇaṁ, aggalā kusalapurapavēsassa. tā ki imiṇā cintiēṇaṁ, kajjaṁ cintēmi. na ēsa kālō ēyassa ālōciyavassa, avi ya ucchāhassa. ucchāhamamuścamāṇō purisō avassaṁ cēva vavasāyāṇurūvaṁ phalaṁ pāvēi, na ya atīyavatthucintā daḍhaṁ kāyavva tti vuḍavāō. thē cimaṁ paōyaṇaṁ purisassa, gatyaṁ ca jaṇaṇijaṇayā; tē ya mē sundarā cēva ti cintiūṇa uḍiō pāyavasamīvāō. gaō thēvaṁ bhūmibhāgaṁ. divāya tēṇaṁ vahaṇabhaṅgavivanāē sāvatthīnaravaïssa sīhaladīvagāmiṇīē dhūyācēḍiyāra[tīsē vēva piusantigā cēḍiyā tīsē samappiyā bhaṇḍāriṇīē, vivannammi ya taṁmi vahaṇaē samuhavīīhiṁ ghattiyā kūlē paścattamuvagayā sā cēḍī tamuddēsāgaraṇa diṭṭhā ya tēṇaṁ tīsē] uttarī yadēsaṁmi tamuddēsamujjōvayantī tellōkasārā nāma rayaṇāvali tti. abujjhamāṇēṇa ya imaṁ vuttantaṁ parakērigāē vi imīē vavahariūṇa puṇō puṇō iṇamēva udisiya kusalapakkhaṁ karessāmi ti cintiūṇa gahiyā ya tēṇaṁ. payaṭṭō visayasaṁmuhaṁ. diṭṭhō ya tēṇaṁ jūyayaravaïyaravi mōiō pavanakāvāliyavaō susiddhagāruḍamantō mantasāhaṇatthaṁ cēva samuddataḍamahivasantō mahēsaradattō. tēṇa vi ēsō tti pañcabhinnāō. tēṇaṁ bhaṇiō ya-satthavāhaputta, kuō tuma,kahaṁ vā tē īisī avasthā? taō na gēhaducca riyamannassa payāsiuṁ jujjaï tti cintiūṇa bhaṇiyaṁ dhaṇēṇaṁ. jalanihīō ahaṁ, vahaṇaviōgī mamēyaṁ īdisī avattha tti. mahēsaradattēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. apahiō vihī unnayāṇaṁ bhaṅgēsu, sucañcalā siri tti saccō lōyavāō. kilēsāyāsabahulō gihavāsō,jēṇa bhavaō vi kappapāyavassa viya parahiyasaṁpāyaṇāmē taphalajammassa ī disī avattha tti. ahavā thēvamēyaṁ. paṇaṭṭhō vi sasī kālajōgaō acirēṇa cēva saṁpuṇṇayaṁ pāvaī, visamadasāvibhāē ya vaṭṭamāṇā dēvā vi parikilēsabhāiṇō havanti,kimaṅga puṇa maccalōyavāsī jaṇō. tā na taē saṁtappiyatvaṁ. āvayāē vajakaḍhiṇa hiyayā cēva mahāpurisā ivanti. uvayārigī ya āvayājaō najaï imīē sajaṇāsajjaṇavisēsō, lakkhijjaē aṇurattēyarapariyaṇō gammanti attaṇō bhāgadhēyāṇi,nivvaḍaï niccapacchannō purisayārō. ṇā'ṇalamasaṁpattassa kālāgarussa savvahā gandhōvaladdhī havaï. na cirakālaṭhāiṇī ya ēsā āvaya tti lakkhaṇāō avagacchāmi tti. annaṁ ca-bhavaō vihavō vya sāhāraṇō cēva mē ēsa khaṇametta pīḍāgarō parikilēsō. paricattasavvasaṅgō ya saṁpayamaha. tā kiṁ tē uvagarēmi? tahā vi geṇhāhi ēyaṁ paḍhiyamētasiddha takkhayāhidahassa vi pāṇadhārayaṁ bhayavayā viṇayāṇandaṇēṇa paṇīyaṁ gāruḍamantaṁ ti. bhavissaï ya imiṇā vi bhavaō savihavēṇa viya paramatthasaṁpāyaṇaṁ ti.

dhaṇēṇa cintiyaṁ — ahō sē akāraṇavacchalattaṇaṁ. ahayā duhiyasattavacchalō cēva muṇijaṇō hōi. u(a)viyākaōvayārō ya kahamaha mimassa santiyaṁ geṇhāmi tti cintiūṇa bhaṇiyaṁ ca tēṇaṁ-bhayavaṁ, aṇuggihīō mhi mama kusalacintaṇaṁ cēva bhayavaō uvayārō. na tavassijaṇāṇuggihīō akallāṇaṁ pāvaï. pamāiṇō ya gihatyā havanti, uggāō ya mantadēvayāō. tā alaṁ mē mantēṇa. mahēsaradattēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — sōmadēvaō nippaccavāō kkhu ēsō. dhaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — tahā vi alamimēṇaṁ ti. mahēsaradattēṇa cintiyaṁ ahō mahāṇubhāvayā satthavāhaputtassa. nūṇamahamaṇēṇa na paccabhinnāō, taō akaōvayārittaṇēṇa uvarōhasīlayāē na ēyaṁ geṇhaï. tā payāsēmi sē appāṇayaṁ. cintiūṇaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ ca tēṇa-satthavāhaputta, sumarēhi maṁ tāmalittīē jūyayaravaïyaravimōiyaṁ mahēsaradattaṁ. tā alamanahā viyappiēṇaṁ. geṇhāhi ēyaṁ,annahā mahaī mē pīḍā samuppajjaï tti. taō sumariūṇa vuttantaṁ sē kayatthō ēsō tti cinti ūṇa hacaï mahaī ēyassa pīḍa tti ayacchiya taduvarōhamīruṇā bhaṇiya dhaṇēṇaṁ-bhayavaṁ, jaṁ tubbhē āṇavēha. tō dinnō mahēsarada tēṇa mantō, gahiō dhaṇēṇaṁ. gayā tabōvaṇaṁ. phaṇasādīēhiṁ kayā pāṇavittī. ṭhiō ēgadivasaṁ. ahivandiūga mahēsaradattaṁ pēsiō ya tēṇaṁ payaṭṭō visayasaṁmuhaṁ. nāraṅgāisaṁpāiyāhārō ya payattagōviyarayaṇāvalī kālakamēga pattō sāvatthi ti. tīē ya nayarīē tīē cēva rayaṇīē rāiṇō viyāradhavalassa takarahiṁ muṭṭhuṁ bhaṇḍāyāraṁ. tannimittaṁ gheppanti bhuyaṅgappāyā nayavāsiṇō annē ya kappaḍiyādaō tti. nijanti mantipuraō muñcanti ya parikkhiuṁ. taō sō dhaṇō ēyamāyaṇṇiūṇa duvāraō cēva annaō gacchamāṇō gahiō niuttapurisēhiṁ, bhaṇiō ya bhadda, kaō tuma ti? tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — susammanayarāō. tēhiṁ bhaṇiyaṁ — kahiṁ vaccihisi? tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — aggō gō āsi, saṁpayaṁ taṁ cēva vaccihāmi tti. tēhi bhaṇiyaṁ — bhadda, na tara kuppiyavvaṁ ti; ajja khu rāiṇō viyāradhavalassa kēhici muṭṭhuṁ bhaṇḍāyāraṁ. tanimittaṁ ca kappaḍiyā tumbhēhiṁ āṇēyavva ti niuttā amhē. tā ēhi, vaccāmō mantigēhaṁ ti. dhaṇēṇa bhaṇiya-bhadda, ahamiyāṇi cē vēhāgaō, nāhaṁ ēyakammayārī. tā kiṁ tahiṁ gaēṇaṁ. tēhiṁ bhaṇiya-niddēsagāriṇō amhē, tā avassaṁ gantavvaṁ ti. aṇicchamāṇō vi hiyaēṇa nīō mantigēhaṁ, daṁsiō mantissa, bhaṇiō ya tēṇaṁ— bhadda kaō tuma ? tēṇaṁ taṁ cēva siḍhē ti. mantiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ — kiṁ tē pāhēyamannaṁ vā? tō tēṇa lōhaannāṇamōhiyamaṇēṇaṁ aviyāriūṇaṁ āyaī bhaṇiyaṁ nidhiyappēṇaṁ na kiṁci saṁsaṇijja ti. mantiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ phuḍaṁ mantejjāsi. tēṇa bhaṇiya-kiṁ bhavō vi annahā nivēīyaï tti. mantiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ — jaï ēvaṁ, tā gaccha. taō gacchamāṇō tatthēva bhavaṇaṅgaṇē kahiṁci pamāyachuḍiēṇa gahiō vendurāpavaṅgamēṇa. phāliyaṁ sē nivasaṇaṁ. etthantaraṁmi tamuddēsamujjōyayantī sattarisimālā viya nivaḍiyā uḍigāō tēlokkasārā rayaṇāvali tti. divā mantiṇā, mōyāviyō pavaṅgamāō, gahiyā rayaṇāvalī paccabhinnāyā ya. bhinna mantihiyayaṁ. nr̥ṇaṁ akusalaṁ rāyadhūyāē, annahā kuō iyaṁ ēyassa? pucchiō khu ēsō. bhadda, kuō tuha ēsā? taō salajja bhaṇiyaṁ dhaṇēṇa-kayāvi ahaṁ khu jāṇavattēṇa mahākaḍāī gayō āsi. tattha maē ēsā kīyā. vivannaṁ ca mē āgacchamāṇassataṁ jāṇavattaṁ. tō ēdahamettaritthasāmī bhayavayā devvēṇa saṁpā iō mhi. mantiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ — kayā kīya tti? dhaṇēṇa-bhaṇiyaṁ atthi vāsamettaṁ. mantiṇā cintiyaṁ. timāsamettō kālō ēyāē viināē, dumāsamettō ya kālō rāyadhūyāē iō gayāē, ēsō ya ēvaṁ jaṁpaï ti, tā kahamēyaṁ? avalattā ya ēsā ēraṇāsi, asaṁbaddha palāvī khu ēsō, dēvassa nivēēmi. nivēiyaṁ mantiṇā. āulīhūō rāyā. nirūviyā rayaṇāvalī. hakkāriūṇa daṁsiyā bhaṇḍagāri gāṇaṁ, pañcabhinnāyā ya tēhiṁ. taō rāiṇā cintiyaṁ-cāvāiyā muṭṭhā vāṇēṇa mē dhūyā, annahā kahamēva mēyaṁ jujjaï. kōhābhibhūē ṇāvi accantanayāṇusāriṇā puṇō vi pucchāviō tti. dhaṇēṇaṁ puṇō vitaṁ cēva sāhiyaṁ. taō rāiṇā puṇō vi rayaṇāvaliṁ niēūṇa tti. kō paccabhinnāṇēṇa ahiyayaraṁ kuviēṇa na ēyamanahā havaï tti vajjhō samāṇattō. taō ya taṇamasivilittagattō vajantavirasaḍiṇḍimō avarāhathāvaṇatthaṁ ca paḍaligānimiyarayaṇāvalī payaṭṭāviō vajjhathāmaṁ. taō nīyamāṇassa haṭṭamaggāvasēsē maṁsāhilāsiṇā ōlā vaēṇa maṁsamēyaṁ ti kaliūṇa avahariyā rayaṇāvalī, nīyā sanīḍaṁ. dhaṇō vi ya ahiyayaraṁ kuvirahiṁ rāyapurisēhiṁ nīō masāṇaṁ ti. taṁ ca kērisaṁ?

sukkapāyabasāhānilīṇavāyasaṁ vāyasarasantakarayararavaṁ vantasivānāyabhīsaṇaṁ bhīsaṇadaradaḍḍamaḍayadurahigandhaṁ gandhavasāluddharuruventa sāṇaṁ sāṇakaṅkālanivahabhāsuraṁ bhāsurakavvāyapīijaṇayaṁ ti. avi ya—

puraō patthiyadaṇḍō uggāhiyakālacakkaduvvārō

kalikālavanhisarisō kālō vi jahiṁ chalijjējā

tattha vōlāviō lōhiyāmuhābhihāṇaṁ pāṇavāḍayāsannakhaṇḍaṁ. taō vahagacaṇḍālassa ādēsaṁ dāūṇa gayā rāyapurisā. nīśrō thēvaṁ bhūmibhāyaṁ caṇḍālēṇa, pulaïō pacchā, cintiyaṁ ca tēṇaṁ-ahō imāē āgitīē kahamakajjayārī bhavissaï? ahavā nidēsayārī ahaṁ, tā ki mēma ēiṇā. sayaṁ niōyamaṇuciṭṭhāmi. nivēsāvitrō jamagaṇḍīē, bhaṇiō ya-aja, sudilu jīvalōyaṁ karēhi, ēvama vasāṇō ya tē ēsa lōō. annaṁ ca-vayaṁsagāṇē sāvagā, tassaṁsaggiyō ya gantakūradidviṇō amhē. rāyasāsaṇaṁ cimaṁ avassaṁ saṁpāḍē yavvaṁ. vinnattō ya amhēhiṁ naravaī. jahā vāvāijamāṇassa muhapariṇāmō maraü tti muhuttamettaṁ amhēhiṁ samīhiyatthasaṁpāḍaṇaṁ kāyadhvaṁ ti. kaō ya ṇē pasāō rāiṇā. tā āṇavēu ajjō, kiṁ tē saṁpāḍīyaï? dhaṇēṇa cintiyaṁ-ahō visiṭṭaṇa caṇḍālassa. ahavā dīṇasattavacchalō parōvayāraniraō aṇuyampāraī na ēsa kammacaṇḍālō, kiṁ tu jāicaṇḍālō. sajjaṇō khu ēsō. akālē ya mē daṁsaṇaṁ ētēṇa saha jāyaṁ ti. ahavā kiṁ ēiṇā, gaō mē kālō purisaceṭṭiyassa; na saṁpajjaï samīhiyaṁ appapuṇṇāṇaṁ ti dīhaṁ nīsasiūṇa bhaṇiyaṁ saviliēṇaṁ. bhadda, saṁpāḍēhi rāyasāsaṇaṁ, kimannēṇaṁ ti. tō adīṇabhāvapisuṇiyamahāpurisabhāvō aō cēva aṇavarāhō vi ēsō maē vāvāiyavvō tti visaṇṇēna bāhaja labhariyalōyaṇēṇaṁ sagaggayaṁ bhaṇiō caṇḍālēṇa-ajja, jaï ēvaṁ, tā sumarēhi iṭṭhadēvayaṁ,pariccaya visayarāyaṁ, aṅgīkarēhi dhamma, tahā ṭhāhi saggāhimuhaṁ ti. tō dhiratthu jīvalōyassa, na saṁpāḍiō paratthō ti cintiūṇa ṭhiō saggāhimuhaṁ. gahiyaṁ caṇḍālēṇa kayantanīhāyarālabhāsuraṁ karavālaṁ, nikaḍḍiyaṁ paḍiyārāō, vāhiyaṁ īsi niyabhuyāsiharē. bhaṇiyaṁ ca tēṇaṁ-ahō jaṇā, imiṇā kila kahaṁvi rāyadhūyaṁ vaściūṇa avahaḍā tēlōkasārā rayaṇāvalī. imiṇā avarāhēṇa ēsa vāvāijjaï, tā jaï annō vi kōi rāyaviruddhamāsēvaïssaï taṁ pi rāyā sutikkhēṇa deṇḍēṇa ēvaṁ cēva sāsaïssaï tti bhaṇiūṇa vāhiyaṁ karavālaṁ. kāruṇṇamunna bhāvayāē ya adāūṇa pahāraṁ vimukkakhaggō nivaḍiō dharaṇīē caṇḍālō. bhaṇiō dhaṇēṇa-bhadda, mā mē imiṇā aïsaṁbhamēṇa hiyayaṁ pīḍēhi. aṇuciṭṭāhi rāyasāsaṇaṁ, niōgakārī tumaṁ ti. caṇḍālēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — ajja, na sakkuṇōmi asaṁpāḍiōvayārantarassa pahariu. tā ki tē piyayaraṁ saṁpāḍēmi tti āṇavēu ajjō.

etthantaraṁmi rāiṇō padamaputtō sumaṅgalō nāma, sō ujjāṇamuvagō ahiṇā daṭṭhō. uggayāē visassa thēvavēlāē cēva paṇa?sannō jāō. āṇīō naravaïsamīvaṁ. sadāviyā gāruḍiyā, āgayā ya turiyaturiyaṁ. diṭṭhō tēhiṁ. ahō paṇaṭṭhā sē sanna ti visaṇṇā khu ēē. paüttāī mantōsahāī, na jāō sē visēsō. visaṇṇō rāyā. cintiyaṁ ca tēṇaṁ-acintāō purisasattīō. kayāi annō vi kōi susiddhagāruḍamantō narindō jīvāvēi ti. tō ghōsāvēmi tāva samantaō paḍahagēhiṁ. jahā-ahō ajja cēva etya rāyaputtō [sumaṅgalō nāmaṁ sō ujjāṇamuvagaō] ahiṇā daṭṭhō. jō taṁ jīvāvēi, sō jaṁ cēva patthaē taṁ cēva dijjaï ti cintiūṇa ādivā pāḍahigā payaṭṭā nayarārāmadēulasahāimaggēhi.

etthantaraṁmi āgaō ēgō pāḍa higō tamuddēsaṁ. āyaṇṇiō sē sadō dhaṇēṇa jahā-ahiṇā daṭṭhō rāyaputtō; jō taṁ jīvāvēi, sō jaṁ cēva patthēi taṁ cēva dijjaï ti. taō sahari sēṇa bhaṇiō caṇḍālō. bhadda, jaï tē nibbandhō, tā ēvaṁ saṁpāḍēhi. jīvāvēmi tāva ēyaṁ bhuyaṅgadaha, pacchā mārejjāsi tti. harisiō caṇḍālō. cintiyaṁ ca tēṇa-jō mē sāmisuyaṁ sayalanarindapaccakkhāyaṁ pi jīvāva issaï, taṁ kahaṁ dakkhiṇṇamahōyahī guṇēgantapakkhavāī mahārāō vāvāissaï?. tā jīviō khu ēsō, kahaṁ vā ēsa ēvaṁ vivajjaïssaï tti cintaūṇa tēṇa sadiō pāḍahiō. sāhiō ya vuttantō rāyapurisassa. tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — bhadda,kimettha saccaya,jaṁ ēsa jaṁpaï? dhaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — atthi tāva mama pannagavisāvahārī mantō. kajjasiddhīē u dēvō pamāṇaṁ. avisaō khu ēsō purisayārassa. tahāvi pecchāmi tāva tti. rāyapurisēṇa cintiyaṁ-ahō sē avasthāṇagaruō ālāvō aṇuddhaō ya. tā avamsaṁ jīvāvēi ēsa rāyaputtaṁ ti. mōyā viūṇa nīō naravaïsamīvaṁ, daṁsiō rāiṇō, sāhiō vuttantō. taō taṁ dadṇa cintiyamaṇēṇa-mahāṇubhāvāgiī khu ēsō. tā kahaṁ paradavvāvahāraṁ karissaï? ahavā puṇō vigappissāmi, na ēsa biyāraṇāē samō; visamā gatī visassa, mā accāhiyaṁ mē bhavissaï puttayassa ti cintiūṇa bāhajalabharivanayaṇēṇaṁ īsiparikkhalantavaïyaṇa bhaṇiyō khu tēṇaṁ rāiṇā. bhadda, jīvāvēhi mē suyaṁ ti. taō dhaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — dēva, muśca visāya, peccha bhayavaō mantassa sāmatthaṁ ti bhaṇiūṇa sumarimō mantō. acinta sāmatthaō ya tassa viyambhantavayaṇakamalō pasuttō vva suhanidākhaē uḍiō kumārō.

etthantaraṁbhi samuddhāiō sāhuvāyakalayalō. parituṭṭhō rāyā, harisavisēsaō aṇuciyaṁ pi thēvayāē khittaṁ dhaṇassa kaḍisuttayaṁ. varisiyaṁ ca dēvīhiṁ āharaṇavarikha. dhaṇēṇa bhaṇiya-mahārīya, kimaṇēṇaṁ. rāīṇā bhaṇiyaṁ — bhaī, bhaṇē, kiṁ tē avaraṁ saṁpāḍīyaü 1. dhaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — dēva, alamaṇēṇa. imaṁ puṇa saṁpāḍēu dēvō tassa vahaniōgakāriṇō acaṇḍālabhāvassa caṇḍālābhihāṇassa samīhiyaṁ maṇōrahaṁ ti. rāiṇā cintiyaṁ-ahō sē garuyayā. na īisō visuddhasattajuttō akajjaṁ samāyaraï. tā kō uṇa ēsō? pucchāmi ēyaṁ. ahavā saṁpāḍēmi tāva ēyassa samīhiyaṁ, puṇō pucchissaṁ ti cintiūṇa bhaṇiyaṁ rāhaṇā-sadāvēha caṇḍālaṁ, pucchaha ya, kō sē maṇō rahō? taō gaō paḍihārō, pucchiō ya tēṇa. arē khagilaya, parituṭṭhō tē rāyā, ahabā rāyaputtajīviyadāyagō narindacūḍāmaṇī; tā bhaṇa, kiṁ tē karīyaü tti? taō khaṅgilēṇa cintiyaṁ-natthi agyō sajjaṇacariyassa, na yā'visaō mahāṇubhāvayāē tti cintiūṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — bhadda, avi mukkō sō dēvēṇaṁ narindacūḍāmaṇī? tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — arē khaṅgilaya, kō etya saṁdēhō? kayannusēharayabhūō dēvō, tā bhaṇa samīhiyaṁ. tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — jaï ēvaṁ, tā karēu dēvō pasāyaṁ; alaṁ amhāṇaṁ imīē buhajaṇagarahaṇijjāē ubhayalōyaviruddhāē jīvigāē tti. paḍihārēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — arē davvajāyaṁ patthēhi, ki imēṇaṁ. khaṅgilēṇa bhaṇiya-aō vi abaraṁ davvajāyaṁ ti? taō paḍisōūṇa nivēiyaṁ paḍihārēṇa rāiṇō. bhaṇiyaṁ ca rāiṇā-ahō sē vivēgō alobhayā ya. dhaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — dēva, jāimettacaṇḍālō khu ēsō mahāṇubhāvō; tā karēu ēyassa vavasiyaṁ dēvō tti. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ — bhadda, vataṁ cēva ēvaṁ; imaṁ puṇa sē avaraṁ, dēu bhaddō sahatthēṇa ēyassa dīṇāralakkhaṁ caṇḍālakuḍumbasahassavāsiṇi vijhavāsiṇi ca paṭṭaṇassa avarabāhiriyaṁ ti. taō dhaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ jaṁ dēvō bhaṇaï tti. paḍivajiūṇa saṁpāḍiyaṁ rāyasāsaṇaṁ ti. tuṭṭhō khaṅgilagō na tahā vittalāhēṇa jahā dhaṇajīviēṇa.

tō dhaṇamuvacariūṇa bhaṇiyaṁ rāiṇā. bhadda, vavasāyāō cēva avagaō tē mukulajammō. tā kinnivāsiṇaṁ kināmadhēyaṁ vā bhavantamavagacchāmi? taō parasantiyā rayaṇāvalī, tahāvi gahiyā, ahō mē sukulajammō tti sariūṇa vimukkadīhanīsāsaṁ lajjāvaṇa yavayaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ dhaṇēṇaṁ. dēva, kōisō ajhajjayāriṇōṁ vavasāō, kō vā etya dōsō sukulassa? kiṁ na saṁbhavanti lacchinila ēsu kamalēsu kimaō? vāṇiyō ahahaṁ jāimettēṇa, na uṇa sīlēṇaṁ, susammanayaravāsī dhaṇābhihāṇō ya. taō rāiṇā ahō mē dhanayā, jaṁ na ēyaṁ purisarayaṇaṁ viṇāsiyaṁ ti cintiūṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. kahaṁ taējārisā akajayāriṇō havanti? tā kahēhi paramatthaṁ, kahaṁ tumaē ēmā rayaṇāvalī pāviya tti?

etthantarami ya sasaṁbhamamuvasappiūṇa vinattaṁ mahāpaḍihārīē. dēva, ēsā khu maṇōramābhihāṇā ujjāṇavāliyā rāyadhūyāvayaṇāō vahaṇabhaṅgēṇa viuttapariyaṇā dēvaṁ vinavēi. jahā-dēva, iō gacchantāṇaṁ amhāṇaṁ samuddamajjhami takkhaṇā cēva caṇḍamāruyapaṇolliyaṁ itthiyāhiyaē vva gujjhaṁ phuḍhē jāṇavattaṁ ti. taō ya dēvassa pahāvēṇaṁ tahāvihaphalagalāmasaṁpāiyapāṇavittī jīviyā rāyadhūyā viṇayavaī. saṁpattā ya kahaṁci niyabhāyadhēēhi nayarisamīvaṁ. mēhavaṇasaṁṭhiyāē pēsiyā ahaṁ, jahā vinavēhi ēyaṁ vuttantaṁ tāyassa. ēyaṁ suṇiūṇa dēvō pamāṇaṁ ti. taō sasaṁbhantō imīē cēva rayaṇāvalīvuttantamuvalabhissaṁ ti uḍhiō rāyā, payaṭṭō ya mēhavaṇaṁ, pattō ya mahayā caḍa garēṇaṁ. diṭṭhā ya rāyadhūyā. alaṁkārēūna ya pavēsiyā sāvatthiṁ. pucchiyā ya rayaṇāvalīvuttantaṁ. sāhiō ya tīē. jahā-tami vahaṇabhaṅgadiyahē cūyalaīyāē samappiyā saṁgōviyā ya tīē uttarīyavandhaṇēṇa. taō ya vivannē jāṇavattē kāyantavasaviuttē ya pariyaṇē na yāṇāmi kīisō sē vipariṇāmō ti. taō rāiṇā dhaṇamavalōiuṇa bhaṇiya-bhadda, kahaṁ tuha ēsā hatthagōyaraṁ gaya tti? dhaṇēṇa bhaṇiya-dēva, samuddatīrē saṁyaṁ gahaṇēṇaṁ ti. rāiṇā cintiyaṁ-vivannā cūyalaïyā, kahamanahā sayaṁ gahaṇaṁ ti. bhaṇiyaṁ ca-mada, avi dilu taē tattha kiṁci kaṅkālapāyaṁ ti. dhaṇēṇa bhaṇiya-dēva,didvaṁ; aō cēva paradavvāvahārēṇa akajjakāriṇamappāṇaṁ mannēmi tti. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ — na ērisaṁ paradabāvaharaṇaṁ gihiṇō; tā alamaīyavatthucintaṇēṇaṁ. bhaṇa, kiṁ tē karēmi tti? dhaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — kayaṁ dēvēṇa kara ṇijja, jaṁ tassa niōgakāriṇō samīhiyabhahiyamaṇōrahāpūraṇaṁ ti. rāiṇā bhaṇiya — bhadda, kiṁ tēṇaḥ thēvaṁ khu taṁ tassa vi samikkhi yakāriṇō ceṭṭhiyassa, kimaṅga puṇa bhavaō jīviyabbhahiyasuyajīviyadāyagassa. dhaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — dēvadaṁsaṇāō vi aparaṁ karaṇijja ti? dēva, saṁpuṇṇā mē maṇōrahā dēvadaṁsaṇēṇaṁ ti. taō rāiṇā dāūṇamaṇagdhēyaṁ niyamāharaṇaṁ viiṇṇapaccaïyanarasahāō pēsiō susa mmanayaraṁ. tō āpucchiūṇa naravaī niggaō saha rāyapurisēhi dhaṇō.

pattō ya kaïvayadiyahēhiṁ girithalayaṁ nāma paṭṭaṇaṁ. tattha vi ya taṁmi cēya diyahē rāiṇō caṇḍasēṇassa muṭṭhuṁ sabdasāraṁ nāma bhaṇḍā gārabhavaṇaṁ. taō āulīhūyā nāyarayā nagarārakkhiyā ya. gavēsijanti cōrā, muddijjanti bhavaṇavīhīō, parikkhijanti āgantugā.

etthantaraṁmi ya saṁpattamettā cēva gahiyā imē rāyapurisēhiṁ, bhaṇiyā ya tēhiṁ. bhaddā, na tubbhēhiṁ kuppiyavvaṁ. sāhiō vuttantō. tēhiṁ bhaṇiyaṁ—kō ēsa abasarō kōvassa ? tēhiṁ vaccāmō jattha tubbhē nēha tti. nīyā pañcaülasamīvaṁ, pucchiyā paścaüliēhiṁ kaō tumbhē tti? tēhiṁ bhaṇiyaṁ — sāvatthīō . kāraṇiēhiṁ bhaṇiyaṁ — kahiṁ gamissaha tti? tēhiṁ bhaṇiyaṁ — susammanayaraṁ. kāraṇiēhiṁ bhaṇiyaṁ kiṁnimittaṁ ti? tēhiṁ bhaṇiyaṁ — naravaïsamāēsāō ēyaṁ satyavāhaputtaṁ geṇhium̐ ti. kāraṇiēhiṁ bhaṇiyaṁ — atthi tumhāṇaṁ kiṁci davi ṇajāyaṁ? tēhi bhaṇiyaṁ — atthi. kāraṇiēhi bhaṇiyaṁ kiṁ tayaṁti? tēhiṁ bhaṇiyaṁ — imasta satthavāhaputtassa naravaï viiṇṇaṁ rāyālaṁkaraṇayaṁ ti. kāraṇiēhi bhaṇiyaṁ — pecchāmō tāva kērisaṁ?. taō visuddhacittayāē dasiyaṁ. paccabhinnāyaṁ bhaṇḍāriēṇa. bhaṇiyaṁ ca tēṇa-ēyaṁ pi dēvasantiyaṁ cēya kālantarāvahariyaṁ rāyālaṁkaraṇayaṁ ti. taō saṁkhuddhā tē purisā pucchiyā ya pañcaülēṇa. bhadā, avitahaṁ kahēha, kī tumhāṇamēyaṁ? tēhiṁ bhaṇiyaṁ — kimanahā tumhāṇaṁ nivēīyaï? tī kāragiēhiṁ nivēiō ēsa vuttantō caṇḍasēṇassa. sō cēva mē rāyā savvamēyaṁ kāra vēi tti kuviō ēsō. nēyāviyā imē cārayaṁ; pāviyabyō ērasiṁ sayāsāō savvō atthō tti dharāviyā payattēṇa.

tahiṁ ca paramaduksiyā jā: kaïyayadiyahē parivasanti, tāva tatthēva rāyapurisēhiṁ parivāyagarūvadhārī rayaṇīē paribhamantō saritthō cēva gahiō mahābhuyaṅgō tti. nīlō mantisamīvaṁ. tēṇa vi ya liṅgadhārī cōriyaṁ karēi tti, natthi sē an pi aka raṇijjaṁ ti kaliūṇa vajjhō samāṇatō.

rāyapurisēhi taṇamasigēruyabhūī vilittasavvaṅgō

kōsiyamālābhūsiyasirōharō vigayavasaṇō ya

nihiuttamaṅgakaṇavīradāmalambantabhāsurālōō

chittarakayāyavattō unbhaḍasiyarāsahārūḍhō

ḍiṇḍimayasabamēliyabahujaṇaparivāriō va sō navaraṁ

dakṣiṇadisāē nīō bhīmaṁ aha vajjhathāṇaṁ ti

nīsasiūga sudīhaṁ savilayamaha pecchiūṇa ya jaṇōhaṁ

paricintiyaṁ ca tēṇaṁ kahamaliyaṁ hōi muṇivayaṇaṁ

eṇhiṁ pi majjha juttaṁ gahiyaṁ jaṁ jassa santiyaṁ ritthaṁ

sāhēmi tayaṁ savvaṁ dharaṇigayaṁ tassa kiṁ tēṇaṁ

iya cintiūṇa bhaṇiyā tēṇaṁ naraṇāhasantiyā purisā

mōtūṇa mēṁ na muṭṭhuṁ thāṇamiṇaṁ kēṇaï niruttaṁ

savvaṁ ca tayaṁ davvaṁ ciṭṭhaï etthēva navara thāṇami

ārāmasunnadēulagirinaditīrē dharaṇigayaṁ

ghettūṇa ya taṁ tubbhē appēha jaṇassa jassa jaṁ taṇayaṁ

siṭṭhuṁ maē sacihaṁ pacchā mārējaha mamaṁ ti

siṭṭhuṁ ca taō sabbaṁ sapaccayaṁ jaṁ jaō jayā gahiyaṁ

ciṭṭaï ya jatya dēulagirinaditīrāisu tahēva

gantūṇa tēhi vi taō siṭṭhamamaccassa savvamēyaṁ tu

jōyāviyaṁ ca tēṇa vi paccaïyanarēhi taṁ davvaṁ

diḍaṁ ca niravasēsaṁ siṭṭha jaṁ jami jaṁmi thāṇami

pucagahiēṇa rahiyaṁ rāyālaṁkāradavvēṇaṁ

daṭhṭhaṇa ya taṁ dadhvaṁ cintā mantissa navaramuppannā

puvagahiēhi pattaṁ taṁ davaṁ annahā kahavi

ēvaṁ cintiūṇaṁ sō parivāyagarūvadhārī bhuyaṅgō

karuṇāpavannēṇa mantiṇā sadāviūṇa saviṇayaṁ bhaṇiō ti

vēsasahāvaviruddhaṇa tujjha cariēṇa vimhaō majjha

sāhēhi tā phuḍatthaṁ kimēyamavaropparaviruddhaṁ

ēvaṁ ca bhaṇiyamettēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ parivvāyaēṇa. natthi khalu visayaluddhāṇamavaropparaviruddhaṁ ti. avi ya—

jaṇaṇijaṇayāṇa mukayaṁ na gaṇenti na bandhumittasāmīṇaṁ

visayavisamōhiyamaṇā purisā paralōgamaggaṁ ca

ēvaṁ ca siṭṭhamettē bhaṇiyamamaccēṇa jujjaē ēyaṁ

vinnāṇadaridāṇaṁ na uṇō tumaē saricchāṇaṁ

tā sāhēhi avitahaṁ paradhaṇagahaṇasta kāraṇaṁ majjha. sayalāṇuvālaṇassa ya hiriyaṁ mottūṇa kiṁ bahuṇā.

ēvaṁ ca bhaṇiē bhaṇiyaṁ parivāyaēṇa.

nimuṇasu avahiyamaṇasō vuttan majjha pucchiō jō tē

taha sāhēmi phuḍatthaṁ jaha kahiyaṁ ōhināṇēṇaṁ

atthi ihēba bharahaṁmi puṇḍō nāma jaṇavaō. taṁmi amarāvaïsarisaṁ puṇḍavaddhaṇaṁ nāma nayaraṁ. tattha aggivēsāyaṇasagottō sōmadēvō nāma māhaṇō. tassa suō nārāyaṇābhihāṇō ahaṁ ti. tami nayarē jīvadhāraṇa saggō tti kusatthaṁ parūventō ciṭṭhāmi jāva kēi purisā samantaō vuṇṇavayaṇataralacchaṁ palōēmāṇā cōra tti kaliūṇa vajjhā nijjanti. tē ya daḷuṇa bhaṇiyaṁ maē ghāēha ēē mahā bhuyaṅgē tti. taō taṁ mama vayaṇaṁ sōūṇa ekkēṇa sāhuṇā samuppannōhināṇēṇa nāidūreṭṭhiēṇēva jaṁpiyamahō kaṭṭhamannāṇaṁ ti. taṁ ca mē sāhu vayaṇaṁ sōūga samuppanā cintā. kimēēṇa maṁ uddisiūṇa pasantarūvēṇāvi ēyaṁ jaṁpiyaṁ ti. taō sō maē calaṇēsu nivaḍiūṇa pucchiō bhayavaṁ, kimannāṇaṁ ti. tēṇa kahiyaṁ-savvasattāṇamasantādiōyadāṇaṁ viruddhōvaēsō ya. maē bhaṇiyaṁ — kō asantāhiō ō, kō vā viruddhōvaēsō ti? sāhuṇā bhaṇiyaṁ — jamēē puyakayakammapariṇaïvasēṇa vasaṇapattē niravarāhē vi mahābhuyaṅgē ti ahi lavasi, ēsa asantāhiōō; jaō saccaṁ pi parapīḍākaraṁ na vattavaṁ ti. ēsā ya vō mutī païyapaïyābhihāṇē cōracōrabhaṇaṇē ya tattulladōsayā, saībhūyā[ē] vi sayāsuddhasahāvā[ē] vi asaïpayābhihāṇē acōracōrabhaṇaṇēṇa ya micchāmihāṇāō duguṇō dōsō tti. jaṁ puṇa jīvadhāraṇa saggō tti parūvēsi ēsa viruddhōvaēsō; jō na jīvadhāō paralōē muhaphalaō hōi. bhaṇiyaṁ ca saya lēhi titthanāyagēhiṁ. na hiṁsiyavvāṇi savvabhūyāṇi. ahavā—

jammantaradinnasya ya phalasēsamihēva pāvihisi jammē

thēvadiyahēhi bālaya navaramasantāhiōgassa

maē bhaṇiyaṁ — bhayavaṁ, kērisō jammantaraviiṇṇō asantāhiōgō, kērisaṁvā tassa phalamaṇuhūyaṁ maē, kērisaṁ vā phalasēsaṁ ti?

sāhuṇā bhaṇiyaṁ — vaccha suṇa.

atthi ihēva bhārahē vāsē uttarāvahē visaē gajaṇayaṁ nāma paṭṭaṇaṁ. tattha āsāḍhō nāma māhaṇō. racchuyā sē bhāriyā. tāṇaṁ iō atīyapañcamabhavaṁmi caṇḍadēvābhihāṇō puttō tumaṁ āsi. kārāviō vēyajjhayaṇaṁ, suṇāviō satthāī āsāḍhēṇa. samuppannō tē vijā himāṇō. ṭhiō gajjaṇayasāmiṇō vīrasēṇassa samīvē, saṁpūiō tēṇa, viiṇṇa jīvaṇaṁ, bahu mannara rāyā. aïkkantō kōi kālō.

annayā ya taṁmi cēva nayarē parivāyagabhattā viṇīyasedvissa dhūyā bālavihavā vīramaī nāmaḥ sā ya avivēyabahulayāē ithiyāṇaṁ dujjayayāē mōhassa ahilasaṇīyayāē visayāṇaṁ viyārakulaharayāē jovvaṇassa aṇavekkhiūṇa niyakulaṁ aṇālōciūṇa āyaī tanna yarivatthavvagasīhalābhihāṇēṇa mālāgārēṇa samaṁ pavasiya tti. ibhō ya taṁmi cēva diyahē tīsē cēva pūyaṇijjō sasamayāyāraparivālaṇaraī jōgappā nāma parivyāyagō, sō nissaṅgayāē pavvaïyagāṇaṁ kajjābhāvēṇa ya saṁsiyavvassa aṇāikkhiūṇa kassaï thāṇēsaraṁ gaō ti. jāō ya lōyavāō ahō vīramaī pavasiya tti. vinayaṁ ca tumaē parivāyayagamaṇaṁ. tō asuyāē āsayassa vicittacariyayāē sattāṇaṁ samuppannā tē cintā. nūṇaṁ sā jōyappaṇā saha pavasiyā bhavissaï. anayā pavattā rāyakulē kahā, jahā viṇīyasē hissa dhūyā na yāṇijjaï kahiṁ pavasiya tti? taō taē ujjhiūṇa satthāyāraṁ avalambiūṇa iyarapurisamaggaṁ aṇavekkhiūṇa attaṇō lahuyayaṁ tti.

ayāṇiūṇa seṭṭhiummāhayaṁ ēvaṁ jaṁpiyaṁ ti. kimettha jāṇiyavvaṁ, ahaṁ jāṇāmi. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ — kaha ti? taē bhaṇiyaṁ — jōyappaṇā saddhiṁ pavasiya ni. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ — paricattaniyakalattārambhō khu sō bhagavaṁ. taē bhaṇiyaṁ — aō cēva parakalattāī patthēi. mahārāya, ēvaṁvihā cēva ēē pāsaṇḍiṇō. na ettha paramatthabuddhī kāyavva tti. ēyaṁ ca sōūṇa vipariṇayā dhammami kēi pāṇiṇō. savaṇaparaṁ parāē ya āyaṇṇiyamiṇaṁ sēsaparivāyaēhi vajjhō kō jōyappā, jāyā ya sē sapaksaparapakkhēhiṁ pāyaṁ viḍambaṇā. ēvaṁvihamicchā pariṇāmavattiṇā baddhaṁ taē tivvaṁ kammaṁ. aïkantō kōi kālō. parikkhīṇamahāuyaṁ. tō aparicattayāē ārambhassa māyābahula yāē sēsakālaṁ aṇāsēvaṇāē dhammassa vicittayāē kammapariṇaīṇaṁ maō samāṇō kollāgasannivēsē samuppannō ēlagattāē aïkkantō kōi kālō takkammadōsēṇa ya saḍiyā tē jīhā. gahiō mahāvēyaṇāē. thēvakālēṇaṁ cēva jhīṇaṁ ca tē āuyaṁ. taō mariūṇa takammasēsayāē kollāgasabhivēsāḍavīē cēva samuppannō gōmāugattāē ti. tattha vi ya takammapēriyatahāvihaphalabhavakha ṇēṇa saḍiyā tē jīhā. aïkantō kōi kālō. taō mariūṇa takkammasēsayāē cēva samuppannō sāēyanaravaïvilāsiṇīē mēyaṇa lē hābhihāṇāē suyattāē tti. pattō jodhaṇaṁ, ballahō naravaïssa. annayā takammadōsaō cēva surāpāṇamattēṇaṁ viṇāvi kajjēṇaṁ daḍhamakōsiyā rāyajaṇaṇī. suō rāya uttēṇa, vārāviō tēṇaṁ. taō taṁ pi akōsiuṁ payattō. kuviēṇa chindāviyā tē jīhā. vavagaō maō. lajiō khu attaṇō vuttantēṇaṁ. paḍivanō ya aṇasaṇaṁ. māsamettēṇa kālēṇa vimukkī pāṇēhiṁ. samuppannō ya ettha puṇḍavaddhaṇaṁmi māhaṇasuyattāē ti. ēyamaṇuhūyaṁ taē.

taō mamēyaṁ sōūṇa samuppannō saṁvēgō, jāō bhavavirāō. cintiyaṁ maē. ahō dukkhahē uttaṇaṁ pamāyacariyassa. pucchiō sāhū. bhayavaṁ, kērisaṁ phalasēsaṁ ti? tō tēṇa aïsayanāṇiṇā visēsēṇaṁ imaṁ avalōiūṇa bhaṇiyaṁ sakaruṇēṇaṁ. vaccha, avivēginaṇāṇurūvā sayalalōē viḍambaṇā sēsaṁ ti. taō maē samuṣpannavēraggēṇa muṇivayaṇabhīēṇa sugahiyanāmagurusamīvē pavanā pancajjā. aïkantō kōi kālō. laddhāō ya gurusuralōyagamaṇakālē maē gurusussūsāparēṇa gurusayāsāō tālugghāḍaṇigayaṇagāmiṇīō duvē mahāvijjāō.

bhaṇiō mhi guruṇā-vaccha! ēyāō dhammakāyaparivālaṇatthaṁ karhipi mahāvasaṇakālaṁmi cēva taē paüñjiyanāō, na uṇa sayā asāra visayasuhasāhaṇatyaṁ ti. annaṁ ca, ēyāō dhārayantēṇaṁ parihāsēṇāvi aliyaṁ na jaṁpiyavaṁ; pamāyaō jaṁpiē samāṇē takkhaṇaṁ cēva nāhippamāṇavimalajalagaēṇaṁ uddhabāhuṇā aṇimisalōyaṇēṇaṁ ēyāsiṁ cēva aṭṭhasahassēṇaṁ jāvō dāyavvō tti. taō maē pābamōhiyamaṇēṇaṁ sāhusihaniyaïvasavattiṇā avijāṇurāyaṇaḍiēṇaṁ guruvayaṇapaḍikūla ihaparalōgamangaviruddhaṁ savvamiyamaṇuciṭṭhiyaṁ. jaṁpiyaṁ ca maē kallaṁ asaṁpattāē bhayavaīē samjhāē āvasahāsanārāmabaülatalagaēṇaṁ pamāyaō taruṇarāmāyaṇapucchiēṇa aparihāsasīlēṇa vi parihāsēṇaṁ ubhayalōyaviruddhaṁ aliyavayaṇaṁ ti. mantiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ kiṁ jaṁpiyaṁ ti? pariyāyaēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — pucchiō mhi kallaṁ takkhaṇakayajalāva gāhaṇāhiṁ āvasahadēvayādasaṇatthamāgayāhiṁ mahuraparikkhalantatrayaṇāhiṁ savinbhantapecchirīhiṁ taruṇarāmāhiṁ. bhayavaṁ, kīsa tuma taruṇagō cēva jīvalōyasārabhūyaṁ jammantaraṁmi vi tavassijaṇapatthaṇijjaṁ hariharapiyāmahappamuhatiyasavara sē viyaṁ sayalalōyasalāhaṇijja visayasokkhaṁ ujjhiūṇa imaṁ īisaṁ dukaraṁ vayavisēsaṁ pavanō ti? taō maē tāsi hiyayagayaṁ parihāsagahiraṇaṁ bhāvaṁ viyāṇiūṇa vimukkadīhanīsāsaṁ kālāṇurūvamaliyaṁ cetra jaṁpiyaṁ. jahā hiyayāṇukūlapiyayamāvirahasaṁtāvapīḍiēṇaṁ imaṁ īisaṁ dukaraṁ vayamabbhuvagayaṁ ti. jaṁpiūṇa ya imaṁ vayaṇaṁ pamāyaō cēva na kaō gurujaṇōvaïṭṭō jāvō. akayajāvō ya vasaṇavasagō vi ya jāē aḍḍarattasamaē atthamiē bhuvaṇapadīpē candē pasuttē nāyaralōyanivahē timira dussaṁcarēsu rāyamaggēsu kahakahavi gantūṇa puvvabhaṇḍiyaṁ piva akayapaḍidu kārapihāṇaṁ paviṭṭhō sāgaraseṭṭhigēhaṁ ti. taō gahiyasuvaṇṇaruppabhaṇḍō niggacchantō cēva sāgarasē higēhāō āyaṇṇiyapurisapayasaṁcārō vijāṇusaraṇadināvahāṇō khaliyavijānahaṅgaṇagamagō sumariyavijjāvihaṅgadīṇabhāvō visamabhayavasapalāyamāṇō kuntakaravālavāvaḍagga hatthēhiṁ gaddabbhasadaravāvūriyadisāyakō hiṁ iō tō turiyamavadhāvantēhiṁ gahiyō rāyapurisēhiṁ. aō paramavagō cēva tē madīō vuttantō. saṁpaï tuma pamāṇaṁ ti bhaṇiūna tuhikkō ṭhiō parivyāyagō ti.

mantiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ — bhayavaṁ, kahaṁ puṇa ettha ēgadivasāvaṇīō rāyālaṁkārō natthi? tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — dinnō khu ēsō maē sāvatthī naravaïssa. mantiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ — kiṁ nimittaṁ ti? tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — suṇa.

atthi mē sāvatthīnivāsī gandhavvadattō nāma vayaṁsaō jīviyāō ya abbhahiō. tēṇa tanayaranigasiṇō indadattābhihāṇassa seṭṭhimahantagassa dhūyā vāsavadattā nāma kannagā nēhāṇurāyavasaō annadinnā vi patthuē vivāhamahū savē jōvaṇābhimāṇiṇā iharahā vi attaṇō viṇāsamālōciya avalambiūṇa purisayāraṁ avahariūṇa pariṇīya tti. ēyavaïyaraṁmi ruṭṭhō sē ra.yā. avahariyā vāsavadattā. nicchūḍhō nayarīō. āgaō yē samīyaṁ jīviyābhihāṇavayaṁsagasahāō. pucchiō ya āgamaṇapaōyaṇaṁ. sāhiyaṁ ca tēṇaṁ. taō maē tamaṇupucchiūṇa rāyālaṁkārakōsalliyasahāō pēsiō narindapañcāyaṇanimittaṁ jīviō. gaō ya sō sāvatthi. alaṁkāradarisaśa puvvayaṁ vinnattō tēṇa rāyā ēyavaïyarēṇa. kaō sē rāiṇā pasāyō. pēsiyā gandhavvadattasya sāvatthipavērāṇanimittaṁ mahantayā. nīō mahantapahiṁ, pavēsiō rāiṇā mahāvibhūīē, diṭṭhō ya jaṇaṇi jaṇayapamuhēṇa sayaṇabaggēṇa. pāviyā tēṇa kaṇṭhagayapāṇā vāsava dattā. tā ēyaṁ nimittaṁ.

mantiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ — sāhu vavasiya, mittakajjavacchalā cēva sappurisā havanti. nidōsā khu tē pubbagahiya tti mantiūṇa mōyā viyā dhaṇāī. bhayavaṁ, tumaē tri savivēgāṇurūvamāyariyavvaṁ ti bhaṇiūṇa visajjiō parivvāyaō. dhaṇō vi ya tē rāyapurisē pēsiūṇa sāvathi payaṭṭō jalanihitīrasaṁṭhiyaṁ vayarāḍaṁ nāma nayaraṁ. kahāṇayavisēsēṇa pattō paümāvaī nāma aḍaviṁ. tīē vi ya kaïvayakappaḍiyaparivāriyassa ēgami vibhāgē uṭṭhiyaṁ vaṇagaïndapīḍhaṁ. paṇahā disōdisaṁ kappaḍiyā. dhāiō gayakalahagō dhaṇamaggēṇaṁ. gahiō khu ēsō, pāḍiō dharaṇivaḍhē. pariṇō gayakalahagō. dēvajīēṇaṁ na vāvāiō dhaṇō. taō upari ghattiūṇa dantamusalēhiṁ paḍicchissa ti gahiō karēṇaṁ, vikkhittō ya uvariṁ vilaggō samāsamnavattiṇīē naggōhasālāē. iō ya tayannakalahagapīḍayāē rasiyaṁ karēṇuyāē. taō taṁ mottūṇa valiō gayakalahagō. ārūḍhō dhaṇō naggōhasiharaṁ. diṭṭhā ya tēṇa tattha nīḍaṁmi ōlāvagavimukkā tellokkasārā rayaṇāvalī. pañcabhinnāyā gahiyā ya. cintiyaṁ ca tēṇaṁ. chuṭṭāmi jaï gaōvaddavassa, tā parāṇēmi ēyaṁ paramōvayāriṇō sāvatthīnaravaïssa; pacchā jahāsamīhiyamaṇucihissaṁ ti. ṭhiō kaṁci vēlaṁ, aïkkantaṁ gayapīḍhaṁ, ōiṇṇō taruvarāō, payaṭṭō sāvatthi, saṁpattō vasimaṁ.

iō ya gayā tē purisā sāvatthi. nivēiō vuttantō naravaïssa. kuvibhō tēsiṁ rāyā. ahō abuddhiyā tumhē, jaṁ tahāvihaṁ purisarayaṇaṁ tahā ēgāgiṇaṁ mottaṇamāgaya ti. tā ēsa bhē daṇḍō; taṁ cēva agihiūṇa na tumbhēhiṁ sāvatthi païsiyavvaṁ ti. bhaṇiūṇa nicchūḍhā nayarīō. laggā dhaṇaṁ gavēsiuṁ. diṭṭhō ya tē hiṁ piya mēlagābhihāṇē sannivēsē satyavāhaputtō. sāhiō ṇēhi vuttantō imassa, imēṇa vi ya tēsiṁ. taō kaïvayadiyahē hiṁ pattō sāvatthi. diṭṭhō naravaī, parituṭṭō hiyaēṇa, sāhiō vuttantō naravaïssa. dēva, imiṇā payārēṇa laddhā rayaṇāvalī dasiyā ya. vimhiō rāyā. ahō vicittayā kajjapariṇaīṇa ti cintiūṇa bhaṇiyaṁ ca tēṇa—

bhadda, tuha cēva maē ēsā saṁpāḍiya tti, na kāyayō mē paṇayabhaṅgō. ahavā sāhāraṇaṁ cēva tē ēyaṁ rajja pi, kiṁ saṁpāḍīyaï tti? taō aïkkantēsu kaïvayadiṇēsu kāūga mahāmahantaṁ satyaṁ bhariūṇa vicittabhaṇḍassa dāūṇa nāṇāmaṇirayaṇasāramaṇagdhēyamāharaṇaṁ uciyavāṇi yagavēsēṇēva pēsiō musammaṇayaraṁ dhagō tti.
