pattō kālakkamēṇaṁ, vināō jaṇēṇa. parituṭṭhō sē gurujaṇō, niggaō paccōṇiṁ. diṭṭhō ya jaṇaṇijaṇaēhiṁ, nivaḍiō calaṇēsu tēsiṁ, abhiṇandiō jaṇaṇi naṇaēhiṁ. kayā savvāyayaṇēsu pūyā, dinnaṁ mahādāṇaṁ, pavēsiō narindēṇa sammāṇiūṇa mahayā vibhūīē. kayaṁ ca gurūhi mahocchavabhūyaṁ vaddhāvaṇayaṁ ti. païrikkē pucchiō dhaṇasirivuttantaṁ jaṇaṇijaṇaēhiṁ. sāhiō tēṇa. vimhiyā jaṇaṇi jaṇayā. bhaṇiyō ya tēhiṁ-vaccha, alaṁ tīē. aṇuciyā khu sā pāvakammā bhavaō. na rēhaï kappapāyavē kavikacchuvalli tti. tā annaṁ tē samāṇarūvakulavihavasahāvaṁ dāriyaṁ gavēsāmō. na taē etya saṁtappiyavvaṁ. na muccaï sasī joṇhāē tti. tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — kō ettha avasarō saṁtāvassa; īisō khala saṁsārasahāvō tti. tēhiṁ bhaṇiyaṁ — sāhu sāhu, mahāpurisō khu tuma. tā kiṁ ettha avaraṁ bhaṇīyaetti. taō kayā sē gurūhiṁ dhaṇadēvamahimā. niggaō dhaṇō saha niddhamittēhiṁ. pūjiō jakkhō, kayā atthijaṇapaḍivatī. gaō ya bhuttuttarasamaē tayāsannaṁ cēva siddhatthaṁ nāma ujāṇaṁ. diṭṭhō ya tatya asōyapāyavatalagaō iriyāipañcasamiiō maṇavayakāyaguttō guttindiō guttabambhayārī amamō akiñcaṇō chinnaganthō niruvalēvō, kiṁ bahuṇā, aṭṭhārasasīlaṅgasahassadhārī aṇēyasāhupariyō jasōharō nāma kōsalāhivassa viṇayaṁdharassa puttō samaṇasīhō tti. taṁ ca daṭṭaṇa samuppannō sē pamōō, viyambhiō dhammavavasāō. cintiyaṁ ca ṇēṇaṁ. ahō sē rūvaṁ, ahō cariyaṁ, ahō sē dittī, ahō sōmayā, ahō sē purisayārō, ahō mahavaṁ; ahō sē lāyaṇṇaṁ, ahō visayanippivāsayā; ahō sē jovvaṇaṁ ahō aṇaṅgavijaō tti. tā dhannō khu ēsō daṭṭayō pajjuvāsaṇijjō ya. gaō tassa samīvaṁ. vandiō ṇēṇa bhayavaṁ jasōharō sēsasāhuṇō ya. dinnō sē guruṇā dhammalāhō sēsasāhūhi ya. ubaviṭṭhō gurupāyamūlē. bhaṇiyaṁ ca tēṇaṁ-bhayavaṁ, kiṁ puṇa tē nivvēyakāraṇaṁ, jēṇa tuma rūvi vya paścabāgō visayasuhamavahatthiūṇa pavvajja pavannō si? jasōharēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — ēgantanivvēyakulaharāō saṁsārāō vi avaraṁ nivvēyakāraṇaṁ ti? dhaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — bhayavaṁ, sayalajaṇasāhāraṇō khu ēsa saṁsārō; aō visēsakāraṇaṁ pucchāmi. jasōharēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — visēsō vi sāmannamajjhagaō cēva, tahāvi niyayamēva cariyaṁ mē nivvēyakāraṇaṁ ti. dhaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — karēu bhayavaṁ aṇuggahaṁ, kahēu amhāṇaṁ pi nivvēyakāraṇaṁ niyayacariyaṁ ti. taō jasōharēṇa kallāṇāgiī pasantarūvō ya ēsō kayāi nivvēyamuvagacchaï ti cintiūṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. sōma! jaï ēvaṁ, tā suṇa. atthi ihēva vāsē visālā nāma nayarī. tattha amaradattō nāma naravaī hotthā. iō ya atīyanavamabhavaṁmi tassa puttō surinda dattō nāma ahamāsi tti. jaṇaṇī ya mē jasōharā, bhajjā ya nayaṇāvali tti. tāō ya mē rajjaṁ dāūṇa pavannō samaṇattaṇaṁ. ahamavi saṁpattasammattō nayaṇāvalīnēhamōhiyamaṇō rajasaṇāhaṁ visayasuhamaṇuhavantō ciṭṭhāmi, jāva āgaō mē paliyacchalēṇa dhammadūō. nivēiō ya mē sārasiyābhihāṇāē nayaṇāvalīcēḍiyāē. taō samuppannō mē nivvēō. cintiyaṁ maē. ahō cañcalayā jīva lōyassa, ahō pariṇāmō poggalāṇaṁ, ahō asāraṁ maṇuyattaṇaṁ, ahō pahavaï mahāmōhō. avi ya—

aṇudiyahaṁ vacantāṇi'māi kaha ki jaṇō na lakkhēi

jīyassa jodhaṇassa ya diyahanisākhaṇḍakhaṇḍāī

diyahanisāghaḍimālaṁ āuyasalilaṁ jaṇassa ghettūṇa

candāicabaïllā kālarahaṭṭa bhamāḍenti

jhīṇē āuyasalilē parisussantaṁmi dēhasassaṁmi. natthi hu kōvi uvāō taha vi jaṇō pāvamāyaraï. alaṁ tā mē pamāēṇaṁ. pavajjāmō puvyapurisa sēviyaṁ samaṇattaṇaṁ. sāhiō niyayāhippābhō nayaṇāvalīē. bhaṇiyaṁ ca tīē ajjaütta, jaṁ vō rōyaï tti. na khalu ahaṁ ajjaüttassa paḍikūlayāriṇī; avi va jaṁ tumaṁ pavvajihisi, ahaṁ pitaṁ cēva tti nivēiyaṁ cēva ajjaüttassa. taō maē cintiyaṁ. ahō nibbharāṇurāyayā mamōvari dēvīē, ahō mahatthattaṇaṁ, ahō vivēgō, ahō cittaṇuyayā, ahō chandāṇuvattaṇaṁ, ahō samasuhadukkhayā, ahō aïgasahāvattaṇaṁ ti.

etthantaraṁmi nivēiō mē kālō maṅgalapāḍhaēhiṁ. paḍhiyaṁ ca tēhiṁ.

āsāiūṇa uyayaṁ kamēṇa pariyaṭṭiūṇa ya payāvaṁ

ujjōviūṇa bhuvaṇaṁ atyamaï divāyarō eṇḍiṁ

taō maē cintiyaṁ-dhiratthu jīvalōyassa; ēyassa vi diṇayarassa ēgadivasaṁmi cēva ettiyā avattha tti. taō ahaṁ atthāiyā maṇḍavaṁmi kaṁci kālaṁ gamēūṇa miyaṅkajoṇhāpasāhiyabhuvaṇabhavaṇē uddāmakāmiṇīyaṇaviyambhiyamayaṇapasarē ya pōsē gaō viiṇṇamaṇira yaṇamaṅgalapadīvasaṇāī kuṭṭimavimukkavarasurahikusumapayaraṁ bahalakatthūriyāvilitavimalamaṇibhittiṁ pavaradēvaṁgavatthavokkhāriyakayakhambhaṁ ujjalavicittavatthaviraïyaviyāṇayaṁ jaraḍhavidamāya-baghaḍiyapallaṅkasaṇāhaṁ atthuriyāpavaratūlīviiṇṇagaṇḍōvahāṇayaṁ vimalakaladhōyamaōva ṇīya[maṇō]harapaḍiggahaṁ ullambiyasurahikusumadāmaniyaraṁ kaṇayamayamahamahentadhūvaghaḍiyāulaṁ pajaliyaviittadhūmavattinivahaṁ caḍulakalahaṁsa pārāvayamihuṇasōhiyaṁ viraïyakappūravīḍayasaṇāhatambōlapaḍalayaṁ vaṭṭiyavilēvaṇapuṇavivihavāyāyaṇanimiyamaṇivaṭṭayaṁ surahipaḍavāsabhariya maṇōharōvaṇīyakaṇayakaccōlaṁ tappiyavaravāruṇīsurahikusumasaṁpāiyamayaṇapūyaṁ raīē viva saparivārāē nayaṇāvalīē samaddhāsiyaṁ vāsagēhaṁti. uvaviṭṭhō pallaṅkē. kaṁci kālaṁ gamēūṇa niggaō dēvīpariyaṇō. thēvavēlāē pasuttā dēvī. ahaṁ ca visayasuhavimuhiyacittōvi nēhāṇu rāgaō dēvī pariccaïyavvā, ēdahamettaṁ ettha dukkarati cintayantō ciṭṭhāmi, jāva sā dēvī pasuttō naravaï tti mannamāṇā mottūṇa pallaṅka mōiṇṇā koṭṭimatalaṁ. sasaṅkā ya ugghāḍiūṇa duvāraṁ niggayā vāsagēhāō. taō maē cintiyaṁ-kiṁ puṇa ēsā avēlāē aïnnaduvāraṁ niggaya tti? nūṇaṁ mama bhāviviōyakāyarā dēhacāyaṁ vavasissaï tti. taō ahaṁ ghettūṇa asivaraṁ niggaō tīē piṭṭaō. gayā ya sā pāsāyavālassa khujjayassa samīvaṁ. uṭṭhaviō tīē khujjaō. taō maē cintiyaṁ-haddhī ēyassa sāhiūṇa jahāsamōhiyaṁ karissaï tti.

etthantaraṁmi ghummantalōyaṇēṇaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ khujja ēṇaṁ-kīsa tumaṁ aja ettiyāō vēlāō tti? tō maē cintiyaṁ-hā kimēyaṁ aja tti saṁlabaï? ahavā aṇuciyāgamaṇā imāē vēlāē dēvī, aō ēvaṁ mantiyaṁ ti. hōu, paḍivayaṇaṁ suṇēmi. taō dēvīē bhaṇiyaṁ — ajja khu visamadhāuō cirāō pasuttō rāyā, aō ēsa kālakarakhēvō ti. tō maē cintiyaṁ-hā kimēyaṁ? etthantaraṁmi kaḍhiṇahatthēṇa tēṇa gahiyā agarudhūmāmōyagambhiṇē kēsa hatthē dēvī. taō pāḍiyā tēṇa samayaṁ dēvī. sikāramaṇaharaṁ ca tassa ya mamaṁ ca mayaṇakōvāṇalasaṁdhu kaṇaṁ viyambhiyaṁ tīē saha mōhaceṭṭiyaṁ. āliṅgiyā tēṇa, cumbiyaṁ ca sē calantatārayaṁ bayaṇaṁ. ēyaṁ ca vāyāyaṇapaviṭhṭhacandālōyabhāsiyaṁ baïyaramavayacchiūṇa avivēyapavaṇasaṁdhuvikaō pajjaliō mē maṇammi kōvāṇalō. kaḍḍiyaṁ ca tamāladalanīlaṁ maṇḍalaggaṁ. cintiyaṁ ca vāvāēmi ēē duvē vi pāvē ti. tō taṁ cēva kiraṇāvalībhāsuraṁ jalantamiva pecchiūṇa isi paṇaṭṭhamavivēyandhayārēṇa. jāyā ca mē cintā. jēṇa maē paracakkagayaghaḍāviyāraṇalālasā narindakēsariṇō viṇivāiyā, sō kahaṁ imaṁ purisasāramēyaṁ dēvi ca akajāyaraṇa vāvannasīlajīviyaṁ vāvāēmiti? annaṁ ca-vīsatthaṁ jaṁpiyamimīē kīliyaṁ ca ā bālabhāvāō, bhuttā siṇēhasāraṁ, jaṇiō appāṇa yatullō puttō. tā kiṁ ēiṇā. avi ya — avivēyabahulā cēva itthiyā hōi. ujjaō ya ahaṁ sāmaṇṇapaḍivattīē. ēvaṁ ca guṇaharakumārassa vi lāghavabhāvēṇa patthuyavidhāō tti. ahō mē asarisavavasāō tti viliēṇa takkhaṇaṁ cēva samāṇiyaṁ maṇḍalaggaṁ, virattaṁ ca mē cittaṁ dēvīō. uvaḍhiō dhammavavasāō. gō vāsaharaṁ, ṇuvannō sayaṇijjē, pavattō cintiuṁ. ahō mahiliyā nāma abhūmī visalayā, aṇaggī cuḍulī, abhōyagā visūiyā, aṇāmiyā vāhī, avēyaṇā mucchā, aṇunasammā mārī, aṇiya kā gōtī, arajjuō pāsō, ahē uō maccu tti. ahabā kiṁ imīē cintāē. īisō ēsa saṁsārō. aō cēva pavajjāmō samaṇattaṇaṁ ti. ēvaṁ jāva suhapariṇāmō kaṁci kālaṁ ciṭṭhāmi, tāva āgayā dēvī. kayaṁ maē pasuttacēḍa(ṭṭhi)yaṁ. ṇuvannā ya mama samīvē. ṭhiyā kaṁci kālaṁ. pavattā cāḍuyammakaraṇē. ahamavi tamēva suttaceḍḍa(8)yaṁ avalambiūṇa ṭhiō kaṁci kālaṁ. samāliṅgiō ahaṁ tīē. maē vi attaṇō citta viyāramadaṁsayantēṇa puvviṁ va bahu manniyā. etthantaraṁmi pahayāī pāhāuyatūrāī. paḍhiyaṁ kālanivēyaraṇa—

ēsā vaccaï rayaṇī vimukkatamakēsiyā vivaṇṇamuhī

pāṇīyaṁ piva dāuṁ paralōyagayassa sarassa

pahāyā rayaṇī, kayaṁ gōsakiccaṁ. ṭhiō mhi atthāiyāmaṇḍavē. kayā savisēsaṁ sāmantappamuhāṇamaṇujīvīṇaṁ pasāga. paviṭṭhō manti varayaṁ. āgayā vimalamaïppamuhā mahāmantiṇō. sāhiō maē ētēmi niyayāhippāō, na bahumaō tēsiṁ. bhaṇiyaṁ ca ṇēhiṁ. dēva, apariṇaō tāva kumāraguṇaharō, payāparirakkhaṇa pi dhammō cēva tti. taō maē bhaṇiyaṁ — kiṁ na yāṇaha tumbhē, kulahiī ēsā amhāṇaṁ, jamāgaē dhammadūra na ciṭṭhiyavvaṁ ti. tēhiṁ bhaṇiyaṁ — dēvō jāṇaï ti. aïkkantō sō diyahō, samāgayā rayaṇī. ṭhiō atthāiyāmaṇḍavē. kaṁci vēlaṁ ganēūṇa gaō vāsabhavaṇaṁ. niyattadēvīsiṇēhabhāvaō samāpayā mē nidā. rayaṇīcarimajāmami diṭṭhō maē suviṇaō. kilāhaṁ dhavalaharōpari siṁhāsaṇōpaviṭṭhō paḍikūla bhāsiṇīē pāḍiō kahām̐va ambāē jasōharāē, paloṭṭamāṇō gaō sattamabhūmiyāē, aṇupaloṭṭamāṇā ambā vi taha cēva ttiḥ uṭṭhiūga kahavi ārūḍhō mandaragiriṁ. etthantaraṁmi viudghō. cintiyaṁ ca maē. dāruṇārambhō vivāgasundarō ya ēsa sumiṇaō. tā na yāṇāmō, kiṁ bhavissaï tti? ahavā patthuyaṁ maē paralōyasāhaṇaṁ. jaṁ hōi, taṁ hōu tti.

taō dhammajjhāṇamaṇusarantassa cēva ikantā rayaṇī. kayaṁ pabhāōciyaṁ. ṭhiō mhi atthāiyāmaṇḍavē. āgayā mē mahallu jjalapariya ṇaparivāriyā ambā. abbhuṭṭhibhī saviṇayaṁ. pucchiō ahaṁ tīē sarīrakusalaṁ. nivēiyaṁ maē īsiṁ avaṇaüttimadrēṇa. nisaṇṇā ya sā dhavaladugullotyayāē mahāpīḍhiyāē. taō maē cintiyaṁ. ahō laṭṭhayaṁ jāyaṁ, jaṁ ambā vi ettha āgaya ti. nivē ēmi imīē niyayāhippāya, vinavēmi ēvaṁ pavvajjamantarēṇaṁ. ahavā añcantanēhālayā ambā dukha mē samīhiyaṁ saṁpāḍaïssaï tti. diṭṭhō ya akusalasumiṇaō; taō āsaṅkēmi ambāō ettha antarāyaṁ. na juttaṁ ca imīē paḍikūlamāsēviuṁ, jaō duppaḍiyārāṇi ammāpiīṇi havanti. virattaṁ ca mē cittaṁ bhavapavaścāō. na sakkuṇōmi iha cihium̐. tā uvāraṇa vinavēmi, jēṇa nissaṁsayaṁ cēva ēsā aṇujāṇaï tti. ēsō ya etthuvāō hōu. taṁ cēva sumiṇayaṁ tahā sāhēmi, jahā tassa paḍighāyaṇanimittaṁ vēsamettaṁ paḍucca aṇu jāṇihii ittarakāliya pabajjamambā. taō ahaṁ tahā pabvaïō cēva hōhāmi ti cintiūṇa savvatthāiyāsamakkhaṁ viśnattā ambā maē. amba, ajja maē rayaṇīra caramajāmaṁmi diṭṭhō sumiṇaō. taṁ muṇēu ambā. ambāē bhaṇiyaṁ — kahēhi putta! kaïrisō tti. tō maē bhaṇiyaṁ. ahaṁ khu kila guṇaharakumārassa rajjaṁ dāūṇa kayasiratuṇḍamuṇḍaṇō sayalasaṅgacāī samaṇagō saṁvuttō, dhavalaharōvarisaṁṭhiō ya paḍiō. tō viuddhō sasajjhasō tti. tō appasatthasuviṇayaṁ sōūṇa suviṇayatthakōviyāē bhayasaṁbhantatharaharentahiyayāē vāmapāēṇa mahimaṇḍalaṁ akkamiūga thuthukkayasaṇāhaṁ jaṁpiyaṁ ambāē. putta, paḍihayaṁ tē amaṅgalaṁ, ciraṁ jīva, niruvasaggaṁ ca mahiṁ pālēhi. ēyassa vi ya paḍighāyaṇanimittaṁ kīraü ima, kumārassa rajjaṁ dāūga gihami cēva ittiriyakālaṁ samaṇaliṅgapaḍivajaṇaṁ ti. maē bhaṇiyaṁ amba, jaṁ tumaṁ āṇavēsi. ampāē bhaṇiyaṁ — nivaḍaṇanimittaṁ ca nivāiūṇa vēyavihiṇā jalathalakhahayarē jīvē karēhi kuladēvayaccaṇēṇaṁ santikammaṁ ti. taō maē ṭhaïyā kaṇṇā, bhaṇiyaṁ ca-amba, kīisaṁ jīvaghāēṇaṁ santikammaṁ ti? ahiṁsālakkhaṇō khu dhammō. suṇa—

maṇamettēṇa vi ihaī parassa ekkaṁ pi maraṇabhīrusa

maraṇaṁ bhūyāṇa kayaṁ bahubhavamaraṇubbhavaṁ hōi

jō iha parassa dukkhaṁ karēi sō appaṇō visēsēṇaṁ

na pamāyakayaṁ kammaṁ jaṁ vihalaṁ hōi jīvāṇaṁ

jaṁ pi āiṭṭhēṁ karēhi sentikamma ti

taṁ muṇasu santikammaṁ narassa sambatthasāhaṇasamatthaṁ

jaṁ payaṇuyaṁ pi niccaṁ parassa pāvaṁ na cintēi

ihalōē paralōē ya santiyamma aṇuttaraṁ tasma

jaha pecchaï appāṇaṁ taha jō savvē sayā jīvē

ambāē bhaṇiyaṁ — putta, pariṇāmavisēsaō puṇṇapāvē, ēsā ya dhammasuī. suṇa—

jassa na lippaï buddhī hantūṇa imaṁ jagaṁ niravasēsaṁ

pāvēṇa sō na lippaï paṅkayakōsō bva salilēṇaṁ

ahavā jaï vi pāvaṁ havaï, taha vi dēhārogganimittaṁ kīraü imaṁ. pāvaṁ pi hu kāyavvaṁ buddhimayā kāraṇaṁ gaṇantēṇaṁ. taha hōi kiṁpi kajjaṁ visaṁ pi jaha ōsahaṁ hōi. maē bhaṇiyaṁ — amba, jaṁ tara āṇattaṁ pariṇāmavisēsaō puṇṇapāvē tti, ettha akajapavattaṇē kīisō pariṇāmō tti? annaṁ ca suṇa—

puṇṇamiṇaṁ pāvaṁ ciya sēvantō tapphalaṁ na pāvēi

hālāhala visabhōī na ya jīvaï amayabuddhī vi

na ya tihuyaṇē vi pāvaṁ annaṁ pāṇāivāyaō atthi

jaṁ savvē vi ya jīvā suhalavataṇhāluyā ihaī

ēvaṁ ca ṭhiē samāṇē kahaṁ hiṁsāvaī dhammasui tti? jaṁ ca āṇattaṁ jaï vi pāvaṁ havaï, tahavi dēhārōganimittaṁ kīraü imaṁ ti, ettha suṇa.

dīhāuō surūvō nīrōgō hōi abhayadāṇēṇaṁ

jammantarēvi jīvō sayalajaṇasalāhaṇijjō ya

dēhārogganimittaṁ pi ēyavayapālaṇaṁ ciya khamaṁ mē

pāvāhivaḍḍiēṇa ya dēhēṇa vi amba kiṁ kajja 1

ambāē bhaṇiyaṁ — putta, alaṁ risivayaṇaviyāraṇāē, kīraü imaṁ cēva maha vayaṇaṁ ti jaṁpamāṇī nivaḍiyā mē calaṇēsu. tō maē cintiyaṁ-ahō dāruṇaṁ; ēgattō guruvayaṇabhaṅgō annattō ya kkhabhaṅgō tti. tā kiṁ pattha kāyavvaṁ? ahavā guruvayaṇabhaṅgāō vi vayabhaṅgō cēva vivāgadāruṇō tti cintiūṇa vinattā ambā. jahā-amba, jaï tē ahaṁ piō, tā alaṁ imiṇā doggaïṁnivāyahē. uṇā samāiṭṭhēṇa. ahavā vāvāēmi attāṇaya, karēu ambā mama maṁsasōṇiēṇaṁ kuladēvayaccaṇaṁ ti. taō maē kaḍḍiya maṇḍalaggaṁ.

etthantaraṁmi hā hā mā sāhasaṁ ti samuddhāiyō atthāiyāmaṇḍavaṁmi kalayalō. sasajjhā viya udviyā ambā, dhariō tīē dāhiṇabhu yādaṇḍē, bhaṇiō ya. putta, ahō tē māivacchalattaṇaṁ; kiṁ vivannē tumaṁmi ahaṁ jīvāmi? tā payārantarakō māivahō cēva taē ēsō vavasiō tti ēvaṁ nirūvēhi. etthantaraṁmi kūiyaṁ kukkuḍēṇaṁ. suō ambāē saddō, bhaṇiyaṁ ca tīē. putta, sūēi appāṇaṁ ēsa kukkuḍō. atthi ya imō kappō, jaṁ īisē patthuyaṁmi jassa cēva sadō suṇīyaï, tassa tappaḍivimbasta vā vācāyaṇēṇa samīhiya saṁpāyaṇaṁ ti. tā ciṭṭhantu annē jīvā, ēyaṁ cēva kukkuḍaṁ vāvāēhi tti. maē bhaṇiya-amba, na khalu ahaṁ ambāēsēṇāvi attāṇayaṁ mottūṇa annaṁ vāvāēmi. ambāē bhaṇiyaṁ — putta jaï ēvaṁ, tā kiṁ ēiṇā; piṭṭhamayakukkuḍavahēṇāvi tāva saṁpāḍēhi mē vayaṇaṁ ti jaṁpa māṇī avahariūṇa maṇḍalaggaṁ puṇō vi nivaḍiyā mē calaṇēsu. etthantaraṁmi tannēhamōhiyamaṇēṇa paṇaṭṭhanāṇāvalōēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ maē pāvakammēṇa. amba, ēvaṁ jaṁ tuma āṇāvēsi tti. avi ya.

bahuyaṁ pi vināṇaṁ nāisahaṁ hōi niyayakajjammi

suṭṭhu vi dūrālōyaṁ ṇa pecchaē appayaṁ acchi

etthantaraṁmi dinā samāṇattī leppayārāṇaṁ. jahā-nivvattēha akālahīṇaṁ piṭṭhamayaṁ kukkuḍaṁ ti. nivvattiō ya tē hiṁ, uvaṇīō mē samīvaṁ. taō sā ambā taṁ ca kukkuḍaṁ mamaṁ ca ghettūṇa gayā dēvayāpāyamūlaṁ. ṭhāviō sē aggaō. bhaṇiō ahaṁ tīē. putta, kaḍḍēhi maṇḍalaggaṁ. taō maē īsi vihasamāṇēṇa kaḍḍiyaṁ. ambāē ya bhaṇiyaṁ — bhayavaï kuladēvaē, ēsa savvajīvāṇa vāvāyaṇavāraē puttadiṭṭhadussumiṇapaḍighāyaṇatthamuvaṇīō tē kukkuḍō. vāvāēi ya imaṁ ēsō. tā ēyassa sarīrē kusalaṁ karijjāsi tti bhaṇiūṇa saniō ahaṁ jahā vāvāēhi ēyaṁ ti. taō maē ghāiō kukkuḍō. kayaṁ dēvayaccaṇaṁ. bhaṇiō ambāē siddhakammō nāma svayārō. imaṁ sasēsaṁ lahuṁ randhēhi, jēṇa mē puttō ahaṁ ca dēvayāsēsaṁ pāsāmō tti. maē bhaṇiyaṁ. amba, alaṁ maṁsabhakkhaṇēṇa. suṇa.

muṭhṭha vi guṇappasiddhā tavaṇiyamā dāṇajhāṇaviṇiōgā

mantōsahā ya vihalā narassa maṁsāsiṇō honti

khaïyaṁ varaṁ visaṁ pi hu khaṇēṇa mārēi ēkasiṁ cēva

maṁsaṁ puṇō vi khaïyaṁ bhavamaraṇaparaṁparaṁ ṇēi

maṁsāsiṇō narassa hu pārataṁ āuyaṁ ca parihāi

parivaḍaï dōhaggaṁ dūsaha dukkhaṁ ca niraēmu

bhēsajja pi ya maṁsa dēī aṇumannaī ya jō jassa

sō tassa maggalaggō vaccaï narayaṁ na saṁdēhō

duggandhaṁ bībhatthaṁ indiyamalasaṁbhavaṁ asuiyaṁ ca

khaïēṇa narayapaḍaṇaṁ vivajaṇijja aō maṁsaṁ

ēē ya maṁsāsigō dōsā. imē puṇa amaṁsāsiṇō guṇā.

savvajalamajaṇāī savvapayāṇāi sabadikkhāō

ēyāi amaṁsāsittaṇassa taṇuyaṁ pi na samāī

jē cōramumiṇasaüṇā vaṇhipisāyā ya bhūyagahadōsā

ekkaṇa amaṁsāsittaṇēṇa tē taṇasamī(mā)honti

maṁsassa vajjaṇaguṇā dō cēba alaṁ narassa jiyalōē

jaṁ jiyaï niruvasāgaṁ jaṁ ca maō soggaī lahaï

ambāē bhaṇiyaṁ. putta, alaṁ viyāraṇāē. kayaṁ cēva mē vayaṇaṁ tumaē tti. tā kiṁ ēiṇā. na ya imaṁ sañcayaṁ maṁsaṁ ti. pariyappaṇā khu ēsā. taō maē ēyaṁ pi paḍivanamaṇuciṭṭhiyaṁ ca.

etthantaraṁmi baddhaṁ sāṇubandhamamuhakammaṁ ti. biiyadiyahami ya kaō kumārassa rajābhisēō. pavattō ahaṁ pavvaïuṁ. bhaṇiō ya dēvīē-ajjaütta, ajjēkaṁ puttarajjamuhamaṇubhavānō, suē pavvaïssāmō tti. taō maē cintiyaṁ-kimēyamavaropparaviruddhaṁ dēvīē vava siyaṁ. ahavā ēyaṁ pi atthi cēva.

chaḍḍēi jiyantaṁ pi hu mayaṁ pi aṇumaraï kāi bhattāraṁ

visaharagayaṁ va cariyaṁ vaṅkavivarṣaṁ mahiliyāṇaṁ

tā kiṁ mama ēiṇā; jaṁ ēsā bhagaï ti cintiūṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — sundari, pahabasi tumaṁ mama jīviyāō vi. kiṁ maē kayāi tuha paṇayabhaṅgō kō ti? taō cintiyaṁ dēvīē-pabdhayantē naravaïṁmi apavvayantīē maē mahantō kalaṅgō, vāvannē uṇa mantivayaṇaō aṇaṇumarantīē vi bālara japarivālaṇanimittaṁ na tahāvihō ti. tā vāvāēmi aja kēṇaï payārēṇa mahārāyaṁ ti. cintiō uvāō. dēmi sē bhōyaṇagayaṁ cēva kahaṁci cōradihi vañciūṇa akālakkhēvaghāyaṇaṁ visaṁ ti. aïkantā kāi vēlā. taō saṁpattāē bhōyaṇavē lāē uvaviṭhṭhō ahaṁ. vitthariyaṁ mahayā vicchaḍḍēṇa bhōyaṇaṁ. muhanāsiyaṁ saṁchaïūṇa hukkā bhuñjāvayā. sadāviyā dēvī, āgayā ya ēsā. alakkhijjamāṇatālaüḍa visasaṁjōiraṇa śilāhārapariṇāmaṇasamatthēṇaṁ aliyapaüttēṇa jōgavaḍaēṇa saha āgantūṇa uvaviṭṭhā. ēsā ya bhuttā saha mara. bhuttātrasāṇē ya āyamaṇavēlāē avaṇīēsu cōrēsu pajantabhakkhaṇijja āhārapariṇāmaṇasamatthaṁ aṇēgadavvasaṁjuyaṁ uvaṇīyaṁ mē jōyavaḍayaṁ, bhakviyaṁ maē nidhiyappēṇaṁ. bhuttāvasāṇē ya kayasōyāyārō gaō vāsabhavaṇaṁ. etthantaraṁmi viyambhiō visa viyārō, simisimiyaṁ mē aṅgēhi, jaḍḍathaṁ gayā jīhā, sāmalīhūyā kararuhā, pavvāyaṁ vayaṇakamalaṁ, niruddhō lōyaṇapasarō. taō ahaṁ tahāvihamaṇācikkhaṇīyamabatyantaramaṇuhavantō niḍiō sīhāsaṇāō. hā hā kimēyaṁ ti visaṇṇō mē samīvamāgaō paḍihārō. bhaṇiō ya tēṇa dava, kimaya ti. taō jaḍā jīha tti na jaṁpiyaṁ maē. nirūviō tēṇa, ubaladdhō mē visaviyārō. bhaṇiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa. arē bāharaha sigya visappōyanigghāyaṇasamatthē vejjē. taō na sōhaṇaṁ vejjavāharaṇaṁ ti cintayantī sasaṁbhamasamukkhittuttarīyā hāhāravaṁ karēmāṇī nivaḍiyā mamōvari dēvī. avaṇīyaṁ ca tīē niraṁsugaṁ cēva kandamāṇīē mahaṁ achuṭṭayaṅgulīhiṁ kaṇṭhagayaṁ mamapī ḍāē jīviyaṁ. taō ahaṁ dēvāṇuppiyā, piyāē bābāiō samāgō ajjhāṇadōsēṇa himavantadāhiṇadisālaggē silindhapabaē samuppayō barihi ṇīra kucchisi. jāō kālakamēṇa. taā bālabhō cēva jaṇaṇi bābāiūṇa gahiō vā hajuvāṇēṇa, dinnō sayapatthaēṇaṁ nandāvāḍaya vāsigō gāmatalavarassa. tattha ya anāyapakkhō sīuṇhātaṇhāvēyaṇāō aṇuhavantō ciṭṭhāmi. tibdhayarīē chuhāvēyaṇāē paḍipelliō kimiē khāiuṁ payattō mhi. tēhi ya mē pāvakammēhi saṁdhukijamāṇaṁ vitthāramukgayaṁ sarīraṁ. jāō mē viviharayaṇāmēlasacchahō piccha yabhārō. taō ahaṁ gāhiō naṭṭakalaṁ, pēsiō ya tēṇa sundarō tti kaliūṇa niyaputtassa cēva pāhuḍaṁ rāiṇō guṇaharassa. iō ya jasōharā vi mē puvvajammajagaṇī mama maraṇadivasaṁmi cēva aṭṭavasaṭṭā mariūṇa pāvakammabaliyayāē karahāḍayavisaē dhannaūrayasannivēsaṁmi kukkurīgabhaṁmi kukkurattāē uvavanā. jāō ya kukkurō. sō ya maṇapavaṇavēyadakkhō tti dhannapūrayasāmiṇā guṇadharassa cēva pēsiō kōsalliyaṁ ti. pattā amhē duvē vi samayaṁ cēva visālaṁ, pēsiyā ya atthāiyāmaṇḍavagayassa ranō, dihā ya tēṇa. jāyā ēyassa amhēsu pīī, pasaṁsiyā duvē vi. samappiō suṇaō ayaṇḍamaccussa sōṇahiyamayaharassa, ahaṁ ca rāyasaüṇaparivālayassa nīla kaṇṭhassa. bhaṇiō ya sōṇahiō. arē jāṇāsi cēva tumaṁ, jahā ahaṁ dōsu dadaṁ pasattō payāvālaṇē pāraddhīē ya. suṇaēsu jīva ghāyaṇaṁ muhaṁ ti, tā mahantaṁ jattaṁ karējāsi tti. tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ jaṁ dēvō āṇavēi ti. duvē vi ya amhē jahāvihiṁ lālēi naravaī. ēvaṁ ca aïkantō kōi kālō.

annayā ya ahaṁ gayaṇayalapāsāyasaṁṭhiyaṁ ārūḍhō indanīlanijjūhayaṁ. tattha antēurāṇaṁ rasaṇanēuraniṇāyagabhiṇaṁ navajalaharasadaṁ pitra guṇaṇiyāmurayanigyōsamāyaṇṇiūṇa naciuṁ payattō. tayavasāṇē ya vāyāyaṇavivarēgadēsēṇa dihā maē cittasāliyāē saha khujaēṇa sayaṇucchaṅgē raïsuhamaṇuhavantī nayaṇāvalī. taṁ ca mē da?ṇa samuppanna jāissaraṇaṁ. taō kammavasayattaṇēṇa amarisāṇalapalitēṇaṁ cañcunahaggēhi vi[la]kkhiumāraddhō. tīē vi tassa santiyaṁ khujjassa geṇhiūṇaṁ lōhamayalaüḍayaṁ kōhābhibhūyāē pahaō ahaṁ pahāravihalō nivaḍiō sōvāṇavattaṇīē, luḍhamāṇō pattō tamuddēsaṁ, jattha naravaī jū khellaï tti. maggaō ya mē geṇha geṇha tti saṁlavantō samāgaō dēvīpariyaṇō. taṁ ca tahāvihaṁ sadaṁ sōūṇa taddēsavattiṇā tēṇa puvvabhavajaṇaṇīsuṇaēṇa dhāviūṇa gahiō ahaṁ. gheppamāṇaṁ ca mēṁ pecchiūṇa rāiṇā hāhāravaṁ karēmāṇēṇa pahaō sō muṇaō akkhapāḍaēṇaṁ ti. pahāravihalaṁghalēṇa vamantaruhiraṁ mukkō ahaṁ tēṇa. kaṇṭhagayapāṇā nivaḍiyā duvē vi amhē dharaṇivaḍhē. saügamuvagī rāyā. āṇattā tēṇa purōhiyappamuhā maṇussā. jahā tāyassa uvarayassa ajjiyāē ya kālāyarulavaṅgacandaṇakaṭṭhēhi mahantō sakkārō kaō, soggaïnibandhaṇāī dinnāī mahādāṇāī, tahā ēyāṇa vi uvarayāṇa kāyavvaṁ ti. ēyapāyaṇṇiūṇa cintiyaṁ maē. ahō ṇu khalu puttaēṇaṁ savvasakārō pāviō, dināī ṇē soggaï nirandhaṇāī dāṇāī, ahaṁ puṇa tirikkhajōṇīē vi abbocchinnāē chuhāē kimiē khāyantō suṇaēhi ya khajjamāṇō ciṭṭhāmi. ahō garuyayā kammāṇaṁ. ēvaṁ cintayantassa vimukkaṁ sarīrayaṁ jīviēṇaṁ.

tō ahaṁ dēvāṇuppiyā, suvēlapavvayāvaradisābhāē atthi duppavēsaṁ nāma varṇa, tammi ya—

uvabhōgajoggapallavapupphaphalacchāhiudagapanbhaṭṭhē

sīyani-ghōḍi-baïbbūla-kayara-khaïrāisaṁkiṇṇē

tāḍa-vaḍa-khaja-khajaṇa-mukkata rugahīradukkhasaṁcārē

vivihavisaviḍaviniggayavaṅkaḍatikkhaggakaṇṭaïē

ēyārisaṁmi ya vaṇē nīsēsaṁ ciya nirābhirāmaṁmi

kāṇapasatīē gambhē jaṇiō'haṁ kuṇṭapasaēṇaṁ

tattha ganbhē narayakumbhīpāgāirēgavēyaṇaṁ visahamāṇō asaṁpaḍiē cēva pasabakālē jāō mhi duppavēsē vaṇē. abbocchinnachuhā pīḍiyāē ya paṇaḍhē mē jaṇaṇīē thaṇaēsu khīraṁ. tō ahaṁ bubhukkhāparimilāṇadēhō tattha paribhamantō gokkhurayakaṇṭaē khāiumāḍhattō. taō samaṁ pāvēṇa vitthāramuvagayaṁ mē sarīraṁ. iō ya sō pubbayarajammamāisuṇaō aṭṭajjhāṇamuvagō mariūṇa samuppannō imami cēva duppavēsē vaṇē bhuyaṅgamattāē tti. diṭṭhō ya sō maē kālapāsō va viddumamaṇirattanayaṇō ghaṇandhayāracchavī sasikalākōḍidhavaladāḍhō calantajamalajīhō jalāsayasamīvē daduraṁ khāyamāṇō tti. taō bubhukkhāparigaēṇaṁ aviyāriūṇa pariṇaī gahiō maē pucchadēsē. tēṇa vi ya nayaṇasihisihājālābhāmuramavalōiūṇa ḍakō ahaṁ vayaṇadēsē. ēvaṁ ca annāṇakōhavasayā duvē vi amhē parōparaṁ khāiumā raddhā. etthantaraṁmi adiṭṭaputvēṇa gahiō ahaṁ taracchēṇa, pāḍiō mahiyalē. taō sō mamaṁ khāiuṁ payattō. kiha? cammaṁ caracarāē phālayantō, chirāō taḍataḍāē tōḍayantō sōṇiyaṁ ḍheggaḍhaggāē ghoṭṭayantō aṭṭhiyāī kaḍakaḍāē mōḍayantō tti. avi ya—

taha khāiuṁ pavattō naha majjhaṁ khajamāṇasadēṇa

bhīēṇa va nīsēsaṁ jīvēṇa kalēvaraṁ mukkaṁ

tō ahaṁ, dēvāṇuppiyā, ēvaṁ sakammaviṇivāiō samāgō tatthēva visālāē nayarīē duṭṭhōdayābhihāṇāē ninnayāē mahādahaṁmi tattha mīṇīē gambhapuḍaē rōhiyamacchattāē samuppannō mhi. sō vi ya kaṇhasappō tahā mariūṇa imāē cēva sariyāē suṁsumārattāē tti. jāyā kālakkamēṇaṁ. annayā ahaṁ tattha cēva paribhamantō diṭṭhō susumārēṇa, gahiō pucchabhāē. etthantaraṁmi majaṇanimittaṁ samāgayāō antēuracēḍiyāō. dinā cilāiyābhihāṇāē cēḍiyāē jhampā. taō mēṁ mōtūṇa sā gahiyā aṇēṇa. sayarāhaṁ ca palāṇō ahaṁ । tīē vi ya hā kē(a)haṁ gahiyā gahiya tti mahantamāraḍiyaṁ. dhariyā lōēṇa. kalayalaravēṇa samāgayā macchabandhā. ōyariūṇa muyāviyā cēḍi, gahiō ya suṁmumārō, māriō durakhamārēṇaṁ. aïkantō kōi kālō. etthantaraṁmi ahaṁ kēvaṭṭapurisēhi samāsāiō jālēṇaṁ gahiō jīvantaō, mahāmacchō tti kaliūṇa samuppannakajjēhiṁ pāhuḍanimittamuvaṇīō guṇaharassa. parituṭṭhō rāyā. saṁpāḍiyaṁ paōyaṇaṁ tē siṁ. nīō tēṇa nayaṇāvalīē samīvaṁ. bhaṇiyā ya ēsā. amba, ēyassa rōḍiyamacchassa pucchabhāyaṁ tāyaṁ ajjiyaṁ ca uddisiūṇa māhaṇāṇaṁ randhāvēhi, uvarimabhāyaṁ ca pakkataliyaṁ kāūṇa majjhamattaṇō ya visasaṁ[saṁ]karējāsi. ēvaṁ ca mē suṇamāṇassa dēviṁ ca pecchiūṇa samuppanna jāissaraṇaṁ. ēvaṁ ca ranā samāṇattē chindiūṇa puccha khaṇḍaṁ pēsiyaṁ māhaṇāṇaṁ nayaṇāvalīē. sēsadēhami nicchalliyāī khāllāī, dinnaṁ tigaḍukkaḍaṁ hiṅgulōṇaṁ, parisittō halihāpāṇiēṇa. taō uvvatantamakkhaṇabhariyāē pakkhittō mahākavallīē, saṁvattuvvattaēṇa talijiuṁ payattō.

tō chinnabhinnapakkaṁ khāhii puttō mamaṁ ti jāṇāmi

tivvaviyaṇāhibhūō na dhammajhāṇaṁ jhiyāēmi

iya vikayatthiō mē nirayagaïsamāṇaēhi dukkhēhiṁ

dahakammaniyalabaddhō na muyaï jīvō sarīraṁ ti

ēvaṁ ca tattha tivvavēyaṇābhibhūō ciṭṭhāmi

ēyaṁ ca tāva ēyaṁ

iō ya visālānayarīē pāṇavāḍaē jā sā putra bhavajaṇaṇī suṁsumārabhavē vaṭṭamāṇī vāvāiyā, sā tattha chēliyattāē samuppannā. taō tīē garbhami ēlayattāē pakkhittō mhi. jāō kālakkamēṇaṁ. pattō jōvaṇaṁ. mahāmōhamōhiyamaṇō mēhuṇanimittaṁ ārūḍhō ammayaṁ. diṭṭhō ya niyajūhavaïṇā kasāyajōēṇaṁ tahā haō mammadēsē, jahā pāṇē paricaïūṇaṁ niyayavīēṇa cēva samuppannō tīē gambhaṁmi. avi ya—

kammamalaviṇaḍiēṇaṁ tattha marantēṇa mandabhaggēṇaṁ

appā hu appaṇa ciya jaṇiō jaṇaṇīē gabhaṁmi

sā ya paccāsannē pasavakālē guṇaharēṇa ramnā pāraddhīō niyattamāṇēṇa aṇāsāiyannapāṇiṇā tahāvihacchettabhāyaṁmi kāyajaḍḍayāē manda mandaṁ parisakamāṇī āyaṇṇamāyaḍiūṇa kōḍaṇḍaṁ viddhā kaṇṇiyasarēṇa. pahāragaruyayāē nivaḍiyā dharaṇivaṭṭhē. laddhalakkhō parituṭṭhō rāyā, samāgaō tamuddēsaṁ. diṭṭhā phuraphurentapāṇā āvanasattā ēsa tti lakkhiyā tēṇaṁ. taō ya sē uyaraṁ viyāriūṇaṁ nīṇiō ahaṁ. samappiō ayāpālayassa. annathaṇapāṇēṇaṁ jīviō. pattō kumārabhāvaṁ. etthantaraṁmi pāradīphaïlaṇanimittaṁ guṇaharēṇa rannā kuladēvayā pūyāvihāṇaṁ kaya. bhōyaṇatthaṁ vāvāiyā pannarasa mahisayā. bambhaṇajaṇabhōyaṇatthaṁ ca susaṁbhiyaṁ kayaṁ mahisamaṁsaṁ. iō ya kira pavittamuhō mēsō havaï tti lōyavāō(ā)āṇāviō ahayaṁ kāyasuṇaüciṭṭaraddhapakkaparisōhaṇanimittaṁ sūvayārēṇaṁ, ṭhāviō mahāṇasaduvārē. taō maē ussiḍiyaṁ taṁ maṁsa, bhuttaṁ bambhaṇēhi, viiṇṇaṁ āyamaṇaṁ. uṭṭhiyā diyavarā, ṭhiyā ya pantiyā-pantiyāhiṁ. etthantaraṁmi visēsujalanēvatthaṁ antēuraṁ ghettūṇa āgaō guṇaharō. taṁ ca mē dahraṇa samuppannaṁ jāissaraṇaṁ. vināō mē sancavuttantō. calaṇēmu nivaḍiūṇaṁ vāiyā bambhaṇā. bhaṇiyaṁ ca tēṇa-ēsā pantiyā tāyassa uvaṇamaü, ēsā ya ajjiyāē, ēyāō ya kuladēvayāē tti. taṁ paḍissuyaṁ bambhaṇēhiṁ. cintiyaṁ ca mara-ahō ēvaṁ pi nāma puttaē jayantē ahaṁ dukkhiō tti. etthantaraṁmi bhōyaganimittaṁ cēva sayalamāilōyapariyō ubaviṭṭhō rāyā. diṭṭhāō dēvīō, na diṭṭhā nayaṇāvalī. taō maē cintiyaṁ-aha kahiṁ puṇa sā bhavissaï?

etthantaraṁmi annaṁ uddisiūṇa bhaṇiyaṁ ēgāē cēḍīē. halā sundariē, iha ajja cēva imē mahisayā vāvāiyā, tā kiṁ puṇa ēsa ēvaṁvihō pūigandhō tti? tīē bhaṇiyaṁ — halā pemmamañjūsiē, na ēsa mahisagandhō; ēsō khu dēvīē nayagāvalīē tahā'jiṇṇē rasa lōluyattaṇēṇa macchayaṁ khāiūṇa koḍhagahiyāē vaṇantaruggiṇṇō dēhanissandavāō. iyarīē bhaṇiya-halā-sundariē, na ēsa macchayā hāramettasamuppannō koḍhō, kiṁ tu tahāsabbhāviyamahārāyavisappaōyavāvāyaṇamaṇiyapāvasamutthō tti. tā alamamhāṇamimīē. ēhi anaō gacchamha, tā mā kiṁpi āṇattiyaṁ dēissaï ti. gayāō cēḍiyāō. taō savisēsaṁ palōiyā maē, divā ya ēkapāsōvavidyā makkhiyasahassasaṁpāyasiyā viṇiggayātambanayaṇā nayaṇāvali tti. taō taṁ pecchiūṇa tivyaparadukkhasaṁtattō sōiuṁ pavattō. kahaṁ?

hā kiha sā pañcakkhaṁ kammamalocchāiyā paṇaïṇī mē

jammantaraṁ va pattā svavivajjāsabhēēṇa

vayaṇēṇa thaṇaharēṇaṁ caraṇēhi ya jīē nijiyā āsi

sabavilayāṇamahiyaṁ sōhā sasikalasakamalāṇaṁ

tivratavāṇa muṇīṇa vijā cittaharā daḍhamāsi

ēvaṁ ca cintayanō jāva kaṁci kālaṁ ciṭṭhāmi, tāva sadāviō rāiṇā svayārō, bhaṇiō ya. arē na rucaï mē imaṁ mahisayamaṁsaṁ, tā annaṁ kiṁpi lahuṁ āṇēhi tti. taō sūvayārēṇa kaliūṇa caṇḍasāsaṇō dēvō, mā kālakkhēvō havissaï tti mamaṁ cēva ēkaṁ satthiyaṁ chettūṇa kayaṁ bhaḍittayaṁ, pēsiyaṁ ca rabhō. tēga vi ya tāyassa uvaṇamaü tti bhaṇiūṇa dēvāviyaṁ thēvamaggāsaṇiyabambhaṇāṇaṁ, pēsiyaṁ ca kiṁpi nayaṇāvalīē, bhuttaṁ ca sēsamappaṇā. etthantaraṁmi ya jā sā mahaṁ jaṇaṇī guṇaharēṇa vāvāiyā āsi, sā kaliṅgavisaē mahi sīē kucchisi mahisaō samuppannō; vaḍiō kālakkamēṇaṁ. sō ya bhaṇḍabharayaṁ vahantō samāgaō visālaṁ nayariṁ. vāvāiō ya tēṇa jalapiyaṇaṇhāṇanimittaṁ sippānaī samōyaratō āsamandurāpahāṇō vollāhakisōrō. nivēiyaṁ ranō. bhaṇiyaṁ ca ṇa-arē āṇēhataṁ duṭṭamahisayaṁ. naravaïsamāēmāṇantaraṁ ca āṇīō ēsō. taō taṁ daṭṭaṇa rōsaphuriyāharēṇa sūtrayāra sadāviūṇa bhaṇiyaṁ rāigā. arē ēyaṁ durāyāraṁ duṭṭhamahisayaṁ sajīvaṁ cēva lahum̐ bhaḍitayaṁ karēhi tti. tēṇa vi ya nihayā sayaladisāsu lōhakhōyā, lōhasaṅkalāhiṁ ca niyāmiō lōhakhoṇṭaēmu. kayaṁ ca sē tigaḍugahiśulavaṇa jalabhariya puraō mahākaḍāhaṁ. panjāliō ya caüsu vi disāsu nāi dūraṁmi cēva khaïkharasārakaḍēhi huyāsaṇō. taō ya sō mahāmahantēṇa aggiṇā pañcamāṇō sukkoṭṭha bhaṇṭhatālū tivyatipāpariṁgō ahiyayaraṁ dukkhaṁ jaṇayantaṁ khārapāṇiyaṁ piviumāraddhō. palīviō tēṇa sō dēhamajjhē. niggayaṁ ca sē bīyapāsēṇaṁ kibdhisaṁ etyanta raṁmi samāṇattaṁ rāiṇā-pēsēhi lahuṁ mahisayabhaḍittayaṁ ti. taō jattha pakkamaṁsaṁ, tō taō chidiūga pēsiyaṁ sūkkhārēṇa. sittō ya ēsō ghayaüttēḍaēhiṁ. pakkhittaṁ ca sahiṇavaṭṭiyaṁ lōṇaṁ. visēsēṇa pajāliō jalaṇō. etthantaraṁmi āgaō rāyaparivēsaō। bhaṇiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa-arē anna pi vijāīyaṁ bhaḍittayaṁ lahuṁ dēhi tti. taō pulaïō ahaṁ sūvayārēṇē. bhaḍittayaṁ kajihāmi tti saṁmūhō hiyaēṇa, ullukkaṁ sirājālaṁ, vihaḍiō aṭṭhibandhō, galiyāī samvindiyabalāī. taō kaṇṭhagayapāṇō cēva gahiō sūvayārēṇa, chinnaṁ mē biiyapāsayaṁ. vimukō ya mē dēhō jīviēṇa. taō dēvāṇuppiyā, ēgasamayaṁmi cēva sō mahisayajīvō ahaṁ ca mariūṇa uppannā visālāpāṇavāḍaē kukkuḍīē ganbhami. aïkantō kōi kālō. um̐vahiē pasavalālē vāvāiyā ṇē jaṇaṇī majjārapōyaēṇa. kayavarōvariṁ ca taṁ khāyamāṇassa galiyaṁ aṇḍayadurga gaō majjārō. pakkhittō ya ṇē uvari kāēvi caṇḍālīē suppakōṇēṇa kajjayō. taṁdumhāpahāvēṇa jīviyā amhē. phuḍiyāī aṁḍayāī। niggayā amhē. gahiyāī aṇahulābhihāṇēṇa caṇḍāladāraēṇaṁ, jīvāviyā tēṇa. jāyāō ṇē candacandimāsacchahāō picchā valīō, samunbhūyā mē suyamuhaguñjaddharāyasarisā cūlā garuḍacañcusarisā ya mē cañcū. etthantaraṁmi divāī amhē kāladaṇḍavāsiēṇa. ahō imāī rāiṇō khellaïṇajoggā īti gahiyāī tēṇa. uvaṇīyāī ca guṇaharassa. parituṭṭhō rāyā. samappiyāī ca ṇē ēyassa cēva kāladaṇḍavāsiyassa. bhaṇiō ya ēsō-arē jattha jattha vaccāmi, tattha tattha ēyāī āṇēyabvāī. paḍissuyamaṇēṇa. annayā sayalantēurapariyariō vasantakīlānimittaṁ gaō kusumāyarujjāṇaṁ rāyā. nīyāī amhē tahiṁ kāladaṇḍavāsiēṇaṁ. ṭhiō ujāṇa tilayabhūē bālakayalīharayaparikkhittē māhavīlayāmaṇḍavē rāyā. iyarō vi saha amhēhiṁ gaō asōyabīhiyaṁ. diṭṭhō ya tattha bhayavaṁ saïsissagaṇaparivuḍō sasippahābhihāṇō āyariō tti. taō aliyavandaṇaṁ karentō ucagaō sāhumūlaṁ, dhammalāhiō tēṇaṁ. taō taṁ tavasirivirāyantadēhaṁ daṇaṁ āyaṇiūṇa payāsundaraṁ tassa vayaṇaṁ uvasantō viya ēsō. bhaṇiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa-bhayavaṁ, kōisō tumhāṇa dhammō? bhayavayā bhaṇiyaṁ — muṇaï.

sayalasattasāhāraṇō ēgō cēva dhammō. mūḍhō ya ettha aṇahigayasatthaparamatthō jaṇō bhēē kappēi. sō usa samāsēṇa imō maṇavayaṇakāyajōgēhiṁ parapīḍāē akaraṇaṁ, tahā suparisuddhassa aṇaliyassa bhāsaṇaṁ, taṇamettassa vi adattādāṇassa aggahaṇaṁ, maṇavayaṇakāyajōgēhiṁ avambhacēraparivajjaṇaṁ, gōsuvaṇṇahiraṇṇāiēmuṁ ca apariggahō; tahā nisibhattavajjaṇaṁ, bāyālīsēsaṇādōsasuddha piṇḍaparibhōō.

etthantaraṁmi bhaṇiyaṁ daṇḍavāsiēṇaṁ. bhayavaṁ, alaṁ ēiṇā; kahēhi gihidhamma. kahiō sē bhayavayā paścāṇuvvayāiō sāvayadhammō. bhaṇiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa-bhayavaṁ, karēmi ahamēyaṁ dhammaṁ. navaraṁ puvvapurisakkamāgayaṁ vēyavihiēṇa vihiṇā na paricaēmi pasuvahaṁ ti. bhayavayā bhaṇiyaṁ — jaï na paricayasi, taō imaṁ kukkuḍamihuṇayaṁ jahā tahā pāvihisi saṁsārasāyarē agatthaṁ ti. deṇḍavāsiēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — bhayavaṁ vahō kaō, jahā ya

sihisāṇasappapasayā mīṇōhārā ya aïyamēsā ya

pahisayakukkuḍapakkhī jāyā saṁsārajalahiṁmi

jāī ca ṇē pattāī tibdukkhāī, savvamēyaṁ suyāisayanāgiṇā sāhiyaṁ ti. ēyaṁ ca sōūṇa paraṁ saṁvēgamāvannō daṇḍa vāsiō. bhaṇiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa-bhayavaṁ, alaṁ mē iya pariṇāmadāruṇēṇaṁ vēyavihiēṇāvi pasuvahēṇaṁ dēhi mē gihidhammōciyāī vayāī. tō bhayavayā titthayarabhāsiēṇaṁ vihiṇā sē dinō saṁsārajalahibōhittha bhūō pañcanamōkārō, tahā thūlayapāṇāivāyaviramaṇāiyāī ca vayāī. gahiyāī ca ṇēṇa niyacariya pakṣaṇasabhupanajāissaraṇēhiṁ paramasaṁvēgāgaēhi ya amhēhiṁ. tō pariōsavisēsaō saṁpatta bhuvaṇagurudhammabōhēhiṁ nidvaviyasāṇubandhāsuhakammēhiṁ kūjiyaṁ amhē hiṁ. suyaṁ ca taṁ rāiṇā dūsaharantaragaēṇaṁ jayāvalīē saha suraya sokkhāṇuhavantēṇaṁ ti. gahiyamaṇēṇa pāsatthaṁ dhaṇuvaraṁ, sandhiō tīriyāsarō, dēvi, peccha mē sahavēhittaṇaṁ ti bhaṇiūṇa mukkō, taō ṇēṇa vāvāiyāiṁ amhē.

samuppannāṇi takkhaṇaṁ cēva bhuttamuttāē jayāvalīē cēva kucchisi. ābibhūyajiṇadhammabōhigabbhapahāvēṇa samuppannō tīē daḍhaṁ abhayadāṇapariṇāmō. dinnaṁ sattēsu abhayadāṇaṁ. jāyāiṁ kālakkamēṇaṁ ahaṁ dāraō jaṇaṇī mē dāriya tti. gabbhatthēhiṁ ca amhēhiṁ jaṇaṇī abhayadāṇaparā āsi; aō païṭṭhāviyāī nāmāī manaṁ abhayaruī iyarīē abhayamaï tti. vaḍḍiyāī amhē dēhōvacaraṇa kalā kalāvēṇa ya. cintiyaṁ ca rāiṇā — karēmi abhayamaīē vivāhaṁ abhayaruiṇō ya juyarajābhisēyaṁ ti.

etthantaraṁmi payaṭṭō pāraddhiṁ rāyā, niggaō visālāō, pattō ujāṇantaraṁ. chikō kusumāmōyasurahiṇā māruēṇaṁ. avalōiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa tamujjāṇaṁ. divō ya tattha tilayapāyavāsannē jhāṇamuvagaō mudattō nāma muṇivarō. kuviō rāyā, avasaüṇō khu ēsō pāraddhīē payaṭṭassa, tā ēyasta kayatthaṇāē cēva māṇēmi ēyaṁ ti cintiūṇa chucchukkārasāraṁ muyāviyā suṇayā. ayālamaccū viya sigghavēēṇa pattā muṇivarasamīvaṁ. muhuyahuyāsaṇō viva tavappahāē jalantadēhō divō tēhiṁ muṇivarō.

tō taṁ samujjalantaṁ sāṇā daṇa niṣpahā jāyā

ōsahigandhāmōḍiyapabhaṭṭavisā bhuyaṅga va

tavakammapahāvēṇaṁ kāūṇa payāhiṇaṁ suṇayavandraṁ

dharaṇigayamatthaēhi paḍiyaṁ pāē muṇivarassa

taō taṁ daṭhūṇa viliō rāyā. cintiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa-ahō varaṁ ēē suṇahapurisā, na uṇa ahaṁ purisamuṇahō, jēṇa ēvaṁ tavacaraṇa nirayassa bhayavaō vi akusalaṁ cintiyaṁ ti. etthantaraṁmi samāgaō sayalāē visālānayarīē pahāṇō sāhuvandaṇanimittaṁ rāiṇō cēva bālamittō jiṇavayaṇabhāviyamaī arahadattō nāma seṭṭiputtō ti. vināō ya tēṇa rāiṇō paralō yaniravekkhayāē muṇivērōvasaggō. taō paṇamiūṇa bhaṇiō tēṇa naravaī dēva, kim ēyaṁ ti. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ — jamuciyaṁ purisasāramēyassa. arahayattēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — dēva, purisasīhō khu tumaṁ, tā kiṁ ēiṇā. ōyaraha turaṅgamāō, vandaha bhayavantaṁ sudattamuṇivaraṁ. ēsō khu kaliṅgāhivassa amaradattassa puttō sudattō nāma naravaī. ēyassa paḍhamajōvaṇē vaṭṭamāṇassa uvaṇīō ārakkhiēṇa takarō. bhaṇiyaṁ ca tēṇē-dēva, ēēṇa paragharaṁ pavisiūṇa ēgaṁ mahallagaṁ vāvāiya muṭṭhuṁ gharaṁ, nīsarantō gaḍiō amhēhi; saṁpayaṁ dēvō pamāṇaṁ ti. ēyaṁ ca sōūṇa sadāviyā ṇēṇa dhammasatthapāḍhayā, bhaṇiyā ya. ēyassa imiṇā ārakkhiraṇa ēsa dōsō kahiyō, tā kīisō imassa daṇḍō tti. tēhiṁ bhaṇiyaṁ dēva, purisaghāyō paradavvāvahārī ya ēsō; tā tiyacaükkacaccarēhiṁ nivēiūṇa jaṇavayāṇaṁ taō nettuppāḍaṇakaṇṇanāsukattaṇakaracaraṇa chēyaṇēhiṁ jīviyanāsō cēva imassa daṇḍō tti risivayaṇaṁ. ēvaṁ cāyaṇṇiūṇa cintiyamaṇēṇa. ahō jahannā rāyakulajīviyā, jaṁ īdisaṁ pi aṇumannīyaï ti. tā alaṁ mē aṇēgōvadavabhāyaṇēṇaṁ rajasuhēṇaṁ ti. āṇandasanniyassa bhāiṇēyassa dāūṇa rajjaṁ muhamma gurusamīvē pavanō pavvaja ti. tā vandaṇīō khu ēsō.

ēyaṁ sōūṇa sasaṁbhantō gaō rāyā muṇivarasamīvaṁ. vandiō ṇēṇa bhayavaṁ sudattamuṇivarō. etthantaraṁmi samattō jhāṇajōgō. taō dhammalāhiō ṇēṇaṁ bhaṇiō ya. mahārāya, uvavisasu ti. taō ahō maē akajja vavasiya tti ahiyajāyapacchāyāvō lajjā vaṇayavayaṇakamalō uvaviṭhṭhō rāyā. cintiyaṁ ca ṇēṇaṁ. imassa risissa ghāyaō ahaṁ ti. ēvaṁ ca payāsiūṇa attaṇō siracchēyamanta rēṇa na pāyacchittaṁ pekkhāmi. tā kiṁ bahuṇā; na sakkuṇōmi akajjāyaraṇakalaṅkadūsiyaṁ attāṇaṁ muhuttayaṁ pi dhārēuṁ. aō alaṁ mē ihatthiraṇaṁ; saṁpāḍēmi jahā samōhiyaṁ ti. etthantaraṁmi samuppannamaṇapajjavanāṇāīsaēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ mudattamuṇivarēṇa. mahārāya, alaṁ tē imiṇā cintiēṇa. na khalu ēyaṁ ettha pacchitaṁ, jaṁtaē pariyappiyaṁ. jō āyaghāō vipaḍikuṭṭō cē dhammapayatthajāṇaēhi. bhaṇiyaṁ ca —

bhāviyajiṇavayaṇāṇaṁ mamattarahiyāṇa natthi hu visēsō

appāṇami paraṁmi ya tō vajjē pīḍamubhaō vi

jaṁ ca aphajāyaraṇakalaṅkasiyaṁ attāṇaṁ mannasi tti, ēyassa vi jiṇavayaṇāṇuṭāṇajalaṁ cēva pakkhālaṇaṁ na uṇa annaṁ ti. jaṁ pi cintiyaṁ saṁpāḍēmi jahā samīhiyaṁ ti, etthaṁ pi alaṁ tēṇa bhavāṇubandhiṇā saṁpāḍiēṇa. saṁpāḍēhi asaṁpāḍiyapuvvaṁ tēlōkabandhavāṇaṁ jāijarāmaraṇabandhaṇavimukkāṇaṁ titthayarāṇaṁ sāsaṇaṁ. etthantaraṁmi maṇagayāhippāyapayaḍaṇēṇaṁ ahō bhagavaō nāṇaṁ ti mannamāṇō imāō cēva pacchittamavayacchissaṁ ti āṇandabāhajalabhariyalōyaṇō paḍiō muṇivarassa calaṇēsu rāyā. viśnattō tēṇa bhayavaṁ muṇivarō bhayavaṁ, kahēhi kimestha pāyacchittaṁ ti? muṇivarēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — mahārāya, paḍivakkhāsēvaṇaṁ. taṁ puṇa na niyāṇavajjaṇamantarēṇaṁ ti, niyāṇaṁ parihariyavvaṁ. niyāṇaṁ ca ettha micchattamōhaṇīyasaṁgayaṁ annāṇaṁ. taṁ ca annahā ṭhiēma bhāvēsu anahā pavajjaṇaṁ ti. cintiyaṁ ca tumaē avasaüṇō khu ēsō, aō kayatthaṇāē māṇēmi tti. avasaüṇattē ya imaṁ tē nimittaṁ paḍihāi, jahā kila ēsa aṇhāṇasēvī kayasiratuṇḍamuṇḍaṇō viruddhapāsaṇḍavēsadhārī bhikkhōvajīvagō tti. tā ettha mahārāya, majjhatthō bhaviūṇa nisāmēhi kāraṇaṁ, kē vhāṇasēvaṇāsēvaṇāē guṇadōsa tti? tattha ṇhāṇasēvaṇaguṇā.

dēhō khaṇamettasuī tami ya rāō tahāhimāṇō ya

vilayāṇa patthaṇijjō sui tti dappō ya akkhāṇaṁ

imē ya dōsā.

jalagayajīvavidhāō uppīlaṇī ya annasattāṇaṁ

aṅgārakhīradhuvaṇē annāṇapayāsaṇaṁ cēva

ēē cēva vivajjaēṇaṁ aṇhāṇaguṇā.

dōsā uṇa vibuhajaṇaṁ paḍuca na hu kēi ettha vijanti

jaṁ sabasasthasārō pāṇidayā tigaraṇavisuddhā

ēvaṁ gaṇamāṇēhiṁ cūlōvaṇayaṁmi jamnadikkhāē

sabbāyarēṇa gahiyaṁ aṇhāṇavayaṁ diēhiṁ pi

annaṁ ca—

akkhaṇḍiyavayaniyamā guttā dantindiyā jiyakasāyā

sajjhāyajhāṇanirayā nicasuī muṇivarā honti

siratuṇḍamuṇḍaṇaṁ pi hu jaïssa sanyāsavā niyattassa

paḍhamavayarakkhaṇaṭṭhā guṇāvahaṁ hōi niyamēṇaṁ

pāsaṇḍaṁ pi ya ēyaṁ sumaṅgalaṁ vīyarāyadōsēhiṁ

jamhā jiṇēhi bhaṇiyaṁ aō viruddhaṁ ti vāmōhō

savvārambhaniyattō appaḍibaddhō ya ubhayalōēsu

bhikkhōvajīvagō ciya pasaṁsiō sancasatthēsu

ēvaṁ ca, mahārāya, paramaguṇajuttattaṇēṇa tiyasāṇa vi mahāmaṅgalaṁ samaṇarūvaṁ kahaṁ tē avasaüṇō tti?

ēyam āyaṇiūṇa paṇaṭṭhaṁ rāiṇō micchattaṁ. ahō nāṇāisaō tti japamāṇō nivaḍiō calaṇēsu. bhaṇiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa-bhayavaṁ, ēvamēyaṁ, jamāiṭṭhēṁ bhayavayā. vajiyaṁ maē niyāṇaṁ. tā khaïmasu mē ēyamavarāhaṁ ti. bhayavayā bhaṇiyaṁ — uṭṭhēhi dēvāṇuppiyā uṭṭhēhi, alaṁ tē saṁbhamēṇaṁ. khamāpahāṇā cēva muṇiṇō havanti. khamiyaṁ maē savvasattāṇaṁ. nisāmēhi tityayarabhāsiyaṁ samāē paraṁparābhāvaṇaṁ. viṇā vi vaïyaraṁ bālēṇa'kōsiēṇāvi sāhuṇā khamā bhāviyavvā sundarō khu ēsō jamēvamavi ahiṇiviṭṭhō na maṁ tālēi. tāliēṇāvi sāhuṇā khamā bhāvēyavvā sundarō khu ēsō, jamēvabhavi ahiṇiviṭṭhō na maṁ jīviyāō vavarōvēi tti. vavarōijjamāṇēṇāvi sāhuṇā khamā bhāvēyavvā sundarō khu ēsō, jamēvamavi ahiṇiviṭṭhō na mēṁ saṁjamāō bhaṁsēī, kiṁ tu mamaṁ cēva puvyakammapariṇaī ēsa tti. ēyaṁ ca sōūṇa parituṭṭhō rāyā. cintiyamaṇēṇaṁ-natthi avisaō nāma bhayavaō nāṇasta. aō pucchāmi bhayavantaṁ tāyassa ajjiyāē ya gaïvisēsaṁ ti. pucchiō bhayavaṁ, sāhiō ya bhayakkhā piṭṭhakukkuḍavavaha nimittō maūrāilakkhaṇō jayāvalīgabbhasamuppattipajjavasāṇō tti. rāiṇā cintiyaṁ-ahō jugucchaṇīyayā saṁsārassa, ahō aṇavatthiyasiṇēhayā itthiyāṇaṁ, ahō garuyayā mōhassa, ahō dāruṇa vivāgayā akajjāyaraṇāṇaṁ, jamiha dēvayānimittaṁ piṭṭhamayakukkuḍavahō vi ēvaṁ pariṇaō tti.

hā ahayaṁ ki kāhaṁ niratthayaṁ jēṇa jiyasayā bahuyā

vāvāiyā phurantā anāṇamalāvalittēṇa

tā nūṇaṁ gantavvaṁ nirayaṁ keṇḍujjuēṇa panthēṇa

natthi hu ettha uvāō ahavā pucchāmi bhayavantaṁ

etthantaraṁmi muṇiyanarindāhippāraṇaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ mudattamuṇivarēṇa-mahārāya, atthi uvāō. sō uṇa tigaraṇavisuddhā jiṇadhamma paḍivattī. sā puṇa puvvadukkaḍēsu añcantamaṇuyāvō, jiṇavayaṇajalēṇa cittarayaṇasōhaṇaṁ, savvārambhacāraṇa cārittapaḍivattī, mettīpa mōyakāruṇṇamajhatthayāṇaṁ ca jīvaguṇāhiyakilissamāṇāviṇīēmu bhāvaṇā. paḍivanacaraṇabhāvaṇā ya pāṇiṇō taïppabhiimēva appamā yāisaraṇa païvaḍḍamāṇasaṁvēgā niraïyārasīlayāē khaventi puvvadukkaḍāiṁ pāvakammāī, abhāvaō nimittassa na bandhenti navāī. tō tē, dēvāṇuppiyā, paramasuhasamēyā suhaparaṁparāē cēva khaviūṇa kammajālaṁ pāventi jāijarāmaraṇarōyasōyarahiyaṁ paramāyaṁ ti.

rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ — bhayavaṁ, jaï tāva tāyaajjiyāṇaṁ ēdahamettassa vidukkaḍassa īisō vivāō, tā kahamahaṁ mahāpāvakammayārī vivāgaō nirayāiēmu abhujiūṇa taṁ kammavivāgaṁ soggaī lahāmi tti? bhayavayā bhaṇiyaṁ — mahārāya, muṁṇa. natthi asajhaṁ nāma caraṇapariṇāmassa. ēsō khalu paramāmayaṁ pāvavisapariṇaīē, vajja kammapavvayassa,cintāmaṇī samīhiyāṇaṁ, kappapāyavō siddhisuhaphalassa. jahēva mahārāya, visalēsabhōiṇō vi ettha pāṇiṇō akayapaḍiyārā pāventi āvaī, munjhanti hiyāhiēma, na sēvanti māṇussayamuhāī, paricayanti jīviyaṁ tahēva ēē pamāiṇō jīvā kāūṇa pāvakammāiṁ akāūṇa paḍiyāraṁ pāvanti tapphalaṁ jāijarāmaraṇarōyasōyaṁ ti. kayapaḍiyārā uṇa paramāmayasāmatthāō nijiṇanti kālakūḍa pi mahāvisa, kimaṅga puṇa visalēsaṁ ti; ēvaṁ ca aṇāibhavabhāvaṇāō jīvā kāūṇa pāvakammaṁ sēviūṇa tassa paḍivakkhabhūyaṁ mahācaraṇapariṇāmaṁ nijiṇanti aṇēyabhavajaṇayaṁ pi pāvakammaṁ, kimaṅga puṇa ēgabhaviyaṁ ti. aïyaṁ sōūṇa harisiō rāyā, bhaṇiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa. bhayavaṁ, aha kīisō puṇa ēsa caraṇapariṇāmō tti vuccaï? bhayavayā bhaṇiyaṁ — sammannāṇapuvvayaṁ tinvaruīē dōsanivattaṇaṁ ti. bhaṇiyaṁ ca—

jāṇaï uppannaī jaï tā dōsā niyattaī sammaṁ

iharā apavittī ya vi aṇiyattī cēva bhāvēṇaṁ

ēsō aṇuhavasiddhō kammavigamahēū. rāiṇā cintiyaṁ-bhayavantamaṇusēvantāṇaṁ na dullahaṁ sammannāṇaṁ, samuppannasammannāṇāṇa ya saṁbhavaï tivvaruī, taō ya sāyattaṁ dōsaniyattaṇaṁ. tā dhannō ahaṁ, jassa mē bhaïyavayā dasaṇaṁ jāyaṁ ti. na appapuṇṇā mahānihi pecchanti. tā alamannēṇa, bhayavaō cēva āṇamaṇuciṭṭhāmi tti cintiūṇa bhaṇiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa. bhayavaṁ, uciō ahaṁ sāmaṇṇapaḍivattīē? bhayavayā bhaṇiyaṁ — mahārāya, kō annō uciō ti?

taō saṁjāyaharisēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ rāiṇā-arē nivēēha maïsāyarappamuhāṇaṁ aja mantīṇaṁ. jahā kāyavvō dēvāṇuppiēhiṁ abhayaruiṇō rejjābhisēōni, na kāyanyō ya mama santiō khēō; pavajāmi ahaṁ bhayavayā surāsuranamiēṇa bhuvaṇaguruṇā paṇīyaṁ samaṇaliṅgaṁ. jaṁ dēvō āṇavēi tti jaṁpiūṇa gayā niyōgakāriṇō. nivēiyaṁ tēhi mantijaṇavayāṇaṁ. suō ēsa vuttantō antēurēṇa. taō nēhamaya saṁbhamēṇaṁ pariccaïya asamāṇiyaṁ ālekkhagandhadavvāi hāhāravasaṇāhaṁ payaṭṭamantēuraṁ. ahaṁ pi tēhitō cēva ēyaṁ vaïyaramāyaṇṇiūṇa abhaya maīē samēō tti. calaṇaparisakaṇēṇēva pattā ya ṇē naravaïsamīvaṁ. diṭṭhō muṇindapāyamūlē saṁvēgamukgō rāyā rāyapattīhiṁ, kiha tō tāhi sappaṇāma samayaṁ pakkhubhiyabhūsaṇaravēṇaṁ. aṇirūviyakkharatthō jayasadō sē samugghuṭṭhō.

tēṇa vi vēraggavasā aṇāyaraviiṇṇamantharacchēṇa

ullōlantasiṇēhaṁ īsi samōṇāmiyaṁ vayaṇaṁ

ēvaṁ ca saṁbhāsiēṇa sambantēurajaṇēṇa pāyavaḍiēṇa vinattō naravaī.

khayadāḍhō vya bhuyaṅgō ki ēyaṁ vāriniyaliyagaō vva

sīhō va pañjaratthō jhāyasi panbhaṭṭharajjō vtra

taō ēvaṁ vighnattēṇa rāiṇā sāhiyaṁ niravasēsaṁ muṇivayaṇāiyaṁ ti. taṁ ca ṇē sōūṇa samuppannaṁ jāissaraṇaṁ. taō tassaṁbhamēṇaṁ nivaḍiyāi dharaṇivaḍhē. hā kimēyamavaraṁ ti mannamāṇīhiṁ viruiyaṁ rāyapanīhiṁ. bāhajalasittagattaṁ ca ṇē uvari mucchamuvagayā ambā. taō laddhāō cēyaṇāō, viuddhā amhē, samāsāsiyā ambā, viśnattō rāyā. tāya, alaṁ ṇē saṁsārakilēsāyāsakārarahiṁ visaēhi; aṇujāṇāhi tāva amhāṇaṁ pi sayaladukkhavirēyaṇaṁ samaṇattaṇaṁ ti. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ — ahāsuhaṁ dēvāṇuppiyāī, mā paḍibandhaṁ karēha. taō vijayavaṁmmaṇō niyabhāiṇēyassa dāūṇa rajjaṁ kāūṇa aṭṭhāhiyāmahāmahimaṁ sayalantēurapahāṇajaṇasamēō ghettūṇa amhē abhiṇikkha nō rāyā. viśnattō maē bhayavaṁ sudattamuṇivarō. bhayavaṁ, kaïrēhi aṇuggahaṁ nayaṇāvalīē dhammakahāē; pāvēu bhayavaō pabhāvēṇa ēsā vi sayaladukkhacigicchayaṁ jiṇapaṇīyaṁ dhammaṁ. bhayavayā bhaṇiyaṁ -sōma, avisaō khu ēsā dhammakahāē. saṁtappiō imīē aka jāyaraṇāpacchāsēvaṇāē kammavāhī, baddhaṁ ca taccapuḍhavīē parabhavāuyaṁ aō pāviyabvamavassaṁ tīē nāragattaṇaṁ, na pavajaï ya ēsā mahāmōhāō jiṇadhammarayaṇaṁ ti. taō maē cintiyaṁ-ahō dāruṇavivāgayā akajāyaraṇassa, īisō ēsa saṁsārasahāvō; tā kiṁ karēmi tti? taō aïsayanāṇāvalōyarēṇa bhayatrayā bhaṇiyaṁ — alaṁ tē imiṇā saṁsāravivaddhaṇēṇa tīē uvari aṇubandhēṇa. ēyaṁ cēva sayalalōyadullahaṁ kahaṁci laddhaṁ pavvajjaṁ karēhi tti. taō guruguṇāṇubhāvēṇaṁ pāliyaṁ samaṇattaṇaṁ, kālamāsē ya siddhantavihiṇā karē ūṇa kālamuvavannāiṁ sahassārābhihāṇē dēvalōē.

tattha vi uvabhunniūṇa murāuyaṁ caviūṇa dēvalōyāō kōsalāē visayaṁmi sāraē nayarē viṇayaṁdharassa rabhō lacchimaīē mahā dēvīē suyattāē uvavannō mhi. jāō kālakkamēṇaṁ. kayaṁ ca mē nāma jasōharō tti. abhayamaījīvadēvō vi caviūṇa dēvalōgāō pāḍaliputtē nayarē īsāṇasēṇassa rāiṇō vijayāē mahādēvīē kucchisi dhūyattāē samuvavannō tti. jāyā kālakamēṇaṁ. païṭāviyaṁ ca sē nāmaṁ viṇayapaï tti. vaḍḍiyāī ca amhē dēhōvacaēṇaṁ kalākalāvēṇa ya. pēsiyā ya mē sayaṁvarā īsāṇasēṇēṇa viṇayamaī. suyaṁ ca maē ēyaṁ. parituṭṭhō hiyaēṇaṁ. pattā ya sā mahayā caḍayarēṇaṁ, bahumaniyā tāraṇaṁ, āvāsiyā nayarabāhi. kayaṁ vaddhāvaṇayaṁ. gaṇāviō vārējadiyahō, samāgaō mē maṇōrahēhiṁ. nivvattaṁ ṇhavaṇayaṁ. payaṭṭō ahaṁ mahāvibhūīē viṇayamaī pariṇēuṁ. vajantēhiṁ vivihamaṅgala māṇō pāsāyamālātalagayāhiṁ purasundarīhiṁ pattō rāyamaggaṁ. etthantaraṁmi phuriyaṁ mē dāhiṇalōyaṇēṇaṁ, samuppannō harisavisēsō. cintiyaṁ maē-bhaviyavvaṁ aō vi avarēṇaṁ mahāpamōēṇaṁ ti.

etthantaraṁmi diṭṭhō maē gōyarapaviṭṭhō kallāṇasedvibhavaṇaṅgaṇē sāhū. taṁ ca mē datr̥̄ṇa samuppannō saṁbhamō. taō abbhatyayāē sāhu dhammassa vicittayāē kammapariṇaīra amōhadaṁsaṇayāē bhayavaō samuppanna jāissaraṇaṁ. mucchiō gaïndakhandhē, nivaḍamāṇō dhāriō pāsavattiṇā rāmabhaddābhihāṇēṇa sayalahatyārōhapahāṇamayaharēṇaṁ. hā kim ēyaṁ ti visaṇō rāmabhaddō. mā vāyaha tti vāriyā tūriyādī, uvasantā ya khippaṁ. hā kim ēyaṁ ti avisādī vi daḍhaṁ visaṇṇacittō samāgaō tāō. pūgaphalāimayamaïō havissaï ti siñcā viō candaṇapāṇiēṇaṁ. laddhā maē cēyaṇā, ummililayaṁ lōyaṇajuyaṁ, kō āsaṇapariggahō, virattaṁ saṁsārasāyarāō cittaṁ. bhaṇiyaṁ ca tāraṇa putta, kim ēyaṁ ti. maē bhaṇiya-tāya, dāruṇaṁ saṁsāravilasiyaṁ. tāraṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — putta, kō etya āsarō saṁsārasta? maē bhaṇiyaṁ — taya, mahantī khu ēsā kahā, na saṁkhēvaō kahiuṁ pārīyaï. tā ēgaṁmi dēsē uvavisaü tāō, saddāvēu mē māilōyaṁ pahāṇajaṇavayaṁ ca, jēṇa sāhēmi lāyasa saṁsārāvasarakāraṇaṁ ti. taō rāyamaggāsanāē mahāsahāē ubaviṭṭhō rāyā saha bhaē. saddā viō ammayājaṇō pahāṇajaṇaō ya, ṭhiō uciyaṭhāṇēsu. bhaṇiyaṁ ca tāēṇa-putta, kimēya; sāhēhi taṁ saṁsāravilasiyaṁ. maē bhaṇiyaṁ — āyaṇṇasu tāō, jahā maē aṇuhūyaṁ ti. taō pāraddhō kahēuṁ. tāya, nigguṇō ēsa saṁsārō. mōhābhibhūyā khu pāṇiṇō na niyanti ēyasta sarūvaṁ, ālōcenti aṇālōciyabāī, payanti ahiē, na pecchanti āyaī. ettha khalu surāsurasāhāraṇā tāva ēē jāijarāmaraṇarōyasōyapiyavippaōyāiyā viyārā. dārugō ya vivāō thēvassa vi pamāyaceṭṭhiyassa, jēṇa piṭṭhamayakukkuḍakahō vi peccha kahaṁ pariṇaō ti? bhaṇiūṇa sāhiō surindadattajammāiō jāissaraṇapajjavasāṇō niyayavuttantō. taṁ ca sōūṇa ahō dāruṇavivāgayā akajjāyaraṇassa tijapamāṇō saṁvēgamuvagaō rāyā ambāō sēsajaṇavaō ya. taō maē bhaṇiyaṁ — tāya, īdisaṁ akajjā. yaraṇapariṇāmaṁ pecchiūṇa virattaṁ mē bhavacāragāō cittaṁ, viyambhiō jiṇakkhaṇapaḍibōhō. tā aṇujāṇaü tāō, jēṇa tāyappahāvē ṇēva karēmi saphalaṁ maṇuyattaṇaṁ ti. taō agāibhavabbhatyamōhadōsēṇa aviyāriūṇāyaī jaṁpiyaṁ tāraṇa. putta, kō puttayassa paṇaya bhaṅgaṁ karēi, saphalaṁ cēva bhavaü maṇuyattaṇaṁ, tā pariṇēhi tāva ēvaṁ īsāṇasēṇadhūyaṁ. tō karejjāsi sammaṁ payāparivālaṇēṇa mahantaṁ puṇṇa khandhaṁ ti. maē bhaṇiyaṁ — tāya, vighnattaṁ maē tāyassa, virattaṁ mē cittaṁ bhavacāragāō. tā alaṁ mē dārapariggahēṇa. tāraṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — putta, kō viya dōsō dārapariggahassa? maē bhaṇiyaṁ — tāya, dārapariggahō hi nāma nirōsahō vāhī, jēṇa āyayaṇaṁ mōhassa, avacaō dhiīē, su(sa)hā vikkhēvassa paḍivakkhō santīē, bhavaṇaṁ mayassa, vēriō suddhajjhāṇāṇaṁ, pahavō dukkha samudayassa, nihaṇaṁ suhāṇaṁ, ā vāsō mahāpāvassa. paḍivajjiūṇa ēvaṁ pañjaragayā viya sīhā samatthā vi paralōyasāhaṇē māṇusabhāvalambhē vi sīyanti pāṇiṇō. annaṁ ca-tāya, na juttaṁ rayaṇacittēṇaṁ kaścaṇathālēga purīsasōhaṇaṁ. purīsasōhaṇamettā ya ettha visayā, acintacintāmaṇisannihaṁ ca jiṇavayaṇabōhasaṁgayaṁ māṇusattaṇaṁ, kammabhūmī ya ēsā, paramapadasāhaṇaṁ ca caraṇāṇuṭṭhāṇaṁ. tā alamannahāviyappiēṇa. aṇujāṇāhi mē sayaladuvakhavium̐ḍaṇi pabajjaṁ ti. taō bāhollalōyaṇēṇaṁ jaṁpiyaṁ tāraṇa. putta, ēvamēyaṁ, kiṁ tu paramatyaṁ pi jaṁpamāṇō nēhakāyaraṁ pīḍēsi mē hiyayaṁ ti. maē bhaṇiyaṁ — tāya, alaṁ mē aparamatthapecchiṇā nē hēṇa. ēsō cēva ettha pahāṇaṁ saṁsārakāraṇaṁ, jēṇa dīvō vva sabalōgō khaṇē khaṇē jāyaē viṇassaï ya. saṁsaraï ya nēhavasā niruvāyāṇō u ulhāi. tāēpā bhaṇiya-ēvamēyaṁ, kiṁ tu khijihii sā tavassiṇī īsāṇasēṇadhūya tti. maē bhaṇiyaṁ — tāya, thetramēyaṁ kāraṇaṁ. annaṁ ca-nivēyā vēu tāō tīē vi ya ēvaṁ vuttantaṁ. kayāi sā vi ēyaṁ sōūga paḍivōhaṁ pāvaï ti. tō tāraṇa juttamēyaṁ ti maṇiūṇa pēsiō saṅkṣavaddhaṇābhihāṇō purōhiō, bhaṇiō ya tāraṇa. jahāsuyaṁ nivēēhi rāyaduhiyāē, bhaṇāhi ya taṁ ēvaṁ ṭhiē kiṁ amhēhiṁ kāyavvaṁ' ti? gaō saṅkṣabaddhaṇō. āgaō thēvavēlāē, bhaṇiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa. mahārāya, saṁsiddhā maṇōrahā kumārassaḥ suṇēu mahārāō. gaō ahaṁ iō rāyadhūyāsamīvaṁ, pavēsiō sabahumāṇaṁ paḍi hārēṇa; mahārāyapurōhiō tti ahiṇandiō rāyadhūyāē, davāviyaṁ āsaṇaṁ, uvaviṭṭhō ahayaṁ. taō mara bhaṇiyaṁ — rāyaputti, atthi kiṁci vattavvaṁ ti. tīē bhaṇiyaṁ — bhaṇāu anjō. maē bhagiyaṁ-rāyaputti, dēvasāsaṇamiṇaṁ apahiyāē sōyavvaṁ ti. taō tīē kāuṇa aṅgului ōyariūṇa āsaṇāō jaṁ gurū āṇavēi tti baddhō añjalī. tō mara bhaṇiyaṁ rāyaputti, iha āgacchamāṇassa kumārassa sāhudaṁsaṇēṇaṁ samuppanna jāissaraṇaṁ, saṁbhariyā ya nava bhavā, siṭṭhā ya tēṇaṁ. tē muṇāu bhōī.

atthi ihēva vāsē visālā nāma nayarī, tattha amaradattō nāma naraī hotyā, iō ya atīyanavamabhavaṁmi tassa puttō surindadattō nāma ahamāsi tti, jaṇaṇī mē jasōharā, bhajjā ya nayaṇāvali tti. jāba ettiyaṁ jaṁpāmi tāva mōhaṁ gayā rāyadhūyā. āulīhūō pariyaṇō; 'hā kimēyaṁ ti visaṇṇō ya ahayaṁ. parisittā candaṇapāṇiēṇaṁ, laddhā tīē cēyaṇā. maē bhaṇiyaṁ — rāyaputti, kim ēyaṁ ti? tīē bhaṇiyaṁ — vicittayā saṁsārassa maē bhaṇiyaṁ — kahaṁ vicittayā ? tīē bhaṇiyaṁ — jō saccēva ahaṁ jasōharā tassa māyā aīyapari yāē tti sāhiūṇa siddhaṁ kumārasāhiyaṁ niyayacariyaṁ. taō maē bhaṇiyaṁ — rāyaputti, imiṇā vaïyarēṇa virattaṁ cittaṁ bhavacāragāō kumārassa, icchaï khu sō pavvaïuṁ. taō mahārāēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — tā ēvaṁ ṭhiē ki amhēhi kāyavvaṁ ti? tīē bhaṇiyaṁ — vinnēvēhi mahā rāyaṁ. jahā tāya, īisō cēva ēsa saṁsārasahāvō, kassa vā sayaṇṇavināṇassa na virāgaṁ karēi? tā alametya mumiṇayamētavimbhamē paḍibandhēṇa, saṁpāḍēhi kumārassa samīhiya; aṇujāṇāhi ya mamaṁ pi pavvajjaṁ, jō mamaṁpi virattaṁ cēva cittaṁ bhavacāragāō tti. ēyaṁ ca sōūṇa ahō māindajālasarisayā jīvalōyassa tti bhaṇiūṇa paraṁ saṁvēgamuvagō rāyā. bhaṇiyaṁ ca tēṇa — putta, na tuma mama puttō avi ya dhammaniutraṇāō gurū. tā alaṁ amhāṇaṁ pi imiṇā parikilē sēṇaḥ ahaṁ pi pavajāmi tumaē cēva saha pavvajja. ambāhī bhaṇiyaṁ — ajjaütta, juttamēyaṁ kimettha naḍapēḍagōvamē asāsayaṁmi jīvalōē paḍibandhēṇa. taō maē bhaṇiyaṁ — ahāsuhaṁ dēvāṇuppiyā! mā paḍibandhaṁ karēha. taō tāraṇa davāviyaṁ mahādāṇaṁ, kārāviyā sabbāyayaṇēsu pūyā, saṁmāṇiō rāyasatthō, ṭhāviō rajjami khuḍḍa bhāyā mē jasavaddhaṇābhihāṇō. pavvaïō tāō samaṁ maē ambāē viṇayamaīē pahāṇajaṇavaēṇa ya sugihīyanāmadhēyassa bhagavaō indabhū issa samīvē. tā ēvaṁ niyayamēva mē cariyaṁ nivvayakāraṇaṁ ti.

dhaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ, bhayavaṁ sōhaṇaṁ tē nivvēyakāraṇaṁ. kassa vā sahiyayassa annassa vi imaṁ na nivvēyakāraṇa? īisō ēsa saṁsārō. tā āisaü bhayavaṁ, jaṁ maē kāyavvaṁ ti. jasōharēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — sōma, suṇa. dullahā caraṇadhammasāmaggī; jō bhaṇiyaṁ bhayavayā. duvihā khalu jīvā havanti, thāvarā jaṅgamā ya. tattha thōparā puḍhavijalajalaṇamāruyavaṇassaïkāyabhēyabhinnā, jaṅgamā uṇa kimikīḍapayaṅgagōma hisasarahavasahapasayamāiṇō. tattha thāvarattamuvagaō puḍhavāiēsu asaṁkhējāō vaṇassaïṁmi aṇantāō usappiṇisappiṇīō parivasaï jīvō ti. aō thāvarattāō jaṅgamattaṁ dullahaṁ. jaṅgamattaṁ pi pattō samāṇō kimikīḍapayaṅgēsu aṇēyabhēyabhinnēsu āhiṇḍiūṇa tō paścindiyatta pāuṇaï tattha vi kharakarahagōṇamahisuṭṭāiēsu parimbhamiūṇa māṇusattaṇa; tattha vi ya sagajavaṇasavarababbarakāyamuruṇḍōḍa gōḍāiēmu āhiṇḍiūṇa āriyadēsajammā tattha vi ya caṇḍālaḍombilayarayayacammayarasāuṇiyamacchabandhāiēsu āhiṇḍiūṇa īkkhā gāisu kulajamma, tattha vi ya kāṇakuṇṭakhujjapālayamūyandhavahiravāhivigaṁlindiyasarīragēsu paribhamiūṇa nirubadduyaṁ sarīraniphatti, tattha vi ya ḍaṇḍakasasattharajjumāiēhiṁ jīviōvakkamēhi ahāuyāṇuhēvaṇaṁ, tattha vi ya kōhamāṇamāyālōharāgadōsandhayāramōhiōṁ dhammabuddhiṁ, tattha vi ya bahuvihēsu indiyāṇukūlajaṇamaṇōramēsu annāṇipavattiēmu kuhammēsu paribbhamantō jahaṭṭhiyaṁ saccannubhāsiyaṁ siddhisuhekkakulaharaṁ dhamma, tattha vi ya agāibhavaparaṁparabbhatthaasuhabhāvaṇāō asaṁpatta puvvaṁ siddhibahupaḍhamapāhuḍa saddha, saparokkhāraya mahāpurisasēviyaṁ ēgantapasaṁsaṇīyaṁ caraṇadhammaṁ. saṁpattō ya imaṁ dēvāṇuppiyā, acirēṇēva pāvēi jāijarāmaraṇarōyasōya virahiyaṁ paramapayaṁ ti. tā ēyasaṁpāyaṇē karēhi ujjama, kimannēṇa saṁpāiēṇa. asāsayā savvasaṁjōyā, pahavaï viṇijjiyasurāsurō maccū, ēgarukkhanivāsisaüṇatullā bandhavā, vivāyadāruṇō ya visayapamāō ti.

taō ēyamāyaṇṇiūṇa saṁjāyacaraṇapariṇāmēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ dhaṇēṇa. bhayavaṁ aṇuggihīō mhi imiṇā āēsēṇa. tā saṁpāḍēmi ēyaṁ. karēu bhayavaṁ aṇuggahaṁ, jāva nivēiūṇa bhayavaō buttantaṁ ammāpiīṇaṁ pavajāmō pavvaja ti. bhayavayā bhaṇiyaṁ — jahāmuhaṁ, dēvāṇuppiyā, mā paḍibandhaṁ karēhi tti.

taō gaō ammāpiisagāsaṁ dhaṇō. paramasaṁvēgamuvagaēṇa ya tēṇa sāhiō ēsa vuttantō ammāpiīṇaṁ. paḍibuddhā ēē. cintiyaṁ ca tēhiṁ-alaṁ ṇē ēvamasuhapariṇāmē bhavē paḍibandhēṇaṁ, jogyō ya ṇē puttō; tā nikkhiviūṇa imassa bhāraṁ pavajjāmō pavanaṁ ti bhaṇiō dhaṇō. vaccha, paḍiyaggēhi maṇimottiyāiyaṁ sāradavvaṁ pavajjāmō amhē mahāpurisasēviyaṁ pavvaja ti. dhaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — tāya, juttamēya; saṁpattamaṇuyabhāvēṇa pāṇiṇā imaṁ cēva kāyavvaṁ ti. jaṁ puṇa samāi8 tāēṇa, jahā paḍiyaggēhi maṇimottiyāiyaṁ sāradavvaṁ ti ettha kā uṇa sārayā maṇimottiyāidavvassa. kiṁ samatthamiṇaṁ maccuṇō rakkhēuṁ, kiṁ vā na honti ēyappahāvaō jammarāiyā viyārā, kiṁ tīraï imiṇā samatthassa atthivaggassa maṇōrahāpūraṇaṁ kāuṁ, kiṁ vā na paricayaï imaṁ payattarakkhiyaṁ pi khīṇabhāgadhēyaṁ ahōpurisiyāvaṣphārapāraṇaṁ; aṇumannaü tāō majjhaṁ pi attaṇō sarisamaṇuciṭṭhiyaṁ ti. seṭṭhiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ — vaccha, aṇumayaṁ maē. kiṁ puṇa visamā gaī jokṇassaettha khalu duimāī indiyāī, pahavaï saṁsārataruvīyabhūō aṇaṅgō, āyanti ya maṇōharā visaya tti. dhaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — tāya, na khalu avivēgaō annaṁ jovvaṇaṁ ti. aṇāimantā imē jīvā, na ettha paramatthō kōi jōvaṇatthō na vā vuḍḍaō tti. dīsanti avivēgasāmatthō vuḍḍā vi ettha jammē aṇiyattavisayavisāhilāsā agaṇēūṇa lōyavayaṇijja aviyāriūṇa paramatyaṁ appāṇayaṁ viḍambēmāṇa tti hiyayāhiyamalēṇa vi ya davvantarajōēṇa kālapariṇāmamukkilē vi karenti kālaē kēsē, aṅgakaṭṭhiṇayāhēḍaṁ ca sēvanti pārayamaddaṇaṁ, buḍḍhabhāvadōsabhīrū sāhenti ittaraṁ jammakālaṁ, viyārasīlayāē parisakkenti viyaḍayāī, payanti apayaṭṭiyavvē, na pecchanti jhīṇamāuṁ, na cintenti jammantaraṁ ti. abarē uṇa suyambhatthaparalōyamaggā taruṇayā vi ettha jammē vivē yasāmatthēṇa nāūṇa vijjulayāḍōvacañcalaṁ jīyaṁ asāraya visayasuhāṇaṁ vivāyadāruṇayaṁ ca pamāyaceṭṭiyasma maccubhayabhīyā viya hariṇayā uttatthā pāvahēūṇaṁ sēvanti paralōyabandhavaṁ caraṇadhammaṁ ti. tā akāraṇaṁ etya jodhaṇaṁ ti. na ya vivē giṇō viiyasaṁsārasaruvassa duimāī indiyāī. adantēhiṁ ēēhiṁ damiyanbō appā dōgāīē; damiēhi ya etya pasamamuhaṁ paralōē ya bhavaparaṁparāē mokkhanuhaṁ ti jāṇamāṇō kō imē na damēi? aṇakō vi ya agajasaṁkappamūlō paricattēhi aṇajasaṁkappēhiṁ bhāviē bīyarāgadhayaṇē uvaladdhē païsamasuhasarūvē amuya ntāṇa gurupāyamūlaṁ cintayantāṇa paḍivakkhabhāvaṇaṁ kahaṁ pahabaï tti? kiṁ vā maïṇōharattaṁ visayāṇaṁ?. poggalapariṇāmā hi ēē pharisara sarūpagandhasadā vicittapariṇa mā poggalā suhā vi hōūṇa asuhā havanti, asuhā vi ya suhā; kiṁ vā ēēhiṁ attaṇō atyantarabhū ēhi na ēēsiṁ saṁjōō paramatthaō muhahēū, avi ya dukkhahēū; asaṁjōē ya niyasarūvapañcāsannayāē pāṇiṇō paramatthaō muhaṁ ti manamāṇaṁ kēhaṁ āyaḍanti visaya tti. tā kiṁ ēiṇā. tāyapahāvaō cēva mē avigdhaṁ bhavissaï tti.

taō paḍi suyaṁ tēṇa, davā viyaṁ ca ghōsaṇāpuvvayaṁ mahādāṇaṁ, karāviyā aṭṭāhiyā mahimā. taō mahāpurisaïnikkhamaṇavihīē ammāpiīsamēō annēṇaṁ ca pahāṇapariyaṇēṇa pavanō dhaṇō jasōharāyariyasamīvē pavvajjaṁ ti.

aïkkantō kōi kālō. ahijjiyaṁ suttaṁ, abbhatyō kiriyākalāvō, bhāviyāō bhāvaṇāō, vēraggāisayaō pavanō ēgalla vihārapaḍimaṁ. viharamāṇō ya gāmē ēgarāyaṁ nagarē paścarāyavihārēṇaṁ samāgaō kōsambi.

iō ya sō nandaō gōsē tamapecchiūṇa dhagasirisamēō laḍiūṇa jalanihiṁ tīē vayaṇēṇaṁ thīdavvalōhēṇa ya agaṇiūṇa seṭṭhi dhaṇakayāī mukayāī kōsambi āgaō tti. samuddadattanāmaparivattēṇaṁ ca ṭhiō tīē cēva nayarīē. uciyasamaēṇaṁ ca paviṭṭhō bhayavaṁ gōyarē, tattha vi ya nandayagihaṁ. di@ō dhasirī ē pañcabhinnāō ya. cintiyaṁ ca tīē-kahaṁ na vivannō cēva sō samuhamajjhē vi. ahō mē ahannayā, jaṁ puṇō vi ēsō diṭṭhō ti. ahavā tahā karēmi saṁpayaṁ, jahā na puṇō jīvaï tti. etthantaraṁmi aïkkantō jāyaṇāsa maō ti niggaō bhayavaṁ. ahiyayaraṁ sē pōsa pāvanā dhaṇasirī. pañcabhinnāyā ahaṁ, annahā kahaṁ sigdhamēva niggaō ti cintiūṇa pēsiyā cēḍī. halā, kahiṁ puṇa ēsa samagaō ṭhiō tti sammaṁ viyāṇiūṇa lahuṁ mē saṁvāēhi. tīē bhaṇiyaṁ — jaṁ sāmiṇī āṇavēi' tti bhaṇiūṇa niggayā cēḍī, laggā ēyassa mapaō. niyayasamaēṇaṁ ca nigaō bhayavaṁ. na paḍuppanō ya sē jahōciō āhārō, gaō nayaridēvayāpaḍibaddhaṁ ujjāṇantaraṁ. etthantaraṁmi ōgāḍhā carimā, ṭhiō bhayavaṁ kāussaggēṇaṁ. saō kaṁci kālaṁ ciṭṭhiūṇa na ēsa iō gacchaï tti muṇiūṇa āgayā cēḍī, nivēiyaṁ dhaṇasirīē. bhaṇiō tīē nandaō. apaḍusarīrē tumaṁmi uvāiyaṁ bhayavaīē nayaridēvayāē, jahā kiṇhapakvaṭṭhamīē gahiōvayāsakkhāē āyayaṇavāsō kāyavvō tti. aïkkantā ya mē pamāyabhō aṭṭhamī. tō mumiṇayami cōiyā ahaṁ bhayavaīē. pasuttāē cēva ya tumaṁ gōsē kiccakaraṇē niggō tti, aō na sāḍiō pahāē suviṇaō. kō ajja upavāsō. aō ahaṁ tattha gacchāmi tti. saṁpāḍē hi mē bhayāīē pūōvayaraṇaṁ ti. saṁpāḍiyaṁ nandaēṇaṁ. taō kammayaradugāhi ṭiyā saha pubacēḍiyāē gayā dhaṇasirī tamujjāṇaṁ. diṭṭhō tīē tavassī. etthantaraṁmi āgaō sārakabhariēṇa pavahaṇēṇa tamuddēsaṁ sāgaḍiō, bhaggō ya sē akhiō. tō atthamuvagayappāō diṇayarō. na kōi kaḍē geṇḍaï tti dhēnūṇa gōṇē gaō niyayagēhaṁ. taō cintiyaṁ dhaṇasirīē-laṭṭayaṁ jāyaṁ, parahi cetra sārakaḍēhiṁ ḍahissāmi ēvaṁ ti. gayā caṇḍiyāyayagaṁ, kayā dēvayāē pūyā, dinaṁ kammayarāṇaṁ pāṇa bhōyaṇaṁ, pasuttā ēē. tō ēyāiṇī cēva gayā muṇivarasayāsaṁ. annāṇakōhamūḍhāē viiyāī bhayavō sabhīmi kaṭṭhāī, na lakkhiyāiṁ ca jhāṇanōyamugaēṇaṁ bhayavayā. pajjāliō jalaṇō, chikkō bhayavaṁ jalaṇajālāvalōē. saṁjāō sē karuṇapahā ṇataṇēṇa jhāṇajōyasaṁkamō. kiha? cintēi ya sō bhagavaṁ kāussaggami acaliyasahāvō. aṇuyampāgayacittō jaliē jalaṇaṁmi ḍajjhantō.

iha dhannā sappurisā jē navaramaṇuttaraṁ gayā mokkhaṁ

jamhā tē jīvāṇaṁ na kāraṇaṁ kammabandhassa

ēsō u mōhavasaō kōi maṁ pāviūṇa kugaīē. baccihii ahō ka8 kaṭṭhuṁ bahudukkhapaürāē.

ahamēyassa nimittaṁ doggaïgamaṇē nimittavirahēṇa

na hu hōi kajasiddhī bhaṇiyamiṇaṁ lōyanāhēṇa

sōēmi na niyadēhaṁ ēyaṁ sōēmi mōhaparatantaṁ

jiṇavayaṇabāhiramaī dukkhasamudaṁmi nivaḍantaṁ

mōhavasayāṇa ahavā kettiyamēyaṁ kiliṭṭhasattāṇa

ēsō mōhasahāvō dhiratthu saṁsāravāsassa

iya sō suhapariṇāmō tīē viṇivāiō u pāvāē. pannarasasāgarāū uvavannō sukkakappami । iō ya sā dhaṇasirī sasajjhasā viya gayā. caṇḍiyāyayaṇaṁ, pavisamāṇī ya vēiyā cēḍiyāē. bhaṇiyā ca tīē — sāmiṇi, kahiṁ gayā āsi? tīē bhaṇiyaṁ — na kahiṁci, paraṁ addharattasaṁjhāē payāhiṇaṁ kayaṁ ti.

etthantaraṁmi uvaladdhō cēḍiyāē huyāsaṇujōō. kimēyaṁ ti viyappiūṇa pasunā ya ēsā. pahāyā rayaṇī. taō kāūṇa dēvayāē pūrya saṁmāṇiūṇa kammayarē patthiyā dhaṇasirī sagihaṁ. dihō ya panthē vāvannō risī dhaṇasirīē kammayarēhi cēḍiyāē ya. ahō kēṇa ēyaṁ vavasiyaṁ ti jaïpiyaṁ kammayarēhiṁ. na yāṇāmi tti bhaṇiyaṁ dhaṇasirīē. samuppanō cēḍiyāē viyappō. pēsiyā ahaṁ bhayavaō annēsaṇanimittaṁ, niggayā ya ēsā addharatcasamaē, uvaladdhō ya maē tīē cēva vēlāē ujjōyō. tā na yāṇāmō kaha mēyaṁ; mannēmi, jōiyā ahaṁ ēyāē mahāpāva(vā)dēsaṁmi. ēvaṁ cintayantī paviṭṭhā saha dhaṇasirīē gēhaṁ ti.

etthantarami agaō sāgaḍiō. diṭṭhō ya ṇēṇaṁ pi ahimettasēsō muṇivarō. cintiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa-ahō mē adhannayā. paḍivannō ahaṁ kassaï kiliṭṭhasattaspta bhagavaō uvasaggakaraṇēṇa sahāyabhāvaṁ. pāḍiō maē appā doggaīē. tā nivērami ēyaṁ naravaïsta. addhajāmamettē ya vāsarē gaō naravaïsamīvaṁ. nivēiyamaṇēṇa. kuviō rāyā. niuttō ṇēṇa daṇḍavāsiō arē lahu risipāyagaṁ lahēhi tti. niggaō daṇḍavāsiō, gaō caṇḍiyāyayaṇaṁ. pucchiyā ṇēṇa bhōiyā. kō uṇa aja etthaṁ vasiō ti?. tīē bhaṇiyaṁ — na kōi bhuyaṅgappāō, jaï paraṁ samuddadattassa dhariṇī dhaṇasiritti. daṇḍavāsiēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — kiṁ puṇa sē nivāsakajjaṁ?. bhōiyāē bhaṇiyaṁ na yāṇāmō tti. daṇḍavāsiēṇa cintiyaṁ-na ajja aṭṭhamī, na navamī, na caüddasī, tā kiṁ puṇa sē nivāsakāraṇaṁ? pavasaṇanimittaṁ hōjā; taṁ pi aghaḍamāṇayaṁ, jaō kallaṁmi aṅgārayadiṇō, caramapōrisīē ya viṭṭhī āsi viṇivāyajōgō tti. na khalu duṭṭamisthiyā yaṇaṁ mottūṇamēvaṁvihaṁ kammaṁ pi pāraṇa kassaï annassa saṁbhavaï. tā gacchāmi tāva samudadattagēhaṁ, tō cēva uvaladdhī havissaï tti. gaō ēsō, diṭṭhā ya tēṇa duvāradēsabhāyaṁmi cēva cēḍī. pucchiyā ēsā. atthi iha satyavāhapariṇī na vatti? taō sasaṁkhōhaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ cēḍiyāē. kiṁ puṇa tīē pōyaṇaṁ? taō daṇḍavāsiēṇa ahippāyamaṇiikusalēṇa sāsyamiva jaṁpiyaṁ-ā pāvē visumariō tē risivu tantō ti? taō samammaduhattaṇa niyaḍibaliyayāē ya bhaṇiya cēḍiyāē. ajja, gavēsaṇanimittaṁ cēva bhagavaō tē ahaṁ sāmiṇīē pēsiyā, na uṇa annaṁ viyāṇāmi. tabhō daṇḍavāsiēṇa na ettha saṁdēhō, annahā kiṁ gavēsaṇanimittaṁ ti cintiūṇa pucchiyā ēsā. sundari, alaṁ bhayasaṅkāē; kiṁ puṇuddisiya tumaṁ bhayavaśrō gavēsaṇanimittaṁ pēsiyā. cēḍiyāē bhaṇiyaṁ — ajja, sō khu bhayavaṁ kallē taïya pōrisīē bhikkhānimitta iha paviṭṭhō tti, ameṇhiūṇa bhikkhaṁ lahu cēva niggaō. taō niggacchamāṇaṁ pecchiūṇa bhaṇiyā ahaṁ sāmiṇīē, jahā mañjariē, gaccha, kahiṁ puṇa ēsa samaṇō ṭhiō tti jāṇiūṇa lahuṁ saṁvāēhi. taō saṁvāiyaṁ maē, na uṇa kajja viyāṇāmi. daṇḍavāsiēṇa bhaṇiya-rāō tattha gantūṇa kiṁ kayaṁ tassa tīē? cēḍiyāē bhaṇiya-ajja, na kiṁci, na bandiō vi ēsō sāmiṇīē, avi caṇḍiyāē kayā pūya tti. daṇḍavāsiēṇa cintiyaṁ. aō cēva kūradēvayāvihāṇanimittaṁ payāriūṇa pariyaṇaṁ ēyāē vāvāiō havissaï. tā pecchāmi tāva satyavāhapariṇiṁ, taō muhaviyāraō cēva lakkhissāmi tti. gō tīē pāsaṁ, saṁkhuddhā dhaṇasirī, lakkhiō sē bhāvō daṇḍavāsiē, bhaṇiyā ya ṇēṇa. pēsiō ahaṁ mahārāēṇa, [*bābāiō risī,] risivāvāyagaaṇṇēsaṇa nimitta, pabattō ya tassa ghāyayaviyāṇaṇatyaṁ ti. pasuttā ya tumaṁ caṇḍiyāyayaṇē, viyāṇiō ya ēsa vuttantō maē. tā ēhi, naravaï samīvaṁ gacchamha. ēyaṁ ca sōūṇa sasajjhasā bhayapavēviraṅgī nivaḍiyā dharaṇivaḍhē dhaṇasirī. daṇḍavāsiēṇa cintiyaṁ-kayamiṇamimīē, kahamannahā ēvaṁvihaṁ bhayaṁ ti. nibbhacchiyā ēsā. miliō jaṇavaō. ēyaṁ ca vaïyaramāyaṇṇiūṇa jaṇasayāsāō mā ahaṁ ca ēvaṁ cēva gheppissāmi ti cintiūṇa appavisiūṇa niyagēhaṁ duvāraō cēva palāṇō nandaō. nīyā ya ēsā naravaïsamīvaṁ. sāhiō vuttantō naravaïssa. pulaïyā ṇēṇaṁ, cintiyaṁ ca. hanta kahamēyāē āgiīē imaṁ īdisaṁ nisaṁsakammaṁ bhavissaï? pucchiyā ya ṇēṇaṁ ।. aha kiṁnimittaṁ tuma caṇḍiyāyayaṇaṁ gayā āsi? taō ya taṁ vayaṇaṁ sōūṇa saṁkhuddhattaṇēṇaṁ na jaṁpiyamimīē. samuppannā saṅkā rāiṇō. thēvavēlāē puṇō vi pucchiyā. kaō tumaṁ kassa vā dhūya tti? taō sāhiyamimīē. susammanayarāō, ahaṁ puṇṇa bhahassa dhūyā, samuddadattassa ghariṇī dhaṇasirī nāma. gavēsāviō sē bhattā, nōvaladdhō ya. taō accantasuddhasahāvayāē jahāṭhiyaṁ payāparivōlaṇasadamuvvahantēṇaṁ kayāi na taraï rāyapuraō sāhiuṁ paōyaṇaṁ, tā vīsatthā sāhissaï tti kulappavāhapariyāṇaṇanimittaṁ pēsiō rāiṇā puṇṇabhaddamantarēṇa ēyavaïyarapaḍibaddhalēhasaṇāhō lēhavāhaō. rakkhāviyā ēsā, païdiyahaṁ pucchāvaē naravaī, na ya kiṁci jaṁpaï tti. āgaō lēhavāhaō, samappiō tēṇa paḍi lē hō, vāiō rāiṇā. lihiyaṁ ca tasya. atthi mē dhūyā dhaṇasirī kuladūsaṇā ya. tō rāiṇā cintiyaṁ-asaṁsayaṁ kayamiṇamimīē, akajjāyaraṇasīlā cēva ēsā mahāpāvā. ahō sē mūḍhayā, ahō mahāpāvakammāṇuḍhāṇaṁ, ahō kūrahiyayayā, ahō aṇālōiyattaṇaṁ. tahā vi avajjhā itthiya tti dhāḍiyā ṇēṇa sarajāō. gaccha māṇī ya vāsarantē taṇhāchuhābhibhūyā pamuttā gāmadēulasamīvē. ḍakkā bhuyaṅgamēṇaṁ. mahāparikilēsēṇa vimukkā jīviēṇaṁ. uvavannā ya ēsā mariūṇa vālayappabhāē puḍhavīē sattasāgarōvamahiī nāragō tti.

vakkhāyaṁ jaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ dhaṇadhaṇasirimō ya ettha païbhajā

jayavijayā ya sahōyara ettō ēyaṁ pavakkhāmi

atthi ihēva jambuddīvē dīvē mārahē vāsē kāyandī nāma nayarī. jīē samuddōīsā viya paṅkayagāhāulāō pharihāō, païvvayājaṇamaṇō viya parapurisālaṇijjō paügārō, dharaṇiharakandarāī viya sīhabālayasamaddhāsiyāī duvāratōraṇāī, sarayajalaha rukkērā viya dhavalābhōyasundarā pāsāyā. avi ya

diyahapiyavirahakhinnō jīē paōsaṁmi kulabahūsatthō

dūmijaï jālantarapaïḍiēhi miyaṅkakiraṇēhiṁ

guruyaṇaviṇaüjjuttō paṇaīyaṇavacchalō suhābhigamō

dhammatthasāhaṇaraī jīē jaṇō guṇanihī vasaï

tīē akhaṇḍiyaniyabhuyaparakkamō sūratēō nāma rāyā.

jami raṇavāsarēsuṁ visālasaṁmi viyaḍa kaḍayaṁmi

atyadharāharasiharē va sūratēō paḍipphaliō

tassa ya sayalantēurappahāṇā rūvi vva kusumacāvapariṇī līlāvaī nāma bhāriyā. tassa rāiṇō imīē saha visayasuhamaṇu havantassa aïkkantō kōi kālō.

iō ya sō mahāmukkakappavāsī dēvō ahāuyamaṇuvāliūṇa taō cuō samāṇō samuppannō līlāvaīē kucchiṁsi. diṭṭhōya tīē sumiṇayaṁmi tīē cēva rayaṇīē pahāyasamayami saṁpuṇṇamaṇḍalō sayalajaṇamaṇāṇandayārī candimāpasāhiyabhuvaṇabhavaṇō mayalanchaṇō vayaṇē. ṇamuyaraṁ pavisamāṇō tti. pāsiūṇa ya taṁ suhavibuddhāē siṭṭhō tīē jahāvihiṁ daïyassa. harisavasubhinnapulaēṇaṁ bhaṇiyā ya tēṇaṁ sundari, sayalasāmantamiyakō puttō tē bhavissaï. paḍissuyamimīē. paritudvā ēsā. tibaggasaṁpāyaṇasuhamaṇuhavantīē pattō pasūisamaō muhajōēṇaṁ ca pasūyā ēsā. jāō sē dāraō. nivēiō nivvuināmāē rāyadāriyāē naravaïssa. kayaṁ jahōciyamaṇēṇaṁ. aïkkantō māsō. païṭāviyaṁ ca sē nāmaṁ dārayassa jayakumārō tti kahāṇayavisē sēṇa. pattō kumārabhā. gahiō tēṇa rāyakumārō ciyakalākalāvō. puvvabhavabhāvaṇāō ya atthi sē dhammacaraṇami aṇurāō.

annayā ya niggaō āsavāhaṇiyāē. diṭṭhō ya tēṇa candōdayaüjjāṇē ahāśāmuē paēsē diṇayarō viya dittayāē candō viya sōmayāē samuddō viya gambhīrayāē rayaṇarāsī viya mahagghayāē kusumāmēlō viya lāyaṇṇayāē saggō viya rammayāē mokkhō viya nivdhayaṇijjayāē sēyaviyāhivassa jasavammaṇō puttō paḍivanasamaṇaliṅgō sasamayagahiyasārō aṇēyasamaṇapariyaō saṇaṁkumārō nāmāyariō tti. taṁ ca daṭṭaṇa samuppanō kumārassa saṁvēgō. cintiyaṁ ca ṇēṇaṁ. ahō ṇu khalu īisī ēsa saṁsārō, jēṇa ēvaṁvihēhiṁ pi suralōyadullahēhiṁ anattasaṁpajantasayalamagōrahēhiṁ mahāpurisēhiṁ paricattō tti. tā kō puṇa ēsō, kiṁ vā sē paricāyavisēsakāraṇaṁ ti pucchāmi ēyaṁ. gaō tassa samīvaṁ, bandiō tēṇa bhayavaṁ saṇaṁkumārāyariō sēsasāhuṇō ya. dhammalāhiō bhayatrayā sēsasāhūhi ya. uva viṭṭhō gurupāyamūlē. viṇayaraïyakarayalacaliuḍaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ ca ṇēṇaṁ. bhayavaṁ, asārō cē ēsa saṁsārō kassa vā sayaṇṇavinnāṇassa na nivvē. yakāraṇaṁ, tahā vi pāēṇaṁ na bajjhanimittamantarēṇa ēsa saṁjāyaï ti. tā ācikkha bhayavaṁ, kiṁ tē visēsanivvēyakāraṇaṁ, kē vā bhayavanta mavagacchāmi tti. taō bhayakkhā ahō sē vivēgō, ahō vayaṇavināsō, ahijjamāṇē mā alōiyaṁ saṁbhāvaïssaï ti cintiūṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. sōma,suṇa. visēsakāraṇaṁ pi na saṁsāraviyāramantarēṇa, tahāvi viiyasaṁsārasahākssavi bhavaō kōuyaṁ ti kaïliūṇa sāhijaïtti.

suṇiūṇa'ppaniyāṇaṁ mahāvivāgaṁ ca kammapariṇāma

cittagayavijjāharasamaṇasamīvaṁmi nikkhantō

kiha?

atthi ihēva bhārahē bāsē sēyaviyā nāma nayarī. tattha jasavammō rāyā. tassa puttō saṇakumārābhihāṇō ahaṁ. jāyamettassa āiṭṭuṁ ca mē saṁvacchariēṇa vijāharanarindattaṇaṁ ti. aïballahō tāyassa kumārabhāvē tattha ciṭṭhāmi jāva gahiyā kēi takarā vajjhā nijanti. divā ya tē maē vāhiyāliṁ gaēṇaṁ. bhagiyaṁ ca tēhiṁ. dēva, saraṇāgayā amhē, parittāyaü dēvō. taō mōyāviyā maē, ruvā nāyarayā, nivēyamārakkhiēhi mahārāyassa. bhaṇiyaṁ ca tēṇaṁ. jahā kumārō na yāṇaï, tahā gēpiūṇa tē nivēiūṇa nāyarayāṇaṁ vāvāēha tti. vāvāiyā ya takarā, vināō maē ēsa vuttantō. ruṭṭhō mahārāyassa niggaō nayarīō balā pahāṇayariyaṇassa, āgō tāmalitti. muṇiō ēsa vuttantō nannayarisāmiṇā īsāṇacandēṇa. niggaō paccōṇiṁ. bahumaniō ahaṁ tēṇa bhaṇiō ya. vaccha, imaṁ pi tē niyayaṁ cēva rajjatā sundaramaṇucidviya, jamihāgaō si tti. paviṭṭhō nayariṁ, dinō mē kumārāvāsō. aïkkantēsu kaïva yadiṇēsu bhaṇāviō ahaṁ tēṇa. gēhāhi jahicchiyaṁ jīvaṇaṁ ti. na paḍivannaṁ ca taṁ maē.

tō tatthēva ciṭṭhamāṇassa āgaō avivēyaṁgyaviyajaṇamaṇāṇandayārī vasantasamaō, viyambhiō malayamāruō, phulliyāī kāṇa. gujjāṇāī, ucchaliō parahuyāravō, payattāō nayaricaccarīō. ēvaṁvihē ya vasantasamaē niyagēhāō cēva visēsujalanēvacchō vayaṁsaya samēō payaṭṭō kīlānimittaṁ tāmalittītilayabhūyaṁ aṇaṅganandaṇaṁ nāma ujjāṇaṁ. aïyaō rāyamagga, diṭṭhō ya vāyāyaṇanividvāē nayarisāmiṇō īsāṇacandassa dhūyāē vilāsavaīē. bhavarantabbhāsaō samuppanō sē mamōvari aṇurāō, vimukkā vāyāyaṇāsannaṁ vaccama ṇassa tīē mamōvari sahatyagutthā baülamāliyā, lakkhiyā ya mē biiyahiyayabhūēṇa vasubhūiṇā, nivaḍiyā mē kaṇṭhadēsabhāē। pulaïyaṁ maē uvarihattaṁ, diṭṭhaṁ sē vāyāyaṇaviṇiggayaṁ vayaṇakamalaṁ, samuppannō mē hiyayaṁmi pariōsō, pecchamāṇīē ya nimiyā sā maē siṇēhabahumāṇaṁ kaṇṭhadēsē. etthantaraṁmi pariōsavisāyagambhiṇaṁ īsivihasiyasaṇāī nīsasiyamimīē. aïkantō ayaṁ tamuddēsaṁ dēha mettēṇaṁ na puṇa cittēṇa, pattō aṇaṅganandaṇaṁ ujjāṇaṁ. tattha vi ya vayaṁsayāṇurōhēṇa vicittakīlāpavattō vi dēhaceṭṭāē taṁ cēva payaï sundaraṁ tīē vayaṇakamalaṁ cintayantō ṭhiō kaṁci kālaṁ. uciyasamaēṇaṁ ca paviṭṭhō rāmalittiṁ. kayaṁ uciyakaraṇijjaṁ. aïkkantō vāsarō, samāgayā rayaṇī. saṁmāṇiūṇa siraṁ mē dukkhēi tti lahuṁ cēva visajjiyā vayaṁsayā. gaō vāsabhavaṇaṁ, ṭhiō sayaṇijjē. tattha ya aṇācikṣaṇīyaṁ asaṁbhāvaṇīyaṁ aṇaṇuhūyapuvvaṁ tahāvihaṁ dukkhāisayamaṇuhavantassa khaṇamettaladdhaniddassa aïkkantā rayaṇī. kayaṁ gōsakiccaṁ. samāgayā vasubhūippamuhā vayaṁsayā. viiṇṇāī taṁbōlāi. gayā amhē kīlānimittaṁ tamēva bhavaṇujjāṇaṁ. pavattā kīliuṁ vicittakīlāhiṁ. sunnahiyayattaṇāō ya lakkhiō mē cittami mayaṇaviyārō vamubhūiṇā. vittē, ya kīlāvaïyarē māhavīlayā maṇḍavaṁmi ciṭṭhamāṇō bhaṇiō ahaṁ tēṇa. bhō vayassa, aha kiṁ puṇa tumaṁ ajja vāsaraṁmiva sasī vicchāō dīsasi, khaṇaṁ ca jhāṇagaō viya muṇī sayalaceṭṭhuṁ nirumbhasi, taō ya laddhalāhō viya jūyārō pariōsamunbahasi tti. taō maē asamikkhiyakāriyāē mayaṇassa bīyahiyayabhūyassa vi gr̥hamāṇēṇa niyayamāyāraṁ jaṁpiyaṁ na kiṁci lakkhēmi tti. vasubhūiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ ahaṁ lakkhēmi. maē bhaṇiyaṁ kiṁ tayaṁ. vasubhūiṇā bhaṇiya-ārōviō tē baülamāliyānihēṇa rāyadāriyāē garuyacintābhārō, viddhō ya tīē diṭṭhipāyacchalēṇa mayaṇasaradhōraṇīhiṁ. tajjaṇiō ēsa viyārō. annahā kahamayaṇḍammi cēva paripaṇḍuraṁ tē vayaṇaṁ, aladdhaniddāsuhāiṁ ca tāratambāī lōya ṇāī, hiyayāyāsakāriṇō dīhadīhā nīsāsa tti. tā mā saṁtappa; icchaï sā taē saha samāgama, pēsiyā ya tīē siṇēhabahumāṇaṁ baü lamāliyā dūī. annaṁ ca-avaḍiō vihī avassabhaviyadhvēsuṁ, ghaḍēi ēsa ahimuhīhūō niyamēṇa annadīvagayaṁ pi pāṇiṇaṁ. karēmi ahaṁ ettha kaṁci uvāyaṁ ti. paḍissuya maē. kaō tēṇa vilāsavaïdhāvidhūyāē aṇaṅgasundarīē saha pasaṅgō. ahigamaṇīyapurisa guṇajōgaō laggā ya sā tassa.

aïkkantā kēivi diyahā. taō na kayamiha kiṁci vasubhūiṇā, na pahavaï vā sē maïgōyarō ti cintayantō mayaṇaparāyattayāē gaō sayaṇijja. tattha puṇa mucchiō viya mūḍhō viya maïttō viya mūō viya bhīō viya gahagahiō viya vēvamāṇahiyō appa havantō indiyāṇaṁ ciṭṭhāmi jāva thēvavēlāē cēva pahaṭṭavayaṇapaṅkō āgaō vasubhūī. vayaṇaviyārēṇa lakkhiyaṁ maē, jahā kayamaṇēṇa paōyaṇaṁ bhavissaï tti. bhaṇiyaṁ ca tēṇa. bhō vayassa, paricaya visāyaṁ, aṅgīkarēhi pamōya, saṁpannaṁ tē samīhiyaṁ ti. maē bhaṇiyaṁ kahaṁ viya. tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ — suṇa

gaō ahamiō aja aṇaṅgasundarīgēhaṁ. diṭṭhā maē pabvāyatrayaṇapaṅkayā aṇaṅgasundarī, bhaṇiyā ya. sundari, kiṁ puṇa tē unvēya kāraṇaṁ; ācikkha, jaï akahaṇīyaṁ na hōi. tīē bhaṇiyaṁ—

kaha taṁmi nivvarijjaï dukkhaṁ keṇḍujjuēṇa hiyaēṇa

adāē paḍibimba jaṁmi dukkhaṁ na saṁkamaï

maē bhaṇiyaṁ — sundari!

viralā jāṇanti guṇā viralā japaïnti laliyakabāī

sāmannadhaṇā viralā paradukkhē dukkhiyā viralā

tahāvi atthi mē tuha maṇōrahasaṁpāyaṇecchā. tīē bhaṇiyaṁ — jaï ēvaṁ, tā suṇa. atthi mahārāyadhr̥yā vilāsavaī nāma kannayā. sā mē bhinnadēhā vi attāṇanivisēsā sāmisālī vi asāmisālisīlā. tīē apacchimā avasthā vaṭṭaï. taō maē bhaṇiyaṁ. kiṁ puṇa ettha kāraṇaṁ. tīē bhaṇiya mayaṇaviyārō. taō maē bhaṇiyaṁ — kaṇa puṇa bhayavayā vīyarāgēga viya khaṇḍiyaṁ viṇijjiyasurāsurassa raïmaṇāṇandayāriṇō pañcabāṇassa sāsaṇaṁ. tīē bhaṇiyaṁ — na yāṇāmi khaṇḍiyaṁ na khaṇḍiyaṁ ti. ettiō uṇa mē saṁtāvō, jaṁ sē maṇō rahavisaō na najjaï. maē bhaṇiyaṁ kahaṁ viya. tīē bhaṇiyaṁ — muṇa. pabattē mayaṇamahūsa niggayāsu nayaracaccarīsu caccariyāmettasaṁga yāē dihrō imīē-aṇumāṇaō viyāṇāmi-muttimantō viya kusumāuhō kōvi juvāṇaō. annahā kēhaṁ īisassa kanayārayaṇassa aṇīisē varē ahilāsō ti. na patthaï paṅkayasirī haḍhavaṇāī. mukkā ya tīē tassuvari sahatthagutthā baülamāliyā, nivaḍiyā sē imī vi ya kaṇṭha dēsē maṇōrahēhiṁ. taō uparihuttamavalōiūṇa nimiyā ya tēṇaṁ annajaṇasaṁpāyabhīruyayāē ghettūṇa tīē hiyayaṁ piba kaṇṭhami. aïkkantō ya sō. vilāvasaī vi ya tayappabhūimēva paricattaniyayavāvārā tahā kayā vammahēṇa, jahā avikkhiuṁ pi na pārīyaï tti. vināō ya ēsa vuttantō maēm̐ babbariyāsayīsāō, puṇō rāyadhūyāō tti. samāsāsiyā sā maē. sāmiṇi, alaṁ visāēṇaṁ, saṁvāēmi sāmiṇi hiyayavallahēṇa. na khaṇḍi jaï kōmuī mayalacchaṇēṇaṁ ti. maṇiūṇa paṇihilōyaṇēhiṁ nirūviō sō, na uṇa uvaladdhōti. taō ya sā ajja mayaṇaviyāraō cēva asaṁpāiyapaōyaṇaṁ maṁ avagacchiūṇa nibbharukkaṇṭhā parāhīṇahiyayā saṁkantadūsahasarīrasaṁtāvaṁ pariccaïya sē yaṇīyaṁ avalambiya sahīyaṇaṁ uvaritalamārūḍhā. dakkhiṇāṇilēṇa ya savisēsapajalijantamayaṇāṇalā uṇhaṁ ca dīhaṁ ca nīsasiya taṁ cēva rāyama gudēsaṁ pulōiuṁ payattā. pavvāliyā ya sē ahiyayaraṁ bāhasalilēṇa diṭṭhī. taō sahasā cēva jhaṇajhaṇāravamuhalamaṇivalayaṁ vihuṇiya kara pallavaṁ avahatthiya aṅgasaṁdhārayaṁ sahiyāyaṇaṁ mōhamuvagaya tti. taō sasaṁbhantō uḍhiō ahaṁ, bhaṇiyō ya vasubhūī. vayassa, kahiṁ sā hiyayāṇandayāriṇī, daṁsēhi mē, alaṁ tīē accāhiē jīviēṇa. vasubhūiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ — dēva, vattaṁ khu ēyaṁ, kahāvasāṇaṁ pi tāva hiyayā ṇandakārayaṁ cēva, taṁ suṇaü dēvō. taō lajjāvaṇayavayaṇakamalaṁ īsi vihasiūṇa ṇuvannō ahaṁ. vasubhūiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ — taō, dēva, nimiyā sahiyāhiṁ ucchaṅgasayaṇijjē,vījiyā maē bāhasalilasittēṇa tāliyaṇṭēṇa, dinnaṁ ca sē sahāvasīyalavacchasthalaṁmi candaṇaṁ,uvaṇīō muṇā liyāvalayahārō, laddhā kahavi tīē cēyaṇā, ummilliyaṁ aladdhanidākkhēyapāḍalaṁ lōyaṇajuyaṁ. maē bhaṇiyaṁ — sāmiṇi, kiṁ tē bāhaï tti. taō ukaḍayāē mayaṇaviyārassa agavē kkhiūṇa sahiyaṇaṁ avvattaṁ cēva jaṁpiyaṁ tīē tassa cēvādasaṇaṁ ti. taō maē tīē sāhāraṇatthaṁ aliyaṁ cēva jaṁpiyaṁ. sāmiṇi, dhīrā hōhi, uvaladdhā tassa maē paüttī, vinavissaṁ, sāmiṇi, tamantarēṇa. tō vihasiya tīē, dinnaṁ ca mē kaḍisuttayaṁ. etthantaraṁmi samāgayā sē jaṇaṇī, bhaṇiyā ya tīē. jāya vilāsavaï, sārēhi vīṇaṁ, jō āṇattaṁ mahārāēṇa ajja taē vīṇāviṇōō kāyayō tti. taō guruyaṇalajjāluyāē jaṁpiyaṁ tīē. jaï ēvaṁ, tā lahuṁ vīṇāyariṇiṁ sadēhi. sadiyā vīṇāya riṇī. etthantaraṁmi kiṁkāyabvamūḍhā avisajjiyā cēva rāyadhūyāē niggayā rāyagēhāō, āgayā sabhavaṇaṁ, nirūviō visēsēṇa, na laddhā ya tassa paüttī. tā kiṁ puṇa ahaṁ sāmiṇīē vinavissaṁ ti samaddhāsiyā cintāpisāiyāē. tā ēyaṁ mē uvvēyakāraṇaṁ ti. maē bhaṇiyaṁ — paricaya cintāpisāiyaṁ, jāṇāmi ahayaṁ taṁ juvāṇayaṁ. tā tahā karisaṁ, jahā tē sāmiṇī nivvuyā bhavissaha tti. aṇaṅga sundarīē bhaṇiyaṁ — sāhēhi tāva, kahaṁ tumaṁ jāṇāsi, kō vā sō juvāṇaō. maē bhaṇiyaṁ — appāṇanivvisēsō vayaṁsaō, ahavā sāmi sālō, aō viyāṇāmi. sō puṇō sēyaviyāhivassa mahārāyajasavammaṇō puttō sarṇakumārō nāma. tassa kīlānimittaṁ aṇaṅganandaṇaṁ patthiyassa pēsiyā tīē baülamāliyā, bahumanniyā ya tēṇaṁ. aṇaṅgasundarīē bhaṇiyaṁ — jaï ēvaṁ, tā alaṁ tē sāmisālēṇa, jō ēvaṁ pi sāmiṇī hiyayaṁ viyāṇiya nirujjamō ciṭṭhaï. maē bhaṇiyaṁ. na nirujamō, kiṁtu uvāyaṁ vicintēi kahaṁ puga aṇindiēṇa vihiṇā ēsā pāviyaca tti. aṇaṅgasundarīē bhaṇiyaṁ — samāṇarūvāṇurāyakulakannayāharaṇaṁ pi aṇindiō cēva vihī. maē bhaṇiyaṁ. atthi ēvaṁ, kiṁtu añcantasiṇēhavantō mahārāōsaṇaṁkumārassa, jaō apaḍihaō savvatthāmēsu gaïpasarō, uvannatthaṁ ca tassa sabahumāṇaṁ mahārāpaṇa jīvaṇaṁ. tā kayāi pathiō cēva dēissaï tti. tā kiṁ ēiṇā. nivēēhi tāva ēvaṁ vuttantaṁ sāmiṇīē, cintēhi ya uvāyaṁ, kahaṁ puṇa ēyāṇaṁ dasaṇaṁ saṁjāissara ti. aṇaṅgasundarīē bhaṇiyaṁ — nivēēmi ēyaṁ. dasaṇōvāō puṇē, nēissaṁ ahaṁ sāmiṇi mandirujjāṇaṁ, tumaṁ pi ya kumāraṁ ghettūṇa tahiṁ cēva sannihiō havejjāsi ti. paḍissuyaṁ ca taṁ maē. saṁparya tumaṁ pamāṇaṁ ti. taō ēyaṁ sōūṇa mōhadōsēṇāraṁ savvasokkhāṇaṁ piva gaō pāraṁ, pīīē vi yaṁ pāviō pīī, dhiīē va avalambiō dhiī ūsavēṇa viya kaō mē ūsavō. dinnaṁ vasubhūiṇō kaḍayajuyalaṁ. bhaṇiō ya ēsō. vayaṁsa, na khu ahaṁ bhavantamappamāṇīkarēmi tti. gayā amhē tamujjāṇaṁ. divā ya tattha rukkhasatyavikōviyapurisasaṁpāiyāgālaḍōhalapasyaviyārōvalakkhijjamāṇasarūvā savvē uū. paḍhamaṁ cēva kusu miyatilayāsōyasinduvāramañjarīmaṇaharō vasantō, tō vi ya viyasiyasurahimalliyākusumasōhiō gimhō, taō kayambakusumagandhā ṇuvāsiō ghaṇasamaō, tayō gaïndamayagandhāṇuvāmiyasattacchayakusumasamuggamō sarayakālō, taō paripicarapiyaṅgumañjarīkayāvayaṁmō hēmantō, taō viyambhiuddāmakunda kusumaharahāsadhavalō sisirasamō tti. taō taṁ daṭṭaṇa cintiyaṁ maē. ahō maṇussalōyadullahā iyaṁ ujjāṇariddhī. tahiṁ ca jāva thēvakālaṁ ciṭṭhāmi, tāva sā āgayā aṇaṅgasundarī. bhaṇiyaṁ ca tīē. kumāra, āsaṇapariggahēṇa alaṁkarēhi ēyaṁ candaṇalayāharayaṁ. taō maē pulōiyaṁ vasubhūivayaṇaṁ. bhaṇiyaṁ ca tēṇa jaṁ ēsā bhaṇaï ti. taō amhē gayā candaṇalayāharayaṁ. diṭṭhā ya tattha jalaharōyaraviṇiggayarayaṇiyarapaṇaïṇi vya tārāyaṇaparivuḍā rāyahaṁsi vva kalahaṁsiparivārā samuddavēla vva thūlamuttāhalaka liyasalāyaṇṇapaōharā, aṇaṅgadhariṇi vva uulacchiparigayā cittāṇukūlāṇurattaniuṇasahiyaṇamajhagayā lahuiyarattakamala pōhē hiṁ kummunnaēhiṁ ghaṇasaralakōmalaṅgulivihūliēhiṁ alavikha jamāṇasirājālamaṇaharēhiṁ nimmalanahamaūhōhapaḍi baddhapariēsamaṇḍalē hiṁ aladdha hiyayapavēsēṇaṁ pitra puvyasēvāsaṁpāyaṇōvāyacaürēṇaṁ jāvayarāēṇaṁ paḍivannaēhiṁ calaṇēhiṁ, calaṇāṇurūvāhiṁ cēva pasannasukumālāhiṁ akkha kuṅkumarāyapiñjarāhiṁ janiyāhiṁ, mayaṇa namalatōṇīrakaraṇillēṇaṁ païyāmathōrēṇaṁ ca nirantarēṇaṁ ca ūrujuyalēṇaṁ, uttattakaṇayanimmiēṇē va pīvarēṇaṁ ghaḍiyavimalamaṇimēhalāharaṇēṇaṁ agaṅgabhavaṇēṇaṁ piva visthiṇṇēṇaṁ niyambabimbēṇaṁ, sayala tēlōkalāyaṇṇasalilanivāṇēṇaṁ piva sahāvagambhīrēṇaṁ nāhimaṇḍalēgaṁ, kusumāuhacāvalē hāvinbhamāē taṇumajjhapasāhaṇāēṁ rōmarāīē, jovvaṇāruhaṇasōvāṇabhūpativalisaṇā hēṇaṁ majjhēṇa, īsānaḍiēṇa lāyaṇṇāisayalampaḍēṇaṁ piva mayaṇēṇa saï samāliṅgiēhiṁ pariṇāhubhijjantaēhi apōharēhiṁ pōharē hiṁ, supaïḍiyāhi bāhulayāhiṁ, asōyapallavavibbhamēhiṁ supasatthalēhālaṁkiēhi māṇikapajjuttakaṇayakaḍayasaṇāhēhiṁ aṇuciyakammākarēhi (payāma) anupūrvasthalēna ca nirantarēṇa ca ūruyugalēna, uttaptakanakanirmitēnēva pīvarēṇa ghaṭṭhitavimalamaṇimekhalābharaṇēna anaṅgabhavanēnēva vistī karēhiṁ, parimaṇḍalāē mahallamuttāhalamālāparigayāē tilēhālaṁkiyāē sirōharāē,bandhūyakaraṇiralēṇaṁ sahāvāruṇēṇa aharēṇa, viṇijjiya kundakusumasōhē hi viṇintamaūhajālasōhillēhiṁ dasaṇēhiṁ, uttuṅgēṇaṁ sahāvaramaṇijjēṇaṁ nāsāvaṁgapaṇa, kantipaḍipūriēhiṁ viṇijjiyacaṁda vimbasōhēhiṁ asōyapallavāvayaṁsapēḍiyapaḍimēḍiṁgaṇḍapāsēhiṁ, viuddhanavakuvalayadalakantisukumālēhiṁ supamhalēhiṁ damaṇagōyarāvaḍiyaja ṇamaṇāṇandaṇēhi nayaṇēhiṁ, gahakallōladaragahiyamiyaṅkamaṇḍalanihēṇa susiṇiddhālayāulēṇaṁ niḍālabaṭṭēṇaṁ, vayaṇāṇurūvēhiṁ jaccatavaṇija taïlavattiyāsaṇā hēhiṁ appiyayayaṇāsavaṇēhiṁ savaṇēhiṁ, jiṇaśāṇāṇalaḍajjhantamayaṇadhūmuggārēṇaṁ pica kasiṇakuḍilēṇaṁ mālaīkusumada ma surahigandhāyaḍiyabhamantamuhalabhamarōlipariyaēṇaṁ kēsakalāvēṇaṁ, tihuyaṇekkasundaraparamāṇurviṇimmiyaṁ piva apaḍirūvaṁ rūbasōhaṁ vahantī, īsivihārāyāraddhasahiyaṇakahāpabandhā vimatramāṇikapajjuttakaṇayāsaṇōvaviṭhṭhā vilāsabaï tti. taō taṁ daṭṭhūṇa mōhatimiradōsēṇa aṇirūviūṇa paramatthaṁ akkhippantahiyayaṁ phurantabāhujuyalō paricintiuṁ payattō. kiha—

ōhāmiyasurasundarikhvāisayaṁ viṇimmiyaṁ darcha

vihiṇō vi nr̥ṇamēyaṁ bahumāṇō āsi appāṇē

ēsā cāvāyaḍaṇaviyalaṁ muṇiūṇa vammahaṁ vihiṇā

jaṇahiyayabhēyaṇasahā viṇimmiyā hatthabhalli vva

etthantaraṁmi samāgaōṁ sē ahaṁ dasaṇagōyaraṁ, pulaïō ya tīē sasiṇēhamārata sagadhavalēhiṁ calantatāraēhiṁ nayaṇēhiṁ sasajjhasā viya aṇācikkhaṇīyaṁ apatthantaramaṇuhavantī samuḍhaiyā ēsā. taō bhaṁgiya aṇaṁgasundarīē susāgayaṁ mayaraddhayassa,] maē vi bhaṇiyaṁ sāgayaṁ vasantalacchīē. sundari, alaṁ saṁbhamēṇa. etthantaraṁmi taṁ cēvāsaṇamukdaṁsiūṇa bhaṇiyaṁ aṇaṅgasundarīē. uvavisaü kumārō. vilāsavaïāsaṇaṁ ti bahumāṇēṇa uvaviṭhṭhō ahaṁ. uvaṇīyaṁ ca mē kaladhōyamayataliyāē tambōlaṁ. taṁ ca ghettūṇa bhaṇiyaṁ maē. uvavisaü rāyadhūya tti. uvaviṭṭhā ēsā. ṭhiyāṇi kaṁci vēlaṁ.

etthantaraṁmi samāgaō mittabhūī nāma kannantēuramahallaō. paṇamiō ahaṁ tēṇa, maē vi ya ahivāiō. bhaṇiyaṁ ca tēṇa. vilāsavaï, mahārāō āṇavēi. visumariyā tē vīṇāpaōgā. kuviō ahaṁ kallaṁ. tā lahuṁ sumarēhi ajja puṇa taē vīṇā vāiyā tti. taō jaṁ mahārāō āṇavēi ti bhaṇiūṇa nigagayā lahuṁ.

aha kancuiyasamēyā saṇēhamārattakasaṇadhavalē hiṁ. nayaṇēhiṁ apecchannaṁ pecchantī valiyatārēhiṁ.

mantharagaīē viyalantahatthasaṁruddhamuhalamaṇirasaṇā

mayaṇasaraghāyabhīya vva vēvamāṇī gayā bhavaṇaṁ

tō vasubhūiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ. vayassa, ēhi gacchāmō, viṇā vilāsavaīē kimiha ciṭṭhiēṇaṁ ti. niggayā amhē, diṭṭhā ya ujjāṇa duvāradēsabhāē aṇabaïnāmāē rāyapattīē. aphajjāyaraṇakulaharattaṇēṇa mayaṇassa samuppanō tīē vi mamōvari ahilāsō. gayā amhē sagiha. vāsarantami ya ghettūṇa vijāharabandhagutthāī sinduvārakusumāī vilēvaṇasaṇāhaṁ ca tambōlamāgayā aṇaṅgasundarī. bhaṇiyaṁ ca tīē. kumāra, vinattaṁ sāmiṇīē ēyāī sinduvārakusumāī avassaṁ ajjaüttēṇaṁ parihiyabvāī ti. taō saṁvāiyaṁ cēva imiṇā uvannāsēṇa mēṁ samīhiyaṁ ti cintiūṇa, jaṁ dēvī āṇavēi tti bhaṇiūṇa gahiyaṁ kusumadāma, viraïyaṁ uttimaṅgē, vilittō vi piyayamābahum̐māṇēṇa puṇō vilittō appā; mottūṇamāvīlaṁ samāṇiyaṁ tambōlaṁ. etthantaraṁmi bhaṇiyaṁ vasubhūiṇā. aṇaṅgasundari, diṭṭhaṁ taē piyavayaṁsassa viṇīyattaṇaṁ. tīē bhaṇiyaṁ. na ēvaṁ vihēsu mahāpurisēsu viṇaō acchērayaṁ ti. taō kaṁci vēlaṁ gamēūṇa payaṭṭā aṇaṅgasundarī. dinnō ya sē mara bhuvagasārō kaṇṭhaō. taō pahāvayaṇakamalā saṁpannā sāmiṇīē maṇōraha ti cinta yantī bhaṇiyā ya ēsā. sundari, sayaṁ tē gēhamēyaṁ, tā ihāgamaṇēṇa khēō na kāyavvō ti. taō jaṁ kumārō āṇavēi tti bhaṇiūṇa gayā aṇaṅgasundarī. pavaḍḍamāṇāṇurāyāṇa aïkantā kaïvi diyahā.
