maggalaggassa ya na pahavanti tti. rukkhā ya ettha ēgē maṇōharā siṇiddhapattalā surahikusumasōhiyā sīyalacchāyā, annē ya parisaḍiyapaṇḍupattā kusumaphalavivijjiyā amaṇōharā ya. tattha paḍhamāṇaṁ chāyā vi viṇāsakāraṇaṁ, ki puṇa pari bhōgō tti. na tēsu vīsamiyabvaṁ, iyarēsa muhuttamettaṁ vīsamiyatvaṁ ti. maṇōhararūvadhāriṇō mahuravayaṇā ya etya maggataḍaṭṭhiyā bahavē purisā hakkārenti ēha bhō satthiyā ēha, ēvaṁ pi taṁ puraṁ gammaï ti. tēsi vayaṇaṁ na sōyavvaṁ. susatthiyā uṇa muhuttamettamavi kālaṁ khaṇamavi na mottavvā. ēyāiṇō niyamā bhayaṁ. durantō ya thēvō davaggī appamattēhiṁ ulhavēyavvō, aṇolhavijjantō niyamēṇa ḍahaï । puṇō ya duggō uccō ya pavvaō, sō vi uvaüttēhiṁ lajiyavvō; alaṅkaṇē ya niyamā marijjaï. tō vi ya mahantī aguvilagabbarā vaṁsakuḍaṅgī, sā vi ya duyayaraṁ bōlē yayā. saṁṭhiyāṇaṁ ca tīē samīvē aṇēē uvaddavā. tō aṇantaraṁ ca lahuō khaḍḍōlaō. tassa samīcē maṇōrahō nāma bambhaṇō niccamēva parivasaï. sō bhaṇaï. bhō bhō satthiyā, maṇāyaṁ pūrēha ēyaṁ, tō gamissaha tti. tassa nō sōyavvaṁ vayaṇaṁ, avagaṇiūṇa gantavvaṁ. na khalu sō pūriyanbō. sō khu pūrijjamāṇō mahallayarō havaï, panthāō ya paṁḍibhaṁsaï. phalāṇi ya ṇaṁ ettha divyāṇi paścappayārāṇi nettāisuhayarāṇi kiṁpāgāṇaṁ, na pekkhiyabāṇi, na vā bhottavāṇi. bāvīsaṁ ca ṇaṁ ettha ghōrā mahākāyā karālā pisāyā khaṇaṁ khaṇamahiddavanti. tē vi ya ṇa gaṇēyavvā. bhattapāṇaṁ ca ettha vibhāgaō paribhujjamāṇamaīva virasaṁ dullahaṁ ca havaï tti (vivāgaō uṇamaīva sarasaṁ jahā bālassa ya jabābhēsajaṁ). tattha na visāiṇā hōyavvaṁ. apayāṇayaṁ na kāyavvaṁ ti, rayaṇīē vi jāmaduyaṁ niyamēṇa vahiyaccha. ēvaṁ ca gacchamāṇēhiṁ dēvāṇuppiyā, khippamēvāḍavī lachi jaï, laṅghittā ya tamēgantadōgacca vajjiyaṁ nivvuipuraṁ pāvijaï tti. tattha na honti puṇō kēi kilēsōbaddavā. ēsa dihantō, imō uṇa uvaṇaō. ettha sattha vāhō tilōyacintāmaṇī surāsurapūiō arahā. ghōsaṇaṁ tu akhēvaṇivikkhēvaṇisaṁvēyaṇinivvēyaṇilakkhaṇā dhammakahā. satthiyā ya saṁsārāḍavilakṣaṇēṇa nivvuipurapatthiyā jīvā. aḍavī puṇa nārayatiriyamaṇuyadēvagaïlakkhaṇō saṁsārō. ujjayapanthō sāhudhammō; maṇāgamaṇujjuō sāvayadhammō, sō vi pajjantē sāhudhammaphalō cēva icchijjaï. na ya bhāvaō apaḍivanasāhudhammā saṁsārāḍavi laḍḍenti. icchiyapuraṁ puṇa jammajarāmaraṇarōgasōgāiubaddavarahiyaṁ sivapuraṁ. vagdhasiṁghā ya mokkhavigdhahēyavō rāgadōsā. abhibhūyā ya ṇēhiṁ pāṇiṇō pecchamāṇā vi māindajālasarisaṁ jīvalōyaṁ na caenti paḍivajiuṁ paramapayasāhayaṁ samaṇattaṇaṁ. pavanavayāṇaṁ pi ya ēē asaṁpattakēvalabhāvāṇaṁ na muyanti maggaṁ, vimukkajiṇavayaṇamaggē ahihavanti jīvē na uṇa iyarē tti. maṇōramarukkhacchāyāō sapaḍibandhāō thīpasupaṇḍayasaṁsattāō vasahīō. parisaṁḍiyapaṇḍupattāō ya aṇavajjavasahīō. mamgataḍatthā ya hakkāraṇapurisā paralōyaviruddhōvaēsadā yagā pāsatthāī akallāṇamittā, susatthiyā uṇa aṭṭhārasasīlaṅgasahassadhāriṇō samaṇā. davaggī kōhō, patraō māṇō, sakuḍaṅgī māyā, khaḍḍōlaō lōhō. maṇōrahabambhaṇō icchāvisēsō, thēvapūraṇē vi imasma apajjavasāṇagamaṇaṁ. kiṁpāgaphalāṇi sadādaō visayā sīoṇhakhuhāpivāsāiyā ya bāvīsaṁ parīsahā pisāyā. virasaṁ bhōyaṇaṁ aṇavajja mahuyaravittīē ēsaṇijja. apayāṇayaṁ sayā appa māō. jāmaduyagamaṇaṁ ca sajjhāyakaraṇaṁ. ēvaṁ ca vaṭṭamāṇēhi dēvāṇuppiyā, sigdhamēva bhavāḍavī laḍijaï, lavitā ya tamēgantamaṇā bāhaṁ sivapuraṁ pāvijjaï tti.

taō saṁjāyasammattadēsaviraïpariṇāmēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ jayakumārēṇa. bhayavaṁ, ēvamēyaṁ na annahā. gahiyāī aṇuvbayāī. paviṭṭhō nayariṁ । kaō sē piuṇā juvarajjāhisēō. papattō sēviuṁ bhayavantaṁ saṇaṁkumārāyariyaṁ. vittō māsakappō. gō bhayavaṁ.

etthantaraṁmi sō dhaṇasirījīvanāraō taō narayāō upaṭṭiūga saṁsāramāhiṇḍiya aṇantarajammami ya tahāvihaṁ kapi akāma nijjaraṁ pāviūṇa maō samāṇō samuppannō imassa cēva jayakumārassa bhāuyattāē ti. jāō kālakamēṇa, païṭāviyaṁ ca sē nāma vijaō tti. pattō kumārabhāvaṁ. vallahō jayakumārassa, aballahō jayakumārō vijayassa. ēvaṁ ca aïkantō kōi kālō.

annayā asārayāē saṁsārassa niravekkhayāē maccugō vicittayāē kammapariṇāmassa sapajjavasāṇayāē jammaṇō pañcattamuvagaō rāyā. ahisittōrajaṁmi sāmantamaṇḍalēṇa jayakumārō. vija bhōya pōsēṇa païlāyamāṇō rajjaḍhaiī kāūṇa baddhō rajacintaēhiṁ. jāō ya sē jaṇaṇīē sōō. annayā ya atyāiyāmaṇḍavagayassa rāiṇō āgayā samubīī viya muttāniyaravāhiṇī pāusasirī viya samunna yapaōharā malayamēhalā viya candaṇagandhavāhiṇī vasantalacchī viya reṭrapattatilayāharagā paḍihārī. tīē ya duhāvirikkasaṁghaḍiyakama lasaṁpuḍēṇa viya matthayāvathiēṇa añjaliṇā paṇāmaṁ kāūṇa viṇatō rāyā. dēva, ēsā khu tē jaṇaṇī kēṇāvi kāraṇēṇa dēvadaṁsaṇamahi lasantī paḍihārabhūmīē ciṭṭhaï. taō sasaṁbhamaṁ ciṭṭhaha tubbhē tti bhaṇantō rāyasaṁghāyaṁ uḍhiō rāyā. gaō duvārabhāgaṁ. paṇamiyā jaṇaṇī bhaṇiyā ya. amba, kiṁ na sadāviō ahaṁ, kiṁ vā āgamaṇapaōyaṇaṁ. taō parujhyā ēsā. bhaṇiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa. amba, kiṁni mittamimaṁ. tīē bhaṇiya. jāya, suyasiṇēhasaṁvaïḍḍiyasōyāṇalaviyārō tā dēhi mē puttajīviyaṁ. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ. amba, kuō bhayaṁ kumārassa. tīē bhaṇiyaṁ. jāya, ṭhiī ēsā payāparivālaṇujjayāṇaṁ naravaīṇaṁ, jaṁ paḍivakkhabhūō mahayā jattēṇa rakkhijjaï. taō sō kumārō mā annasāmantapayāriō saṁpayaṁ ahiddavissaï ti gahiō rajjacintaē hiṁ, aṇumayaṁ ca mē ēyaṁ. kiṁ puṇa jahā tassa sarīrē pamāō na habaï, tahā taē jaïyavvaṁ ti. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ. amba, kiṁ paḍivakkhabhūō mē kumārō; jaï ēvaṁ, tā kō uga sapakkhō tti. tā kiṁ ēiṇā. ēhi, anbhintaraṁ pavisamha. paviṭhṭhō rāyā. uvaṇīyaṁ sē jaṇaṇīē āsaṇaṁ. ubaviṭṭhā ya ēsā. bhaṇiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa. bhō bhō mahannayā, āṇēha iha kumāraṁ. gayā kumārāṇayaṇanimittaṁ rāyapurisā. cintiyaṁ ca rāiṇā. ahō ṇu khalu īisa imaṁ rajja, jassa kaē mahaṁ aṇācikkhiyakāraṇantaramavalambiūṇa ēvaṁ pi vavasiyaṁ mahantaēhiṁ ti. tā ki ēiṇā bandhujaṇasta vi aṇivvuikarēṇa vihala kilēsāyāsamettēṇa paramapamāēkahēuṇā vivāgadāruṇēṇaṁ rajjēṇaṁ. etthaṁ pi bahumāṇō aviiyasaṁsārasarūvāṇaṁ jīvāṇaṁ. aō dēmi imaṁ kumārassa, adhaṇēmi suyasiṇēhasaṁvaḍaiyasōyāṇalaviyāramambāē. etthantaraṁmi puvyakayakammadōsēṇaṁ rāiṇō upari vahapariṇāmapariṇaō āṇiō kumārō. diṭṭhō rāiṇā, sabahumāṇaṁ ca ṭhavibhō sīhāsaṇē. āṇāviyā sugandhōdayabhariyā kaṇayakalasā. gahiō rāiṇā sayamēva ekkō, gahiyā ya annē pahāṇasāmantēhiṁ. ahisittō kumārō. bhaṇiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa. bhō bhō sāmantā, bhō bhō mahantayā, ēsa bhē rāya tti. chūṭā navajjā rāiṇā sēsasāmantaēhi ya. taō calaṇēsu nivaḍiūṇa pucchiyā ambā. amba, avi avagaō tē sōyāṇalō.

taō mahāpurisacariyavimhayakkhittahiyayāē bhaṇiyamambāē. jāya, kahamēvaṁ avēi; na khalu indhaṇēhitō cēva avagamō sōyāṇalassa. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ. amba, kiṁ puṇa etya kāraṇaṁ ti nāgavacchāmi. tīē bhaṇiyaṁ. jāya, suṇa. mahāmisabhūyaṁ khu ēyaṁ rajja. ēyabahu māṇēṇa ya kuṇimagiddhā iva maṇḍalā aparamatthapecchiṇō kāvurisā ṇa gaṇenti sukayaṁ, na jāṇanti uciya, na pecchanti āyaī visa gacchanti tti. mahāpurisō ya tumaṁ ti kajaō'vagacchāmi. ēsō uṇa tē bhāyā kayāi na ēvaṁ vihō havēja tti. akallāṇamittavaṁ ca rāyā havaï. tassa khalu aṇāriyā visayalōluyattaṇēṇa kahaṁ nāma amhē piyā bhavissāmō. taō dēsa iṇē ēsa visayasāhaṇaṁ dhaṇaṁ ti karenti akaraṇijja, jaṁpanti ajaṁpiyavvaṁ, pabattanti ubhayalōgaviruddha, niyattanti dhammavavasāyāō. taō sō sayaṁ pi pāvakammō pāvakammēhi ya pavattiō, nathi taṁja na sēvaï. aō jamāsaṅkiyamimassa, taṁ imāō niyamēṇa tē saṁbhāvēmi. tā kahaṁ sōyāṇalō mē avēi tti. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ. amba, alamāsaṅkāē. satthō khu kumārō. ahavā kimaṇēṇa. pavajāmi ambāra aṇunāō sayalajī vanivvuikāraya samaṇattaṇaṁ ti. tīē bhaṇiyaṁ. jāya, alaṁ tē samaṇataṇēṇaṁ. payaṁ parivālēhi, ēyassa vi ya karēhi juvara jāhisēyaṁ ti. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ. amba, tāyapasāyalāliyāō dhannāō payāō. niuttō ya ēyāsi parivālaṇē kumārō. kayarajjāhisēyassa ya viruddhō juvarajāhisēō. jiṇadhammabōhēṇa virataṁ ca mē cittaṁ saṁsāravāsāō. tā kiṁ bahuṇā. karēu pasāyaṁ ambā, papajjāmi ahaṁ samaṇattaṇaṁ ti. bhaṇiūṇa nivaḍiō calaṇēsu. tīē bhaṇiyaṁ. jāya, jaṁ tē rōyaïḥ kiṁ tu ahaṁ pi paḍivajāmi tti. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ । amba, payaïnigguṇē saṁsārē juttamēyaṁ. ettha khalu savvē sapajjavasāṇā nicayā, paḍaṇantā ussēhā, vibhōyapajjavasāṇā saṁjōyā, mara gantaṁ jīviyaṁ. akayasukayakammāṇa ya dāruṇō vivāō, dullahaṁ ca maṇuyattē jiṇindavayaṇaṁ. tā kiccamēyamambāē vi. bhaṇiō ya kumārō।vaccha, tāyapasāyalāliyāō payāō; taṁtahā ceṭṭhiyavvaṁ, jahā payāō kēṇaï uvaddavēṇa na sumarēṁti tāyassa. pariccaïyavvaṁ kumāra ceṭṭiyaṁ, abalambiyavvaṁ rāyarisicariyaṁ, na maïliyabō puvapurisaviḍhattō jasō. kiṁ bahuṇā. jahā suladdhamiha māṇusattaṇaṁ havaï, tahā kāyavvaṁ ti. bhaṇiyā ya rajjacintayā sāmantā ya. tubbhēhiṁ pi uciyaṁ niyavivēgassa sarisaṁ tāyapasāyāṇaṁ aṇurūvaṁ mahākulassa viddhikārayaṁ kittīē hiyaṁ payākumārāṇaṁ ubhayalōyasuhāvahaṁ ceṭṭhiyavvaṁ ti. tattha kēhiṁci ihalōyasāvekkhaēhi bhaṇiyaṁ. mahārāya, kī isā amhāṇaṁ mahārāyavirahiyāṇaṁ duvē vi lōyā. tahāvi jaṁ dēvō āṇavēi. appaḍihayasāsaṇō dēvō. kē amhē samīhiyantarāya karaṇassa visēsaō paralōyamaggē. taō ahiṇandiūṇa ēyaṁ tēsiṁ vayaṇaṁ uḍiō rāyā. payaṭṭō saṇaṁkumārāyariyasamīvaṁ.

etthantaraṁmi samāgaō gurupavattikaïṇaniuttō siddhatthō nāma bambhaṇō. bhaṇiyaṁ ca tēṇa. dēva, saṁsiddhā tē maṇōrahā. ihēvāgaō bhagavaṁ saṇaṁkumārāyariō, āvāsiō tendugujāṇē. ēyaṁ ca sōūṇa harisiō rāyā. sattaṭṭa vā payāṇi gantūṇa tappaēsaṭṭhiēṇēva paḍi lēhiya mahiyalaṁ samullasiyarōmaśca dharaṇinihiyajāṇukarayalēṇaṁ vandiō ṇēṇa, vandiūṇa payaṭṭō bhayavantadasaṇavaḍiyāē. vinattō mahanta yasāmantēhiṁ. dēva, saṁpannaṁ cetra samīhiyaṁ dēvassa. tā etthēva pasatyatihikaraṇamuhuttajōē pavvaïssaï dēvō. paḍisuyaṁ rāiṇā. gaō gurusamīvaṁ. iyarēhiṁ pi vijayaṁ bhaṇiūṇa davāviyaṁ mahādāṇaṁ, kārāviyā savvāyayaṇēsu pūyā. annayā ya pasatthē tihikaraṇamuhurajōē samārūḍhō rahavaraṁ pariyariō rāyalōēṇa ugghōsijjamāṇāē varavariyāē pūrentō atthijaṇamaṇōrahē ahō accharīyanakō uttimapurisa ceṭṭiyaṁ ti bhaṇamāṇēhi pulōijamāṇō nāyarēhi agāhā kāyandī, ayālō ya ēsō payajāē tti japamāṇī hi sadukkhaṁ kahakahavi dissamāṇō nāyariyāhi vajjantēṇa puṇṇāhatūrēṇa paḍhantēhiṁ maṅgalāī bandivandrēhiṁ panajjānimittaṁ niggaō nayarīō rāyā. pattō tendugujjāṇaṁ. païvaïō ēsō saṇaṁ mārāyariyasamīvē saha jaṇaṇīē pahāṇapariyaṇēṇa ya. kaṁci vēlaṁ ciṭṭhiūṇa ya vandiūṇa ya bhayavantaṁ bāhollalōyaṇā paviṭhṭhā kāyandi rāyanāyarayā. anayā ya samattē māsakappē vihariō bhayavaṁ. ahijjiyaṁ ca suttaṁ jayā ṇagārēṇa. taō niraïyāraṁ sāmaṇṇamaṇuvālentassa aïkkantō kōi kālō.

iō ya navāvāiō pavvaïō tti jāō sē maccharō vijayassa. pēsiyā ya ṇēṇa kuōi kālaḥō imassa niyapaccaïyapurisā vā vāyagā. tēhiṁ ciya kiṁnimittaṁ aṇimittaṁ vāvāyaṇaṁ ti avāvāiūṇa vāvāiō tti nivēiyaṁ vijayassa. parituṭṭō khu ēsō. annayā ya kayāi kassaï maṁdaṭṭaṇa havēja jiṇadhammapaḍibōhō tti avassabhaviyabvayāniōēṇa aṇunaviya guruṁ kaïvayasusāhuparivāriō saya. ṇālōyaṇanimittaṁ kāyandi cēva gaō jayāṇagārō. nivēiyaṁ rāiṇō. kuviō ēsō tēsiṁ vāvāyagapurisāṇaṁ. sadāviyā ṇēṇaṁ pucchiyā ya. arē kattha vā kahaṁ vā tumbhēhiṁ sō samaṇagakhvadhārī vēriō mē vāvāiō tti. tō tēhiṁ vināyatayāgamaṇēhiṁ bhaṇiyaṁ. dēva, nandivaddhaṇē sannivēsē. kēsālaṁkāravigamēṇa na pañcabhinnāō amhēhiṁ. taō pucchiō tattha ēgō samaṇagō kahiṁ kayamō vā ettha jaō tti. tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. ettha nāgadēvaharaē jō ēsa jhāṇamuvagō tti. tō munnamēva tamujjāṇaṁ ti gantūṇa vāvāiō amhēhiṁ. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ. annō kōi tavassī tumbhēhiṁ vāvāiō, sō uṇa mahāpāvō ihāgaō tti. tēhiṁ bhaṇiyaṁ. dēva, na samma viyāṇāmō. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ. kiṁ gayaṁ ettha saṁpayaṁ vāvāessāmō. paḍissuyaṁ ca ṇēhi. niggaō ya ēsō niyamandirāō bhaya vantadasaṇanimittaṁ. diṭṭhō ṇēṇa bhayavaṁ vandiō ya. dhammalāhiō ya bhayavayā. kahiō sē sabannubhāsiō dhammō. na virattō ēsō saṁsāravāsāō tti muṇiō sē ahippāō. bhaṇiō ya ēsaü. mahārāya, avagayaṁ cēva taē ēyaṁ, jahā kammapariṇāmaphalaṁ saṁsāriyāṇa sattāṇaṁ suhaṁ dukkhaṁ ca. savvē ya sattā suhaṁ ahilasanti, na dukkhaṁ. mūlaṁ puṇa imassa dhammō. tassa pariṇāmō suruvayā piyasamāgamasuhāī sōhaggaṁ arōgayā viulā ya bhōyā. tā avalambēhi sayalasokkhanihāṇabhūyaṁ dhamma, āyarasu mettiṁ, veṭṭhēhi dāṇaṁ, karēhi savvasattēsu dayaṁ ti. vijaēṇa cintiyaṁ. samuppannaṁ imassa maraṇabhayaṁ, aō ēvaṁ bhaṇāi. tā karhi vaccaï tti. cintiūṇa bhaṇiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa. bhayavaṁ, jaṁ tumaṁ āṇavēsi. annaṁ ca, jayappabhūimēva paḍivannō tumaṁ vīyarāgabhāsiyaṁ dhamma, taïyappabhūimēva āḍhattaṁ maē imaṁ. bhayavayā bhaṇiyaṁ. sōhaṇaṁ kayaṁ taē. taō kaṁci vēlaṁ pajjuvāsiūṇa paviṭṭhō nayariṁ. cintiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa. ajjēva ēyaṁ durāyāraṁ vāvāēmi. pasantē vi bhayavantē puncakayakililukammapariṇaī cēvettha kāraṇaṁ vijayassa. bhaṇiyaṁ ca—

aïsaṁkiliṭṭakammāṇuvēyaṇē jō u hōi pariṇāmō

sō saṁkilikammassa kāraṇaṁ jamiha pāēṇa

samāgayā rayaṇī. bhaṇiyā ya rāiṇā pudhapēsiyā vācāyagapurisā. arē ajjataṁ durāyāraṁ vāvāēmō tti. paḍissuyamaṇēhiṁ. atthamiō miyakō. kaïvayapurisaparivāriō gaō jayāṇagārasamīvaṁ vijabhō. diṭṭhō ya ṇēṇa nivāyasaraṇapadīvō vva sajjhāṇa. saṁgaō bhayavaṁ. tivvāṇuhāvakasāōdaēṇaṁ ca kaḍḍiyaṁ maṇḍalaggaṁ. ahiyayaraṁ gahiō kasārahiṁ. avagayā sukayavāsaṇā, pavattō mahā. mōhō, āsagaliśrō tivvakammapariṇaīē. pavaḍḍamāṇakōvāṇalēṇa pahaō sirōharāē, ēgapahārēṇēva pāḍiyaṁ uttimaṅgaṁ. vijayakumārō cēva ēsō ti ahō vicittayā jīvacariyāṇaṁ, acintaṇīyā kammuṇō gaï tti cintiūṇa avagayā sāhuṇō.

bhayavaṁ puṇa gambhīrayāē āsayassa visuddhayāē mettīē acaliyayāē jhāgasa nimmamayāē sarīrē bhāviyayāē jiṇavayaṇassa khīṇa ppāyayāē pāvakammuṇō visuddhayāē lēsābhāvassa thirayāē saṁjamadhiīē āsannayāē paramapayassa aparivaḍiyamuhapariṇāmō caïūṇa dēhaṁ samuppannō āṇayābhihāṇē dēvalōē sirippahē vimāṇē aṭṭhārasasāgarōvamāū vēmāṇiō tti. vijayaō vi ya taṁ vāvāiūṇa mahāṇubhāvaṁ kayakiccaṁ mannamāṇō appāṇaṁ paviṭṭhō nayariṁ. sēsasāhuṇō vi gōsē gayā saṇaṁkumārāyariyasamīvaṁ. sāhiō sayala vuttantō āyariyassa. susīsō tti kāūṇamaṇanasarisaṁ kayaṁ paridēvaṇaṁ guruṇā. iyarō vi ya vijayanaravaī tayappabhūimēva mahayā pāvōdaēṇa samuppānamahāvāhivēyaṇō jaō vāvāiyō ti ēdahamettēṇamappāṇaṁ kayatthaṁ mannamāṇō ahāuyaṁ pāliūṇa dukkhamaccuṇā maō samāṇō uppannō paṅkappahāē puḍhavīē dasasāgarōvamāū mahāghōranāraō ti.

jayavijayā ya sahōyara jaṁ bhaṇiyamihāsi taṁ gayamiyāṇi

vocchāmi putravihiyaṁ dharaṇō lacchī ya païmajjā

atthi ihēva jambuddīvē dīvē mārahē vāsē parihariyā ahammēṇaṁ vajjiyā kāladōsēṇa rahiyā uvaddavēṇa nivāsō nayasirīē māyandī nāma nayarī.

jīē mahumattakāmiṇilīlācaṁkamaṇaṇēuraravēṇa

bhavaṇavaṇadīhiōyararayā vi haṁsā naḍijjanti

jīē saralasahāvō piyaṁvaō dhammanihiyaniyacittō

paḍhamābhāsī nēhāluō ya purisāṇa vaggō tti

tattha dariyārimadaṇō sukayadhammādhammavavatyō kālō va rivaṇaṁ] kālamēhō nāma naravaī. tassa aīva bahumaō sayalanayariseṭṭhicūḍā maṇībhūō bandhudattō nāma seṭṭhi ti. sō ya parammuddō parakalattē na abhatthaṇāēṁ,aṁjuddhō paravibhavē na dhamprōvajaṇē, asaṁtuṭṭhō parōvayārē na dhaṇāgamē, ahiṁgaō pīīē na maccharēṇaṁ, daridō dōsēhiṁ na vihavēṇaṁ. tēṇa sā nayahī malayapaṇaṁ pitra pārijāēṇa basantō viya kusumu ggamēṇa pāusasirī viya mēhāvalīē sarayakālō viya candamaṇḍa lēṇaṁ ahiyaṁ vibhūsiya tti. tassa kamalāyarassa viya viluppaï kōsō mittamaṇḍalēṇa, kappataruvarassa viya khandhē pāyaṁ kāūṇa gahiyāī phalāī athinivahēṇa. tassa samāṇa kularūvavihavasahāvā hārappahā nāma bhāriyā. sa imīē saha dhammatthaabhaggapasaraṁ visayasuhamaṇuhēvisu tti. iō ya sō āṇayakappavāsī dēvō tammi dēvalōē ahāuyaṁ pāliūṇa cuō samāṇō samuppanō hārappahāra kucchisi. divā ya pāē tīē cēva rayaṇīē carimajāmaṁmi sumiṇaē divyapaümāsaṇō. vavidvā dhavaladugullanivasaṇā viviharayaṇakhaciyarasaṇākalāvā sukumālamiurpha sēga uttarīpaṇa pacchāiyapōharā muttāvalīvihūsiyāē sirōharāē runtamayarupphullagahiyakamalā dhavalakarivarēhiṁ didhakaścaṇakalasēhi ahisiccamāṇā sirī vayaṇēṇamuyaraṁ pavisamāṇi tti. taō taṁ daṭṭaṇa viuddhā ēsā. sāhiō tīē hērisanibbharāē daïyasta. bhaṇiyā ya ṇēṇaṁ. sundari, sirinivāsō tē puttō bhavissaï. paḍissuyamimīē. taō visē sēṇa tibaggasaṁpāyaṇarayāē aïkkantō kōi kālō. pattō pasūisamaō. pasūyā ya ēsā, jāō sē dāraō nivēiō paritōsanāmāē cēḍiyāē bandhudattasya. parituṭrō ēsō. dinnaṁ tī ē pāriōsiyaṁ. kayaṁ uciyaṁ karaṇijja. aïkkantō māsō dārayassa. païṭāviyaṁ ca sē nāma piyāmahassa santiyaṁ dharaṇō tti. pattō kumārabhāvaṁ. gāhiyō kalākalāvaṁ. nimmāō ya tattha payāṇusārī saṁvuttō.

etthantaraṁmi sō vijayajīvanāraō tō narayāō ubaṭṭiūṇa puṇō saṁpāramāhiṇḍiya aṇantarabhavē tahāvihamaṇuṭāṇaṁ kāūṇa tīa cēva nayarōē kattiyasta sē dvissa japāē bhāriyāē kucchisi itthiyattāē uvavannō ti. jāyā kālakkamēṇa. païṭāviyaṁ ca sē nāma lacchi tti. pattā ya jōvaṇaṁ. acintaṇīyayāē kammapariṇāmassa bhaviyavvayāē niōēṇa mahāvibhūīē pariṇīyā ya ṇēṇaṁ. atthi pīī dharaṇassa lacchīē, na uṇa tīē dharaṇaṁmi. cintēi ēsā. alaṁ mēṁ jīvalōēṇa, jattha dharaṇō païdiṇaṁ dīsaï tti. ēvaṁ ca viḍambaṇāpāyaṁ visayasuhamaṇuhavantāṇaṁ aïkkantō kōi kālō.

annayā ya payattē mayaṇamahūsavē kīlānimittaṁ payaṭṭō rahavarēṇa dharaṇō malayasundaraṁ ujjāṇaṁ. pattō nayariduvāradēsaṁ. etthantaraṁmi tō cēva ujjāṇāō kīliūṇāgaō rahavarēṇa nayariduvāradēsabhāyaṁ paścanandisē dviputtō dēvanandi tti. miliyā rahavarā duvāradēsa bhāē. vitthiṇṇayāē rahavarāṇaṁ na doṇhaṁ pi niggamaṇapavēsabhūmī. bhaṇiyaṁ ca dēvanandiṇā. bhō bhō dharaṇa, ōsārēhi tāva rahavaraṁ, jāva mē pavisaï rahō tti. dharaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. aïṁgaō mē rahō, na tīraē vālēuṁ. tā tumaṁ cetra ōsārēhi, jāva mē nīsaraha tti. dēvanandiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ. bhō bhō dharaṇa, aha kēṇa uṇa ahaṁ bharaō ūṇaō, jēṇa rahavaraṁ ōsārēmi. dharaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. bhī bhō dēvanandi, tullamē vēyaṁ. ēvaṁ ca vitthakkā duvē vi seṭṭiputtā. rurō nimnamaya vēsamaggō nāyarayāṇaṁ. pavitthiṇṇō jaṇavāō. vināō ēsa vuttantō nayarimaha ntarahiṁ. ālōciyaṁ ca ṇēhiṁ. duvē vi khu mahāpurisaputtā, na khalu ettha ēgassa vi nirāgaraṇaṁ jujaï tti. tā imaṁ etya pattayālaṁ; nibbhacchijanti ēē. jahā kīsa tubbhē puvyapurisajjiēṇaṁ vihavēṇaṁ gabamubahaha. kēṇa tumhāṇa niyabhuōjiēṇaṁ daviṇajāṇaṁ dinnaṁ mahādāṇaṁ. kēṇa vā kārāviō dhammāhigārō. kēṇa vā anmuddhariō vihalavaggō. kēṇa vā pariōsiyā jaṇaṇi naṇayā. tā kimēiṇā niratthaēṇa buhajaṇōvahasaṇijjēṇa ahōpurisiyāpāraṇa ceṭṭhiēṇaṁ. aō upasaṁharaha ēyaṁ, ōsārēha niyaniyathāmāō cē piṭṭha bhō rahavarē' kim annēṇaṁ ti. ēvamālōciūṇa iṇamēva tumbhēhiṁ tē vattavva ti bhaṇiūṇa visajjiyā kkhaṇavināsakusalā dhammatyavisārayā pariṇayā vōvatthāē nivāsō usamassa ihaparalōyāvāyadaṁsagā muṭṭhiyā dhammapakkhē sayalanayarijaṇabahumayā cattāri cāriyā. gayā tē tēsiṁ samīvaṁ. abbhuṭṭhiyā ya ṇēhiṁ. aṇusāsiyā cāriēhiṁ. sāhiō paürāhippāō. ahō sōhaṇaṁ ti parituṭṭhō dēvanandī. asōhaṇaṁ tila ō dharaṇō. bhaṇiyaṁ ca tēṇa. bhō bhō mahantayā, jaṁ tubbhē āṇavēha, tamavassaṁ maaï kāyavaṁ. kiṁtu paḍibōhinō ahaṁ tumbhēhi, lajiō ya attaṇō ceṭṭhiēṇaṁ, mahaī mē ōhāvaṇā, āmagabbhapāyaṁ ca mannēmi attāṇayaṁ. tā ēvaṁ mē aṇuggahaṁ karēha. ōsārijjantu ēē rahabarā. gacchāmō ya amhē iō ajēya dēsantaraṁ. taō saṁbaccharēṇa jō cēva ṇē païhūyaṁ daviṇajāyaṁ viḍhaviūṇa ihāgacchiya ahiyaṁ sappu risaceṭṭhiyaṁ karessaï, tassēva santiō rahō ipīē cēva tērasīē pavisissaï vā nikkhamissaï vā. cāriēhiṁ bhaṇiyaṁ. alamēḍaṇā abhinivēsēṇa. dharaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. na annahā mē nivvuī hōi. cāriēhiṁ bhaṇiyaṁ. païurāmettha pamāṇaṁ. dharaṇēṇa bhagiyaṁ. nivēēha paü rāṇaṁ. dēvanandiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ. juttamēyaṁ, kō ettha dōsō. tamō nivēiyaṁ paürāṇaṁ. bahumayaṁ ca tēsiṁ. saddāviyā ya tēsiṁ jaṇaṇijaṇayā. sāhiō vuttantō, bahumaō ya tēsi pi. taō kārāviyā savahaṁ na tubbhēhiṁ ērasiṁ saṁvāhaṇā kāyavvā. saddāviyā dharaṇadēvanandī. sēma ppiyaṁ pattēyaṁ tēsiṁ pañcadīṇāralakkhapamāṇaṁ bhaṇḍamollaṁ. kayaṁ vaktthāpattayaṁ jō cēva ēēsiṁ saṁvaccharabbhantarē ahiyayaradaviṇajāēṇa pōrusaṁ payaḍaïmsaï, tassēva santiēṇa rahavarēṇa gantavvaṁ, na iyaramsa. dinnā ya ṇēhiṁ sahatyā. muddiyaṁ pattayaṁ. chūḍhaṁ paürabhaṇḍārē. niggayā niyaparivārapariyariyā mahayā caḍayarēṇa dharaṇadēvanandī; geṇhiūṇa jahōciyaṁ bhaṇḍaṁ payaṭṭā dēsantaraṁ, ēgō uttarāvaha, avarō puvvadēsaṁ.

etthantaraṁmi cintiyaṁ lacchīē. dīhāṇi dēsantarāṇi, suhēṇa viōō, dukkhēṇa samāgamō; tā na yāṇāmō, antarālē kimahaṁ pāvissaṁ ti. avāvāiō cēva viuttō khu ēsō. gayā ya satthavāhaputtā ēgaṁ payāṇayaṁ. pēsiyāō ya ēēsiṁ bandhudattapaścanandīhi sarārāṭṭahānāmattamālācaya āuācchaūṇa nayāramahantaē sapāravārāā vahūā, mālayāā ya ēpāsa. pādaṇapayāṇaēha ca gaccha• māṇāṇaṁ aïkantā kaïvi diyahā.

anayā ya parivahantē satthē diṭṭhō dharaṇēṇa ēgaṁmi vaṇaniuṭṭhajē añcantasōmarūvō uppāyanivāē karēmāṇō vijjāharakumāraō. gaō tassa samīvaṁ. pucchiō ya ēsō. bhō kiṁnimittaṁ puṇa tumaṁ asaṁjāyapakkhō viya garuḍapōyaō muhaviyārōvalavikhajjamāṇa nahaṅgaṇagamaṇūsuō viya uppāyanivāē karēsi. ācikkha, jaï akahaṇijja na hōi. taō ahō sē bhāvannuyayā, ahō āgaī, ahō vayaṇavinnāsō tti cintiūṇa bhaṇiyaṁ vijjāharēṇa. bhō, suṇa. ahaṁ khu vēyaḍḍapavvaē amarapuranivāsī hēmakuṇḍalō nāma vijā harakumārō aṇabhatthavijjō sayaniōyaparō tatthēva ciṭṭhāmi, jāva samāgaō tāyassa paramamittō vijjumālī nāma vijjāharō. bhāṇā ya tāēṇa. kuā tuma, kāsa vā vimaṇadummaṇā dāsāsa. taga bhaṇiyaṁ. vijhāō ahaṁ. vimaṇadummaṇattē puṇa imaṁ kāraṇaṁ. diṭṭhaṁ maē vijhāō ihāgacchamāṇēṇa ujjēgīē nivēyakāraṇaṁ. tāraṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. kīisaṁ nivēyakāraṇaṁ. vijjumāliṇā bhaṇiyaṁ. suṇa.

atthi ujjēṇīē sirippahō nāma gayā. tassa rūviṇi ba kusumāuhavējayantī jayasirī nāma dhūyā. sā ya patthēmāṇassa vi na dinnā koṅkaṇarāyaputtassa sisuvālassa, dinnā ya īmēṇa vacchēsarasuyassa parokkhārakaraṇēkalālasassa sirivijayassa. kuviō sisu vālō. āgō jayasirivivāhanimittaṁ sirivijaō. taō pāraddhē mahāvibhūīē vivāhamahūsavē niggayā mayaṇavandaṇanimittaṁ samā lōciya vihāēṇamavakkhandaṁ dāūṇaṁ avahariyā sisuvālēṇa jayasirī. uṭhāibhō kalayalō. muṇiō vuttantō siravijaēṇaṁ. laggō maggaō. samāsāiō sisuvālō. āvaḍiyamāōhaṇaṁ. gāḍhapahārīkaēṇaṁ ca jēūṇa sisuvālaṁ niyattiyā jayasirī pahāragaruyayāē ya sō mahāṇubhāvō pāṇasaṁsaē vaṭṭaē. sā vi rāyadhūyā na ahamēyaṁmi akayapāṇabhōyaṇē pāṇavittiṁ karēmi tti vāmakarayalapaṇāmiya vayaṇapaṅkayā aṇācikkhaṇīyaṁ avatthantaramaṇuhavantī dukkhēṇa ciṭṭhui. ēyaṁ mē etya kāraṇaṁ. tāraṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. īisō ēsa saṁsārō. khellaṇēyabhūyā khu ettha kammapariṇaīē pāṇiṇō. tā alaṁ nivvēēṇa. taō maē cintiyaṁ. sāhiyaṁ mē kallaṁ cēva himavantapavva yagayassa dariharuggayaṁ mahōsahimavalōiūṇa gandhabbaraïnāmēṇa gandhavvakumārēṇa mama vayaṁsaraṇa. jahā bhō hēmakuṇḍala, saccō khu ēsa lōyavāō, jaṁ acintō hi maṇimantōsahīṇaṁ pabhāvō tti, jō ēyāē ōsahīē ēsō pahāvō, jēṇa vidāriyaṭṭhī vi khaggāipahārō imīē pakkhālaṇōyaēṇaṁ pi paṇadvavēyaṇaṁ takakhaṇā cēva rujjhaï ti. didrupaccayā ya maïṁē sā. tā gacchāmi ahayaṁ himavantaṁ geṇhiūṇa tayaṁ ōsahiṁ uvaṇēmi sirivijayassa. taō sumariūṇa kahaṁci gayaṇagāmiṇi vijja gaō himavantapavvayaṁ. gahiyā ōsahī । ōiṇṇō himavantāō. mā sirivijayassa acāhiyaṁ bhavissaï tti paḍiniyattō vēēṇa. pattō ēyaṁ niujaṁ, khīṇayāē vēyāgama ṇēṇa vīsamaṇanimittaṁ ōiṇṇō ihaī, kayaṁ calaṇasōyaṁ ubaviṭṭhō kuravayapāyavasamīvē, ṭhiō muhuttamettaṁ, uccaliō ya ujjēṇiṁ. sumariyā gayaṇagāmiṇī vijjā, jāva ahiṇavagihīyettaṇēṇa gamaṇasaṁbhamēṇa ya visumariyaṁ mē payaṁ. taō sā na vaha tti uppāya nivāē karēmi. dharaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. bhō ēvaṁ kvathiē kō iha uvāō. hēmakuṇḍalēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. natthi uvāō. aō cēva rāyaütta viṇāsasaṅkāē uttammaï mē hiyayaṁ, paṇassaï mē maī. sabahā na appapuṇṇāṇaṁ samīhiyaṁ saṁpajjaï ti daḍhaṁ visaṇṇō mhi. dharaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. bhō atthi ēsa kappō, jaṁ sā annaïssa samakkhaṁ paḍhijjaï. hēmakuṇḍalēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ atthi. dharaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. jaï ēvaṁ, tā paḍha; kayāi ahaṁ tē payaṁ lahāmi. tō hēmakuṇḍalēṇa nathi avisaō purisasāmatthassa ti cintiya sāmannasiddhiṁ kāūṇa paḍhiyā vijjā. payāṇusārittaṇēṇa laddhaṁ payaṁ dharaṇēṇa. sāhiyaṁ hēmakuṇḍalassa. parituhrō ēsō. bhaṇiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa. bhō bhō mahā purisa, dinnaṁ taē jīviyaṁ mama samīhiyasaṁpāyaṇēṇa rāyaüttassa, tā kiṁ tē karēmi. dharaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. kayaṁ tē karaṇijja; gaccha samīhiyaṁ saṁpāḍēhi. taō hēmakuṇḍalēṇa ahō sē mahāṇubhāvaya tti cintiya paratyaṁ karejjāsi tti bhaṇiūṇa dinnaṁ ōsahivalaya khaṇḍaṁ. paṇayabhaṅgabhīruttaṇēṇa gahiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa. gaō vijjāharō, āgō ya dharaṇō niyayasatthaṁ. aïkantā kaïvi diyahā. annayā ya girin itīraṁmi samāvāsiē satthē gavalajalayavaṇṇā vellinivaḍuddha kēsahārā bakkaladdhanivasaṇā kaṇṇiyakōḍaṇḍavāva ḍaggahatthā suṇayavandrasaṁgayā sadukkhaṁ ruyamāṇā diṭṭhā dharaṇēṇa nāidūragāmiṇā savarajuvāṇaya tti. sadāviyā ṇēṇa pucchiyā ya. bhō kiṁnimittaṁ ruyaha tti. tēhiṁ bhaṇiyaṁ ajja, atthi amhāṇaṁ kālasēṇō nāma pallīvaī.

jassa iha vimhiyāō sattiniyāṇāṇi cintayantīō

na samalliyanti duggaṁ paracakkabhaē vi vāhīō

ēkasaraghāyaladdhā jassa ya karikumbhadāraṇēkarasā. na vihalantasarīrā gacchanti paya pi kēsariṇō. sō khu kēsarī āgō tti āyaṇṇiya ghettūṇa kordaṇḍaṁ kaṇṇiyasaraṁca ēgāgī cēva niggō pallīō. na diṭṭhō ya ṇēṇa naggō hapāyavantariō kēsarī. gaō tassa samīvaṁ. gahiō ya ṇēṇa paṭṭhidēsē. vāvāiō tēṇa valiūṇa kaṭṭāraraṇa kēsarī. tēṇa vi ya sē tōḍiyaṁ uttimaṅgakhaṇḍaṁ. taō sō natthi mē jīviyaṁ ti mannamāṇō jalaṇapavēsaṁ kāumāradō. muṇiō sē ēsa vuttantō rōhiṇīē.

taō sā vi āvanasattā taṁ cēva kāuṁ vavasiyā, vāriyā vi pallīvaïṇā na viramaï ti. taō tēṇa pēsiyā amhē tīē saṁdhāraṇatthaṁ piuṇō sē āṇayaṇanimittaṁ. vīrarasapahāṇō khu sō sayaṇavacchalō ya. tā na yāṇāmō, kiṁ paḍivajismaï tti. mahādukkhapīḍiyā asamatthā ya dhariuṁ imaṁ sōyāirēya avijamāṇōvāyā ya paḍijiūṇa itthiyābhāva kēvalaṁ ruyamha. dharaṇēṇa bhaṇiya. bhaddā, alaṁ sōēṇa. daṁsēhi mē taṁ pallīvaī. kayāi jīvāvēmi ahayaṁ. taō calaṇēsu nivaḍiūṇa harisavasupphullalōyaṇēhiṁ jaṁpiyaṁ savarēhiṁ. ēvaṁ tuma dēvāvayārō viya āgaīē. tā tumaṁ cēva samatthō si dēvaṁ samāsāsēuṁ. annaṁ ca. jaï amhēsu aṇuggahabuddhī ajassa, tā turiyaṁ gacchaü ajō; mā tassa mahāṇubhāvassa acāhiyaṁ bhavē. taō ghettaṇa vijjāharaviiṇṇaṁ ōsahivalayaṁ āruhiya vēsaraṁ kaïvaya niyapurisaparivāriō turiyaturiyaṁ gaō satyavāhaputtō. divō ya tēṇaṁ naggōhapāyavatalammi ciyagāsanasaṁṭhiō ruhiradhārāparisitta gattō siṇēhasāramasadaṁ ca rōvamāṇīē jāyāē saṁgaō kālasēṇō. nivēiō sē vuttantō savarajuvāṇaēṇa. abbhuṭṭhamāṇō ya mucchāni mīliyalōyaṇō nivaḍiō dharaṇibaḍhē. dharaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. udayamudayaṁ ti. tō āṇīyamudayaṁ naïliṇipattēṇaṁ. ṭhūḍhamōsahivalayaṁ dāū ṇamuttimaṅgakhaṇḍaṁ. sittō ya ṇēṇē, jāva acintayāē ōsahipahāvassa puvvarūvāō vi ahiyayaraṁ dasaṇīō alakkhijjamāṇavaṇavi bhāō uḍhiō kālasēṇō. tuṭṭā ya sē ghariṇī saha pariyaṇēṇa. calaṇēsu nivaḍiūṇa bhaṇiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa. ajja, piyayamājī yarakkhaṇēṇaṁ saṁpāḍiyamahāpaōyaṇā tuha santiyā pāṇā; kimettha avaraṁ bhagīya:. dharaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. sabbasāhāraṇā cēva mahāpurisa, pāṇā havanti. kimetya ahiyaṁ. kālasēṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. tā āisaü ajō, jaṁ maē kāyanvaṁ ti. dharaṇēga bhaṇiyaṁ. mahāpurisō khu tuma; tā kiṁ avaraṁ bhaṇīyaï tahā vi sattēsu dayā. kālasēṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ parivajiyā jāvajīvamēva maē ajjavayaṇēga pāraddhī. dharaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ—

kayaṁ mē karaṇijja

taō gaō satthavāhaputtō niyayasatthaṁ

aïkkantā kaïvi diyahā aṇavasyapayāṇaēṇa. diṭṭhō ya ṇēṇa pakkhasandhīē uvavāsahiēṇaṁ āyāmuhīsannivēsammi āvāsiē satthē jaracīranivasaṇō gēruyavilittasavvagattō khandhadēsārōviyatikkhaliō acōrō cēva cōrō tti kariya gahiō vajjantavirasaḍiṇḍima vajjhatthāmaṁ nīyamāṇō caṇḍālajuvāṇō tti. tēṇa vi ya mahantaṁ satthamavalōiya suddhayāē āsayassa vallahayāē jīviyassa tassa samī vaṁmi cēva mahayā sadēṇa jaṁpiyaṁ. bhō bhō satthiyā, suṇēha tumbhē. mahāsaranivāsī mōriō nāma caṇḍālō ahaṁ, kāraṇēṇa ya kusatthalaṁ payaṭṭō, vippaladdhabuddhīhi ya daṇḍavāsiēhi apecchiūṇa cōrē adōsayārī cēva mandabhāgō gihībhō mhi. tā mōyāvēha, bhō mōyā vēhaḥ saraṇāgō ahaṁ ajjāṇaṁ. annaṁ ca, maraṇadukkhāō vi mē iyamanbhahiyaṁ, jaṁ tahāvihanikalaṅkapunyapurisajjiyassa jaïsassa viṇā vi dōsēṇaṁ maïlaṇa tti. tā mōyāvēha, bhō mōyāvēha. tō suddhacittayāē cintiyaṁ dharaṇēṇa. ṇa khalu dōsayārī ēvaṁ jaṁpaï. karuṇā pavannēṇa bhaṇiyā ṇēṇa ārakkhiyā. bhō bhō kulaüttayā, mama karaṇa vihīraha muhuttayaṁ, jāva ēyamantarēṇa vinaviūṇa naravaī daviṇayāṇē ṇāvi mōyāvēmi ēyaṁ. tēhiṁ bhaṇiyaṁ — jaï ēvaṁ, tā lahuṁ hōhi . taō ghettūṇa narindadarisaṇanimittaṁ dīṇārasayasahassamullaṁ muttāhala mālaṁ gaō naravaïsamīvaṁ. diṭṭhō ya ṇēṇa rāyā. sāhiūṇa vuttantaṁ vinattō caṇḍālamantarēṇa naravaī. kaō sē pasāō. dyasahiō ya tassa mokkhaṇanimittaṁ āgaō tamuddēsaṁ. mōyāviō ēsō. tumbhē imassa jīviyadāyaga tti bhaṇiūṇa pūiyā ārakkhiyā. dēvā viūṇa pāhēyaṁ bhaṇiō ya caṇḍālō. bhadda, saṁpāḍēhi samīhiyaṁ. ajja, mā tuha sā avasthā havaü, jīē maē ciya pōyaṇaṁ ti bhaṇiūṇa [kaïyañjaliuḍō khiinimiyajāṇukarayalapnuttimaṅgō paṇamiūṇa satthavāhaputtaṁ] gaō caṇḍālō.

dharaïṇō vi ya kaïvayapayāṇarahiṁ pattō uttarāvahatilaya bhūyaṁ ayalaüraṁ nāma paṭṭaṇaṁ. diṭṭhō ya rāyā. bahumaniō tēṇaṁ. vibhāgasaṁpa ttīē ya vikiṇiyamaṇēṇa bhaṇḍaṁ. samāsāiō advaïguṇō lābhō. ṭhiō tatthēva kayavikkayanimittaṁ cattāri māsē. puṇṇōyaēṇaṁ ca vidvattaṁ pabhūyaṁ daviṇajāya. saṁkhāviyaṁ ca ṇēga, jāva atthi kōḍimettaṁ ti tō gahiyaṁ māyandisaṁvavahārōciyaṁ bhaṇḍaṁ. bharāviō satthō. payaṭṭō niyadēsāgamaṇanimittaṁ mahayā caḍayarēṇa.

païdiyahapayāṇēṇa ya savarabahū gēyasu (mu) hiyamayajūhaṁ. thēvadiyahēhi satyō pattō kāyambari aḍaviṁ.

vasahamayamahisasadla kōlasa yasaṁkulaṁ mahābhīmaṁ

māindavindacandaṇaniruddhasasisūrakarapasaraṁ

phalapuṭṭataruvara dviyaparapuṭṭhanimukavisamahalabōlaṁ

*tarukēṇaïkayandōlaṇavāṇaravukkāraramaṇijja

mayaṇāhadariyaruñjiyasadasamuttatthaphiḍiyagayajūhaṁ

vaṇadavajālāveḍhiyacalamayarāyantagiriniyaraṁ

niddayavarāhaghōṇāhivāyajajjariyapallalōyanta

dappurdharakariniurumbadaliyahintālasaṁghāyaṁ

tīē vahiūṇa satyō tiṇṇi payāmāi pallalasamīvē

āvāsiō ya pallalajalayarasaṁjaṇiyasaṁkhōhaṁ

āvāsiūṇa tīrē sarassa majjhammi kīliūṇa muhaṁ

tō rayaṇīē satthō suttō dāūṇa thāṇāī

raïyaṇīē carimajāmami bhīsaṇa (ya) siṅgasa ddagadabbhā

aha savarabhillasēṇā paḍiyā satthaṁmi bīsatthē

haṇa haṇa haṇa tti gaddabhatadasaṁjaṇiyajuvaïsaṁtāsā

annonnasambhamālaggadīhakōdaṇḍasaṁghāyā

tīsē sasabōhiyasatthiyapurisēhi saha mahābhīmaṁ

jujjhamaha saṁpalagga sarōhavicchinnasaraniyaraṁ

satthiyapuri sēhi daḍhaṁ sēgā dappudhurēkavīrēhiṁ

āvāē ciya khittā disō disaṁ hariṇajūha vya

tō vīrasēṇapamuhā savarā savvē puṇō vi miliūṇa

annonnatajjaṇājaṇiyarōsapa marā samallīṇā

aha nijiō sa satyō kṣettaṇaō a sabarasēṇāē

payarō pivīliyāṇaṁ bhīmaṁ pi bhuyaṁgamaṁ ḍasaï

nijiṇiūṇa ya satthaṁ ritthaṁ ghettūṇa niravasēsaṁ pi

bandaṁ pi kiṁpi savarā uvaṭṭhiyā kālasēṇassa

bhaṇiyaṁ ca ṇēhiṁ. ēvaṁ ritthaṁ satthāō dēva āṇīyaṁ bandaṁ ca kiṁpi thēvaṁ. saṁpaï dēvō pamāṇaṁ ti. taō kālasēṇēṇa pucchiyā bandayapurisā. bhō kuō ēsa satthō kasta yā santiō tti. etthantaraṁmi sīhakayapahārasaṁrōhaṇanimittaṁ satthavāhaputtēṇa saṁhāgaō uvaladdhō pañcabhinnāō ṇēṇa saṁgamō nāma satyavāhaputtapurisō. bhaṇiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa. bhadda, kahiṁ tuma maē diṭṭhō tti. tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. na yāṇāmō, tuma cēva jāṇasi tti. kālasēṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. avi āsi tumaṁ iō uttarāvahapayaṭṭassa mama pāṇapayāṇahēuṇō avināyanāmadhē yassa satthavāhaputtassa samīvē. saṁgamēṇaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ. kō kahaṁ vā tuha pāṇapayāṇahēū. kālasēṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. atthi iō aīyavari saṁmi kayantēṇēva kēsariṇā kahaṁci kaṇṭhagayapāṇō ahaṁ kō āsi. taō iō uttarāvaha vaccamāṇa kēṇāvi satyavāhaputtēṇa na yāṇāmō kahiṁci jīvāviō mhi. tā ēvaṁ majjha sō pāṇapayāṇahēu tti. taō sumariūṇa vuttantaṁ pañcabhiyāṇiūṇa kāla sēṇaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ saṁgamēṇa. jaï ēvaṁ, tā āsi diṭṭhō tumaē. kālasēṇēṇa sabahumāṇamavaruṇḍiūṇa pucchiō saṁgamaō. bhadda, kahiṁ sō satthavāhaputtō. taō bāhajalabhariyalōyaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ saṁgamaraṇa. bhō mahāpurisa, devyō viyāṇaī ti. kālasēṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. kahaṁ viya. saṁgamaēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. suṇa, ēsō khu tassa santiō cēva satthō. āvaḍiē ya kōdaṇḍasarasahāō dihō maē sabarasaṁmuhaṁ dhāvamāṇō. tēō na saṁpayaṁ viyāṇāmi. taō ēyamāyaṇṇiūṇa dīhaṁ ca nīsasiya hā kayamakajja ti bhaṇiūṇa mōhamukgaō kālasēṇō, vakalāṇilēṇa vīiō savarēhiṁ, laddhā cēyaṇā. bhaṇiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa. harē, na ettha kōi vāvāiō tti. abarēhiṁ bhaṇiyaṁ. na vāvāiō, kēvalaṁ pahārīkō tti. taō nirūviyā paḍibaddhapurisā, na diṭṭhō ya dharaṇō. taō ēgattha ritthaṁ karēūṇa samā sāsiūṇa satthaṁ paḍibaddhapurisāṇa ya vaṇakammamāisiya dharaṇagavēsaṇanimittaṁ payaṭṭāviyā disō disaṁ sabarapurisā. appaṇā vi yē hā duṭṭhaṁ kayaṁ ti cintayamāṇō gaō taṁ gavēsiuṁ. na diṭṭhō ya tēṇa dharaṇō. samāgaō satthaṁ. miliyā savvasabarā. nivēiyaṁ ca ṇēhiṁ. dēva, na diṭṭhō tti. taō paraṁ sōgamukgaō kālasēṇō. bhaṇiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa—

dujaṇajaṇaṁmi sukayaṁ asuhaphalaṁ hōi sajjaṇajaṇassa

jaha bhuyagassa vidinaṁ khīraṁ pi visattaṇamuvēi

dinā ya ṇēṇa pāṇā majjhaṁ jāyāē taha ya puttassa

ēyassa maē puṇa sabvamēva vivarīyamāyariyaṁ

tā kiṁ ēiṇā ayālakusumaniggamēṇa viya nipphalēṇaṁ vāyāvittharēṇaṁ. bhō bhō satthiyā, bhō bhō sabarā, ēsā mahaṁ paīnnā. jaï taṁ na ghaḍēmi ahaṁ imiṇā vihavēṇa pañcahi diṇēhiṁ. païsāmi suhuyahuyavahajālānivahami kiṁ bahuṇā. ēvaṁ ca païnnaṁ kāūṇa kayaṁ kula dēvayāē kāyambarinivāsiṇīē ōvāiyaṁ.

jaï taṁ mahāṇubhāvaṁ jīvantaṁ estha kahavi pecchissaṁ

damahi purisēhi bhayavaï tō tujjha baliṁ karissāmi

ēvaṁ ca ōvāiyaṁ kāūṇa gahiyāṇēyadivasapāhēyā paṭṭaviyā dharaṇagavēsaṇanimittaṁ disō disaṁ sabarā. appaṇā vi ya añcantavi maṇadummaṇō gaō taṁ gavēsiuṁ.

sō puṇa dharaṇō viṇijjiē satthē na estha annō uvāō ti cintiūṇa ōsahivalayamettaritthō ghettūṇa lacchi palāṇō piṭṭaō mē kammapariṇaī; jēṇa piyayamāē vi īīsī avastha tti. lacchīē cintayaṁ. kilēsō vi mē bahumō cēva ēyassa āvaīē. gaviḍhaṁ dharaṇēṇa lacchīē pāṇasaṁdhāraṇanimitta phalōvayaṁ, na uṇa laddhati. aïkkantō vāsarō. pasunāī pallavasattharē. aïkantā rayaṇī. (ugaō aṁsumālī. taō) biiyadiyahē ya jāmamettasēsē vāsarē khudāpivāsāhibhūyā naggōhapāyavacchāyāē nivaḍiyā lacchī. saṁmilliyamimīē lōyaṇajuyaṁ, vimūḍhā sē cēyaṇā, nivaḍiyaṁ tāluyaṁ, milāyaṁ vayaṇakamalaṁ. taō dharaṇēṇa cintiyaṁ. ahō dāruṇō jīvalōgō, acintā kammapariṇaī, na mē jīviēṇāvi ettha sāhārō tti. tahāvi bāhajalabhariyalōyaṇēṇaṁ saṁvāhiyaṁ sē aṅga. samāgayā cēyaṇā. taō avvattasada jaṁpiyamimīē. ajjaütta, daḍhaṁ tisābhibhūya mhi. taō sō sundari, dhīrā hōhi, āṇēmi udaya, taē tāra ihēva ciṭṭiyavvaṁ ti bhaṇiūṇa ārūḍhō taruvaraṁ. palōiyaṁ udayaṁ, na uṇa ubaladdhaṁ. tō udayamantarēṇaṁ na ēsā jīvaï tti tuvariṭṭiyaṁ pecchiūṇa tīē ya kira rasēṇa saṁgayaṁ silībhūyamavi sōṇiyaṁ udayasāricchaṁ havaï ti tā ēēṇa sumariyapaōēṇaṁ dami sē tuvariṭriyā rasēṇaṁ saṁpāḍiōdayabhāvaṁ bāhusirāmokkhaṇēṇa niyamēva ruhiraṁ, imiṇā ya vaṇadavaggiṇā païūṇa chuhāvaṇōyaṇanimittaṁ ūrumaṁsaṁ ti; annahā nissaṁsaya na hōi ēsā, vivanāē ya imīē ki mahaṁ jīviēṇaṁ; atthi ya mē vaṇasaṁ gēhaṇaṁ ōsahivalayaṁ, tēṇa ruhirasaṁgaraṇēva avaṇīyavaṇa vēyaṇō imīē vi na dukkhakāraṇaṁ bhavissaï ti cintiūṇa niyacchuriyāē palāsapattapuḍayaṁmi saṁpāḍiyaṁ samīhiyaṁ ti. gaō ya tīsē samīvaṁ. bhaṇiyā ya ēsā. sundari, saṁpannamudayaṁ, tā piyaü sundarī. piyaṁ ca ṇāē. samāsatyā ēsā. uvaṇīyaṁ ca sē maṁsaṁ. bhaṇiyaṁ ṇēṇaṁ. sundari, payaṁ khu vaṇadavavivannasasayamaṁsaṁ, bhukkhiyā ya tuma, tā āhārasu ti. āhāriyamimīē. taō kaṁci vēlaṁ gamēūṇa payaṭṭāṇi diṇayarāṇusārēṇa uttarāmuhaṁ. pattāṇi ya mahāsaraṁ nāma nayaraṁ. atthamiō sūriō tti na paï hāṇi nayaraṁ. ṭhiyāṇi jakkhālaē. taō aïkantē jāmamettē jaṁpiyaṁ lacchīē. ajjaütta, tisābhibhūya mhi. dharaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. sundari, ciṭṭha tumaṁ, āṇēmi udayaṁ naīō. gahiō tattha vāraō, āṇīyamudayaṁ. pīyaṁ ca ṇāē. pasuttō dharaṇō. carimajāmaṁmi ya viuddhā lacchī. cintiyaṁ ca ṇāē. aṇukūlō mē vihī, jēṇa ēsō īisa avatthaṁ pāviō ti. tā kēṇa uvāēṇa iō vi ahiyayaraṁ sē havēja bhaṇiyaṁ cārakkhiyanarēhiṁ. arē, appamattā havējaha. gahiō khu ēsō, kahiṁ vaccaï tti. suyaṁ ca ēyaṁ lacchīē, āyaṇṇiō caṇḍa ruddapayasadō. cintiyaṁ ca ṇāē. bhaviyabvaṁ ettha kāraṇēṇa. tā pucchāmi ēyaṁ, kiṁ puṇa imaṁ ti. kayāi pujanti mē maṇōrahā. taō dīhasuṁkārapimuṇiyaṁ gayā caṇḍaruisamīvaṁ. pucchiō ēsō. bhadda, kō tuma, kiṁ vā ēē duvāradēsaṁmi imaṁ vāharanti. tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ । mundari, alaṁ maē. kiṁ tu pucchāmi sundariṁ avi atthi kahiṁci thēvamudayaṁ ti. tīē bhaṇiyaṁ. atthi, jaï mē paōyaṇaṁ sāhēsi. tō cintiyamaṇēṇaṁ. ahō dhīrayā itthiyāē, ahō sāhasaṁ, ahō vayaṇavinnāsō; tā bhaṇiyabamimīē pattabhūyāē tti. cintiūga jaṁpiyaṁ caṇḍaruddēṇaṁ. sundari, mahantī khu ēsā kahā, na saṁkhēvaō kahiuṁ pārīyaï. tahāvi suṇa. saṁpayaṁ tāva takarō ahaṁ, narindagē hāō gahēūṇa rayaṇabhaṇḍaṁ nīsarantō nayarāō uvaladdhō daṇḍavāsiēhiṁ. laggā mē maggaō bahuyā daṇḍavāsiyā, ēgō ya ahayaṁ. khīṇagamaṇasattī ya ettha paviṭhṭhō tti. ēē ya andhārayāē rayaṇīē sāvekkhayāē jīviyassa sāhāraṇayāē paōyaṇassa saṁpannaṁ ca ṇē ahilasiyaṁ ti mannamāṇā duvāradēsabhāyaṁ nirumbhiūṇa daṇḍavāsiyā ēvaṁ bāharanti. taō saṁpanna mē samīhiyaṁ, jaï vihī aṇuva vattissaï tti cintiūṇaṁ jaṁpiyaṁ lacchīē. bhadda, jaï ēvaṁ, tā alaṁ tē uvvēēṇaṁ; ahaṁ tuma jīvāvēmi, jaï mē vayaṇaṁ sugasi. caṇḍarudēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. āṇavēu sundarī. lacchīē bhaṇiyaṁ. suṇa. ahaṁ khu māyandīnivāsiṇō kattiyaseṭṭhissa dhūyā lacchimaī nāma pubbavēriēṇa vi ya pariṇīyā dharaṇēṇa. aṇiṭṭhō mē bhattārō, pasuttō ya ēsō ettha dēvaülē. tā aṅgīkarēhi maṁ, paricayasu mōsaṁ,pāvēu ēsō sakanmasarisaṁ gatiṁ. pahāyāē rayaṇīē gihīēhiṁ tubbhēhiṁ naravaïsamakkha pi bhaṇissāmi ēhayaṁ ēsō mahaṁ bhattārō, na uṇa ēsō tti. taō sō aō viyōṇaï mē taṁ agihīyanāma sabalōō cēva ettha mahiliyaṁ tti. lacchīē bhaṇiyaṁ. jaï ēvaṁ, tā kō puṇa iha uvāō. caṇḍa ruddēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. atthi ettha uvāō, jaï thēvamudayaṁ havaï. tīē bhaṇiyaṁ kahaṁ viya. caṇḍarudēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. suṇa. atthi mē cintā maṇirayaṇabhūyā bhayavayā khandaruddēṇa viiṇṇā diṭṭhapaccayā paradidvimōhaṇī nāma cōraguliyā. tīē ya udayapaṁjōēṇa aniēhiṁ nayaṇēhi sahassalōyaṇō dēvāhivō vi na pecchaï pāṇiṇaṁ, kimaṅga puṇa maccalōyavāsī jaṇō. lacchīē bhaṇiyaṁ. jaï ēvaṁ, tā karhi guliyā। caṇḍarudēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ uṭṭiyāē . lacchīē bhaṇiyaṁ. jaï ēvaṁ, tā kiṁ na abbhēsi. caṇḍarudēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ natthi udayaṁ ti. lacchīē bhaṇiyaṁ ahaṁ dēmi . caṇḍaruddēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ jīvāviō bhōīra. dinnamudayaṁ. duvēhi pi añjiyāī lōyaṇāī. bhaṇiyā ya ēsā.

sundari, aṇīṇiē satyavāhaputtami na taē gantavvaṁ ti. paḍissuyamimīē. muka rayaṇabhaṇḍaṁ dharaṇasamīvē. ṭhiyāī ēgadēsē. pahāyā rayaṇī. uḍhiō dharaṇō. mahiō ārakkhiēhi. nihāliyaṁ rayaṇabhaṇḍaṁ, uvaladdhaṁ ca tassa samīvē. taō nīṇiō dēva ulāō. baddhō khu ēsō. cintiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa. hanta kimēyaṁ ti. ahavā na kiṁci anna; avi ya paḍikūlassa vihiṇō viyambhiya ti. paḍikūlē ya ēyaṁmi amayaṁ pi hu visaṁ, rajjū vi ya kiṇhasappō, goppaïyaṁ pi sāyarō, aṇū vi ya girī, mūsayavivaraṁ pi rasāyalaṁ, suyaṇō vi dujaṇō, suō vi vaïirī, jāyā vi bhuyaṅgī, payāsō vi andhayāraṁ, khantī vi kōhō, mahavaṁ pi māṇō, ajjavaṁ pi māyā, saṁtōsō vi lōhō, saccaṁ pi aliyaṁ, piyaṁ pi pharusaṁ, kalattaṁ pi (mittaṁ pi) vēriō ti. tā kiṁ imiṇā vi cintiēṇaṁ. ēyarasa vasavattiṇō na tīraē annahā vaṭṭiuṁ. imāō vi ya kayatthaṇāō imaṁ mē ahiyaṁ bāhaï, jaṁ sā tavassiṇī adiṭṭhabandhuvirahā na dīsaï. ahavā varaṁ na diṭṭhā cēva. mā sā vi mē saṁsaggikalaṅkasiyā imaṁ cēva pāvissaï tti. cintayantō nīō rāyaülaṁ. appatthāvō narindassa tti dhaïriō rāya maggē. aïkantō vāsarō. avasarō ti kaliya nivēiō narindarasa. dēva, salottaō cēva māyāpaōyakusalō vāṇiyayavēsadhārī gahiō mahābhuyaṅgō. saṁpayaṁ dēvō pamāṇaṁ ti. taō rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ. kiṁ tēṇa, vāvāēha tti. nīō ṇēhiṁ pāṇavāḍayaṁ. samappiō rāyaülakamā gayāṇaṁ vahaniōgakārīṇaṁ paccaïyapāṇāṇaṁ. bhaṇiyā ya ēē. harē, dēvō samāisaï ēsa takarō vāvāiyavvō tti. tēhiṁ bhaṇiyaṁ. jaṁ dēvō āṇavēi ti. samappiūṇa tēsiṁ gayā ḍaṁḍavāsiyā. bhaṇiyaṁ caṇḍālamayaharēṇa. harē, kassa vāvāyaṇamāsabāraō. caṇḍālēhi bhaṇiyaṁ mōriyassa. tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. lahuṁ sadāvēha mōriya. sadāviō mōriō, āgaō ya. bhaṇiō mayaharēṇa. harē mōriya, ēsa takarō dēvēṇa pēsiō vāvāiyavvō ti. tā nēūṇa masāṇabhūmi lahuṁ vāvāēhi. jāmamettāvasēsō ya vāsarō, ēhi avāvāiē māraya ṇīē pamāō bhavissaï. mōriyaēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. jaṁ tuma bhaṇasi ti si samappiō mōriyayassa paccabhinnāō ya ṇēṇaṁ. kahaṁ sō cēva ēsō jīviyadāyaō mē satyavāhaputtō; ahō kaḍaṁ, imassa vi īīsī avastha ti cintiūṇa visaṇṇō mōriyō. cintiyaṁ ca ṇēṇaṁ. ahavā pāventi candadivāyarā vi muhuttamettaṁ gahakallōlāō āvaī. bahumaō ya mē sāmisālasamāēsō ēyassa daṁsaṇēṇaṁ. tā nēmi tāva ēvaṁ masāṇabhūmi. jāṇāmi ya imāō jahaṭṭiyaṁ vunantaṁ. nīō masāṇabhūmi, chōḍiyā bandhā, calaṇēsu nivaḍiūṇaṁ pucchiō ya ṇēṇaṁ. ajja, avi sumarēsima āyāmuhīē vimōiyaṁ. dharaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. bhadda, na muṭhṭha mumarēmi. mōriyaēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. kaha ṇa sumarēsi, jō bhavaṁ viya acōrō cēva cōrō tti kaliya gahiō ahaṁ mahayā daviṇajāēṇa pecchiūṇa naravaī taē vimōiō ti. dharaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. thēvamēyaṁ. mōriēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. tā sāhēu ajō, kahaṁ puṇa ajassa īisī atya tti. dharaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. bhadda, devvaṁ ettha pucchasu tti. mōriēṇa cintiyaṁ. na ettha kālakkhēvēṇa pēōyaṇaṁ, ahimāṇī ya ēsō kaha kēhaïsmaï. kiṁ vā kahiēṇaṁ. vicittāṇi vihiṇō vilasiyāṇi. tā kiṁ mamēiṇā nibbandhēṇa. ahavā kahiyaṁ cēvāṇēṇa paramatthaō devvaṁ pucchasu tti bhaṇamāṇēṇa. tā imaṁ tāva ettha patta yālaṁ, jaṁ ēsō ibhō lahuṁ visajjīyaï tti. cintiūṇa bhaṇiō khu ēsō. ajja, kiṁ bahuṇā jaṁpiēṇa; mottūṇa visāyaṁ lahuṁ avaïkamasu. dharaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. bhada, na khalu ahaṁ paramāṇēhiṁ attaṇō pāṇē rakkhēmi. tā vāvāēhi maṁ, niddēsakārī khu tuma ti. mōriēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. ajja, alaṁ majjha pāṇaviṇāsapaṅkāē. sattapurisō khu ēsa rāyā, na amhāṇaṁ abarāhasaē vi ya pāṇavārvattiṁ karēi. agacchamāṇē ya ajjē avassamahamappāṇaṁ vāvāēmi. tā gaccha u ajō. taō nathi avisaō sajaṇasiṇēhassa tti cintiūṇa jaṁpiyaṁ dharaṇēṇaṁ. bhadda, jaï ēvaṁ, tā avakamāmi. mōriēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. aṇuggihī bhō mhi. daṁsiō sē panthō. paṇamiūṇa ya niyattō mōriō. mittōvarō hēṇa palāṇō dharaṇō. cintiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa. aha kahiṁ puṇa sā muddhamayalōyaṇā bhavissaï. nūṇamuṁvarōhasīlayāē maṁ aṇuchaviya pāsavaṇani mittamuṭṭhiyā kēṇāvi takkarēṇaṁ samāsāiyā bhavē, nīyā ya ṇēṇaṁ, mama viṇāsāsaṅkiṇīē na jaṁpiyamimīē; annahā kahaṁ na diṭṭa tti. adaṁsaṇēṇaṁ ca tīsē vihalamēva pāṇalāhaṁ mannāmi tti. cintayantō payaṭṭō gavēsiuṁ. pahāō ujjuvāliyāē. iō ya sō caṇḍaruddō tō dēvaülāō abakamiūṇa gaō ujjuvāliyaṁ naī. cintiyaṁ ca ṇēṇaṁ. ahō dāruṇayā ityivaggassa, jamēsā ēgapaē cēva mahāvasaṇapāyālaṁmi pakkhiviya bhattāraṁ aṇavekkhiūṇa niyakulaṁ siviṇayaṁmi vi adiṭṭhapuvvēṇa maē saha payaṭṭa tti.

hā kiṁha dūrēṇa niyaṁ visavagdhabhuyaṅgasiddhasarahāṇaṁ

kalikālayaṇhirakkhasikayantacariyaṁ mahiliyāhi

asalilapaṅkaggāhī hōi khaṇēṇaṁ akandarā vagyō

aṇiyattā jamabhiuḍī aṇabbhavajāsaṇī mahilā

mahilā ālakulaïgharaṁ mahilā lōyaṁmi duccariyakhēta

mahilā duggaïdāraṁ mahilā jōṇī aṇatthāṇaṁ

vijju va cañcalāō mahilāu visaṁ va pamuhamahurāō. maccu va nigdhiṇāō pāvaṁ piva vajaṇijāō. tā alaṁ mē ēyāē; mā majjha pi iṇamēva saṁpāḍaïssaï ti cintiūṇa ghettūṇamaṅgalaggaṁ suvaṇayaṁ paricattā khu ēsā. cintiyaṁ ca tīē. tahāvi sōhaṇaṁ cetra ēyaṁ, jaṁ sō vācāiō ti. tā gacchāmi annattha. payaṭṭā naītīrāē. diṭṭhā dharaṇēṇa hārasavasupphullalōyaṇaṇaṁ. pucchiyā ēsā. sundāra, kuō tuma ti. tī sārō viu payattā bhaṇiyā ya ṇaṇaṁ. sundāra, mā rāva, iisī ēsa saṁsārō. āvayābhāyaṇaṁ khu ettha pāṇiṇō. tā alaṁ visāraṇa. dhannō ya ahayaṁ, jēṇa tumaṁ saṁpatta tti. taō tīē bhaṇiyaṁ. ajjaütta, pāsavaṇanimittamuṭṭhiyā gahiyā takaraṇa, itthīsahavāō ajjaüttasiṇēhāisaraṇa ya na kiṁpi vāhariyaṁ. aṇicchamāṇī ya itthiyā na gheppaḍa tti kariya musiūṇa ujjhiyā ihaī. annaṁ ca. takkarakayatthaṇāō vi mē ēyaṁ ahiyayaraṁ bāhaï, jaṁ tuma īisiṁ avattha mukgō diṭṭhō tti. taō na anahā mē viyappiyaṁ ti cintiūga bhaṇiyaṁ dharaṇēṇaṁ. sundari, thēmiyaṁ kāraṇaṁ. na mē uvvēvakāriṇō iyēmavatthā tuha daṁsaṇēṇaṁ. tā kiṁ ēiṇā. ēhi, gacchamha. cintiyaṁ ca ṇāē. ahō mē pāvapariṇaī, kayantamuhāō viēsa āgaotti. payaṭṭā ēsā. samāgayāiṁ viyāraüraṁ nāma sannivēsaṁ. kayā pāṇavittī. atyamiō sariō. aïvāhiyārayaṇī. cintiyaṁ dharaṇēṇaṁ. ēvaṁ kayantābhibhūyassa na juttamiha ciṭṭhiuṁ. tā parāṇēmi tāva ēvaṁ dantaüranivāsiṇō khandadēvamāulassa samīvaṁ pacchā jahājuttaṁ karessāmi tti. sāhiyaṁ lacchīē. bahumayaṁ ca tīē. payaṭṭāṇi dantaüraṁ.

iō ya na laddhō satthavāhaputtō tti saṁjāyasōēṇa paccaïyaniyayapurisāṇa samappiō satthō kālasēṇēṇa. bhaṇiyā ya ēē. harē, pāviyanvō tumhēhiṁ ēsa mahāṇubhāvassa gurūṇaṁ ti. cintiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa. jaï vi na saṁpannamōvāiyaṁ, tahāvi kāyambarīē jahā bhaṇiya mēva balivihāṇaṁ kāūṇa païnnaṁ pi tāva saphalaṁ karēmi tti. pēsiyā balipurisanimittaṁ sabarapurisā. karāviyā kāyambarīē pūyā, majjiō girinaīē, parihiyāī vakalāī, kayā kaṇavīramuṇḍamālā, rayāviyā mahāmahallakaṭṭhēhim̐ ciyā, payaṭṭō caṇḍiyāyayaṇaṁ. iō ya dantaürapatthiō biīyadiyahami aruṇuggamē cēva kāyambari paribhamantēhiṁ samāsāiō satyavāhaputtō kālasēṇasabarēhiṁ । baddhō vallirajjūē. payaṭṭāviō samahiliō cēva caṇḍiyāyayaṇaṁ. gaō thēvaṁ bhūmibhāgaṁ. didvaṁ ca ṇēṇa caṇḍiyāyayaṇapāsamaṇḍalaṁ. kīisaṁ. parisaḍiyajiṇṇarukkhagudēhiyakhaïyakaṭṭhasaṁghāyasaṁkulaṁ bhuyaṅgamihuṇasaṇāhaviyaḍavammīyaṁ parattamuhalasaü gagaṇakayavamālaṁ viyaḍata rukhandhabahalaruhirāyaḍḍiyatikhalasaṁghāyaṁ pāyavasāhāvabaddhamahisamēsamuhapucchakhurasiṅgasirōharācīranivahaṁ ti. avi ya—

vāyasasaüntasaṁvaliyagiddhavandrēhi vipphurantēhiṁ

paḍibaddhasūrakiraṇaṁ karaṅkakaliyaṁ masāṇaṁ va

gahabhūyajakkharakkhasapisāyasaṁjaṇiyahiyayapariōsaṁ

ruhirabalikhittapasamiyanissēsadharāraügghāyaṁ

taṁ ca ēvaguṇāhirāmaṁ caṇḍiyāyayaṇapāsamaṇḍalaṁ

sabhayaṁ vōliūṇa āyayaṇaṁ pecchiuṁ payattō

dhavalavaranarakalēvaravitthiṇṇuttuṅgaghaḍiyapāyāraṁ

unbhaḍakabandhaviraïyatōraṇapaḍibaddhasiramālaṁ

mayaṇāhavayaṇabhīsaṇaviraïyapāyārasiharasaṁghāyaṁ

uttuṅgavēṇulambiyadīharapoṇḍariyakattijhayaṁ

dīṇamuhapāsapiṇḍiyabandayabībhaccharuddhaōvāsaṁ

nisiyakaravālavāvaḍakarasabarajuvāṇapariyariyaṁ

visamasamāhayapaḍupaḍahasaddavittatthasaüṇasaṁghāyaṁ

accataruyantasadukkhasabarivilayājaṇāiṇṇaṁ

viyaḍagayadantanimmiyabhittisamukkinamūlasaṁghāyaṁ

takkhaṇamettukkattiyacammasamocchaïyagambhaharaṁ

purisavasāparipūriyakavālapajaliyamaṅgalapaīvaṁ

ḍajjhantavillaguggulupaviyambhiyadhūmasaṁghāyaṁ

savaravaharuhirakkhayagayamottiyaraïyasatthiyasaṇāhaṁ

candakaradhavaladīharaparilambiyacamarasaṁghāyaṁ

ruhirakasabālambiyadīharavaṇakōlavanbhaniurumbaṁ

kaṅkellipallavuppaṅkanimiyarēhantadharaṇitalaṁ

kōdaṇḍakhaggaghaṇṭayamahisāsurapucchavāvaḍakarāē. kaccāiṇipaḍimāē vihūsiyaṁ ghōrarūvāē. tō taṁ daṭṭhūṇa cintiyaṁ dharaṇēṇaṁ

sakkā sīhassa vaṇē palāiuṁ vāraṇassa ya tahēva

sukayassa dukkayassa ya bhaṇa kattha palāiuṁ sakkā

ēvaṁ ca cintayantō chūḍhō savarēhi vandramajhami

aha bandhiūṇa gāḍhaṁ puvvaviruddhēhi va khalē hi

etthantaraṁmi samāgaō caṇḍiyāyayaṇaṁ kālasēṇō, paḍiō caṇḍiyāē calaṇēsu, bhaṇiyaṁ ca sagaggayakkharaṁ. bhayavaï, jaï vi na kaō taē mahaṁ pasāō, tahāvi jammantarē vi jahā na ēvaṁ dukkhabhāyaṇaṁ havāmi, tahā tara kāyavvaṁ ti. satthavāhaputtāvayārakaraṇēṇa jaṁ mahaṁ dukkhaṁ, taṁ tumaṁ cēva jāṇasi tti bhaṇiūṇa bhaṇiō kuraṅgaō. harē, nivēēhi bhayavaīē baliṁ. tēṇa jaṁ dēvō āṇāvēi tti bhaṇiūṇa khittō ṇēṇa kēsēsu kaḍḍiūṇa bhayaparāyattasadhagattō duggilaō nāma lēhavāhaō. ḍhōiyaṁ rattacandaṇasaṇāhaṁ bhāyaṇaṁ. viyagapāgō viva cacciō duggilaō. kālasēṇēṇa kaḍḍiyaṁ vijjuchaḍāḍōvabhāsura maṇḍalaggaṁ, vāhiyaṁ īsi niyabhuyāsiharē. bhaginī va duggilō. bhadda, sudihēṁ jīvalōyaṁ karēhi. saggaṁ taē gantavvaṁ, jīviyaṁ mōtūṇa kiṁ vā tē saṁpāḍiyaü tti. taō bhayābhibhūēṇa na jaṁpiyaṁ duggila ēṇaṁ. puṇō vi bhaṇiō, puṇō vi na jaṁpiyaṁ ti. aṇāvūriyamaṇōrahō ya na vāvāijjaï tti visaṇō kālasēgō. taṁ ca daṭṭaṇa cintiyaṁ dharaṇēṇaṁ. hanta maē vi ēvaṁ mariyavvaṁ ti. tā varaṁ apecchiūṇa dīṇasattaghāyaṁ kāūṇa khaṇamettapāṇaparirakkhaṇēṇa imasma upayāraṁ paḍhama vivannō mhi. vāvaḍō ya mē viṇivāyakaraṇēsu kayantō,ēsō vi nivvuō havaü ti cintiūṇa bhaṇiō kuraṅgaō. bhadda,nivēēhi ēyassa mahāpurisassa, jahā bhayavisaṇṇō khu ēpō tabassī, tā kiṁ ēiṇā;aṇabhinnō ahaṁ patthaṇāē; tahāvi bhavaō paōyaṇaṁ pasāhaṇīyaṁ cēva patthēmi ēgaṁ patthaṇaṁ ti. nivēiyaṁ kālasēṇassa. bhaṇiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa. jīviyaṁ mottūṇa patthēu bhahō ti. dharaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. mōtūṇa ēvaṁ maṁvāyāpasutti. tō bāhajalabhariyalōyaṇēṇa ahē kō uṇa ēsō parōvayāratalicchayāē appāṇayaṁ vāvāyaṇē samappēi sumarāvēi mē sattha vāhaputtaṁti bhaṇiūṇa mucchiō kālasēṇō, nivaḍiō dharaṇivaṭṭhē. vījiō kisōraēṇa. laddhā cēyaṇā. bhaṇiyaṁ ṇēṇa. bhadda kisōraya, nirūvēhi ēyaṁ, kō uṇa ēsō mahāṇubhāvō satyavāha puttassa ceṭṭhiyaṁ aṇukarēi. nirūviūṇa bhaṇiyaṁ kisōraēṇa. bhō imāē aṇamnasarisīē āgiīē sō cēvē mē paḍihāyaï tti. tā sayamēva nirūvēu pallīvaī. taō harisavisāyagambhiṇaṁ nirūviō ṇēṇa pañcabhinnāō ya. chorḍiyā sē bandhā. khaggaṁ mottūṇa niviḍiō calaṇēsu. bhaṇiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa. satthavāhaputta, khamiyanyō maha avarāhō. dharaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. bhō mahāpurisa, ahippēyaphalasāhaṇēṇa guṇō khu ēsō, kahamavarāhō tti kālasēṇēṇa cintiyaṁ. nūṇaṁ na ēsa mēṁ paccabhijāṇaï tti, tēṇa ēvaṁ mantēi tā payāsēmi sē attāṇayaṁ. bhaṇiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa. satyavāha putta, kiṁ tē ahippēyaṁ phalaṁ sāhiya ti. dharaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. bhadda, patthuē vāvāyaṇē ēyaṁ ujjhiūga mamēva maraṇamaṇōrahāvūraṇaṁ ti. kālasēṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. satthavāha putta, kiṁ tē imassa nivvēyāisayassa maraṇavavasāyassa kāraṇaṁ. dharaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. bhō mahāpurisa, alamiyāṇi ēyāē kahāē. saṁpāḍēu bhavaṁ attaṇō samīhiyaṁ ti. taō ahō sē mahāṇubhāvaya ti cintiūṇa bhaṇiyaṁ kālasēṇēṇa. satthavāhaputta, na sumarēsi maṁ sī haviṇi vāiyaṁ nāgapōyayaṁ piva attaṇō viṇāsanimittaṁ attaṇā cēva jīvāviūṇa kayagghasēharayabhūyaṁ kālasēṇaṁ. jīvāvibhō ahaṁ taē. maē puṇa kaō tujha paccuvayārō; viōiō tubhaṁ sasthāō, pāviō ya appatta puvvaṁ imaṁ īisiṁ avatthaṁ ti. taō sumariūṇa puvyavuttantaṁ pañca hiyāṇiūṇa ya kālasēṇaṁ lajāvaṇayavaṣaṇaṁ jaṁpiyaṁ dharaṇēṇa. bhō mahāpurisa, kō ahaṁ jīvāviyavvassa, tuha cēva puṇṇapariṇaī ēsa tti. kahaṁ ca tumaṁ kayagyō, jō diṭṭametta vi jaṇē annāṇō kiṁpi kāūṇa ēvaṁ khijjasi tti. tā alamēiṇā. aha kiṁ puṇa imaṁ patthuyaṁ ti. taō la jāparāhīṇēṇa na jaṁpiyaṁ kālasēṇēṇa. sāhiyaṁ ca niravasēsamēva saṁgamadaṁsaṇāiyaṁ niyapāṇapariccāyavavasāyāva sāṇaṁ ceṭṭhiyaṁ ti kisōraēṇaṁ. taō ahō sē kayannuyā, ahō thirasiṇēhayā, ahō mahāṇubhāvaya ti cintiūṇa jaṁpiyaṁ dharaṇēṇa. bhō mahāpurisa, juttamēva gurudēvapūyaṇaṁ pupphabaligandhacandaṇēhiṁ, na uṇa pāṇighāēṇaṁ. avi ya—

hōjā jalē vijalaṇōṁ hōjā khīraṁ pi gōvisāṇāō

amayarasō vi visāō na ya hiṁsāō havaï dhammō

dāūṇa ya ahiōyaṁ dēvayajannāṇa jē khalu abhavvā

ghāyanti jiyasayāī pāventi duhāi tē naraē

tā virama ēyāō vavasāyāō ti. kālasēgēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. jaṁ tuma āṇavēsitti. taō gāmadēsalūḍaṇē annābhāvē ya bhavakhaṇanimittaṁ ca mottūṇa kō aṇēṇa kāyambariaḍa vipaviṭṭhassa satthassa pāṇighāyaṇassa jāvajjīvibhō niyamō. phullabaligandhacandaṇēhiṁ pūiyā dēvayā. nīō ṇēṇa sayalabandasaṁgaō niyagēhamēva dharaṇō. kaō uciō uvayārō.

bhututtarakālaṁmi ya uvaṇīyaṁ sē samattharitthaṁ ti

sabarāhivēṇa turiyaṁ gahiyaṁ jaṁ satthabhaṅgami

karikumbhasamutthāṇi ya mahallamuttāhalāi parāī

dantā ya gayavarāṇaṁ camarāṇi ya jaccacamarīṇaṁ

dhettūṇa ya taṁ ritthaṁ dāūṇa ya kiṁci bandayāṇaṁ pi

viharaha jahāsuhēṇaṁ maṇiūṇa visajjiyā tēṇaṁ

dharaṇō vi kālasēṇapīīē tatva kaṁci kālaṁ gamēūṇa visajjiō kālasēṇēṇa, payaṭṭō niyayapuri, pattō ya kālakkamēṇaṁ. [vināō ammāpiīhiṁ nāyarēhi ya] parituṭṭhō sē guruyaṇō. niggayā nayarimahantayā. paccuvekkhiyaṁ bhaṇḍaṁ saṁkhiyaṁ ca mollēṇaṁ nāva savāyā kōḍi tti. iō aïkkantē addhamāsē āgaō dēvanandī. tassa vi ya niggayā nayarimahantayā. paccuvekkhiyaṁ bhaṇḍaṁ saṁkhiyaṁ ca mollēṇaṁ jāva addhakōḍi ti. taō viliō dēvanandī. samaṇiyaṁ paürabhaṇḍamollaṁ. sē sēṇa ya paramagōrahasaṁpāyaṇēṇa saphalaṁ purisabhāvamavaṇuhavantassa āgayā mayaṇatērasī. bhaṇiō ya ēsō nayarimahantarahiṁ nīsarēhi rahabaraṁ. dharaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ—

alaṁ bālakīḍāē. pasaṁsiō nayarimahanta ēhiṁ.

aïkāntō ya sē kōi kālō paratthasaṁpāyaṇasuhamaṇuhavantassa. niōiyapāyaṁ ca ṇēṇa niyabhuōbajjiyaṁ daviṇajāyaṁ. samuppanā ya sē cintā. avassamēva purisēṇa uttamakulapamaēṇa tivaggō sēviyabyō. taṁ jahā, dhammō atthō kāmō ya. tattha aparicattasavvasaṁgēṇa attha pahāṇēṇa hōyavvaṁ ti. tō cēva tassa duvē saṁpajjanti. taṁ jahā, dhammō ya kāmō ya. annaṁ ca, ēsa atthō nāma mahantaṁ dēvayārūvaṁ । ēsō khu purisassa bahumāṇaṁ vaïddhāvēi, gōvaṁ jaṇēi, mahagghayaṁ uppāēi, sōhaggaṁ karēi, chāyāmāvahaï, kulaṁ payāsēi, rūvaṁ payāsēi, buddhi payāsēi. atthavantō hi purisā adentā vi lōyāṇaṁ salāhaṇijjā havanti. jaṁ cetra karenti, taṁ caïva tēsiṁ asōhaṇaṁ pi sōhaṇaṁ vaṇṇi jaē. abhaggapaṇaïpatthaṇaṁ ca aṇuvanti paratthasaṁpāyaṇamuhaṁ. tā jaï vi ēsa maha puncapurisōvajjiō aïpabhūō atthi, tahāvi alaṁ tēṇa gurupaṇaïṇisamāṇēṇa. tā annaṁ uvajiṇēmi, gacchāmi disāvaṇijjēṇaṁ ti. cintiūga vinattā jaṇaṇijaṇayā. aṇumaniyō ya ṇēhiṁ gaō mahayā satyēṇaṁ samahiliō puncasamuddataḍaniviṭṭhuṁ vē jayanti nāma nayariṁ. diṭṭhō naravaī. bahumanniō ya ṇēṇaṁ. niōiyaṁ bhaṇḍaṁ, na samāsāiō iṭṭhalābhō. cintiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa. samāgaō cēva jalanihitaḍaṁ. tā gacchāmi tāva paratīraṁ. tattha mē gayassa kayāi ahilasiyapaōyaṇasiddhī bhavissaï tti. gahiya paratīragāmiyaṁ bhaṇḍaṁ. saṁjattiyaṁ pavahaṇaṁ. pasatthatihikaraṇajōgēṇa niggaō nayarīō, gaō samuddatīraṁ, pūiō atthijagō, agghiō jalanihī. tō candiūṇa gurudēvaē uvārūḍhō jāṇavattaṁ. āgaḍiyāō vēgahāriṇīō silāō, pūriō siyavaḍō, vimukkaṁ jāṇavataṁ, gammaē cīṇadīvaṁ ti.

annayā ya aïkkantēsu kaïvayadiṇēsu kusalapurisavimukkē viya nārāē vahantē jāṇavattē gayaṇayalamajjhasaṁhiē diṇayaraṁmi āgampa yantō viya mēiṇiṁ dhuṇantō viya samudaṁ ummūlantō viya kula lajālāṇi payaṭṭō māruō. tō ēravaṇō viya gulagulentō paḍisotta vāhiyasariyāmuhaṁ khuhiō mahaṇṇavō, visaṇṇā nijāmagā. taō samaṁ gamaṇārambhēṇa ōsāriō siyavaḍō, jīviyāsā viya vimukkā naṅga rasilā nijāmaēhiṁ. tahāvi ya tattha kaści vēlaṁ gamēūṇa vivannaṁ jāṇavattaṁ. jīviyasēsayāē samāsāiyaṁ phaïlagaṁ, ahōrattēṇa laḍiūṇa jalanihiṁ suvaṇṇadīvami laggō satyavāhaputtō. cintiyaṁ ca ṇēṇaṁ. ahō pariṇaī dēivvassa. na yāṇāmi avatthaṁ piyayamāē pariyaṇassa ya. avā kiṁ visāēṇaṁ. ēsō cēva etya pamāṇaṁ ti. taō kayalaphalēhiṁ saṁpāiyā pāṇavittī. atthamiō sūriō. kaō ṇēṇa pallavasattharō, sīyāvaṇayaṇatthaṁ ca araṇīpaōēṇa pāḍiō jalaṇō. taïppiūga kaṁci kālaṁ paṇamiūṇa gurudēvaē ya pasuttō ēsō. aïkantā rayaṇī, viuddhō ya. uggō asumālī. diṭṭhaṁ ca ṇēṇa taṁ jalaṇacchikkaṁ savvamēva suvaṇṇīhūyaṁ dhaïraṇikhaḍaṁ. cintiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa. ahō ēvaṁ khu dhāukhēta; tā pāḍēmi ettha suvaṇayaṁ ti. kayāō īṭṭayāō, aṅkiyāō dharaṇanāmaēṇa, ullayāṇaṁ cēva saṁpāiyā saṁpuḍā, pakkā ya suvaṇṇamayā jāyā. ēvaṁ ca kayā ṇēṇa dasa īṭṭayasaṁpuḍasahassā. nibaddhō bhinnapōyaddhaō.

iō ya cīṇāō cēva suvayaṇasatthavāhaputtasantiyaṁ asārabhaṇḍabhariyaṁ anadīvalaggasaṁpāviyalacchisahiyaṁ dēvaüragāmiyaṁ samāgayaṁ tamuddēsaṁ jāṇavattaṁ. diṭṭhō ya bhinnapōyaddhō satyavāhēṇaṁ. lambiyā ya naṅgarā suvayaṇāēsēṇa. samāgayā nijāmagā. diṭṭhō ya ṇēhi dharaṇō bhaṇiō ya. bhō bhō mahāpurisa, ēsō cīṇavatthavvagō dēvaüragāmī jāṇavattasaṁṭhiō suvayaṇō nāma sasthavāhaputtō bhaṇaï, jahā ēhi kūlaṁ gacchamha. dharaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. bhadda, kiṁbhaṇḍabhariyaṁ khu taṁ jāṇavataṁ. nijāmarahiṁ bhaṇiyaṁ. ajja, vihivasēṇa pari vaḍiō khu ēsō satyavāhaputtō vihavēṇa, na uṇa pōrusēṇaṁ. tā na suṭṭhu sārabhaṇḍabhariyaṁ ti. dharaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. jaï ēvaṁ, tā aṇu varōhēṇaṁ āgacchaü aïttiyaṁ bhūmi satthavāhaputtō. nivēiyaṁ suvayaṇassa. āgaō ya ēsō, bhaṇiō dharaṇēṇa. satthavāhaputta, na taē kuppiyavvaṁ, paōyaṇaṁ udisiūṇa kiṁci pucchāmi tti. suvayaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. bhaṇāu ajō. dharaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. kē ttiyassa tē daviṇajāyassa jāṇavataṁmi ritthaṁ. sutrayaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. ajja, dēvassa paḍikūlayāē viṇaṭṭhō khu ahayaṁ. tahāvi purisayārō na mottavvō tti ucchāhamettabhaṇḍamollō suvaṇṇasahassamettassa ghettūṇa kiṁpi bhaṇḍaṁ dēvaüraṁ payaṭṭō mhi. dharaṇēga bhaṇiyaṁ. jaï ēvaṁ, tā paricaya taṁ bhaṇḍaṁ, bharēhi mē santiyamsa suvaṣṇassa jāṇavataṁ; kūlapattassa ya bhavō payacchissaṁ suvaṇṇalakkhaṁ ti. suvayaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. kiṁ suvaṇṇalakkhēṇa, tumaṁ cēva bahuō ti. ujhiyaṁ puvvabhaṇḍaṁ. bhariyaṁ suvaṇṇassa. ṭhāviyā saṁkhā. uvārūḍhō dharaṇō. diṭṭhā ya ṇēṇa lacchī. parituṭṭhō ēsa hiyaēṇaṁ dūmiyā ya ēsā. jāyā mahaṁ ēsa ti sāhiyaṁ suvayaṇassa dharaṇēṇaṁ. āṇandiō ēsō. payarṭa jāṇavattaṁ. gayaṁ pañcajōyaṇamettaṁ bhūmibhāgaṁ.

etthantaraṁmi gayaṇayalacāriṇī vēgāgamaṇēṇāgampayannī samudaṁ ayālavijjū viya asuhayā lōyaṇāṇaṁ arē rē dusatthavāhaputta, akaōvayārō aṇaṇujāṇiyaṁ maē karhi imaṁ maīyaṁ daviṇajāyaṁ geṇhiūṇa gacchasi tti bhaṇamāṇī suṣaṇṇadīvasāmiṇī samāgayā suvaṇṇanāmā vāṇamaṁtarī. dhariyaṁ jāṇavataṁ, bhaṇiyaṁ ca ṇāē. bhō bhō nijāmayā, adāūṇa purisabaliṁ na ettha atthō gheppaï tā purisabaliṁ vā dēha, atthaṁ vā muyaha, vāvāēmi vā ahayaṁ ti dharaṇēga cintiyaṁ. ahō ṇu khalu muyāviō niyayaritthaṁ suvayaṇō, uvayārī ya ēsō lacchī saṁpāyaṇēṇa, ēsā ya ēvaṁ bhaṇāi. tā imaṁ etya pattayālaṁ, ahamēva purisabalī havāmi tti. cintiūṇa bhaṇiyā vāṇamaṁtarī. bhayavaï, ayāṇamāṇēṇa maē ēvaṁ kvasiyaṁ. tā pasīya. ahamēva ettha balipurisō; ma paḍicchasu tti. tīē bhaṇiyaṁ. jaï ēvaṁ, tā ghattēhi appāṇayaṁ samuddē, jēṇa tē vāvāēmi tti. lacchīē cintiyaṁ. aṇuggihīyā bhayavaīē. taō dharaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. vayassa suvayaṇa, pāviyavvā taē lacchī maha gurūṇaṁti. bhaṇiūṇa pavāhiō appā. viddhō ya ṇāē sūlēṇa, nīō suvaṇṇa dīvaṁ. uvasantā cāṇamaṁtarī. payarṭa jāṇavattaṁ dēvaürāhimuhaṁ.

etthantaraṁmi divō ya ēsō kaṇṭhagayapāṇō suvēlāō raṇadīvaṁ patthiēṇaṁ hēmakuṇḍalēṇaṁ, pañcabhinnāō ya ṇēṇa. puvapariciyā ya sā hēmakuṇḍalassa vāṇamaṁtarī. taō hā kimēyamaka jamaṇuciṭṭhiyaṁ ni bhaṇiūṇa mōyāviō vāṇamatarīō. puṣabhaṇiōsahivalayavaïyarēṇa kayaṁ sē vaṇakammaṁ. jīviyasēsēṇa ya pannattō ēsō pañcabhinnāō ya ṇēṇa hēmakuṇḍalō. pucchiō dharaṇēṇaṁ lirivijayabuttantō. sāhiō hēmakuṇḍalēṇa, jahā jīviō sō mahāṇubhāvō tti. parituṭṭhō dharaṇō. hēmakuṇḍalō ya ghettūṇa dharaṇaṁ payaṭṭō rayaṇadīvaṁ. pattō ya ayaṅgagandhavvasundarījaṇāraddhamahuragēyaravāyaḍḍiyadinnāvahāṇanicalaṭṭhiyamayajūhaṁ dariyaṣaṇakōlaghōṇāhighāyaja jariyamahiyalucchaliya mutthākasāyasurahigandhavāsiyadisāyakaṁ tīratarukhuḍiyakusumamayarandavāsiyāsēsavimalajaladullaliyarāyahaṁsāulasara pahassaliyaṁ maha llatarusiharāvaḍiyakusumaniyaraciyavitthiṇṇabhūmimāgaṁ uddāmanāgavallīnivahasamāliṅgiyāsēsapūgaphalīsaṇḍaṁ viyaḍadhaṇa surahimandāra mandirāradavijāhāmihuṇaraïsuhaṁ dariyavaṇahatthipīvarakarāyaḍḍaṇabhaggasamuttuṅgagalanta candaṇavaṇaṁ tīrāsanadviyaṣaṇatamālataruvī hiōhasi yajalahijalaṁ taruṇataruviyaḍamaṇaharālavālayajalasahiyavivihavihaṁganiyaravāpūriuddēsaṁ siddhavijāharalamuttuṅgara yaṇagirimaṇāhaṁ dīvaṁ bhagnasamuttuṅgagalacandanavana tīrāsannatthitaghanatamālāruvīthyupahasitajaladhijalaṁ taruṇataruvikaṭṭhamanōharālavālajalamuhitavividhavihaṅgani nāmēṇa rayaṇasāraṁ ti. avi ya—

rayaṇāyarēṇa dhaṇiyaṁ viyaḍatara gucchalantabāhāhiṁ

savvattō piyakāmiṇiruirasarīraṁ va uvagūḍhaṁ

saṁpāviūṇa phalaharanamiyamahīruhanamijjamāṇō vya

pariṇayakhuḍantabahuvihatarukusumōvaṇiyapūō va

kamalamahupāṇasēvaṇajaṇiyakalālāvamuhalabhamarēhiṁ. kayasāgayasammāṇō vdha aïṁgaō cūyatarusaṇḍaṁ. uvaviṭhṭhō dīhiyātīraṁmi, vīsa miō muhuttayaṁ, gahiyāī sahayāraphalāī, majjiyaṁ dīhiyāē, kayā pāṇavittī. pucchiō hēmakuṇḍa lēṇa dharaṇō. kahaṁ tuma imīē pāviō tti. sāhiō ṇēṇa jahaḍiō sayalavuttantō. hēmakuṇḍa lēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. ahō sē kūrahiyayattaṇaṁ; tā kiṁ ēiṇā, bhaṇa kiṁ tē karīyaü tti. dharaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. kayaṁ sayalakaraṇijja; kiṁ tu dutthiyā mē jāyā, tā tīē saṁjōyaṁ mē karēhi। tō rayaṇagirīō pahāṇarayaṇasaṁjuyaṁ saṁjōēmi ti cintiūṇa bhaṇiyaṁ hēmakuṇḍalēṇaṁ. karēmi saṁjōyaṁ, kiṁ tu atthi ihēva dīmi rayaṇagirī nāma pavvayō. tattha sulōyaṇō nāma kinnarakumāraō mē mittō parivasaï. tā taṁ pecchiūṇa nēmi taṁ dēvaüramēva. tahiṁ gayassa niyamēṇēva tīē saha saṁjōgō bhavissaï tti. paṁḍissuyaṁ dharaṇēṇa. tī ghettūṇa dharaṇaṁ payaṭṭō rayaṇapavvayaṁ. pattō ya mahuramāruyamandandōlentakayalisaṁghāyaṁ. saṁghāyamiliyakipurisajakkhaparihattavaṇaraṇḍaṁ.

vaṇasaṇḍavivihaphalarasasaṁtuṭṭhavihaṁgaïsadagambhīraṁ

gambhīrajalahigajjiyahitthapiōsattasiddhayaṇaṁ

siddhayaṇamiliyacāraṇasiharavaṇāra mahurasaṁgīyaṁ

saṁgīyamurayaghōsāṇandiyanañcantasihiniyaraṁ

sihiniyaravukkaṇṭhiyapasannavarasiddhakinnarinihāyaṁ

kinarinihāyasēviyalavaṅgalavalīharacchāya

chāyāvantamaṇō haramaṇiyaḍavilasantarayaṇani urumbaṁ

niurumbaṭṭhiuppēhaḍasiharuppēyaṁ ca rayaṇagiri

taō ya taṁ pāviūṇa mahāmahallu nurayaṇasiharuppaṅkaniruddharaviraha maggaṁ vivihavarasiddhavijāharaṅgaṇālaliyagamaṇacalaṇālattayarasara ñjiyavitthiṇṇamuttāsilāyalaṁ darivivaraviṇiggayaninjharajharantajhaṁkāraravāyaḍḍiyadariyavaṇahatthiniyarasamāiṇṇaviyaḍakaḍaüddēsaṁ uddāmāha vīlayāharucchaṅganiddayarayāyāsakhinnasuhapasuttavijāharamihuṇaṁ aïkōuhallēṇa āruhiuṁ payattō. kiha

cāliyalavaṅgalavalīcandaṇagandhukkaḍēṇa sisirēṇa

avaṇijjantaparissamasaṁtāvō mahurapavaṇēṇa

pecchantō ya ruiradarimandirāmalamaṇibhittisaṁkantapaḍimāvalōyaṇapaṇayakuviyapasāyaṇūsuyadaïyadaṁsaṇāhiyakuviyaviya sahiyaṇōha siyamuddhamiddhaṅgaṇāsaṇāhaṁ, katthaï ya payāracaliyavaracamariniyaranīhārāmalacandamaūhanimmaluddāmacamaracavalavikkhēvavīi jamāṇaṁ, katthaï ya siddhāṅganāsanātham niyambōvaïyaviyaḍaghaṇagajjiyāyaṇṇaṇubbhantadhuyasaḍājālanahayalucchaṅganimiyakamadariyamayaṇāharuñjiyaravāriuddēsaṁ, annattha sarasaghaṇa candaṇavaṇucchaṅgavivihaparihāsakīlāṇandiyabhuyaṅgamihuṇaramaṇijjaṁ ti. taō āruhiūṇa rayaṇasiharaṁ rayaṇagiritilayabhūyaṁ tattha ya bālakayalīpariveḍhiyaviyaḍapīḍhaṁ sōhāviṇijiyasurindabhavaṇaṁ uttuṅgatōraṇakhambhanimiyavarasālibhaciyāsaṇāī maṇaharālekkha vicitta viyaḍabhittiṁ ruiragavakkhavēiōvasōhiaṁ nimmalamaṇikoṭṭhimaṁ surahikusumasaṁpāiyapūōvayāraṁ ca gaō sulōyaṇasantiyaṁ mandiraṁ ti. diṭṭhō ya ṇēṇa gandhavvadattāē saha vīṇaṁ vāyantō sulōyaṇō. anbhuṭṭhiō sulōyaṇēṇaṁ. saṁpāiō sē uciōvayārō. pucchiō sulōyaṇēṇaṁ hēmakuṇḍalō. kuō bhavaṁ kuō vā ēsa mahāpurisō kiṁnimittaṁ vā bhavaō āgamaṇapaōyaṇaṁ ti. taō suvēlāō niyaṁ dharaṇassa suvaṇṇabhūmimuvalanbhāiyaṁ cintiyarayaṇappadāṇapajjavasāṇaṁ sāhiyamāgamaṇapaōyaṇaṁ. tēṇa vi upphullalōyaṇēṇa paḍissuyaṁ । taō ciṭṭhiūṇa kaïvayadiyahē gahiyāī pahāṇarayaṇāī. nīō ya ṇēṇa dharaṇō dēvaüraṁ. mukkō nayarabāhiriyāē, samappiyāṇi sē raïyaṇāṇi. bhaṇiō ya ēsō. ihaḍiō cēva jāyaṁ paḍivālamu ti. paḍissuyaṁ dharaṇēṇa. gaō hēmakuṇḍalō. dharaṇō puṇa bāhiriyāē cēva kaści vēlaṁ gamēūṇa paviṭṭhō nayaraṁ. diṭṭhō ya ṭoppaseṭṭhiṇā. ahō kallāṇāgiī adiṭhṭhapuvvō ēgāgī ya dīsaï, tā bhaviyavvaṁ ettha kāraṇēṇaṁ ti cintiūṇa ahimayasaṁbhāsaṇapurassaraṁ nīō gēṇa gēhaṁ. kaō uvayārō. pucchiō ya seṭṭhiṇā kuō tumaṁ ti. sāhiō ṇēṇa māyandinivāsaniggamaṇāiō dēvaürasaṁpattipajjavasāṇō niyayavuttantō. samappiyāī rayaṇāī. bhaṇiō ya ṇēṇa seṭṭhī. ēyāī saṁgōvāvasu tti. saṁgōvāviyāṇi seṭṭhiṇā.

iō ya dharaṇasamuddapaḍaṇasamaṇantaramēva samāsāsiyā sukkhaṇēṇa lacchī. bhaṇiyā ya ṇēṇa. sundari, īisō aïsa saṁsārō, viyōgā vasāṇāi etya saṁgayāī tā na taē saṁtappiyanvaṁ. na vivanō ya ēsa tujjha avi ya majjhaṁ ti. taō niyaḍippahāṇāē bāhajala bhariyalōyaṇaṁ jaṁpiyaṁ lacchīē. taē jīvamāṇami kō mahaṁ saṁtāpō ti. tō aïkkantēmu kaïvayadiṇēsu jāṇavattasaṁṭhiyaṁ pahūyaṁ suvaṇṇamavalōiūṇa cintiyaṁ suvayaṇēṇaṁ. vivannō khu sō tabassī, païbhūyaṁ ca ēvaṁ daviṇajāya, taruṇā ya sē bhāriyā rūpavaī ya, saṁgayā ya mē cittēṇa; tā kiṁ ettha juttaṁ ti. ahavā iyamēva juttaṁ, jaṁ imīē gahaṇaṁ ti. kō nāma abālisō sayamēvāgayaṁ lacchi paricayaï. tā geṇhāmi ēyaṁ. taō parihāsasajjhā itthiya tti viyaḍanāyagāṇurūṣā kayā parihāsā, āvajjiyaṁ sē hiyayaṁ. niviṭhṭhō ghariṇisahō. attaḍhiyaṁ suvaṇṇayaṁ. akkantā kaïvi diyahā. samāgayaṁ kūlaṁ jāṇavattaṁ. mahayā darisaṇijjēṇa diṭṭhō sutra yaṇēṇa naravaī. parituṭṭhō ēsō. ussukamēva tuha jāṇavanē ti kaō sē pasāō. gaō jāṇavattaṁ.

etthantaraṁmi cīṇadīvāō āgayaṁ jāṇavattaṁ ti muṇiūṇa niggaō dharaṇō. diṭṭhō ya ṇēṇa sukkhaṇō lacchī ya. parituṭṭhō hiya ēṇaṁ, dūmiyā lacchī suvayaṇō ya. din sē āsaṇaṁ, pucchiō vuttantaṁ, sāhiō jēṇē. taō muvayaṇēṇa cintiyaṁ. ahō mē kammapari ṇaī, ahō paḍikūlayā devvassa. kēvaḷaṁ kayamakajja, na saṁpannaṁ samīhiyaṁ ti. cintiūṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. aja, sōhaṇaṁ saṁjāyaṁ, jaṁ tuma jīviō. tā geṇhāhi ēyaṁ niyayaritthaṁ ti. dharaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. satthavāhaputta, pāṇā vi ēē tuha saïntiyā, jēṇa lacchīē saha samāgamō kaō, kimaṅga puṇa ritthaṁ ti. aïkkantā kāi vēlā. bhaṇiyā ya lacchī gēṇa. ēhi, nayaraṁ pavisamha. lacchīē bhaṇiyaṁ. ajjaütta, kallaṁ visissāmō, ajja uṇa ajjaüttēṇāvi ihēva vasiyadhvaṁ ti. paḍissuyamaṇēṇa. abhaṅgiō ēsō. ālōciyaṁ ca lacchīē suvayaṇēṇa ya. jahā, ajjēva ēvaṁ kayapāṇabhōyaṇaṁ kēṇaï uvāēga rayaṇīē vāvāissāmō tti. majiō ēsō, pāiō mahaṁ, kārāviō pāṇa vittiṁ. aïkkantō vāsarō, samāgayā rayaṇī, atthuyaṁ sayaṇijja. nivaṇṇō ēsō lacchī ya. taō mayaparāhīṇassa simiṇaē viya avaïttaṁ ceṭṭhamaṇuhavantassa dinō imīē galē pāsaō, vaïliō ya ēsō. pariōsaviyasiyacchīē lacchīē suvayaṇēṇa ya vimūḍhō dharaṇō maō tti kāūṇa ujjhiō jalanihitaḍē. gayāiṁ jāṇavattaṁ. jalanihipavaṇasaṁgamēṇa ya samāsatthō ēsō. cintiyaṁ ca ṇēṇaṁ. hanta kimayaṁ ti. kiṁ tāva suviṇaō āō indajālaṁ āō maïvibbhamō āō saccayaṁ cēva tti. uvaladdhaṁ jalanihitaḍaṁ. saccaṁ cēva tti jāō sē vinicchaō. uḍhiūga cintiyamaṇēṇa. ahō lacchīē cariya, ahō suvayaṇassa pōrusaṁ. ahavā durdaïguṁṭhō viya ummagga patthiyā, kiṁpāgaphalabhōgō viya magulāvasāṇā, dussāhiyakiccē va dōsuppāyaṇī, kālarattī viya tamōvalittā, īīsā cēva mahiliyā hōi. avi ya

jalaṇō vi gheppaï suhaṁ pavaṇō bhuyagō ya kēṇaï naēṇa. mahilāmaṇō na gheppaï bahuēhi vi nayasahassēhiṁ. tā kiṁ imīē. suvayaṇassa na juttamēyaṁ ti. ahavā maïrā viya mayarāyabaḍhaṇī cē isthiyā havaï tti. visayavisamōhiyamaṇēṇaṁ tēṇāvi ēvaṁ vavasiyaṁ ti.

ēvaṁ ca cintayantō seṭṭhiniuttēhi kahavi purisēhiṁ

sūruggamavēlāē diṭṭhō bāhollanayaṇēhiṁ

bhaṇiō ya ṇēhiṁ. satyavāhaputta, rayaṇīē, na āgaō tumaṁ ti saṁjāyāsaṅkēṇa rayaṇīē cēva tujjha anēsaṇanimittaṁ pēsiyā amhē ṭoppasē dviṇa tti. kahakahavi diṭṭhō si saṁpayaṁ. tā ēhi, gacchamha, nivvavēhi aṇēyacintāṇalapalittaṁ seṭṭhihiyayaṁ. taō ahō purisā mantaraṁ ti cintiūṇa payaṭṭō dharaṇō, paviṭṭhō nayariṁ, diṭṭhō ya ṇēṇa seṭṭhī. païrikami bhaṇiō seṭṭhiṇā. baccha, kuō tumaṁ kiṁ vā vimaṇadummaṇō dīsasi tti. taō lajjāvaṇijayaṁ aṇācikkhaṇīyamēyaṁ ti cintiūṇa vāhollalōyaṇēṇa nē japiyaṁ dharaṇēṇa. seṭṭhiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ. vaccha, suyaṁ maē, jahā āgayaṁ jāṇavattaṁ cīṇāō, tā taṁ tumaē uvaladdhaṁ na vatti. tō sagaggayakakhara jaṁpiyaṁ dharaṇēṇaṁ. ajja, uvaladdhaṁ ti. sōgāirēgēṇa ya pavattaṁ sē bāhasalilaṁ. taō nūṇaṁ vivannā sē bhāriyā, annahā kahaṁ īisō sōgapasarō tti cintiūṇa bhaṇiyaṁ ṭoppaseṭṭhiṇā. vaccha, avi taṁ cēva taṁ jāṇavattaṁ ti. dharaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ āma. seṭṭhiyā bhaṇiyaṁ. avi kusalaṁ tē bhāriyāē. dharaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. ajja, kusalaṁ. seṭṭhiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ. tā kimannaṁ tē uvvēvakāraṇaṁ. dharaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. ajja, na kiṁci acikkhiyavvaṁ ti. seṭṭhiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ tāki vimaṇō si. dharaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ āma. sedviṇā bhaṇiyaṁ kimāma. dharaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ ēyaṁ . sēhigā bhaṇiyaṁ kimayaṁ . dharaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ na kiṁci. seṭṭhiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ. vaccha, kimēēhiṁ munnabhāsiēhiṁ. acikkha sabbhāvaṁ. na ya ahaṁ ajoggō ācivikhayabassa, paḍivannō ya taē gurū. taō na juttaṁ guruāṇākhaṇḍaṇaṁ ti cintiūṇa jaṁpiyaṁ dharaṇēṇa. ajja, aja ssa āṇa ti kariya īisa pi bhāsīyaï tti. seṭṭhiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ. vaccha, natthi avisaō guruyaṇāṇuvattīē. dharaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. ajja, jaï ēvaṁ, tā kusalaṁ mē bhāriyāē jīviēṇaṁ, na uṇa sīlēṇaṁ. sedviṇā bhaṇiyaṁ. kahaṁ viyāṇasi. dharaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ kajjaō. seṭṭhiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ. vaha viya. taō ācikkhiō sē bhōyaṇāiō jalanihitaḍapajjavasāṇō sayalavuttantō. taṁ ca sōūṇa kuviō ṭoppa seṭṭhī suvayaṇassa. parisaṁṭhaviya dharaṇaṁ gaō naravaïsamīvaṁ. viśnattō ṇēṇa suvayaṇaṁ paï jahaṭṭhiyamēva narabaī. sadāviō rāiṇā muvayaṇō,bhaṇiō kulakamāgayaṁ. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ. bhāriyā kahaṁ ti. tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. guruviiṇṇā. taō pulaïō ṭoppaseṭṭhī. bhaṇiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa. dēva, savvaṁ aliyaṁ ti. sutrayaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. kiṁ puṇa ettha sañcayaṁ. seṭṭhiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ. dharaṇasantiyaṁ ritthaṁ bhāriyā yā ēyaṁ saccayaṁ ti. taō saṁkhu ddhahiyaēṇaṁ jaṁpiyaṁ sutrayaṇēṇa. bhō bhō aüvvajōisiya, kō ettha pañcaō; rāyakulaṁ khu ēyaṁ. ṭoppaseṭṭhiṇā bhagiyaṁ sāhāraṇaṁ rāyakulaṁ; paccaō puṇa, sō cēva jīvaï tti. suvayaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. mahārāya, na maē dharaṇassa nāma pi āyaṇṇiyaṁ ti. parikkhaü dēvō. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ. bhō bhō sēhi, āṇēhi dharaṇaṁ, tuma pitaṁ mahiliyaṁ ti. pēsiyā ṇēhi saha rāyapurisēhiṁ niyayapurisā. āṇiō ya ṇēhi hiyaēṇāṇiccha māṇō vi seṭṭhiubarōhabhāviyacittō dharaṇō, iyarēhi ya bhayahitthahiyayā lacchitti pulaïyāī rāiṇā, bhaṇiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa. sundari, diṭṭhō taē ēsa karmipi satthavāhaputtō. tīē bhaṇiyaṁ. dēva. na diṭṭhō tti. taō pucchiō dharaṇō. satyavāhaputta, avi ēsā tē bhāriyā. dharaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. dēva, kimaṇēṇa pucchiēṇa; suyaṁ cēva dēvēṇaṁ, jaṁ jaṁpiyamimīē. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ. satyavāhayutta, aō cēva pucchāmi. dharaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. dēva, jaï ēvaṁ dēvasta aṇubandhō, tā āsi bhāriyā, na uṇa saṁpayaṁ ti. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ. ēmō satyavāha puttō viṭṭhō taē āsi. dharaṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. dēva, ēsō cetra jāṇaï ti. rāiṇā bhaṇiō suvayaṇō. satyavāha putta; kiṁ viṭṭhō tumaē ēsa kahipi. sukkhaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. dēva, maē tāva ēsō na diṭṭhō tiṁ. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ. hōu, kiṁ ēiṇā; sāhēha tubbhē kiṁ ettha rittha māṇaṁ. suvayaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. dēva, ettha khalu dasasahassāṇi sōvaṇṇigāṇa iṭāsaṁpuḍāṇaṁ, anaṁ pi thēvayaṁ khu surittaṁ bhaṇḍaṁ ti. pucchiō iyarō vi. dharaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. dēva, ēvamēyaṁ. rāigā bhaṇiyaṁ. bhō kiṁpamāṇā khu tē saṁpuḍā. dharaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. dēva, na yāṇāmi. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ. kahaṁ niyayabhaṇḍassa vi pamāṇaṁ na yāṇāsi. dharaṇēṇaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ. dēva, ēvaṁ cēva tē kayā, jēṇa na jāṇāmi. taō pucchiō suvayaṇō. bhadda, tumaṁ sāhēhi. tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. dēva, ahamavi nissaṁsayaṁ na yāṇāmi. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ. bhō ēvaṁ vavatthiē kiṁ maē kāyabvaṁ ti. dharaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. dēva, thēgamēya' kāraṇaṁ. kiṁ bahuṇā jaṁpiēṇaṁ. avivāugō ahaṁ ēyassa; tā giṇḍaü ritthaṁ bhāriyaṁ ca ēsō tti. mukkhaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. bhō mahāpurisa! ēyaṁ pi bhavaō pahūyamēva, jaṁ mē ālō na dinō tti. dharaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. pasiddhō ahaṁ āladāyagō. suvayaṇēga bhaṇiyaṁ. jaï na āladāyagō, tā kimēyaṁ patthuyaṁ ti. ṭōpasē dviṇā bhaṇiyaṁ. arē rē nillajja pāvakamma, ēvaṁ pi vahariuṁ ēvaṁ jaṁpasi tti. puṇō vi amarisāisaraṇa bhaṇiyaṁ ṭoppaseṭṭhigā. mahārāya, kiṁ bahuṇā jaṁpiēṇaṁ. jaï ēyaṁ na dharaṇasantiyaṁ ritvaṁ ēlā yē bhāriyā, tā majjha sabassasahiyā pāṇā niyaraṇaṁ ti. āṇāvēu dēvō mayalē divvē ti. dharaṇēṇaṁ cintiyaṁ. avahariō khu ēsō maha siṇēhāṇubandhēṇa tā na juttaṁ saṁpayaṁ pi udāsīṇayaṁ kāuṁti. jaṁpiyamaṇēṇa. dēva, jā pattha aṇubandhō tāyassa, tā alaṁ divvēhi; annō vi ettha āō atthi cēva. rāiṇā bhagiyaṁ. kahēhi, kīisō uvāō ti. dharaṇēṇa maṇiyaṁ. dēva, tē maē saṁpuḍā sanāmēṇaṁ va aṅkiya tti. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ । kiṁ tujjha nāma. dharaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. dēva, dharaṇō ti. iyarō vi pucchiō. tēṇa bhagiyaṁ. dēva, suvayaṇō tti. rāiṇā maṇiyaṁ. jaï ēvaṁ, tō chinnō khu bāha.rō; navaraṁ āṇēha etyēva kavi saṁpuḍē tti. taō pēsiyaṁ paścaülaṁ, āṇiyā saṁpuḍā, nihā liyā rāiṇā bāhiṁ, na diḍhē dharaṇanāmayaṁ. bhaṇiyaṁ ca ṇa. bhō natthi ettha dharaṇanāmayaṁ. sutrayaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. dēvō pamāṇaṁ ti. annaṁ ca dēva, dēvasta puraō ēsa mahantaṁ pi aliyaṁ jaṁpiūṇa ajja vi pāṇē dhārēi tti. jāṇiyaṁ dēvēṇa, jaṁ ēēṇa pamāṇīkayaṁ. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ. bhō dharaṇa kimayaṁ ti. dharaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. dēva, na annahā ēyaṁ phōḍāviūṇa majjhaṁ nirūvēū dēvō. taō ēyamā yaṇṇiūṇa saṁkhuddhō subayaṇō, harisiō ṭoppaseṭṭhī. sadāviyā suvaṇṇayārā, phōḍāviyā saṁpuḍā, diṭṭhaṁ dharaganāmayaṁ. kuviō rāyā sukkhaṇassa lacchīē ya. bhaṇiyaṁ ca mēṇaṁ. harē vāvāēha ēvaṁ vāṇiyagavēsadhāriṇaṁ mahābhuyaṁgaṁ, nibāsēha ya ēyaṁ mama rajjāō vivanna sīlajīviyaṁ alacchi, samappēha ya samatthamēva ritthaṁ dharaṇasatthavāhassa. annaṁ ca bhaṇa, bhō mahāpurisa, kiṁ tē avaraṁ kīraü. dharaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. dēva, alaṁ mē ritthēṇa. karēu dēvō pasāyaṁ suvayaṇasta abhayappayāṇē. tō ahō sē mahāṇubhāvaya tti cintiūṇa bhaṇiya rāiṇā. satyavāhaputta, na juttamēya, tahāvi alaṅghaṇīyavayaṇō tumaṁ ti; tā tumaṁ cēva jāṇasi. dharaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. dēvapasāō tti, aṇu ggihīō ahaṁ dēvēṇa. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ. bhō satthavāhaputta, geṇhāhi niyayaritthaṁ. dhaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. jaṁ dēvō āṇavēi. taō narinda paścaülāhiḍiō saha suvayaṇēṇaṁ gaō vēlāulaṁ dharaṇō, uvagaṇiyaṁ suvaṇṇaya paṁcaülēga, samappiyaṁ dharaṇassa. taō dharaṇēṇaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ. bhī suvayaṇa! paricaya visāyaṁ, aṅgīkarēhi pōrusaṁ, devyōvarōhēṇa kassa yā khaliyaṁ na jāyaï tti. annaṁ ca, bhaṇiō maē tujjha suvaṇṇalakkhō, taē puṇa mahāṇubhāvattaṇēṇa ahamēva bahumanniō, na uṇa suvaṇṇalakkhō. bhaṇiyaṁ ca taē āsi kiṁ suvaṇṇalakkhēṇa, tumaṁ cēva mē bahumō tti. agagdhēyaṁ ca ēvaṁ saṁbhamāyaṇaṁ. tā gelhāhi saṁpayaṁ, jaṁ tē paḍihāyaï. ēvaṁ ca bhaṇiō samāṇō lajiō suvayaṇō. na jaṁpiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa. taō dāūga aṭṭha supaṇṇalakkhē saṁpūiūṇa naravaī taō kāuṁ sayalasutthaṁ bhaṇḍassa gaō ṭoppaseṭṭhi gēhaṁ. ṭiō kaṁci vēlaṁ saha seṭṭhiṇā. uvagayāē bhōyaṇavēlāē kayamajjaṇā pabhuttā ēē. bhuttuttarakālē.ya calaṇēsu nivaḍiūṇa bhaṇiō dharaṇēṇa ṭoppaseṭṭhī. jāēmi ahaṁ kiṁci vatthu tāya, jaï na karēi mama paṇayabhaṅgaṁ tāō. tō harisavasupphullalōyaṇēṇa ahō ahaṁ kayatthō, ahō ahaṁ dhanō, ahō mama sunīviyaṁ, ahō mama suladdhō jammō tti, jaō īisēṇāvi mahāṇubhāvēṇa sayalasatta kappatarukappēṇa tihuyaṇacintāmaṇībhūēṇa vi ahaṁ patthi jāmi ti cintiūṇa bhaṇiyaṁ ṭoppaseṭṭhiṇā. vaccha, jaha vi sakalattaṁ saputta pariyaṇaṁ dāsattanimittaṁ mamaṁ jāēsi, tahāvi ahaṁ tuha mahāpurisacedviēṇa ākari siyacittō na khaṇḍēmi tē patthaṇāpaṇayaṁ. dharaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. tāya, jaï ēvaṁ tā dēhi tinni vāyāō. īsi vihasiūṇa jāya, jō ēgaṁ vāyaṁ loppaï, sō tinni vi loppayantō kiṁ kēṇāvi dhariuṁ pārīyaï tti bhaṇiūṇa ṭoppaseṭṭhiṇā ka.yāō tini vāyāō. tāya, aṇuggihīō tti bhaṇiūṇa hēmakuṇḍalavi jāharavidinamaïhagdhēyapubbasamappiyarayaṇasahassaṁ maggiō ṭoppaseṭṭhibhaṇḍāriō. tēṇa vi ya jaṁ ajjō āṇavēi tti bhaṇiūṇa sama ppiyāī gahiūṇa rayaṇāī. taō tāṇa majjhē addhaṁ gahēūṇa ṭoppaseṭṭhissa calaṇapūyaṁ kāūṇa puṇō vi ṇivaḍiō pāēmu tāya, ēsā sā patthaṇa ti bhaṇamāṇō dharaṇō. taō aha kahaṁ chaliō ahamaṇēṇaṁ ti suira cininaūṇa agahiē ya vilakkhībhavissā ēsō, nivāriō ahaṁ imiṇā aṇāgayaṁ cēva uḍhaviyō dharaṇō vaccha, paḍivannā tē patthaṇā bhaṇamāṇēṇa ṭoppasē dviṇā.

taō bahumaniō seṭṭhiṇā mahayā satyēṇa samāgaō niyayanayariṁ. āvāsiō bāhiṁ. jāō lōyavāō, jahā āgaō dharaṇō tti. niggaō rāyā paccōṇiṁ. pavēsiō ṇēṇa mahāvibhūīē. nēūṇa niyayabhavaṇaṁ, pūiō majjaṇāiṇā niyābharaṇapajjavasāṇamuvayāra ppayāṇēṇaṁ. gō niyayabhavaṇaṁ. tuṭṭhā ya sē jaṇaṇijaṇayā. viiṇṇaṁ mahādāṇaṁ, kayā savvāyayaṇēsu pūyā. aïkantā kāi vēlā. taō uvaṇimantiyaṁ mahārāyaṁ pūiō aṇēṇē savisēsaṁ. sammāṇiyā ya jahāruhapaḍivattīē paüracāuvējōiyā, paḍipūiō ya tēhiṁ. taō pucchiō jaṇaṇijaṇaēhiṁ. vaccha, avi kahiṁ tē dhēriṇi ti. dharaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. alaṁ tīē kahāē. cintiyaṁ ca ṇēhiṁ. hanta kayaṁ tīē, jaṁ itthiuciyaṁ. tā alaṁ imassa mammaghaṭṭaṇēṇa imiṇā jaṁpiēṇaṁ. annō avagacchisaṁ ti. etthantarami mahāpurisayākhittahiyaō vimhayavasēṇupphullalōyaṇō karyamuddaṅgasāsaṇāvaṇanimittaṁ puṇō vi dharaṇasamīvaṁ samāgaō rāyā. kaō dharaṇēṇa samuciōvayārō. pucchiō ya āgamaṇapaōyaṇaṁ. siṭṭhō sē niyayāhippāō rāiṇā. tō calaṇēsa nivaḍiūṇa bhaṇiyaṁ dharaṇēṇa. dēva, alaṁ muddaṅgēḍiṁ; kiṁtu māṇaṇīō dēvō tti kariya patthēmi patthaṇīyaṁ. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ. bhaṇāu ajō. tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. payacchaü dēvō niyarajjē savva sattāṇaṁ bandimokkhaṇaṁ savvasattāṇamabhayappayāṇaṁ caï. tō ahō sē mahāṇubhāvayā, ahō mahāpurisaceṭṭhiyaṁ satyavāhaputtassa tti bhaṇiūṇa āṇattō paḍihārō. harē kāravēhi cārayaghaṇṭapaōēṇa mama rajjē sayalabandimokkhaṁ, savvasattāṇamabhayapayāṇaṁ ca davāvēhi tti. tō jaṁ dēvō āṇavēī ti bhaṇiūṇa saṁpāḍiyaṁ dēvasāsaṇaṁ. sappurisaceṭṭiēṇa ya parituṭṭhā sē jaṇaṇijaṇayā. pariōsa viyasiyacchēhi kayamaṇēhiṁ rāiṇō uciyaṁ karaṇijjaṁ. taō dharaṇēṇa saha kaṁci vēlaṁ gamēūṇa niggaō rāyā. dharaṇō vi cirayālamiliyavayaṁsayasamēō gaō malayasundarābhihāṇaṁ ujjāṇaṁ. uvaladdhō ya nāgalayāmaṇḍabaṁmi kīlānimitta māgaō kuviyaṁ piyapaṇaïṇiṁ pasāyantō rēvilaïṁgō nāma kulaüttagō. sumariyaṁ lacchīē. cintiyaṁ ca ṇēṇaṁ. ahō ṇu khalu ēvamaē vēlāṁ gamayitvā nirgatō rājā.

ramatthapecchīṇi kāminaṇa hiyayāī havanti. samāgaō saṁvēgaṁ. gaō ya ujjāṇēkadēsasaṁṭhiyaṁ asōyavīhiyaṁ.

diṭṭhō ya ṇēṇa tahiyaṁ phāyadēsaṁmi viyaliyaviyārō

sīsagaṇasaṁparibuḍō āyariō arahadattō ti

añcantasuddhacittō nāṇī vivihatavasōsiyasarīrō

nijiyamayaṇō vi dahēṁ aṇaṅgasuhasiddhitallicchō

taṁ pecchiūṇa cintā jāyā dharaṇassa ēsa lōyaṁmi

jīvaï saphalaṁ ēkō cattō jēṇaṁ gharāvāsō

ghariṇī atthō sayaṇō māyā ya piyā ya jīvalōyaṁmi

māindajālasarisā tahavi jaṇō pāvamāyaraï

jā vi uvayārabuddhī pariṇīpamuhēsu sā vi mōhaphalaṁ

mōtūṇa jaō dhamma na maraṇadhammīṇamukkhārō

sō puṇa

saṁpāḍēuṁ na tīraē āsavāniyattēhiṁ

āsavaviṇivittī vi ya gihāsamaṁ āvasantēhiṁ

niyamā tatyārambhō ārambhēṇaṁ ca vaḍuī hiṁsā

hiṁsāē kō dhammō na dēsiō satthayārēhiṁ

pajantē vi ya ēsō samvēṇaṁ cēva jīvalōyaṁmi

niyamēṇamujjhiyavvō tā alamēēṇa pāvaṇaṁ

ēvaṁ ca cintayantō pattō saṁjāyacaraṇapariṇāmō

gurupāyamūlamaṇahaṁ saṁvayaṁsō nivvuipuraṁ va

aha vandiō ya ṇēṇaṁ bhagavaṁ savayaṁsaraṇa sāhū ya

tēhiṁ ciya dhammalāhō dinō savvēsi vihipuvvaṁ

upaviṭṭhā ya muvimalē muṇīṇa puraō u uvavaṇucchaṅgē

aha pucchiyā ya guruṇā kattō tumbhē ti mahuragiraṁ

ēvaṁ ca pucchiē samāṇē jaṁpiyaṁ dharaṇēṇa. bhayavaṁ, iō cēva amhē. annaṁ ca; atthi mē gihāsamaparicāyabuddhī. tā āisaü bha yavaṁ, jaṁ maē kāyavvaṁ ti. tō ahō sē āgiī, ahō vivēgō tti cintiūṇa āsayaparikkhaṇanimittaṁ aṁpiyaṁ araïhayattēṇaṁ. vaccha, paricattagihāsamēṇaṁ nibhacchiūṇa niyaniyavisayalālasāī indiyāī vijjhaviya kasāyāṇalaṁ nirī hēṇaṁ cittēṇaṁ sayalasokkhanihāga bhūō saṁjamō kāyayō. annahā paricattō vi aparicattō gihāsamō tti. sō puṇa aṇāivisayabhāvaṇābhāviyassa jīvassa accanta dukkhayarō. pavajiūṇa vi ēvaṁ puncakayakammadō sēṇa kēi na taranti parivāliuṁ, mujjhanti niyayakajjē, parikappenti asayālamba ṇāī; vimukkasaṁjamā ya tē, āusō, na gihī na pāiyagā ubhayalōgavihalaṁ nāsanti maṇuyattaṇaṁ. ēvaṁ vavatthiē amuṇiūṇa hēō vāēyāī atuliūṇamappāṇayaṁ na juttō gihāsamapariccāō tti. dharaṇēṇaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ. ēvamēyaṁ, jaṁ tumbhē āṇavēha. kiṁtu hēō gihāsamō mē buddhī samaṇataṇaṁ uvārayaṁ. tulaṇā vi vivēgō cciya kilēsavasayāṇa sattāṇaṁ. bhayavayā cintiyaṁ. ahō sē saüṇṇayā, muṇiō ṇēṇa jahaḍiō saṁsārō, samuppannā jigadhammabōhī. tā pasaṁsēmi ēvaṁ sāhēmi ya imassa imīē dullahattaṇaṁ, jēṇa vayaṁsagāṇa vi sē saṁbōhō samupajjaï. bhaṇiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa. vaccha, dhannō tuma, nāyaṁ taē jāṇiyanvaṁ, saṁpattā sēyalalōyadulla hā jiṇadhammabōhī. tā jaïhaṭṭhiyāsēvaṇēṇa ēvaṁ cēva saphalaṁ karēhi, saṁsijjhaï ya tu: samīhiyaṁ. na khalu aṇabhatthaniraïyārakusalamaggā ēvaṁvihā havanti, avi ya aparamatthapecchiṇō visayalōluyā ya. ēyavaïyaraṁ ca nisuṇēhi mē cariyaṁ. dharaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ kahēu bhayavaṁ. arahadattāyariēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. suṇa.

atthi ihēba vāsē ayala uraṁ nāma nayaraṁ. tattha jiyasattū rāyā, pum̐ttā ya sē abarājiō samarakēū ya. aparājiō juvarāyā, iyarō ya kumārō. dinnā imassa kumārabhuttīē ujjēṇī. ēvaṁ ca aïkkantō kōi kālō. annayā ya vithakkō mārakērī nāma pañcantanaravaī. taō aparājiō tappasāhaṇanimittaṁ gaō. pasāhiō ya ēsō. āgacchamāṇēṇa ya muttimantō viya puṇṇōdaō saṁpatō imēṇa dhammārāmasannivēsē sayalamaṇōrahacintāmaṇī rāhō nāma āyariō tti. taṁ ca daṭṭhūṇa samuppannō ēyassa saṁvēgō. pucchiō ṇēṇa jēhāvihīē dhammō. kahiō bhayavayā jahōvaïṭṭhō paramagurūhiṁ. paḍibuddhō ya ēsō. khaōvasamamuvagayaṁ cāritta mōhaṇīyaṁ. taō māindajālasarisaṁ jīvalōyamavagacchiya pavaïō ēsō. karēi tavasaṁjamujjōyaṁ. annayā ya gurupāyamūlaṁmi ahā saṁjamaṁ viharamāṇō gaō tagarāsannivēsa. etthantaraṁmi samāgayā tattha ujjēṇīō raühāyariyassa antēvāsiṇō ajarāhukhamāsamaṇa santiyā gurusamīvaṁ sāhuṇō tti. kayā sē uciyapaḍiba tti pucchiyā niruvasaggavihāram ujjēṇīē. kahiō ya ṇēhiṁ mundarō vihārō; kēvalaṁ rāyaputtō purōhiyaputtō ya abhaddayā, tē jahōvaladdhīē khaliyārenti sāhuṇō, tanimittō uvasaggō tti. taō ēyamāyaṇṇiya cintiyamavarājiēṇa. ahō pamattayā samarakē ugō, jēṇa pariyaṇaṁ pi na niyamēi. tī aṇunaviya guruṁ gacchāmi aha mujjēṇi. upasāmēmi tē kumārē, mā saṁciṇantu abōhimūlāī. saṁsārabaddhaṇē ya sāhupaōsō. atthi mē taduvasāmaṇasattī. taō aṇunaviya guruṁ pēsiō guruṇā samāgaō ujjēṇiṁ, paviṭṭhō ya ajjarāhukhamāsamaṇagacchē. kayaṁ sē uciyakaraṇijja. samāgayā bhikkhāvēlā. payaṭṭō ēsō. bhaṇiō ya sāhūhiṁ. pāhuṇayā tubbhē, tā acchaha tti. tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. na acchāmi, attaladdhiō ahaṁ, navaraṁ ṭhavaṇakuṁlāīṇi daṁsēha. taō dinō sē cellaō, dasiyāṇi kulāṇi, vāriō ya ṇēṇaṁ ēyaṁ paḍaṇīyagēhaṁ; mā pavi senjama ti bhaṇiūṇa niyattō cellaō. paviṭṭhō ya ēsō paḍhamamēva kumāragēhaṁ. mahayā saddēṇa dhammalāhiyamaṇēṇaṁ. taṁ ca daṭṭaṇa bhīyāō antēuriyāō. hā kaṭṭhuṁ, isī kayatthijissaï ti cintiūṇa saniō ya ṇāhiṁ lahu nigacchasu tti. taō ava hīriūṇa baïhirāviḍaṁ ca kāūṇa mahayā saddēṇa dhammalāhiyamaṇēṇaṁ. etthantaraṁmi dhammalāhasadaṁ sōūṇa hammiyatalāō pahaṭṭamuhapaṅkayā samāgayā kumārayā. kiyaṁ duvāraṁ. aïsaēṇaṁ vandiō ṇēhiṁ sāhū. kayaṁ dhammalāhaṇaṁ. bhaṇiō ya ṇēhiṁ. bhō pabvaïyagā, naccasu tti. tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. kahaṁ gīyavāiēṇa viṇā nacāmi. kumārēhi bhaṇiyaṁ. amhē gīyavāiyaṁ karēmō. sāhuṇā bhaṇiyaṁ mundaraṁ tti. visamatālaṁ kayaṁ gīyavāiyamaṇēhiṁ. akuddhō vi hiyaēṇaṁ kuddhō sāhū. bhaṇiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa. arē rē gōvāladārayā, imiṇā vināṇēṇa mamaṁ naccāvēha tti. ēyaṁ sōūṇa kuviyā kumārā, sāhutāḍaṇanimittaṁ ca dhāviyā abhimuhaṁ. tēṇa vi ya na annō uvāō tti kaliūṇa karuṇāpahāṇacittēṇa nijjuddhavāvārakusalēṇaṁ saṇiyaṁ cēva vētūṇa savvasaṁdhīsu viōiō ēkō. taō dhāviō duiō, sō vi tahēva. taō duvāramugghā ḍiūga gaō sāhū. ēgantē ṭhiō sajjhāyajōgēṇaṁ. iyarē vi niccedvā tahēva ciṭṭhanti. divā pariya ṇēga, udaēṇa siściūṇa sasaṁbhamaṁ vāhittā, jāva na jaṁpanti, taō nivēiyaṁ rāyapurōhiyāṇaṁ, jahā imiṇā vuttantēṇa kēṇaï sāhuṇā kumārā ēvaṁ kaya ti. taō tē nirūviūṇa āyariyasamīvaṁ gaō rāyā. paṇamiō ya ṇēṇāyariō, bhaṇiō ya. bhayavaṁ, khamēha ēyamavarāhaṁ bālayāṇaṁ. āyariēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. kimēyaṁ ti nāvagacchāmi. kahiō sē vuttantō rāiṇā. tō āyariēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. vīyarāgasāsaṇasaṁpāyaṇarēyā tappahāvō viiyaparamatthā paralōyabhīruyattaṇēṇa ya ihalōyasarīrē daḍhamapaḍibandhayāē khamenti sayalasattāṇaṁ sāhuṇō na puṇa pāṇabhaēṇaṁ ti. tahāvi kāraṇaṁ paï samāyariyaṁ jaï kēṇāvi bhavē, taō pucchāvēmi sāhuṇō. taō āyariēṇa pucchiyā sāhuṇō. tēhiṁ bhaṇiyaṁ. bhayavaṁ, na amhē viyāṇāmō tti. āyariēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. mahārāya, nēyamiha sāhūhiṁ vavasiyaṁ. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ. bhayavaṁ, sāhuṇā na ettha saṁdēhō. āyariēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. mahārāya, jaï ēvaṁ, tā ēvaṁ bhavissaï. atthi ēgō āgantugō sāha tēṇēyamaṇuciṭṭhiyaṁ bhavē. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ. bhayavaṁ, kahiṁ puṇa sō sāhū. āyariēṇa
