atthamiyaṁmi diṇayarē daïyaṁmi va baḍhiyāṇurāyami

rayaṇivahū sōēṇa va tamēṇa turiyaṁ tō gahiyā

avahatthiyamittē dujjaṇē va pattē pabhōsasamayaṁmi

cakkāī bhaēṇa va vihaḍiyāi annonnaniravekkhaṁ

āsannacandapiyayamasamāgamāē va nāyalasirīē

diyaha sirimāṇajaṇayaṁ gahiyaṁ varatārayāharaṇaṁ

puvvadisāvahuvayaṇaṁ tōsēṇa va niyasamāgamakaraṇaṁ

ujjōventō jōhānivahēṇa samuggaō candō

māṇaṁsiṇīṇa māṇō mayalacchaṇacandimāē chippantō

agaṇiya sahiuvaēsaṁ naṭṭhō ghaṇatimiranivahō ca

puvadisāē nivaḍiyā sasisaṅgāṇandabāhabindu dha

jāyā kajalakalusā tamabhariyā dharaṇivivarōhā

mayaṇadhaṇujīvarāvō na maṇaharō turiyakhalaṇagamaṇēṇa

ahisāriyāṇa nēuracalavalayarakō pavitthariō

ullasiyarikkharayaṇaṁ viyambhiuddāmavāruṇīgandhaṁ

jāyaṁ miyaṅkasuhayaṁ bhuvaṇaṁ khīrōyamadaṇaṁ va

ēvaṁvihē pōsē savisēsaṁ sanjiya mahārammaṁ

harisiyamaṇō kumārō samāgaō navara vāsaharaṁ

ōhāmiyamurasundarariruvāē vahuē saparivārāē

papphullavayaṇakamalāē sēviyaṁ suravimāṇaṁ va

niuṇēhi kaṁci kālaṁ gamiuṁ hiṭāu hāsakheḍḍēhiṁ

avisajjiyāu vahuyāē niggayāō sahīō sē

anobhamaṅgamaṅgaṇa pelliḍaṁ nēhapariṇaïvasēṇa

suttaṁ varavahumihuṇaṁ jahāsuī nihuyanīsāsaṁ

tōca kupurisariddhi bva jhijiu turiyamēva āḍhattā

rayaṇī sarisitthīṇa vi aṇavekkhiyapiyayamaviōyaṁ

paccūsamāruēṇa va nīō nahakōhimāu avaranta

tārānivahō supaōsaraïyasiyakusumapayarō bva

diyahapiyavirahakāyararāmāyaṇajaṇiyahiyayanivvēyaṁ

bhuvaṇaṁ mi muhala kukkuḍabandiṇasaddō pavitthariō

hontanisāvahudūsahaviōyacintāulō vva nisiṇāhō

jāō bhuvaṇujōyaṇaniyakajjaniyacavāvārō

cāliyalavaṅgacandaṇanamērusuradārugandhasaṁbaliō

avahiyasurayāyāsaṁ vilayāṇa viyambhiō pavaṇō

kheḍḍamahisāriyāō viyapiyayamakayaṁ bhaïrantīō

niyagēhāi saharisaṁ gayāu rōmaniyaṅgīō

ujjhiyatārāharaṇā punvadisā maccharēṇa vāyambā

jāyā avaradisāmuhalaggaṁ daṭhṭhaṇa va miyata

uyayadharāharasiharaṁ sūrō aha viyaḍatuṅgamārūḍhō

āratamaṇḍalō timiranivahasaṁjāyarōsō vya

ghaḍiyāī visamavihaḍiyaviōyadukkhāī cakkavāyāī

duhiyamaha kaṁ va na kuṇaï uya bhō suhiyaṁ sumittassa

kumāraguṇacandō vi ya uciē rayaṇivirāmasamaē gīyamaṅgalummī sēṇa pahāuyatūrasadēṇa vibōhiō samāṇō kāūṇa takkhaṇōciya māvassayaṁ ucivēlāē cēva niggaō ujjāgardasaṇavaḍiyāē. ṭhiō tattha maṇōhāriṇā viṇōēṇa kaṁci kālaṁ. tō paviṭṭhō nayariṁ. kayaṁ uciyakaraṇijjaṁ. ēvaṁ ca païdiṇaṁ rayaṇavaī ē saha pavaḍḍamāṇāṇurāyaṁ sokkhamaṇuhavantassa aïkkantō kōī kālō.

anayā rāiṇō mettībalassa vithakō pañcantavāsī viggahō nāma rāyā. pēsiō ṇēṇa tassuvari vivakhēvō. da'puddharattaṇēṇa akayathāṇa yapayāṇāinīimaggō sammamavagacchiūṇa avasaraviiṇṇaviggahēṇa parāiō viggahēṇaṁ. jāṇāviyamiṇaṁ rāiṇō mettībalassa. kuviyō rāyā, sayamēva payaṭṭō amarisēṇaṁ. vinattō kumārēṇa. tāya, na khala kēsarī siyālē karma vihēi. siyālappāō viggahō. tā alaṁ tami saṁrambhēṇa. āṇavēu maṁ tāō, jēṇa pāvēi sō tāyakōyāṇalapayaṅgataṇaṁ ti. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ. jaï ēvaṁ, tā gevhiūṇa mamgāsanasaṁṭhiē naravaī lahuṁ gaccham. kumārēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. mahāpasāō. alaṁ ca tannimittaṁ khēiēhiṁ sēsanaravaīhiṁ. khuddō khu sō tabassī. tā alaṁ tami saṅkāē tti bhaṇiūṇa ahāsannihiyasēnasaṁgaō alaṁ tāyaparihavalēsa savaṇē aṇavaṇīē ēyaṁmi visayasēvaṇāē vi mottūṇa syagavaī gaō viggahōri viggahēṇa kumārō. pattō ya māsamettēṇa kālēṇa tassa visayaṁ. vigahō vi ya kumārō sayamāgaō ti viyāṇiūṇa sama ssiō duggaṁ. ṭhiō rōhagasaṁjattīē ।rōhiō kumārēṇa. biiyadiyahē ya ukkaḍayāē amarisassaaṇabhatthayāē nīīṇaṁ bhiccayāē vigga hassa samihiyayāē sāmiṇō alliyaṇiyāvavaēsēṇa asāhiūṇa kumārassa samāradō samaṁtaharō (samarō). payaṭṭamāōhaṇaṁ. visamayāē duggassa pīḍi jamāṇaṁ pi kumārasennaṁ abhaggamāṇapasaraṁ ti ahiyayaramāḍhattaṁ jujjhiuṁ. jāō mahāsaṁgāmō. viyāṇiō kumārēṇa. anisāmiō ṇēṇaṁ. niyattiyaṁ kahakahavi sennaṁ. bhaṇiyā ya rāyaütā. ajuttamimaṁ ayattasajjhē paōyaṇē attāṇamāyāsiuṁ. samassiō tāva ēsō duggaṁ. rōhiyaṁ cimaṁ amhēhiṁ. na etya asarō palāiyavvassa. iṭṭhā ya mē kulaüttayā, na bahumaō tēsiṁ nāsō. sāmō ya paḍhamō nīīṇaṁ. appō ya ēsō viggahō bhuttō ya tāēṇaṁ ṭhiō saṁbandhipakkhē. tā na juttagayaṁmi ēgapaē pōrusaṁ daṁsēuṁ. āḍhattō ya aviṇayanāsaṇōvāō. aō mama sarīradōhayāē sāviyā tumbhē, jahā puṇō vi ērisa na kāyavvaṁ ti. tēhi bhaṇiyaṁ. jaṁ dēvō āṇa. vēi. visālabuddhiṇā uvaladdhō visaō. viiṇṇāiṁ gāmāgaramaḍambāī rāyaputtāṇaṁ. niruddhāī gāhagummayāī, niruddhō ya pajjōhārō. aï kkantā kaïvi diyahā.

etthantaraṁmi kahaṁci paribhamantō samāgaō tamuddēsa vāṇamantarō. diṭṭhō ya ṇēṇa vāhayālīgaō kumārī. gahiyō kasāēhiṁ. ci. ntiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa. ēsō sō durāyārō. ahō sē dhīraharuthayā, na tīraē ēsa amhārisēhiṁ vāvāiuṁ. āḍhattaṁ ca ṇēṇa imaṁ duggaṁ. tā ēya sāmiṇō sahāyattaṇēṇa avagarēmi ēyassa tti. cintiūṇa diṭṭō ya ṇēṇa pāsāyatalasaṁṭhiō viggahō. bahumaniō viggahēṇaṁ. bhaṇiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa. kimatthaṁ puṇa bhavaṁ ihāgaō tti. vāṇamantarēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. tuha sahāyanimitta. vēriō vi ya mē ēsa durāyāraguṇacandō, na sakkuṇōmi ēyassa uyayaṁ pecchiuṁ. addhavāvāiō ya chuṭṭō mahaṁ ēsa aojjhāē sanibhōgavāvaḍattaṇa. diṭṭhō na antarālē, diṭṭhō ya saṁpayaṁ malayapatthiēṇa. tā alaṁ tāva mama malayagamaṇēṇaṁ. samāṇēmi antarē bhavaō viggahaṁ ti. viggahēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. jaï ēvaṁ, tā thēvami yaṁ kāraṇaṁ. kiṁ bahuṇā jaṁpiēṇaṁ. nēhi mēṁ aja rayaṇīē guṇacandasamīvaṁ, jēṇa ajjēta samāmi viggahaṁ ti. vāṇamantarēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. sāyattamēyaṁ, tō payaṅgavittikālō cetra ēsō tti. saṁpahāriūṇa saha pahāṇapariyaṇēṇaṁ ṭhiō gamaṇasajjō viggahō. aïkkantō vāsarō, samāgayā majjharayaṇī. bhaṇiyaṁ vāṇamantarēṇaṁ ēsa dēsayālō ti. appapaścamō uccaliō viggahō. vijāpahāvēṇa nīō vāṇamantarēṇa pavēsiō guṇacandavāsabhavaṇē. diṭṭhō ya ṇēṇa pasuttō kumārō. bhaṇiō ya dhīragaruyaṁ. bhō bhō guṇacanda, maē saha viggahaṁ kāūṇa vīsatyō suvasi. tā uṭṭhēhi saṁpayaṁ, kērēhi haïtthiyāraṁ ti. sāhu, sāhu bhō vigāha, sāhu, sōhaṇō tē vavasāō ti bhaṇa māṇō uhiō kumārō. gahiyamaṇēṇa khaggaṁ. etthantaraṁmi imaṁ vaïyaramāyaṇṇiūṇa dhāviyā aṅgarakkhā, nivāriyā kumārēṇa. bhaṇiyā yaṇa. bhō bhō sāviyā mama sarīradōhayāē; na ettha annēṇa pahariyavvaṁ. kiṁ na āvajiyā tumbhē imassa imiṇā vavasāraṇa. tā tubbhē cēva ettha viggahasahāsayā, viggahō uga mamaṁ saha imēṇa. etthantaraṁmi vāṇamantarēṇa arē khuddapurisa, kōisō tuha imiṇā vi ggahō tti bhaṇamāṇēṇa samāhaō khaggalaṭṭhīē kumārō. iṇa haṇa ti bhaṇamāṇō ya sapariyaṇō uvaḍiō vigga hō. chūḍhāī ōharaṇāī. sikkhāisaraṇa pāyaṁ vañciyāī kumārēṇa. jāō ya sē bhāsurabhāvō. taō ukkaḍa yāē puṇgassa pagiṭṭayāra vīriyapariṇaīē duppadharisa yāē sāmibhāvassa hīṇayāē viggahādīṇaṁ kēsarikisōraraṇa viya bhindiūṇa gaïyapīḍhaṁ vikkhi viya viggahapurisē uvayāri tti adāūṇa khaggappahāraṁ kēsāya gēṇa pāḍiō vigahō. kaō sē ubari pāō. etthantaraṁmi kumārapariyaṇēṇa pāḍiyā viggahapurisā, jayaï kumārō tti samuddhāiō kalayalō. paṇaṭṭhō vāṇamantarō. cintiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa. ahō sē pāvakammassa aṇāulattaṇaṁ, ahō māhappapagarisō, ahō kayannuyā ahō ēgasārattaṇaṁ; ahō mē ahamnayā, jamēvamavi ēsō na vāvāiō tti. tā imaṁ ettha tāva pattayālaṁ, jamaojhāuriṁ gantūṇa nivēēmi ēyassa viṇivāya, jaṇēmi ēyāriyaṇassa sōyaṁ. ēvamavi kaē samāṇē avagayaṁ cēva ēyassa ti. cintiūṇa payaṭṭō ajojjhāmantarēṇa.

iō ya uṭṭhēhi bhō mahāpurisa udvēhi, kuṇasu hathiyāraṁ ti bhaṇiūṇa mukkō kumārēṇa viggahō. na utthiō ēsō. bhaṇiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa. dēva, kīisa dēvēṇa saha hathiyārakaraṇaṁ. ajuttamēyaṁ pubi pi, visēsaō saṁpayaṁ. viṇijjiō ahaṁ dēvēṇa. pattē vi vāvāyaṇē na vāvāiō ti ahiyayaraṁ vāvāiō tti. tā kiṁ imiṇā asiliṭṭhaceṭṭhiēṇaṁ. kumārēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. uciyamēyaṁ tuha mahāṇubhākkhāē. ahavā kimettha accharīyaṁ, īisā cēva mahāvīrā havanti. viggahēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. dēva, kīisā mama mahāṇubhāvayā mahāvīrayā yā kiṁvā iyāṇi bahuṇā jaṁpiēṇaṁ. vinavēmi dēvaṁ. dēu dēvō samāṇattiṁ niyanarindāṇaṁ, vāvārantu mēṁ ēē, pekkhaü ya dēvō mamāvi kāvurisa ceṭṭhiyaṁ ti. kumārēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. sōhaṇō kāvurisō, jō ēvamajhavasaï pasuttaṁ ca sattuṁ viṇā pahārēṇa bōhēi. tā kiṁ ēiṇā asaṁbaddhapa lāvēṇaṁ. dinā taē mama pasuttāvāvāyaṇēṇa pāṇā, maē vi bhavaō ēsa visaō ti. gacchaü bhava. vigahēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. jaï ēvaṁ, tā annaṁ pi dēvaṁ jāēmi. kumārēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. sāhīṇaṁ bhavaō, jaṁ maē āyattaṁ ti. viggahēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. karēu dēvō pasāyaṁ mama ōla gagāē. kumārēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. mā ēvaṁ bhaṇa; tāyabhiccō tuma mama jebhāugō. tā jaï bhavaō vi bahumayaṁ, tā tāyasayāsaṁ cēva gacchasu tti. paḍibannaṁ viggahēṇa. kārāviyaṁ ca ṇēṇa vaddhāvaṇayaṁ ti. taddiyahamēva ukkoṭṭiyaṁ duggaṁ. payaṭṭō saha viggahēṇamaojjhāuri kurō.

etthantaraṁmi samāgaō tattha bhayavaṁ samataṇamaṇimuttaleṭṭhukaścaṇō dayālū savvajīvēsu aṇuvagiyaparahiyaraō visuddhēhiṁ caühi nā ṇēhiṁ paḍibōhasamaō guṇacandassa tti viyāṇiūṇa samaniō laddhimantasāhūhiṁ puṣvapariyāyamihilāhivō vijayadhammō nāmāyariō tti. ṭhiō guṇasaṁbhavāhihāṇē ujjāṇē. diṭṭhō kumārapariyaṇēṇaṁ. nivēiyaṁ kumārasta. dēva, mahātavassī iō nāidūrē tavōvaṇē cihaï । ēyaṁ sōūṇa dēvō pamāṇaṁ ti. mahātavassi tti harisiō kumārō. gaō tassa candaṇanimittaṁ saha viggahēṇa pahāṇapariyaṇēṇa ya.

diṭṭhō ya ṇēṇa tadivasamēva guṇasaṁbhavaṁmi ujāṇē

dhammō va muttimantō āyariō vijayadhammō tti

sumaṇāṇandiyavibuhō bahusaüṇanisēviō amayasārō

cattabhavakhīrasāyaranilayaraī tiyasaviḍavō vva

uyahi ba dhīragaruō sūrō va paṇāsiyākhilatamōhō

candō va sōmalēsō jiṇindavayaṇaṁ va akalakō

bhavaṭṭhiinisāē jēṇa ya viyaliyatāvēṇa bhavdhakamalāṇa

niṇṇāsiō asēsō aüvvasrēṇa tamanivahō

daṇa ya taṁ jāō muhapariṇāmō dada kumārassa

paricintiyaṁ ca ṇēṇaṁ ahō ṇu khalu ēsa kayaüṣṇō

jō savvasaṅgacāī jō parapīḍāniyattavāvārō

jō parahiyakaraṇaraī jō saṁsārāu nimvinnō

tā vandāmi ahamiṇaṁ bhayavantaṁ taha ya pajjuvāsāmi

sāhūṇa daṁsaṇaṁ pi hu niyamā duriyaṁ paṇāsēi

ēvaṁ ca cintiūṇaṁ vihiṇā saha vigahēṇa tō bhayavaṁ

ahivandiō ya ṇēṇaṁ āyariō saparivārō tti

tēṇa vi ya dhammalāhō tassa kaō mokkhasokhalāhassa

jō niruvamamuhakāraṇamaüvvacintāmaṇīkappō

upavisasu tti ya bhaṇiō guruṇā caraṇantiē tō tassa

uvakṭiō u kumārō viggahaparivārapariyariō

etthantaraṁmi sahasā gayaṇāō divvarūpasaṁpannō

tatthāgaō pahaṭṭhō juimaṁ vijāharakumārō

aha vandiūṇa ya guruṁ bhaṇiyamaṇēṇa bhayavaṁ mahantaṁ mē

kōḍaṁ tuha vuttantē kahiō jō saṁpayaṁ tumaē

kaṇagaürasāmiṇō tami cēva nayarē daḍhappahārissa

maggapaḍivattimāī ihabhavapajjāyapajantō

ōhēṇa maē ēsō tanayarajēṇāu(ṇa) vimhayaṁ daṭṭhuṁ

tē pucchiūṇa nāō tō ya ahamāgēō iyaṁ

tā jaï na antarāyaṁ jāyaï anassa kusalōjōyessa

sāhēhi tō bhayavaṁ taṁ majjhamaṇuggahahāē

bhaṇiyamaha kumārēṇaṁ amha vi bhaya aṇuggahō ēsa

kīraü imassa vayaṇaṁ avā bhayavaṁ pamāṇaṁ ti

tō jaṁpiyaṁ bhayavayā nisuṇaha jaï tuma ettha kōḍaṁ ti

maggapaḍivattimāī sundara jō majśa vusantō

atthi iha bharahavāsē mihilā nayarī jaṇaṁmi vikkhāyā

tīē ahamāsi rāyā nāmēṇaṁ vijayadhammō ti

iṭṭhā ya aggamahisī dēvī nāmēṇa candadhamma tti

sā annayā ya sahasā itthīrayaṇaṁ ti kāūṇaṁ

mantavihāṇanimittaṁ hariyā kēṇāvi mantasiddhēṇa

antēuramajhagayā maha hiyayamayāṇamāṇēṇa

kahiō ya majjha ēsō vuttantō kahavi vijayadēvīē

sōūma ya mōhāō gaōmi ahayaṁ mahāmōha

parivījiūṇa ya taō candaṇarasasittatāliyaṇṭēhiṁ

paḍiyōhiō mhi dukkhaṁ savēviraṁ vāravilayāhiṁ

gahiō ya mahādukkhēṇa taha jahā vikkhiuṁ pi na caēmi

taha dukkhattassa ya mē vōlīṇā tiṇṇi'hōrattā

navaraṁ caütthadiyahē samāgaō tibvatavaparikkhīṇō

bhūipasāhiyadēhō jaḍādharō mantasiddhī ti

bhaṇiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa naravaï kajjēṇa viṇāulō tumaṁ kīsa

mantavihāṇa nimittaṁ naṇu jāyā tuha maē nīyā

kappō ya tattha ēsō jēṇa tumaṁ jāiō na ta paḍhamaṁ

na tīē sīlabhēō jāyaï dēhassa pīḍā vā

tā mā saṁtappa dahaṁ chammāsā āraō tuma taüē

juji si niyamaō iya bhaṇiuṇamadasaṇī jāō

mōhavasayāṇa jē jē ālāvā honti taṁmi kālaṁmi

paricattarajaka jō ḍiō ahaṁ tattha vilavantō

daṇa bhavaṇavāvīrayāi vilasantahaṁsamihuṇāī

pariyaṇapīḍājaṇayaṁ mōhaṁ bahusō gaō ayaṁ

kiṁ bahuṇā nirayasamaṁ majjha tayā dukkhamaṇuhavantassa

vōlīṇā paliōvamatullā māsā kahavi paśca

kahavayadiṇēhi navaraṁ mukō animittamēva dukkhēṇa

pariyaṇahiyayāṇandaṁ jāō ya mahāpamōō mē

jāyā ya mahaṁ cintā anō viya majjha antarappā mē

jāō pasannacittō tā kiṁ puga kāraṇaṁ ettha

patthantaraṁmi sahasā siḍhē paviyasiyalōyaṇajuēṇa

baddhāvaraṇa majjhaṁ jahāgaō dēva titthayarī

sōuṇa imaṁ vayaṇaṁ harisarvasapayadr̥payaḍapulaēṇaṁ

vaddhāvayassa rahasā dāūṇa jahōciyaṁ kiṁpi

gantūṇa bhūmibhāyaṁ thēvaṁ puraō jiṇassa kāūṇa

tatthēva namokkāraṁ pariyariō rāyavandēhiṁ

dāūṇa ya āṇattiṁ karēha kariturayajuggajāṇāī

sayarāī sajāī vaccāmō jiṇavaraṁ namiuṁ

bhūsēha ya appāṇaṁ vatthāharaṇēhi paramarammēhiṁ

sayamavi ya jiṇasayāsaṁ jāō aha gamaṇajoggī tti

bhuvaṇaguruṇō vi tāva ya pāraddhaṁ tiyasanāhabhaṇiēhiṁ

dēvēhi samōsaraṇaṁ nayarīē uttaradisāē

vāukumārēhi sayaṁ cāliyanandaṇavaṇēṇa pavaṇēṇa

jōyaṇamettē khētē avahariō rēṇutaṇanivahō

mēhakumārēhi taō surahijalaṁ sīyalaṁ pavuṭṭhuṁ ti

uudēvēhi ya sahasā dasaddhavaṇṇāi kusumāī

pāyārō rayaṇamō nimmaviō kappayāsidēvēhiṁ

bīō ya kaścaṇamaō jōisiyasurēhi sayarāhaṁ

taïō kalahōyamaō nimmaviō bhavaṇavāsidēvēhiṁ

vantarasurēhi ya kayaṁ ekkekkē tōraṇāīyaṁ

majjhē asōyarukkhō gandhāyaḍḍiyabhamantabhamaraülō

kusuma bharanimiyaḍālō nimmaviō vantarasurēhiṁ

sīhāsaṇaṁ ca tassa ya rayaṇamayamahō ya pāyapīḍhaṁ tu

vivihamaṇirayaṇakhaciyaṁ tēhiṁ ciya bhattijuttēhiṁ

paḍibuddhakundadhavalaṁ maṇaharavilasantamōtiōūlaṁ

chattattayaṁ ca guruṇō tihuyaṇanāhattaṇupphōlaṁ

hēmamayacittadaṇḍē pakṇapaṇacantadhayavaḍasaṇāhē

gayaṇatalamaṇulihantē nimmaviē sīhacakkadhara

haṁsaülapaṇḍurāō gayaṇami kayāu cāmarāō ya

jalaharathaṇiyasarāō maṇaharasuradunduhīō ya

taruṇaravimaṇḍalanihaṁ nimiyaṁ gharakaṇayapaüṇḍīyami

puraō yaṁ dhammacakkaṁ nimnaviyaṁ vanārasurēhiṁ

bhāmaṇḍalaṁ ca viyarḍa nimmaviyaṁ dittadiṣayaracchāyaṁ

tēhiṁ ciya jayaguruṇō rūvi tavatēyavandraṁ va

iya tiyasē hi viraïē tihuyaṇagāhasta aha samōsaragē

puvadārēṇa tō tatya paviṭhṭhō jiṇō bhayavaṁ

kāūṇa namōkāraṁ tityasta payāhiṇaṁ ca uvaviṭhṭhō

puyābhimuhō tahiyaṁ paḍipuṇṇō sārayasasi ca

sēsēsu vi tisu pāsēsu bhayavaō tatya tiṇi paḍimāō

dēvēhi nimmiyāō jigavimbasamāu divāō

indā ya vimalacāmaramaṇaharaparibhūsiēkarakamalā

ubhaō pāsēsu ṭhiyā jiṇāṇa vēubdhiyasarīrā

sīhāsaṇaṁmi vimalē dāhiṇapuvvēṇa nāidūraṁmi

tityayarasma nisaṇṇō muṇinamiō gaṇaharō jeṭṭhō

pukhadārēṇa pavisiya muṇiṇō taha kappayāsi dēvīō

anjāu ṭuṁti tahiṁ namiuṁ aggēyadisibhāē

dāhiṇadārēṇaṁ pavisiūgamaha dāhiṇāvaravibhāē

bhavaṇavaṇa nōisāṇaṁ dēvīu ṭhiyāu aïnihuyaṁ

ārahārēṇaṁ pavisiūṇamavaruttarēṇa nisaṇṇā

jōisiyā vantariyā dēvā taha bharaṇavāsī ya

uttaradārēṇaṁ pavisiūṇa puvvuttarēṇa u nisaṇṇā

vēmāṇiyā suravarā naranāriṁgaṇā ya saṁviggā

ahinaülamayamayādibakukkuḍamajjāramāiyā savvē

vavagayabhayā nisaṇṇā pāyāvarantarē bīē

tiya sahi vi jāṇāī maṇirayaṇa vihūsiyāi rammāiṁ

ṭhaviyāi maṇaharāī pāyāravarantarē tadaē

ēvaṁ ca niravasēsa siṭṭhuṁ tattō samāgaraṇa mahaṁ

kallāṇaēṇa navaraṁ dēvī tatva diṭṭa ti

tattō ya saṁpayaṭṭō jiṇavandaṇavattiyāē sayarāhaṁ

siṅgāriyamuttuṅgaṁ dhavalagaïndaṁ samārūḍhō

tūraravapphuṇṇadisaṁ diṭṭhō nayarīu niggaō navaraṁ

jampāṇajuggarahavaragaēhi rāīhi pariyariō

thēvamiha bhūmibhāyaṁ turiyaṁ gantūṇa karibarāu ahaṁ

ōiṇṇō tiyasakayaṁ daṭṭa mahāsamōsaraṇaṁ

harisavasapulāyaṅgō tattha paviṭṭhō ya pariyagasamēō

dārēṇa uttarēṇaṁ diṭṭhō ya jiṇō jaya khāyō

daṭṭaṇa ya niṇayandaṁ harisavasullasiyabahalarōmañcō

dharaṇinimiuttamaṅgō iya nāhaṁ thuṇiumāḍhattō

jaya tihuyaṇekkamaṅgala jaya naravara lacchivallaha jiṇinda

jaya tabasirisaṁsēviya jaya dujjayanijjiyāṇaṅga

jaya ghōrajiyaparīsaha jaya laḍa habhuyaṅgasundarīnamiya

jaya sayalamuṇiyatihuyaṇa jaya surakayasuhasamōsaraṇa

jaya bhaviyakamadiṇayara jaya asuranarāmarīsapaṇivaïya

jaya tihuyaṇacintāmaṇi jaya jīvapayāsiyasuhamma

jaya saṁsāruttāraya jaya jiṇa gayarāgarōsarayanivaha

jaya sayalajīvavacchala jaya muṇivaï paramanīsaṅga

jaya rāgasōgavajjiya jaya jaya nīsēsavandhaṇavimukka

jaya bhayavaṁ apuṇabhava jaya niruvamasokkhasaṁpatta

jaya guṇarahiya mahāguṇa jaya paramāṇu jaya guru aṇanta

jaya jaya nāha sayaṁbhuva jaya muhuma nirañjaga muṇīsa

iya thōūṇa saharisaṁ jiṇayandaparamabhattisaṁjuttō

gaṇaharapamuhē ya tō namiūgaṁ sāhuṇō samvē

tiyasāīē ya tahiṁ namiūṇa jahārihē sara ṭhāṇē

uvakṭṭhiō bhuvaṇaguruṁ namiūṇa puṇō saparivārō

aha bhayavaṁ pi jiṇavarō niyaṭhāgaṭṭhiyāga sabyasattāṇa

bhavanalahipōyabhūyaṁ isa dhamma kahiumāḍhattō

jīvō aṇāinihaṇō pavāhō'ṇāikammasaṁjuttō

pāvēṇa sayā duhiō muhiō uṇa hōi dhammēṇa

dhammō carittadhammō suyadhammāō taō ya niyamēṇa

kasacchēyatāvasuddhō sō cciya kaṇayaṁ va vinnēō

pāṇavahāīyāṇaṁ pāvaṭṭhāṇāṇa jaü u paḍisēhō

prāṇajjhayaṇāīṇaṁ jō ya vihī ēsa dhammakasō

bajāṇuṭāṇēṇaṁ jēṇa na vāhijjaï tayaṁ niyamā

sambhavaï ya parisuddhaṁ sō uga dhammami chēō tti

jīvāibhāvavāō bandhāipasāhaō iha tāvō

ēēhi suparisuddhō dhammō dhammattaṇamuvēi

ēēhi jō na suddhō annayaraṁmi va na suṭṭhu nivvaḍiō

sō tārisaō dhammō niyamēṇa phalē visaṁvayaï

ēsō ya uttimō jaṁ purisatthō estha vaściō ṇiyamā

vañcijaï sayalēsuṁ kallāṇēsuṁ na saṁdēhō

ettha ya apaściō ṇa hi vañcijaï tēsu jēga tēṇēsō

samma parikkhiyabyō buhēhi maïniuṇadiṣṭrīē

suhumō asēsavisaō sāvajjē jattha atthi paḍisēhō

rāyāiviuḍaṇasahaṁ jhāṇāi ya ēsa kasamuddhō

jaha maṇabaïkāēhi parassa pīḍā dahaṁ na kāyayā

jhāpayatraṁ ca sayā rāgāivipakkha nālaṁ tu

thūlō na samvavisaō sāvajjē jattha hōi paḍi sē hō

rāgāiviuḍaṇa sahaṁ na ya jhāṇāi vi tayāsuddhō

jaha pañcahi bahuēhi vi ēgā hiṁsā musaṁ visaṁvāē

iccāi jhāṇami ya jhāēyacaṁ agārāī

saïi appamattayāē saṁjamanōēma vivihabhēram

jā dhammiyassa vittī ēyaṁ bajhaṁ aṇudvāṇaṁ

ēēṇa na vāhijjaï saṁbhavaï ya taṁ durga pi niyamēga

ēēga jō visuddhō sō khalu chēēṇa suddhō tti

jaha pañcasu samiīsuṁ tīsu ya guttīmu appamatēgaṁ

sa ciya kāyanaṁ jaïiṇā saha kāigāī vi

jē khalu pamāyanaṇayā vasahāī tē vi vajjaṇīyā u

mahuyaravittīē tahā pālēyanyō ya appāṇō

jattha u pamattayāē saṁjamajōēmu vivihabhēēsu

nō dhammiyassa vittī aṇaṇuṭāṇaṁ taya hōi

ēēṇaṁ vāhijjaï saṁbhavaï ya taṁ dugaṁ na niyamēṇaṁ

ēēṇa jō samēō sō uṇa chēēṇa nō suddhō

jaha dēvāṇaṁ saṁgīyagāikajjami ujjamō jaïṇō

kandappāīkaraṇaṁ asambhavayaṇābhihāṇaṁ ca

taha anammiyāṇaṁ ucchēō bhōyaṇaṁ gihē gēmaṇaṁ

asidhāragāi ēyaṁ pāvaṁ bajjhaṁ aṇuḍhāṇaṁ

jīvāibhāvavāō jō diveṭṭha [] nō khalu viruddhō

bandhāisāhagō taha ettha imō hōi tāvō ti

ēēṇa jō visuddhō sō khalu tāvēṇa hōī suddhō tti

ēēṇaṁ cāsuddhō asuddhō hōi nāyavvō

santāsantē jīvē niccāṇiccē ya ṇēgadhammē ya

jaha suhabandhāīyā jujjanti na annahā niyamā

yē khalu pramāijanakā āvasathādayastē'pi varjanīyāstu

madhukaravr̥ttyā tathā pālayitavvaścātmā

santassa sarūvēṇaṁ pararūvēṇaṁ tahā asantassa

haṁdi visittaṇō honti visiṭṭhā suhāīyā

iharā sattāmettāibhāvaō kaha visiṭṭayā tēsiṁ

tadabhāvaṁmi tadatthō haṁdi payattō mahāmōhō

nicō vēgasahāvō sahāvabhūyaṁmi kaha nu sō dukkhē

tassucchēyanimittaṁ asaṁbhavāō payaṭṭejjā

ēgantāṇiccō vi ya saṁbhavasamaṇantaraṁ abhāvāō

pariṇāmihēuvirahā asaṁbhavāō ya tassa ti

na visiṭṭhakajabhāvō aṇaīyavisikāraṇattaṁmi

ēgantabhēyavakkhē niyamā taha bhēyapakkhē ya

piṇḍō paḍō vva na ghaḍō tapphalamaṇaīyapiṇḍa bhāvāō

tadaīyattē tassa u taha bhāvādaśyādittaṁ

ēvaṁvihō u appā micchattādīhi bandhaē kammaṁ

sammattāīēhi ya muccaï pariṇāmabhāvābhō

sakaduvabhōgē vaṁ kahacidēgāhigaraṇabhāvāō

iharā kattā bhottā ubhayaṁ vā pāvaī sayā vi

vēdēi juvāṇakayaṁ vuḍḍō cōrāiphalamihaṁ kōī

na ya sō taō na annō paccakkhāippasiddhīō

na ya nāṇanō sō'haṁ ki pattō pāvapariṇaïvasēṇa

aṇuhavasaṁdhāṇāō lōgāgamasiddhiō cetra

iya maṇuyāibhavakayaṁ vēyaï dēvāibhavagaō appā

tassēva tahā bhāvā sabamiṇaṁ hōi uvavannaṁ

ēgantēṇa u niccō'ṇiccō vā kaha nu vēyaē sakaḍaṁ

ēgasahāvattaṇaō tadaṇantaranāsaō cēva

jīvasarīrāṇaṁ pi hu bhēyābhēō tahōvalambhāō

muttāmuttattaṇaō chikkaṁmi pavēyaṇāō ya

ubhayakaḍobhayabhōgā tadabhāvāō ya hōi nāyabbō

bandhāivisayabhāvā tēsiṁ taha saṁbhavāō ya

ettha sarīrēṇa kaḍaṁ pāṇahāsēvaṇāra jaṁ kammaṁ

taṁ khalu cittavivāgaṁ vēēi bhavantarē jīvō

na u taṁ cēva sarīraṁ naragāisu tassa taha abhāvāō

bhinnakaḍavēyaṇami ya aïppasaṅgō balā hōī

ēvaṁ jīvēṇa kayaṁ kūramaṇapayaṭṭaēṇa jaṁ kammaṁ

taṁ paï rōdavivāgaṁ vēēi bhavantarasarīraṁ

na u kēvalaō jīvō tēṇa vimukkassa vēyaṇābhāvē

na ya sō cēva tayaṁ khalu lōgāivirōhabhāvāō

ēvaṁ ciya dēhavahē uvayārē vā vi puṇṇapāvāiṁ

iharā ghaḍāibhaṅgāināyaō nēva jujjanti

tayabhinnami ya niyamā tannāsē tassa pāvaï nāsō

ihaparalōgābhāvā bandhādīṇaṁ abhāvāō

dēhēṇaṁ dēhami ya uvaghāyāṇuggahāi bandhādī

na puṇa amuttō muttasma appaṇō kuṇaï kiṁcidavi

akarentō ya na bajjhaï aïppasaṅgā sadēva bhāvāō

tamhā bhēyābhēē jīvasarīrāṇa bandhāī

mokkhō vi ya baïddhassā tayabhāvē sa kaha kīsa vā na sayā

kiṁ vā hēūhi tahā kahaṁ va sō hōi purisatthō

tamhā baddhassa taō bandhō vi aṇāimaṁ pavāhēṇa

iharā tadabhāvammī puvvaṁ ciya mokkharasiddhī

aṇubhūyavattamāṇō bandhō kayagattaṇāimaṁ kaha nu

jaha u aīō kālō tahāvihō taha pāhēṇa

dīsaï kammōvacaō saṁbhavaī tēṇa tassa vigamō vi

kaṇagamalassa ya tēṇa u mukkō mukkō tti nāyavō

ēmāibhāvavāō jattha tō hōi tāvasuddhō tti

ēsa uvāēō khalu buddhimayā dhīrapurisēṇa

ēyassa uvāyāṇaṁ kāuṁ āsēviūṇa bhāvēṇa

pattā aṇantajīvā sāsayasokkhaṁ lahum̐ mokkhaṁ

tā paḍivajaha sammaṁ dhammamiṇaṁ bhāvō mara bhaṇiyaṁ

añcantadullahaṁ khalu karēha saphalaṁ maṇuyajamma

iya bhaṇiūṇa jāē tuhikē tarakhaṇaṁ jiṇavaraṁmi

parisā kayañjaliuḍā dhaṇiyaṁ pariōsamāvanā

dharaṇinamiuttimaṅgā icchāmō sāsaṇaṁ ti jaṁpantī

unnāmiyamuhakamalā puṇō vi ṭhāṇaṁ gayā niyayaṁ

tattha ya kēi pavanā sammattaṁ dēsaviraïvayamannē

annē u cattasaṅgā jāyā samaṇā samiyapāvā

etthantaraṁmi ya maē diṭṭhā dēvī tahiṁ samōsaraṇē

jāyā ya majjha cintā hanta kuō estha dēvi ti

sariyaṁ ca mantasiddhassa taṁ maē punamantiyaṁ vayaṇaṁ

paricintiyaṁ ca etthaṁ pucchāmi jiṇaṁ niyāṇaṁ ti

kiṁ puṇa maē kayaṁ parabhavaṁmi jassīisō vivāgō tti

dēvīvirahaṁmi dadaṁ aṇuhūyaṁ dāruṇaṁ dukkhaṁ

paripucchiō ya ēvaṁ namiūga maē jiṇō nirava sēsaṁ

puvāyakammadōtaṁ taō vi iya kahi māḍhattō

atthi ihēva girivarō jambuddīvami bhārahē vāsē

vi'jhō tti siharasañcayapajaliyamahōsahisaṇāhō

dariyagayadaliyapariṇayahariyandaṇasurahipasariyāmōō

phalapurataruvarahiyavihaṅgagaṇaviruyasadālō

nāmēṇa siharasēṇō tattha tumaṁ āsi sabararāō tti

bahusattaghāyaṇaraō accantavisayagiddhō ya

tattha aṇēgāṇi tumē varāhavasaya sayahariṇajuyalāī

rapaṇē viōiyāī bhīyāi suhābhilāsīṇi

dēvī vi ya tē ēsā tuha jāyā āsi sirimaī nāma

bakkaladugullabasaṇā guñjāphalamāliyāharaṇā

sa tuma imīē saddhiṁ sacchandaṁ giriniuñjadēsēsu

visayasuhamaṇuhavantō ciṭṭhasi kālē nidāīmi

etthantaraṁmi ēkō gacchō sāhūṇa pahaparibhaṭṭhō

parikhīṇō hiṇḍantō taṁ dēsaṁ āgaō navaraṁ

daṭṭhūṇa sāhugacchaṁ aṇugampā tuha maṇami uppanā

hā ki bhamanti ēē aïvisapē vijhakantārē

gantūṇa pucchiyā tē kiṁ hiṇḍaha estha vijharaṇami

sāhūhi tō bhaṇiyaṁ sāvaya panthāu pabbhaṭṭhā

bhaṇiō ya sirimaīē taṁ sāmi mahātabassigō ēē

uttārēhi sapuṇṇē bhīmāō vijharaṇāō

pīṇēhi ya phalamūlāiēhi aïvisamatavaparikkhīṇē

nūgaṁ nihāṇalambhō ēsa tuha pagāmiō vihiṇā

iya bhaṇiēṇa sasaṁbhamaharisabasapayaṭṭapayaḍa pula ēṇaṁ

uvaṇīyāi saviṇayaṁ pēsaïlaphalamūlakandāī

sāhūhi taō bhaṇiyaṁ sākkha nē yāṇi kappaṇi jāṇi

amhāṇa jiṇavarēhiṁ jamhā samaē nisiddhāṇi

bhaṇiyaṁ tumaē taha vi ya tumbhēhi aṇugahō u kāyayō

>annahakaraṇa gāī nivēō hō amhāṇaṁ

pariyāṇiūṇa bhāvaṁ navaraṁ saddhāluyāṇa guṇajuttaṁ

tēhi aṇuggahatthaṁ kajja hiyayaṁmi kāūṇaṁ

sāhūhi tō bhaṇiyaṁ jaï ēvaṁ vigayavaṇṇagandhāī

tā amha dēha navaraṁ phalāi cirakālagahiyāī

iya bhaṇiēṇaṁ tumaē sigdhaṁ girikandarāu ghettūṇa

paḍilāhiyā tavastī pariṇayaphalamūla sandēhiṁ

panthaṁmi pāḍiyā taha jāyāsahiēṇa suddhabhāvēṇa

mannantēṇa kayatthaṁ appāṇaṁ jīvalōgaṁmi

tēhi vi ya tujha dhammō kahiō jigadēsiō susāhūhiṁ

paḍivanā iya tumbhē kammōvasamēṇa taṁ dhamma

dinnō ya namōkārō sāsayasivasokkhakāraṇabhūō

bhattibharōṇayavayaṇēhi sō ya tumbhēhi gahiō tti

muṇiūṇa taha ya tubhaṁ jammaṁ kammāṇuhāvacariyaṁ ca

sāhū hi samāiḍhē kāyacamiṇaṁ ti tubbhēhiṁ

pakkhassēgadiṇaṁmī ārambhaṁ vajjiūga sāvajja

païrikasaṁṭhiēhi aṇusariyanyō namōkārō

tami ya diṇami tubhaṁ jaï vi sarīra viṇivāyaṇaṁ kōi

cintēja taha karejja va tahāvi tumbhēhi khamiyavvaṁ

ēvaṁ sēvantāṇaṁ tumbhaṁ jiṇabhāsiyaṁ imaṁ dhammaṁ

acirēṇa hōhii dhuvaṁ maṇaharasurasokkhasaṁpattī

tumbhēhi vi bhattīē sōūṇamiṇaṁ susāhuvayaṇaṁ ti

ēvaṁ ti abbhuvayaṁ gaēhi sāhūhi ciṇṇaṁ ca

taha cēva kaṁci kālaṁ annonnavēḍamāṇa saḍḍēhiṁ

aha annayā ya tumbhaṁ pōsahapaḍimaṁ pavanāṇaṁ

tuṅgami vijhasiharē gayakumbhasthalaviyāraṇēkarasō

dhuyapiṅgakēsarasaḍhō dariyamaïndō samallīṇō

taṁ daṭṭaṇaṁ tumaē tabbhīyaṁ sirimaī niēūṇa

vāmakaragōyaratthaṁ gahiyaṁ kōdaṇḍamuddāmaṁ

bhaṇiyaṁ ca bhīru mā bhōyasu ti ēyassa mēṁ samallīṇā

ēsō hu pēsavarāyā mamēkasaravāyasajjhō tti

tō sirimaīē bhaṇiyaṁ ēvaṁ ēyaṁ ti kō'ttha saṁdēhō

kiṁ tu guruvayaṇamēyaṁ pāmukaṁ hōi amhēhi

jamhā gurūhi bhaṇiyaṁ sarīraviṇivāyaṇaṁ pi tubmāṇa

jaï kōi taṁmi diyahē karejja tumbhēhi khamiyavvaṁ

tā kaha gurūṇa vayaṇaṁ sumarantēhi guṇabhūsiyaṁ nāha

paralōyabandhubhūyaṁ kīraï vivarīyamamhēhiṁ

aha mottūṇa dhaṇuvaraṁ tumaē tō sirimaī imaṁ bhaṇiyā

saccaṁ gurūṇa vayaṇaṁ kaha kīraï annahā suyaṇu

tuha nēhēmōhiēṇaṁ maē vi ēyamiha vavasiyaṁ āsi

tā alamēēṇa piē guruvayaṇē āyaraṁ kuṇasu

etthantaraṁmi ruñjiyasadēṇa nahaṅgaṇaṁ sa pūrentō

mahidinnatalapahārī uvaḍhiō tujjha sīhō tti

paricintiyaṁ ca tumaē gurūvaēsaparivālaṇānihasō

uvayāri cciya ēsō amhāṇaṁ pasavanāhō tti

iya cintintō ya tuma naharēhi viyārilō sutikhēhiṁ

kuviēṇa akuviyamaṇō jāyāsahiō maïndēṇa

ahiyāsiō ya tumaē jāyāsahiēṇa sō ubasaggō

jō kupurisāṇa sāvaya accatthaṁ durahiyāsō ti

caïūṇa taō dēhaṁ visuddhacittāi dō vi samakālaṁ

sōhammē ughavannāi iḍḍimantāi sayarāī

paliōvamāuyāī tatya ya bhōē jahicchiē bhottuṁ

khīṇāuyāi tattō caïūṇa ihēba dīvaṁmi

jāyāi jattha jaha vā saṁjōyaṁ sundaraṁ ca pattāī

jaha pāviō ya dukkhaṁ virasaṁ taha saṁpayaṁ suṇasu

avaravidēhē khettē cakkaüraṁ nāma puravaraṁ rammaṁ

uttuṅgadhālapāyāramaṇḍiyaṁ tiyasanayaraṁ va

tassāsi agamahisī dēvī nāmēṇa bālacanda tti

tīsē garbhami tumaṁ caïūṇa muhaṁmi uvavannō

dēvī vi ya tē ranō sālassa subhūsaṇassa gēhaṁmi

uvavamā kayaüṇṇā kurumaïdēvīē kucchisi

tāṇa bahuēhi doṇḍa vi maṇōrahasaēhi diṇē pasatthaṁmi

jāyāi tayā tubbhē rūbāiguṇēhi kaliyāī

tattha ya samaramiyakō nāmaṁ tu ṭhāviyaṁ guruyaṇēṇa

dēvīē vi ya nāmaṁ asōyadēvi tti saṁgīyaṁ

kālēṇa dōṇi vi taō sayalakalāgahaṇadudhiyaḍḍāī

kusumāuhavarabhavaṇaṁ jovvaṇamaha tattha pattāī

dinā asōyadēvī taïyā tujjha subhūsaṇanivēṇa

pariṇīyā ya taē vi ya supasatyavivāhajōēṇa

bhuñjantāṇa payāmaṁ visayamuhaṁ nāra vaccaē kālō

tumhāṇa sapariōsaṁ annonnaṁ baddharāyāṇaṁ

sapariyaṇā rayaṇavaï tti.

gaṇiṇīē bhaṇiyaṁ. vacchē, saṁsārasamāvannā khu pāṇiṇō sabvē dukkhatarubīyanammasaṁgayā ahihavīyanti aṇusamayaṁ jarāē, utthā rijjanti mōhatimirēṇa, vāhijjanti visayataṇḍāē, kayatthijjanti indiēhiṁ, pacanti kōhaggiṇā, avaṭṭhamanti māṇapavvaēṇaṁ, mōhi. jjanti māyājāliyāē, palāvijjanti lōhasāyarēṇa, khaṇḍijjanti iṭṭaviōēhi, bhamāḍijjanti kālapariṇaīē, kavalijjanti maccuṇa tti. paramatthō na kēi suhiyā mottūṇa tappaḍivakkhujjaē mahāṇubhāvē. tē uṇa, jahā kēi mahāvāhigahiyā pīḍijjamāṇā mahāvēyaṇāē samāvannanivvēyā gavēsiūṇa kusalavejjaṁ nivēiūṇa appāṇayaṁ tassa vayaṇēṇa paḍibannā jahuttakiriyaṁ vāhijamāṇā vi tevvēyaṇāē vimu camāṇā vāhiṇā antō-āroggalāhadhiīē agaṇēmāṇātaṁ bajjhadukkhaṁ īsi avimukkā vivāhiṇā saṁjāyavimokkhanicchayamaī ārogga samēyā viya na khalu nō muhiyā vavahārēṇa tahā jē imē bhayavantō muṇivarā tē saṁsāramahāvāhigahiyatti paḍijjamāṇā jammāimahāvē yaṇāē samāvannanivvēyā gavēsiūṇa bhāvaō kusalavēja bhayavantaṁ vīyarāyaṁ taduvaēsasamuṭṭiyaṁ vā guruṁ nivēiūṇamappāṇayaṁ tassa vayaṇēṇa paḍivānā savvadukkhanivāraṇiṁ saṁjamakiriyaṁ vāhijjamāṇā vi parīsahōvasaggavēyaṇāē vimuccamāṇā mahāmōhavāhiṇā antōpasamārōgagalā bhadhiīē agaṇēmāṇātaṁ parīsahādivajjhadukkha īsi avimukkā vi saṁkilēsavāhiṇā paramaguruvīyarāgāṇāsēvamāē saṁjāyavimokkhaniccha maī sayalābāhākhayasamunbhūyaparamapaṇihāṇabhāvāroggasamēyā vīyarāyā viya na khalu nō suhiyā niccha ēṇa. jō paṇaṭṭhuṁ tēsiṁ mōha timiraṁ, āvibhūyaṁ sammanāṇaṁ, niyattō asaggahō, pariṇayaṁ saṁtōsāmayaṁ, avagayā asakiriyā, tuṭṭapāyā bhavavallī,thirīhūyaṁ śāṇarayaṇaṁ āsannaṁ paramasivamuhaṁ. tā ēvaṁ paramatthacintāē thēvā ettha muhiyā bahavē uṇa dukkhiya tti. lōyadiṭṭhīē u vacchē annārisē muha dukkhē. lōēhi jammajarāmaraṇaghatthā vi pāṇiṇō āhārāisaṁpattimettēṇa kūravāhasaragōyaragayā viya hariṇayā māyācariyaṁ. jārisaṁ taē mantiyaṁ ti, tārisaṁ cēva imīē saṁpāḍiyaṁ. kaō kila tuha santiō vēsō. tīē bhaṇiyaṁ. ajjaütta, alamimīē dasaṇēṇa, niyāsēhi ēvaṁ mahāpāvaṁ ti । taō rāiṇā sadāviyā aṭṭhapāhariyā. samāgayā havē. bhaṇiyā ya ṇēṇa. bhō bhō ēyaṁ dēvīsvadhāriṇi duṭṭanavikhaṇiṁ kayatthiūṇa niyaṁ lahuṁ nivāsēha. taō tēhiṁ jaṁ dēvō āṇavēi ti bhaṇiūṇa pubavēriēhi viya ā pāvē, ā pāvē tti bhaṇamāṇēhiṁ gahiyā ahaṁ kēṇāvi kēsēsu, avarēṇa uttarīē, annēṇa bāhāhiṁ, kayatthiyā naravaïpuraō, nīṇiyā bāhiṁ. tattha vi ya ahiyayaraṁ kayatthiūṇa, jahā kāi duhrasīlā nivāsīyaï, tahā nivāsiya mhi. vimukkā nayarakāṇaṇasamīvē, bhaṇiyā ya ṇēhiṁ. ā pāvē, jaï puṇō gayabhavaṇaṁ pavi sasi, taō muyā amhāṇa hatthō tti. niyattā rāyapurisā. taō cintiyaṁ maē. hanta kimēyaṁ ti. ahō mē pāvapariṇaī, peccha ki (mē) pāviyaṁ ti. ahō ṇu khalu niravarāhā vi pāṇiṇō pukhaducariēhiṁ ēvaṁ kayatthijanti. tā alaṁ mē jīviēṇa, vāvāēmi attāṇayaṁ. na anō vācāyaṇōvāō tti gantūṇa mēyamadūrōvalakkhijamāṇapabvayaṁ bhañjami attāṇayaṁ ti payaṭṭā girisamuha, pattā ya mahayā parikilēsēṇa । samāḍhattā ya āruhium̐. divā giriguhāgaēhiṁ sāhahiṁ. samāgaō ya tō aṇēyaguṇarayaṇabhūsiō dippamāṇō tavatēēṇa muṭṭhiō para lōyapakkhē bacchalō duhiyasattāṇaṁ samuppannadivbaṇāṇō dēsabhō saṁsārāḍavīē ciṁtāmaṇī samīhiyasuhassa aṇēyasāhupariyariō sugihīya nāmō bhayavaṁ guru tti. taṁ ca dadruṇa avagaō viya mē kilēsō, samaddhāsiyā viya dhammēṇa. vandiō saviṇayaṁ, dhammalāhiyā ya ṇēṇa bhaṇiyā sabahumāṇaṁ. vacchē susaṁgaē, na taē saṁtappiyavvaṁ. īisō ēsa saṁsārō, āvayābhāyaṇaṁ khu ettha pāṇiṇō; ahihayā mahāmōhēṇa na pecchanti paramatthaṁ, na muṇanti paramamittāṇaṁ vayaṇaṁ, payaṭṭanti ahiēsu, bandhanti tivya kammayāī, viuḍi janti tēhiṁ, na chuṭṭanti punca dakkaḍāṇaṁ viṇā vīyarāgavayaṇakaraṇēṇaṁ ti. taō maē bhaṇiyaṁ. bhayatraṁ, ēvamēyaṁ aha kiṁ puṇa maē kayaṁ pāvakamma, jassa īisō vivāō tti. bhayavagā bhaṇiyaṁ. vacchē suṇa, jassa vivāgasēsamēyaṁ. maē bhaṇiyaṁ. bhayavaṁ, abahiya mhi. bhayavayā bhaṇiyaṁ. vacchē, suṇa । atthi ihēva bhārahē vāsē uttarāvahē visaē bambhaüra nāma nayaraṁ. tattha bambhasēṇō nāma naravaī ahēsi. tassa bahumaō viurō nāma māhaṇō, purandarajasā sē bhāriyā. tāṇaṁ tuma iō aīyanavamabhavaṁmi candajasāhihāṇā dhūyā ahēsi tti, vallahā jagaṇijaṇayāṇaṁ. jiṇavayaṇabhāviyattaṇēṇa tāṇi dēsanti tē dhamma, nivārenti ahiyāō. aṇāibhavabhāvaṇādōsēṇa bālayāē ya na pariṇamaï tē samma. samuppannā ya tē pīī jasōdāsasē dvibhāriyāē bandhusundarīē saha. sā ya aïsaṁkiliṭṭhucitā saṁsārāhiṇandiṇī giddhā kāmabhōēmu nira vekkhā paralōyamaggē. taō vāriyā tumaṁjaṇaṇijaṇaēhiṁ. vacchē, alamimīē saha saṅgēga, pāramittathāṇīyā khu ēsā, paḍisiddhō ya bhaya. vayā pāvamittasaṅgō. na paḍivannaṁ ca taṁ taē guruāyaṇaṁ. anayā gayā tumaṁ bandhusundarisamīvaṁ. diṭṭhā vimaṇadummaṇā bandhusundarī. bhaṇiyā ya ēsā. halā, kīsa tumaṁ vimaṇadummaṇa tti. tīē bhaṇiyaṁ. piyasahi, virattō mē bhattā gāḍharatō maïrāvaīē, ajāyaputtabhaṇḍā ya ahayaṁ । tā na-yāṇāmō, kahaṁ bhavissaï tti daḍaṁ visaṇṇa bhiḍa. taē bhaṇiyaṁ. alaṁ visāēṇa, uvāē jattaṁ kuṇasu tti. tīē bhaṇiyaṁ. na yāṇāmi etthuvāyaṁ, suyaṁ ca maē, atthi iha uppalā nāma paridhāiyā, sā ēvaṁvihēsu kusalā, na ya ṇētaṁ pekkhiuṁ avasarō tti. taē bhaṇiyaṁ. kahiṁ sā parivasaï, sāhēhi majjha; ahaṁ tamāṇēmi tti. sāhiyaṁ bandhusundarīē, jahā kila pubabāhiriyāē. taō gayā tuma, diṭṭhā parivāiyā. bandhusundarī tumaṁ dadrumicchaï tti bhaṇiūṇa āṇiyā tumaē, āṇiūṇa gayā tumaṁ sagihaṁ. pūiyā sā bandhusundarīē, sā hiō sē niyavuttantō. bhaṇiyaṁ parivāiyāē. avihavē, dhīrā hōhi. thēva mēyaṁ kajja. karēmi ahamettha jōya, jēṇa sō tīsē paōsamā. vajaïtti. bandhusundarīē bhaṇiyaṁ. bhayāi, aṇuggihīya mhi. gayā parivāiyā, kōya ṇāē jasōdāsaseṭṭhiṇō mahāvaī paï vidēsa ṇajōō. paüttō vihiṇā. acintasāmatthayāē ōsahīṇaṁ vicittayāē kammarariṇāmaspa virattō tīē seṭṭhī. paricattā maïrāvaī, gahiyā sōēṇa. ēyanimittaṁ ca baddhaṁ taē kiliṭṭhukammaṁ. parivāliūṇa aghāuyaṁ mayā samāṇī takkammadōsēṇēva samuppanā karēṇuyattāē appiyā jahāhissa; gahiyā vārimajjhē. taō tattha mahantaṁ kilēsamaṇuhaviya mayā samāṇī takkammadōsēṇa samuppannā vāgarittāē tti. tattha vi ya accantamappiyā jūhāhivassa. vicchūṭā jūhāō gahiyā jaraṭṭhakurēṇa, nibaddhā lōhasaṅkalāē. mahādukkhapīḍiyā ahā uyaṁ pāliūṇa mayā samāṇī takammadōsēṇēva samuppannā kukkurittāē. tattha vi ya riukālē vi agahimayā sabakukkurāṇaṁ kīḍāniyara khaïyaviṇahadēhā mahantaṁ kilēsamaṇuhaviya mayā samāṇī takkammadōsēṇēva samuppannā majārigattāē tti. tattha vi ya amaṇōramā sabamajā. rāṇaṁ gēhāṇaladaḍḍadēhā ahāuya skhaē mariūṇa takkammadōsēṇēva samuppannā cakavāiyattāē tti. tatya vi sayā piyayamaparivajjiyā kilē. sasaṁpāiyavittī mahantaṁ dukkhamaṇuhaviya mayā samāṇī takammadōsēṇēva samuppannā caṇḍālaïtthigattāē ti. tattha vi ya daḍhaṁ amaṇōramā piyayamassa mayaṇadukkhapīḍiyā ahāuyakkhaēṇa mariūṇa takammadō sēṇēva samuppamā savaraïsthigattāē. tattha vi ya amaṇōramā savvasa varāṇaṁ vicchūḍhā ṇēhiṁ pallīō paribbhamantī ya visamasajjhakantārē kilēsasaṁpāiyasarīraṭṭhiī parikkhīṇakāyā addhāṇapaḍivanapahaparibhaṭṭhēhi diṭṭhā tumaṁ sāhahiṁ, tē vi ya tu rāē ti. tē ya daṭṭhūṇa samuppannō tē pamōō. pucchiyā ya ṇēhiṁ. dhammasīlē, kō uṇa imō paēsō kēdurē vā iō vattaṇi tti. taē sabahumāṇamāikkhiyaṁ. sajjhakantāramēyaṁ, iō nāidūrē vattaṇī. sāhūhi bhaṇiyaṁ. dhammasīlē, kayarīē disīē battaṇī. taē bhaṇiyaṁ. avaramaggēṇa iō vōliūṇa imaṁ tarulayāgahaṇaṁ. ahavā ēha, ahaṁ cēva daṁsēmi tti. daṁsiyā vattaṇī. cintiyaṁ ca suddhacittāē. ahō imē amacchariyā piyabhāsiṇō pasantarūvā abhigamaṇīyā; dhannāṇamēvaṁvihēhi saha saṁgamō bhavaï. ēvaṁ visuddhacintaṇēṇa khaviō kammasaṁghāō āsagaliyaṁ bodhivīyaṁ. etthantaraṁmi dhammalāhiyā sāhūhiṁ suhayarapariṇāmā ya paḍiyā tēsiṁ calaṇēsuṁ. esthantaraṁmi appārambhapariggahattaṇēṇa sahāvamaddavajayayāē sāhusannihisāmatthaō suddhabhāvayāē ya baddhaṁ sumāṇusā uyaṁ. gayā bhayavantō sāhuṇō. gaēmu vi ya na tuṭṭō tē tayaṇusaraṇasaṁgaō suhabhāvāṇubandhō. ahāuyaparikkhaēṇaṁ ca mayā samāṇī takammadōsa sēsasaṁgayā cēva samuppannā sēyaviyāhivassa dhūya tti. pattavayā ya pariṇīyā kōsalāhivēṇa; takkammasēsayāē ya jakkhiṇīrūvadhippala. dēṇa kayatyāviyā ṇēṇaṁ. tā ēvaṁ vacchē duṭṭhaparivāiyāhavaṇakammavivāgasēsamēyaṁ ti.

ēyamāyaṇṇiūṇa avagayaṁ ciya mē mōhatimiraṁ, jāō bhavavirāō, utpannaṁ jāisaraṇaṁ, baḍiō saṁvēgō. vandiūṇa bhaṇiō bhayavaṁ gurū. bhayavaṁ, ēvamēyaḥ, aha kayā uṇa takkammavivāō nīsēsībhavissaï. bhayavayā bhaṇiyaṁ. vacchē, imiṇā ahōrattēṇa. maē bhaṇiyaṁ । bhayavaṁ, kayā kaha vā taṁ jakkhiṇi viyāṇissaï annaüttō. bhayatrayā bhaṇiya vacchē, ajjā rayaṇīē tuha saṁhāvāsarisayāē samuppannā saṅkō nivēiuṇa mantiṇō takayavīyarāyapaḍimālavaṇapaōēṇa nīsaṁsayaṁ viyāṇiūṇa, jahā na ēsā dēvi tti; tō haṇa haṇa tti bhaṇa māṇō khaggaṁ gahē ūṇa uḍhiō rāyā, jāva takkhaṇaṁ adaṁsaṇā jāya tti. maē bhaṇiyaṁ bhayavaṁ, na tīē kiṁci akusalaṁ karissaï ajjaüttō bhayavayā bhaṇiyaṁ. vacchē, na hi, kiṁ tu kayatthiyā tumaṁ ti ahiyaṁ saṁtappissaï. maē bhaṇiyaṁ. bhaya kō ettha dōsō ajja uttassa, kammapariṇaī ēsa tti. bhayavayā bhaṇiyaṁ. vacchē, ēvamēyaṁ tahāvi mōhadōsēṇa daḍha saṁtappissaï mahārāō. suē āgamissaï ihaī, pekkhissaï tumaṁ. taō saha taē accaṁtasuhiō havissaï tti viyāṇiūṇa na taē saṁtappiyavvaṁ. maē bhaṇiyaṁ,. bhayavaṁ, avagaō mē saṁtāvō tuha daṁsaṇēṇa, virattaṁ ca mē cittaṁ bhavacāragāō. lā kiṁ mahārāyāmamaṇēga. puṇō vi vibhōgāvasāṇā saṁgamā. kīisaṁ ca jarāmaraṇapīḍiyāṇaṁ muhiyattaṇaṁ. bhayavayā bhaṇiyaṁ. vacchē, ēvamēyaṁ, kiṁ tu saha taē accantasuhiō havissaï ti. bhaṇiyaṁ maē. :accantasuhiō jīvō na vīyarāyaśyaṇāṇuḍhāṇamantarēṇa havaï. tō bhayavayā bhaṇiyaṁ. saha taē jagaïdōsanigghāyaṇasamatthaṁ dukaraṁ kāvuri sāṇa vīyarāgavayaṇāṇuṭṭhāṇaṁ karaïssaï. ēēṇa kāraṇēṇa accantamuhiō hōhi tti. bhaṇiūṇa tuṇhikō ṭhiō bhayavaṁ. ēyamāyaṇṇiūṇa ahō dhannō mahārāō ti harisiyā ahaṁ. hiyayatthaṁ viyāṇiūṇa bhaṇiyā ya bhayavayā. vacchē, tumaṁ pi geṇhāhi tāva savvamantaparama mantaṁ aïdullahaṁ jīvalōē viṇāsaṇaṁ bhayāṇaṁ sāhaṇaṁ paramapayassa pūṇijja savāṇaṁ acintasattijuttaṁ māhagaṁ sayalaguṇāṇaṁ uvamāīyakallāṇa kāraṇaṁ bhayavayā vīyarāgēṇa paṇīyaṁ pañcanamokkāraṁ ti. maē bhaṇiyaṁ. bhayavaṁ, aṇuggihīya hi. bhayakkhā bhaṇiyaṁ. ṭhāyasu mē vāmapāsē puvāhimuḍa tti. ṭhiyā īsi avaṇayā, vandiō bhayavaṁ. kayaṁ bhayavayā paramagurusaraṇaṁ. tō uvaüttēṇa akkhaliyāiguṇasamēō dinnō namōkārō, paḍicchiō maē suddhabhāvāisaraṇa. tayaṇantaraṁ ca paṇamiva bhavabhayaṁ, samāgaya viya muttimuhaṁ ti. bhayadayā bhaṇiyaṁ. bacchē, iṇamēva aṇusarantīē gamēyavvā taē imāē ēgapāsaḍhiyāē giriguhāē rayaṇī, na bīhiyadhvaṁ ca. saṁpayaṁ gacchāmi ahayaṁ, muē puṇō amhāṇaṁ saṇaṁ ti. maē bhaṇiyaṁ. bhayavaṁ, aṇuggihīya mhi. gaō bhayavaṁ.

namōkāraparāē ya paramapamōyasaṁgayāē thēvavēlā viya aïkkantā rayaṇī. pahāyasamaē ya āsasāhēṇa annēsagatthaṁ samāga bhō rāyā. pattā ya ṇē' samīvē kaïvi āsavārā. divā ya ṇēhi, harisanimmarē hiṁ sāhiyā rāiṇō. āgō mē samīvaṁ rāyā. bāhollalōyaṇēṇaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ ca ṇēṇaṁ. dēvi, na mē kuppiyavvaṁ, annāṇa patthamavarajjhaï. maē bhaṇiyaṁ. ajjaütta, kō etya avasarō kōvassa; niyaduccariya vivāgarōsamēyaṁ. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ. dēvi, ahametya nimitta. maē bhaṇiyaṁ. ajja utta, janmantarē viōyapaḍibaddhaniyaduccariyasāmatthēṇa pahr̥yayaramaṇubhūyaṁ, tatya kiṁ tumaṁ nimittaṁ ti. sabahā maē kaō ēsa dōsō tti. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ. dēvi, sāmannēṇa viyāṇāmi aha miṇaṁ, jamaṇādī saṁsārō kammavasagā ya pāṇiṇō. dēvī uṇa visēsaparinnāṇasaṁgayā viya mantēi. maē bhaṇiyaṁ. ajja utta, ēvaṁ. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ. dēvi, kaha diya. sāhiō maē maraṇavavasāyagurudaṁsaṇāiō namōkāralāhapajjavasāṇō parikahiyavuttantō. ahō bhayavaō nāṇāisaō ti vimhiō rāyā. ahō asārayā saṁsārasta, ēihamettassa vi dukaḍassa īisō vivāō tti saṁviggō rāyā. bhaṇiyaṁ ca ṇa. dēvi, kēdūrē iō bhayavaṁ guru tti. maē bhaṇiyaṁ. ajja utna, iō thōvantarē. rāṇā bhaṇiyaṁ. tā ēhi, gacchamha bhayavantadaṁ saṇavaḍiyāē. maē bhaṇiyaṁ. ajjaütta, jutta mēyaṁ ti. gaō maṁ cettaṇa saha pariyaṇēṇa rāyā. dihō bhayavaṁ, vandiō harisiyamaṇēṇa, dhanmalāhiō bhayayayā. bhaṇiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa. bhayavaṁ, sāhiō mamaṁ bhayavantadaṁsaṇāiyō sayalavuttantō cēva dēvīē. jāō ya mē saṁtāsō, ahō ēhamettassa vi dukkaḍassa īisō vivāō tti. aṇēyadukkaḍasamanniō ya ahayaṁ. tā na-yāṇāmō, kimettha kāyavvaṁ ti. bhaya. vayā bhaṇiyaṁ. mahārāya muṇa, jamettha kāya. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ. āṇavēu bhayā. bhayavayā bhaṇiyaṁ. suppaṇihāṇaṁ vaṭṭamāṇasayalasāvajja jōyaviramaṇaṁ saṁviggayāē aīyapaḍikkamaṇaṁ accantamaṇiyāṇamaṇāgayapaccakkhāṇa ti. ēvaṁ ca kara samāṇē mahantakusalāsayabhāvēṇa mahā mēhabuṭṭihayāṇi viya khuddajalaśudittayāī pasamanti dukkaḍāī. taō vittharaï kupalāsō, ullapaï jīvavīriyaṁ, visujjhaē antarappā, pariṇamaï appamāō, niyattara micchāviyappaṇaṁ, avēi kammāṇubandhō, khijaï bhavasaṁtatī, pāvijaï paramapayaṁ. tattha uṇa savvakālaṁ na honti dukkaḍajōyā, accantiyaṁ ca nirupamamuhaṁ. tā imaṁ kāyavvaṁ. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ. bhayavaṁ, ēva mēyaṁ, aṇuggihīō ahaṁ bhayavayā, kusa lajōēṇa karēmi bhayavaō āṇaṁ ti. bhaṇiūṇa pulaïyā ahaṁ bhaṇiyā ya. dēvi, dullahō bhayavantatullō dhammasārahī. uvāēō ya savvahā dhammō sayamannaṁ saṁkilē sakāragaṁ. na hōi dhammō gurumantarēṇa, tā saṁpāḍēmi bhayaraō āṇaṁ ti. maē bhaṇiyaṁ. ajjaütta, juttamēyaṁ । taō davāviyaṁ rāṇā mahādāṇaṁ, kārāviyā aṭṭhāhiyāmahimā, sammāṇiyā paürajaṇavayā, ṭhāviōrajjē surasundarō nāma jeṭṭaputtō. taō aṇēyasāmantāmaccapariyō saha mara sayalantēurēṇa ya mugihīyanāmadhēyagurusamīvē suttabhaṇiēṇa vihiṇā patramāṇēṇaṁ suhapariṇāmēṇaṁ pāiō rāyā. tā ēvaṁ, bacchē, thēvēga kamnuṇā iyaṁ maē pāviyaṁ ti. aō agacchāmi. thēvassa anāṇaceṭṭiyassa, vacchē, ēsō vivāō, pahūyassa u tiriyāirasuṁ havaï. ēvaṁ ca kammapariṇaīē samāvaḍiyāra vi assā udaē pubdhakaḍamēyaṁ ti na saṁtappiyavvaṁ jāṇa ēṇa. rayamāyaṇṇiūṇa āvibhūyasammattadēsaviraïpariṇāmāē jaṁpiyaṁ rayaṇavaīē. bhayavaï, mahantaṁ dukhamaṇubhūyaṁ bhayavaīē. ahavā īimō ēsa saṁsārō. sabahā kayatthā bhayavaī, nā samuttiṇṇā imāō kilēsanambālāō. haṁ pi dhannā cēva, jīēmaē tuma diṭṭhā. na appapugṇāṇaṁ cintāmaṇirayaṇasaṁpattī habaï. tā āisaü bhayabaī, naṁ maē kāyavvaṁ ti. taō viyāṇiūṇa tīē bhāvaṁ sāhiō sāva yadhammō gaṇiṇīē. ēyamahaṁ caēmi kāuṁ ti harisiyā rayaṇavaī. namokkārapuvvayaṁ siddhantavihāṇēṇa gahiyāī aṇuvvaguṇavbaya sikkhāyavayāī. vandiyā gaṇiṇī, pucchiyā rayaṇavaïē. bhayavaï, kī isō majjha saravisēsō tti pucchiyāē jaṁ taē samāṇattaṁ "jārisō paramānandajōē bhattuṇō havaï" tti tā kīisō ajjaüttassa paramāṇandajōō, kiṁ suyaṁ kuōi ajjaüttēṇa vīyarāyavayaṇaṁ. gaṇiṇīē bhaṇiyaṁ. vacchē, ēvamahaṁ takkēmi. etthantaraṁ guluguliyaṁ gandha hathiṇā, samāhayaṁ saṁjhāmaṅgalatūraṁ, paḍhiyaṁ ca bandiṇā.

dhammōdaēṇa taṁ natyi jaṁ na hōi tti sundaraṁ lōē

iya jāṇiūṇa sundari saṁpaï dhammaṁ daḍhaṁ kuṇasu

ḍhōiyāṇi ya sē nandābhihāṇāē bhaṇḍāriṇīē mahānāyagasaṁjuyāṇi kaḍayāṇi, samāgaō siyakusumahatthō purōhiō. bhaṇiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa. dēvi, dēvaguruvandaṇasamaō vaṭṭaï tti. harisiyā rayaṇavaï. cintiyaṁ ca ṇāē. na etya saṁdēhō, aṇukulō saüṇasaṁghāō tti sammamāyaṇiyaṁ vīyarāgavayaṇaṁ annaüttēṇa, pāviyaṁ pāviyavvaṁ, ubaladdhō siddhimaggō. kahaṁ ca annahā paramāṇandasadō muyadēvayākappāē bhayavaīē muhāō nikkhamaï. amahiyajāyaharisāē vandiyā gaṇiṇī, bhaṇiyā ya saviṇayaṁ. bhayavaï, kiṁ kappaï, ettha bhayavaīē raïyaṇīē cihium̐, na hi. gaṇiṇīē bhaṇiyaṁ. dhammasīlē, jattha tuma, tattha natthi virōhō. tahāvi gacchāmi tāva saṁpayaṁ. adūrē cēva amhāṇa paḍissaō. tā puṇō āgamissāmi tti. rayaṇavaīē bhaṇiya. bhayavaï, aṇuggahō. vandiūṇamabbhuṭṭhiyā gaṇiṇī. aṇuvva iyā ya ṇāē. vandiūga ya niyattā urciyadēsāō. kayaṁ pōsakaraṇijja. namōkāraparāē ya aïgayā rayaṇī. pahāē ya āucchi ūṇa sasuramaṇunāyā ya ṇēṇa gayā gaṇiṇīsamī. vandiyā gaṇiṇī. suā dhammadēsaṇā. samāgayā sagihaṁ bīyadiyahē dhammāṇusa yō sagihatthiyāē cēva samāgayā gaṇiṇō. ēvaṁ païdiṇaṁ gaṇiṇīpajjuvāsaṇaparāē aïkantā cattāri divasā. samāgaō pañcamē diṇē kumārō. nivēiō candasundarīē gaṇiṇīsamīvasaṁṭhiyāē rayaṇavaīē, jahā dēvi, na annahā bhayavaīvayaṇaṁ ti; samāgaō tē hiya yaṇandaṇō. ēyamāyaṇṇiūṇa parituhā rayaṇavaī. dinnaṁ tīē pāriōsiyaṁ.

etthantaraṁmi kumārō vi saha viggahēṇa daga naravaī sāhiūṇa viggahavutantaṁ rāiṇō sabahumāṇaṁ sammāṇiō gēṇa samāgaō rayaṇavaïsamīvaṁ. daṭhūṇa ya kaha kayatthā cetra dēvī saṁgayā gaṇiṇīē ti harisiō cittēṇaṁ. vandiyā ṇēṇa gaṇiṇī. dhammalāhiō gaṇiṇīē. bhaṇiyaṁ kumārēṇa. bhayavaï, peccha mama puṇṇōdayaṁ, jēṇa paḍibōhiō ahaṁ bhayavayā sugihīyanāmadhēpaṇa guruṇā bīyahiyaya bhūyā ya mē taē dēvī tti; diḥ ya bhavasayadullahadasaṇā bhayavaī. gaṇiṇīē bhaṇiyaṁ. kumāra, natthi asanjhaṁ kusalāṇubandhipuṇṇōda yassa. ēēṇa pāṇiṇō pāvanti suhaparaṁparāē muttisuhaṁ pi, kimaṅga puṇa annaṁ. kumārēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. jaï vi puṇṇapāvakkhaēṇa muttī tahāvi tassa kusalāṇubandhipuṇṇamēva kāraṇaṁ. na kusalāṇubandhipugṇavivāgamantarēṇa tārisā bhāvā labbhanti, jārisēsu pugṇapāvakkha yanimittakusalajōyārāhaṇaṁ ti. gaṇiṇīē bhaṇiyaṁ. sāhu, sammamavadhāriyaṁ kumārēṇa. ahavā na ettha accharīyaṁ. nimittamettaṁ cēva dēsaṇā tattōvalambhē kusalāṇaṁ. ēvaṁ ca dhammakahāvāvarēṇa kaṁci vēla gamēūṇa gayā gaṇiṇī paḍissayaṁ. annonnadhammasaṁpattīē ya pari tuḍhaṁ mihuṇayaṁ. bhuttuttarakālaṁ ca sāhiō paropparamimēhiṁ dhammavuttantō. gayāī gaṇiṇīsamīvaṁ, suyā dhammadēsaṇā. samāgayāṇi uciyasamaēṇa. ēvaṁ ca païdiṇaṁ dhammajōgārāhaṇaparāṇa aïkkantō kōi kālō. bhāviyāṇi dhammē. kālakkamēṇēva samuppannō rayaṇavaīē puttō. nattuyamuhadasaṇakayasthattaṇēṇaṁ ca kumāraṁ rajjē ahisiñciya pavāō mettībalō. kumārō vi jāō mahārāō tti. tassa ya dhammaguṇappahāvēṇa aṇuratta sāmantamaṇḍalaṁ rahiyaṁ kaṇṭa ēhi alaṁkiyaṁ rajaguṇēṇa samaddhāsiyaṁ lacchīē niccapamuiyajaṇaṁ muṭṭiyāē tivaggaṇīīē sayalajaṇapasaṁsajjiṁ dēvagurupajjuvāṁsaṇēparayāē rē jamaṇupālentassa aïkkantō kōi kālō.

annayā samāgaō jalayakālō, otthariyamambaraṁ jalaharēhi, pavāiyā kalambavāyā, viyambhiō gajjiyaravō ullasiyā balā yapantī, vipphuriyā vijjulēhā, harisiyā vappīhayā, jāya parisaṇaṁ, paṇacciyā sihaṇḍiṇō, paṇaṭṭhā rāyahaṁsā, pavvāliyā vasu maī, bhariyā kutārā, parattō daduraravō, ubbhinnā kandalā, ukkaṇṭhiyāō pahiyajāyāō, nivvyaṁ gōmāhisakkaṁ. pavaḍḍamāṇā ṇubandhē ya jalayakālē sarasariyāpūradasaṇatthaṁ samaṁ ahāsannihiyapariyaṇēṇa niggaō rāyā. diṭṭhā sariyā kaḍhataṇakalilēṇa pūriyā jalōhēṇa vittharantī sabaō, nivāḍayantī kūlāṇi, viṇāsayantī ārāmē, kalusayantī appāṇaya, saṁgayā kūrajalayarēhi, rahiyā buhajaṇasēvaṇijjēga jalēṇa, ahiṭṭhiyā kallōlēhiṁ, bajjiyā majjāyāē, accantabhōsaṇēṇaṁ mahāvattasaṁghāēṇaṁ bālāibhayajaṇaṇi tti । taṁ ca kaṁci vēlaṁ pulaśya paviṭṭhō nayariṁ rāyā. manā kara diyahā. pāya ra āsaparivāhaṇanimittaṁ vāhiyāliṁ gacchamāṇēga puṇō payaïbhāvaṭṭhiyā saṁgayā sacchōdaēṇa vajjiyā kūrajalayarēhiṁ visiṭṭhanaṇōvabhōyasaṁpāyaṇasamatthā sa ccēva diṭṭha tti. taṁ ca daṭṭhūṇa sumariyapuvyavuttantasma rāiṇō tahāphammaparigaïbasēṇa samuppannō saṁvēō. cintiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa. ahō ṇu khalu asārō bajjhariddhivi ttharō, saparāvagāraō ya parama-thēṇa. ēsēva sariyā etya nirdasaṇaṁ ti. jahā imā vittharantī sacaō appaparāvagāriṇī pubōva laddhavuttantēṇa, tahā purisō vi vittharantō bajjhavittharēṇa; sō khalu mahārambhapariggayāē nivāḍēi muhabhāvakulāṇi, viṇāsēi dhamma caraṇārāmē, kalu sēi kammuṇā apāṇaya, saṁjujjaē kūrasattēhi, viujjaē nirīhasāhujaṇēṇa, sēvijaē ummāyakallōlēhi, vajijaē kiccamajjāyāē. ēvaṁ ca mahāmōhāva tamajhavattī niratthiyāē ahō purisiyāē aviyāriūṇa paramatthaṁ, aṇālōciūṇa tassa bhaṅgurattaṁ, māindayālavibbhamē tami asaï pattē vi apariciē aśyāraē niyamēṇa accantagiddhō saparāvayāraē tti. rahiō ya ṇēṇaṁ, jahā imī sariyā payaïbhāvē vaṭṭamāṇī sōhaṇā, tahā purisō vi vijamāṇē vivēē niratyayaparikilēsarahiō saṁgaō suddhāsaraṇa vanjiō pāvamittahiṁ jīvalōōvayārōvabhōyasaṁpāyaṇasamatthō havaï, avijamāṇē avāyagamaṇapaḍibandhē bajjhavihavavittharabhāvō uṇa vivēiṇō vi mahantaṁ paralōyantarāyaṁ nibandhaṇaṁ micchāhimāṇassa ucchāyaṇaṁ cittanivvuīē saṁpāyaṇaṁ parikilēsāṇa paṇāsaṇaṁ nāṇapariṇaīē vēriyaṁ saṁtōsāmayassa bandhavaṁ asañcavasāyāṇaṁ ayāṇayaṁ viyambhasuhassa viyāṇayaṁ kavaḍanīiṇaṁ vajiya kusalajōēṇaṁ saṁgayaṁ pāvāṇumaīē. tahā jaï vi kēsiṁci dabośyārasaṁpāyaṇasamatthamēyaṁ, tahāvi ittarōtaō na annapīḍāē viṇā paramasthō sō vi saṁbhavaï. pahāṇō ya bhāvō vayārō na-yāparicattārambhaparicattārambhapariggaḍō sacahā taṁ saṁpāḍēi. juttaṁ ca maṇuyabhāvē tassa saṁpāyaṇaṁ, kimannēṇa niratthaēṇaṁ ti. cintayantassa samuppanō sayaladukkhaviuḍaṇekkapaccalō kusalapariṇāmō. pavaḍamāṇasuhapariṇāmō ya niyattō rāyā. sāhiō ṇēṇa ēsa vaïyarō raya gavaī pahiyāga manīṇaṁ. bhaṇiyaṁ ca ṇēhiṁ. dēva, ēvamēyaṁ, na annaha ti. karēu sanōhiyaṁ dēvō. ala ettha kālakkhēvēṇa aïcaścalā jīvalōyaṭṭhiī, muhuttamētaṁ pi ya taṁ pasaṁsi jaē jaṁ pāmastha sāha gaparāṇaṁ. tō kiccamēyaṁ ti cintiūṇa rāigā davāviya māghōsaṇāpubdhayaṁ mahādāṇaṁ, kārāviyā sanyāyayaṇēsu pūyā, sammāgiyāō payāō, nivēsiō rajjē dhiibalō.

tō ya paüttipurisēhitō kāsiyāvisayasaṁṭhiyaṁ viyāṇiūṇa bhavantaṁ vijayadhammāyariyaṁ pahāṇa sāmantāmaccasaṁgō samaṁ rayaṇa vaīē payaṭṭō gurusamīvaṁ rāyā. pattō kālakamēga. diṭṭhō vāṇārasīnayarisaṁṭhiō bhaya vinayadhammō. vandiō pahaḍhavayaṇakamalēṇaṁ dhammalāḍiō gurugā, pucchi bhō āganagapaōyaṇaṁ. sāhiyaṁ rāigā. parijuṭṭō gurū, upavūhiō.ya ṇēṇa. taō pasatyēṇa tihi karaṇamuhutta nōēṇa vāṇārasīnayarisāmiṇā saṁpāḍiyamahādayōvayārō samaṁ pubbabhaṇiyapariyaṇēṇaṁ mahāvibhūīē visujjhamāṇēṇa pariṇā mēṇaṁ saṁjāyacaraṇapariṇāmō pacāiō rāyā.

aïntō kōi kālō. ahinjiya muttaṁ, amatyō kiriyākalāyō. uciyasamaē ya jāyā sē icchā pavajāmi ahayaṁ ēga llavihārapaḍima. pucchiō gurū, aṇu-nāō ya ṇēṇaṁ. kayā sattāitulaṇā. nibūḍhēṇa pabannō siddhantavihiṇā ēgallavihāra paḍimaṁ ti. niraïyārakappēṇa ya viharamāṇasta aïkkantō kōi kālō.

annayā ya gō kollāgamannivēsaṁ ṭhiō ya tattha paḍimāē. diṭṭhō malayapatthiēṇaṁ vāṇamaṁtarēṇa. jāō sē kotrō. cintiyaṁ ca ṇēṇaṁ. peccha sō pāyō pāvapariṇaīē kīisō jāō ti. vāvāēmi saṁparya, ēmō ya etthuvāō. ēvaṁ cēva saṁṭhiyasta muēmi uvari mahāmahanti silaṁ ti. tīē saṁcuṇiyajuvaṅgō vajjapahārabhinnō viya girī sayasikakarō gamissaï. vāvāiē ya ēyaṁmi kayatyō ahaṁ, saphalaṁ vijāvalaṁ. tā lahuṁ samīhiyaṁ karēmi tti. cintiūṇa aïroddajjhāṇasaṁ gaēṇaṁ adūradēsavattigiriparāō gahiyā mahāśilā, uppaïūṇa dūramambaraṁ bhayavaō upari mukkā ya ṇēṇa. pīḍiō tīē bhayavaṁ kāraṇa, na uṇa bhāvēṇa. nirūviō vāmatarēṇa. jāva na vāvāiō ti, kuvitrō vāṇamaṁtarō. cintiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa. ahō sē mahāpāvassa sāmatyaṁ, ahō jīvaṇasattī, ahō mamōpari avannā, ahō paralōyapakkhavāō. tā tahā karēmi, jahā savvaṁ sē avēi. gahiyā mahallayarī milā, vimukkā tahēva. pīḍiō tīē vibhayavaṁ kāraṇa na uga bhāvēṇa. nirūviō vāṇamaṁtarēṇa. jāva na vāvāiō ti. annā vimukkā, tīē vi na vāvāiotti. visaṇṇō vāṇamaṁtarō. cintayaṁ ca ṇēga. na ēsa mahāpāyō vāvāiuṁ tīraï. tā karēmi sē dhamnantarayaṁ. viḍambēmi lōē. kaṁci gēhaṁ musiūṇa muēmi ēya samīvē mōsa, payāsēmi ya lōē, jahā imiṇā mahāpāvēga iyamaṇuciṭṭhiyaṁ ti. ēvaṁ ca kaē samāṇē pāvirūpaï mahāpāvō mahaī kayatthaṇaṁ ti. ciniūṇa saṁpāḍiyamaṇēṇaṁ! sāhiyaṁ daïṇḍavāsiyāṇaṁ gayā daïṇḍavāsiyā. diṭṭhō ṇēhiṁ bhayavaṁ. jāō tēsiṁ viyappō. ahō imassa pasannā muttī, tavasōsiyaṁ śarīraṁ, uvabhōyarahiō āgārō, agāulaṁ cittaṁ. tā kahaṁ ēsa ēvaṁ karissaï. ahavā vicittā gaī kavaḍāṇa. tā nirūvēmō tāva mōsaṁ. nirūviō niuñjadēsē diṭṭhō ya ṇēhiṁ. samuppannā saṅkā. pucchiō bhayavaṁ. jāva na jaṁpaï tti, tāḍiō ekkēṇa. tahāvi na jaṁpaï tti. kūrayāē harisiō vāṇamaṁtarō. baddhaṁ nira gāuyaṁ, nikāciyaṁ roddajjhāṇāhiṇivēsēṇa. cintiyaṁ daṇḍavāsiēhi. kimamhāṇamēiṇā, rāiṇō sāhēmō tti sāhiyaṁ vīsasēṇarāiṇō. samāō rāyā. hiṭṭhō ṇēṇa bhayavaṁ, pañcabhinnāō ya. vandiō paramabhattīē. bhaṇiyā daṇḍavāsiyā. bhō bhō na tumbhēhiṁ bhayavaō kiṁci paḍikūlamāsēviyaṁ ti. daṇḍavāsiēhiṁ bhaṇiya. na kiṁci tārisaṁ. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ. bhō ēsa bhayavaṁ amhāṇa sāmī mahārāyaguṇacandō niruvasaggaṁ mahiṁ pāliūiṇa sayalasaṅgacāī saṁpattajjhā dēva, dhannō khu ēsō. khāmiō tēhiṁ. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ. kēṇē tumhāṇa ēvaṁ sāhiyaṁ. daṇḍavāsirahiṁ bhaṇiyaṁ. dēva, ihēva sō ciṭṭhaï tti. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ. kahiṁ, kahi, āṇēha sigdhaṁ. ēyaṁ sōūṇa adaṁsaṇībhūō vāṇamaṁtarō. na diṭṭhō daṇḍavāsiēhiṁ, bhaṇiyaṁ ca ēhiṁ. dēva, saṁpayaṁ cēva dihō, iyāṇi na dīsaï ti. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ. bhō jaï ēvaṁ, tā amāṇusō sō bhayavaō uvasaggakārī bhavissaï. tā alaṁ tēṇa kiliṭṭhasattēṇa. nivēraha tumbhē antē rāṇaṁ sayalanaṇavayasta ya, jahā samāgaō bhayavaṁ tumhāṇa paramasāmī, ṭhiō uttamavaē muttimantō viya dhammō, pāvapasamagō daṁsaṇēga, vandaṇijjō sayāṇaṁ, nibandhaṇaṁ paramanivvuī ē mahārāyaguṇacandō; tā ēha, taṁattaṇō'ṇu gahaṭāē bhattimantō vihavāṇurūvēṇamuvayārēṇa vandaha tti. daṇḍavāsiēhi bhaṇiyaṁja dēvō āṇavēi. gayā daṇḍavāsiyā. nivēiyaṁ rāyasā saṇaṁ antēurajaṇāṇaṁ. āṇandiyā ēē, payaṭṭā bhayavantavandaṇavaḍiyāē, pattā mahāvicchaḍḍēṇa. pūiō bhayavaṁ vandiō harisanibbharēhi thuō santaguṇadīvaṇāē. vimhiyā tassa dēsaṇēṇaṁ.

etthantaraṁmi nivēiyaṁ rāiṇō silāvaḍaṇaniggaghāyamōhapaḍibuddhēṇa kaṭṭhuvāhaēṇa, jahā mahārāya, ēyassa bhayavaā uvāra kaṇāāva gaya ṇacāriṇā vimukkā mahantī sigā; na cāliō bhayavaṁ taō vibhāgāō; tanivaḍaṇanigghāyaō samāgayā mē mucchā; taō paraṁ na yāṇāmi, kiṁ kayaṁ tēṇa bhayavaō; ettiya puṇa jāṇāmi, ēyaṁ pi silāduyaṁ tēṇēva mahāpāvakammēṇa mukkaṁ ti. ēvaṁ sōūṇa unvi ggā antēurajaṇā. pīḍiō rāyā, bhaṇiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa. ahō mahāduknamaguhūyaṁ bhayavayā, ahō kilittaṇaṁ khuḍḍajīvāṇaṁ, ahō vivēya munnayā, ahō jahannattaṇaṁ, ahō nisaṁsayā, ahō alōiyattaṁ, ahō guṇapaōsō, ahō akallāṇabhāyaṇayā, ahō kammapariṇāmasāmatthaṁ, jēṇa bhayavaō vi paricattasavvasaṅgasya savvabhāvayattiṇō sayalajaṇōvayāranirayassa appaḍibaddhavihāriṇō ēvamuvasaggakaraṇaṁ ti. savvahā natthi nāmākaraṇijjaṁ mōhaparatantāṇaṁ. ēvaṁ vilaviūṇa ahō bhayavaō vi utrasaggō ti gahiō mahāsōēṇa. taṁ ca tahāvihaṁ viyā ṇaruṇa abhippēyajjhāṇasamattīē aṇāḍhaviūṇamannajjhāṇaṁ ōsaïriūṇa kāyaceṭṭhaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ bhayavayā. mahārāya, alamettha sōēṇa. sakaya kammaphalamēyaṁ, kettiyaṁ vā imaṁ. aṇādikrammasaṁtāṇavasavattiṇō jīvassa dukkharūbō cēva saṁsārō.

annaṁ ca suṇasu jīvō sakammapariṇāmaō vicittāī

sārīramāṇasāiṁ dukkhāi bhamanti bhunanti

jēṇēva u saṁsārē jammajarāmaraṇarōgaṇiyāī

piyavirahaparabbhatthaṇahīṇa jaṇōmāṇaṇāī ca

tēṇēva u sappurisā kilē sabahulasta bhavasamudassa

dhaṇīyaṁ viratta bhāvā dhammataruvaraṁ pavajanti

sammattamūlamantaṁ mahantasuyanāṇabaddhakhandhillaṁ

chaṭṭhaṭṭhamāivitthiyapavaratavacarittasāhālaṁ

sīlaṅgavaradvāra sasahassaghaṇapattabahalachāillaṁ

tiyasindaramaṇuyabahuvihapāyaḍaruiriddhikusumālaṁ

avvābāhuppēhaḍaniruvamakhayarahiyabhuvaṇamahiēṇaṁ

muṇijaṇakamaṇijjēṇaṁ sivasokkhaphalēṇa phalavantaṁ

jiṇajalayakēvalāmalajaladhārānivaharuirasiñcantaṁ

vivihamuṇivihagasēviyamaṇudiyahamachinnasaṁtāṇaṁ

tē uṇa tiyasavila siṇimuhapaṅkayabhamarabhāvamaṇuhaviuṁ

dhammatarukusumabhūyaṁ pāvanti phalaṁ pi muttimuhaṁ

kāvurisā uga bandhayanēhakkhayalakkhaṇicavēhīṇa

mūḍhā tucchāṇa kaē daḍhaṁ kilissanti bhōyāṇa

nīyajaṇapajjuvāsaṇamaṇabhimayāṇēya vēsakaraṇaṁ ca

ubbhaḍasamarapavēsaṁ niyabandhavaghāyaṇaṁ cēva

vitthiṇṇajalahitaraṇaṁ sabbhāviyamittavañcaṇaṁ taha ya

taṁ natthi jaṁ na bahusō karenti visayāhilāsēṇa

taha vi ya puvvajjiyavivihakammapariṇāmaō u saṁpattī

pariṇāmadāruṇēhi vina hōi bhōēhi savvēhi

pecchantā vi ya dhaṇiyaṁ vijjulayāḍōvacañcalaṁ jīyaṁ

ayarāmaraṁ va muṇiūṇa tahavi appāṇayaṁ mūḍhā

kāmaṁ visayāsēvaṇapamuhēhi sakammarukkhamūlāī

kaïlasēhi siściūṇaṁ phalāi pariṇāmavirasāī

nirayagamaṇāiyāī bhuñjantā ṇēya bhēyabhinnāī

hiṇḍanti akayapuṇṇā ghōrē saṁsārakantārē

tā ēvaṁviharūvē saṁsārē payaïnigguṇē sōma

kammavasayāṇamēvaṁ vihāi kō pucchaē ihaī

naraēsu kammavasaraṇa dāruṇaṁ suṇasu jaṁ maē dukkhaṁ

patta aṇantakhuttō parimbhamantēṇa saṁsārē

apaïṭāṇē naraē tettīsa sāgarāi aṇavarayaṁ

vasilāpaümēsu bhinnō upphiḍaṇapaḍaṇēhiṁ

sīmantayami ya tahā pakō nirayaggisaṁpalittāmu

kandasu ya kumbhīmu ya lōhakavallīmu ya ghaṇāsu

sēsēsu vi narasu pavvaya jantēhi karagaēhiṁ ca

vahiō mhi mandabhaggō annēhi ya tivvasatthēhiṁ

bhinnō khaïō ya ahaṁ aïrōdatimūlabajatuṇḍēhiṁ

tattajuyarahavarēsu ya bhinnacchō vāhiō bahusō

kappēūṇa ya sahasā tilaṁ tilaṁ tattha nisyapālēhi

parihiṁsādōsēṇaṁ kō bali phuraphurantō'haṁ

ukkhaṇiūṇa ya jīha virasaṁ bollāviō balā bhīō

aliyavayaṇadōsēṇaṁ dukkhattō kaṇṭhagayapāṇō

asicakkabhinnadēhō bahusō paradabaharaṇadōsēṇaṁ

vikkhittō chettūṇaṁ disōdisaṁ giddhavandrēṇa

vāyasasuṇahayahiṅkāiēhi karuṇaṁ samāra ḍantō ya

khaïō vahuēhi dahaṁ pariggahārambhadōsēṇaṁ

ukattiūṇa bahumō virasāiṁ khāviō samaṁsāi

maṁsaṁmi lōluyattaṇadōsēṇaṁ āmapakkāī

taha pāiō rasantō tattāī ta uyatambasīsāī

saṁḍāsadhariyamuhō majjarasāsaṅgadōsēṇaṁ

tiriēmu vi saṁsārē asaī pattāi tivvadukkhāī

vahabāhaṇanēlacchaṇadahaṇaṅkaṇabhēyabhinnāī

maṇuēmu vi ya narāhiba : parabasadāridda paṇḍagādīṇi

ēvaṁ na kiṁci ēyaṁ ti cayasu nikkāraṇaṁ sōyaṁ

rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ. bhayatraṁ asōyaṇijō tuma, kō taē saphalō maṇuyajammō, pattaṁ vivēyāuhaṁ, niuttō vavasāō, thirīkō appā, vijiō, bhāvasattū, vasīkayā tabasirī, ujjhiō pamāō, bōliyaṁ bhavagahaṇaṁ, pattappāō mokkhō ti. sōyaṇijjō uṇa sō kiliṭṭhusattō, jō bhayavaō uvasaggakāri tti. bhayavayā bhaṇiyaṁ. mahārāya, iīsō ēsa saṁsārō; tā kimannacintāē, appā ṇaya cintēhi. rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ. āisaü bhayavaṁ, kassa uṇa samīvē ahaṁ sayalasaṅgacāyaṁ karēmi. bhayavayā bhaṇiyaṁ. bhayavaō vijayadhammaguruṇō tti. paḍissuyaṁ rāiṇā, aṇuciṭriyaṁ vihāṇēṇa. vihariō bhayavaṁ. aïkkantō kōi kālō. iō ya vāṇamaṁtarassa khīṇappāē ihabhavāuē udayābhimuhīhūyaṁ risivahapariṇāmasaṁciyaṁ amuhakamma, samuppannō tivyō vāhī, uva hayāi indiyāī, paṇaṭṭhō niyasahāvō, uiṇṇā asuhavēyaṇā. tō ya uvayarijamāṇō pasiddhōvakkamēṇa sahāvavivarīyayāē ahiyayaramakka damāṇō aïniuṇavejjavayaṇēṇa appasiddhīvakkamēṇa viṭṭhāiviṭṭālaṇāikaṇṭayasayaṇīyasaṁgaō mahāmōhagamaṇēṇa paricattakandasadō gami ūga kaṁci kālaṁ aïroddajjhāṇadōsēṇa maō samāṇō samuppannō mahātamāhihāṇāē niāyapuḍhavīē tettīsasāgarōvamāū nāragattāē ti. bhayavaṁ pi vihariūṇa visuddhavihārēṇa sēviūṇa paramasaṁjama khaviūṇa kammarāsiṁ kāūga bhāvasalēhaṇaṁ bhāviūṇa bhāvaṇāō khāmiūṇa savvajīvē gantūṇa pahāṇathaṇḍilaṁ bandiūṇa vīyarāgē rumbhiūṇa ceṭṭhāō kāūga mahāpayattaṁ pavannō pāyavōvargamaṇaṁ ti. aṇupāliūṇa tamēgantaniraïyāraṁ vandijamāṇō muṇigaṇēhiṁ lōēṇa ubagijamā gō accharāhiṁ thuvyamāṇō dēvasaṁghāraṇa caïūṇa dēha samuppannō savaṭṭhasiddhē mahāvimāṇē tettīsasāgarōvamāū dēvattāē tti.

guṇacandavāṇamaṁtara jaṁ bhaṇiyamihāsi taṁ gayamiyāṇi

vocchāmi jamiha sēsaṁ gurūvaēmāṇusārēṇaṁ

atthi ihēva jambuddīvē dīvē bhārahē vāsē uttuṅgabhavaṇasaṁruddharavirahamaggā māṇikkamuttāhiragṇadhannāularundahaṭṭamaggā susanniviṭṭha tiyacaükkacaṁcarā dēvaülavihārārāmamaṇḍiyā ujjēṇī nāma nayarī.

jā tilayakayacchāyā viyaḍavēsāhirāmamuhakamalā

pāyārēṇa piēṇa va piya vya gāḍhaṁ samavagūḍhā

athirattaṇakuviēṇa va daṭṭaṇaṁ kahavi mahiyalōiṇṇā

phalihārajjunibaddhā tihuyaṇariddhi va jā vihiṇā

sabō jīē surūvō sabō gugarayaṇabhūsiō niccaṁ

sabbō suvisthayadhaṇō sabō dhammujjuā lōō

rēhanti jīē sīmā sarēhi naliṇīvaṇēhi ya sarāī

kamalēhi ya naliṇīō kamāi ya bhamaravandēhi

tīē ya rāyā paṇayārivandrasāmannasayalavihavō vi

navaramasāmannajasō nāmēṇaṁ purisasīhō tti

kitti vva tassa jāyā nimmalavamubhavā'kalaṅkā ya

sabaṅgasundarī sundari tti nāmēṇa sasivayaṇā

dhammatthabhaggapasaraṁ tīē saha sokkhamaṇuhavantassa

paṇaïyaṇakayāṇadaṁ vōlīṇō kōi kālō tti

ibhō ya sō savvasiddhamahāvimāṇavāsī dēvō ahāuyama gupāliūṇa taō cuō samāṇō samuppannō sundarīē kucchisi. diṭṭhō ya tīē suviṇayaṁmi tīē cēva rayaṇīē pahāyasamayaṁmi paṇāsayantō timiraṁ maṇḍayantō nahasiri vibōhayantō kaïmalāyarē paṁgāsa yantō jīvalōyaṁ vandijjamāṇō lōēhiṁ dhuvvamāṇō risigaṇēhiṁ ubagijjamāṇō kinnarēhiṁ agghijamāṇō lacchīē añcantapasanta maṇḍalō nibandhaṇaṁ savakiriyāṇa cūḍāmaṇī udayadharāharassa savvuttamatēyarāsī diṇayarō vayaṇēṇamuyaraṁ pavisamāṇō tti. pāsiūṇa ya taṁ suhaviuddhā. siṭṭhōṁ ya tīē jahāvihiṁ daïyassa. harisavasubhinnapula ēṇaṁ bhaṇiyā ya tēṇaṁ. dēvi, tellokkavikkhāō tē puttō bhavissaï. taō sā ēvaṁ ti bhattāravayaṇamahiṇandiūṇa irisiyā cittēga. tō visēsaō tivaggasaṁpāyaṇarayāē saṁpā ḍiyasayalamaṇōrahāē abhaggamāṇapasaraṁ puṇṇahalamaṇuhavantīē pattō pasaïsamaō. tō pasatthē tihikaraṇamuhuttajōē viṇā parikilē sēṇa pasūyā ēsā. jāō sē dāraō. nivēiō rāiṇō purisasīhassa harisanimbharāē siddhimahanāmāē sundaricēḍiyāē. parituṭṭō rāyā. dinnaṁ siddhimaīē pāriōsiyaṁ. bhaṇiyā ya paḍihārī, jahā samāisamu ṇaṁ mama vayaṇēṇa jahāsannihiē paḍihārē, jahā mōyāvēha mama rajjē kālaghaṇṭāpaōēṇa savvabandhaṇāṇi, davāvēha ghōsaṇāpuvvayaṁ aṇavekkhiyāṇurūvaṁ mahādāṇaṁ, visajjāvēha paümarāya pamuhāṇa naravaīṇaṁ mama puttajammapaütti, nivēēha dēvīputtījammanbhudayaṁ paürāṇaṁ, kāravēha ayālachaṇanbhūyaṁ nayaramahasavaṁ ti. samā iṭṭhā ya tīē jahāiṭṭhaï paḍihārā. aṇuciṭṭhiyaṁ rāyasāsaṇaṁ paḍihārēhiṁ.

kārāviyaṁ ca tēhiṁ bahuvihavaratūrajaṇiyanigyōsaṁ

līlāvikāsakinbhamamaggapaṇacantajubaïnaṇaṁ

vellahalabāhulaïyāvilōlavalaüllasantajhaṁkāraṁ

hēlucchalanta karakamaladhariyavimalavaraddhantaṁ

kappūrakuṅkumuppaṅkapaṅkapūriyanahaṅgaṇābhōyaṁ

bahalamayaṇāhikadamakhuppantapaḍantanāyarayaṁ

karakaliyakaṇayasiṅgayasalilapahārullasantasikkāraṁ

mayavasavisaṅkhalucchaliyagīyalayajaṇiyajaṇahāsaṁ

līlālasavisamacalantalaliyapayaraṇaraṇantamañjīraṁ

calamēhalākalāvullasantakalakiṅkiṇikalāvaṁ

annonnasamukkhittuttarōyadīsantathaṇayavitthāraṁ

halahalayamiliyanāyarayalōyaruddhantasaṁcāraṁ

tūriyajaṇāṇamaṇavaracittakkhippantamaharihābharaṇaṁ

vijiyasuralōyavihavaṁ baddhāvaṇayaṁ maṇabhirāmaṁ

āṇandiyā paürajaṇavayā. saṁpāḍiyaṁ vaddhāvaṇāiyaṁ uciyakaraṇijjaṁ. ēvaṁ ca païdiṇaṁ mahantamāṇandasokkhamaṇuhavantassa samaï cchiō paḍhamō māsō. païṭāviyaṁ nāmaṁ dārayasta uciō ēsa ēyassa tti kaliūṇa sumiṇayadaṁsaṇēṇa piyāmahasantiyaṁ samarāiccō ti.

etthantaraṁmi sō vi vāṇamaṁtarajīvō nāraō taō narayāō uccaṭṭiūṇa nāṇāvihatiriēsu āhiṇḍiūṇa pāviūṇa dukkhāī tahākammapariṇaïvasēṇa gōmāuattāē mariūṇa imīē cēva nayarīē pāṇavāḍayaṁmi gaṇṭhigābhihāṇassa pāṇassa jakkhadēvābhihāṇāē bhāriyāē kucchisi samuppannō suyattāē tti. jāō kālakkamēṇa. païṭāviyaṁ sē nāmaṁ girisēṇō tti. sō ya kurūvō jaḍamaī dukkhiō dāridō tti dukkhēṇa kālaṁ gamēi.

samarāiccō ya visiṭṭhuṁ puṇṇaphalamaṇuhavantō pubvabhavamukayavāsaṇāguṇēṇa bālabhāvē vi abālabhāvacariō sayalasatthakalāsaṁpattisundaraṁ pattō kumārabhāvaṁ. puvabhavamāsēṇa aṇurattō satyepnu cintaē ahiṇivē sēṇa, uppikśaē cittabhāvē nirūvēi samma gaḍēi tattajuttīē, bhāvaē samabhāvēṇa, vaḍḍaē saddhāē, paüñjaē gōyaraṁmi, gacchaē saṁvēyaṁ. ēvaṁ ca satyasaṁgayassa tattabhāvaṇāṇusaraṇavalēṇaṁ jāyaṁ jāisaraṇaṁ. na vināyaṁ jaṇēṇa. taō sō abhatthayāē kusalabhāvassa pahīṇayāē kammuṇō visuddhayāē nāṇassa hēyayāē visayāṇaṁ uvāēyayāē pasamassa avijamāṇayāē dukkaḍayāṇaṁ ukkaḍayāē jīvavīriyassa āsanayāē siddhisaṁpattīē na bahu mannaē rāyalacchi, na ujjaō sarīrasa kārē, na kīlaē cittakīlāhiṁ, na sēvara gāmadhammē, kēvalaṁ bhavavirattacittō suhajhāṇajōēṇaṁ kālaṁ gamēi ti.

taṁ ca tahāvihaṁ dadrūṇa samuppannā purisasīhassa cintā. ahō ṇu khalu ēsa kumārō aṇanasarisē vi cittē sundarō vi rūvēṇa pattē vipaḍhamajōvaṇē saṁgaō vi kalāhi pecchantō vi rāyakannayāōx nirubahaō vi dēhēṇa juttō vi indiyasirīē rahiō vi muṇidaṁsaṇēṇa na chippaē jovvaṇaviyārēhi, na pecchaē addhacchipecchiēṇa, najaṁpaē khaliyavayaṇēhi, na sēvaē gēyāikalāō, na bahu mannaē bhūsaṇāī, na gheppaē maraṇa, na muccaē ajavayāē, na patthara visayasokkhaṁ. tā kiṁ puṇa imaṁ ti. puṇṇasaṁbhārajuttō ya ēsō, jēṇa divō dēvīē ēyasaṁbhavakālē pasatthamuviṇaō; gambhasaṁgaē ēyaṁmi natthi ja mē na saṁjāyaṁ. aō bhaviyavvamēyassa mahāpaïṭṭhāē, pāviyanvamēyasaṁbandhēṇa mamhēhiṁ pārattiyaṁ. tā ēsa etthuvāō. karēmi sē dullaliyagoṭṭhisaṁgaē nimmāē kalāhiṁ viyakkhaṇē raïkīlāmu ārāhaē paracittassa addhāsiē mayaṇēṇa visiṭṭakulasamuppannē pahāṇamittē. taō tēsiṁ saṁsaggīē saṁpāḍissaï mē paramapamōyaṁ ti. cintiūṇa kayā kumārassa dullaliyagōṭīcūḍāmaṇibhūyā muttimantā vitha mahumayaṇadōgundugāī asōyakāmakuralaliyaṅgayappamuhā pahāṇamittā. bhaṇiyā ya rāiṇā. tahā tumbhēhiṁ jaïyavvaṁ, jahā kumārō visiddhalōyamagaṁ pavajaï. tēhiṁ bhaṇiyaṁ. jaṁ dēvō āṇavēi । aïkkantā kaïi diyahā. uvagayā vīsatthayaṁ. āḍhattō ya ṇēhiṁ mahurōvaka mēga, kumārō gāyanti maṇaharaṁ, pahanti gāhāō, pucchanti vīṇāpaōē, pasaṁsanti nāḍayāī, viyārendhi kāmasatthaṁ, daṁsenti cittāī, vaṇṇēni sārasamihuṇayāī nindanti cakkāī, kuganti itthikahaṁ, daṁsenti saravarāī, karenti jalakīḍaṁ, nivēsanti ujjāṇēsu, pasāhinti sundaraṁ, kīlanti ḍōlāhiṁ, raenti kusumasattharē thuṇanti visamabāṇaṁ ti. kumārō uṇa pavaṅkamāṇasaṁvēō ahō ēēsi mūḍhayā! kahaṁ puṇa ēē paḍibōhiyanca tti uvāyacintāparō uparōhasīlayāē paḍikūlamabhaṇamāṇō ciṭṭhaï. ēvaṁ ca aïkkantō kōi kālō. tēsiṁ paḍibōhaṇatthaṁ tu kiṁci nāḍayapecchaṇāi abbhuvagayaṁ kumārēja, vaḍiyā pīī, nīyā ya paramavīsatthayaṁ.

annayā ya ēsa ettha visayāhiō uvāō ti mantiūṇa paropparaṁ kaō asōēṇa kāmasatthapasaṅgō. bhaṇiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa. bhō kiparaṁ puṇa imaṁ kāmasatthaṁ. kāmaṅkurēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. bhō kimettha pucchiyadhvaṁ; avigalativaggamāhaṇaparaṁ ti. kāmasatthabhaṇiyapaōyannuṇō hi purisassa sadāracittārāhaṇa saṁrakkhaṇēṇa suddhasuyabhāvō visuddhadāṇāikiriyāpasiddhīē ya mahantō dhammō. aṇurattadārasuddhasuēhitō ya tayaṇubandhaphalasārā saṁpajjanti atthakāmā; vivajjaē uṇa tiṇhaṁ pi vivajjō. jaō aṇārāhaṇēṇa dāracittassa na paramatthaō saṁrakkhaṇaṁ, asaṁrakkhaṇē ya tassa asuddhamuyabhāvaō tēsi nirayāijōyaṇāē visuddhadāṇāikiriyābhāvō mahantō ahammō, aṇaṇurattadārā visuddhasuēhitō ya paṇassanti atthakāmā, na ya kāmasatthabhaṇiyapaōyaparināṇarahiō niyamēṇa sadāracittaṁ ārāhēi tti. ēēṇa kāra ṇēṇaṁ tivaggasāhaṇaparaṁ kāmasatthaṁ ti. laliyaṅgaēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. sōhaṇamiṇaṁ, na ettha kōi dōsō. ēyaṁ tu sōhaṇayaraṁ, dhammatthāṇa sāphalla. yānidarisaṇaparaṁ ti; na jaō kāmābhāvē dhammatthāṇamannaṁ phalaṁ, na ya niṣphalattē tēsiṁ purisatthayā. na ya mokkhaphalasāhagattaṇēṇaṁ saphalā imē, jaō alōiō mokkhō samāhibhāvaṇājhāṇapagarisaphalō ya. tamhā dhammatthāṇa sāphallayānidarisaṇaparamēyaṁ ti. ēvaṁ cēva sōha ṇayaraṁ. asōēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. kumārō etya pamāṇaṁ ti. kāmakurēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. suṭchu pamāṇaṁ. laliyaṅgaēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. jaï ēvaṁ, tā karēu pasāyaṁ kumārō; sāhēu, kimettha sōhaṇayaraṁ ti. kumārēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. bhō na tumbhēhiṁ kuppiyadhvaṁ, bhaṇāmi ahamettha paramatthaṁ. savvēhi bhaṇiyaṁ kumāra, annāṇanāsaṇē kō kōyō. karēu pasāyaṁ kumārō, bhaṇāu paramatthaṁ ti. kumārēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. bhō suṇaha. kāmasatthaṁ khu paramatthō karentasuṇentaya ṇamannāṇapayāsaṇaparaṁ, jaō kāmā asundarā payaīē viḍambaṇā jaṇāṇaṁ visōvamā paribhōē vacchalā kuceṭṭhiyassa. ēēhiṁ ahihūyā pāṇiṇō mahāmōhadōsēṇa na pecchanti paramatthaṁ, na muṇanita hiyāhiyāī, na viyāranti kajja, na cintanti āyaī. jēṇa kāmiṇō sayā'suiēsu asuddanibandhaṇēsu kalamalabhariēsu mahilāyaṇaṅgēsu candakundendīvarēhitō vi ahiyayararammabuddhīē ahilāsāirēgēṇa asuiē viya gaḍasūyarā dhaṇiyaṁ payaṭṭanti; aō na pecchanti paramatthaṁ. jaō ya dullahē maṇuyajammē laddhē kanmapariṇaīē sāhaē suddhadhammassa cañcalē payaīē saṁsārabaddhaṇēsu nivvāṇavērisu bālabahumaēsu buhayaṇagarahiēsu sajjanti kāmēsuḥ aō na muṇanti hiyāhiyāī. jaō ya asantēsu vi imēsu kāmasaṁpāḍaṇanimittaṁ niṣphalaṁ ubhayalōēmu kuṇanti cittaceṭṭhiyaṁ, khamanti akkhamāē, kilissanti akilisiyavvaṁ thuṇanti athōyavvāī, jhāyanti ajjhāiyavvāī, aō na viyārenti kajjaṁ. jō ya uvahasanti saccaṁ, kuṇanti kandappaṁ, nindanti guruyaṇaṁ, cayanti kusalamaggaṁ, havanti ōhasaṇijjā, pāvanti, ummāyaṁ, nindijanti lōēṇaṁ, gacchanti naraēmuaō na pecchanti āyaī. annaṁ ca. ihalōē cēva kāmā kāraṇaṁ vahabandhaṇāṇa, kulaharaṁ issāē, nivāsō aṇuvasamassa, khētaṁ visāyabhayāṇa, abhō cēva nindiyā dhammasatthēsu. ēvaṁvaṭṭhiē samāṇē nirūvēha majjhatyabhāvēṇa, kaha ṇu kāmasatthaṁ avigalativagga sāhaṇaparaṁ ti jaṁ ca bhaṇiyaṁ kāmasatyamaṇiyapaōyannuṇō hi purisassa sayāracittārāhaṇasaṁrakkhaṇēṇa suddhasuyabhāvaō visuddhadāṇāi kiriyāpasiddhīē ya mahantō dhammo tti, ēyaṁ pi na juttisaṁgayaṁ. jō na kāmasatyabhaṇiyapōyanna vi purisō niyamēṇa sadāraci. sārāhaṇaṁ karēti. dīsanti khalu imēsi pi vahicarantā dārā. nayāsamprapaōyajaṇiō taō bahicārō tti juttamāsakiuṁ, na jaō ettha nicchaē pamāṇaṁ. dīsaï ya tappaōyannū ēgadāracittārāhaṇaparō vi annasa tamagārāhayantō, apaōyanna vi yārāhayantō tti. tamhā jaṁ kiṁci ēyaṁ. jaṁ pi vejjagōdāharaṇēṇa ettha jāijutti bhaṇanti, sā vi ya payaïnigguṇa taṇēṇa kāmāṇa jīviyatthiṇō khagga siracchēkiriyāvihāṇajuttitulla tti na bahumayā buhāṇaṁ. ēvaṁ suddhasuyabhārī visuddhadāṇāikiriyāpasiddhī ya vabhicāriṇī dīsanti. kāmasatthaparāṇaṁ pi suyā akulaüttayā payaīē bhupaṅgamāyā ceṭṭhiēṇa. aṇurattadārāī pi ya niravekkhāṇi dāṇāikiriyāsu, tucchayāṇi payaīē, ahiyaṁ vivajjayakārīṇi. aō jaṁ pi jaṁpiyaṁ aṇurattadārāsuddhasuēhiṁtō ya tayaṇubaddhaphala sārā saṁpa janti atthakāma tti, taṁ pi ya asamañjasamēva. ēvaṁ ca ṭhiē samāṇē jaṁ pi bhaṇiya vivajaē uga tiṇhaṁ pi vivajaō tti iccēvamāi, taṁ pi parihariyamēva, vabhicāradōsēṇa samāṇō khu ēsaü. ihaī na hi na kāmasatthabhaṇiyapaōyannuṇō vi ēsō na hōi. aō na tagvijayanimittō khalu ēsō, avi ya akusalāṇubandhikammōdayanimittō, vivajaō vi akusalāṇubandhi kammōdayanimittō ti niratthayaṁ kāmasatyaṁ. tahā jaṁ ca bhaṇiyaṁ ēyaṁ tu sōhaṇayaraṁ, dhammatthāṇa sāphallayānidarisaṇaparaṁ kāmasatthaṁ ti, na jaō kāmābhāvē dhammatthāṇamannaṁ phalaṁ, na ya niṣpha lattē tēsiṁ purisatyayā, na ya mokṣaphalasāhagattēṇa saphalā imē, jaō alōiō mokkhō samāhibhāvaṇājhāṇapagarisaphalō ya tti, ēyaṁ puṇa asōhaṇayaraṁ. jaō pāmāgahiyakaṇḍuyaṇapāyā kāmā virasayarā avasāṇē bhāvandhayārakāriṇō asuhakammaphalabhūyā kahēṁ dhammatthāṇa phalaṁ ti, kaī vā tahāvihāṇaṁ dhammatthāṇa purisatthayā, jē jaṇenti kāmē nāsenti uvasamaṁ kuṇanti amittasaṁgamāṇi atra ṇenti savvavasāya saṁpāḍayanti agāyaïṁ abapūranti sōyaṁ vihenti lāghavāī ṭhāventi appaccayaṁ haranti appamāyapāṇē kārenti aṇuvā ēyaṁ ti. jaṁpi ya sarīraṭṭhiihēubhāvēṇa āhārasadhammāṇō kāmā parihariyavvā ya etya dōsa ti mōhadōsēṇa bhaṇanti mandabuddhiṇō, taṁ pi na hu buhanaṇamaṇōharaṁ. jī viṇā vi ēēhiṁ muṇiyatattāṇaṁ pecchamāṇāṇa jahābhāvamēva bōṁdiviratāṇa tīē suddhajjhāṇāga risīṇa dīsaha sarīraṭṭhiī sēvamāṇāṇa vi ya tē tajaṇiyapāvamōhēṇa accantasēvaṇaparāṇaṁ khayādirōgabhāṣaō viṇāsō tti. tā kahaṁ tē sarīra hiihēyavō, kahaṁ vā āhārasadhammāṇō ti. na ya ēyasaṁgayā dōsā aparivattēhiṁ ērahiṁ abhinnanivandhamattēṇa tīranti parihari. na khalu mottaṇa mōhē kāmāṇamaṇuvasamāīṇa ya annaṁ nimittaṁ ti cintēha cittēṇa. ēvaṁvadvira samāṇē na hi hariṇā vijanti tti javā na parijanti' ēvamādi pahasaṇappāyaṁ kāmasatyavayaṇaṁ. tamhā na kāmaphalāṇa dhammatyāṇa purisatthayā, avi ya mokkhaphalāṇamēva. na ya alōiō mokkhō; jō vibhiṭṭamuṇilōyalōiō, rahiō jammāiē hiṁ, vajiō āvāhāē, samattī sanaka jāṇaṁ, pagarisō muha ssa. samāhi bhāvaṇājhāṇādaō vi na hi na dhammasarūvā, avi ya tē cēva bhāvadhammō. iyaśē vi nirōhaspa tapphalō cēva havaï, annahā garahiyāṇi iṭāpūyāṇi ti bhāviyavvaṁ satthavayaṇaṁ. na ya kāmā aṇindiyā, payaṭṭani. payaīē pasiddhā tiriyāṇaṁ pi mālā sarū vēṇaṁ. tā kimēēsi satthēṇa. jaṁ pi bhaṇiyaṁ vālāsaṁpaōō parāhīṇōti uvāyaṁ avekkhaḥ, uvāyapaḍibattī ya kāmasatthāō, tiriyāṇaṁ tu aṁgāvariyā ithijāī riukālē ya niyamiyā pavittī abuddhipuyāya ti, ēvaṁ pi mōhapisuṇayaṁ; jō uvāēyā cēva na havanti kāmā asundarā payaīē viḍambagā jaṇāṇa visōvamā paribhōē vacchalā kubēḍiyarasa tti daṁsiyaṁ maē. aō adanādāṇagahaṇa visayasatthakappaṁ khu ēyaṁ ti. karentasuṇentayāṇamannāṇapayāsaṇaparaṁ kāmasatthaṁ. bhaṇiyaṁ ca suddhacittahi.

taṁ nāma hōḍa satthaṁ jaṁ hiyamatthaṁ jaṇassa daṁsēi

jaṁ puṇa ahiyaṁ ti sayā taṁ naṇu kattoccayaṁ satthaṁ

ahiyā tō pavittō hōi ajaṁmi mandabuddhīṇaṁ

asuhōvaēsarūvaṁ jattēṇa tayaṁ payahiyadhvaṁ

iharā pējalaï cciya vamaha jalagō jaṇasta hiyayaṁmi

kiṁ puṇa agatyapaṇḍiyakukanyahavihōmiō santō

tā jaṁ kāmuddīraṇasamatyametthaṁ na taṁ buhajaṇēṇa

sumiṇē vi jaṁpiyavvaṁ pasaṁsiyavvaṁ ca duvyayaṇaṁ

pasamāibhāvajaṇayaṁ hiyamēgantēṇa savvasattāṇa

niuṇēṇa jaṁpiyadhvaṁ pasaṁsiyavvaṁ ca suvisuddha

ēvaṁ ca ṭhiē samāṇē alaṁ dubbayaṇasaṁgayāē kāmasatthacintāē tti.

ēyaṁ sōūṇa vimhayā asōyādī. cintiyaṁ ca ṇēhiṁ. ahō vivēgō kumārassa, ahō bhāvaṇā, ahō bhavavirāō, ahō kayannuyā. sacahā na īisō muṇijaṇassa vi pariṇāmō hōi, kiṁ tu phuḍaṁ pi jaṁpamāṇō dūmēē ēsa amhē tti. cintiūṇa jaṁpiyaṁ apōēṇa. kumāra, ēvamēyaṁ, kiṁ tu savvamēva lōyamaggāīyaṁ jaṁpiyaṁ kumārēṇa. tā alamimīē aïparamatthacintāē. na aṇāsē viē lōyamaggē imīē vi ahigārō tti. tā lōyamaggaṁ paḍucca kiṁparaṁ puṇa kāmasatthaṁ ti sāhēu kumārō. kāmaṅkurēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. sōhaṇaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ asōēṇa laliya gaēṇa bhaṇiya. na asōō asōhaṇaṁ bhaṇiuṁ jāṇaï. kumārēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. bhada, aparamatthapicchō pāēṇa lōō bhinnaī ya. tā na taṁ maggēṇa imassa ahaṁ kiṁpi parayaṁ avēmi. savvahā kandappiyāṇa bālāṇamaviṇōyaviṇōyapāyaṁ ēyaṁ, jō kāmasuhāī pi kammapariṇāma nibandhaṇāī jīvāṇaṁ, viuṇē ya taṁmi na paramatthēṇa imiṇā paōyaṇaṁ ti. uttarapayāṇāsāmatthēṇa ēvamēya ti abbhuvagayaṁ asōāīhiṁ. aïkkantā kaïi diyahā. ālōciyamaṇēhiṁ. tavassippāō kumārō, kahaṁ amhārisēhiṁ visaēsu payaṭṭāviuṁ tīraï. tahāvi atthi ekkō uvāō. uvarōhasīlō khu ēsō, paḍivanā ya amhē imēṇa mittā. tā abbhatthemha ēvaṁ kalattasaṁgahamantarēṇa, kayāi saṁpāḍēi amhāṇaṁ samīḍiyaṁ ti. ṭhāviūṇa siddhantaṁ samāgaē avasarē bhaṇiyaṁ asōēṇa. bhō kumāra, pucchāmi ahaṁ bhavantaṁ, kimettha jīvalōē supurisēṇa mittavaccha lēṇa hōyavvaṁ kiṁvā nahi. kumārēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. bhō sāhu pucchiyaṁ, sāhēmi bharaō. etya khalu tivihō mittō havaï. taṁ jahā. ahamō majjhimō uttimō tti. jō khalu saṁjōiō appaṇā dissamāṇō attāhiyaṁ aṇuyatti jamāṇō payaīē sēvijamāṇō païdiṇaṁ lālijamāṇō jattēṇa viloṭṭara vihuraṁmi, nāvekkhaï sukayāī, na rakkhaï vayaṇijjaṁ, pariccaï khaṇēṇa; ēsa ēyārisō aṇusama yasēviyaparicāī nāma jahannamittō. jō uga jahākahaṁci saṁgaō dissamāṇō attabuddhīē aṇuyattijamāṇō ajattēṇa sēvijamāṇōṁ vibhāē lālijjamāṇō ūsavāiēsu takkhaṇaṁ na visaṁvayaï, vihurē avekkhaï īsi sukayāī, rakkhaï maṇāgaṁ vayaṇijja, pariccayaï vilāvapubvayaṁ vilambēṇa; ēsa ēyārisō chaṇasēviyapariccāī nāma majjhimamittō. jō uṇa ajattēṇa diṭṭhābhaṭṭhō bahu mannaē sukayaṁ, uvāgacchaē metti, payaṭṭaē uvayārē, mōyāvaē duhāō, jaṇēi gōravaṁ, vaḍi māṇaṁ, karēi saṁpayaṁ, vihēi sokkhaṁ, na paricayaï āvayāē; ēsa ēyārisō jō kāramettēṇē sēviyāpariccāī nāma uttimamittō tti. ēvaṁṣahiē samāṇē supurisēṇālōciūṇa niyamaīē savvahā uttimamittavacchalēṇa hōyavvaṁ ti. kāmakurēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. bhō kō uṇa ihāhippāō. pasiddhamēvēyaṁ, jahannamajjhimē caïūṇa uttimō sēvijaï. kumārēṇa bhaṇiya. naṇu ēvamēva etyāhippāō, jaṁ jahannamajjhimē caïūṇa uttimō sēvijaï tti. laliyaṅgaēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. bhō na ēyamujjuyaṁ, gambhīraṁ khu ēyaṁ na visēsaō avivariyaṁ jāṇīyaï. tā vivarēhi saṁpayaṁ, kē uṇa imē tiṇṇi mittā. kumārēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. bhō jaï nāvagayaṁ tumhāṇaṁ, tā suṇaha saṁpayaṁ. ettha khalu paramatyamittē paḍucca pasiṇō uttaraṁ ca junjaïtti jaṁpiyaṁ maē. pasiddhaṁ tu lōiyaṁ,kō vā savē yaṇō tayatthaṁ na yāṇaï. tā imē mittā dēisavaṇadhammā. tatya jahannamittō dēhō, majjhimō sayaṇō, uttamō dhammō tti. jēṇa dēhō nahātahōvacarijamāṇō vi aṇusamayamēva daṁsēi viyārē, aśyiākhasaṁgayaṁ aṇuyattaï jaraṁ, carimāvayāē ya ujjhaï nirālambaṁ ti; ēsa jahannamittō. sayaṇō uṇa mamattāṇurūvaṁ karēi paḍimamattaṁ, kilissaï gilāṇāikajjē, paricayaï gayajīyasāraṁ, sumaraï ya patthāsu, ēsa majjhimamittō tti. dhammō uṇa saṁgaō jahākahaṁci vacchalō ēgantēṇa avisāī bhaēsu nimbāhaē mittayaṁ ti; ēsa uttamō. ēvaṁ ca nāūṇa adhuvē visaya sokkhē asārē payaīē mōhaṇē paramatthassa dāruṇē vivāē abahīriē dhīrēhiṁ, pāviē māṇusattē uttamē bhavāṇa dullahē bhavāḍavīē sukhettē guṇadhaṇāṇa sāhaē nidhāṇassa ujjhiūṇa mōhaṁ cintiūṇāyaī acintacintāmaṇisannihē vīyarāyappaṇīē uvādēē niyamēṇa hōha vacchalā sappurisasē viē uttamamittē dhammē tti ।. ēyaṁ muṇamāṇāṇa tahābhabvayāē asōyāīṇa vicittayāē kammapariṇāmassa kumārasannihāṇasāma tthēṇa visuddhayāē jōyāṇa ukaḍayāē vīriyassa viyambhiō kusalapariṇāmō, viyaliō kilikammarāsī, avagayā mōhavāsaṇā, tuṭṭā asuhāṇubandhā, jāō kammagaṇṭhibhēō, khaōvasamamuvagayaṁ micchattaṁ, āvihūō sammattapariṇāmō. taō samuppannasaṁvēgēṇa jaṁpiyaṁ asō ēṇa. kumāra, ēvamēyaṁ, na etya saṁdēhō, sōhaṇa samāiṭṭha kumārēṇaṁ. kāmakurēṇa bhagiya. sōhaṇāō vi sōhaṇaṁ. ahavā iyamēva ēka sōhaṇaṁ, natthi annaṁ sōhaṇaṁ ti. laliyaṅgaraṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. kiṁ bahugā, annāṇanidāpasuttā paḍibōhiyā amhē kumārēṇa, daṁsiyāī hēōvā dēyāī. tā payaṭṭamha sahiē, saṁpāḍēmō kumārasāsaṇaṁ. asōēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. kumāra, sāhu jaṁpiyaṁ laliyaṅgaēṇa; tā samāisaü kumārō, jamamhēhi kāyavvaṁ ti. kupārēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. bhō saṁkhēvaōtāva ēyaṁ. ujjhiyayō visayarābhō, ciniya bhavasarūpaṁ, vajjiyavvā kusaṁsaggī, sēviyavvā sāhuṇō; tō jahāsattīē dāṇa pīlatabhāvaṇāpahāṇēhiṁ hōyavvaṁ ti. asōyāīhiṁ bhaṇiyaṁ. sāhu kumāra sāhu, paḍivannamiṇa mamhēhiṁ. kumārēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. bhō dhannā khu tumbhē pāviyaṁ tumhēhiṁ phalaṁ maṇuya jammasta. tēhiṁ bhaṇiyaṁ. kumāra sāhu, ēvamēyaṁ dhannā khu amhē, na khalu ahanāṇa kumāradasaṇaṁ saṁpajaï. ēvaṁ cāhiṇandiruṇa kumāraṁ saṁpūiyā visē sēṇa kumārēṇa uciyāē vē lāē gayā saṭṭhāṇāī asōyāī. pāradaṁ jahōciyamaṇuṭāṇamēēhiṁ. aïkantā kaïi diyahā.

etthantaraṁmi samāgaō mahusamaō, viyambhiyā vaṇasirī, mañjariśrō cūyaniyarō, kusumiyā tilayāī, ullasiyā aïmuttayā, pavattō malayāṇilō, muiyaṁ bhamarajālaṁ, pasariō parahuyāravarē; jahiṁ ca mama mittara jamimaṁ ti uttugō kayatthēi bālavuṭṭhuṁ pi mayaṇō, sisirasattuvigamēṇa viya viyasiyakamalava yaṇā kamaliṇī,mahusamāgamasu hēṇa viya paṇanamāō janti jāmigīō, uulacchidasaṇapasattā viya tahā parimantharagamaṇā vāsarā; jahiṁ ca agdhaē navaraṅgaya, bahumayā pasannā, vahanti ḍōlāō, sēvijanti kāṇaṇāī, maṇaharō candō, ahimaō gēyavihī, vaṭṭanti pēraṇāī, piyānō kāmiṇīō; jahiṁ ca visēsujala nēvacchāī kīlanti taruṇavandrāī, bhamanti mahā vibhūīē dēvayāṇaṁ pi rahavarā, mayaṇavāha bhaēṇa viya saragāī alliyabhi piyayamēsu piyāō. ēvaṁvihē ya mahusamaē rāigō purisasī. hassa nayaricchaṇadasaṇanimittaṁ samāgayā nayarimahantayā. vinattō ṇēhiṁ rāyā. dēva, dēvē naravaïṁmi niccacchaṇō nayarīē; tahāvi samā gaō mahusamabhō tti vivihacacarīdaṁsaṇēṇa dēvapasāyalāliyāṇaṁ payāṇaṁ chaṇāō vi garuyaṁ chaṇantaraṁ karēu dēvō nāyarayāṇaṁ ti. rāiṇā cintiyaṁ. ahō sōhaṇamuvatthiya, mayaṇamittō khu mahusamaō. tā kumāraṁ ettha niuñjāmi, jēṇa tahā vicittasaṁsāraviyāradasaṇēṇa saṁjāyarasantarō saṁpāḍēi mē pariyaṇassa ya samīhiyāhiyaṁ sokkhaṁ ti. cintiūṇa bhaṇiyā mahantayā. bhō saṁpāḍiyā mama tumbhēhiṁ bahusō niyavibhūidaṁsaṇēṇa nivvuī, ahaṁ puṇa tumhāṇa kumāradasaṇēṇa ahiyaṁ saṁpāḍēmi. annaṁ ca, saṁparya kumārō etya kāraṇapurisō; tā taṁmi cēva bahumāṇō kāyayō tti. mahantaēhi bhaṇiyaṁ. jaṁ dēvō āṇavēi. annaṁ ca, dēvapasāyāō vi ēsa mahāpasāō jahiṁ kumāradasaṇaṁ ti. niggayā mahantayā. rāiṇā vi sahāviō kumārō, bhaṇiō ya sabahumāṇaṁ. vaccha, ṭhiī ēmā imīē nayarīē, jaṁ mayaṇamahūsavē daṭṭavvāō nayaricaccarīō rāiṇā, diṭṭhāō ya maē aṇēgasō. saṁpayaṁ puṇa aṇugantavvō gurusamaṇugō maggō tti tēṇēva vihiṇā tuma pi pecchāhi. ēvaṁ ca kaē samāṇē mamaṁ pariyaṇassa nāyarayāṇa ya mahantō pamōō havaï. kumārēṇa bhaṇiya. jaṁ tāō āṇavēi. tō hariliō rāyā, dinā samāṇattī paḍihārāṇaṁ. harē bhaṇaha mama vayaṇāō nāṇagabbhapamuhē pahāṇasacivē, jahā nayaricchaṇaca carīdaṁsaṇasuhaṁ saṁjattēha rahabarāiyaṁ kumārassa, mama vayaṇāō nāyarayāiparibhōsanimittaṁ rāyapayavattiṇā gantavvamajē ṇēṇē chaṇacaccarī dasaṇanimittaṁ ti. jaṁ dēvō āṇavēi tti bhaṇiūṇa kumārō ajja chaṇacaccarīō pekkhissaï, bhaviyāmamhāṇaṁ pikallāṇēṇaṁ ti hari siyamaṇēhiṁ turiyaturiyaṁ nivēiyā samāṇattī paḍihārēhiṁ. ahō bhaviyavamettha paramāṇandēṇaṁ ti āṇandiyā sacivāḥ. bhaṇiyaṁ ca ṇēhiṁ. jaṁ dēvō āṇavēi. tayaṇantaraṁ ca sajiō rahabarō, kayā jantajōyā, nivēsiyaṁ āyavattaṁ, dināō vējayantīō, nibaddhaṁ kiṅki ṇījālaṁ, niviṭṭhāī rayaṇadāmāī, ōlambiyā muttāhārā, viraïyāō maṇitārayāō, uvagappiyaṁ āsaṇaṁ, lambiyā cāmarōūlā. ettha ntaraṁmi imaṁ vaïyaramavayacchiūṇa visēsujjala nēvacchāī saharisaṁ samāgayāī pāyamūlāī, kuṅkumakhōyabhariēhiṁ kacōlēhiṁ vasantanēvacchadhārī maṇḍayantō viya chaṇaṁ miliō bhuyaṅgalōmō, vicittajāgārūḍhā saṁgaēṇaṁ pariyaṇēṇaṁ pamōyaviyapantalōyaṇaṁ kumāradasaṇūmuyatēṇa upatthiyā rāyaüttā, dhavalaharanijjūhaēhiṁ chagāisayadasaṇatyaṁ ōisiyathalanaliṇisōhāī viṇiggayavayaṇakamalaṁ ṭhiyāī antē ugaī. etthantaraṁmi pavattō nayarīē usayō. nivēiyaṁ rāṇī ci vēhiṁ. dēva, saṁpāḍiyaṁ kumāramantarēṇa dēvasāsaṇaṁ; saṁparya dēvō pamāṇaṁ ti. harisiō rāyā. bhaṇiō ya ṇēṇa kumārō. vaccha, karēhi mahāyurisakaraṇijaṁ vaḍḍēhi ūsavaṁ nāyarayāṇaṁ. kumārēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. jaṁ tāō āṇavēi. paṇami ūṇa saha aṁsōyāiēhiṁ payahō rahāhi puhaṁ ahigandi jamāṇō antēurēhiṁ paṇamijjamāṇō rāya uttēhiṁ thutramāṇō bhuyaṅgalōēṇa pulaïjjamāṇō pāyamūlēhiṁ pattō raha pamīvaṁ, ārūḍhō rahavarē, uvaviṭṭhō pahāgāsaṇaṁmi. nivēsiyā asōyāī jahājogganāṇēsu. bhaṇiyaṁ ca ṇēṇa. ajja sārāha, cāēāha āhamayadasagamaṇa paï turaṅgamē. ja dēvō āṇa vēi tti bhaṇiūṇa cōiyā turaṅgamā. etthantaraṁmi samuddhāiō jayajayāravō, pahayaṁ gamaṇaturaṁ, caliyā rāyaüttā, paṇacciyāi, pāyamūlāī, ullasiyā bhuyaṅgā, khuhiō pecchayajaṇō, pavattā kēlī, vimbhiō kuṅku maraō. ēvaṁ ca mahayā vimadēṇa pecchamāṇō satyamēya saṁvēgabhāviyamaī samōigaṇō rāyamaggaṁ kumārō. pattō pecchiuṁ caccarīō nāṇā vihāō riddhivisēsasōhiyāō juttā viyaḍḍavinbhamēhiṁ tiyasacaccarīsamāō saṁgayāō harisēga vajantēhiṁ vivihatūrēhiṁ maṇaharāō lōyasta saṁvēgajagaṇīō buhāṇa. pecchamāṇō ahō mōhasāmatthaṁ, ahō ajadhīrayā, ahō pamāyaceṭṭhiyaṁ, ahō adīhadarisiyā, ahō aṇālōyagataṁ, ahō asuhabhāṣaṇā, ahō apittajōō, ahō saṁsāravilasiyaṁ ti cintayantō pacaḍḍamāṇēga saṁvēēṇa viyārayantō kammāī, bhāvayantō kusala jōē visujjhamāṇēṇa nāṇēga pulaï jamāṇō caccarīhiṁ jaṇintō tāsi tōsaṁ nirūvayantō pēraṇāī dēva peccha ēyaṁ ti bhaṇi jamāṇō sārahiṇā aïga bhō kaṁci bhūmibhāgaṁ.

diṭṭhōya ṇēṇa dēvaülapīḍhiyāē aïbī icchadasaṇī asuiṇā dēhēṇa galantabhāsuravayaṇō saṁkuciēhiṁ hatthēhiṁ usmūṇacalaṇajuyalō paṇa dvāē nāsiyāē viṇiggayatambanayaṇō pariṁgaō macchiyāhiṁ mahāvāhigahiō kōi purisō tti. taṁ ca daṭṭhūṇa ahō kammapariṇatti karuṇāpavannahiyaraṇa paḍibōhaṇanimittaṁ jaṇasamūhassa bhaṇiō sārahī. ajja sārahi, aha kiṁ puṇa imaṁ pēraṇaṁ ti. tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. dēva, na khalu ēyaṁ pēraṇaṁ, ēsō khu vāhigahiō purisō tti. kumārēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. ajja, aha kō uga imō vāhī. sārahiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ. dēva, jō sundaraṁ pi sarīraṁ ayālēṇa ēvaṁ viṇāsēi. kumārēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. ajja, duṭṭhō khu ēsō ahiō lōyassa; tā kīsa tāō aïyaṁ visahaï. sāra hiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ. kumāra, abajjhō ēsa tāyassa. kumārēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. ā kahamavajjhō nāma. lōyapaḍibōhaṇatthaṁ ca maggiya khaggaṁ. arē rē duvāhi, mucca, muśca, ēyaṁ ṭhēāhi vā jujjhasanjō tti bhaṇamāṇō uḍhiō rahavarāō, payaṭṭō tassa samuhaṁ. hā kimēyaṁ ti uvasantāō caccarīō, miliyā nāyarayā ।payaṁpiō sārahī. dēva, na khalu vāhī nāma kōi duṭṭhupurisōniggahārihō naravaīṇa, avi ya jīvāṇamēva sakammapariṇāmajaṇiō saṁkilēsavisēsō. tā appaha ēyassa rāiṇō, sāhāraṇō khu ēsō sabajīvāṇa. kumārēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. bhō nāyarayā, kimēvamēyaṁ. nāyaraēhiṁ bhaṇiyaṁ dēva, ēṁvamē. kumārēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ ana sārahi, ēēṇa gahiō vi ēsō caïūṇa niyabalaṁ amaṇōramāē ēyamavatthāē kīsa ēvaṁ ciṭṭhaï. sārahiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ. dēva, īisō, cēva ēsō vāhī; jēṇa ēēṇa gahiyassa paṇassaï balaṁ, asōhaṇā avatthā, dukkhaphalaṁ ceṭṭhiyaṁ ti. kumārēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ ajja sārahi, kassa uṇa ēsō na pahavaï. sārahiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ dēva, paramatyēṇa dhamma paccha sēviṇō ahammāpacchavirayassa kassaï mahābhāgassa. kumārēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. ajja sārahi jaï ēvaṁ, tā kō uṇa iha uvāō. sārahiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ. dēva, khettaṁ vāhiṇō pāṇiṇō, paramatthēṇa natthi uvāō maüttūṇaṁ dhammatigicchaṁ. kumārēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ. bhō nāyarayōṁ,
